yuṣmad asmat pratyaya gocarayoḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ tamaḥ prakāśa vat viruddha svabhāvayoḥ itaretara bhāva anupapattau siddhāyām tad dharmāṇām api sutarām itaretara bhāva anupapattiḥ iti atas
asmad pratyaya gocare viṣayiṇi cit ātmake yuṣmad pratyaya gocarasya viṣayasya tad dharmāṇām ca adhyāsaḥ tad viparyayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ tad dharmāṇām ca viṣaye
adhyāsaḥ mithyā iti bhavitum yuktam
tathā api anyonyasmin anyonya ātmaka tām anyonya dharmān ca adhyasya itaretara avivekena atyanta viviktayoḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ mithyājñāna nimittaḥ satya anṛte mithunīkṛtya aham idam mama idam iti naisārgikaḥ
ayam lokavyavahāraḥ
āha kaḥ
ayam adhyāsaḥ nāma iti
ucyate smṛti rūpaḥ paratra pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ
tam kecid anyatra anya dharma adhyāsaḥ iti vadanti
kecid tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tad viveka agraha nibandhanaḥ bhramaḥ iti
anye tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tasya eva viparīta dharma tva kalpanām ācakṣate iti
sarvathā api tu anyasya anya dharma avabhāsa tām na vyabhicarati
tathā ca loke
anubhavaḥ śuktikā hi rajata vat avabhāsate ekaḥ candraḥ sa dvitīya vat iti
katham punar pratyagātmani aviṣaye
adhyāsaḥ viṣaya tad dharmāṇām
sarvaḥ hi puras
avasthite viṣaye viṣaya antaram adhyasyati yuṣmad pratyaya apetasya ca pratyagātmanaḥ
aviṣaya tvam bravīṣi
ucyate na tāvat ayam ekāntena aviṣayaḥ asmad pratyaya viṣaya tvāt
aparokṣa tvāt ca pratyagātma prasiddheḥ
na ca ayam asti niyamaḥ puras
avasthite eva viṣaye viṣaya antaram adhyasitavyam iti
a pratyakṣe
api hi ākāśe bālāḥ tala malina tā ādi adhyasyanti
evam aviruddhaḥ pratyagātmani api anātma adhyāsaḥ
tam etam evaṃlakṣaṇam adhyāsam paṇḍitāḥ avidyā iti manyante
tad vivekena ca vastu svarūpa avadhāraṇam vidyām āhuḥ
tatra evam sati yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tad kṛtena doṣeṇa guṇena vā
aṇu mātreṇa api sa na sambadhyate
tam etam avidyā ākhyam ātma anātmanoḥ itaretara adhyasam puraskṛtya sarve pramāṇa prameya vyavahārāḥ laukikāḥ vaidikāḥ ca pravṛttāḥ sarvāṇi ca śāstrāṇi vidhi pratiṣedha mokṣa parāṇi
katham punar avidyāvat viṣayāṇi pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni śāstrāṇi ca iti
ucyate deha indriya ādiṣu ahaṃmama abhimāna rahitasya pramātṛ tva anupapattau pramāṇa pravṛtti anupapatteḥ
na hi indriyāṇi an upādāya pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati
na ca adhiṣṭhānam antareṇa indriyāṇām vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati
na ca anadhyasta ātma bhāvena dehena kaścid vyāpriyate
na ca etasmin sarvasmin asati asaṅgasya ātmanaḥ pramātṛ tvam upapadyate
na ca pramātṛ tvam antareṇa pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ asti
tasmāt avidyāvat viṣayāṇi eva pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni śāstrāṇi ca
paśu ādibhiḥ ca aviśeṣāt
yathā hi paśu ādayaḥ śabda ādibhiḥ śrotra ādīnām saṃbandhe sati śabda ādi vijñāne pratikūle jāte tatas nivartante anukūle ca pravartante
yathā daṇḍa udyata karam puruṣam abhimukham upalabhya gām hantum ayam icchati iti palāyitum ārabhante harita tṛṇa pūrṇa pāṇim upalabhya tam prati abhimukhībhavanti
evam puruṣāḥ api vyutpanna cittāḥ krūra dṛṣṭīn ākrośataḥ khaḍga udyata karān balavataḥ upalabhya tatas nivartante tad viparītān prati pravartante atas samānaḥ paśu ādibhiḥ puruṣāṇām pramāṇa prameya vyavahāraḥ paśu ādīnām ca prasiddhaḥ
aviveka puraḥasaraḥ pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad sāmānya darśanāt vyutpattimatām api puruṣāṇām pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad kālaḥ samānaḥ iti niścīyate
śāstrīye tu vyavahāre yadi api buddhi pūrva kārī na a viditvā ātmanaḥ para loka saṃbandham adhikriyate
tathā api na vedānta vedyam aśanāya ādi atītam apeta brahma kṣatra ādi bhedam asaṃsāri ātma tattvam adhikāre
apekṣyate
anupayogāt adhikāra virodhāt ca
prāk ca tathābhūta ātma vijñānāt pravartamānam śāstram avidyāvat viṣaya tvam na ativartate
tathā hi brāhmaṇaḥ yajeta ityādīni śāstrāṇi ātmani
avasthā ādi viśeṣa adhyāsam āśritya pravartante
adhyāsaḥ nāma a tasmin tad buddhiḥ iti avocāma
tat yathā putra bhāryā ādiṣu vikaleṣu sakaleṣu vā aham eva vikalaḥ sakalaḥ vā iti bāhya dharmān ātmani adhyasyati
tathā deha dharmān
aham kṛśo
aham gauḥ
aham tiṣṭhāmi gacchāmi laṅghayāmi ca iti
tathā indriya dharmān mūkaḥ kāṇaḥ klībaḥ badhiraḥ andho
aham iti
tathā antaḥkaraṇa dharmān kāma saṃkalpa vicikitsā adhyavasāya ādīn
evam aham pratyayinam aśeṣa isva pracāra sākṣiṇi pratyagātmani adhyasya tam ca pratyagātmānam sarva sākṣiṇam tad viparyayeṇa antaḥkaraṇa ādiṣu adhyasyati
evam ayam anādiḥ anantaḥ naisargikaḥ
adhyāsaḥ mithyā pratyaya rūpaḥ kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva pravartakaḥ sarva loka pratyakṣaḥ
asya anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāya ātma eka tva vidyā pratipattaye sarve vedāntāḥ ārabhyate sic
yathā ca ayam arthaḥ sarveṣām vedāntānām tathā vayam asyām śārīraka mīmāṃsāyām pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ
vedānta mīmāṃsā śāstrasya vyācikhyāsitasya idam ādimam sūtram
prathamaḥ dhyāyaḥ
prathamaḥ pādaḥ
atha atas brahma jijñāsā
jijñāsā adhikaraṇam
atra atha śabdaḥ ānantarya arthaḥ parigṛhyate
na adhikāra arthaḥ brahma jijñāsāyāḥ an adhikārya tvāt
maṅgalasya ca vākya arthe samanvaya abhāvāt
artha antara prayuktaḥ eva hi athaśabdaḥ śrutyāḥ maṅgala prayojanaḥ bhavati
pūrva prakṛta apekṣāyāḥ ca phalataḥ ānantarya avyatirekāt
sati ca ānantarya artha tve yathā dharma jijñāsā pūrva vṛttam veda adhyayanam niyamena apekṣate evam brahma jijñāsā api yat pūrva vṛttam niyamena apekṣate tat vaktavyam
svādhyāya adhyayana ānantaryam tu samānam
nanu iha karma avabodha ānantaryam viśeṣaḥ
na
dharma jijñāsāyāḥ prāk api adhīta vedāntasya brahma jijñāsā upapatteḥ
yathā ca hṛdaya ādi avadānānām ānantarya niyamaḥ kramasya vivakṣita tvāt na tathā iha kramaḥ vivakṣitaḥ
śeṣa śeṣi tve adhikṛta adhikāre vā pramāṇa abhāvāt dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ
phala jijñāsya bhedāt ca
abhyudaya phalam dharma jñānam tat ca anuṣṭhāna apekṣam
niḥśreyasa phalam tu brahma jñānam na ca anuṣṭhāna antara apekṣam
bhavyaḥ ca dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ na jñāna kāle sti puruṣa vyāpāra tantra tvāt
iha tu bhūtam brahma jijñāsyam nitya vṛtta tvāt na puruṣa vyāpāra tantram
codanā pravṛtti bhedāt ca
yā hi codanā dharmasya lakṣaṇam sā sva viṣaye niyuñjānā eva puruṣam avabodhayati
brahma codanā tu puruṣam avabodhayati eva kevalam
avabodhasya codanā janya tvāt na puruṣaḥ vabodhe niyujyate yathā akṣa artha saṃnikarṣeṇa artha avabodhe tadvat
tasmāt kim api vaktavyam yat anantaram brahma jijñāsā upadiśyate iti
ucyate nitya anitya vastu vivekaḥ iha amutra artha bhoga virāgaḥ śama dama ādi sādhana saṃpad mumukṣu tvam ca
teṣu hi satsu prāk api dharma jijñāsāyāḥ ūrdhvam ca śakyate brahma jijñāsitum jñātum ca
na viparyaye
tasmāt athaśabdena yathā ukta sādhana saṃpatti ānantaryam upadiśyate
atas śabdaḥ hetvarthaḥ
yasmāt vedaḥ eva agnihotra ādīnām śreyaḥ sādhanānām anitya phalatām darśayati tat yathā iha karma citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate evam eva amutra puṇya citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate iti ādiḥ
tathā brahma jñānāt api param puruṣa artham darśayati brahma vid āpnoti param ityādiḥ
tasmāt yathā ukta sādhana saṃpatti anantaram brahma jijñāsā kartavyā
brahmaṇaḥ jijñāsā brahma jijñāsā
brahma ca vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇam janma ādyasya yatas iti
atas eva na brahma śabdasya jāti ādi artha antaram āśaṅkitavyam
brahmaṇaḥ iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī na śeṣe
jijñāsya apekṣa tvāt jijñāsāyāḥ jijñāsya antara anirdeśāt ca
nanu śeṣa ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe pi brahmaṇaḥ jijñāsā karma tvam na virudhyate saṃbandha sāmānyasya viśeṣa niṣṭha tvāt
evam api pratyakṣam brahmaṇaḥ karma tvam utsṛjya sāmānya dvāreṇa parokṣam karma tvam kalpayataḥ vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ syāt
na vyarthaḥ brahma āśrita aśeṣa vicāra pratijñāna artha tvāt iti ced na
pradhāna parigrahe tad apekṣitānām api artha ākṣipta tvāt
brahma hi jñānena āptum iṣṭatama tvāt pradhānam
tasmin pradhāne jijñāsā karmaṇi parigṛhīte yaiḥ jijñāsitaiḥ vinā brahma jijñāsitam na bhavati tāni artha ākṣiptāni eva iti na pṛthak sūtrayitavyāni
yathā rājā asau gacchati iti ukte sa parivārasya rājñaḥ gamanam uktam bhavati tadvat
śruti anugamāt ca
yatas vai imāni bhūtāni jāyante ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ tat vijijñāsasva tat brahma iti pratyakṣam eva brahmaṇaḥ jijñāsā karma tvam darśayanti
tat ca karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe sūtreṇa anugatam bhavati
tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī
jñātum icchā jijñāsā
avagati paryantam jñānam san vācyāyāḥ icchāyāḥ karma phala viṣaya tvāt icchāyāḥ
jñānena hi pramāṇena avagantum iṣṭam brahma
brahma avagatiḥ hi puruṣa arthaḥ niḥśeṣa saṃsāra bīja avidyā ādi anartha nibarhaṇāt
tasmāt brahma jijñāsitavyam
tat punar brahma prasiddham a prasiddham vā syāt
yadi prasiddham na jijñāsitavyam
atha aprasiddham na eva śakyam jijñāsitum iti
ucyate asti tāvat brahma nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam sarvajñam sarva śakti samanvitam
brahma śabdasya hi vyutpādyamānasya nitya śuddha tva ādayaḥ rthāḥ pratīyante bṛṃhateḥ dhātoḥ artha anugamāt
sarvasya ātma tvāt ca brahma astitva prasiddhiḥ
sarvaḥ hi ātmā astitvam pratyeti na na aham asmi iti
yadi hi na ātma astitva prasiddhiḥ syāt sarvaḥ lokaḥ na aham asmi iti pratīyāt
ātmā ca brahma
yadi tarhi loke brahma ātma tvena prasiddham asti tatas jñātam eva iti ajijñāsya tvam punar āpannam
na
tad viśeṣam prati vipratipatteḥ
deha mātram caitanya viśiṣṭam ātmā iti prākṛtāḥ janāḥ laukāyatikāḥ ca pratipannāḥ
indriyāṇi eva cetanāni ātmā iti apare
manaḥ iti anye
vijñānamātram kṣaṇikam iti eke
śūnyam iti apare
asti deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ saṃsārī kartā bhoktā iti apare
bhoktā eva kevalam na kartā iti eke
asti tad vyatiriktaḥ īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva śaktiḥ iti kecid
ātmā sa bhoktuḥ iti apare
evam bahavaḥ vipratipannāḥ yukti vākya tad ābhāsa samāśrayāḥ santaḥ
tatra a vicārya yat kiṃcid pratipadyamānaḥ niḥśreyasāt pratihanyeta anartham ca iyāt
tasmāt brahma jijñāsā upanyāsa mukhena vedānta vākya mīmāṃsā tad avirodhi tarka upakaraṇā niḥśreyasa prayojanā prastūyate
brahma jijñāsitavyam iti uktam
kiṃlakṣaṇam punar tat brahma iti atas āha bhagavān sūtrakāraḥ
janma ādi asya yatas
janma ādi adhikaraṇam
janma utpattiḥ ādiḥ asya iti tad guṇa saṃvijñānaḥ bahuvrīhiḥ
janma sthiti bhaṅgam samāsa arthaḥ
janmanaḥ ca ādi tvam śruti nirdeśa apekṣam vastu vṛtta apekṣam ca
śruti nirdeśaḥ tāvat yatas vai imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti asmin vākye janma sthiti pralayānām krama darśanāt
vastu vṛttam api janmanā labdha sattākasya dharmiṇaḥ sthiti pralaya saṃbhavāt
asya iti pratyakṣa ādi saṃnidhāpitasya dharmiṇaḥ idam nirdeśaḥ
ṣaṣṭhī janma ādi dharma saṃbandha arthā
yatas iti kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ
asya jagataḥ nāma rūpābhyām vyākṛtasya aneka kartṛ bhoktṛ saṃyuktasya pratiniyata deśa kāla nimitta kriyā phala āśrayasya manasā api acintya racanā rūpasya janma sthiti bhaṅgam yatas sarvajñāt sarva śakteḥ kāraṇāt bhavati tat brahma iti vākyaśeṣaḥ
anyeṣām api bhāva vikārāṇām triṣu eva antarbhāvaḥ iti janma sthiti nāśānām iha grahaṇam
yāska paripaṭhitānām tu jāyate sti ityādīnām grahaṇe teṣām jagataḥ sthiti kāle saṃbhāvyamāna tvāt mūlakāraṇāt utpatti sthiti nāś jagataḥ na gṛhītāḥ syuḥ iti āśaṅkyeta
tat mā śaṅki
iti yā utpattiḥ brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇāt tatra eva sthitiḥ pralayaḥ ca te gṛhyante
na ca yathā ukta viśeṣaṇasya jagataḥ yathā ukta viśeṣaṇam īśvaram muktvā anyatas pradhānāt acetanāt aṇubhyaḥ vā abhāvāt vā saṃsāriṇaḥ vā utpatti ādi saṃbhāvayitum śakyam
na ca svabhāvataḥ viśiṣṭa deśa kāla nimittānām iha upādānāt
etat eva anumānam saṃsāri vyatirikta īśvara astitva ādi sādhanam manyante īśvara kāraṇa vādinaḥ
nanu iha api tat eva upanyastam janma ādi sūtre
na
vedānta vākya kusuma grathana artha tvāt sūtrāṇām
vedānta vākyāni hi sūtraiḥ udāhṛtya vicāryante
vākya artha vicāraṇa adhyavasāna nirvṛttā hi brahma avagatiḥ na anumāna ādi pramāṇa antara nirvṛttā
satsu tu vedānta vākyeṣu jagataḥ janma ādi kāraṇa vādiṣu ārḍhyāya anumānam api vedānta vākya avirodhi pramāṇam bhavat na nivāryate śrutyā eva ca sahāya tvena tarkasya api abhyupeta tvāt
tathā hi śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ iti śrutiḥ paṇḍitaḥ medhāvī gandhārān eva upasaṃpadyeta evam eva iha ācāryavān puruṣaḥ veda iti ca puruṣa buddhi sāhāyyam ātmanaḥ darśayati
na dharma jijñasāyām iva śruti ādayaḥ eva pramāṇam brahma jijñāsāyām
kiṃtu śruti ādayaḥ nubhava ādayaḥ ca yathāsaṃbhavam iha pramāṇam anubhava avasāna tvāt bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt ca brahma jñānasya
kartavye hi viṣaye na anubhava apekṣā asti iti śruti ādīnām eva prāmāṇyam syāt puruṣa adhīna ātmalābha tvāt ca kartavyasya
kartum a kartum anyathā vā kartum śakyam laukikam vaidikam ca karma
yathā aśvena gacchati padbhyām anyathā vā na vā gacchati iti
tathā atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti na atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti udite juhoti an udite juhoti iti
vidhi pratiṣedhāḥ ca atra arthavantaḥ syuḥ vikalpa utsarga apavādāḥ ca
na tu vastu evam na evam asti na asti iti vā vikalpyate
vikalpanāḥ tu puruṣa buddhi apekṣāḥ
na vastu yāthātmya jñānam puruṣa buddhi apekṣam
kim tarhi vastu tantram eva tat
na hi sthāṇau ekasmin sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ nyaḥ vā iti tattva jñānam bhavati
tatra puruṣaḥ nyaḥ vā iti mithyājñānam
sthāṇuḥ eva iti tattva jñānam vastu tantra tvāt
evam bhūta vastu viṣayāṇām prāmāṇyam vastu tantram
tatra evam sati brahma jñānam api vastu tantram eva bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt
nanu bhūta vastu viṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvam eva iti vedānta vākya vicāraṇā anarthikā eva prāptā
na
indriya aviṣaya tvena saṃbandha agrahaṇāt
svabhāvataḥ viṣaya viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi na brahma viṣayāṇi
sati hi indriya viṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ idam brahmaṇā saṃbaddham kāryam iti gṛhyeta
kārya mātram eva tu gṛhyamāṇam kim brahmaṇā saṃbaddham
kim anyena kenacid vā saṃbaddham
iti na śakyam niścetum
tasmāt janma ādi sūtram na anumāna upanyāsa artham kim tarhi vedānta vākya pradarśana artham
kim punar tat vedānta vākyam yat sūtreṇa iha
bhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ
varuṇam pitaram upasasāra
adhīhi bhagavaḥ brahma iti iti upakramya āha yatas vai imāni bhūtāni jāyante
yena jātāni jīvanti
yat prayanti abhisaṃviśanti
tat vijijñāsasva
tat brahma iti
tasya ca nirṇaya vākyam ānandāt hi eva khalu imāni bhūtāni jāyante
ānandena jātāni jīvanti
ānandam prayanti abhisaṃviśanti iti
anyāni api evaṃjātīyakāni vākyāni nitya śuddha buddham ukta svabhāva sarvajña sva rūpa kāraṇa viṣayāṇi udāhartavyāni
jagat kāraṇatva pradarśanena sarvajñam brahma iti upakṣiptam tat eva draḍhayan āha
śāstra yoni tvāt
śāstra yoni tva adhikaraṇam
mahataḥ ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya aneka vidyā sthāna upabṛṃhitasya pradīpa vat sarva artha avadyotinaḥ sarvajña kalpasya yoniḥ kāraṇam brahma
na hi īdṛśasya śāstrasya ṛgveda ādi lakṣaṇasya sarvajña guṇa anvitasya sarvajñāt anyatas saṃbhavaḥ sti
yat yat vistara artham śāstram yasmāt puruṣa viśeṣāt saṃbhavati yathā vyākaraṇa ādi pāṇini ādeḥ jñeya eka deśa artham api sa tatas pi adhikatara vijñānaḥ iti prasiddham loke
kimu vaktavyam aneka śākhā bheda bhinnasya deva tiryak manuṣya varṇa āśrama ādi pravibhāga hetoḥ ṛgveda ādi ākhyasya sarva jñāna ākarasya aprayatnena eva līlā nyāyena puruṣa niḥśvāsa vat yasmāt mahataḥ bhūtāt yoneḥ saṃbhavaḥ asya mahataḥ bhūtasya niḥśvasitam etat yat ṛgvedaḥ ityādi śruteḥ tasya mahataḥ bhūtasya niratiśayam sarvajña tvam sarva śaktimat tvam ca iti
athavā yathā uktam ṛgveda ādi śāstram yoniḥ kāraṇam pramāṇam asya brahmaṇaḥ yathāvat svarūpa adhigame
śāstrāt eva pramāṇāt jagataḥ janma ādikāraṇam brahma adhigamyate iti abhiprāyaḥ
śāstram udāhṛtam pūrva sūtre yatas vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante ityādi
kimartham tarhi idam sūtram yāvatā pūrva sūtreṇa eva evaṃjātīyakam śāstram udāharatā śāstra yoni tvam brahmaṇaḥ darśitam
ucyate tatra sūtra akṣareṇa spaṣṭam śāstrasya anupādānāt janma ādi sūtreṇa kevalam anumānam upanyastam iti āśaṅkyeta
tām āśaṅkām nivartayitum idam sūtram pravavṛte śāstra yoni tvāt iti
katham punar brahmaṇaḥ śāstra pramāṇaka tvam ucyate yāvatā āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt ānarthakyam a tad arthānām iti kriyā para tvam śāstrasya pradarśitam
atas vedāntānām ānarthakyam akriyā artha tvāt kartṛ devatā ādi prakāśana artha tvena vā kriyā vidhi śeṣa tvam upāsana ādi kriyā antara vidhāna artha tvam vā
na hi pariniṣṭhita vastu svarūpa pratipādanam saṃbhavati
pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya tvāt pariniṣṭhita vastunaḥ tad pratipādane ca heya upādeya rahite puruṣa artha abhāvāt
atas eva saḥ
arodīt iti evamādīnām ānarthakyam mā bhūt iti vidhinā tu ekavākya tvāt stuti arthena vidhīnām syuḥ iti stāvaka tvena arthavat tvam uktam
mantrāṇām ca iṣe tvā ityādīnām kriyā tad sādhana abhidhāyaka tvena karma samavāyi tvam uktam
atas na kvacid api veda vākyānām vidhi saṃsparśam antareṇa arthavat tā dṛṣṭā upapannā vā
na ca pariniṣṭhite vastu svarūpe vidhiḥ saṃbhavati kriyā viṣaya tvāt vidheḥ tasmāt karma apekṣita kartṛ devatā ādi sva rūpa prakāśanena kriyā vidhi śeṣa tvam vedāntānām
atha prakaraṇa antara bhayāt nā etat abhyupagamyate tathā api sva vākya gata upāsana ādi karma paratvam
tasmāt na brahmaṇaḥ śāstra yoni tvam iti prāpte ucyate
tat tu samanvayāt
samanvaya adhikaraṇam
tu śabdaḥ pūrvapakṣa vyāvṛtti arthaḥ
tat brahma sarvajñam sarva śakti jagat utpatti sthiti laya kāraṇam vedānta śāstrāt avagamyate
katham
samanvayāt
sarveṣu hi vedānteṣu vākyāni tātparyeṇa etasya arthasya pratipādaka tvena samanugatāni
sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt tat etat brahma apūrvam anaparam anantaram abāhyam ayam ātmā brahma sarva anubhūḥ brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt ityādīni
na ca tad gatānām padānām brahma svarūpa viṣaye niścite samanvaye vagamyamāne artha antara kalpanā yuktā śruta hāni aśruta kalpanā prasaṅgāt
na ca teṣām kartṛ devatā ādi svarūpa pratipādana para tā avasīyate tat kena kam paśyet ityādi kriyā kāraka phala nirākaraṇa śruteḥ
na ca pariniṣṭhita vastu svarūpa tve pi pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya tvam brahmaṇaḥ tat tvam asi iti brahma ātma bhāvasya śāstram antareṇa anavagamyamāna tvāt
yat tu heya upādeya rahita tvāt upadeśa ānarthakyam iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
heya upādeya śūnya brahma ātmatā avagamāt eva sarva kleśa prahāṇāt puruṣa artha siddheḥ
devatā ādi pratipādana parasya tu sva vākya gata upāsana artha tve pi na kaścid virodhaḥ
na tu tathā brahmaṇaḥ upāsanā vidhi śeṣa tvam saṃbhavati ekatve heya upādeya śūnyatayā kriyā kāraka ādi dvaita vijñāna upamarda upapatteḥ
na hi brahma eka tva vijñānena unmathitasya dvaita vijñānasya punar saṃbhavaḥ sti yena upāsanā vidhi śeṣa tvam brahmaṇaḥ pratipādyeta
yadi api anyatra veda vākyānām vidhi saṃsparśam antareṇa pramāṇa tvam na dṛṣṭam tathā api ātma vijñānasya phala paryanta tvāt na tad viṣayasya śāstrasya prāmāṇyam śakyam pratyākhyātum
na ca anumāna gamyam śāstra prāmāṇyam yena anyatra dṛṣṭam nidarśanam apekṣyeta
tasmāt siddham brahmaṇaḥ śāstra pramāṇaka tvam
atra apare pratyavatiṣṭhante yadi api śāstra pramāṇakam brahma tathā api pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā eva śāstreṇa brahma samarpyate
yathā yūpa āhavanīya ādīni alaukikāni api vidhi śeṣa tayā śāstreṇa samarpyante tadvat
kutas etat
pravṛtti nivṛtti prayojana para tvāt śāstrasya
tathā hi śāstra tātparya vidām anukramaṇam dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam nāma iti
codanā iti kriyāyāḥ pravartakam SNNe vacanam SNNe tasya jñānam SNNe upadeśaḥ SNM

iti ca
atas puruṣam kvacid viṣaya viśeṣe pravartayat kutaścid viṣaya viśeṣāt nivartayat ca arthavat śāstram
tad śeṣa tayā ca anyat upayuktam
tad sāmānyāt vedāntānām api tathā eva arthavat tvam syāt
sati ca vidhi paratve yathā svarga ādi kāmasya agnihotra ādi sādhanam vidhīyate evam amṛta tva kāmasya brahma jñānam vidhīyate iti yuktam
nanu iha jijñāsya vailakṣaṇyam uktam karmakāṇḍe bhavyaḥ dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ iha tu bhūtam nitya nirvṛttam brahma jijñāsyam iti
tatra dharma jñāna phalāt anuṣṭhāna sāpekṣāt vilakṣaṇam brahma jñāna phalam bhavitum arhati
na arhati evam bhavitum kārya vidhi prayuktasya eva brahmaṇaḥ pratipādyamāna tvāt
ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā
saḥ nveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ ātmā iti eva upāsīta ātmānam eva lokam upāsīta brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati ityādiṣu vidhāneṣu satsu kaḥ sau ātmā
kim tat brahma
iti ākāṅkṣāyām tad svarūpa samarpaṇena sarve vedāntāḥ upayuktāḥ nityaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva gataḥ nitya tṛptaḥ nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvaḥ vijñānam ānandam brahma iti evamādayaḥ
tad upāsanāt ca śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ mokṣaḥ phalam bhaviṣyati
kartavya vidhi ananupraveśe tu vastu mātra kathane hāna upādāna asaṃbhavāt saptadvīpā vasumatī rājā asau gacchati ityādi vākya vat vedānta vākyānām ānarthakyam eva syāt
nanu vastu mātra kathane rajjuḥ iyam na ayam sarpaḥ ityādau bhrānti janita bhīti nivartanena arthavat tvam dṛṣṭam
tathā iha api asaṃsāri ātma vastu kathanena saṃsāri tva bhrānti nivartanena arthavat tvam syāt
syāt etat evam yadi rajju sva rūpa śravaṇa mātreṇa iva sarpa bhrāntiḥ saṃsāri tva bhrāntiḥ brahma sva rūpa śravaṇa mātreṇa nivarteta
na tu nivartate
śruta brahmaṇaḥ u pi yathāpūrvam sukha duḥkha ādi saṃsāri dharma darśanāt śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti ca śravaṇa uttara kālayoḥ manana nididhyāsanayoḥ vidhi darśanāt
tasmāt pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā eva śāstra pramāṇakam brahma abhyupagantavyam iti
atra abhidhīyate na
karma brahma vidyā phalayoḥ vailakṣaṇyāt
śārīram vācikam mānasam ca karma śruti smṛti siddham dharma ākhyam yad viṣayā jijñāsā atha atas dharma jijñāsā iti sūtritā
adharmaḥ u pi hiṃsā ādiḥ pratiṣedha codanā lakṣaṇa tvāt jijñāsyaḥ parihārāya
tayoḥ codanā lakṣaṇayoḥ artha anarthayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ phale pratyakṣe sukha duḥkhe śarīra vāc manobhiḥ eva upabhujyamāne viṣaya indriya saṃyoga janye brahma ādiṣu sthāvara anteṣu prasiddhe
manuṣya tvāt ārabhya brahma anteṣu dehavatsu sukha tāratamyam anuśrūyate
tatas ca tad hetoḥ dharmasya api tāratamyam gamyate
dharma tāratamyāt adhikāri tāratamyam
prasiddham ca arthi tva sāmarthya vidvas tā ādi kṛtam adhikāri tāratamyam
tathā ca yāga ādi anuṣṭhāyinām eva vidyā samādhi viśeṣāt uttareṇa pathā gamanam kevalaiḥ iṣṭāpūrta datta sādhanaiḥ dhūma ādi krameṇa dakṣiṇena pathā gamanam tatra api sukha tāratamyam tad sādhana tāramyam ca śāstrāt yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā iti asmāt gamyate
tathā manuṣya ādiṣu sthāvara anteṣu sukha lavaḥ codanā lakṣaṇa dharma sādhyaḥ eva iti gamyate tāratamyena vartamānaḥ
tathā ūrdhva gateṣu adhas gateṣu ca dehavatsu duḥkha tāratamya darśanāt tad hetoḥ adharmasya pratiṣedha codanā lakṣaṇasya tad anuṣṭhāyinām ca tāratamyam gamyate
evam avidyā ādi doṣavatām dharma adharma tāratamya nimittam śarīra upādāna pūrvakam sukha duḥkha tāratamyam anityam saṃsāra rūpam śruti smṛti nyāya prasiddham
tathā ca śrutiḥ na ha vai sa śarīrasya sataḥ priya apriyayoḥ apahatiḥ asti iti yathā varṇitam saṃsāra rūpam anuvadati
aśarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti priya apriya sparśana pratiṣedhāt codanā lakṣaṇa dharma kārya tvam mokṣa ākhyasya aśarīra tvasya pratiṣidhyate iti gamyate
dharma kārya tve hi priya apriya sparśana pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyeta
aśarīra tvam eva dharma kāryam iti ced na
tasya svābhāvika tvāt aśarīram śarīreṣu anavastheṣu avasthitam
mahāntam vibhum ātmānam matvā dhīraḥ na śocati a prāṇaḥ hi amanāḥ śubhraḥ a saṅgaḥ hi ayam puruṣaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
atas eva anuṣṭheya karma phala vilakṣaṇam mokṣa ākhyam aśarīra tvam nityam iti siddham
tatra kiṃcid pariṇāmi nityam syāt yasmin vikriyamāṇe
api tat eva idam iti buddhiḥ na vihanyate
yathā pṛthivī ādi jagat nitya tva vādinām yathā vā sāṃkhyānām guṇāḥ
idam tu pāramārthikam kūṭastha nityam vyoma vat sarva vyāpi sarva vikriyā rahitam nitya tṛptam niravayavam svayam jyotiḥ svabhāvam yatra dharma adharmau saha kāryeṇa kāla trayam ca na upāvartete
tat etat aśarīra tvam mokṣa ākhyam anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt anyatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt
anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
atas tat brahma yasya iyam jijñāsā prastutā
tat yadi kartavya śeṣa tvena upadiśyeta tena ca kartavyena sādhyaḥ ced mokṣaḥ
abhyupagamyeta anityaḥ eva syāt
tatra evam sati yathā ukta karma phaleṣu eva tāratamya avasthiteṣu anityeṣu kaścid atiśayaḥ mokṣaḥ iti prasajyeta
nityaḥ ca mokṣaḥ sarvaiḥ mokṣa vādibhiḥ abhyupagamyate
atas na kartavya śeṣa tvena brahma upadeśaḥ yuktaḥ
api ca brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān na bibheti kutaścana abhayam vai janaka tat ātmānam eva avet aham brahma asmi iti tasmāt tat sarvam abhavat tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam anupaśyataḥ iti evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ brahma vidyā anantaram eva mokṣam darśayantyaḥ madhye kārya antaram vārayanti
tathā tat ha etat paśyan ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede ham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti brahma darśana sarva ātma bhāvayoḥ madhye kartavya antara vāraṇāya udāhāryam yathā tiṣṭhan gāyati iti tiṣṭhati gāyatyoḥ madhye tad kartṛkam kārya antaram na asti iti gamyate
tvam hi naḥ pitā smākam avidyāyāḥ param pāram tārayasi śrutam hi eva me bhagavat dṛśebhyaḥ tarati śokam ātma vid iti
saḥ ham bhagavaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu tasmai mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāram darśayati bhagavān sanātkumāraḥ iti ca evamādyāḥ śrutayaḥ mokṣa pratibandha nivṛtti mātram eva ātma jñānasya phalam darśayanti
tathā ca ācārya praṇītam nyāya upabṛṃhitam sūtram duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyājñānānām uttara uttara apāye tad anantara apāyāt apavargaḥ SNM
iti
mithyājñāna apāyaḥ ca brahma ātma eka tva vijñānāt bhavati
na ca idam brahma ātma eka tva vijñānam saṃpad rūpam yathā anantam vai manaḥ nantāḥ viśvedevāḥ anantam eva sa tena lokam jayati iti
na ca adhyāsa rūpam yathā manaḥ brahma iti upāsīta ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ iti ca manaḥ āditya ādiṣu brahma dṛṣṭi adhyāsaḥ
na api viśiṣṭa kriyā yoga nimittam vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ prāṇaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ itivat
na api ājya avekṣaṇa ādi karma vat karma aṅga saṃskāra rūpam
saṃpad ādi rūpe hi brahma ātma eka tva vijñāne bhyupagamyamāne tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi ayam ātmā brahma iti evamādīnām vākyānām brahma ātma eka tva vastu pratipādana paraḥ pada samanvayaḥ pīḍyeta
bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ iti ca evamādīni avidyā nivṛtti phala śravaṇāni uparudhyeran
brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti ca evamādīni tad bhāva āpatti vacanāni saṃpad ādi rūpa tve na sāmañjasyena upapadyeran
tasmāt na saṃpad ādi rūpam brahma ātma ekatva vijñānam
atas na puruṣa vyāpāra tantrā brahma vidyā
kim tarhi pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa viṣaya vastu jñāna vat vastu tantrā eva
evaṃbhūtasya brahmaṇaḥ tad jñānasya ca na kayācid yuktyā śakyaḥ kārya anupraveśaḥ kalpayitum
na ca vidi kriyā karma tvena kārya anupraveśaḥ brahmaṇaḥ anyat eva tad viditāt atha u aviditāt adhi iti vidi kriyā karma tva pratiṣedhāt yena idam sarvam vijānāti tam kena vijānīyāt iti ca
tathā upāsti kriyā karma tva pratiṣedhaḥ u pi bhavati yat vācā an abhyuditam yena vāc abhyudyate iti aviṣaya tvam brahmaṇaḥ upanyasya tat eva brahma tvam viddhi na idam yat idam upāsate iti
aviṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ śāstra yoni tva anupapattiḥ iti ced na
avidyā kalpita bheda nivṛtti para tvāt śāstrasya
na hi śāstram idaṃtayā viṣaya bhūtam brahma pratipipādayiṣati
kim tarhi pratyagātma tvena aviṣaya tayā pratipādayat avidyā kalpitam vedya veditṛ vedana ādi bhedam apanayati
tathā ca śāstram yasya amatam tasya matam matam yasya na veda saḥ
a vijñātam vijānatām vijñātam a vijānatām na dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram paśyeḥ na śruteḥ śrotāram śrṛṇuyāḥ na mateḥ mantāram manvīthāḥ na vijñāteḥ vijñātāram vijānīyāḥ iti ca evamādi
atas vidyā kalpita saṃsāri tva nivartanena nitya mukta ātma svarūpa samarpaṇāt na mokṣasya anitya tva doṣaḥ
yasya tu utpādyaḥ mokṣaḥ tasya mānasam vācikam kāyikam vā kāryam apekṣate iti yuktam
tathā vikārya tve ca
tayoḥ pakṣayoḥ mokṣasya dhruvam anitya tvam
na hi dadhi ādi vikāryam utpādyam vā ghaṭa ādi nityam dṛṣṭam loke
na ca āpya tvena api kārya apekṣā sva ātma svarūpa tve sati an āpya tvāt
sva rūpa vyatirikta tve pi brahmaṇaḥ na āpya tvam sarvagata tvena nitya āpta svarūpa tvāt sarveṇa brahmaṇaḥ ākāśasya iva
na api saṃskāryaḥ mokṣaḥ yena vyāpāram apekṣeta
saṃskāraḥ hi nāma saṃskāryasya guṇa ādhānena vā syāt doṣa apanayanena vā
na tāvat guṇa ādhānena saṃbhavati anādheya atiśaya brahma sva rūpa tvāt mokṣasya
nā api doṣa apanayanena nitya śuddha brahma sva rūpa tvāt mokṣasya
sva ātma dharmaḥ eva san tirobhūtaḥ mokṣaḥ kriyayā ātmani saṃskriyamāṇe bhivyajyate yathā ādarśe nigharṣaṇa kriyayā saṃskriyamāṇe bhāsvara tvam dharmaḥ iti ced na
kriyā āśraya tva anupapatteḥ ātmanaḥ
yad āśrayā kriyā tam a vikurvatī na eva ātmānam labhate
yadi ātmā sva āśraya kriyayā vikriyeta anitya tvam ātmanaḥ prasajyeta
avikāryaḥ yam ucyate iti ca evamādīni vākyāni bādhyeran
tat ca aniṣṭam
tasmāt na sva āśrayā kriyā ātmanaḥ saṃbhavati
anya āśrayāyāḥ tu kriyāyāḥ aviṣaya tvāt na tayā ātmā saṃskriyate
nanu deha āśrayayā snāna ācamana yajñopavīta dhāraṇa ādikayā kriyayā dehī saṃskriyamāṇaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na
deha ādi saṃhatasya eva avidyā gṛhītasya ātmanaḥ saṃskriyamāṇa tvāt
pratyakṣam hi snāna ācamana ādeḥ deha samavāyi tvam
tayā deha āśrayayā tad saṃhataḥ eva kaścid avidyayā ātma tvena parigṛhītaḥ saṃskriyate iti yuktam
yathā deha āśraya cikitsā nimittena dhātu sāmyena tad saṃhatasya tad abhimāninaḥ ārogya phalam aham arogaḥ iti yatra buddhiḥ utpadyate evam snāna ācamana yajñopavīta dhāraṇa ādikayā aham śuddhaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ iti yatra buddhiḥ utpadyate sa saṃskriyate
sa ca dehena saṃhataḥ eva
tena eva ahaṃkartrā ahaṃpratyaya viṣayeṇa pratyayinā sarvāḥ kriyāḥ nirvartyante
tad phalam ca saḥ eva aśnāti tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādu atti an aśnan anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti mantra varṇāt ātma indriya manaḥ yuktam bhoktā iti āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ iti ca
tathā ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā
karma adhyakṣaḥ sarva bhūta adhivāsaḥ sākṣī cetā kevalaḥ nirguṇaḥ ca iti sa paryāgāt śukram akāyam avraṇam a snāviram śuddham a pāpa viddham iti ca etau mantrau anādheya atiśaya tām nitya śuddha tām ca brahmaṇaḥ darśayataḥ
brahma bhāvaḥ ca mokṣaḥ
tasmāt na saṃskāryaḥ u pi mokṣaḥ
atas mokṣam prati kriyā anupraveśa dvāram na śakyam kenacid darśayitum
tasmāt jñānam ekam muktvā kriyāyāḥ gandha mātrasya api anupraveśaḥ iha na upapadyate
nanu jñānam nāma mānasī kriyā na
vailakṣaṇyāt
kriyā hi nāma sā yatra vastu svarūpa nirapekṣā eva codyate puruṣa citta vyāpāra adhīnā ca yathā yasyai devatāyai haviḥ gṛhītam syāt tām manasā dhyāyet vaṣaṭ kariṣyan iti saṃdhyām manasā dhyāyet iti ca evamādiṣu
dhyānam cintanam yadi api mānasam tathā api puruṣeṇa kartum a kartum anyathā vā kartum śakyam puruṣa tantra tvāt
jñānam tu pramāṇa janyam
pramāṇam ca yathā bhūta vastu viṣayam
atas jñānam kartum a kartum anyathā vā kartum na śakyam
kevalam vastu tantram eva tat
na codanā tantram na api puruṣa tantram
tasmāt mānasa tve pi jñānasya mahat vailakṣaṇyam
yathā ca puruṣaḥ vāva gautama agniḥ yoṣā vāva gautama agniḥ iti atra yoṣit puruṣayoḥ agni buddhiḥ mānasī bhavati
kevala codanā janya tvāt tu kriyā eva sā puruṣa tantrā ca
yā tu prasiddhe gnau agni buddhiḥ na sā codanā tantrā
na api puruṣa tantrā
kim tarhi pratyakṣa viṣaya vastu tantrā eva iti jñānam eva etat
na kriyā evam sarva pramāṇa viṣaya vastuṣu veditavyam
tatra evam sati yathā bhūta brahma ātma viṣayam api jñānam na codanā tantram
tad viṣaye liṅ ādayaḥ śrūyamāṇāḥ api aniyojya viṣaya tvāt kuṇṭhībhavanti upala ādiṣu prayukta kṣura taikṣṇya ādi vat aheya anupādeya vastu viṣaya tvāt
kimarthāni tarhi ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ ityādīni vidhi chāyāni vacanāni
svābhāvika pravṛtti viṣaya vimukhīkaraṇa arthāni iti brūmaḥ
yaḥ hi bahirmukhaḥ pravartate puruṣaḥ iṣṭam me bhūyāt aniṣṭam mā bhūt iti na ca tatra ātyantikam puruṣa artham labhate tam ātyantika puruṣa artha vāñchinam svābhāvikāt kārya karaṇa saṃghāta pravṛtti gocarāt vimukhīkṛtya pratyagātma srotaḥ tayā pravartayanti ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ ityādīni
tasya ātma anveṣaṇāya pravṛttasya aheyam anupādeyam ca ātma tattvam upadiśyate idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet
kena kam vijānīyāt vijñātāram are kena vijānīyāt ayam ātmā brahma ityādibhiḥ
yat api akartavya pradhānam ātma jñānam hānāya upādānāya vā na bhavati iti tat tathā eva iti abhyupagamyate
alaṃkāraḥ hi ayam asmākam yat brahma ātmau agatau satyām sarva kartavya tā hāniḥ kṛtakṛtya tā ca iti
tathā ca śrutiḥ ātmānam ced vijānīyāt ayam asmi iti pūruṣaḥ
kim icchan kasya kāmāya śarīram anusaṃjvaret iti etat buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaḥ ca bhārata iti ca smṛtiḥ
tasmāt na pratipatti vidhi śeṣa tayā brahmaṇaḥ samarpaṇam
yat api kecid āhuḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti vidhi tad śeṣa vyatirekeṇa kevala vastu vādī veda bhāgaḥ na asti iti tat na
aupaniṣadasya puruṣasya an anya śeṣa tvāt yaḥ sau upaniṣatsu eva adhigataḥ puruṣaḥ saṃsārī brahma svarūpaḥ utpādi ādi caturvidha dravya vilakṣaṇaḥ sva prakaraṇa sthaḥ na asau na asti iti na adhigamyate iti vā śakyam vaditum
saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmā iti ātma śabdāt ātmanaḥ ca pratyākhyātum aśakya tvāt yaḥ eva nirākartā tasya eva ātma tvāt
nanu ātmā ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tvāt upaniṣatsu eva vijñāyate iti anupapannam
na tad sākṣi tvena pratyukta tvāt
na hi ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya kartṛ vyatirekeṇa tad sākṣī sarva bhūta sthaḥ samaḥ ekaḥ kūṭastha nityaḥ puruṣaḥ vidhi kāṇḍe tarka samaye vā kenacid adhigataḥ sarvasya ātmā
atas sa na kenacid pratyākhyātum śakyaḥ vidhi śeṣa tvam vā netum ātma tvāt eva ca sarveṣām na heyaḥ nā api upādeyaḥ
sarvam hi vinaśyat vikāra jātam puruṣa antam vinaśyati
puruṣaḥ hi vināśa hetu abhāvāt avināśī
vikriyā hetu abhāvāt ca kūṭastha nityaḥ
atas eva nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvaḥ
tasmāt puruṣāt na param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ tam tu aupaniṣadam puruṣam pṛcchāmi iti ca aupaniṣada tva viśeṣaṇam puruṣasya upaniṣatsu prādhānyena prakāśyamāna tve upapadyate
atas bhūta vastu paraḥ veda bhāgaḥ nā asti iti vacanam sāhasa mātram
yat api śāstra tātparya vidām anukramaṇam dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam iti evamādi tat dharma jijñāsā viṣaya tvāt vidhi pratiṣedha śāstra abhiprāyam draṣṭavyam
api ca āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt ānarthakyam a tad arthānām iti etat ekāntena abhyupagacchatām bhūta upadeśānām ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ
pravṛtti nivṛtti vyatirekeṇa bhūtam ced vastu upadiśati bhavya artha tvena kūṭastha nityam bhūtam na upadiśati iti kaḥ hetuḥ
na hi bhūtam upadiśyamānam kriyā bhavati
akriyā tve pi bhūtasya kriyā sādhana tvāt kriyā arthaḥ eva bhūta upadeśaḥ iti ced nā eṣa doṣaḥ
kriyā artha tve pi kriyā nirvartana śaktimat vastu upadiṣṭam eva
kriyā artha tvam tu prayojanam tasya
na ca etāvatā vastu anupadiṣṭam bhavati
yadi nāma upadiṣṭam kim tava tena syāt iti ucyate anavagata ātma vastu upadeśaḥ ca tathā eva bhavitum arhati
tad avagatyā mithyājñānasya saṃsāra hetoḥ nivṛttiḥ prayojanam kriyate iti aviśiṣṭam arthavat tvam kriyā sādhana vastu upadeśena
api ca brāhmaṇaḥ na hantavyaḥ iti ca evamādyā nivṛttiḥ upadiśyate
na ca sā kriyā
na api kriyā sādhanam
akriyā arthānām upadeśaḥ narthakaḥ ced brāhmaṇaḥ na hantavyaḥ ityādi nivṛtti upadeśānām ānarthakyam prāptam
tat ca aniṣṭam
na ca svabhāva prāpta hanti artha anurāgeṇa nañaḥ śakyam aprāpta kriyā artha tvam kalpayitum hanana kriyā nivṛttyā audāsīnī avyatirekeṇa
nañaḥ ca eṣa svabhāvaḥ yat sva saṃbandhinaḥ bhāvam bodhayati iti
abhāva buddhiḥ ca audāsīnye kāraṇam
sā ca dagdha indhana agni vat svayam evā upaśāmyati
tasmāt prasakta kriyā nivṛtti audāsīnyam eva brāhmaṇaḥ na hantavyaḥ ityādiṣu pratiṣedha artham manyāmahe anyatra prajāpati vrata ādibhyaḥ
tasmāt puruṣa artha anupayogi upākhyāna ādi bhūta arthavāda viṣayam ānarthakya abhidhānam draṣṭavyam
yat api uktam kartavya vidhi anupraveśam antareṇa vastu mātram ucyamānam anarthakam syāt saptadvīpā vasumatī ityādi vat iti tat parihṛtam
rajjuḥ iyam na ayam sarpaḥ iti vastu mātra kathane pi prayojanasya dṛṣṭa tvāt
nanu śruta brahmaṇaḥ pi yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tva darśanāt na rajju sva rūpa kathana vat arthavat tvam iti uktam
atrā ucyate na avagata brahma ātma bhāvasya yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tvam śakyam darśayitum veda pramāṇa janita brahma ātma bhāva virodhāt
na hi śarīra ādi ātma abhimāninaḥ duḥkha bhaya ādimat tvam dṛṣṭam iti tasya eva veda pramāṇa janita brahma ātma avagame tad abhimāna nivṛttau tat eva mithyājñāna nimittam duḥkha bhaya ādimat tvam bhavati iti śakyam kalpayitum
na hi dhaninaḥ gṛhasthasya dhana abhimāninaḥ dhana apahāra nimittam duḥkham dṛṣṭam iti tasya eva pravrajitasya dhana abhimāna rahitasya tat eva dhana apahāra nimittam duḥkham bhavati
na ca kuṇḍalinaḥ kuṇḍali tva abhimāna nimittam sukham dṛṣṭam iti tasya eva kuṇḍala viyuktasya kuṇḍali tva abhimāna rahitasya tat eva kuṇḍali tva abhimāna nimittam sukham bhavati
tat uktam śrutyā aśarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti
śarīre patite śarīra tvam syāt na jīvataḥ iti ced na
sa śarīram tu asya mithyājñāna nimitta tvāt
na hi ātmanaḥ śarīra ātma abhimāna lakṣaṇam mithyājñānam muktvā anyatas sa śarīra tvam śakyam kalpayitum
nityam aśarīra tvam akarma nimitta tvāt iti avocāma
tat kṛta dharma adharma nimittam sa śarīra tvam iti ced na
śarīra saṃbandhasya asiddha tvāt dharma adharmayoḥ ātma kṛta tva asiddheḥ śarīra saṃbandhasya dharma adharmayoḥ tad kṛta tvasya ca itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt
andha paramparā eṣā anādi tva kalpanā kriyā samavāya abhāvāt ca ātmanaḥ kartṛ tva anupapatteḥ
saṃnidhāna mātreṇa rāja prabhṛtīnām dṛṣṭam kartṛ tvam iti ced na
dhana dāna ādi upārjita bhṛtya saṃbandhi tvāt teṣām kartṛ tva upapatteḥ
na tu ātmanaḥ dhana dāna ādi vat śarīra ādibhiḥ sva svāmi bhāva saṃbandha nimittam kiṃcid śakyam kalpayitum
mithyā abhimānaḥ tu pratyakṣaḥ saṃbandha hetuḥ
etena yajamāna tvam ātmanaḥ vyākhyātam
atra āhuḥ deha ādi vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ ātmīye deha ādau aham abhimānaḥ gauṇaḥ na mithyā iti ced na
prasiddha vastu bhedasya gauṇa tva mukhya tva prasiddheḥ
yasya hi prasiddhaḥ vastu bhedaḥ yathā kesara ādi māna ākṛti viśeṣaḥ nvaya vyatirekābhyām siṃha śabda pratyaya bhāj mukhyaḥ nyaḥ siddhaḥ tatas ca anyaḥ puruṣaḥ prāyikaiḥ kraurya śaurya ādibhiḥ siṃha guṇaiḥ saṃpannaḥ siddhaḥ tasya tasmin puruṣe siṃha śabda pratyayau gauṇau bhavataḥ
na aprasiddha vastu bhedasya
tasya tu anyatra anya śabda pratyayau bhrānti nimittau eva bhavataḥ na gauṇau
yathā manda andhakāre sthāṇuḥ ayam iti agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣe puruṣa śabda pratyayau sthāṇu viṣayau yathā vā śuktikāyām akasmāt rajatam idam iti niścitau śabda pratyayau tadvat deha ādi saṃghāte aham iti nirupacāreṇa śabda pratyayau ātma anātma avivekena utpadyamānau katham gauṇau śakyau vaditum
ātma anātma vivekinām api paṇḍitānām aja avi pālānām iva a viviktau śabda pratyayau bhavataḥ
tasmāt deha ādi vyatirikta ātma astitva vādinām dehāt āvahaṃpratyayaḥ mithyā eva na gauṇaḥ
tasmāt mithyā pratyaya nimitta tvāt sa śarīra tvasya siddham jīvataḥ pi viduṣaḥ śarīra tvam
tathā ca brahma vidviṣayā śrutiḥ tat yathā ahiniḥ lvayanī valmīke mṛtā pratyastā śayīta evam eva idam śarīram śete atha ayam aśarīraḥ mṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ brahma eva tejaḥ eva iti
sa cakṣuḥ a cakṣuḥ iva sa karṇo karṇaḥ iva sa vāc a vāc iva sa manāḥ a manāḥ iva sa prāṇo prāṇaḥ iva iti ca
smṛtiḥ api sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā ityādyā sthita prajñasya lakṣaṇāni ācakṣāṇā viduṣaḥ sarva pravṛtti asaṃbandham darśayati
tasmāt na avagata brahma ātma bhāvasya yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tvam
yasya tu yathāpūrvam saṃsāri tvam na asau avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ iti anavadyam
yat punar uktam śravaṇāt parācīnayoḥ manana nididhyāsanayoḥ darśanāt vidhi śeṣa tvam brahmaṇaḥ na svarūpa paryavasāyi tvam iti tat na
śravaṇa vat avagati artha tvāt manana nididhyāsanayoḥ
yadi hi avagatam brahma anyatra viniyujyeta bhavet tadā vidhi śeṣa tvam
na tu tat asti manana nididhyāsanayoḥ api śravaṇa vat avagati artha tvāt
tasmāt na pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā śāstra pramāṇaka tvam brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati iti atas svatantram eva brahma śāstra pramāṇakam vedānta vākya samanvayāt iti siddham
evam ca sati atha atas brahma jijñāsā iti tad viṣayaḥ pṛthak śāstra ārambhaḥ upapadyate
pratipatti vidhi para tve hi atha atas dharma jijñāsā iti eva ārabdha tvāt na pṛthak śāstram ārabhyet
ārabhyamāṇam ca evam ārabhyeta atha atas pariśiṣṭa dharma jijñāsā iti atha atas kratu artha puruṣa arthayoḥ jijñāsāḥ itivat
brahma ātma aikya avagatiḥ tu apratijñātā iti tad arthaḥ yuktaḥ śāstra ārambhaḥ atha atas brahma jijñāsā iti
tasmāt aham brahma asmi iti etat avasānāḥ eva sarve vidhayaḥ sarvāṇi ca itarāṇi pramāṇāni
na hi aheya anupādeya advaita ātma avagatau satyām nirviṣayāṇi apramātṛkāṇi ca pramāṇāni bhavitum arhanti iti
api ca āhuḥ gauṇa mithyā ātmanoḥ sattve putra deha ādi bādhanāt
sat brahma ātmā aham iti evam bodhe kāryam katham bhavet
anveṣṭavya ātmā avijñānāt prāk pramātṛ tvam ātmanaḥ
anviṣṭaḥ syāt pramātā eva pāpma doṣa ādi varjitaḥ
deha ātma pratyayaḥ yadvat pramāṇa tvena kalpitaḥ
laukikam tadvat evā idam pramāṇam tu ātma niścayāt iti
evam tāvat vedānta vākyānām brahma ātma avagati prayojanānām brahma ātmani tātparyeṇa samanvitānām antareṇa api kārya anupraveśam brahmaṇi paryavasānam uktam
brahma ca sarvajñam sarva śakti jagat utpatti sthiti laya kāraṇam iti uktam
sāṃkhya ādayaḥ tu pariniṣṭhitam vastu pramāṇa antara gamyam eva iti manyamānāḥ pradhāna ādīni kāraṇa antarāṇi anumimānāḥ tad para tayā eva vedānta vākyāni yojayanti
sarveṣu eva vedānta vākyeṣu sṛṣṭi viṣayeṣu anumānena eva kāryeṇa kāraṇam
pradhāna puruṣa saṃyogāḥ nitya anumeyāḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ manyante
kāṇādāḥ tu etebhyaḥ eva vākyebhyaḥ īśvaram nimitta kāraṇam anumimate aṇūn ca samavāyi kāraṇam
evam anye pi tārkikāḥ vākya ābhāsa yukti ābhāsa avaṣṭambhāḥ pūrvapakṣa vādinaḥ iha uttiṣṭhante
tatra pada vākya pramāṇa jñena ācāryeṇa vedānta vākyānām brahma ātma avagati para tva pradarśanāya vākya ābhāsa yukti ābhāsa pratipattayaḥ pūrvapakṣīkṛtya nirākriyante
tatra sāṃkhyāḥ pradhānam triguṇam acetanam svatantram jagat kāraṇam iti manyamānāḥ āhuḥ yāni vedānta vākyāni sarvajñasya sarva śakteḥ brahmaṇaḥ jagat kāraṇa tvam pradarśayanti iti avocaḥ tāni pradhāna kāraṇa pakṣe pi yojayitum śakyante
sarva śakti tvam tāvat pradhānasya api sva vikāra viṣayam upapadyate
evam sarvajña tvam api upapadyate
katham
yat tvam jñānam manyase sa sattva dharmaḥ sattvāt saṃjāyate jñānam
iti smṛteḥ
tena ca sattva dharmeṇa jñānena kārya karaṇavantaḥ puruṣāḥ sarvajñāḥ yoginaḥ prasiddhāḥ
sattvasya hi niratiśaya utkarṣe sarvajña tvam prasiddham
na kevalasya akārya karaṇasya puruṣasya upalabdhi mātrasya sarvajñatvam kiṃcijjñatvam vā kalpayitum śakyam
triguṇa tvāt tu pradhānasya sarvajñāna kāraṇa bhūtam sattvam pradhāna avasthāyām api vidyate iti pradhānasya acetanasya eva sataḥ sarvajña tvam upacaryate vedānta vākyeṣu
avaśyam ca tvayā api sarvajñam brahma iti abhyupagacchatā sarva jñāna śaktimat tvena eva sarvajña tvam abhyupagantavyam
na hi sarvadā sarva viṣayam jñānam kurvat eva brahma vartate
tathā hi jñānasya nitya tve jñāna kriyām prati svātantryam brahmaṇaḥ hīyeta
atha anityam tat iti jñāna kriyāyāḥ uparame uparameta api brahma tadā sarva jñāna śaktimat tvena eva sarvajña tvam āpatati
api ca prāk utpatteḥ sarva kāraka śūnyam brahma iṣyate tvayā
na ca jñāna sādhanānām śarīra indriya ādīnām abhāve jñāna utpattiḥ kasyacid upapannā
api ca pradhānasya aneka ātmakasya pariṇāma saṃbhavāt kāraṇatva upapattiḥ mṛd ādi vat na asaṃhatasya eka ātmakasya brahmaṇaḥ
iti evam prāpte idam sūtram ārabhyate
īkṣateḥ na a śabdam
īkṣati adhikaraṇam
na sāṃkhya parikalpitam acetanam pradhānam jagataḥ kāraṇam śakyam vedānteṣu āśrayitum
aśabdam hi tat
katham aśabda tvam
īkṣateḥ īkṣitṛ tva śravaṇāt kāraṇasya
katham
evam hi śrūyate sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti upakramya tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti
tatra idam śabda vācyam nāma rūpa vyākṛtam jagat prāk utpatteḥ sat ātmanā avadhārya tasya eva prakṛtasya sat śabda vācyasya īkṣaṇa pūrvakam tejaḥ prabhṛteḥ sraṣṭṛ tvam darśayati
tathā anyatra ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt
na anyat kiṃcana miṣat
saḥ īkṣata lokān nu sṛjai iti
saḥ imān lokān asṛjata iti īkṣā pūrvikām eva sṛṣṭim ācaṣṭe
kvacid ca ṣoḍaśa kalam puruṣam prastutya āha saḥ īkṣāṃcakre sa prāṇam asṛjata iti
īkṣateḥ iti ca dhātvartha nirdeśaḥ bhipretaḥ yajateḥ iti vat na dhātu nirdeśaḥ
tena yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid yasya jñāna mayam tapaḥ
tasmāt etat brahma nāma rūpam annam ca jāyate iti evamādīni api sarvajña īśvara kāraṇa parāṇi vākyāni udāhartavyāni
yat tu uktam sattva dharmeṇa jñānena sarvajñam pradhānam bhaviṣyati iti tat na upapadyate
na hi pradhāna avasthāyām guṇa sāmyāt sattva dharmaḥ jñānam saṃbhavati
nanu uktam sarva jñāna śaktimat tvena sarvajñam bhaviṣyati iti
tat api na upapadyate
yadi guṇa sāmye sati sattva vyapāśrayām jñāna śaktim āśritya sarvajñam pradhānam ucyeta kāmam rajaḥ tamaḥ vyapāśrayām api jñāna pratibandhaka śaktim āśritya kiṃcijjñam ucyeta
api ca na a sākṣikā sattva vṛttiḥ jānātinā abhidhīyate
na ca acetanasya pradhānasya sākṣi tvam asti
tasmāt anupapannam pradhānasya sarvajña tvam
yoginām tu cetana tvāt sattva utkarṣa nimittam sarvajña tvam upapannam iti anudāharaṇam
atha punar sākṣi nimittam īkṣitṛ tvam pradhānasya api kalpyeta yathā agni nimittam ayaḥ piṇḍa ādeḥ dagdhṛ tvam
tathā sati yad nimittam īkṣitṛ tvam pradhānasya tat eva sarvajñam brahma mukhyam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti yuktam
yat punar uktam brahmaṇaḥ u pi na mukhyam sarvajña tvam upapadyate nitya jñāna kriya tve jñāna kriyām prati svātantrya asaṃbhavāt iti
atrā ucyate idam tāvat bhavān praṣṭavyaḥ katham nitya jñāna kriya tve sarvajña tva hāniḥ iti
yasya hi sarva viṣaya avabhāsana kṣamam jñānam nityam asti saḥ sarvajñaḥ iti vipratiṣiddham
anitya tve hi jñānasya kadācid jānāti kadācid na jānāti iti asarvajña tvam api syāt
na asau jñāna nitya tve doṣaḥ sti
jñāna nitya tve jñāna viṣayaḥ svātantrya vyapadeśaḥ na upapadyate iti ced na
pratata auṣṇya prakāśe savitari dahati prakāśayati iti svātantrya vyapadeśa darśanāt
nanu savituḥ dāhya prakāśya saṃyoge sati dahati prakāśayati iti vyapadeśaḥ syāt
na tu brahmaṇaḥ prāk utpatteḥ jñāna karma saṃyogaḥ sti iti viṣamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ
na
asati api karmaṇi savitā prakāśate iti kartṛ tva vyapadeśa darśanāt evam asati api jñāna karmaṇi brahmaṇaḥ tadā aikṣata iti kartṛ tva vyapadeśa upapatteḥ na vaiṣamyam
karma apekṣāyām tu brahmaṇi īkṣitṛ tva śrutayaḥ sutarām upapannāḥ
kim punar tat karma yat prāk utpatteḥ īśvara jñānasya viṣayaḥ bhavati iti tattva anyatvābhyām anirvacanīye nāma rūpe avyākṛte vyācikīrṣite iti brūmaḥ
yad prasādāt hi yoginām api atīta anāgata viṣayam pratyakṣam jñānam icchanti yoga śāstra vidaḥ kim u vaktavyam tasya nitya siddhasya īśvarasya sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhṛti viṣayam nitya jñānam bhavati iti
yat api uktam prāk utpatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ śarīra ādi saṃbandham antareṇa īkṣitṛ tvam anupapannam iti na tat codyam avatarati
savitṛ prakāśa vat brahmaṇaḥ jñāna svarūpa nitya tve jñāna sādhana apekṣā anupapatteḥ
api ca avidyā ādimataḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ śarīra ādi apekṣā jñāna utpattiḥ syāt
na jñāna pratibandha kāraṇa rahitasya īśvarasya
mantrau ca imau īśvarasya śarīra ādi anapekṣa tām anāvaraṇa jñāna tām ca darśayataḥ na tasya kāryam karaṇam ca vidyate na tad samaḥ ca abhyadhikaḥ ca dṛśyate
parā asya śaktiḥ vividhā eva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñāna bala kriyā ca iti
a pāṇi pādaḥ javanaḥ grahītā paśyati a cakṣuḥ sa śrṛṇoti a karṇaḥ
sa vetti vedyam na ca tasya asti vettā tam āhuḥ agryam puruṣam mahāntam iti ca
nanu nā asti tava jñāna pratibandha kāraṇa rahita īśvarāt anyaḥ saṃsārī sti draṣṭā na anyaḥ sti vijñātā ityādi śruteḥ
tatra kim idam ucyate saṃsāriṇaḥ śarīra ādi apekṣā jñāna utpattiḥ na īśvarasya iti
atrā ucyate satyam na īśvarāt anyaḥ saṃsārī
tathā api deha ādi saṃghāta upādhi saṃbandhaḥ iṣyate eva ghaṭa karaka giri guhā ādi upādhi saṃbandhaḥ iva vyomnaḥ
tad kṛtaḥ ca śabda pratyaya vyavahāraḥ lokasya dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭa chidram karaka chidram ityādiḥ ākāśa a vyatireke pi
tad kṛtā ca ākāśe ghaṭa ākāśa ādi bheda mithyā buddhiḥ dṛṣṭā
tathā iha api deha ādi saṃghāta upādhi saṃbandha aviveka kṛta īśvara saṃsāri bheda mithyā buddhiḥ
dṛśyate ca ātmanaḥ eva sataḥ deha ādi saṃghāte na ātmani ātma tva abhiniveśaḥ mithyā buddhi mātreṇa pūrva pūrveṇa
sati ca evam saṃsāri tve deha ādi apekṣam īkṣitṛ tvam upapannam saṃsāriṇaḥ
yat api uktam pradhānasya aneka ātmaka tvāt mṛd ādi vat kāraṇatva upapattiḥ na asaṃhatasya brahmaṇaḥ iti tat pradhānasya aśabda tvena eva pratyuktam
yathā tu tarkeṇa api brahmaṇaḥ eva kāraṇa tvam nirvoḍhum śakyate na pradhāna ādīnām tathā prapañcayiṣyati na vilakṣaṇa tvāt asya iti evamādinā
atra āha yat uktam na acetanam pradhānam jagat kāraṇam īkṣitṛ tva śravaṇāt iti tat anyathā api upapadyate
acetane pi cetana vat upacāra darśanāt
yathā pratyāsanna patana tām nadyāḥ kūlasya ālakṣya kūlam pipatiṣati iti acetane pi kūle cetana vat upacāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tadvat acetane pi pradhāne pratyāsanna sarge cetana vat upacāraḥ bhaviṣyati tadā aikṣata iti
yathā loke kaścid cetanaḥ snātvā bhuktvā ca aparāhṇe grāmam rathena gamiṣyāmi iti īkṣitvā anantaram tathā eva niyamena pravartate tathā pradhānam api mahat ādi ākāreṇa niyamena pravartate
tasmāt cetana vat upacaryate
kasmāt punar kāraṇāt vihāya mukhyam īkṣitṛ tvam aupacārikam kalpyate
tat tejaḥ aikṣata tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣanta iti ca acetanayoḥ api ap tejasoḥ cetana vat upacāra darśanāt
tasmāt sat kartṛkam api īkṣaṇam aupacārikam iti gamyate upacāra prāye vacanāt
iti evam prāpte idam sūtram ārabhyate
gauṇaḥ ced na ātma śabdāt
yat uktam pradhānam acetanam sat śabda vācyam tasmin aupacārikam īkṣitṛ tvam ap tejasoḥ iva iti tat asat
kasmāt
ātma śabdāt
sat eva somya idam agre āsīt iti upakramya tat aikṣata tat tejaḥ
asṛjata iti ca tejaḥ bannānām sṛṣṭim uktvā tat eva prakṛtam sat īkṣitṛ tāni ca tejaḥ bannāni devatā śabdena parāmṛśya āha sā iyam devatā aikṣata hanta aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti
tatra yadi pradhānam acetanam guṇa vṛttyā īkṣitṛ kalpyeta tat eva prakṛta tvāt sā iyam devatā iti parāmṛśyeta
na tadā devatāḥ jīvam ātma śabdena abhidadhyāt
jīvaḥ hi nāma cetanaḥ śarīra adhyakṣaḥ prāṇānām dhārayitā tad prasiddheḥ nirvacanāt ca
sa
katham acetanasya pradhānasya ātmā bhavet
ātmā hi nāma svarūpam
na acetanasya pradhānasya cetanaḥ jīvaḥ svarūpam bhavitum arhati
atha tu cetanam brahma mukhyam īkṣitṛ parigṛhyeta tasya jīva viṣayaḥ ātma śabda prayogaḥ upapadyate
tathā sa yaḥ eṣaḥ ṇimā etat ātmyam idam sarvam tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti atra saḥ ātmā iti prakṛtam sat aṇimānam ātmānam ātma śabdena upadiśya tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti cetanasya śvetaketoḥ ātma tvena upadiśati
ap tejasoḥ tu viṣaya tvāt acetana tvam nāma rūpa vyākaraṇa ādau ca prayojya tvena eva nirdeśāt na ca ātma śabda vat kiṃcid mukhya tve kāraṇam asti iti yuktam kūla vat gauṇa tvam īkṣitṛ tvasya
tayoḥ api sat adhiṣṭhita tva apekṣam eva īkṣitṛ tvam
sataḥ tu ātma śabdāt na gauṇam īkṣitṛ tvam iti uktam
atha ucyeta acetane pi pradhāne bhavati ātma śabdaḥ ātmanaḥ sarva artha kāri tvāt
yathā rājñaḥ sarva artha kāriṇi bhṛtye bhavati ātma śabdaḥ mama ātmā bhadrasenaḥ iti
pradhānam hi puruṣasya ātmanaḥ bhoga apavargau kurvat upakaroti rājñaḥ iva bhṛtyaḥ saṃdhi vigraha ādiṣu vartamānaḥ
athavā ekaḥ eva ātma śabdaḥ cetana acetana viṣayaḥ bhaviṣyati bhūtātmā indriyātmā iti ca prayoga darśanāt
yathā ekaḥ eva jyotiḥ śabdaḥ kratu jvalana viṣayaḥ
tatra kutas etat ātma śabdāt īkṣateḥ agauṇa tvam iti atas uttaram paṭhati
tad niṣṭhasya mokṣa upadeśāt
na pradhānam acetanam ātma śabda ālambanam bhavitum arhati
saḥ ātmā iti prakṛtam sat aṇimānam ādāya tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti cetanasya śvetaketoḥ mokṣayitavyasya tad niṣṭhām upadiśya ācāryavān puruṣaḥ veda tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣye saṃpatsye iti mokṣa upadeśāt
yadi hi acetanam pradhānam sat śabda vācyam tat asi iti grāhayet mumukṣum cetanam santam acetana u si iti tadā viparīta vādi śāstram puruṣasya anarthāya iti apramāṇam syāt
na tu nirdoṣam idam śāstram apramāṇam kalpayitum yuktam
yadi ca ajñasya sataḥ mumukṣoḥ acetanam anātmānam ātmā iti upadiśet pramāṇa bhūtam śāstram sa śraddadhāna tayā andha golāṅgūla nyāyena tad ātma dṛṣṭim na parityajet tad vyatiriktam ca ātmānam na pratipadyeta
tathā sati puruṣa arthāt vihanyeta anartham vā ṛcchet
tasmāt yathā svarga ādi arthinaḥ gnihotra ādi sādhanam yathābhūtam upadiśati tathā mumukṣoḥ api saḥ ātmā tattvam asi śvetaketo iti yathābhūtam eva ātmānam upadiśati iti yuktam
evam ca sati tapta paraśu grahaṇa mokṣa dṛṣṭāntena satya abhisaṃdhasya mokṣa upadeśaḥ upapadyate
anyathā hi amukhye sat ātma tattva upadeśe aham uktham asmi iti vidyāt iti vat saṃpad mātram idam anitya phalam syāt
tatra mokṣa upadeśaḥ na upapadyeta
tasmāt na sat aṇimani ātma śabdasya gauṇa tvam
bhṛtye tu svāmi bhṛtya bhedasya pratyakṣa tvāt upapannaḥ gauṇaḥ ātma śabdaḥ mama ātmā bhadrasenaḥ iti
api ca kvacid gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti na etāvatā śabda pramāṇake rthe gauṇī kalpanā nyāyyā sarvatra anāśvāsa prasaṅgāt
yat tu uktam cetana acetanayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ ātma śabdaḥ kratu jvalanayoḥ iva jyotiḥ śabdaḥ iti tat na
aneka artha tvasya anyāyya tvāt
tasmāt cetana viṣayaḥ eva mukhyaḥ ātma śabdaḥ cetana tva upacārāt bhūta ādiṣu prayujyate bhūtātmā indriyātmā iti ca
sādhāraṇa tve pi ātma śabdasya na prakaraṇam upapadam vā kiṃcid niścāyakam antareṇa anyatara vṛtti tā nirdhārayitum śakyate
na ca atra acetanasya niścāyakam kiṃcid kāraṇam asti
prakṛtam tu sa dīkṣitṛ saṃnihitaḥ ca cetanaḥ śvetaketuḥ
na hi cetanasya śvetaketoḥ acetanaḥ ātmā saṃbhavati iti avocāma
tasmāt cetana viṣayaḥ iha ātma śabdaḥ iti niścīyate
jyotiḥ śabdaḥ api laukikena prayogeṇa jvalanaḥ eva rūḍhaḥ arthavāda kalpitena tu jvalana sādṛśyena kratau pravṛttaḥ iti adṛṣṭāntaḥ
athavā pūrva sūtre eva ātma śabdam nirasta samasta gauṇatva sādhāraṇa tva āśaṅkatayā vyākhyāya tatas svatantraḥ eva pradhāna kāraṇa nirākaraṇa hetuḥ vyākhyeyaḥ tad niṣṭhasya mokṣa upadeśāt iti
tasmāt na acetanam pradhānam sat śabda vācyam
kutas ca na pradhānam sat śabda vācyam
heya tva avacanāt ca
yadi anātmā eva pradhānam sat śabda vācyam saḥ ātmā tattvam asi iti iha upadiṣṭam syāt
sa tad upadeśa śravaṇāt anātma jña tayā tad niṣṭhaḥ mā bhūt iti mukhyam ātmānam upadidikṣu śāstram tasya heya tvam brūyāt
yathā arundhatīm didarśayiṣuḥ tad samīpa sthām sthūlām tārām amukhyām prathamam arundhatī iti grāhayitvā tām pratyākhyāya paścāt arundhatīm eva grāhayati
tadvat na ayam ātmā iti brūyāt
na ca evam avocat
sanmātra ātma avagati niṣṭhā eva hi ṣaṣṭha prapāṭhake parisamāptiḥ dṛśyate
ca śabdaḥ pratijñā virodha abhyuccaya pradarśana arthaḥ
sati api heya tva vacane pratijñā virodhaḥ prasajyeta
kāraṇa vijñānāt hi sarvam vijñātam iti pratijñātam uta tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ yena a śrutam śrutam bhavati a matam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti
katham nu bhagavaḥ saḥ ādeśaḥ bhavati iti
yathā somya ekena mṛd piṇḍena sarvam mṛd mayam vijñātam syāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam evam somya saḥ ādeśaḥ bhavati iti vākya upakrame śravaṇāt
na ca sat śabda vācye pradhāne bhogya varga kāraṇe heya tvena aheya tvena vā vijñāte bhoktṛ vargaḥ vijñātaḥ bhavati a pradhāna vikāra tvāt bhoktṛ vargasya
tasmāt na pradhānam sat śabda vācyam
kutas ca na pradhānam sat śabda vācyam
sva apyayāt
tat eva sat śabda vācyam kāraṇam prakṛtya śrūyate yatra etat puruṣaḥ svapiti nāma satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati
svam api itas bhavati
tasmāt enam svapiti iti ācakṣate
svam hi api itas bhavati iti
eṣā śrutiḥ svapiti iti etad puruṣasya loka prasiddham nāma nirvakti
sva śabdena iha ātmā ucyate
yaḥ prakṛtaḥ sat śabda vācyaḥ tam apītaḥ bhavati apigataḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ
api pūrvasya aiteḥ laya artha tvam prasiddham prabhava apyayau iti utpatti pralayayoḥ prayoga darśanāt
manaḥ pracāra upādhi viśeṣa saṃbandhāt indriyārthān gṛhṇan tad viśeṣa āpannaḥ jīvaḥ jāgarti
tad vāsanā viśiṣṭaḥ svapnān paśyanmanaḥ śabda vācyaḥ bhavati
saḥ upādhi dvaya uparame suṣupta avasthāyām upādhi kṛta viśeṣa abhāvāt sva ātmani pralīnaḥ iva iti svam hi api itas bhavati iti ucyate
yathā hṛdaya śabda nirvacanam śrutyā darśitam sa vai eṣaḥ ātmā hṛdi tasya etat eva niruktam hṛdi ayam iti
tasmāt hṛdayam iti
yathā vā aśanāya udanyā śabda pravṛtti mūlam darśayati śrutiḥ āpaḥ eva tat aśitam nayante tejaḥ eva tat pītam nayate iti ca
evam svam ātmānam sat śabda vācyam apītaḥ bhavati iti imam artham svapiti nāma nirvacanena darśayati
na ca cetanaḥ ātmā acetanam pradhānam sva rūpa tvena pratipadyeta
yadi punar pradhānam eva ātmīya tvāt sva śabdena eva ucyeta evam api cetano cetanam apyeti iti viruddham āpadyeta
śruti antaram ca prājñena ātmanā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ na bāhyam kiṃcana veda na antaram iti suṣupta avasthāyām cetane apyayam darśayati
atas yasmin apyayaḥ sarveṣām cetanānām tat cetanam sat śabda vācyam jagataḥ kāraṇam syāt na acetanam pradhānam
kutas ca na pradhānam jagataḥ kāraṇam
gati sāmānyāt
yadi tārkika samaye iva vedānteṣu api bhinnā kāraṇa avaga gatiḥ abhaviṣyat kvacid cetanam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam kvacid acetanam pradhānam kvacid anyat eva iti
tatas kadācid pradhāna kāraṇa vāda anurodhena api īkṣati ādi śravaṇam akalpayiṣyat
na tu etat asti
samānā eva hi sarveṣu vedānteṣu cetana kāraṇa avagatiḥ
yathā agneḥ jvalataḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vipratiṣṭheran evam eva etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ yathāyatanam vipratiṣṭhante prāṇebhyaḥ devāḥ devebhyaḥ lokāḥ iti tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti ātmanaḥ eva idam sarvam iti ātmanaḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ jāyate iti ca ātmanaḥ kāraṇa tvam darśayanti sarve vedāntāḥ
ātma śabdaḥ ca cetana vacanaḥ iti avocāma
mahat ca prāmāṇya kāraṇam etat yat vedānta vākyānām cetana kāraṇa tve samāna gati tvam cakṣuḥ ādīnām iva rūpa ādiṣu
atas gati samānyāt sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam
kutas ca sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam
śruta tvāt ca
sva śabdena eva ca sarvajñaḥ īśvaraḥ jagataḥ kāraṇam iti śrūyate śvetāśvatarāṇām mantra upaniṣadi sarvajñam īśvaram prakṛtya sa kāraṇam karaṇa adhipa adhipaḥ na ca asya kaścid janitā na ca adhipaḥ iti
tasmāt sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam na acetanam pradhānam anyat vā iti siddham
janma ādyasya yatas iti ārabhya śruta tvāt ca iti etad antaiḥ sūtraiḥ yāni udāhṛtāni vedānta vākyāni teṣām sarvajñaḥ sarva śaktiḥ īśvaraḥ jagataḥ janma sthiti pralaya kāraṇam iti etasya arthasya pratipādaka tvam nyāya pūrvakam pratipāditam
gati sāmānya upanyāsena ca sarve vedāntāḥ cetana kāraṇa vādinaḥ iti vyākhyātam
atas parasya granthasya kim utthānam iti ucyate dvirūpam hi brahma avagamyate nāma rūpa vikāra bheda upādhi viśiṣṭam tad viparītam ca sarva upādhi vivarjitam
yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet yatra na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anyat vijānāti sa bhūmā
atha yatra anyat paśyati anyat śṛṇoti anyat vijānāti tat alpam
yaḥ vai bhūmā tat amṛtam
atha yat alpam tat martyam sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīraḥ nāmāni kṛtvā abhivadan yat āste niṣkalam niṣkriyam śāntam niravadyam nirañjanam
amṛtasya param setum dagdha indhanam iva analam na iti na iti a sthūlam an aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham iti nyūnam anyat sthānam saṃpūrṇam anyat iti ca evam sahasraśas vidyā avidyā viṣaya bhedena brahmaṇaḥ dvi rūpa tām darśayanti vedānta vākyāni
tatra avidyā avasthāyām brahmaṇaḥ upāsya upāsaka ādi lakṣaṇaḥ sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ
tatra kānicid brahmaṇaḥ upāsanāni abhyudaya arthāni kānicid krama mukti arthāni kānicid karma samṛddhi arthāni
teṣām guṇa viśeṣa upādhi bhedena bhedaḥ
ekaḥ eva tu paraḥ ātmā īśvaraḥ taiḥ taiḥ guṇa viśeṣaiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ upāsyaḥ yadi api bhavati tathā api yathā guṇa upāsanam eva phalāni bhidyante
tam yathā yathā upāsate tat eva bhavati iti śruteḥ yathā kratu rasimant loke puruṣaḥ bhavati tathā itas pretya bhavati iti ca
smṛteḥ ca yam yam vā api smaran bhāvam tyajati ante kalebaram
tam tam eva eti kaunteya sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ iti
yadi api ekaḥ ātmā sarva bhūteṣu sthāvara jaṅgameṣu gūḍhaḥ tathā api citta upādhi viśeṣa tāratamyāt ātmanaḥ kūṭastha nityasya ekarūpasya api uttarottaram āviṣkṛtasya tāratamyam aiśvarya śakti viśeṣaiḥ śrūyate tasya yaḥ ātmānam āvistarām veda iti atra
smṛtau api yat yat vibhūtimat sattvam śrīmat ūrjitam eva vā
tat tat eva avagaccha tvam mama tejaḥ ṃśa saṃbhavam iti yatra yatra vibhūti ādi atiśayaḥ sa saḥ īśvaraḥ iti upāsya tayā codyate
evam iha api āditya maṇḍale hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ sarva pāpma udaya liṅgāt paraḥ eva iti vakṣyati
evam ākāśaḥ tat liṅgāt ityādiṣu draṣṭavyam
evam sadyas mukti kāraṇam api ātma jñānam upādhi viśeṣa dvāreṇa upadiśyamānam api avivakṣita upādhi saṃbandha viśeṣam parāpara viṣaya tvena saṃdihyamānam vākya gati paryālocanayā nirṇetavyam bhavati yathā iha eva tāvat ānanda mayaḥ bhyāsāt iti
evam ekam api brahma apekṣita upādhi saṃbandham nirasta upādhi saṃbandham ca upāsya tvena jñeya tvena ca vedānteṣu upadiśyate iti pradarśayitum paraḥ granthaḥ ārabhyate
yat ca gati sāmānyāt iti acetana kāraṇa nirākaraṇam uktam tat api vākya antarāṇi brahma viṣayāṇi vyācakṣāṇena brahma viparīta kāraṇa niṣedhena prapañcyate
ānanda mayaḥ bhyāsāt
ānanda maya adhikaraṇam
taittirīyake anna mayam prāṇa mayam manaḥ mayam vijñāna mayam ca anukramya āmnāyate tasmāt vai etasmāt vijñāna mayāt anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā ānanda mayaḥ iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha ānanda maya śabdena param eva brahma ucyate yat prakṛtam satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti kim vā anna maya ādi vat brahmaṇaḥ rtha antaram iti
kim tāvat prāptam
brahmaṇaḥ ṛtha antaram amukhyaḥ ātmā ānanda mayaḥ syāt
kasmāt
anna maya ādya mukhya ātma pravāha patita tvāt
atha api syāt sarva antara tvāt ānanda mayaḥ mukhyaḥ eva ātmā iti
na syāt priya ādi avayava yogāt śārīra tva śravaṇāt ca
mukhyaḥ ced ātmā syāt na priya ādi saṃsparśaḥ syāt
iha tu tasya priyam eva śiraḥ ityādi śrūyate
śārīra tvam ca śrūyate tasya eṣaḥ eva śārīraḥ ātmā yaḥ pūrvasya iti
tasya pūrvasya vijñāna mayasya eṣaḥ eva śārīraḥ ātmā yaḥ eṣaḥ ānanda mayaḥ iti arthaḥ
na ca sa śarīrasya sataḥ priya apriya saṃsparśaḥ vārayitum śakyaḥ
tasmāt saṃsārī eva ānanda mayaḥ ātmā iti evam prāpte idam ucyate ānanda mayaḥ bhyāsāt
paraḥ eva ātmā ānanda mayaḥ bhavitum arhati
kutas
abhyāsāt

kaḥ hi eva anyāt kaḥ prāṇyāt

ānandaḥ brahma iti vyajānāt iti ca
śruti antare ca vijñānam ānandam brahma iti brahmaṇi eva ānanda śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
evam ānanda śabdasya bahu kṛtvas brahmaṇi abhyāsāt ānanda mayaḥ ātmā brahma iti gamyate
yat tu uktam anna maya ādi amukhya ātma pravāha patita tvāt ānanda mayasya api amukhya tvam iti na asau doṣaḥ ānanda mayasya sarva antara tvāt
mukhyam eva hi ātmānam upadidikṣu śāstram loka buddhim anusarat anna mayam śarīram anātmānam atyanta mūḍhānām ātma tvena prasiddham anūdya antaram tatas ntaram iti evam pūrveṇa pūrveṇa samānam uttaram uttaram anātmānam ātmā iti grāhayat pratipatti saukarya apekṣayā sarva antaram mukhyam ānanda mayam ātmānam upadideśa iti śliṣṭataram
yathā arundhatī darśane bahvīṣu api tārāsu amukhyāsu arundhatīṣu darśitāsu yā antyā pradarśyate sā mukhyā eva arundhatī bhavati
evam iha api ānanda mayasya sarva antara tvāt mukhyam ātma tvam
yat tu brūṣe priya ādīnām śiraḥ tva ādi kalpanā anupapannā mukhyasya ātmanaḥ iti atīta anantara upādhi janitā sā
na svābhāvikī iti adoṣaḥ

na punar sākṣāt eva śārīra tvam saṃsāri vat

vikāra śabdāt

tasmāt anna maya ādi śabda vat vikāra viṣayaḥ eva ayam ānanda maya śabdaḥ iti ced na
prācurya arthe pi mayaṭaḥ smaraṇāt
tad prakṛta vacane mayaṭ SNM
iti hi pracura tāyām api mayaṭ smaryate
yathā anna mayaḥ yajñaḥ iti anna pracuraḥ ucyate evam ānanda pracuram brahma ānanda mayam ucyate
ānanda pracura tvam ca brahmaṇaḥ manuṣya tvāt ārabhya uttarasmin uttarasmin sthāne śataguṇaḥ ānandaḥ iti uktvā brahma ānandasya niratiśaya tva avadhāraṇāt

tad hetu vyapadeśāt ca

yaḥ hi anyān ānandayati sa pracura ānandaḥ iti prasiddham bhavati
yathā loke yaḥ nyeṣām dhanika tvam āpādayati sa pracura dhanaḥ iti gamyate tadvat

māntravarṇikam eva ca gīyate

yasmāt brahma vid āpnoti param iti upakramya satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti asmin mantre yat brahma prakṛtam satya jñāna ananta viśeṣaṇaiḥ nirdhāritam yasmāt ākāśa ādi krameṇa sthāvara jaṅgamāni bhūtāni ajāyanta yat ca bhūtāni sṛṣṭvā tāni anupraviśya guhāyām avasthitam sarva antaram yasya vijñānāya anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā iti prakrāntam tat māntravarṇikam eva brahma iha gīyate anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā ānanda mayaḥ iti
mantra brāhmaṇayoḥ ca eka artha tvam yuktam avirodhāt

anupapatteḥ

bheda vyapadeśāt ca
itas ca na ānanda mayaḥ saṃsārī
yasmāt ānanda maya adhikāre rasaḥ vai saḥ
rasä hi eva ayam labdhvā ānandī bhavati iti jīva ānanda mayau bhedena vyapadiśati
na hi labdhā eva labdhavyaḥ bhavati
katham tarhi ātmā anveṣṭavyaḥ ātma lābhāt na param vidyate iti śruti smṛtī yāvatā na labdhā eva labdhavyaḥ bhavati iti uktam
bāḍham tathā api pracyuta ātma bhāvasya eva sataḥ tattva anavabodha nimittaḥ mithyā eva deha ādiṣu anātmasu ātma tva niścayaḥ laukikaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
tena deha ādi bhūtasya ātmanaḥ u pi ātmā an anviṣṭaḥ anveṣṭavyaḥ alabdhaḥ labdhavyaḥ aśrutaḥ śrotavyaḥ amataḥ mantavyaḥ avijñātaḥ vijñātavyaḥ ityādi bheda vyapadeśaḥ upapadyate
pratiṣidhyate eva tu paramārthataḥ sarvajñāt parameśvarāt anyaḥ draṣṭā śrotā vā draṣṭā ityādinā
parameśvaraḥ tu avidyā kalpitāt śārīrāt kartuḥ bhoktuḥ vijñāna ātma ākhyāt anyaḥ
yathā māyāvinaḥ carma khaḍga dharāt sūtreṇa ākāśam adhirohataḥ saḥ eva māyāvī paramārtha rūpaḥ bhūmiṣṭhaḥ

anyaḥ

anupapatteḥ bheda vyapadeśāt ca iti uktam
kāmāt ca na anumāna apekṣā
ānanda maya adhikāre ca sā u kāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti kāmayitṛ tva nirdeśāt ca na ānumānikam api sāṃkhya parikalpitam acetanam pradhānam ānanda maya tvena kāraṇa tvena vā apekṣitavyam
īkṣateḥ na a śabdam iti nirākṛtam api pradhānam pūrva sūtra udāhṛtām kāmayitṛ tva śrutim āśritya prasaṅgāt punar nirākriyate gati sāmānya prapañcanāya
asmin asya ca tad yogam śāsti
itas ca na pradhāne jīve vā ānanda maya śabdaḥ
yasmāt asmin ānanda maye prakṛte ātmani pratibuddhasya asya jīvasya tat yogam śāsti tat ātmanā yogaḥ tad yogaḥ tad bhāva āpattiḥ muktiḥ iti arthaḥ tad yogam śāsti śāstram yadā hi eva eṣa etasmin adṛśye nātmye nirukte nilayane bhayam pratiṣṭhām vindate
atha saḥ bhayam gataḥ bhavati
yadā hi eva eṣa etasmin udaram antaram kurute
atha tasya bhayam bhavati iti
etat uktam bhavati yadā etasmin ānanda maye lpam api antaram a tādātmya rūpam paśyati tadā saṃsāra bhayāt na nivartate
yadā tu etasmin ānanda maye nirantaram tādātmyena pratitiṣṭhati tadā saṃsāra bhayāt nivartate iti
tat ca paramātma parigrahe ghaṭate na pradhāna parigrahe jīva parigrahe vā
tasmāt ānanda mayaḥ paramātmā iti siddham
idam tu iha vaktavyam sa vai eṣa puruṣaḥ nna rasa mayaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt anna rasa mayāt anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā prāṇa mayaḥ tasmāt anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā manaḥ mayaḥ tasmāt anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā vijñāna mayaḥ iti ca vikāra arthe mayaṭ pravāhe sati ānanda mayaḥ eva akasmāt ardha jaratīya nyāyena katham iva mayaṭaḥ prācurya artha tvam brahma viṣaya tvam ca āśrīyate iti
māntravarṇika brahma adhikārāt iti ced na
anna maya ādīnām api tarhi brahmatva prasaṅgaḥ
atra āha yuktam anna maya ādīnām abrahmatvam tasmāt tasmāt āntarasya āntarasya anyasya anyasya ātmanaḥ ucyamāna tvāt
ānanda mayāt tu na kaścid anyaḥ āntaraḥ ātmā ucyate
tena ānanda mayasya brahmatvam anyathā prakṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriyā prasaṅgāt iti
atrā ucyate yadi api anna maya ādibhyaḥ iva ānanda mayāt anyaḥ ntaraḥ ātmā iti na śrūyate tathā api na ānanda mayasya brahmatvam
yatas ānanda mayam prakṛtya śrūyate tasya priyam eva śiraḥ modaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ pramodaḥ uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ ānandaḥ ātmā brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti
tatra yat brahma iha mantra varṇe prakṛtam satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti tat iha brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti ucyate
tad vijijñāpayiṣayā eva anna maya ādayaḥ ānanda maya paryantāḥ pañca kośāḥ kalpyante
tatra kutas prakṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriyā prasaṅgaḥ
nanu ānanda mayasya avayava tvena brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti ucyate anna maya ādīnām iva idam puccham pratiṣṭhā ityādi
tatra katham brahmaṇaḥ svapradhāna tvam śakyam vijñātum
prakṛta tvāt iti brūmaḥ
nanu ānanda maya avayava tvena api brahmaṇi vijñāyamāne na prakṛta tvam hīyate ānanda mayasya brahma tvāt iti
atra ucyate tathā sati tat eva brahma ānanda mayaḥ ātmā avayavī tat eva ca brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā avayavaḥ iti asāmañjasyam syāt
anyatara parigrahe tu yuktam brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti atra eva brahma nirdeśaḥ āśrayitum brahma śabda saṃyogāt
na ānanda maya vākye brahma śabda saṃyoga abhāvāt iti
api ca brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti uktvā idam ucyate tat api eṣa ślokaḥ bhavati
asan eva sa bhavati
asat brahma iti veda ced
asti brahma iti ced veda
santam enam tatas viduḥ iti

na ca ānanda mayasya ātmanaḥ bhāva abhāva āśaṅkā yuktā priyamoda ādi viśiṣṭasya ānanda mayasya sarva loka prasiddha tvāt

na eṣa doṣaḥ

etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti iti śruti antarāt
api ca ānanda mayasya brahmatve priya ādi avayava tvena sa viśeṣam brahma abhyupagantavyam

a prāpya manasā saha
ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān

api ca ānanda pracuraḥ iti ukte duḥkha alpīyaḥ tvam api gamyate
prācuryasya loke pratiyogi alpatva apekṣa tvāt
tathā ca sati yatra na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anyat vijānāti sa bhūmā iti bhūmni brahmaṇi tad vyatirikta abhāva śrutiḥ uparudhyeta
pratiśarīram ca priya ādi bhedāt ānanda mayasya bhinna tvam
brahma tu na pratiśarīram bhidyate satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti ānantya śruteḥ ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā iti ca śruti antarāt
na ca ānanda maya abhyāsaḥ śrūyate
prātipadika artha mātram eva hi sarvatra abhyasyate rasaḥ vai saḥ
rasä hi eva ayam labdhvā ānandī bhavati
kaḥ hi eva anyāt kaḥ prāṇyāt
yat eṣaḥ ākāśe ānandaḥ na syāt sā eṣā ānandasya mīmāṃsā bhavati ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān na bibheti kutas cana iti ānandaḥ brahma iti vyajānāt iti ca
yadi ca ānanda maya śabdasya brahma viṣaya tvam niścitam bhavet tatas uttareṣu ānanda mātra prayogeṣu api ānanda maya abhyāsaḥ kalpyeta
na tu ānanda mayasya brahmatvam asti priya śiraḥ tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ iti avocāma
tasmāt śruti antare vijñānam ānandam brahma iti ānanda pada prātipadikasya brahmaṇi prayoga darśanāt yat eṣaḥ ākāśe ānandaḥ na syāt iti brahma viṣayaḥ prayogaḥ na tu ānanda maya abhyāsaḥ iti avagantavyam
yaḥ tu ayam mayaṭ antasya eva ānanda maya śabdasya abhyāsaḥ etam ānanda mayam ātmānam upasaṃkrāmati iti na tasya brahma viṣaya tvam asti
vikāra ātmanām eva anna maya ādīnām anātmanām upasaṃkramitavyānām pravāhe patita tvāt
nanu ānanda mayasya upasaṃkramitavyasya anna maya ādi vat abrahmatve sati nā eva viduṣaḥ brahma prāptiḥ phalam nirdiṣṭam bhavet
na eṣa doṣaḥ ānanda maya upasaṃkramaṇa nirdeśena eva viduṣaḥ puccha pratiṣṭhā bhūta brahma prāpteḥ phalasya nirdiṣṭa tvāt tat api eṣa ślokaḥ bhavati yatas vācaḥ nivartante ityādinā ca prapañcyamāna tvāt
yā tu ānanda maya saṃnidhāne saḥ u kāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti iyam śrutiḥ udāhṛtā sā brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti anena saṃnihitatareṇa brahmaṇā saṃbadhyamānā na ānanda mayasya brahma tām pratibodhayati
tad apekṣa tvāt ca uttarasya granthasya rasaḥ vai saḥ ityādeḥ na ānanda maya viṣaya tā
nanu saḥ kāmayate iti brahmaṇi puṃliṅga nirdeśaḥ na upapadyate
na ayam doṣaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti atra pum liṅgena api ātma śabdena brahmaṇaḥ prakṛta tvāt
yat tu bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā ānandaḥ brahma iti vyajānāt iti tasyām mayaṭ a śravaṇāt priya śiraḥ tva ādi a śravaṇāt ca yuktam ānandasya brahmatvam
tasmāt aṇu mātram api viśeṣam an āśritya na svatas eva priyaśiraḥ tva ādi brahmaṇaḥ upapadyate
na ca iha sa viśeṣam brahma vāc manasa gocara atikramaṇa śruteḥ
tasmāt anna maya ādiṣu iva ānanda maye vikāra arthe eva mayaṭ vijñeyaḥ na prācurya arthaḥ
sūtrāṇi tu evam vyākhyeyāni brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti atra kim ānanda maya avayava tvena brahma vivakṣyate uta svapradhāna tvena iti
puccha śabdāt avayava tvena iti prāpte ucyate ānanda mayaḥ bhyāsāt ānanda mayaḥ ātmā iti atra brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti svapradhānam eva brahma upadiśyate
abhyāsāt asan eva sa bhavati iti asmin nigamana śloke brahmaṇaḥ eva kevalasya abhyasyamāna tvāt
vikāra śabdāt na iti ced na prācuryāt vikāra śabdaḥ vayava śabdaḥ bhipretaḥ
puccham iti avayava śabdāt na svapradhāna tvam brahmaṇaḥ iti yat uktam tasya parihāraḥ vaktavyaḥ
atrā ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ prācuryāt api avayava śabda upapatteḥ
prācuryam prāya āpattiḥ avayava prāye vacanam iti arthaḥ
anna maya ādīnām hi śiraḥ ādiṣu puccha anteṣu avayaveṣu ukteṣu ānanda mayasya api śiraḥ ādīni avayava antarāṇi uktvā avayava prāya āpattyā brahma puccham pratiṣṭhā iti āha na avayava vivakṣayā
yatkāraṇam abhyāsāt iti svapradhāna tvam brahmaṇaḥ samarthitam
tad hetu vyapadeśāt ca sarvasya hi vikāra jātasya sa ānanda mayasya kāraṇa tvena brahma vyapadiśyate idam sarvam asṛjata yat idam kiṃca iti
na ca kāraṇam sat brahma sva vikārasya ānanda mayasya mukhyayā vṛttyā avayavaḥ upapadyate
aparāṇi api sūtrāṇi yathāsaṃbhavam puccha vākya nirdiṣṭasya eva brahmaṇaḥ upapādakāni draṣṭavyāni
antar tad dharma upadeśāt
antar adhikaraṇam
idam āmnāyate atha yaḥ eṣaḥ ntarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ dṛśyate hiraṇya śmaśruḥ hiraṇya keśaḥ ā praṇakhāt sarvaḥ eva suvarṇaḥ tasya yathā kapyāsam puṇḍarīkam evam akṣiṇī tasya uditi nāma saḥ eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ uditaḥ udeti ha vai sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ yaḥ evam veda iti adhidaivatam
atha adhyātmam api atha yaḥ eṣaḥ ntarakṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim vidyā karma atiśaya vaśāt prāpta utkarṣaḥ kaścid saṃsārī sūrya maṇḍale cakṣuṣi ca upāsya tvena śrūyate kim vā nitya siddhaḥ parameśvaraḥ
iti
kim tāvat prāptam
saṃsāri iti
kutas
rūpavat tva śravaṇāt
āditya puruṣe tāvat hiraṇya śmaśruḥ ityādi rūpam udāhṛtam
akṣi puruṣe tat eva atideśena prāpyate tasya etasya tat eva rūpam yat amuṣya rūpam iti
na ca parameśvarasya rūpavat tvam yuktam aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam iti śruteḥ
ādhāra śravaṇāt ca yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar āditye yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar akṣiṇi iti
na hi anādhārasya sva mahima pratiṣṭhitasya sarva vyāpinaḥ parameśvarasya ādhāraḥ upadiśyeta
sa bhagavaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti sve mahimni iti ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ iti ca śrutī bhavataḥ
aiśvarya maryādā śruteḥ ca saḥ eṣa ye ca amuṣmāt parāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca īṣṭe deva kāmānām ca iti āditya puruṣasya aiśvarya maryādā
saḥ eṣa ye ca etasmāt arvāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca īṣṭe manuṣya kāmānām ca iti akṣi puruṣasya
na ca parameśvarasya maryādāvat aiśvaryam yuktam
eṣa sarva īśvaraḥ eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ eṣa bhūta pālaḥ eṣa setuḥ vidharaṇaḥ eṣām lokānām a saṃbhedāya iti a viśeṣa śruteḥ
tasmāt na akṣi ādityayoḥ antar parameśvaraḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ antar tad dharma upadeśāt iti
yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar āditye yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar akṣiṇi iti ca śrūyamāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva na saṃsārī
kutas
tad dharma upadeśāt
tasya hi parameśvarasya dharmāḥ iha upadiṣṭāḥ
tat yathā tasya uditi nāma iti śrāvayitvā tasya ādityapuruṣasya nāma saḥ eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ uditaḥ iti sarva pāpma apagamena nirvakti
tat eva ca kṛta nirvacanam nāma akṣi puruṣasya api atidiśati yat nāma tat nāma iti
sarva pāpma apagamaḥ ca paramātmanaḥ eva śrūyate yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā ityādau
tathā cākṣuṣe puruṣe sā eva ṛc tat sāma tat uktham tat yajuḥ tat brahma iti ṛk sāma ādi ātmaka tām nirdhārayati
sā ca parameśvarasya upapadyate sarva kāraṇa tvāt sarva ātmaka tva upapatteḥ
pṛthivī agni ādi ātmake ca adhidaivatam ṛk sāme vāc prāṇa ādi ātmake ca adhyātmam anukramya āha tasya ṛc ca sāma ca geṣṇau iti adhidaivatam
tathā adhyātmam api yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau iti
tat ca sarva ātmaka tve sati eva upapadyate
tat ye ime vīṇāyām gāyanti etam tu eva te gāyanti tasmāt te dhana sanayaḥ iti ca laukikeṣu api gāneṣu asya eva gīyamāna tvam darśayati
tat ca parameśvara parigrahe eva ghaṭate yat yat vibhūtimat sattvam śrīmat ūrjitam eva vā
tat tat eva avagaccha tvam mama tejaḥ oṃśa saṃbhavam iti bhagavadgītā darśanāt
loka kāma īśitṛ tvam api niraṅkuśam śrūyamāṇam parameśvaram gamayati
yat tu uktam hiraṇya śmaśru tva ādi rūpavat tva śravaṇam parameśvare na upapadyate iti atra brūmaḥ syāt parameśvarasya api icchā vaśāt māyā mayam rūpam sādhaka anugraha artham māyā hi eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yat mām paśyasi nārada
sarva bhūta guṇaiḥ yuktam mā evam mām jñātum arhasi iti smaraṇāt
api ca yatra tu nirasta sarva viśeṣam pārameśvaram rūpam upadiśyate bhavati tatra śāstram aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam ityādi
sarva kāraṇa tvāt tu vikāra dharmaiḥ api kaiścid viśiṣṭaḥ parameśvaraḥ upāsya tvena nirdiśyate sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ sarva gandhaḥ sarva rasaḥ ityādinā
tathā hiraṇya śmaśru tva ādi nirdeśaḥ pi bhaviṣyati
yat api ādhāra śravaṇāt na parameśvaraḥ iti atrā ucyate sva mahima pratiṣṭhasya api ādhāra viśeṣa upadeśaḥ upāsana arthaḥ bhaviṣyati
sarvagata tvāt brahmaṇaḥ vyoma vat sarva antara tva upapatteḥ
aiśvarya maryādā śravaṇam api adhyātma adhidaivata vibhāga apekṣam upāsana artham eva
tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva akṣi ādityayoḥ antar upadiśyate
bheda vyapadeśāt ca anyaḥ
asti ca āditya ādi śarīra abhimānibhyaḥ jīvebhyaḥ nyaḥ īśvaraḥ ntaryāmī yaḥ āditye tiṣṭhan ādityāt antaraḥ yam ādityaḥ na veda yasya ādityaḥ śarīram yaḥ ādityam antaraḥ yamayati eṣa te ātmā antaryāmī amṛtaḥ iti śruti antare bheda vyapadeśāt
tatra hi ādityāt antaraḥ yam ādityaḥ na veda iti vedituḥ ādityāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ nyaḥ ntaryāmī spaṣṭam nirdiśyate
saḥ eva iha api antarāditye puruṣaḥ bhavitum arhati śruti sāmānyāt
tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva iha upadiśyate iti siddham
ākāśaḥ tad liṅgāt
ākāśa adhikaraṇam
idam āmananti asya lokasya kā gatiḥ iti ākāśaḥ iti ha uvāca sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante ākāśam prati astam yanti ākāśaḥ hi eva ebhyaḥ jyāyān ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ākāśa śabdena param brahma abhidhīyate uta bhūtākāśam iti
kutas saṃśayaḥ
ubhayatra prayoga darśanāt
bhūta viśeṣe tāvat su prasiddhaḥ loka vedayoḥ ākāśa śabdaḥ
brahmaṇi api kvacid prayujyamānaḥ dṛśyate yatra vākyaśeṣa vaśāt asādhāraṇa guṇa śravaṇāt vā nirdhāritam brahma bhavati yathā yat eṣaḥ ākāśaḥ ānandaḥ na syāt iti ākāśaḥ ha vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yat antarā tat brahma iti ca evamādau
atas saṃśayaḥ
kim punar atra yuktam
bhūta ākāśam iti
kutas
tat hi prasiddhatareṇa prayogeṇa śīghram buddhim ārohati
na ca ayam ākāśa śabdaḥ ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ śakyaḥ vijñātum aneka artha tva prasaṅgāt
tasmāt brahmaṇi gauṇaḥ eva ākāśa śabdaḥ bhavitum arhati
vibhu tva ādibhiḥ hi bahubhiḥ dharmaiḥ sadṛśam ākāśena brahma bhavati
na ca mukhya saṃbhave gauṇaḥ rthaḥ grahaṇam arhati
saṃbhavati ca iha mukhyasya eva ākāśasya grahaṇam
nanu bhūta ākāśa parigrahe vākyaśeṣaḥ na upapadyate sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante ityādiḥ
na eṣa doṣaḥ bhūtākāśasya api vāyu ādi krameṇa kāraṇa tva upapatteḥ
vijñāyate hi tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agniḥ ityādi
jyāyaḥ tu aparāyaṇa tve api bhūta antara apekṣayā upapadyete bhūtākāśasya api
tasmāt ākāśa śabdena bhūtākāśasya grahaṇam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ
ākāśaḥ tad liṅgāt
ākāśa śabdena iha brahmaṇaḥ grahaṇam yuktam
kutas
tad liṅgāt
parasya hi brahmaṇaḥ idam liṅgam sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante iti
parasmāt hi brahmaṇaḥ bhūtānām utpattiḥ iti vedānteṣu maryādā
nanu bhūtākāśasya api vāyu ādi krameṇa kāraṇa tvam darśitam
satyam darśitam
tathā api mūla kāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ parigrahāt ākāśāt eva iti avadhāraṇam sarvāṇi iti ca bhūta viśeṣaṇam na anukūlam syāt
tathā ākāśam prati astam yanti iti brahma liṅgam ākāśaḥ hi eva ebhyaḥ jyāyān ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam iti ca jyāyaḥ tu a parāyaṇa tve
jyāyaḥ tvam hi an āpekṣikam paramātmani eva ekasmin āmnātam jyāyān pṛthivyāḥ jyāyān antarikṣāt jyāyān divaḥ jyāyān ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ iti
tathā parāyaṇa tvam api parama kāraṇa tvāt paramātmani eva upapannataram bhavati
śrutiḥ ca vijñānam ānandam brahma rātiḥ dātuḥ parāyaṇam iti
api ca anta vat tu adoṣeṇa śālāvatyasya pakṣam ninditvā anantam kiṃcid vaktu kāmena jaivalinā ākāśaḥ parigṛhītaḥ
tam ca ākāśam udgīthe saṃpādya upasaṃharati saḥ eṣa paras varīyān udgīthaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ nantaḥ iti
tat ca ānantyam brahma liṅgam
yat punar uktam bhūtākāśam prasiddhi balena prathamataram pratīyate iti atra brūmaḥ prathamataram pratītam api tad vākya śeṣa gatān brahma guṇān dṛṣṭvā na parigṛhyate
darśitaḥ ca brahmaṇi api ākāśa śabdaḥ ākāśaḥ ha vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā ityādau
tathā ākāśa paryāya vācinām api brahmaṇi prayogaḥ dṛśyate ṛcaḥ akṣare parame vyoman yasmin devāḥ adhi viśve niṣeduḥ sā eṣā bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā parame vyoman pratiṣṭhitā Ä kam brahma kham brahma kham purāṇam iti ca evamādau
vākya upakrame vartamānasya ākāśa śabdasya vākyaśeṣa vaśāt yuktā brahma viṣaya tva avadhāraṇā
agniḥ adhīte nuvākam iti hi vākya upakrama gataḥ pi agni śabdaḥ māṇavaka viṣayaḥ dṛśyate
tasmāt ākāśa śabdam brahma iti siddham
atas eva prāṇaḥ
prāṇa adhikaraṇam
udgīthe prastotar yā devatā prastāvam anvāyattā iti upakramya śrūyate katamā sā devatā iti prāṇaḥ iti ha uvāca sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni prāṇam eva abhisaṃviśanti prāṇam abhyujjihate sā eṣā devatā prastāvam anvāyattā iti
tatra saṃśaya nirṇayau pūrvavat eva draṣṭavyau
prāṇa bandhana hi somya manaḥ prāṇasya prāṇam iti ca evamādau brahma viṣayaḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ dṛśyate
vāyu vikāre tu prasiddhataraḥ loka vedayoḥ
atas iha prāṇa śabdena katarasya upādānam yuktam iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ
kim punar atra yuktam
vāyu vikārasya pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya upādānam yuktam
tatra hi prasiddhataraḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ iti avocāma
nanu pūrvavat iha api tad liṅgāt brahmaṇaḥ eva grahaṇam yuktam
iha api hi vākyaśeṣe bhūtānām saṃveśana udgamanam pārameśvaram karma pratīyate
na mukhye pi prāṇe bhūta saṃveśana udgamanasya darśanāt
evam hi āmnāyate yadā vai puruṣaḥ svapiti prāṇam tarhi vāc apyeti prāṇam cakṣuḥ prāṇam śrotram prāṇam manaḥ sa yadā prabudhyate prāṇāt eva adhi punar jāyante iti
pratyakṣam ca etat svāpa kāle prāṇa vṛttau a parilupyamānāyām indriya vṛttayaḥ parilupyante prabodha kāle ca punar prādurbhavanti iti
indriya sāra tvāt ca bhūtānām aviruddhaḥ mukhye prāṇe bhūta saṃveśana udgamana vādī vākyaśeṣaḥ
api ca ādityaḥ annam ca udgītha pratihārayoḥ devate prastāva devatāyāḥ prāṇasya anantaram nirdiśyeta
na ca tayoḥ brahmatvam asti
tad sāmānyāt ca prāṇasya api na brahma tvam iti evam prāpte sūtrakāraḥ āha atas eva prāṇaḥ iti
tad liṅgāt iti pūrva sūtre nirdiṣṭam
atas eva tad liṅgāt prāṇa śabdam api param brahma bhavitum arhati
