prāṇasya api hi brahma liṅga saṃbandhaḥ śrūyate sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni prāṇam eva abhisaṃviśanti prāṇam abhyujjihate iti
prāṇa nimittau sarveṣām bhūtānām utpatti pralayau ucyamānau prāṇasya brahma tām gamayataḥ
nanu uktam mukhya prāṇa parigrahe saṃveśana udgamana darśanam aviruddham svāpa prabodhayoḥ darśanāt iti
atrā ucyate svāpa prabodhayoḥ indriyāṇām eva kevalānām prāṇa āśrayam saṃveśana udgamanam dṛśyate na sarveṣām bhūtānām
iha tu sa indriyāṇām sa śarīrāṇām ca jīva āviṣṭānām bhūtānām sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni iti śruteḥ
yadā api bhūta śrutiḥ mahābhūta viṣayā parigṛhyate tadā api brahma liṅga tvam aviruddham
nanu saha api viṣayaiḥ indriyāṇām svāpa prabodhayoḥ prāṇe pi ayam prāṇāt ca prabhavam śrṛṇumaḥ yadā suptaḥ svapnam na kaṃcana paśyati atha asmin prāṇe eva ekadhā bhavati tadā enam vāc sarvaiḥ nāmabhiḥ saha apyeti iti
tatra api tad liṅgāt prāṇa śabdam brahma iva
yat punar uktam anna āditya saṃnidhānāt prāṇasya a brahmatvam iti tat ayuktam
vākyaśeṣa balena prāṇa śabdasya brahma viṣaya tāyām pratīyamānāyām saṃnidhānasya akiṃcitkara tvāt
yat punar prāṇa śabdasya pañca vṛttau prasiddhatara tvam tat ākāśa śabdasya iva pratividheyam
tasmāt siddham prastāva devatāyāḥ prāṇasya brahmatvam
atra kecid udāharanti prāṇasya prāṇam prāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ iti ca
tat ayuktam
śabda bhedāt prakaraṇāt ca saṃśaya anupapatteḥ
yathā pituḥ pitā iti prayoge anyaḥ pitā ṣaṣṭhī nirdiṣṭāt prathamā nirdiṣṭaḥ pituḥ pitā iti gamyate
tadvat prāṇasya prāṇam iti śabda bhedāt prasiddhāt prāṇāt anyaḥ prāṇasya prāṇaḥ iti niścīyate
na hi saḥ eva tasya iti bheda nirdeśa arhaḥ bhavati
yasya ca prakaraṇe yaḥ nirdiśyate nāma antareṇa api saḥ eva tatra prakaraṇī nirdiṣṭaḥ iti gamyate
yathā jyotiṣṭoma adhikāre vasante vasante jyotiṣā yajeta iti atra jyotiḥ śabdaḥ jyotiṣṭoma viṣayaḥ bhavati tathā parasya brahmaṇaḥ prakaraṇe prāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ iti śrutaḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ vāyu vikāra mātram katham avagamayet
atas saṃśaya aviṣaya tvāt na etat udāharaṇam yuktam
prastāvadevatāyām tu prāṇe saṃśaya pūrvapakṣa nirṇayāḥ upapāditāḥ
jyotiḥ caraṇa abhidhānāt
jyotiścaraṇa adhikaraṇam
idam āmananti atha yat atas paras divaḥ jyotiḥ dīpyate viśvatas pṛṣṭheṣu sarvatas pṛṣṭheṣu anuttameṣu uttameṣu lokeṣu idam vāva tat yat idam asmin antar puruṣe jyotiḥ iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha jyotiḥ śabdena āditya ādikam jyotiḥ abhidhīyate kim vā paraḥ ātmā
iti
artha antara viṣayasya api prāṇa śabdasya tad liṅgāt brahma viṣaya tvam uktam
iha tu tat liṅgam eva asti na asti iti vicāryate
kim tāvat prāptam
āditya ādikam eva jyotiḥ śabdena parigṛhyate iti
kutas
prasiddheḥ
tamaḥ jyotiḥ iti hi imau śabdau paraspara pratidvandvi viṣayau prasiddhau
cakṣuḥ vṛtteḥ nirodhakam śārvara ādikam tamaḥ ucyate
tasyāḥ eva anugrāhakam āditya ādikam jyotiḥ
tathā dīpyate iti iyam api śrutiḥ āditya ādi viṣayā prasiddhā
na hi rūpa ādi hīnam brahma dīpyate iti mukhyām śrutim arhati
dyu maryāda tva śruteḥ ca
na hi carācara bījasya brahmaṇaḥ sarva ātmakasya dyauḥ maryādā yuktā
kāryasya tu jyotiśaḥ paricchinnasya dyauḥ maryādā syāt
paras divaḥ jyotiḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam
nanu kāryasya api jyotiṣaḥ sarvatra gamyamāna tvāt dyu maryādāvat tvam asamañjasam
astu tarhi atrivṛt kṛtam tejaḥ prathama jam
na a trivṛt kṛtasya tejasaḥ prayojana abhāvāt iti
idam eva prayojanam yat upāsya tvam iti ced na
prayojana antara prayuktasya eva āditya ādeḥ upāsya tva darśanāt tāsām trivṛtam trivṛtam ekaikām karavāṇi iti ca a viśeṣa śruteḥ
na ca a trivṛt kṛtasya api tejasaḥ dyu maryāda tvam prasiddham
astu tarhi trivṛt kṛtam eva tat tejaḥ jyotiḥ śabdam
nanu uktam arvāk api divaḥ avagamyate gni ādikam jyotiḥ iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ
sarvatra api gamyamānasya jyotiṣaḥ paras divaḥ iti upāsana arthaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa parigrahaḥ na virudhyate
na tu niṣpradeśasya api brahmaṇaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa kalpanā bhāginī
sarvatas pṛṣṭheṣu anuttameṣu uttameṣu lokeṣu iti ca ādhāra bahutva śrutiḥ kārye jyotiṣi upapadyatetarām
idam vāva tat yat idam asmin antar puruṣe jyotiḥ iti ca kaukṣeye jyotiṣi param jyotiḥ adhyasyamānam dṛśyate
sārūpya nimittāḥ ca adhyāsāḥ bhavanti yathā tasya bhūḥ iti śiraḥ śiraḥ ekam etat akṣaram iti
kaukṣeyasya tu jyotiṣaḥ prasiddham a brahma tvam
tasya eṣā dṛṣṭiḥ tasya eṣā śrutiḥ iti ca auṣṇya ghoṣa viśiṣṭa tvasya śravaṇāt
tat etat dṛṣṭam ca śrutam ca iti upāsīta iti ca śruteḥ
cakṣuṣyaḥ ca śrutaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda iti ca alpa phala śravaṇāt abrahmatvam
mahate hi phalāya brahma upāsanam iṣyate
na ca anyat api kiṃcid sva vākye prāṇa ākāśa vat jyotiṣaḥ
asti brahmatva liṅgam
na ca pūrvasmin api vākye brahma nirdiṣṭam asti gāyatrī vai idam sarvam bhūtam iti chandaḥ nirdeśāt
atha api kathaṃcid pūrvasmin vākye brahma nirdiṣṭam syāt evam api na tasya iha pratyabhijñānam asti
tatra hi tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti dyauḥ adhikaraṇa tvena śrūyate
atra punar paras divaḥ jyotiḥ iti dyauḥ maryādā tvena tasmāt prākṛtam jyotiḥ iha grāhyam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ jyotiḥ iha brahma grāhyam
kutas
caraṇa abhidhānāt pāda abhidhānāt iti arthaḥ
pūrvasmin hi vākye catuṣpād brahma nirdiṣṭam tāvān asya mahimā tatas jyāyāḥ ca puruṣaḥ
pādaḥ u sya sarvā bhūtāni tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti anena mantreṇa
tatra yat catuṣpadaḥ brahmaṇaḥ tripād amṛtam dyu saṃbandhi rūpam nirdiṣṭam tat eva iha dyu saṃbandhāt nirdiṣṭam iti pratyabhijñāyate
tat parityajya prākṛtam jyotiḥ kalpayataḥ prakṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriye prasajyeyātām
na kevalam jyotiḥ vākye eva brahma anuvṛttiḥ
parasyām api hi śāṇḍilya vidyāyām anuvartiṣyate brahma
tasmāt iha jyotiḥ iti brahma pratipattavyam
yat tu uktam jyotiḥ dīpyate iti ca etau śabdau kārye jyotiṣi prasiddhau iti na ayam doṣaḥ
prakaraṇāt brahma avagame sati anayoḥ śabdayoḥ aviśeṣaka tvāt dīpyamāna kārya jyotiḥ upalakṣite brahmaṇi api prayoga saṃbhavāt
yena sūryaḥ tapati tejasā iddhaḥ iti ca mantra varṇāt
yat vā na ayam jyotiḥ śabdaḥ cakṣuḥ vṛtteḥ eva anugrāhake tejasi vartate anyatra api prayoga darśanāt vācā eva ayam jyotiṣā āste manaḥ jyotiḥ juṣatām iti ca
tasmāt yat yat kasyacid avabhāsakam tat tat jyotiḥ śabdena abhidhīyate
tathā sati brahmaṇaḥ pi caitanya rūpasya samasta jagat avabhāsa hetutvāt upapannaḥ jyotiḥ śabdaḥ
tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ āyuḥ ha upāsate mṛtam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca
yat api uktam dyu maryāda tvam sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ na upapadyate iti atra ucyate sarva gatasya api brahmaṇaḥ upāsana arthaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa parigrahaḥ na virudhyate
nanu uktam niṣpradeśasya brahmaṇaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa kalpanā na upapadyate iti
na ayam doṣaḥ niṣpradeśasya api brahmaṇaḥ upādhi viśeṣa saṃbandhāt pradeśa viśeṣa kalpanā upapatteḥ
tathā hi āditye cakṣuṣi hṛdaye iti pradeśa viśeṣa saṃbandhīni brahmaṇaḥ upāsanāni śrūyante
etena viśvatas pṛṣṭheṣu iti ādhāra bahutvam upapāditam
yat api etat uktam auṣṇya ghoṣābhyām anumite kaukṣeye kārye jyotiṣi adhyasyamāna tvāt param api divaḥ kārya jyotiḥ eva iti tat api ayuktam
parasya api brahmaṇaḥ nāma ādi pratīka tva vat kaukṣeya jyotiṣpratīka tva upapatteḥ
dṛṣṭam ca śrutam ca iti upāsīta iti tu pratīka dvārakam dṛṣṭa tvam śruta tvam ca bhaviṣyati
yat api uktam alpa phala śravaṇāt ca na brahma iti tat anupapannam
na hi iyate phalāya brahma āśrayaṇīyam iyate na iti niyame hetuḥ asti
yatra hi nirasta sarva viśeṣa saṃbandham param brahma ātma tvena upadiśyate tatra eka rūpam eva phalam mokṣaḥ iti avagamyate
yatra tu guṇa viśeṣa saṃbandham pratīka viśeṣa saṃbandham vā brahma upadiśyate tatra saṃsāra gocarāṇi eva uccāvacāni phalāni dṛśyante anna ādaḥ vasu dānaḥ vindate vasu yaḥ evam veda ityādyāsu śrutiṣu
yadi api na sva vākye kiṃcid jyotiṣaḥ brahmatva liṅgam asti tathā api pūrvasmin vākye dṛśyamānam grahītavyam bhavati
tat uktam sūtrakāreṇa jyotiścaraṇa abhidhānāt iti
katham punar vākya antara gatena brahma saṃnidhānena jyotiḥ śrutiḥ sva viṣayāt śakyā pracyāvayitum
na eṣa doṣaḥ atha yat atas paras divaḥ jyotiḥ iti prathamatara paṭhitena yad śabdena sarvanāmnā dyu saṃbandhāt pratyabhijñāyamāne pūrva vākya nirdiṣṭe brahmaṇi sva sāmarthyena parāmṛṣṭe sati arthāt jyotiḥ śabdasya api brahma viṣaya tva upapatteḥ
tasmāt iha jyotiḥ iti brahma pratipattavyam
chandaḥ bhidhānāt na iti ced na tathā cetaḥ ṛpaṇa nigadāt tathā hi darśanam
atha yat uktam pūrvasmin api vākye na brahma abhihitam asti gāyatrī vai idam sarvam bhūtam yat idam kiṃca iti gāyatrī ākhyasya chandasaḥ bhihita tvāt iti
tat parihartavyam
katham punar chandaḥ abhidhānāt na brahma abhihitam iti śakyate vaktum
yāvatā tāvān asya mahimā iti etasyām ṛci catuṣpād brahma darśitam
na etat asti
gāyatrī vai idam sarvam iti gāyatrīm upakramya tām eva bhūta pṛthivī śarīra hṛdaya vāc prāṇa prabhedaiḥ vyākhyāya sā eṣā catuṣpadā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī tat etat ṛcā abhyanūktam tāvān asya mahimā iti tasyām eva vyākhyāta rūpāyām gāyatryām udāhṛtaḥ mantraḥ katham akasmāt brahma catuṣpād abhidadhyāt
yaḥ u pi tatra yat vai tat brahma iti brahma śabdaḥ saḥ u pi chandasaḥ prakṛta tvāt chandaḥ viṣayaḥ eva
yaḥ etām evam brahma upaniṣadam veda iti atra hi veda upaniṣadam iti vyācakṣate
tasmāt chandaḥ abhidhānāt na brahmaṇaḥ prakṛta tvam iti ced nā eṣa doṣaḥ
tathā cetaḥ arpaṇa nigadāt tathā gāyatrī ākhya chandaḥ dvāreṇa tad anugate brahmaṇi cetasaḥ rpaṇam citta samādhānam anena brāhmaṇa vākyena nigadyate gāyatrī vai idam sarvam iti
na hi akṣara saṃniveśa mātrāyāḥ gāyatryāḥ sarva ātmaka tvam saṃbhavati
tasmāt yat gāyatrī ākhya vikāre nugatam jagat kāraṇam brahma nirdiṣṭam tat iha sarvam iti ucyate yathā sarvam khalu idam brahma iti
kāryam ca kāraṇāt avyatiriktam iti vakṣyāmaḥ tad ananyatvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti atra
tathā anyatra api vikāra dvāreṇa brahmaṇaḥ upāsanam dṛśyate etam hi eva bahvṛcāḥ mahati ukthe mīmāṃsante etam agnau adhvaryavaḥ etam mahāvrate chandogāḥ iti
tasmāt asti chandaḥ abhidhāne pi pūrvasmin vākye catuṣpād brahma nirdiṣṭam
tat eva jyotiḥ vākye pi parāmṛśyate upāsana antara vidhānāya
aparaḥ āha
sākṣāt eva gāyatrī śabdena brahma pratipādyate saṃkhyā sāmānyāt
yathā gāyatrī catuṣpadā ṣaḍakṣaraiḥ pādaiḥ tathā brahma catuṣpād
tathā anyatra api chandaḥ abhidhāyī śabdaḥ rtha antare saṃkhyā sāmānyāt prayujyamānaḥ dṛśyate
tat yathā te vai ete pañca anye pañca anye daśa santaḥ tat kṛtam iti upakramya āha sā eṣā virāj annādī iti
asmin pakṣe brahma eva abhihitam iti na chandaḥ abhidhānam
sarvathā api asti pūrvasmin vākye prakṛtam brahma iti
bhūta ādi pāda vyapadeśa upapatteḥ ca evam
itas ca evam abhyupagantavyam asti pūrvasmin vākye prakṛtam brahma iti
yatas bhūta ādīn pādān vyapadiśati śrutiḥ
bhūta pṛthivī śarīra hṛdayāni hi nirdiśya āha sā eṣā catuṣpadā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī iti
na hi brahma an āśrayaṇe kevalasya chandasaḥ bhūta ādayaḥ pādāḥ upapadyante
api ca brahma an āśrayaṇe na iyam ṛc saṃbadhyeta tāvān asya mahimā iti
anayā hi ṛcā sva rasena brahmā eva abhidhīyate pādaḥ u sya sarvā bhūtāni tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti sarva ātma tva upapatteḥ
puruṣasūkte pi iyam ṛc brahma para tayā eva samāmnāyate
smṛtiḥ ca brahmaṇaḥ evaṃrūpa tām darśayati viṣṭabhya aham idam kṛtsnam eka aṃśena sthitaḥ jagat iti
yat vai tat brahma iti ca nirdeśaḥ
evam sati mukhya arthaḥ upapadyate
te vai ete pañca brahma puruṣāḥ iti ca hṛdaya suṣiṣu brahma puruṣa śrutiḥ brahma saṃbandhi tāyām vivakṣitāyām saṃbhavati
tasmāt asti pūrvasmin vākye brahma prakṛtam
tat eva brahma jyotiḥ vākye dyu saṃbandhāt pratyabhijñāyamānam parāmṛśyate iti sthitam
upadeśa bhedāt na iti ced na ubhayasmin api avirodhāt
yat api etat uktam pūrvatra tripādasya amṛtam divi iti saptamyā dyauḥ ādhāra tvena upadiṣṭā
iha punar atha yat atas paras divaḥ iti pañcamyā maryādā tvena
tasmāt upadeśa bhedāt na tasya iha pratyabhijñānam asti iti tat parihartavyam
atrā ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ ubhayasmin api avirodhāt
ubhayasmin api saptamī ante pañcamī ante ca upadeśe na pratyabhijñānam virudhyate
yathā loke vṛkṣa agreṇa saṃbaddhaḥ u pi śyenaḥ ubhayathā upadiśyamānaḥ dṛśyate vṛkṣa agre śyenaḥ vṛkṣa agrāt paratas śyenaḥ iti ca evam divya eva sat brahma divaḥ param iti upadiśyate
aparaḥ āha yathā loke vṛkṣa agreṇa asaṃbaddhaḥ pi śyenaḥ ubhayathā upadiśyamānaḥ dṛśyate vṛkṣa agre śyenaḥ vṛkṣa agrāt paratas śyenaḥ iti ca evam divaḥ param api sat brahma divi iti upadiśyate
tasmāt asti pūrva nirdiṣṭasya brahmaṇaḥ iha pratyabhijñānam
atas param eva brahma jyotiḥ śabdam iti siddham
prāṇaḥ tathā anugamāt
prātardana adhikaraṇam
asti kauṣītakibrāhmaṇa upaniṣadi indrapratardana ākhyāyikā pratardanaḥ ha vai daivodāsiḥ indrasya priyam dhāma upajagāma yuddhena ca pauruṣeṇa ca iti ārabhya āmnātā
tasyām śrūyate sa ha uvāca prāṇaḥ smi prajñā ātmā tam mām āyuḥ amṛtam iti upāssva iti
tathā uttaratra api atha khalu prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti
tathā na vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt iti
ante ca saḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā ānandaḥ jaraḥ mṛtaḥ ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha prāṇa śabdena vāyu mātram abhidhīyate uta devatā ātmā uta jīvaḥ athavā param brahma iti
nanu atas eva prāṇaḥ iti atra varṇitam prāṇa śabdasya brahma para tvam
iha api ca brahma liṅgam asti ānandaḥ jaraḥ mṛtaḥ ityādi
katham iha punar saṃśayaḥ saṃbhavati
aneka liṅga darśanāt iti brūmaḥ
na kevalam iha brahma liṅgam eva upalabhyate
santi hi itara liṅgāni api mām eva vijānīhi iti indrasya vacanam devatā ātma liṅgam
idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti prāṇa liṅgam
na vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi jīva liṅgam
atas upapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ
tatra prasiddheḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti prāpte idam ucyate prāṇa śabdam brahma vijñeyam
kutas
tathā anugamāt
tathā hi paurvāparyeṇa paryālocyamāne vākye padānām samanvayaḥ brahma pratipādana paraḥ upalabhyate
upakrame tāvat varam vṛṇīṣva iti indreṇa uktaḥ pratardanaḥ paramam puruṣa artham varam upacikṣepa tvam eva me varam vṛṇīṣva yam tvam manuṣyāya hitatamam manyase iti
tasmai hitatama tvena upadiśyamānaḥ prāṇaḥ katham paramātmā na syāt
na hi anyatra paramātma vijñānāt hitatama prāptiḥ asti tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate yanāyaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
tathā sa yaḥ mām veda na ha vai tasya kenacana karmaṇā lokaḥ mīyate na steyena na bhrūṇahatyayā ityādi ca brahma parigrahe ghaṭate
brahma vijñānena hi sarva karma kṣayaḥ prasiddhaḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare ityādyāsu śrutiṣu
prajñā ātma tvam ca brahma pakṣe eva upapadyate
na hi acetanasya vāyoḥ prajñā ātma tvam saṃbhavati
tathā upasaṃhāre pi ānandaḥ jaraḥ mṛtaḥ iti ānanda tva ādīni ca na brahmaṇaḥ nyatra samyak saṃbhavanti
sa na sādhunā karmaṇā bhūyān bhavati na u eva a sādhunā karmaṇā kanīyān eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ unninīṣate
eṣaḥ u eva asādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ ninīṣate iti eṣa loka adhipatiḥ eṣa lokapālaḥ eṣa loka īśaḥ iti ca
sarvam etat parasmin brahmaṇi āśrīyamāṇe nugantum śakyate na mukhye prāṇe
tasmāt prāṇaḥ brahma
na vaktuḥ ātma upadeśāt iti ced adhyātma sambandha bhūmā hi asmin
yat uktam prāṇaḥ brahma iti tat ākṣipyate na param brahma prāṇa śabdam
kasmāt
vaktuḥ ātma upadeśāt
vaktā hi indraḥ nāma kaścid vigrahavān devatā viśeṣaḥ svam ātmānam pratardanāya ācacakṣe mām eva vijānīhi iti upakramya smi prajñā ātmā iti ahaṃkāra vādena
saḥ eva vaktuḥ ātma tvena upadiśyamānaḥ prāṇaḥ katham brahma syāt
na hi brahmaṇaḥ vaktṛ tvam saṃbhavati avāgamanāḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
tathā vigraha saṃbandhibhiḥ eva brahmaṇi asaṃbhavadbhiḥ dharmaiḥ indraḥ ātmānam tuṣṭāva triśīrṣāṇam tvāṣṭra mahana marut mukhāni atīn śālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyaccham iti evamādibhiḥ
prāṇa tvam ca indrasya balavat tvāt upapadyate
prāṇaḥ vai balam iti hi vijñāyate
balasya ca indraḥ devatā prasiddhā
yā ca kācid bala prakṛtiḥ indrasya karma eva tat iti hi vadanti
prajñā ātmatvam api apratihata jñāna tvāt devatā ātmanaḥ saṃbhavati
a pratihata jñānāḥ devatāḥ iti hi vadanti
niścite ca evam devatā ātma upadeśe hitatama tva ādi vacanāni yathāsaṃbhavam tad viṣayāṇi eva yojayitavyāni
tasmāt vaktuḥ indrasya ātma upadeśāt na prāṇaḥ brahma iti ākṣipya pratisamādhīyate adhyātma saṃbandha bhūmā hi asmin iti
adhyātma saṃbandhaḥ pratyagātma saṃbandhaḥ tasya bhūmā bāhulyam asmin adhyāye upalabhyate
yāvat hi asmin śarīre prāṇaḥ vasati tāvat āyuḥ iti prāṇasya eva prajñā ātmanaḥ pratyak bhūtasya āyuḥ pradāna upasaṃhārayoḥ svātantryam darśayati na devatā viśeṣasya parācīnasya
tathā astitve ca prāṇānām niḥśreyasam iti adhyātmam eva indriya āśrayam prāṇam darśayati
tathā prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti
na vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt iti ca upakramya tat yathā rathasya areṣu nemiḥ arpitā nābhau arāḥ arpitāḥ evam eva etāḥ bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsu arpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ prāṇe rpitāḥ saḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā ānandaḥ jaraḥ mṛtaḥ iti viṣaya indriya vyavahāra ara nābhi bhūtam pratyagātmānam eva upasaṃharati
sa me ātmā iti vidyāt iti ca upasaṃhāraḥ pratyagātma parigrahe sādhuḥ na parācīna parigrahe
ayam ātmā brahma sarva anubhūḥ iti ca śruti antaram
tasmāt adhyātma saṃbandha bāhulyāt brahma upadeśaḥ eva ayam na devatā ātma upadeśaḥ
katham tarhi vaktuḥ ātma upadeśaḥ
śāstra dṛṣṭyā tu upadeśaḥ vāmadeva vat
indraḥ nāma devatā ātmā svam ātmānam paramātma tvena aham eva param brahma iti ārṣeṇa darśanena yathāśāstram paśyan upadiśati sma mām eva vijānīhi iti
yathā tat ha etat paśyan ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede ham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti tadvat
tat yaḥ yaḥ devānām pratyabudhyata saḥ eva tat abhavat iti śruteḥ
yat punar uktam mām eva vijānīhi iti uktvā vigraha carmaiḥ indraḥ svam ātmānam tuṣṭāva tvāṣṭra vadha ādibhiḥ iti tat parihartavyam
atrā ucyate na tāvat tvāṣṭra vadha ādīnām vijñeya indra stuti artha tvena upanyāsaḥ yasmāt evaṃkarmā aham tasmāt mām vijānīhi iti
katham tarhi
vijñāna stuti artha tvena
yatkāraṇam tvāṣṭra vadha ādīni sāhasāni upanyasya pareṇa vijñāna stutim anusaṃdadhāti tasya me tatra loma ca na mīyate sa yaḥ mām veda na ha vai tasya kena ca karmaṇā loke mīyate ityādinā
etat uktam bhavati yasmāt īdṛśāni api krūrāṇi karmāṇi kṛtavataḥ mama brahma bhūtasya loma api na hiṃsyate sa yaḥ mām veda na tasya kenacid api karmaṇā lokaḥ hiṃsyate iti
vijñeyam tu brahma eva prāṇaḥ smi prajñā ātmā iti vakṣyamāṇam
tasmāt brahma vākyam etat
jīva mukhya prāṇa liṅgāt na iti ced na upāsā traividhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt
yadi api adhyātma saṃbandha bhūma darśanāt na parācīnasya devatā ātmanaḥ upadeśaḥ tathā api na brahma vākyam bhavitum arhati
kutas
jīva liṅgāt mukhya prāṇa liṅgāt ca
jīvasya tāvat asmin vākye vispaṣṭam liṅgam upalabhyate na vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi
atra hi vāc ādibhiḥ karaṇaiḥ vyāpṛtasya kārya karaṇa adhyakṣasya jīvasya vijñeya tvam abhidhīyate
tathā mukhya prāṇa liṅgam api atha khalu prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti
śarīra dhāraṇam ca mukhya prāṇasya dharmaḥ
prāṇa saṃvāde vāc ādīn prāṇān prakṛtya tān variṣṭhaḥ prāṇaḥ uvāca mā moham āpat yathā aham eva etat pañcadhā ātmānam pravibhajya etat bāṇam avaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi iti śravaṇāt
ye tu imam śarīram parigṛhya iti paṭhanti teṣām imam jīvam indriya grāmam vā parigṛhya śarīram utthāpayati iti vyākhyeyam
prajñā ātma tvam api jīve tāvat cetana tvāt upapannam
mukhye pi prāṇe prajñā sādhana prāṇa antara āśraya tvāt upapannam eva
evam jīva mukhya prāṇa parigrahe ca prāṇa prajñā ātmanoḥ saha vṛtti tvena abheda nirdeśaḥ svarūpeṇa ca iti ubhayathā api nirdeśaḥ upapadyate yaḥ vai prāṇaḥ sā prajñā yā vai prajñā sa prāṇaḥ saha hi etau asmin śarīre vasataḥ saha utkrāmataḥ iti
brahma parigrahe tu kim kasmāt bhidyeta
tasmāt iha jīva mukhya prāṇayoḥ anyataraḥ ubhau vā pratīyeyātām na brahma iti ced na etat evam
upāsā traividhyāt
evam sati trividham upāsanam prasajyeta jīva upāsanam mukhya prāṇa upāsanam brahma upāsanam ca iti
na ca etat ekasmin vākye bhyupagantum yuktam
upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām hi vākya eka vākya tvam avagamyate
mām eva vijānīhi iti upakramya prāṇaḥ smi prajñā ātmā tam mām āyuḥ amṛtam iti upāssva iti uktvā ante saḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā ānandaḥ jaraḥ mṛtaḥ iti eka rūpau upakrama upasaṃhārau dṛśyete
tatra artha ekatvam yuktam āśrayitum
na ca brahma liṅgam anya paratvena pariṇetum śakyam
daśānām bhūtamātrāṇām prajñāmātrāṇām ca brahmaṇaḥ nyatra arpaṇa anupapatteḥ
āśrita tvāt ca anyatra api brahma liṅga vaśāt prāṇa śabdasya brahmaṇi pravṛtteḥ iha api ca hitatama upanyāsa ādi brahma liṅga yogāt brahma upadeśaḥ eva ayam iti gamyate
yat tu mukhya prāṇa liṅgam darśitam idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti tat asat
prāṇa vyāpārasya api paramātma āyatta tvāt paramātmani upacaritum śakya tvāt na prāṇena nā apānena martyaḥ jīvati kaścana
itareṇa tu jīvanti yasmin etau upāśritau iti śruteḥ
yat api na vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi jīva liṅgam darśitam tat api na brahma pakṣam nivārayati
na hi jīvaḥ nāma atyanta bhinnaḥ brahmaṇaḥ tattvam asi aham brahma asmi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
buddhi ādi upādhi kṛtam tu viśeṣam āśritya brahma eva san jīvaḥ kartā bhoktā ca iti ucyate
tasya upādhi kṛta viśeṣa parityāgena sva rūpam brahma darśayitum na vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādinā pratyagātma abhimukhīkaraṇa arthaḥ upadeśaḥ na virudhyate
yat vācā an abhyuditam yena vāc abhyudyate
tat eva brahma tvam viddhi na idam yat idam upāsate ityādi ca śruti antaram vacana ādi kriyā vyāpṛtasya eva ātmanaḥ brahmatvam darśayati
yat punar etat uktam saha hi etau asmin śarīre vasataḥ saha utkrāmataḥ iti prāṇa prajñā ātmanoḥ bheda darśanam brahma vādinaḥ na upapadyate iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
jñāna kriyā śakti dvaya āśrayayoḥ buddhi prāṇayoḥ pratyagātma upādhi bhūtayoḥ bheda nirdeśa upapatteḥ
upādhi dvaya upahitasya tu pratyagātmanaḥ svarūpeṇa abhedaḥ iti atas prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā iti ekīkaraṇam aviruddham
athavā na upāsā traividhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt iti asya ayam anyaḥ rthaḥ na brahma vākye jīva mukhya prāṇa liṅgam virudhyate
katham
upāsā traividhyāt
trividham iha brahmaṇaḥ upāsanam vivakṣitam prāṇa dharmeṇa prajñā dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ca
tatra āyuḥ amṛtam iti upāssva āyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti tasmāt etat eva uktham upāsīta iti ca prāṇa dharmaḥ
atha yathā asyai prajñāyai sarvāṇi bhūtāni ekībhavanti tat vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti upakramya vāc eva asyāḥ ekam aṅgam adūduhat tasyai nāma parastāt prativihitā bhūtamātrā prajñayā vācam samāruhya vācā sarvāṇi nāmāni āpnoti iti ādiḥ prajñā dharmaḥ
tāḥ vai etāḥ daśa eva bhūtamātrāḥ adhiprajñam daśa prajñāmātrāḥ adhibhūtam
yadi bhūtamātrāḥ na syuḥ na prajñāmātrāḥ syuḥ
yadi prajñāmātrāḥ na syuḥ na bhūtamātrāḥ syuḥ
na hi anyataratas rūpam kiṃcana sidhyet
na u etat nānā
tat yathā rathasya areṣu nemiḥ arpitā nābhau arāḥ arpitāḥ evam eva etāḥ bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsu arpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ prāṇe rpitāḥ saḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ eva prajñā ātmā iti ādiḥ brahma dharmaḥ
tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ eva etat upādhi dvaya dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ca ekam upāsanam trividham vivakṣitam
anyatra api manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ ityādau upādhi dharmeṇa brahmaṇaḥ upāsanam āśritam
iha api tat yujyate vākyasya upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām eka artha tva avagamāt prāṇa prajñā ātma brahma liṅga avagamāt ca
tasmāt brahma vākyam eva etat iti siddham
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ

prathamaḥ dhyāyaḥ
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ
sarvatra prasiddha upadeśāt
sarvatraprasiddhi adhikaraṇam
idam āmnāyate sarvam khalu idam brahma tat jalān iti śāntaḥ upāsīta
atha khalu kratu mayaḥ puruṣaḥ yathā kratuḥ asimant loke puruṣaḥ bhavati tathā itas pretya bhavati sa kratum kurvīta manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha manaḥ maya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ śārīraḥ ātmā upāsya tvena upadiśyate āhosvit param brahma iti
kim tāvat prāptam
śārīre iti
kutas
tasya hi kārya karaṇa adhipateḥ prasiddhaḥ manaḥ ādibhiḥ saṃbandhaḥ na parasya brahmaṇaḥ
aprāṇaḥ hi amanāḥ śubhraḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
nanu sarvam khalu idam brahma iti sva śabdena eva brahma upāttam
katham iha śārīraḥ ātmā upāsya tvena āśaṅkyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ
na idam vākyam brahma upāsana vidhi param
kim tarhi
śama vidhi param
yatkāraṇam sarvam khalu idam brahma tat jalān iti śāntaḥ upāsīta iti āha
etat uktam bhavati yasmāt sarvam idam vikāra jātam brahmā eva tad ja tvāt tad la tvāt tad anatvāt ca na ca sarvasya eka ātma tve rāga ādayaḥ saṃbhavanti tasmāt śāntaḥ upāsīta iti
na ca śama vidhi para tve sati anena vākyena brahma upāsanam niyantum śakyate
upāsanam tu sa kratum kurvīta iti anena vidhīyate
kratuḥ saṃkalpaḥ dhyānam iti arthaḥ
tasya ca viṣaya tvena śrūyate manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti jīva liṅgam
atas brūmaḥ jīva viṣayam etat upāsanam iti
sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ ityādi api śrūyamāṇam paryāyeṇa jīva viṣayam upapadyate
eṣa me ātmā antar hṛdaye ṇīyān vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā iti ca hṛdaya āyatana tvam aṇīyaḥ tvam cāra agra mātrasya jīvasya avakalpate na aparicchinnasya brahmaṇaḥ
nanu jyāyān pṛthivyāḥ ityādi api na paricchinne iti
atra brūmaḥ na tāvat aṇīyaḥ tvam jyāyaḥ tvam ca ubhayam ekasmin samāśrayitum śakyam virodhāt
anyatara āśrayaṇe ca prathama śruta tvāt aṇīyaḥ tvam yuktam āśrayitum
jyāyaḥ tvam tu brahma bhāva apekṣayā bhaviṣyati iti
niścite ca jīva viṣaya tve yat ante brahma saṃkīrtanam etat brahma iti tat api prakṛta parāmarśa ārtha tvāt jīva viṣayam eva
tasmāt manaḥ maya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ jīvaḥ upāsyaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ param eva brahma iha manaḥ maya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ upāsyam
kutas
sarvatra prasiddha upadeśāt
yat sarveṣu vedānteṣu prasiddham brahma śabdasya ālambanam jagat kāraṇam iha ca sarvam khalu idam brahma iti vākya upakrame śrutam tat eva manaḥ maya tva ādi dharmaiḥ viśiṣṭam upadiśyate iti yuktam
evam ca sati prakṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriye na bhaviṣyataḥ
nanu vākya upakrame śama vidhi vivakṣayā brahma nirdiṣṭam na sva vivakṣayā iti uktam
atrā ucyate yadi api śama vidhi vivakṣayā brahma nirdiṣṭam tathā api manaḥ maya tva ādiṣu upadiśyamāneṣu tat eva brahma saṃnihitam bhavati jīvaḥ tu na saṃnihitaḥ na ca sva śabdena upāttaḥ iti vaiṣamyam
vivakṣita guṇa upapatteḥ ca
vaktum iṣṭāḥ vivakṣitāḥ
yadi api apauruṣeye vede vaktuḥ abhāvāt na icchā arthaḥ saṃbhavati tathā api upādānena phalena upacaryate
loke pi yat śabda abhihitam upādeyam bhavati tat vivakṣitam iti ucyate yat anupādeyam tat avivakṣitam iti
tadvat vede pi upādeya tvena abhihitam vivakṣitam bhavati itarat avivakṣitam
upādāna anupādāne tu veda vākya tātparya a tātparyābhyām avagamyete
tat iha ye vivakṣitāḥ guṇāḥ upāsanāyām upādeya tvena upadiṣṭāḥ satya saṃkalpa prabhṛtayaḥ te parasmin brahmaṇi upapadyante
satya saṃkalpa tvam hi sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhāreṣu apratibaddha śakti tvāt paramātmanaḥ eva avakalpate
paramātma guṇa tvena ca yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti atra satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti śrutam ākāśa ātmā iti ca
ākāśa vat ātmā asya iti arthaḥ
sarvagata tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ saṃbhavati ākāśena sāmyam brahmaṇaḥ
jyāyān pṛthivyāḥ ityādinā ca etat eva darśayati
yat api ākāśaḥ ātmā asya iti vyākhyāyate tat api saṃbhavati sarva jagat kāraṇasya sarva ātmanaḥ brahmaṇaḥ ākāśa ātma tvam
atas eva sarva karmā ityādi
evam iha upāsya tayā vivakṣitāḥ guṇāḥ brahmaṇi upapadyante
yat tu uktam manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti jīva liṅgam na tat brahmaṇi upapadyate iti
tat api brahmaṇi upapadyate iti brūmaḥ
sarva ātma tvāt hi brahmaṇaḥ jīva saṃbandhīni manaḥ maya tva ādīni brahma saṃbandhīni bhavanti
tathā ca brahma viṣaye śruti smṛtī bhavataḥ tvam strī tvam pumān asi tvam kumāraḥ uta vā kumārī
tvam jīrṇaḥ daṇḍena vañcasi tvam jātaḥ bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ iti
sarvatas pāṇi pādam tat sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham
sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati iti ca
aprāṇaḥ hi amanāḥ śubhraḥ iti śrutiḥ śuddha brahma viṣayā iyam tu śrutiḥ manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti saguṇa brahma viṣayā iti viśeṣaḥ
atas vivakṣita guṇa upapatteḥ param eva brahma iha upāsya tvena upadiṣṭam iti gamyate
anupapatteḥ tu na śārīraḥ
pūrveṇa sūtreṇa brahmaṇi vivakṣitānām guṇānām upapattiḥ uktā
anena śārīre teṣām anupapattiḥ ucyate
tu śabdaḥ vadhāraṇa arthaḥ
brahma eva uktena nyāyena manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇam
na tu śārīraḥ jīvaḥ manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇaḥ
yatkāraṇam satya saṃkalpaḥ ākāśa ātmā avākī anādaraḥ jyāyān pṛthivyāḥ iti ca evaṃjātīyakāḥ guṇāḥ na śārīre āñjasyena upapadyante
śārīre iti śarīre bhavaḥ iti arthaḥ
nanu īśvaraḥ pi śarīre bhavati
satyam śarīre bhavati
na tu śarīre eva bhavati
jyāyān pṛthivyāḥ jyāyān antarikṣāt ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ iti ca vyāpi tva śravaṇāt
jīvaḥ tu śarīre eva bhavati tasya bhoga adhiṣṭhānāt śarīrāt anyatra vṛtti abhāvāt
karma kartṛ vyapadeśāt ca
itas ca na śārīraḥ manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇaḥ
yasmāt karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ bhavati etam itas pretya abhisaṃbhavitāsmi iti
etam iti prakṛtam manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇam upāsyam ātmānam karma tvena prāpya tvena vyapadiśati
abhisaṃbhavitāsmi iti śārīram upāsakam kartṛ tvena prāpaka tvena
abhisaṃbhavitāsmi iti prāptā asmi iti arthaḥ
na ca satyām gatau ekasya karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ yuktaḥ
tathā upāsya upāsaka bhāvaḥ pi bheda adhiṣṭhānaḥ eva
tasmāt api na śārīraḥ manaḥ maya tva ādi viśiṣṭaḥ
śabda viśeṣāt
itas ca śārīrāt anyaḥ manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇaḥ
yasmāt śabda viśeṣaḥ bhavati samāna prakaraṇe śruti antare yathā vrīhiḥ vā yavaḥ vā śyāmākaḥ vā śyāmāka taṇḍulaḥ vā evam ayam antarātman puruṣaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ iti
śārīrasya ātmanaḥ yaḥ śabdaḥ bhidhāyakaḥ saptamī antaḥ antarātman iti
tasmāt viśiṣṭaḥ nyaḥ prathama antaḥ puruṣa śabdaḥ manaḥ maya tva ādi viśiṣṭasya ātmanaḥ bhidhāyakaḥ
tasmāt tayoḥ bhedaḥ dhigamyate
smṛteḥ ca
smṛtiḥ ca śārīra paramātmanoḥ bhedam darśayati īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe rjuna tiṣṭhati
bhrāmayan sarva bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā ityādyā
atra āha kaḥ punar ayam śārīraḥ nāma paramātmanaḥ nyaḥ yaḥ pratiṣidhyate anupapatteḥ tu na śārīraḥ ityādinā
śrutiḥ tu sti draṣṭā na anyaḥ taḥ sti śrotā iti evaṃjātīyakā paramātmanaḥ vārayati
tathā smṛtiḥ api kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi sarva kṣetreṣu bhārata iti evaṃjātīyakā iti
atra ucyate satyam eva etat paraḥ eva ātmā deha indriya manaḥ buddhi upādhibhiḥ paricchidyamānaḥ bālaiḥ śārīraḥ iti upacaryate
yathā ghaṭa karaka ādi upādhi vaśāt aparicchinnam api nabhaḥ paricchinna vat avabhāsate tadvat
tad apekṣayā ca karma kartṛ tva ādi bheda vyavahāraḥ na virudhyate prāk tat tvam asi iti ātma ekatva upadeśa grahaṇāt
gṛhīte tu ātma ekatve bandha mokṣa ādi sarva vyavahāra parisamāptiḥ eva syāt
arbhaka okaḥ tvāt tad vyapadeśāt ca na iti ced na nicāyya tvāt evam vyoma vat ca
arbhakam alpam okaḥ nīḍam eṣa me ātmā antar hṛdaye iti paricchinna āyatana tvāt sva śabdena ca aṇīyān vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā iti aṇīyaḥ tva vyapadeśāt śārīraḥ eva ara agra mātraḥ jīvaḥ iha upadiśyate na sarva gataḥ paramātmā iti yat uktam tat parihartavyam
atra ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ
na tāvat paricchinna deśasya sarvagata tva vyapadeśaḥ katham api upapadyate
sarvagatasya tu sarva deśeṣu vidyamāna tvāt paricchinna deśa vyapadeśaḥ u pi kayācid apekṣayā saṃbhavati
yathā samasta vasudhā adhipatiḥ api hi san ayodhyā adhipatiḥ iti vyapadiśyate
kayā punar apekṣayā sarva gataḥ san īśvaraḥ aṇīyān ca vyapadiśyate iti
nicāyya tvāt evam iti brūmaḥ
evam aṇīyaḥ tva ādi guṇa gaṇa upetaḥ īśvaraḥ tatra hṛdaya puṇḍarīke nicāyyaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ upadiśyate
yathā sālagrāme hariḥ
tatra asya buddhi vijñānam grāhakam
sarva gataḥ pi īśvaraḥ tatra upāsyamānaḥ prasīdati
vyoma vat ca etat draṣṭavyam
yathā sarva gatam api sat vyoma sūcī pāśa ādi apekṣayā arbhakaukaḥ ṇīyaḥ ca iti vyapadiśyate evam brahmā api
tat evam nicāyya tva apekṣam brahmaṇaḥ ṛbhaka okaḥ tvam aṇīyaḥ tvam ca na pāramārthikam
tatra yat āśaṅkyate hṛdaya āyatana tvāt brahmaṇaḥ hṛdayānām ca pratiśarīram bhinna tvāt bhinna āyatanānām ca śuka ādīnām aneka tva sāvayava tva anitya tva ādi doṣa darśanāt brahmaṇaḥ u pi tadvat prasaṅgaḥ iti tat api parihṛtam bhavati
sambhoga prāptiḥ iti ced na vaiśeṣyāt
vyoma vat sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ sarva prāṇi hṛdaya saṃbandhāt cit rūpa tayā ca śārīrāt a viśiṣṭa tvāt sukha duḥkha ādi saṃbhogaḥ
api a viśiṣṭaḥ prasajyeta
eka tvāt ca na hi parasmāt ātmanaḥ
anyaḥ kaścid ātmā saṃsārī vidyate
a taḥ
asti vijñātā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
tasmāt parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhoga prāptiḥ iti ced na
vaiśeṣyāt
na tāvat sarva prāṇi hṛdaya saṃbandhāt cit rūpa tayā ca śārīra vat brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhoga prasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt
viśeṣaḥ hi bhavati śārīra parameśvarayoḥ
ekaḥ kartā bhoktā dharma adharma ādi sādhanaḥ sukha duḥkha ādimān ca
ekaḥ tad viparītaḥ
apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ
etasmāt anayoḥ viśeṣāt ekasya bhogaḥ na itarasya
yadi ca saṃnidhāna mātreṇa vastu śaktim an āśritya kārya saṃbandhaḥ
abhyupagamyeta ākāśa ādīnām api dāha ādi prasaṅgaḥ
sarvagata aneka ātma vādinām api samau etau codya parihārau
yat api eka tvāt brahmaṇaḥ ātma antara abhāvāt śārīrasya bhogena brahmaṇaḥ bhoga prasaṅgaḥ iti atra vadāmaḥ idam tāvat devānām priyaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ katham ayam tvayā ātma antara abhāvaḥ
adhyavasitaḥ iti
tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi na anyaḥ
a taḥ
asti vijñātā ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ iti ced yathāśāstram tarhi śāstrīyaḥ rthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ na tatra ardhajaratīyam labhyam
śāstram ca tat tvam asi iti apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇam brahma śārīrasya ātmatvena upadiśat śārīrasya eva tāvat upabhoktṛ tvam vārayati
kutas tad upabhogena brahmaṇaḥ upabhoga prasaṅgaḥ
atha a gṛhītam śārīrasya brahmaṇā ekatvam tadā mithyājñāna nimittaḥ śārīrasya upabhogaḥ
na tena paramārtha rūpasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsparśaḥ
na hi bālaiḥ tala malina tā ādibhiḥ vyomni vikalpyamāne tala malina tā ādi viśiṣṭam eva paramārthataḥ vyoma bhavati
tat āha na vaiśeṣyāt iti
na eka tve pi śārīrasya upabhogena brahmaṇaḥ upabhoga prasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt
viśeṣaḥ hi bhavati mithyājñāna samyak jñānayoḥ
mithyā jñāna kalpitaḥ upabhogaḥ samyak jñāna dṛṣṭam ekatvam
na ca mithyājñāna kalpitena upabhogena samyak jñāna dṛṣṭam vastu saṃspṛśyate
tasmāt na upabhoga gandhaḥ śakyaḥ īśvarasya kalpayitum
attā cara acara grahaṇāt
attṛ adhikaraṇam
kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate yasya brahma ca kṣatram ca ubhe bhavataḥ odanaḥ
mṛtyuḥ yasya upasecanam kaḥ itthā veda yatra saḥ iti
atra kaścid odana upasecana sūcitā u ttā pratīyate
tatra kim agniḥ attā syāt uta jīvaḥ athavā paramātmā iti saṃśayaḥ
viśeṣa an avadhāraṇāt trayāṇām ca agni jīva paramātmanām asmin granthe praśna upanyāsa upalabdheḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
agniḥ attā iti
kutas
agniḥ anna ādaḥ iti śruti prasiddhibhyām
jīvaḥ vai attā syāt tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti darśanāt
na paramātmā an aścan anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti darśanāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ attā atra paramātmā bhavitum arhati
kutas
cara acara grahaṇāt
carācaram hi sthāvara jaṅgamam mṛtyu upasecanam iha ādya tvena pratīyate
tādṛśasya ca ādyasya na paramātmanaḥ nyaḥ kārtsnyena attā saṃbhavati
paramātmā tu vikāra jātam upasaṃharan sarvam atti iti upapadyate
nanu iha carācara grahaṇam na upalabhyate
katham siddha vat carācara grahaṇam hetu tvena upādīyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ mṛtyu upasecana tvena iha ādya tvena sarvasya prāṇi nikāyasya pratīyamāna tvāt brahma kṣatrayoḥ ca prādhānyāt pradarśana artha tva upapatteḥ
yat tu paramātmanaḥ api na attṛ tvam saṃbhavati an aśnan anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti darśanāt iti atra ucyate karma phala bhogasya pratiṣedhakam etat darśanam tasya saṃnihita tvāt
na vikāra saṃhārasya pratiṣedhakam sarva vedānteṣu sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhāra kāraṇa tvena brahmaṇaḥ prasiddha tvāt
tasmāt paramātmā eva iha attā bhavitum arhati
prakaraṇāt ca
itas ca paramātmā eva iha attā bhavitum arhati
yatkāraṇam prakaraṇam idam paramātmanaḥ na jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi
prakṛta grahaṇam ca nyāyyam
kaḥ itthā veda yatra saḥ iti ca durvijñāna tvam paramātma liṅgam
guhām praviṣṭau ātmānau hi tad darśanāt
guhā praviṣṭa adhikaraṇam
kaṭha vallīṣu eva paṭhyate ṛtam pibantau sukṛtasya loke guhām praviṣṭau parame para ardhe
chāyā ātapau brahma vidaḥ vadanti pañca agnayaḥ ye ca triṇāciketāḥ
iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha buddhi jīvau nirdiṣṭau uta jīva paramātmānām iti
yadi buddhi jīvau tatas buddhi pradhānāt kārya karaṇa saṃghātāt vilakṣaṇaḥ jīvaḥ pratipāditaḥ bhavati
tat api iha pratipādayitavyam yā iyam prete vicikisā manuṣye sti iti eke na ayam asti iti ca eke
etad vidyām anuśiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti pṛṣṭa tvāt
atha jīva paramātmānau tatas jīvāt vilakṣaṇaḥ paramātmā pratipāditaḥ bhavati
tat api iha pratipādayitavyam anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt anyatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt
anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yat tat paśyasi tat vada iti pṛṣṭa tvāt
atra āha ākṣeptā ubhau api etau pakṣau na saṃbhavataḥ
kasmāt
ṛta pānam hi karma phala upabhogaḥ sukṛtasya loke iti liṅgāt
tat ca cetanasya kṣetrajñasya saṃbhavati na acetanāyāḥ buddheḥ
pibantau iti dvivacanena dvayoḥ pānam darśayati śrutiḥ
atas buddhi kṣetrajña pakṣaḥ tāvat na saṃbhavati
atas eva kṣetrajña paramātma pakṣaḥ pi na saṃbhavati
cetane pi paramātmani ṛta pāna asaṃbhavāt an aśnan anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti mantra varṇāt iti
atrā ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ
chatriṇaḥ gacchanti iti ekena api chatriṇā bahūnām a chatriṇām chatri tva upacāra darśanāt
evam ekena api pibatā dvau pibantau ucyeyātām
yat vā jīvaḥ tāvat pibati
īśvaraḥ tu pāyayati
pāyayan api pibati iti ucyate pācayitari api paktṛ tva prasiddhi darśanāt
buddhi kṣetrajña parigrahaḥ pi saṃbhavati
karaṇe kartṛ tva upacārāt edhāṃsi pacanti iti prayoga darśanāt
na ca adhyātma adhikāre nyau kaucid dvau ṛtam pibantau saṃbhavataḥ
tasmāt buddhi jīvau syātām jīva paramātmānau vā iti saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
buddhi kṣetrajñau iti
kutas
guhām praviṣṭau iti viśeṣaṇāt
yadi śarīram guhā yadi vā hṛdayam ubhayathā api buddhi kṣetrajñau guhām praviṣṭau upapadyete
na ca sati saṃbhave sarvagatasya brahmaṇaḥ viśiṣṭa deśa tvam yuktam kalpayitum
sukṛtasya loke iti ca karma gocara anatikramam darśayati
paramātmā tu na sukṛtasya vā duṣkṛtasya vā gocare vartate na karmaṇā vardhate na u kanīyān iti śruteḥ
chāyā ātapau iti ca cetana acetanayoḥ nirdeśaḥ upapadyate chāyā ātapa vat paraspara vilakṣaṇa tvāt
tasmāt buddhi kṣetrajñau iha ucyeyātām iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vijñāna ātma paramātmānau iha ucyeyātām
kasmāt
ātmānau hi tau ubhau api cetanau samāna svabhāvau
saṃkhyā śravaṇe ca samāna svabhāveṣu eva loke pratītiḥ dṛśyate
asya goḥ dvitīyaḥ nveṣṭavyaḥ iti ukte gauḥ eva dvitīyaḥ nviṣyate na aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ vā
tat iha ṛta pānena liṅgena niścite vijñāna ātmani dvitīya anveṣaṇāyām samāna svabhāvaḥ cetanaḥ paramātmā eva pratīyate
nanu uktam guhā hita tva darśanāt na paramātmā pratyetavyaḥ iti
guhā hita tva darśanāt eva paramātmā pratyetavyaḥ iti vadāmaḥ
guhā hita tvam tu śruti smṛtiṣu asakṛt paramātmanaḥ eva dṛśyate guhā hitam gahvareṣṭham purāṇam yaḥ veda nihitam guhāyām parame vyoman ātmānam anviccha guhām praviṣṭam ityādyāsu
sarva gatasya api brahmaṇaḥ upalabdhi arthaḥ deśa viśeṣa upadeśaḥ na virudhyate iti etat api uktam eva
sukṛta loka varti tvam tu chatri tva vat ekasmin api vartamānam ubhayoḥ aviruddham
chāyā ātapau iti api a viruddham
chāyā ātapa vat paraspara vilakṣaṇa tvāt saṃsāri tva asaṃsāri tvayoḥ avidyā kṛta tvāt saṃsāri tvasya pāramārthika tvāt ca asaṃsāri tvasya
tasmāt vijñāna ātma paramātmānau guhām praviṣṭau gṛhyete
kutas ca vijñāna ātma paramātmānau gṛhyete
viśeṣaṇāt ca
viśeṣaṇam ca vijñāna ātma paramātmanoḥ eva bhavati
ātmānam rathinam viddhi śarīram ratham eva tu ityādinā pareṇa granthena rathi ratha ādi rūpaka kalpanayā vijñāna ātmānam rathinam saṃsāra mokṣayoḥ gantāram kalpayati
saḥ dhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti paramātmānam gantavyam kalpayati
tathā tam durdarśam gūḍham anupraviṣṭam guhā hitam gahvareṣṭham purāṇam
adhyātma yoga adhigamena devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti iti pūrvasmin api granthe mantṛ mantavya tvena etau eva viśeṣitau
prakaraṇam ca idam paramātmanaḥ
brahma vidaḥ vadanti
iti ca vaktṛ viśeṣa upādānam paramātma parigrahe ghaṭate
tasmāt iha jīva paramātmānau ucyeyātām
eṣaḥ eva nyāyaḥ dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā iti evamādiṣu api
tatra api hi adhyātma adhikārāt na prākṛtau suparṇau ucyete
tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti adana liṅgāt vijñāna ātmā bhavati
an aścan anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti anaśana cetana tvābhyām paramātmā
anantare ca mantre tau eva draṣṭṛ draṣṭavya bhāvena viśinaṣṭi samāne vṛkṣe puruṣaḥ nimagnaḥ nīśayā śocati muhyamānaḥ
juṣṭam yadā paśyati anyam īśam asya mahimānam iti vīta śokaḥ iti
aparaḥ āha dvā suparṇāḥ iti neya mṛgasya adhikaraṇasya siddhāntam bhajate paiṅgi rahasya brāhmaṇena anyathā vyākhyāta tvāt tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti sattvam anaḥ can anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti anaḥ can anyaḥ bhipaśyati jñaḥ tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau iti
sattva śabdaḥ jīvaḥ kṣetrajña śabdaḥ paramātmā iti yat ucyate tat na
sattva kṣetrajña śabdayoḥ antaḥkaraṇa śārīra para tayā prasiddha tvāt
tatra eva ca vyākhyāta tvāt tat etat sattvam yena svapnam paśyati atha yaḥ yam śārīraḥ upadraṣṭā sa kṣetrajñaḥ tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau iti
na api asya adhikaraṇasya pūrvapakṣa bhāvam bhajate
na hi atra śārīraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva ādinā saṃsāra dharmeṇa upetaḥ vivakṣyate
katham tarhi
sarva saṃsāra dharma atītaḥ brahma svabhāvaḥ caitanya mātra svarūpaḥ
anaścan anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti anaścan anyaḥ bhipaśyati jñaḥ iti vacanāt tat tvam asi kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi ityādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ ca
tāvatā ca vidyā upasaṃhāra darśanam evam eva avakalpate tau etau sattva kṣetrajñau na ha vai evaṃvidi kiṃcana rajaḥ ādhvaṃsate ityādi
katham punar asmin pakṣe tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti sattvam iti acetane sattve bhoktṛ tva vacanam iti ucyate na iyam śrutiḥ acetanasya sattvasya bhoktṛ tvam vakṣyāmi iti pravṛttā
kim tarhi
cetanasya kṣetrajñasya abhoktṛ tvam brahma svabhāvatām ca vakṣyāmi iti
tad artham sukha duḥkha ādi vikriyāvati sattve bhoktṛtvam adhyāropayati
idam hi kartṛ tvam bhoktṛ tvam ca sattva kṣetrajñayoḥ itaretara svabhāva aviveka kṛtam kalpyate
paramārthataḥ tu na anyatarasya api saṃbhavati acetana tvāt sattvasya avikriya tvāt ca kṣetrajñasya
avidyā pratyupasthāpita svabhāva tvāt ca sattvasya sutarām na saṃbhavati
tathā ca śrutiḥ yatra vai anyat iva syāt tatra anyaḥ nyat paśyet ityādinā svapna dṛṣṭa hasti ādi vyavahāra vat avidyā viṣayaḥ eva kartṛ tva ādi vyavahāram darśayati
yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet ityādinā ca vivekinaḥ kartṛ tva ādi vyavahāram nivārayati
antare upapatteḥ
antara adhikaraṇam
yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate eṣaḥ ātmā iti ha uvāca etat amṛtam abhayam etat brahma iti
tat yadi api asmin sarpiḥ vā udakam vā siñcati vartmanī eva gacchati ityādi śrūyate
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ayam pratibimba ātmā akṣi adhikaraṇaḥ nirdiśyate atha vijñāna ātmā uta devatā ātmā indriyasya adhiṣṭhātā athavā īśvaraḥ iti
kim tāvat prāptam
chāyā ātmā puruṣa pratirūpaḥ iti
kutas
tasya dṛśyamāna tva prasiddheḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti ca prasiddha vat upadeśāt
vijñāna ātmanaḥ vā ayam nirdeśaḥ iti yuktam
sa hi cakṣuṣā rūpam paśyan cakṣuṣi saṃnihitaḥ bhavati
ātma śabdaḥ ca asmin pakṣe nukūlaḥ bhavati
āditya puruṣaḥ vā cakṣuṣaḥ nugrāhakaḥ pratīyate raśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ smin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti śruteḥ amṛta tva ādīnām ca devatā ātmani api kathaṃcid saṃbhavāt
na īśvaraḥ sthāna viśeṣa nirdeśāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva akṣiṇi abhyantaraḥ puruṣaḥ iha upadiṣṭaḥ iti
kasmāt
upapatteḥ
upapadyate hi parameśvare guṇa jātam iha upadiśyamānam
ātmatvam tāvat mukhyayā vṛttyā parameśvare upapadyate saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti śruteḥ
amṛta tva abhaya tve ca tasmin asakṛt śrūyete
tathā parameśvara anurūpam etat akṣi sthānam
yathā hi parameśvaraḥ sarva doṣaiḥ aliptaḥ apahata pāpma tva ādi śravaṇāt
tathā akṣi sthānam sarva lepa rahitam upadiṣṭam tat yadi api asmin sarpiḥ vā udakam vā siñcati vartmanī eva gacchati iti śruteḥ
saṃyat vāma tva ādi guṇa upadeśaḥ ca tasmin avakalpate
etam saṃyat vāmaḥ iti ācakṣate
etam hi sarvāṇi vāmāni abhisaṃyanti eṣaḥ u eva vāmanīḥ eṣa hi sarvāṇi vāmāni nayati
eṣaḥ u eva bhāmanīḥ eṣa hi sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti iti ca
atas upapatteḥ antaraḥ parameśvaraḥ
sthāna ādi vyapadeśāt ca
katham punar ākāśa vat sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ
akṣi alpam sthānam upapadyate iti atra ucyate bhavet eṣā anavakḷptiḥ yadi etat eva ekam sthānam asya nirdiṣṭam bhavet
santi hi anyāni api pṛthivī ādīni sthānāni asya nirdiṣṭāni yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan ityādinā
teṣu hi cakṣuḥ api nirdiṣṭam yaḥ cakṣuṣi tiṣṭhan iti
sthāna ādi vyapadeśāt iti ādi grahaṇena etat darśayati na kevalam sthānam eva ekam anucitam brahmaṇaḥ nirdiśyate
kim tarhi nāma rūpam iti evaṃjātīyakam api anāma rūpasya brahmaṇaḥ nucitam nirdiśyamānam dṛśyate tasya uditi nāma hiraṇya śmaśruḥ ityādi
nirguṇam api sat brahma nāma rūpa gataiḥ guṇaiḥ saguṇam upāsana artham tatra tatra upadiśyate iti etat api uktam eva
sarva gatasya api brahmaṇaḥ upalabdhi artham sthāna viśeṣaḥ na virudhyate sālagrāme iva viṣṇoḥ iti etat api uktam eva
sukha viśiṣṭa abhidhānāt eva ca
api ca na eva atra vivaditavyam kim brahma asmin vāṃkye bhidhīyate na vā iti
sukha viśiṣṭa abhidhānāt eva brahma tvam siddham
sukha viśiṣṭam hi brahma yat vākya upakrame prakrāntam prāṇaḥ brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti tat eva iha abhihitam
prakṛta parigrahasya nyāyya tvāt ācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā iti ca gati mātra abhidhāna pratijñānāt
katham punar vākya upakrame sukha viśiṣṭam brahma vijñāyate iti ucyate prāṇaḥ brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti etat agnīnām vacanam śrutvā upakosalaḥ uvāca vijānāmi aham yat prāṇaḥ brahma kam ca kham ca tu na vijānāmi iti
tatra idam prativacanam yat vāva kam tat eva kham yat eva kham tat eva kam iti
tatra khaṃśabdaḥ bhūtākāśe nirūḍhaḥ loke
yadi tasya viśeṣaṇa tvena kaṃśabdaḥ sukha vācī nā upādīyeta tathā sati kevale bhūtākāśe brahma śabdaḥ nāma ādiṣu iva pratīka abhiprāyeṇa prayuktaḥ iti pratītiḥ syāt
tathā kaṃ śabdasya viṣaya indriya saṃparka janite sāmaye sukhe prasiddha tvāt yadi tasya khaṃ śabdaḥ viśeṣaṇa tvena na upādīyeta
laukikam sukham brahma iti pratītiḥ syāt
itaretara viśeṣitau tu kaṃ khaṃ śabdau sukha ātmakam brahma gamayataḥ
tatra dvitīye brahma śabde kam kham brahma iti eva ucyamāne kaṃśabdasya viśeṣaṇa tvena eva upayukta tvāt sukhasya guṇasya adhyeya tvam syāt
tat mā bhūt iti ubhayoḥ kaṃ khaṃ śabdayoḥ brahma śabda śiraḥ tvam kam brahma kham brahma iti
iṣṭam hi sukhasya api guṇasya guṇi vat dhyeya tvam
tat evam vākya upakrame sukha viśiṣṭam brahma upadiṣṭam
pratyekam ca gārhapatya ādayaḥ gnayaḥ svam svam mahimānam upadiśya eṣā somya te smadvidyā ātma vidyā ca iti upasaṃharantaḥ pūrvatra brahma nirdiṣṭam iti jñāpayanti
ācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā iti ca gati mātra abhidhāna pratijñānam artha antara vivakṣām vārayati
yathā puṣkarapalāśe āpaḥ na śliṣyante evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma na śliṣyate iti ca akṣi sthānam puruṣam vijānataḥ pāpmanā anupaghātam bruvan akṣi sthānasya puruṣasya brahmatvam darśayati
tasmāt prakṛtasya eva brahmaṇaḥ kṣi sthānatām saṃyat vāma tva ādi guṇatām ca uktvā arciḥ ādikām tad vidaḥ gatim vakṣyāmi iti upakramate yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate eṣaḥ ātmā iti ha uvāca iti
śruta upaniṣatka gati abhidhānāt ca
itas ca akṣi sthānaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ yasmāt śruta upaniṣatkasya śruta rahasya vijñānasya brahma vidaḥ yā gatiḥ deva yāna ākhyā prasiddhā śrutau atha uttareṇa tapasā brahmacaryeṇa śraddhayā vidyayā ātmānam anviṣya ādityam abhijayante
etat vai prāṇānām āyatanam etat amṛtam abhayam etat parāyaṇam etasmāt na punar āvartante iti smṛtau api agniḥ jyotiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ uttarāyaṇam
tatra prayātāḥ gacchanti brahma brahma vidaḥ PNM janāḥ PNM
iti sā eva iha akṣi puruṣa vidaḥ abhidhīyamānā dṛśyate
atha yat u ca eva asmin śavyam kurvanti yadi ca na arciṣam eva abhisaṃbhavanti iti upakramya ādityāt candramasam candramasaḥ vidyutam tad puruṣaḥ mānavaḥ saḥ enān brahma gamayati eṣa deva pathaḥ brahma pathaḥ etena pratipadyamānāḥ imam mānavam āvartam na āvartante iti
tat iha brahma vid viṣayayā prasiddhayā gatyā akṣi sthānasya brahma tvam niścīyate
anavasthiteḥ asambhavāt ca nā itaraḥ
yat punar uktam chāyā ātmā vijñāna ātmā devatā ātmā vā syāt akṣi sthānaḥ iti atra ucyate na chāyā ātma ādiḥ itaraḥ iha grahaṇam arhati
kasmāt
anavasthiteḥ
na tāvat chāyā ātmanaḥ cakṣuṣi nityam avasthānam saṃbhavati
yadā eva hi kaścid puruṣaḥ cakṣuḥ āsīdati tadā cakṣuṣi puruṣa chāyā dṛśyate
apagate tasmin na dṛśyate
yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ iti ca śrutiḥ saṃnidhānāt sva cakṣuṣi dṛśyamānam puruṣam upāsya tvena upadiśati
na ca upāsanā kāle chāyākaram kaṃcid puruṣam cakṣuḥ samīpe saṃnidhāpya upāste iti yuktam kalpayitum
asya eva śarīrasya nāśam anu eṣa naśyati iti śrutiḥ chāyā ātmanaḥ api anavasthita tvam darśayati
asaṃbhāvat ca
tasmin amṛta tva ādīnām guṇānām na chāyā ātmani pratītiḥ
tathā vijñāna ātmanaḥ api sādhāraṇe kṛtsna śarīra indriya saṃbandhe sati na cakṣuṣi eva avasthita tvam śakyam vaktum
brahmaṇaḥ tu sarva vyāpinaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ upalabdhi arthaḥ hṛdaya ādi deśa viśeṣa saṃbandhaḥ
samānaḥ ca vijñāna ātmani api amṛta tva ādīnām guṇānām asaṃbhavaḥ
yadi api vijñānātmā paramātmanaḥ nanyaḥ eva tathā api avidyā kām akarma kṛtam tasmin martya tvam adhyāropitam bhayam ca iti amṛta tva abhaya tve na upapadyete
saṃyat vāma tva ādayaḥ ca etasmin anaiśvaryāt anupapannāḥ eva
devatā ātmanaḥ tu raśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ u smin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti śruteḥ yadi api cakṣuṣi avasthānam syāt tathā api ātmatvam tāvat na saṃbhavati parāc rūpa tvāt
amṛta tva ādayaḥ pi na saṃbhavanti utpatti pralaya śravaṇāt
amara tvam api devānām cira kāla avasthāna apekṣam
aiśvaryam api parameśvara āyattam na svābhāvikam
bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣā udeti sūryaḥ
bhīṣā asmāt agniḥ ca indraḥ ca mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti mantra varṇāt
tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva ayam akṣi sthānaḥ pratyetavyaḥ
asmin ca pakṣe dṛśyate iti prasiddha vat upādānam śāstra ādi apekṣam vidvat viṣayam prarocana artham iti vyākhyeyam
antaryāmi adhidaiva ādiṣu tad dharma vyapadeśāt
antaryāmi adhikaraṇam
yaḥ imam ca lokam param ca lokam sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni antaraḥ yamayati iti upakramya śrūyate yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan pṛthivyāḥ antaraḥ yam pṛthivī na veda yasya pṛthivī śarīram yaḥ pṛthivīm antaraḥ yamayati eṣa te ātmā antaryāmī amṛtaḥ ityādi
atra adhidaivatam adhilokam adhivedam adhiyajñam adhibhūtam adhyātmam ca kaścid antar avasthitaḥ yamayitā antaryāmī iti śrūyate
sa kim adhidaiva ādi abhimānī devatā ātmā kaścid kim vā prāpta aṇima ādi aiśvaryaḥ kaścid yogī kim vā paramātmā kim vā artha antaram kiṃcid iti apūrva saṃjñā darśanāt saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat naḥ pratibhāti
saṃjñāyāḥ aprasiddha tvāt saṃjñinā api aprasiddhena artha antareṇa kenacid bhavitavyam iti
athavā na anirūpita rūpam arthāntaram kiṃcid api śakyam asti iti abhyupagantum
antaryāmi śabdaḥ ca antaryamana yogena pravṛttaḥ na atyantam aprasiddhaḥ
tasmāt pṛthivī ādi abhimānī kaścid devaḥ antaryāmī syāt
tathā ca śrūyate pṛthivī eva yasya āyatanam agniḥ lokaḥ manaḥ jyotiḥ ityādi
sa ca kārya karaṇavat tvāt pṛthivī ādīn antar tiṣṭhan yamayati iti yuktam devatā ātmanaḥ yamayitṛ tvam
yoginaḥ vā kasyacid siddhasya sarva anupraveśena yamayitṛ tvam syāt
na tu paramātmā pratīyate akārya karaṇa tvāt
iti evam prāpte idam ucyate yaḥ ntaryāmī adhidaiva ādiṣu śrūyate sa paramātmā eva syāt na anyaḥ iti
kutas
tad dharma vyapadeśāt
tasya hi paramātmanaḥ dharmāḥ iha nirdiśyamānāḥ dṛśyante
pṛthivī ādi tāvat adhidaiva ādi bheda bhinnam samastam vikāra jātam antar tiṣṭhan yamayati iti paramātmanaḥ yamayitṛ tvam dharmaḥ upapadyate
sarva vikāra kāraṇa tve sati sarva śakti upapatteḥ
eṣa te ātmā antaryāmī amṛtaḥ iti ca ātma tva amṛta tve mukhye paramātmanaḥ upapadyete
yam pṛthivī na veda iti ca pṛthivī devatāyai avijñeyam antaryāmiṇam bruvan devatā ātmanaḥ darśayati
pṛthivī devatā hi aham asmi pṛthivī iti ātmānam vijānīyāt
tathā a dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ ityādi vyapadeśaḥ rūpa ādi vihīna tvāt paramātmanaḥ upapadyate iti
yat tu akārya karaṇasya paramātmanaḥ yamayitṛ tvam na upapadyate iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
yān niyacchati tad kārya karaṇaiḥ eva tasya kārya karaṇavat tva upapatteḥ
tasya api anyaḥ niyantā iti anavasthā doṣaḥ ca na saṃbhavati bheda abhāvāt
bhede hi sati anavasthā doṣa upapattiḥ
tasmāt paramātmā eva antaryāmī
na ca smārtam a tad dharma abhilāpāt
syāt etat adṛṣṭa tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ sāṃkhya smṛti kalpitasya pradhānasya api upapadyante rūpa ādi hīna tayā tasya taiḥ abhyupagamāt
apratarkyam avijñeyam prasuptam iva sarvatas iti hi smaranti
tasya api niyantṛ tvam sarva vikāra kāraṇa tvāt upapadyate
tasmāt pradhānam antaryāmi śabdam syāt
īkṣateḥ na aśabdam iti atra nirākṛtam api sat pradhānam iha adṛṣṭa tva ādi vyapadeśa saṃbhavena punar āśaṅkyate
atas uttaram ucyate na ca smārtam pradhānam antaryāmi śabdam bhavitum arhati
kasmāt
a tad dharma abhilāpāt
yadi api adṛṣṭa tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ pradhānasya saṃbhavati tathā api na draṣṭṛ tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ saṃbhavati pradhānasya acetana tvena taiḥ abhyupagamāt
a dṛṣṭaḥ draṣṭā a śrutaḥ śrotā a mataḥ mantā a vijñātaḥ vijñātā iti hi vākya śeṣaḥ iha bhavati
ātma tvam api na pradhānasya upapadyate
yadi pradhānam ātma tva draṣṭṛ tva ādi asaṃbhavāt na antaryāmī abhyupagamyate śārīraḥ tarhi antaryāmī bhavatu
śārīraḥ hi cetana tvāt draṣṭā śrotā mantā vijñātā ca bhavati ātmā ca pratyak tvāt
amṛtaḥ ca dharma adharma phala upabhoga upapatteḥ
adṛṣṭa tva ādayaḥ ca dharmāḥ śārīre su prasiddhāḥ
darśana ādi kriyāyāḥ kartari pravṛtti virodhāt na dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram paśyeḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca
tasya ca kārya karaṇa saṃghātam antar yamayitum śīlam bhoktṛ tvāt
tasmāt śārīraḥ ntaryāmī iti atas uttaram paṭhati
śārīraḥ ca ubhaye hi bhedena enam adhīyate
na iti pūrva sūtrāt anuvartate
śārīraḥ ca na antaryāmī syāt
kasmāt
yadi api draṣṭṛ tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ tasya saṃbhavanti tathā api ghaṭa ākāśa vat upādhi paricchinna tvāt na kārtsnyena pṛthivī ādiṣu antar avasthātum niyantum ca śaknoti
api ca ubhaye hi śākhinaḥ kāṇvāḥ mādhyaṃdināḥ ca antaryāmiṇaḥ bhedena enam śārīram pṛthivī ādi vat adhiṣṭhāna tvena niyamya tvena ca ādhīyate yaḥ vijñāne tiṣṭhan iti kāṇvāḥ
yaḥ ātmani tiṣṭhan iti mādhyaṃdināḥ
yaḥ ātmani tiṣṭhan iti asmin tāvat pāṭhe bhavati ātma śabdaḥ śārīrasya vācakaḥ
yaḥ vijñāne tiṣṭhan iti asmin api pāṭhe vijñāna śabdena śārīraḥ ucyate vijñāna mayaḥ hi śārīraḥ iti
tasmāt śārīrāt anyaḥ īśvaraḥ ntaryāmī iti siddham
katham punar ekasmin dehe dvau draṣṭārau upapadyete yaḥ ca ayam īśvaraḥ ntaryāmī yaḥ ca ayam itaraḥ śārīraḥ
kā punar iha anupapattiḥ
na anyaḥ taḥ sti draṣṭā ityādi śruti vacanam virudhyeta
atra hi prakṛtāt antaryāmiṇaḥ draṣṭāram śrotāram mantāram vijñātāram ca ātmānam pratiṣedhati
niyantṛ antara pratiṣedha artham etat vacanam iti ced na
niyantṛ antara aprasaṅgāt aviśeṣa śravaṇāt ca
atrā ucyate avidyā pratyupasthāpita kārya karaṇa upādhi nimittaḥ yam śārīra antaryāmiṇoḥ bheda vyapadeśaḥ na pāramārthikaḥ
ekaḥ hi pratyagātmā bhavati na dvau pratyagātmānau saṃbhavataḥ
ekasya eva tu bheda vyavahāraḥ upādhi kṛtaḥ yathā ghaṭa ākāśaḥ mahā ākāśaḥ iti
tatas ca jñātṛ jñeya ādi bheda śrutayaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni ca pramāṇāni saṃsāra anubhavaḥ vidhi pratiṣedha śāstram ca iti sarvam etat upapadyate
tathā ca śrutiḥ yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati iti avidyā viṣaye sarvam vyavahāram darśayati
yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet iti vidyā viṣaye sarvam vyavahāram vārayati
adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ dharma ukteḥ
adṛśya tva ādi adhikaraṇam
atha parā yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate yat tat a dreśyam a grāhyam a gotram a varṇam a cakṣuḥ śrotram tat a pāṇi pādam nityam vibhum sarva gatam su sūkṣmam tat avyayam yat bhūta yonim paripaśyanti dhīrāḥ iti śrūyate
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ayam adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ bhūtayoniḥ pradhānam syāt uta śārīraḥ āhosvit parameśvaraḥ iti
tatra pradhānam acetanam bhūta yoniḥ iti yuktam acetanānām eva tatra dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānāt
yathā ūrṇanābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate ca yathā pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavanti
yathā sataḥ puruṣāt keśa lomāni tathā akṣarāt saṃbhavati iha viśvam iti
nanu ūrṇanābhiḥ puruṣaḥ ca cetanau iha dṛṣṭānta tvena upāttau
na iti brūmaḥ
na hi kevalasya cetanasya tatra sūtra yoni tvam keśa loma yoni tvam vā asti
cetanā dhiṣṭhitam hi acetanam ūrṇanābhi śarīram sūtrasya yoniḥ puruṣa śarīram ca keśa lomnām iti prasiddham
api ca pūrvatra adṛṣṭa tva ādi abhilāpa saṃbhave pi draṣṭṛ tva ādi abhilāpa asaṃbhavāt na pradhānam abhyupagatam
iha tu adṛśya tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ pradhāne saṃbhavanti
na ca atra virudhyamānaḥ dharmaḥ kaścid abhilapyate
nanu yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid iti ayam cetane pradhāne na saṃbhavati katham pradhānam bhūta yoniḥ pratijñāyate iti
atrā ucyate yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate yat tat adreśyam iti akṣara śabdena adṛśya tva ādi guṇakam bhūtayonim śrāvayitvā punar ante śrāvayiṣyati akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti
tatra yaḥ kṣarāt śrutaḥ sa sarvajñaḥ sarva vid saṃbhaviṣyati
pradhānam eva tu akṣara śabda nirdiṣṭam bhūta yoniḥ
yadā tu yoni śabdaḥ nimitta vācī tadā bhūtayoniḥ syāt dharma adharmābhyām bhūta jātasya upārjanāt iti
evam prāpte abhidhīyate yaḥ yam adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ bhūtayoniḥ sa parameśvaraḥ eva syāt na anyaḥ iti
katham etat avagamyate
dharma ukteḥ
parameśvarasya hi dharmaḥ iha ucyamānaḥ dṛśyate yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid iti
na hi pradhānasya acetanasya śārīrasya vā upādhi paricchinna dṛṣṭeḥ sarvajña tvam sarva vid tvam vā saṃbhavati
nanu akṣara śabda nirdiṣṭāt bhūtayoneḥ parasya eva etat sarvajña tvam sarva vid tvam ca na bhūtayoni viṣayam iti uktam
atra ucyate na evam saṃbhavati
yatkāraṇam akṣarāt saṃbhavati iha viśvam iti prakṛtam bhūta yonim iha jāyamāna prakṛti tvena nirdiśya anantaram api jāyamāna prakṛti tvena eva sarvajñam nirdiśati yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid yasya jñāna mayam tapaḥ
tasmāt etat brahma nāma rūpam annam ca jāyate iti
tasmāt nirdeśa sāmyena pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt prakṛtasya eva akṣarasya bhūtayoneḥ sarvajña tvam sarva vid tvam ca dharmaḥ ucyate iti gamyate
akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti atra api ca prakṛtāt bhūta yoni ikṣarāt paraḥ kaścid abhidhīyate
katham etat avagamyate
yena akṣaram puruṣam veda satyam provāca tām tat tvattaḥ bahma vidyām iti prakṛtasya eva akṣarasya bhūtayoneḥ adṛśya tva ādi guṇakasya vaktavya tvena pratijñāta tvāt
katham tarhi akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti vyapadiśyate iti uttara sūtre tat vakṣyāmaḥ
api ca atra dve vidye veditavye ukte parā ca eva aparā ca iti
tatra aparām ṛgveda ādi lakṣaṇām vidyām uktvā bravīti atha parā yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate ityādi
tatra parasyāḥ vidyāyāḥ viṣaya tvena akṣaram śrutam
yadi punar parameśvarāt anyat adṛśya tva ādi guṇakam akṣaram parikalpyeta na iyam parā vidyā syāt
para apara vibhāgaḥ hi ayam vidyayoḥ abhyudaya niḥśreyasa phala tayā parikalpyate
na ca pradhānasya vidyā niḥśreyasa phalā kenacid abhyupagamyate
tisraḥ ca vidyāḥ pratijñāyeran tvad pakṣe kṣarāt bhūtayoneḥ parasya paramātmanaḥ pratipādyamāna tvāt
dve eva tu vidye veditavye iha nirdiṣṭe
kasmin nu bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti ca eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna apekṣaṇam sarva ātmake brahmaṇi vivakṣyamāṇe na acetana mātra eka āyatane pradhāne bhogya vyatirikte vā bhoktari
api ca sa brahma vidyām sarva vidyā pratiṣṭhām atharvāya jyeṣṭhaputrāya prāha iti brahma vidyām prādhānyena upakramya para apara vibhāgena parām vidyām akṣara adhigamanīm darśayan tasyāḥ brahma vidyā tvam darśayati
sā ca brahma vidyā samākhyā tad adhigamyasya akṣarasya abrahmatve bādhitā syāt
aparā ṛgveda ādi lakṣaṇā karma vidyā brahma vidyā upakrame upanyasyate brahma vidyā praśaṃsāyai plavāḥ hi ete adṛḍhāḥ yajña rūpāḥ aṣṭādaśa uktam avaram yeṣu karma
etat śreyaḥ ye bhinandanti mūḍhāḥ jarām mṛtyum te punar evā api yanti iti evamādi nindā vacanāt
ninditvā ca aparām vidyām tatas viraktasya para vidyā adhikāram darśayati parīkṣya lokān karma citān brāhmaṇaḥ nirvedam āyāt na asti akṛtaḥ kṛtena
tad vijñāna artham sa gurum eva abhigacchet samidh pāṇiḥ śrotriyam brahmaniṣṭham iti
yat tu uktam acetanānām pṛthivī ādīnām dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānāt dārṣṭāntikena api acetanena eva bhūtayoninā bhavitavyam iti tat ayuktam
na hi dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭāntikayoḥ atyanta sāmyena bhavitavyam iti
api ca sthūlāḥ pṛthivī ādayaḥ dṛṣṭānta tvena upāttāḥ iti na sthūlaḥ eva dārṣṭāntikaḥ bhūtayoniḥ abhyupagamyate
tasmāt adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ bhūtayoniḥ parameśvaraḥ eva
viśeṣaṇa bheda vyapadeśābhyām ca na itarau
itas ca parameśvaraḥ eva bhūtayoniḥ na itarau śārīraḥ pradhānam vā
kasmāt
viśeṣaṇa bheda vyapadeśābhyām
viśinaṣṭi hi prakṛtam bhūtayonim śārīrāt vilakṣaṇa tvena divyaḥ hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sa bāhya abhyantaraḥ hi ajaḥ
a prāṇaḥ hi a manāḥ śubhraḥ iti
na hi etat divya tva ādi viśeṣaṇam avidyā pratyupasthāpita nāma rūpa pariccheda abhimāninaḥ tad dharmān sva ātmani kalpayataḥ śārīrasya upapadyate
tasmāt sākṣāt aupaniṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ iha ucyate
tathā pradhānāt api prakṛtam bhūta yonim bhedena vyapadiśati akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti
akṣaram avyākṛtam nāma rūpa bīja śakti rūpam bhūta sūkṣmam īśvara āśrayam tasya eva upādhi bhūtam sarvasmāt vikārāt paraḥ yaḥ vikāraḥ tasmāt paratas paraḥ iti bhedena vyapadiśan paramātmānam iha vivakṣitam darśayati
na atra pradhānam nāma kiṃcid svatantram tattvam abhyupagamya tasmāt bheda vyapadeśaḥ ucyate
kim tarhi
yadi pradhānam api kalpyamānam śruti avirodhena avyākṛta ādi śabda vācyam bhūta sūkṣmam parikalpyeta kalpyatām
tasmāt bheda vyapadeśāt parameśvaraḥ bhūtayoniḥ iti etat iha pratipādyate
kutas ca parameśvaraḥ bhūtayoniḥ
rūpa upanyāsāt ca
api ca akṣarāt paratas paraḥ Muṇḍaka
iti asya anantaram etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ iti prāṇa prabhṛtīnām pṛthivī paryantānām tattvānām sargam uktvā tasya eva bhūtayoneḥ sarva vikāra ātmakam rūpam upanyasyamānam paśyāmaḥ agniḥ mūrdhā cakṣuṣī candra sūryau diśaḥ śrotre vāc vivṛtāḥ ca vedāḥ
vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ hṛdayam viśvam asya padbhyām pṛthivī hi eṣa sarva bhūta antarātmā
iti
tat ca parameśvarasya eva ucitam sarva vikāra kāraṇatvāt
na śārīrasya tanu mahimnaḥ
na api pradhānasya ayam rūpa upanyāsaḥ saṃbhavati sarva bhūta antarātma tva asaṃbhavāt
tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva bhūtayoniḥ na itarau iti gamyate
katham punar bhūtayoneḥ ayam rūpa upanyāsaḥ iti gamyate
prakaraṇāt eṣaḥ iti ca prakṛta anukarṣaṇāt
bhūta yonim hi prakṛtya etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ eṣa sarva bhūta antarātmā iti vacanam bhūta yoni viṣayam eva bhavati
yathā upādhyāyam prakṛtya etasmāt adhīṣva eṣa veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ iti vacanam upādhyāya viṣayam bhavati tadvat
katham punar adṛśya tva ādi guṇakasya bhūtayoneḥ vigrahavat rūpam saṃbhavati
sarva ātma tva vivakṣayā idam ucyate na tu vigrahavat tva vivakṣayā iti adoṣaḥ aham annam aham annam aham anna aham anna ādaḥ ityādi vat
anye punar manyante na ayam bhūtayoneḥ rūpa upanyāsaḥ jāyamāna tvena upanyāsāt
etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca
kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇī iti hi pūrvatra prāṇa ādi pṛthivī antam tattva jātam jāyamāna tvena niradikṣat
uttaratra api ca tasmāt agniḥ samidhaḥ yasya sūryaḥ iti evamādi atas ca sarvāḥ oṣadhayaḥ rasāḥ ca iti evam antam jāmāna tvena eva nirdekṣyati
iha eva katham akasmāt antarāle bhūtayoneḥ rūpam upanyasyet
sarva ātma tvam api sṛṣṭim parisamāpya upadekṣyati puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma ityādinā
śruti smṛtyoḥ ca trailokya śarīrasya prajāpateḥ janma ādi nirdiśyamānam upalabhāmahe hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartata agre bhūtasya jātaḥ patiḥ ekaḥ āsīt
sa dādhāra pṛthivīm dyām uta imām kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema iti samavartata iti ajāyata iti arthaḥ tathā sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣaḥ ucyate
ādikartā sa bhūtānām brahma agre samavartata iti ca
vikārapuruṣasya api sarva bhūta antarātma tvam saṃbhavati prāṇa ātmanā sarva bhūtānām adhyātmam avasthānāt
asmin pakṣe puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma iti ādi sarva rūpa upanyāsaḥ parameśvara pratipatti hetuḥ iti vyākhyeyam
vaiśvānaraḥ sādhāraṇa śabda viśeṣāt
kaḥ naḥ ātmā kim brahma iti ātmānam eva imam vaiśvānaram saṃprati adhyeṣi tam eva naḥ brūhi iti ca upakramya dyu sūrya vāyu ākāśa vāri pṛthivīnām sutejaḥ tva ādi guṇa yogam ekaika upāsana nindayā ca vaiśvānaram prati eṣām mūrdha ādi bhāvam upadiśya āmnāyate yaḥ tu etam evam prādeśa mātram abhivimānam ātmānam vaiśvānaram upāste sa sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu ātmasu annam atti
tasya ha vai etasya ātmanaḥ vaiśvānarasya mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ cakṣuḥ viśva rūpaḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ pṛthak vartmā ātmā saṃdehaḥ bahulaḥ vastiḥ eva rayiḥ pṛthivī eva pādau uraḥ eva vediḥ lomāni barhiḥ hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ manaḥ nu āhāryapacanaḥ āsyam āhavanīyaḥ ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim vaiśvānara śabdena jāṭharaḥ gniḥ upadiśyate uta bhūtāgniḥ atha tad abhimāninī devatā athavā śārīraḥ āhosvit parameśvaraḥ iti
kim punar atra saṃśaya kāraṇam
vaiśvānaraḥ iti jāṭhara bhūtāgni devatānām sādhāraṇa śabda prayogāt ātmā iti ca śārīra parameśvarayoḥ
tatra kasya upādānam nyāyyam kasya vā hānam iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
jāṭharaḥ gniḥ iti
kutas
tatra hi viśeṣeṇa kvacid prayogaḥ dṛśyate ayam agniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ yaḥ yam antar puruṣe yena idam annam pacyate yat idam adyate ityādau
agni mātram vā syāt tad sāmānyena api prayoga darśanāt viśvasmai agnim bhuvanāya devāḥ vaiśvānaram ketum ahnām akṛṇvan ityādau agni śarīrā vā devatā syāt tasyām api prayoga darśanāt vaiśvānarasya sumatau syāma rājā hi kam bhuvanānām abhiśrīḥ iti evamādyāyāḥ śruteḥ devatāyām aiśvarya ādi upetāyām saṃbhavāt
atha ātma śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyāt upakrame ca kaḥ naḥ ātmā kim brahma iti kevala ātma śabda prayogāt ātma śabda vaśena vaiśvānara śabdaḥ pariṇeyaḥ iti ucyate tathā api śārīraḥ ātmā syāt
tasya bhoktṛ tvena vaiśvānara saṃnikarṣāt prādeśa mātram iti ca viśeṣaṇasya tasmin upādhi paricchinne saṃbhavāt
tasmāt na īśvaraḥ vaiśvānaraḥ iti evam prāptam
tatra idam ucyate vaiśvānaraḥ paramātmā bhavitum arhati
kutas
sādhāraṇa śabda viśeṣāt
sādhāraṇa śabdayoḥ viśeṣaḥ sādhāraṇa śabda viśeṣaḥ
yadi api etau ubhau api ātma vaiśvānara śabdau sādhāraṇa śabdau vaiśvānara śabdaḥ tu trayāṇām sādhāraṇaḥ ātma śabdaḥ ca dvayoḥ tathā api viśeṣaḥ dṛśyate yena parameśvara paratvam tayoḥ abhyupagamyate tasya ha vā etasya ātmanaḥ vaiśvānarasya mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādiḥ
atra hi parameśvaraḥ eva dyumūrdha tva ādi viśiṣṭaḥ vasthā antara gataḥ pratyagātma tvena upanyastaḥ ādhyānāya iti gamyate kāraṇa tvāt
kāraṇasya hi sarvābhiḥ kārya gatābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ avasthāvat tvāt dyu loka ādi avayava tvam upapadyate
sa sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu ātmasu annam atti iti ca sarva loka ādi āśrayam phalam śrūyamāṇam parama kāraṇa parigrahe saṃbhavati eva iha asya sarve pāpmānaḥ pradūyante iti ca tad vidaḥ sarva pāpma pradāha śravaṇam kaḥ naḥ ātmā kim brahma iti ca ātma brahma śabdābhyām upakramaḥ
iti evam antāni brahma liṅgāni parameśvaram eva gamayanti
tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva vaiśvānaraḥ
smaryamāṇam anumānam syāt iti
itas ca parameśvaraḥ eva vaiśvānaraḥ
yasmāt parameśvarasya eva agniḥ āsyam dyauḥ mūrdhā iti īdṛśam trailokya ātmakam rūpam smaryate yasya agniḥ āsyam dyauḥ mūrdhā kham nābhiḥ caraṇau kṣitiḥ
sūryaḥ cakṣuḥ diśaḥ śrotram tasmai loka ātmane namaḥ iti
tat smaryamāṇam rūpam mūla bhūtām śrutim anumāpayat asya vaiśvānara śabdasya parameśvara paratve anumānam liṅgam gamakam syāt iti arthaḥ
iti śabdaḥ hetu arthe yasmāt idam gamakam tasmāt api vaiśvānaraḥ paramātmā eva iti arthaḥ
yadi api stutiḥ iyam tasmai loka ātmane namaḥ iti tathā api stuti tvam api na asati mūla bhūte veda vākye samyak īdṛśena rūpeṇa saṃbhavati
dyām mūrdhānam yasya viprāḥ vadanti kham vai nābhim candra sūryau ca netre
diśaḥ śrotre viddhi pādau kṣitim ca saḥ u cintya ātmā sarva bhūta praṇetā iti evaṃjātīyakā ca smṛtiḥ iha udāhartavyā
śabda ādibhyaḥ ntar pratiṣṭhānāt ca na iti ced na tathā dṛṣṭi upadeśāt asambhavāt puruṣam api ca enam adhīyate
atra āha na parameśvaraḥ vaiśvānaraḥ bhavitum arhati
kutas
śabda ādibhyaḥ ntar pratiṣṭhānāt ca
śabdaḥ tāvat vaiśvānara śabdaḥ na parameśvare saṃbhavati artha antare rūḍha tvāt
tathā agni śabdaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ gniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ iti
ādi śabdāt hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ iti ādi agni tretā prakalpanam
tat yat bhaktam prathamam āgacchet tat homīyam ityādinā ca prāṇa āhuti adhikaraṇa tā saṃkīrtanam
etebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāṭharaḥ vaiśvānaraḥ pratyetavyaḥ
tathā antar pratiṣṭhānam api śrūyate puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti
tat ca jāṭhare saṃbhavati
yat api uktam mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādeḥ viśeṣāt kāraṇāt paramātmā vaiśvānaraḥ iti atra brūmaḥ kutas nu eṣa nirṇayaḥ yat ubhayathā api viśeṣa pratibhāne sati parameśvara viṣayaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ āśrayaṇīyaḥ na jāṭhara viṣayaḥ iti
athavā bhūtāgneḥ antar bahis ca avatiṣṭhamānasya eṣa nirdeśaḥ bhaviṣyati
tasya api hi dyu loka ādi saṃbandhaḥ mantra varṇe avagamyate yaḥ bhānunā pṛthivīm dyām uta imām ātatāna rodasī antarikṣam ityādau
athavā tad śarīrāyāḥ devatāyāḥ aiśvarya yogāt dyu loka ādi avayava tvam bhaviṣyati
tasmāt na parameśvaraḥ vaiśvānaraḥ iti
atra ucyate na tathā dṛṣṭi upadeśāt iti
na śabda ādibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ parameśvarasya pratyākhyānam yuktam
kutas
tathā jāṭhara aparityāgena dṛṣṭi upadeśāt
parameśvara dṛṣṭiḥ hi jāṭhare vaiśvānare iha upadiśyate manaḥ brahma iti upāsīta ityādi vat
athavā jāṭhara vaiśvānara upādhiḥ parameśvaraḥ iha draṣṭavya tvena upadiśyate manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ ityādi vat
yadi ca iha parameśvaraḥ na vivakṣyeta kevalaḥ eva jāṭharaḥ gniḥ vivakṣyeta tatas mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādeḥ viśeṣasya asaṃbhavaḥ eva syāt
yathā tu devatā bhūta agni vyapāśrayeṇa api ayam viśeṣaḥ upapādayitum na śakyate tathā uttara sūtre vakṣyāmaḥ
yadi ca kevalaḥ eva jāṭharaḥ vivakṣyeta puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhita tvam kevalam tasya syāt
na tu puruṣa tvam
puruṣam api ca enam adhīyate vājasaneyinaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ gniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ yat puruṣaḥ sa yaḥ ha etam evam agnim vaiśvānaram puruṣam puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti
parameśvarasya tu sarva ātma tvāt puruṣa tvam puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhita tvam ca ubhayam upapadyate
ye tu puruṣavidham api ca enam adhīyate iti sūtra avayavam paṭhanti teṣām eṣaḥ rthaḥ kevala jāṭhara parigrahe puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhita tvam kevalam syāt
na tu puruṣavidha tvam
puruṣavidham api ca enam adhīyate vājasaneyinaḥ puruṣavidham puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti
puruṣavidha tvam ca prakaraṇāt yat adhidaivatam dyu mūrdha tva ādi pṛthivī pratiṣṭhita tva antam yat ca adhyātmam prasiddham mūrdha tva ādi cubuka pratiṣṭhita tva antam tat parigṛhyate
śabda ādibhyaḥ ntar pratiṣṭhānāt ca na iti ced na tathā dṛṣṭi upadeśāt asambhavāt puruṣam api ca enam adhīyate
atra āha na parameśvaraḥ vaiśvānaraḥ bhavitum arhati
kutas
śabda ādibhyaḥ ntar pratiṣṭhānāt ca
śabdaḥ tāvat vaiśvānara śabdaḥ na parameśvare saṃbhavati artha antare rūḍha tvāt
tathā agni śabdaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ gniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ iti
ādi śabdāt hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ iti ādi agni tretā prakalpanam
tat yat bhaktam prathamam āgacchet tat homīyam ityādinā ca prāṇa āhuti adhikaraṇa tā saṃkīrtanam
etebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāṭharaḥ vaiśvānaraḥ pratyetavyaḥ
tathā antar pratiṣṭhānam api śrūyate puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti
tat ca jāṭhare saṃbhavati
yat api uktam mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādeḥ viśeṣāt kāraṇāt paramātmā vaiśvānaraḥ iti atra brūmaḥ kutas nu eṣa nirṇayaḥ yat ubhayathā api viśeṣa pratibhāne sati parameśvara viṣayaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ āśrayaṇīyaḥ na jāṭhara viṣayaḥ iti
athavā bhūtāgneḥ antar bahis ca avatiṣṭhamānasya eṣa nirdeśaḥ bhaviṣyati
tasya api hi dyu loka ādi saṃbandhaḥ mantra varṇe avagamyate yaḥ bhānunā pṛthivīm dyām uta imām ātatāna rodasī antarikṣam ityādau
athavā tad śarīrāyāḥ devatāyāḥ aiśvarya yogāt dyu loka ādi avayava tvam bhaviṣyati
tasmāt na parameśvaraḥ vaiśvānaraḥ iti
atra ucyate na tathā dṛṣṭi upadeśāt iti
na śabda ādibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ parameśvarasya pratyākhyānam yuktam
kutas
tathā jāṭhara aparityāgena dṛṣṭi upadeśāt
parameśvara dṛṣṭiḥ hi jāṭhare vaiśvānare iha upadiśyate manaḥ brahma iti upāsīta ityādi vat
athavā jāṭhara vaiśvānara upādhiḥ parameśvaraḥ iha draṣṭavya tvena upadiśyate manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ ityādi vat
yadi ca iha parameśvaraḥ na vivakṣyeta kevalaḥ eva jāṭharaḥ gniḥ vivakṣyeta tatas mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ ityādeḥ viśeṣasya asaṃbhavaḥ eva syāt
yathā tu devatā bhūta agni vyapāśrayeṇa api ayam viśeṣaḥ upapādayitum na śakyate tathā uttara sūtre vakṣyāmaḥ
yadi ca kevalaḥ eva jāṭharaḥ vivakṣyeta puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhita tvam kevalam tasya syāt
na tu puruṣa tvam
puruṣam api ca enam adhīyate vājasaneyinaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ gniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ yat puruṣaḥ sa yaḥ ha etam evam agnim vaiśvānaram puruṣam sākṣāt api avirodham jaiminiḥ
pūrvam jāṭhara agni pratīkaḥ jāṭhara agni upādhikaḥ vā parameśvaraḥ upāsyaḥ iti uktam antar pratiṣṭhita tva ādi anurodhena
idānīm tu vinā eva pratīka upādhi kalpanābhyām sākṣāt api parameśvara upāsana parigrahe na kaścid virodhaḥ iti jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
nanu jāṭhara agni aparigrahe ntar pratiṣṭhita tva vacanam śabda ādīni ca kāraṇāni virudhyeran iti
atrā ucyate antar pratiṣṭhita tva vacanam tāvat na virudhyate
na hi iha puruṣavidham puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti jāṭhara agni abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate tasya a prakṛta tvāt a saṃśabdita tvāt ca
katham tarhi yat prakṛtam mūrdha ādi cubuka anteṣu puruṣa avayaveṣu puruṣavidha tvam kalpitam tad abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate puruṣavidham puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti
yathā vṛkṣe śākhām pratiṣṭhitām paśyati iti tadvat
athavā yaḥ prakṛtaḥ paramātmā adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca puruṣavidha tva upādhiḥ tasya yat kevalam sākṣi rūpam tad abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate puruṣavidham puruṣe ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti
niścite ca pūrva apara ālocana vaśena paramātma parigrahe tad viṣayaḥ eva vaiśvānara śabdaḥ kenacid yogena vartiṣyate viśvaḥ ca ayam naraḥ ca iti viśveṣām vā ayam naraḥ viśve vā narāḥ asya iti viśvānaraḥ paramātmā sarva ātma tvāt viśvānaraḥ eva vaiśvānaraḥ
taddhitaḥ na anya arthaḥ rākṣasa vāyasa ādi vat
agni śabdaḥ pi agraṇī tva ādi yoga āśrayaṇena paramātma viṣayaḥ eva bhaviṣyati
gārhapatya ādi kalpanam prāṇa āhuti adhikaraṇa tvam ca paramātmanaḥ sarva ātma tvāt upapadyate
katham punar parameśvara parigrahe prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ upapadyate iti tām vyākhyātum ārabhate
abhivyakteḥ iti āśmarathyaḥ
atimātrasya api parameśvarasya prādeśa mātra tvam abhivyakti nimittam syāt
abhivyajyate kila prādeśa mātra parimāṇaḥ parameśvaraḥ upāsakānām kṛte
pradeśa viśeṣeṣu vā hṛdaya ādiṣu upalabdhi sthāneṣu viśeṣeṇa abhivyajyate
atas parameśvare pi prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ abhivyakteḥ upapadyate iti āśmarathyaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
anusmṛteḥ bādariḥ
prādeśa mātra hṛdaya pratiṣṭhitena vā ayam manasā anusmaryate
tena prādeśa mātraḥ iti ucyate
yathā prastha mitāḥ yavāḥ prasthāḥ iti ucyante tadvat
yadi api ca yaveṣu sva gatam eva parimāṇam prastha saṃbandhāt vyajyate na ca iha parameśvara gatam kiṃcid parimāṇam asti yat hṛdaya saṃbandhāt vyajyeta
tathā api prayuktāyāḥ prādeśa mātra śruteḥ saṃbhavati yathā kathaṃcid anusmaraṇam ālambanam iti ucyate
prādeśa mātra tvena vā ayam a prādeśa mātraḥ anusmaraṇīyaḥ prādeśa mātra śruti arthavat tāyai
evam anusmṛti nimittā parameśvare prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ iti bādariḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
āmananti ca enam asmin
ca enam parameśvaram asmin mūrdha cubuka antarāle jābālāḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ nantaḥ vyaktaḥ ātmā saḥ vimukte pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti
saḥ vimuktaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti
varaṇāyām na asyām ca madhye pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti
kā vai varaṇā kā ca nā asi iti
tatra ca imām eva nāsikām sarvāṇi indriya kṛtāni pāpāni vārayati iti sā varaṇā sarvāṇi indriya kṛtāni pāpāni nāśayati iti sā nāsī iti varaṇānāsī iti nirucya punar api āmananti katamat ca asya sthānam bhavati iti
bhruvoḥ ghrāṇasya ca yaḥ saṃdhiḥ saḥ eṣa dyu lokasya parasya ca saṃdhiḥ bhavati iti
tasmāt upapannā parameśvare prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ
abhivimāna śrutiḥ pratyagātma tva abhiprāyā
pratyagātma tayā sarvaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ abhivimīyate iti abhivimānaḥ
abhigataḥ vā ayam pratyak ātma tvāt vimānaḥ ca māna viyogāt iti abhivimānaḥ
abhivimimīte vā sarvam jagat kāraṇa tvāt iti abhivimānaḥ
tasmāt parameśvaraḥ vaiśvānaraḥ iti siddham
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ

prathamaḥ dhyāyaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
dyu bhū ādi āyatanam sva śabdāt
dyu bhū ādi adhikaraṇam
idam śrūyate yasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī ca antarikṣam ā utam manaḥ saha prāṇaiḥ ca sarvaiḥ
tam eva ekam jānatha ātmānam anyāḥ vācaḥ vimuñcatha amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti
atra yat etat dyu prabhṛtīnām ota tva vacanāt āyatanam kiṃcid avagamyate tat kim param brahma syāt āhosvit artha antaram iti saṃdihyate
tatra artha antaram kim api āyatanam syāt iti prāptam
kasmāt
amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti śravaṇāt
pāravān hi loke setuḥ prakhyātaḥ
na ca parasya brahmaṇaḥ pāravat tvam śakyam abhyupagantum anantam apāram iti śravaṇāt
artha antare ca āyatane parigṛhyamāṇe smṛti prasiddham pradhānam parigrahītavyam tasya kāraṇa tvāt āyatana tva upapatteḥ
śruti prasiddhaḥ vā vāyuḥ syāt vāyuḥ vāva gautama tat sūtram vāyunā vai gautama sūtreṇa ayam ca lokaḥ paraḥ ca lokaḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni saṃdṛbdhāni bhavanti iti vāyoḥ api vidhāraṇa tva śravaṇāt
śārīraḥ vā syāt
tasya api bhoktṛ tvāt bhogyam prapañcam pratyāyatana tva upapatteḥ iti evam prāpte idam āha dyu bhu ādi āyatanam iti
dyauḥ ca bhūḥ ca dyubhuvau dyubhuvau ādī yasya tat idam dyubhu ādi
yat etat asmin vākye dyauḥ pṛthivī antarikṣam manaḥ prāṇāḥ iti evam ātmakam jagat ota tvena nirdiṣṭam tasya āyatanam param brahma bhavitum arhati
kutas
sva śabdāt ātma śabdāt iti arthaḥ
ātma śabdaḥ hi iha bhavati tam eva ekam jānatha ātmānam iti
ātma śabdaḥ ca paramātma parigrahe samyak avakalpate na artha antara parigrahe
kvacid ca sva śabdena eva brahmaṇaḥ āyatana tva śrūyate sat mūlāḥ somya imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ sat āyatanāḥ sat pratiṣṭhāḥ iti
sva śabdena eva ca iha purastāt upariṣṭāt ca brahma saṃkīrtyate puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma tapaḥ brahma para amṛtam iti brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt brahma paścāt brahma dakṣiṇatas ca uttareṇa iti ca
tatra tu āyatana āyatanavat bhāva śravaṇāt
sarvam brahma iti ca sāmānādhikaraṇyāt yathā hi aneka ātmakaḥ vṛkṣaḥ śākhā skandhaḥ mūlam ca iti evam nānā rasaḥ vicitraḥ ātmā iti āśaṅkā saṃbhavati
tām nivartayitum sa avadhāraṇam āha tam eva ekam jānathaḥ ātmānam iti
etat uktam bhavati na kārya prapañca viśiṣṭaḥ vicitraḥ ātmā vijñeyaḥ
kim tarhi avidyā kṛtam kārya prapañcam vidyayā pravilāpayantaḥ tam eva ekam āyatana bhūtam ātmānam jānatha ekarasam iti
yathā yasmin āste devadattaḥ tadā ānaya iti ukte āsanam eva ānayati na devadattam
tadvat āyatana bhūtasya eva eka rasasya ātmanaḥ vijñeya tvam upadiśyate
vikāra anṛta abhisaṃdhasya ca apavādaḥ śrūyate mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti
sarvam brahma iti tu sāmānādhikaraṇyam prapañca vilāpana artham na aneka rasa tā pratipādana artham sa yathā saindhava ghanaḥ nantaraḥ bāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ rasa ghanaḥ eva evam vai are yam ātmā anantaraḥ bāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ prajñāna ghanaḥ eva iti eka rasa tā śravaṇāt
tasmāt dyubhva ādi āyatanam param brahma
yat tu uktam setu śruteḥ setoḥ ca pāravat tva upapatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ rtha antareṇa dyubhvā ādi āyatanena bhavitavyam iti atra ucyate vidhāraṇa tva mātram eva setu śrutyāḥ vivakṣyate na pāravat tva ādi
na hi mṛd dāru mayaḥ loke setuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti atra api mṛd dāru mayaḥ eva setuḥ abhyupagamyate
setu śabda arthaḥ vidhāraṇa tva mātram eva na pāravat tva ādi bandhana karmaṇaḥ setu śabda vyutpatteḥ
aparaḥ āha tam eva ekam jānatha ātmānam iti yat etat saṃkīrtitam ātma jñānam yat ca etat anyāḥ vācaḥ vimuñcatha iti vāc vimocanam tat atra amṛta tva sādhana tvāt amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti setu śrutyā saṃkīrtyate
na tu dyu bhu ādi āyatanam
tatra yat uktam setu śruteḥ brahmaṇaḥ rtha antareṇa dyubhvā ādi āyatanena bhavitavyam iti etat ayuktam
mukta upasṛpya vyapadeśāt
itas ca param eva brahma dyubhvā ādi āyatanam
yasmāt mukta upasṛpya tā asya vyapadiśyamānā dṛśyate
muktaiḥ upasṛpyam mukta upasṛpyam
deha ādiṣu anātmasu aham asmi iti ātma buddhiḥ avidyā tatas tad pūjana ādau rāgaḥ tad paribhava ādau ca dveṣaḥ tad uccheda darśanāt bhayam mohaḥ ca iti evam ayam ananta bhedaḥ nartha vrātaḥ saṃtataḥ sarveṣām naḥ pratyakṣaḥ
tad viparyayeṇa avidyā rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa muktaiḥ upasṛpyam upagamyam etat iti dyubhvā ādi āyatanam prakṛtya vyapadeśaḥ bhavati
katham
bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ
kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare iti uktvā bravīti tathā vidvān nāma rūpāt vimuktaḥ parātparam puruṣam upaiti divyam iti
brahmaṇaḥ ca mukta upasṛpya tvam prasiddham śāstre yadā sarve pramucyante kāmāḥ ye hṛdi śritāḥ
atha martyaḥ mṛtaḥ bhavati atra brahma samaśnute iti evamādau
pradhāna ādīnām tu na kvacid mukta upasṛpya tvam asti prasiddham
api ca tam eva ekam jānatha ātmānam anyāḥ vācaḥ vimuñcatha amṛtasya eṣa setuḥ iti vāc vimoka pūrvakam vijñeya tvam iha dyubhvā ādi āyatanasya ucyate
tat ca śruti antare brahmaṇaḥ dṛṣṭam tam eva dhīraḥ vijñāya prajñām kurvīta brāhmaṇaḥ
na anudhyāyāt bahūn śabdān vācaḥ viglāpanam hi tat iti
tasmāt api dyubhva ādi āyatanam param brahma
na anumānam a tad śabdāt
yathā brahmaṇaḥ pratipādakaḥ vaiśeṣikaḥ hetuḥ uktaḥ na evam artha antarasya vaiśeṣikaḥ hetuḥ pratipādakaḥ sti iti āha
na anumānam sāṃkhya smṛti parikalpitam pradhānam iha dyubhvā ādi āyatana tvena pratipattavyam
kasmāt
a tad śabdāt
tasya acetanasya pradhānasya pratipādakaḥ śabdaḥ tad śabdaḥ na tad śabdaḥ a tad śabdaḥ
na hi atra acetanasya pradhānasya pratipādakaḥ kaścid śabdaḥ sti yena acetanam pradhānam kāraṇa tvena āyatana tvena vā avagamyeta
tad viparītasya cetanasya yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid ityādiḥ
atas eva na vāyuḥ api iha dyubhvā ādi āyatana tvena āśrīyate
prāṇabhṛt ca
yadi api prāṇabhṛtaḥ vijñāna ātmanaḥ ātma tvam cetana tvam ca saṃbhavati tathā api upādhi paricchinna jñānasya sarvajña tva ādi asaṃbhave sati asmāt eva a tad śabdāt prāṇabhṛt api na dyubhvā ādi āyatana tvena āśrayitavyaḥ
na ca upādhi paricchinnasya a vibhoḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ dyubhu ādi āyatana tvam api samyak saṃbhavati
pṛthak yoga karaṇam uttara artham
kutas ca na prāṇabhṛt dyubhu ādi āyatana tvena āśrayitavyaḥ
bheda vyapadeśāt
bheda vyapadeśaḥ ca iha bhavati tam eva ekam jānatha ātmānam iti jñeya jñātṛ bhāvena
tatra prāṇabhṛt tāvat mumukṣu tvāt jñātā
pariśeṣāt ātma śabda vācyam brahma jñeyam dyu bhvā ādi āyatanam iti gamyate na prāṇabhṛt
