kutas ca na prāṇabhṛt dyubhu ādi āyatana tvena āśrayitavyaḥ
prakaraṇāt
prakaraṇam ca idam paramātmanaḥ kasmin nu bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna apekṣaṇāt
paramātmani hi sarvātmake vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam syāt na kevale prāṇabhṛti
kutas ca na prāṇabhṛt dyubhu ādi āyatana tvena āśrayitavyaḥ
sthiti adanābhyām ca
dyubhvā ādi āyatanam ca prakṛtya dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyau iti atra sthiti adane nirdiśyete
tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādu atti iti karma phala aśanam
an aścan anyaḥ bhicākaśīti iti audāsīnyena avasthānam
tābhyām ca sthiti adanābhyām īśvara kṣetrajñau tatra gṛhyete
yadi ca īśvaraḥ dyubhvā ādi āyatana tvena vivakṣitaḥ tatas tasya prakṛtasya īśvarasya kṣetrajñāt pṛthak vacanam avakalpate
anyathā hi aprakṛta vacanam ākasmikam asaṃbaddham syāt
nanu tava api kṣetrajñasya īśvarāt pṛthak vacanam ākasmikam eva prasajyeta
na tasya avivakṣita tvāt
kṣetrajñaḥ hi kartṛ tvena bhoktṛ tvena ca pratiśarīram buddhi ādi upādhi saṃbaddhaḥ lokataḥ eva prasiddhaḥ na asau śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate
īśvaraḥ tu prasiddha tvāt śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate iti na tasya ākasmikam vacanam yuktam
guhām praviṣṭau ātmānau hi iti atra api etat darśitam dvā suparṇā iti asyām ṛci īśvara kṣetrajñau ucyete iti
yadā api paiṅgī upaniṣad kṛtena vyākhyānena asyām ṛci sattva kṣetrajñau ucyete tadā api na virodhaḥ kaścid
katham
prāṇabhṛt hi iha ghaṭa ādi chidra vat sattva ādi upādhi abhimāni tvena pratiśarīram gṛhyamāṇaḥ dyubhvā ādi āyatanam na bhavati iti pratiṣidhyate
yaḥ tu sarva śarīreṣu upādhibhiḥ vinā upalakṣyate paraḥ eva sa bhavati
yathā ghaṭa ādi chidrāṇi ghaṭa ādibhiḥ upādhibhiḥ vinā upalakṣyamāṇāni mahā ākāśe eva bhavanti tadvat prāṇabhṛtaḥ parasmāt anya tva anupapatteḥ pratiṣedhaḥ nā upapadyate
tasmāt sattva ādi upādhi abhimāninaḥ eva dyubhva ādi āyatana tva pratiṣedhaḥ
tasmāt param eva brahma dyubhvā ādi āyatanam
tat etat adṛśya tva ādi guṇakaḥ dharma ukteḥ iti anena eva siddham
tasya eva hi bhūtayoni vākyasya madhye idam paṭhitam yasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī ca antarikṣam iti
prapañca artham tu punar upanyastam
bhūmā samprasādāt adhyupadeśāt
bhūma adhikaraṇam
idam samāmananti bhūmā tu eva vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti bhūmānam bhagavaḥ vijijñās SPs1In
iti
yatra na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anyat vijānāti sa bhūmā
atha yatra anyat paśyati anyat śṛṇoti anyat vijānāti tat alpam ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim prāṇaḥ bhūmā syāt āhosvit paramātmā iti
kutas saṃśayaḥ
bhūmā iti tāvat bahu tvam a bhidhīyate
bahoḥ lopaḥ bhū ca bahoḥ iti bhūma śabdasya bhāva pratyaya anta tā smaraṇāt
kimātmakam punar tat bahu tvam iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām prāṇaḥ vai āśāyāḥ bhūyān iti saṃnidhānāt prāṇaḥ bhūmā iti pratibhāti
tathā śrutam hi eva me bhagavat dṛśebhyaḥ tarati śokam ātma vid iti
saḥ ham bhagavaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu iti prakaraṇa utthānāt paramātmā bhūmā iti api pratibhāti
tatra kasya upādānam nyāyyam kasya vā hānam iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
prāṇaḥ bhūmā iti
kasmāt
bhūyas praśna prativacana paraṃparā darśanāt
yathā hi asti bhagavaḥ nāmnaḥ bhūyaḥ iti vāc vāva nāmnaḥ bhūyasī iti
tathā asti bhagavaḥ vācaḥ bhūyaḥ iti manaḥ vāva vācaḥ bhūyaḥ iti ca nāma ādibhyaḥ hi ā prāṇāt bhūyaḥ praśna prativacana pravāhaḥ pravṛttaḥ
na evam prāṇāt param bhūyaḥ praśna prativacanam dṛśyate asti bhagavaḥ prāṇāt bhūyaḥ iti adaḥ vāva prāṇāt bhūyaḥ iti
prāṇam eva tu nāma ādibhyaḥ āśā antebhyaḥ bhūyāṃsam prāṇaḥ vai āśāyāḥ bhūyān ityādinā sa prapañcam uktvā prāṇa darśinaḥ ca ativādi tvam ativādyasi iti ativādyasmi iti brūyāt na apahnuvīta iti abhyanujñāya eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti prāṇa vratam ativādi tvam anukṛṣya a parityajya eva prāṇam satya ādi paraṃparayā bhūmānam avatārayan prāṇam eva bhūmānam manyate iti gamyate
katham punar prāṇe bhūmani vyākhyāyamāne yatra na anyat paśyati iti etat bhūmnaḥ lakṣaṇa param vacanam vyākhyāyeta iti ucyate suṣupta avasthāyām prāṇa grasteṣu karaṇeṣu darśana ādi vyavahāra nivṛtti darśanāt saṃbhavati prāṇasya api yatra na anyat paśyati iti etat lakṣaṇam
tathā ca śrutiḥ na śrṛṇoti na paśyati ityādinā sarva karaṇa vyāpāra prati astamaya rūpām suṣupti avasthām uktvā prāṇa agnayaḥ eva etasmin pure jāgrati iti tasyām eva avasthāyām pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya jāgaraṇam bruvatī prāṇa pradhānām suṣupti avasthām darśayati
yat ca etat bhūmnaḥ sukha tvam śrutam yaḥ vai bhūmā tat sukham iti tat api aviruddham
atra eṣa devaḥ svapnāt na paśyati atha yat etasmin śarīre sukham bhavati iti suṣupti avasthāyām eva sukha śravaṇāt
yat ca yaḥ vai bhūmā tat amṛtam iti tat api prāṇasya a viruddham
prāṇaḥ vai amṛtam iti śruteḥ
katham punar prāṇam bhūmānam manyamānasya tarati śokam ātma vid iti ātma vividiṣayā prakaraṇasya utthānam upapadyate
prāṇaḥ eva iha ātmā vivakṣitaḥ iti brūmaḥ
tathā hi prāṇaḥ ha pitā prāṇaḥ mātā prāṇaḥ bhrātā prāṇaḥ svasā prāṇaḥ ācāryaḥ prāṇaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ iti prāṇam eva sarva ātmānam karoti yathā vai arāḥ nābhau samarpitāḥ evam asmin prāṇe sarvam samarpitam iti ca
sarva ātma tva aranābhi nidarśanābhyām ca saṃbhavati vaipulya ātmikā bhūma rūpa tā prāṇasya
tasmāt prāṇaḥ bhūmā iti evam prāptam
tatas idam ucyate paramātmā eva iha bhūmā bhavitum arhati na prāṇaḥ
kasmāt
saṃprasādāt adhyupadeśāt
saṃprasādaḥ iti suṣuptam sthānam ucyate
samyak prasīdati asmin iti nirvacanāt bṛhadāraṇyake ca svapna jāgarita sthānābhyām saha pāṭhāt
tasyām ca saṃprasāda avasthāyām prāṇaḥ jāgarti iti saṃprasādaḥ abhipreyate
prāṇāt ūrdhvam bhūmnaḥ upadiśyamāna tvāt iti arthaḥ
prāṇaḥ eva ced bhūmā syāt saḥ eva tasmāt ūrdhvam upadiśyeta iti āśliṣṭam etat syāt
na hi nāma eva nāmnaḥ bhūyaḥ iti nāmnaḥ ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam
kim tarhi nāmnaḥ nyat artha antaram upadiṣṭam vāc ākhyam vāc vāva nāmnaḥ bhūyasī iti
tathā vāc ādibhyaḥ pi ā prāṇāt artha antaram eva tatra tatra ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam
tadvat prāṇāt ūrdhvam upadiśyamānaḥ bhūmā prāṇāt artha antara bhūtaḥ bhavitum arhati
nanu iha na asti praśnaḥ asti bhagavaḥ prāṇāt bhūyaḥ iti
na api prativacanam asti prāṇāt vāva bhūyaḥ sti iti
katham prāṇāt adhi bhūmā upadiśyate iti ucyate
prāṇa viṣayam eva ca ativādi tvam uttaratra anukṛṣyamāṇam paśyāmaḥ eṣa tu vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti
tasmāt na asti prāṇāt adhyupadeśaḥ iti
atrā ucyate na tāvat prāṇa viṣayasya eva ativādi tvasya etat anukarṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum viśeṣa vādāt yaḥ satyena ativadati iti
nanu ayam prāṇa viṣayaḥ eva bhaviṣyati
katham
yathā eṣaḥ gnihotrī yaḥ satyam vadati iti ukte na satya vadanena agnihotri tvam
kena tarhi
agnihotreṇa eva
tat satya vadanam tu agnihotriṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ ucyate
tathā eṣa tu vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti ukte na satya vadanena ativādi tvam
kena tarhi
prakṛtena prāṇa vijñānena eva
satya vadanam tu prāṇa vidaḥ viśeṣaḥ vivakṣyate iti na iti brūmaḥ
śruti artha parityāga prasaṅgāt
śrutyā hi atra satya vadanena ativādi tvam pratīyate yaḥ satyena ativadati saḥ u tivadati iti
na atra prāṇa vijñānasya saṃkīrtanam asti
prakaraṇāt tu prāṇa vijñānam saṃbadhyeta
tatra prakaraṇa anurodhena śrutiḥ parityaktā syāt
prakṛta vyāvṛtti arthaḥ ca tu śabdaḥ na saṃgaccheta eṣa tu vai ativadati iti
satyam tu eva vijijñāsitavyam iti ca prayatna antara karaṇam artha antara vivakṣām sūcayati
tasmāt yathā eka veda praśaṃsāyām prakṛtāyām eṣa tu mahābrāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ caturaḥ vedān adhīte iti eka vedebhyaḥ rtha antara bhūtaḥ catur vedaḥ praśasyate tādṛś etat draṣṭavyam
na ca praśna prativacana rūpayā evā artha antara vivakṣayā bhavitavyam iti
prakṛta saṃbandha asaṃbhava kārita tvāt artha antara vivakṣāyāḥ
tatra prāṇa antam anuśāsanam śrutvā tūṣṇīṃbhūtam nāradam svayam eva sanatkumāraḥ vyutpādayati yat prāṇa vijñānena vikāra anṛta viṣayeṇa ativādi tvam anativādi tvam eva tat eṣa tu vai ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti
tatra satyam iti param brahma ucyate paramārtha rūpa tvāt
satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti ca śruti antarāt
tathā vyutpātitāya nāradāya saḥ u ham bhagavaḥ satyena ativadāni iti evam pravṛttāya vijñāna ādi sādhana paraṃparayā bhūmānam upadiśati
tatra yat prāṇāt adhi satyam vaktavyam pratijñātam tat eva iha bhūmā iti ucyate iti gamyate
tasmāt asti prāṇāt adhi bhūmnaḥ upadeśaḥ iti atas prāṇāt anyaḥ paramātmā bhūmā bhavitum arhati iti
evam ca iha ātma vividiṣayā prakaraṇasya utthānam upapannam bhaviṣyati
prāṇaḥ eva iha ātmā vivakṣitaḥ iti etat api na upapadyate
na hi prāṇasya mukhyayā vṛttyā ātma tvam asti
na ca anyatra paramātma jñānāt śoka vinivṛttiḥ asti na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate yanāyaḥ iti śruti antarāt
tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu iti ca upakramya upasaṃharati tasmai mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāram darśayati bhagavān sanatkumāraḥ iti
tamaḥ iti śoka ādi kāraṇam avidyā ucyeta
prāṇa ante ca anuśāsane na prāṇasya anya āyatta tā ucyate
ātmataḥ prāṇaḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam
prakaraṇa ante paramātma vivakṣā bhaviṣyati
bhūmā atra prāṇaḥ eva iti ced na
sa bhagavaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti sve mahimni ityādinā bhūmnaḥ eva ā prakaraṇa samāpteḥ anukarṣaṇāt
vaipulya ātmikā ca bhūma rūpatā sarva kāraṇa tvāt paramātmanaḥ sutarām upapadyate
dharma upapatteḥ ca
api ca ye bhūmni śrūyante dharmāḥ te paramātmani upapadyante
yatra na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anyat vijānāti sa bhūmā iti darśana ādi vyavahāra abhāvam bhūmani avagamayati
paramātmani ca ayam darśana ādi vyavahāra abhāvaḥ vagataḥ yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet ityādi śruti antarāt
yaḥ pi asau suṣupti avasthāyām darśana ādi vyavahāra abhāvaḥ uktaḥ saḥ pi ātmanaḥ eva asaṅga tva vivakṣayā uktaḥ na prāṇa svabhāva vivakṣayā paramātma prakaraṇāt
yat api tasyām avasthāyām sukham uktam tat api ātmanaḥ eva sukha rūpatva vivakṣayā uktam
yatas āha eṣaḥ u sya paramaḥ ānandaḥ etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti iti
iha api yaḥ vai bhūmā tat sukham na alpe sukham asti bhūmā eva sukham iti sāmaya sukha nirākaraṇena brahma eva sukham bhūmānam darśayati
yaḥ vai bhūmā tat amṛtam iti amṛta tvam api iha śrūyamāṇam parama kāraṇam gamayati
vikārāṇām amṛta tvasya āpekṣika tvāt atas iti ca śruti antarāt
tathā ca satya tvam sva mahima pratiṣṭhita tvam sarvagata tvam sarva ātma tvam iti ca ete dharmāḥ śrūyamāṇāḥ paramātmani eva upapadyante na anyatra
tasmāt bhūmā paramātmā iti siddham
akṣaram ambara anta dhṛteḥ
akṣara adhikaraṇam
kasmin nu khalu ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca potaḥ ca iti sa ha uvāca etat vai tat akṣaram gārgi brāhmaṇāḥ abhivadanti a sthūlam an aṇu ityādi śrūyate
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim akṣara śabdena varṇaḥ ucyate kim vā parameśvaraḥ iti
tatra akṣara samāmnāyaḥ ityādau akṣara śabdasya varṇe prasiddha tvāt prasiddhi atikramya ca ayukta tvāt oṃkāraḥ eva idam sarvam ityādau ca śruti antare varṇasya api upāsya tvena sarva ātmaka tva avadhāraṇāt varṇaḥ eva akṣara śabdaḥ iti evam prāpte ucyate paraḥ eva ātmā akṣara śabda vācyaḥ
kasmāt
ambara anta dhṛteḥ pṛthivī ādeḥ ākāśa antasya vikāra jātasya dhāraṇāt
tatra hi pṛthivī ādeḥ samasta vikāra jātasya kāla traya vibhaktasya ākāśe eva tadā ūtam ca protam ca iti ākāśe pratiṣṭhita tvam uktvā kasmin nu khalu ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti anena praśnena idam akṣaram avatāritam
tathā ca upasaṃhṛtam etasmin nu khalu akṣare gārgya ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti
na ca iyam ambara anta dhṛtiḥ brahmaṇaḥ nyatra saṃbhavati
yat api oṃkāraḥ eva idam sarvam iti tat api brahma pratipatti sādhanatvāt stuti artham draṣṭavyam
tasmin na kṣarati aśnute ca iti nitya tva vyāpi tvābhyām akṣaram param eva brahma
syāt etat kāryasya ced kāraṇa adhīna tvam ambara anta dhṛtiḥ abhyupagamyate pradhāna kāraṇa vādinā u pi iyam upapadyate
katham ambara anta dhṛteḥ brahmatva pratipattiḥ iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
sā ca praśāsanāt
sā ca ambara anta dhṛtiḥ parameśvarasya eva karma
kasmāt
praśāsanāt
praśāsanam hi iha śrūyate etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādi
praśāsanam ca pārameśvaram karma
na acetanasya praśāsanam bhavati
na hi acetanānām ghaṭa ādi kāraṇānām mṛd ādīnām ghaṭa ādi viṣayam praśāsanam asti
anya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ ca
anya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ ca kāraṇāt brahma eva akṣara śabda vācyam tasya eva ambara anta dhṛtiḥ karma nā anyasya kasyacid
kim idam anya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ iti
anyasya bhāvaḥ nyabhāvaḥ tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ anya bhāva vyāvṛttiḥ iti tasyāḥ
etat uktam bhavati yat anyat brahmaṇaḥ kṣara śabda vācyam iha āśaṅkyate tad bhāvāt idam ambara anta vidhāraṇam akṣaram vyāvartayati śrutiḥ tat vai etat akṣaram gārgi a dṛṣṭam draṣṭṛ a śrutam śrotṛ a matam mantṛ a vijñātam vijñātṛ iti
tatra adṛṣṭa tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ pradhānasya api saṃbhavati
draṣṭṛ tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ tu na tasya saṃbhavati acetana tvāt
tathā na anyat atas sti draṣṭṛ na anyat atas sti śrotṛ na anyat atas sti mantṛ na anyat atas sti vijñātṛ iti ātma bheda pratiṣedhāt na śārīrasya api upādhimataḥ kṣara śabda vācya tvam
acakṣuṣkam aśrotram avāgamanaḥ iti ca upādhimat tā pratiṣedhāt
na hi nirupādhikaḥ śārīraḥ nāma bhavati
tasmāt param eva brahma akṣaram iti niścayaḥ
īkṣati karma vyapadeśāt saḥ
īkṣati karma adhikaraṇam
etat vai satyakāma param ca aparam ca brahma yat oṃkāraḥ tasmāt vidvān etena eva āyatanena ekataram anveti iti prakṛtya śrūyate yaḥ punar etam tri mātreṇa ūm iti etena eva akṣareṇa param puruṣam abhidhyāyīta iti
kim asmin vākye param brahma abhidhyātavyam upadiśyate āhosvit aparam iti
etena eva āyatanena param aparam vā ekataram anveti iti prakṛta tvāt saṃśayaḥ
tatra aparam idam brahma iti prāptam
kasmāt
sa tejasi sūrye saṃpannaḥ sa sāmabhiḥ unnīyate brahma lokam iti ca tad vidaḥ deśa paricchinnasya phalasya ucyamāna tvāt
na hi para brahma vid deśa paricchinnam phalam aśnuvīta iti yuktam
sarva gata tvāt parasya brahmaṇaḥ
nanu apara brahma parigrahe param puruṣam iti viśeṣaṇam na upapadyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ piṇḍa apekṣayā prāṇasya para tva upapatteḥ
iti evam prāpte abhidhīyate
param eva brahma iha abhidhyātavyam upadiśyate
kasmāt
īkṣati karma vyapadeśāt
īkṣatiḥ darśanam
darśana vyāpyam īkṣati karma
īkṣati karma tvena asya abhidhyātavyasya puruṣasya vākyaśeṣe vyapadeśaḥ bhavati saḥ etasmāt jīva ghanāt parātparam puriśayam puruṣam īkṣate iti
tatra abhidhyāyateḥ atathābhūtam api vastu karma bhavati manoratha kalpitasya api abhidhyāyati karma tvāt
īkṣateḥ tu tathābhūtam eva vastu loke karma dṛṣṭam iti atas paramātmā eva ayam samyak darśana viṣaya bhūtaḥ īkṣati karma tvena vyapadiṣṭaḥ iti gamyate
saḥ eva ca iha para puruṣa śabdābhyām abhidhyātavyaḥ pratyabhijñāyate
nanu abhidhyāne paraḥ puruṣaḥ uktaḥ īkṣaṇe tu parātparaḥ
katham itaraḥ itaratra pratyabhijñāyate iti atra ucyate para puruṣa śabdau tāvat ubhayatra sādhāraṇau
na ca atra jīva ghana śabdena prakṛtaḥ bhidhyātavyaḥ paraḥ puruṣaḥ parāmṛśyate
yena tasmāt parātparaḥ yam īkṣitavyaḥ puruṣaḥ nyaḥ syāt
kaḥ tarhi jīvaghanaḥ iti ucyate ghanaḥ mūrtiḥ jīva lakṣaṇaḥ ghanaḥ jīvaghanaḥ
saindhava khilya vat yaḥ paramātmanaḥ jīva rūpaḥ khilya bhāvaḥ upādhi kṛtaḥ paraḥ ca viṣaya indriyebhyaḥ saḥ tra jīva ghanaḥ iti
aparaḥ āha sa sāmabhiḥ unnīyate brahma lokam iti atīta anantara vākya nirdiṣṭaḥ yaḥ brahma lokaḥ paras ca loka antarebhyaḥ saḥ tra jīva ghanaḥ iti ucyate
jīvānām hi sarveṣām karaṇa parivṛtānām sarva karaṇa ātmani hiraṇyagarbhe brahma loka nivāsini saṃghāta upapatteḥ bhavati brahma lokaḥ jīva ghanaḥ
tasmāt paraḥ yaḥ puruṣaḥ paramātmā īkṣaṇa karma bhūtaḥ saḥ eva abhidhyāne pi karma bhūtaḥ iti gamyate
param puruṣam iti ca viśeṣaṇam paramātma parigrahe eva avakalpate
paraḥ hi puruṣaḥ paramātmā eva bhavati yasmāt param kiṃcid anyat na asti
puruṣāt na param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti ca śruti antarāt
param ca aparam ca brahma yat oṃkāraḥ iti ca vibhajya anantaram oṃkāreṇa param puruṣam abhidhyātavyam bruvan param eva brahma param puruṣam gamayati
yathā pāda udaraḥ tvacā vinirmucyate evam ha vai sa pāpmanā vinirmucyate iti pāpma vinirmoka phala vacanam paramātmānam iha abhidhyātavyam sūcayati
atha yat uktam paramātma abhidhyāyinaḥ na deśa paricchinnam phalam yujyate iti atra ucyate tri mātreṇa oṃkāreṇa ālambanena paramātmānam abhidhyāyataḥ phalam brahma loka prāptiḥ krameṇa ca samyak darśana utpattiḥ iti krama mukti abhiprāyam etat bhaviṣyati iti adoṣaḥ
daharaḥ uttarebhyaḥ
dahara adhikaraṇam
atha yat idam asmin brahma pure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma daharaḥ u smin antarākāśaḥ tasmin yat antar tat anveṣṭavyam tat vāva vijijñāsitavyam ityādi vākyam samāmnāyate
tatra yaḥ yam dahare hṛdaya puṇḍarīke daharaḥ ākāśaḥ śrutaḥ sa kim bhūtākāśaḥ atha vijñāna ātmā athavā paramātmā iti saṃśayyate
kutas saṃśayaḥ
ākāśa brahma pura śabdābhyām
ākāśa śabdaḥ hi ayam bhūtākāśe parasmin ca brahmaṇi prayujyamānaḥ dṛśyate
tatra kim bhūtākāśe eva daharaḥ syāt kim vā paraḥ iti saṃśayaḥ
tathā brahmapuram iti kim tasya idam puram śarīram brahmapuram athavā parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ puram brahmapuram iti
tatra jīvasya parasya vā anyatarasya pura svāminaḥ daharākāśa tve saṃśayaḥ
tatra ākāśa śabdasya bhūtākāśe rūḍha tvāt bhūtākāśaḥ eva dahara śabdaḥ iti prāptam
tasya ca dahara āyatana apekṣayā dahara tvam
yāvān vai ayam ākāśaḥ tāvān eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ iti ca bāhya abhyantara bhāva kṛta bhedasya upamāna upameya bhāvaḥ
dyāvāpṛthivī ādi ca tasmin antar samāhitam avakāśa ātmanā ākāśasya ekatvāt
athavā jīvaḥ daharaḥ iti prāptam brahma pura śabdāt
jīvasya hi idam puram sat śarīram brahmapuram iti ucyate tasya sva karmaṇā upārjita tvāt
bhaktyā ca tasya brahma śabda vācya tvam
na hi parasya brahmaṇaḥ śarīreṇa sva svāmi bhāvaḥ saṃbandhaḥ sti
tatra pura svāminaḥ pura eka deśe dṛṣṭam yathā rājñaḥ
manaupādhikaḥ ca jīvaḥ
manaḥ ca prāyeṇa hṛdaye pratiṣṭhitam iti atas jīvasya eva idam hṛdaya antar avasthānam syāt
dahara tvam api tasya eva ārā agra upamita tvāt avakalpate
ākāśa upamita tva ādi ca brahma abheda vivakṣayā bhaviṣyati
na ca atra daharasya ākāśasya anveṣṭavya tvam vijijñāsitavya tvam ca śrūyate
tasmin yat antar iti para viśeṣaṇa tvena upādānāt iti
atas uttaram brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva atra daharākāśaḥ bhavitum arhati na bhūtākāśaḥ jīvaḥ vā
kasmāt
uttarebhyaḥ vākyaśeṣa gatebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ
tathā hi anveṣṭavya tayā abhihitasya daharākāśasya tam ced brūyuḥ iti upakramya kim tat atra vidyate yat anveṣṭavyam yat vāva vijijñāsitavyam iti evam ākṣepa pūrvakam pratisamādhāna vacanam bhavati sa brūyāt yāvān vai ayam ākāśaḥ tāvān eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśe ubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī antar eva samāhite ityādi
tatra puṇḍarīka dahara tvena prāpta dahara tvasya ākāśasya prasiddha ākāśa aupamyena dahara tvam nivartayan bhūtākāśa tvam daharasya ākāśasya nivartayati iti gamyate
yadi api ākāśa śabdaḥ bhūtākāśe rūḍhaḥ tathā api tena eva tasya upamā na upapadyate iti bhūtākāśa śaṅkā nivartitā bhavati
nanu ekasya api ākāśasya bāhya abhyantara tva kalpitena bhedena upamāna upameya bhāvaḥ saṃbhavati iti uktam
na evam saṃbhavati
agatikā hi iyam gatiḥ yat kālpanika bheda āśrayaṇam
api ca kalpayitvā bhedam upamāna upameya bhāvam varṇayataḥ paricchinna tvāt abhyantara ākāśasya na bāhya ākāśa parimāṇa tvam upapadyeta
nanu parameśvarasya api jyāyān ākāśāt iti śruti antarāt na eva ākāśa parimāṇa tvam upapadyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ
puṇḍarīka veṣṭana prāpta daharatva nivṛtti paratvāt vākyasya na tāvattva pratipādana paratvam
ubhaya pratipādane hi vākyam bhidyeta
na ca kalpita bhede puṇḍarīka veṣṭite ākāśa eka deśe dyāvāpṛthivya ādīnām antar samādhānam upapadyate
eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ viśokaḥ vijighatsaḥ pipāsaḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti ca ātma tva apahata pāpma tva ādayaḥ ca guṇāḥ na bhūta ākāśe saṃbhavanti
yadi api ātma śabdaḥ jīve saṃbhavati tathā api itarebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ jīva āśaṅkā api nivartitā bhavati
na hi upādhi paricchinnasya arā agra upamitasya jīvasya puṇḍarīka veṣṭana kṛtam dahara tvam śakyam nivartayitum
brahma abheda vivakṣayā jīvasya sarvagata tva ādi vivakṣyeta iti ced
yad ātmatayā jīvasya sarvagata tva ādi vivakṣyeta tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ sākṣāt sarvagata tva ādi vivakṣyatām iti yuktam
yat api uktam brahmapuram iti jīvena purasya upalakṣita tvāt rājñaḥ iva jīvasya eva idam pura svāminaḥ pura eka deśa varti tvam astu iti
atra brūmaḥ parasya eva idam brahmaṇaḥ puram sat śarīram brahmapuram iti ucyate brahma śabdasya tasmin mukhya tvāt
tasya api asti pureṇa anena saṃbandhaḥ upalabdhi adhiṣṭhāna tvāt saḥ etasmāt jīva ghanāt parātparam puriśayam puruṣam īkṣate sa vai ayam puruṣaḥ sarvāsu pūrṣu puriśayaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
athavā jīva pure eva asmin brahma saṃnihitam upalakṣyate yathā sālagrāme viṣṇuḥ saṃnihitaḥ iti tadvat
tat yathā iha karma citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate evam eva amutra puṇya citaḥ lokaḥ kṣīyate iti ca karmaṇām antavat phala tvam uktvā atha ye iha ātmānam anuvidya vrajanti etān ca satyān kāmān teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati iti prakṛta dahar ākāśa vijñānasya ananta phala tvam vadan paramātma tvam asya sūcayati
yat api etat uktam na daharasya ākāśasya anveṣṭavya tvam vijijñāsitavya tvam ca śrutam para viśeṣaṇa tvena upādānāt iti
atra brūmaḥ yadi ākāśaḥ na anveṣṭavya tvena uktaḥ syāt yāvān vai ayam ākāśaḥ tāvān eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ ityādi ākāśa svarūpa pradarśanam na upapadyeta
nanu etat api antar varti vastu sadbhāva darśanāya eva pradarśyate tam ced brūyuḥ yat idam asmin brahma pure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma daharaḥ smin antar ākāśaḥ kim tat atra vidyate yat anveṣṭavyam yat vāva vijijñāsitavyam iti ākṣipya parihāra avasare ākāśa aupamya upakrameṇa dyau ā pṛthivī ādīnām antar samāhita tva pradarśanāt
na etat evam
evam hi sati yat antar samāhitam dyāvāpṛthivya ādi tat anveṣṭavyam vijijñāsitavyam ca uktam syāt
tatra vākyaśeṣaḥ na upapadyeta
asmin kāmāḥ samāhitāḥ eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti hi prakṛtam dyāvāpṛthivya ādi samādhāna ādhāram ākāśam ākṛṣya atha ye iha ātmānam anuvidya vrajanti etān ca satyān kāmān iti samuccaya arthena ca śabdena ātmānam kāma ādhāram āśritān ca kāmān vijñeyān vākya śeṣaḥ darśayati
tasmāt vākya upakrame daharaḥ eva ākāśaḥ hṛdaya puṇḍarīka adhiṣṭhānaḥ saha antar sthaiḥ samāhitaiḥ pṛthivī ādibhiḥ satyaiḥ ca kāmaiḥ vijñeyaḥ uktaḥ iti gamyate
sa ca uktebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ parameśvaraḥ iti sthitam
gati śabdābhyām tathā hi dṛṣṭam liṅgam ca
daharaḥ parameśvaraḥ uttarebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ iti uktam
te eva uttare hetavaḥ idānīm prapañcyante
itas ca parameśvaraḥ eva daharaḥ
yasmāt dahara vākya śeṣe parameśvarasya eva pratipādakau gati śabdau bhavataḥ imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ ahar ahar gacchantyaḥ etam brahma lokam na vindanti iti
tatra prakṛtam daharam brahma loka śabdena abhidhāya tad viṣayā gatiḥ prajā śabda vācyānām jīvānām abhidhīyamānā daharasya brahma tām gamayati
tathā hi aharahar jīvānām suṣupta avasthāyām brahma viṣayam gamanam dṛṣṭam śruti antare satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati iti evamādau
loke kila gāḍham suṣuptam ācakṣate brahmībhūtaḥ brahmatām gataḥ iti
tathā brahma loka śabdaḥ pi prakṛte dahare prayujyamānaḥ jīva bhūta ākāśa āśaṅkām nivartayan brahma tām asya gamayati
nanu kamalāsana lokam api brahma loka śabdaḥ gamayet
gamayet yadi brahmaṇaḥ loke iti ṣaṣṭhī samāsa vṛttyā vyutpādyeta
sāmānādhikaraṇya vṛttyā tu vyutpādyamānaḥ brahma eva lokaḥ brahma lokaḥ iti param eva brahma gamayiṣyati
etat eva ca aharahar brahmaloka gamanam dṛṣṭam brahmaloka śabdasya sāmānādhikaraṇya vṛtti parigrahe liṅgam
na hi ahar ahar imāḥ prajāḥ kārya brahma lokam satya loka ākhyam gacchanti iti śakyam kalpayitum
dhṛteḥ ca mahimnaḥ sya asmin upalabdheḥ
dhṛteḥ ca hetoḥ parameśvaraḥ eva ayam daharaḥ
katham
daharaḥ smin antarākāśaḥ iti hi prakṛtyai ākāśa aupamya pūrvakam tasmin sarva samādhānam uktvā tasmin eva ca ātma śabdam prayujya apahatapāpma tva ādi guṇa yogam ca upadiśya tam eva anativṛtta prakaraṇam nirdiśati atha yaḥ ātmā sa setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ eṣām lokānām a saṃbhedāya iti
tatra vidhṛtiḥ iti ātma śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyāt vidhārayitā ucyate
kticaḥ kartari smaraṇāt
yathā udaka saṃtānasya vidhārayitā loke setuḥ kṣetra saṃpadām a saṃbhedāya evam ayam ātmā eṣām adhyātma ādi bheda bhinnānām lokānām varṇa āśrama ādīnām ca vidhārayitā setuḥ a saṃbhedāya a saṃkarāya iti
evam iha prakṛte dahare vidharaṇa lakṣaṇam mahimānam darśayati
ayam ca mahimā parameśvaraḥ eva śruti antarāt upalabhyate etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādeḥ
tathā anyatra api niścite parameśvara vākye śrūyate eṣa sarva īśvaraḥ eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ eṣa bhūta pālaḥ eṣa setuḥ vidharaṇaḥ eṣām lokānām a saṃbhedāya iti
evam dhṛteḥ ca hetoḥ parameśvaraḥ eva ayam daharaḥ
prasiddheḥ ca
itas ca parameśvaraḥ eva daharaḥ smin antarākāśaḥ iti ucyate
yatkāraṇam ākāśa śabdaḥ parameśvare prasiddhaḥ ākāśaḥ vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante iti ādi prayoga darśanāt
jīve tu na kvacid ākāśa śabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ dṛśyate
bhūtākāśaḥ tu satyām api ākāśa śabda prasiddhau upamāna upameya bhāva ādi asaṃbhavāt na grahītavyaḥ iti uktam
itara parāmarśāt saḥ iti ced na asambhavāt
yadi vākyaśeṣa balena daharaḥ iti parameśvaraḥ parigṛhyeta asti hi itarasya api jīvasya vākyaśeṣe parāmarśaḥ atha yaḥ eṣa saṃprasādaḥ u smāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate eṣaḥ ātmā iti ha uvāca iti
atra hi saṃprasāda śabdaḥ śruti antare suṣupta avasthāyām dṛṣṭa tvāt avasthāvantam jīvam śaknoti upasthāpayitum na artha antaram
tathā śarīra vyapāśrayasya eva jīvasya śarīrāt samutthānam saṃbhavati yathā ākāśa vyapāśrayāṇām vāyu ādīnām ākāśāt samutthānam tadvat
yathā ca adṛṣṭaḥ api loke parameśvara viṣayaḥ ākāśa śabdaḥ parameśvara dharma samabhivyāhārāt ākāśaḥ vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā iti evamādau parameśvara viṣayaḥ bhyupagataḥ evam jīva viṣayaḥ api bhaviṣyati
tasmāt itara parāmarśāt daharaḥ smin antarākāśaḥ iti atra saḥ eva jīvaḥ ucyate iti ced na etat evam syāt
kasmāt
asaṃbhavāt
na hi jīvaḥ buddhi ādi upādhi pariccheda abhimānī san ākāśena upamīyeta
na ca upādhi dharmān abhimanyamānasya apahatapāpma tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ saṃbhavanti
prapañcitam ca etat prathame sūtre
atireka āśaṅkā parihārāya atra tu punar upanyastam
paṭhiṣyati ca upariṣṭāt anya arthaḥ ca parāmarśaḥ iti
uttarāt ced āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ tu
itara parāmarśāt yā jīva āśaṅkā jātā sā asaṃbhavāt nirākṛtā
atha idānīm mṛtasya iva amṛta sekāt punar samutthānam jīva āśaṅkāyāḥ kriyate uttarasmāt prājāpatyāt vākyāt
tatra hi yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam ātmānam anveṣṭavyam vijijñāsitavyam ca pratijñāya yaḥ eṣaḥ
akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate eṣaḥ ātmā iti bruvan akṣi stham draṣṭāram jīvam ātmānam nirdiśati
etam tu eva te bhūyas
anuvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca tam eva punar punar parāmṛśya yaḥ eṣa svapne mahīyamānaḥ carati eṣaḥ ātmā iti tat yatra etat suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasannaḥ svapnam na vijānāti eṣaḥ ātmā iti ca jīvam eva avasthā antara gatam vyācaṣṭe
tasya eva ca apahata pāpma tva ādi darśayati etat amṛtam abhayam etat brahma iti
na aha khalu ayam evam saṃprati ātmānam jānāti ayam aham asmi iti na u eva imāni bhūtāni iti ca suṣupta avasthāyām doṣam upalabhya etam tu eva te bhūyas
anuvyākhyāsyāmi no eva anyatra etasmāt iti ca upakramya śarīra saṃbandha nindā pūrvakam eṣa saṃprasādaḥ
asmāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti jīvam eva śarīrāt samutthitam uttamam puruṣam darśayati
tasmāt asti saṃbhavaḥ jīve pārameśvarāṇām dharmāṇām
ataḥ daharo
asmin antar ākāśaḥ iti jīvaḥ eva uktaḥ iti ced kaścid brūyāt
tam prati brūyāt āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ tu iti
tu śabdaḥ pūrvapakṣa vyāvṛtti arthaḥ
na uttarasmāt api vākyāt iha jīvasya āśaṅkā saṃbhavati iti arthaḥ
kasmāt
yatas tatra api āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ jīvaḥ vivakṣyate
āvirbhūtam sva rūpam asya iti āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ
bhūta pūrva gatyāḥ jīva vacanam
etat uktam bhavati yaḥ eṣa
akṣiṇi iti akṣi lakṣitam draṣṭāram nirdiśya udaśarāva brāhmaṇena enam śarīra ātma tayā vyutthāpya etam tu eva te iti punar punar tam eva vyākhyeya tvena ākṛṣya svapna suṣupta upanyāsa krameṇa param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti yat asya pāramārthikam svarūpam param brahma tad rūpa tayā enam jīvam vyācaṣṭe
na jaivena rūpeṇa
yat tat param jyotiḥ upasaṃpattavyam śrutam tat param brahma
tat ca apahata pāpma tva ādi dharmakam
tat eva ca jīvasya pāramārthikam svarūpam tat tvam asi ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ na itarat upādhi kalpitam
yāvat eva hi sthāṇau iva puruṣa buddhim dvaita lakṣaṇām avidyām nivartayan kūṭastha nitya dṛś svarūpam ātmānam aham brahma asmi iti na pratipadyate tāvat jīvasya jīva tvam
yadā tu deha indriya manaḥ buddhi saṃghātāt vyutthāpya śrutyā pratibodhyate na asi tvam deha indriya manaḥ buddhi saṃghātaḥ na api saṃsārī kim tarhi tat yat satyam saḥ ātmā caitanya mātra svarūpaḥ tat tvam asi iti
tadā kūṭastha nitya dṛś svarūpam ātmānam pratibudhya asmāt śarīra ādi abhimānāt samuttiṣṭhan saḥ eva kūṭastha nitya dṛś svarūpaḥ ātmā bhavati sa yaḥ ha vai tat paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
tat eva ca asya pāramārthikam svarūpam yena śarīrāt samutthāya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate
katham punar svam ca rūpam svena eva ca niṣpadyate iti saṃbhavati kūṭastha nityasya
suvarṇa ādīnām tu dravya antara saṃparkāt abhibhūta sva rūpāṇām anabhivyakta asādhāraṇa viśeṣāṇām kṣāra prakṣepa ādibhiḥ śodhyamānānām sva rūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ syāt
tathā nakṣatra ādīnām ahani abhibhūta prakāśānām abhibhāvaka viyoge rātrau sva rūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ syāt
na tu tathā ātma caitanya jyotiṣaḥ nityasya kenacid abhibhavaḥ saṃbhavati a saṃsargi tvāt vyomnaḥ iva dṛṣṭa virodhāt ca
dṛṣṭi śrutim ati vijñātayaḥ hi jīvasya svarūpam
tat ca śarīrāt asamutthitasya api jīvasya sadā niṣpannam eva dṛśyate
sarvaḥ hi jīvaḥ paśyan śrṛṇvan manvānaḥ vijānan vyavaharati anyathā vyavahāra anupapatteḥ
tat ced śarīrāt samutthitasya niṣpadyeta prāk samutthānāt dṛṣṭaḥ vyavahāraḥ virudhyeta
atas kimātmakam idam śarīrāt samutthānam kim ātmikā vā svarūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ iti
atrā ucyate prāk viveka vijñāna utpatteḥ śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi viṣaya vedanā upādhibhiḥ aviviktam iva jīvasya dṛṣṭi ādi jyotiḥ svarūpam bhavati
yathā śuddhasya sphaṭikasya svācchyam śauklyam ca svarūpam prāk viveka grahaṇāt rakta nīla ādi upādhibhiḥ aviviktam iva bhavati
pramāṇa janita viveka grahaṇāt tu parācīnaḥ sphaṭikaḥ svācchyena śauklyena ca svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti ucyate prāk api tathā eva san
tathā deha ādi upādhya viviktasya eva sataḥ jīvasya śruti kṛtam viveka vijñānam śarīrāt samutthānam viveka vijñāna phalam sva rūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ kevala ātma svarūpa avagatiḥ
tathā viveka aviveka mātreṇa eva ātmanaḥ
aśarīra tvam sa śarīra tvam ca mantra varṇāt aśarīram śarīreṣu iti
api kaunteya na karoti na lipyate iti ca sa śarīra tva aśarīra tva viśeṣa abhāva smaraṇāt
tasmāt viveka vijñāna abhāvāt anāvirbhūta svarūpaḥ san viveka vijñānāt āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ iti ucyate
na tu anyādṛśau āvirbhāva anāvirbhāvau svarūpasya saṃbhavataḥ sva rūpa tvāt eva
evam mithyā jñāna kṛtaḥ eva jīva parameśvarayoḥ bhedaḥ na vastu kṛtaḥ
vyoma vat asaṅga tva aviśeṣāt
kutas ca etat evam pratipattavyam
yatas yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti upadiśya etat amṛtam abhayam etat brahma iti upadiśati
yaḥ kṣiṇi prasiddhaḥ draṣṭā draṣṭṛ tvena vibhāvyate saḥ mṛta abhaya lakṣaṇāt brahmaṇaḥ ced syāt tatas mṛta abhaya brahma sāmānādhikaraṇyam na syāt
nā api praticchāyā ātmā ayam akṣi lakṣitaḥ nirdiśyate prajāpateḥ mṛṣāvādi tva prasaṅgāt
tathā dvitīye pi paryāye yaḥ eṣa svapne mahīyamānaḥ carati iti na prathama paryāya nirdiṣṭāt akṣi puruṣāt draṣṭuḥ anyaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ etam tu eva te bhūyas nuvyākhyāsyāmi iti upakramāt
kiṃca aham adya svapne hastinam adrākṣam na idānīm tam paśyāmi iti dṛṣṭam eva pratibuddhaḥ pratyācaṣṭe
draṣṭāram tu tam eva pratyabhijānāti yaḥ eva aham svapnam adrākṣam saḥ eva aham jāgaritam paśyāmi iti
tathā tṛtīye pi paryāye na āha khalu ayam evam saṃprati ātmānam jānāti ayam aham asmi iti na u eva imāni bhūtāni iti suṣupta avasthāyām viśeṣa vijñāna abhāvam eva darśayati na vijñātāram pratiṣedhati
yat tu tatra vināśam eva api itas bhavati iti tat api viśeṣa vijñāna vināśa abhiprāyam eva na vijñātṛ vināśa abhiprāyam
na hi vijñātuḥ vijñāteḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate vināśi tvāt iti śruti antarāt
tathā caturthe pi paryāye etam tu eva te bhūyas nuvyākhyāsyāmi no eva anyatra etasmāt iti upakramya maghavat martyam vai idam śarīram ityādinā prapañcena śarīra ādi upādhi saṃbandha pratyākhyānena saṃprasāda śabda uditam jīvam svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti brahma svarūpa āpannam darśayan na parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ mṛta abhaya svarūpāt anyam jīvam darśayati
kecid tu paramātma vivakṣāyām etam tu eva te iti jīva ākarṣaṇam anyāyyam manyamānāḥ etam eva vākya upakrama sūcitam apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam ātmānam te bhūyas nuvyākhyāsyāmi iti kalpayanti
teṣām etam iti saṃnihita avalambinī sarvanāma śrutiḥ viprakṛṣyeta
bhūyas śrutiḥ ca uparudhyeta
paryāya antara abhihitasya paryāya antareṇa an abhidhīyamāna tvāt
etam tu eva te iti ca pratijñāya prāk caturthāt paryāyāt anyam anyam vyācakṣāṇasya prajāpateḥ pratāraka tvam prasajyeta
tasmāt yat avidyā pratyupasthāpitam apāramārthikam jaivam rūpam kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa kaluṣitam aneka anartha yogi tad vilayanena tad viparītam apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam pārameśvaram svarūpam vidyayā pratipadyate sarpa ādi vilayanena iva rajju ādīn
apare tu vādinaḥ pāramārthikam eva jaivam rūpam iti manyante smadīyāḥ ca kecid
teṣām sarveṣām ātma ekatva samyagdarśana pratipakṣa bhūtānām pratiṣedhāya idam śārīrakam ārabdham ekaḥ eva parameśvaraḥ kūṭastha nityaḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ avidyayā māyayā māyāvi vat anekadhā vibhāvyate na anyaḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ asti iti
yat tu idam parameśvara vākye jīvam āśaṅkya pratiṣedhati sūtrakāraḥ na asaṃbhavāt ityādinā tatra ayam abhiprāyaḥ nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāve kūṭastha nitye ekasmin asaṅge paramātmani tad viparītam jaivam rūpam vyomni iva tala mala ādi parikalpitam
tat ātma ekatva pratipādana paraiḥ vākyaiḥ nyāya upetaiḥ dvaita vāda pratiṣedhaiḥ ca apaneṣyāmi iti paramātmanaḥ jīvāt anyatvam draḍhayati
jīvasya tu na parasmāt anya tvam
kim tu anuvadati eva avidyā kalpitam loka prasiddham jīva bhedam
evam hi svābhāvika kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva anuvādena pravṛttāḥ karma vidhayaḥ na virudhyante iti manyate
pratipādyam tu śāstra artham ātma ekatvam eva darśayati śāstra dṛṣṭyā tu upadeśaḥ vāmadeva vat ityādinā
varṇitaḥ ca asmābhiḥ vidvat avidvat bhedena karma vidhi virodha parihāraḥ
anya arthaḥ ca parāmarśaḥ
atha yaḥ yam dahara vākya śeṣe jīva parāmarśaḥ darśitaḥ atha yaḥ eṣa saṃprasādaḥ ityādiḥ sa dahare parameśvare vyākhyāyamāne na jīva upāsana upadeśaḥ na api prakṛta viśeṣa upadeśaḥ iti anarthaka tvam prāpnoti iti atas āha anya arthaḥ yam jīva parāmarśaḥ na jīva svarūpa paryavasāyī
kim tarhi parameśvara svarūpa paryavasāyī
katham
saṃprasāda śabda uditaḥ jīvaḥ jāgarita vyavahāre deha indriya pañjara adhyakṣaḥ bhūtvā tad vāsanā nirmitān ca svapnān nāḍīcaraḥ nubhūya śrāntaḥ śaraṇam prepsuḥ ubhaya rūpāt api śarīra abhimānāt samutthāya suṣupta avasthāyām param jyotiḥ ākāśa śabditam param brahma upasaṃpadya viśeṣa vijñānavat tvam ca parityajya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate
yat asya upasaṃpattavyam param jyotiḥ yena svena rūpeṇa ayam abhiniṣpadyate saḥ eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ upāsyaḥ iti evam arthaḥ yam jīva parāmarśaḥ parameśvara vādinā u pi upapadyate
alpa śruteḥ iti ced tat uktam
yat api uktam daharaḥ smin antarākāśaḥ iti ākāśasya alpatvam śrūyamāṇam parameśvare na upapadyate jīvasya tu ārā agra upamitasya alpatvam avakalpate iti
tasya parihāraḥ vaktavyaḥ
uktaḥ hi asya parihāraḥ parameśvare
api āpekṣikam alpatvam avakalpate iti arbhaka okastvāt tad vyapadeśāt ca na iti ced na nicāyya tvāt evam vyoma vat ca iti atra
saḥ eva iha parihāraḥ
anusaṃdhātavyaḥ iti sūcayati
śrutyā eva ca idam alpa tvam pratyuktam prasiddhena ākāśena upamimānayā yāvān vai ayam ākāśaḥ tāvān eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ iti
anukṛteḥ tasya ca
anukṛti adhikaraṇam
na tatra sūryaḥ bhāti na candra tārakam na imāḥ vidyutaḥ bhānti kutas yam agniḥ
tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti samāmananti
tatra yam bhāntam anubhāti sarvam yasya ca bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti sa kim tejaḥ dhātuḥ kaścid uta prājñaḥ ātmā iti vicikitsāyām tejaḥ dhātuḥ iti tāvat prāptam
kutas
tejaḥ dhātūnām eva sūrya ādīnām bhāna pratiṣedhāt
tejaḥ svabhāvakam hi candra tārakā ādi tejaḥ svabhāvake eva sūrye bhāsamāne ahani na bhāsate iti prasiddham
tathā saha sūryeṇa sarvam idam candra tārakā ādi yasmin na bhāsate tejaḥ svabhāvaḥ eva kaścid iti avagamyate
anubhānam api tejaḥ svabhāvake eva upapadyate samāna svabhāvakeṣu anukāra darśanāt
gacchantam anugacchati itivat
tasmāt tejaḥ dhātuḥ kaścid iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ prājñaḥ eva ayam ātmā bhavitum arhati
kasmāt
anukṛteḥ
anukaraṇam anukṛtiḥ
yat etat tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam iti anubhānam tat prājña parigrahe
bhā rūpaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti hi prājñam ātmānam āmananti
na tu tejaḥ dhātum kaṃcid sūrya ādayaḥ nubhānti iti prasiddham
sama tvāt ca tejaḥ dhātūnām sūrya ādīnām na tejaḥ dhātum anyam pratyapekṣā asti yam bhāntam anubhāyuḥ
na hi pradīpaḥ pradīpa antaram anubhāti
yat api uktam samāna svabhāvakeṣu anukāraḥ dṛśyate iti na ayam ekāntaḥ niyamaḥ
bhinna svabhāvakeṣu api hi anukāraḥ dṛśyate
yathā su taptaḥ yaḥ piṇḍaḥ gni anukṛtiḥ agnim dahantam anudahati bhaumam vā rajaḥ vāyum vahantam anuvahati iti
anukṛteḥ iti anubhānam asusūcat
tasya ca iti caturtham pādam asya ślokasya sūcayati
tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti ca tad hetukam bhānam sūrya ādeḥ ucyamānam prājñam ātmānam gamayati
tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ āyuḥ ha upāsate mṛtam iti hi prājñam ātmānam āmananti
tejaḥ ntareṇa tu sūrya ādi tejaḥ vibhāti iti aprasiddham viruddham ca
tejaḥ ntareṇa tejaḥ ntarasya pratighātāt
athavā na sūrya ādīnām eva śloka paripaṭhitānām idam tad hetukam vibhānam ucyate
kim tarhi sarvam idam iti aviśeṣa śruteḥ sarvasya eva asya nāma rūpa kriyā kāraka phala jātasya yā abhivyaktiḥ sā brahma jyotiḥ sattā nimittā
yathā sūrya jyotiḥ sattā nimittā sarvasya rūpa jātasya abhivyaktiḥ tadvat
na tatra sūryaḥ bhāti iti ca tatra śabdam āharan prakṛta grahaṇam darśayati
prakṛtam ca brahma yasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī ca antarikṣam ā utam ityādinā
anantaram ca hiraṇmaye pare kośe virajam brahma niṣkalam
tat śubhram jyotiṣām jyotiḥ tat yat ātma vidaḥ viduḥ iti
katham tat jyotiṣām jyotiḥ iti atas idam utthitam na tatra sūryaḥ bhāti iti
yat api uktam sūrya ādīnām tejasām bhāna pratiṣedhaḥ tejaḥ dhātau eva anyasmin avakalpate sūryaḥ iva itareṣām iti
tatra tu saḥ eva tejaḥ dhātuḥ anyaḥ na saṃbhavati iti upapāditam
brahmaṇi api ca eṣām bhāna pratiṣedhaḥ
yatas yat upalabhyate tat sarvam brahmaṇā eva jyotiṣā upalabhyate
brahma tu na anyena jyotiṣā upalabhyate svayam jyotiḥ sva rūpa tvāt yena sūrya ādayaḥ tasmin bhāyuḥ
brahma hi anyat vyanakti na tu brahma anyena vyajyate ātmanā eva ayam jyotiṣā āste a gṛhyaḥ na hi gṛhyate ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
api ca smaryate
api ca īdṛś rūpa tvam prājñasya eva ātmanaḥ smaryate bhagavadgītāsu na tat bhāsayate sūryaḥ na śaśāṅkaḥ na pāvakaḥ
yat gatvā na nivartante tat dhāma paramam mama iti
yat āditya gatam tejaḥ jagat bhāsayate khilam
yat candramasi yat ca agnau tat tejaḥ viddhi māmakam iti ca
śabdāt eva pramitaḥ
pramita adhikaraṇam
aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ madhye ātmani tiṣṭhati iti śrūyate
tathā aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ jyotiḥ iva adhūmakaḥ
īśānaḥ bhūta bhavyasya saḥ eva adya saḥ u śvas etat vai tat iti ca
tatra yaḥ yam aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ śrūyate sa kim vijñāna ātmā kim vā paramātmā iti saṃśayaḥ
tatra parimāṇa upadeśāt vijñāna ātmā iti tāvat prāptam
na hi ananta āyāma vistārasya paramātmanaḥ ṅguṣṭha parimāṇa tvam upapadyate
vijñānātmanaḥ tu upādhimat tvāt saṃbhavati kayācid kalpanayā aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam
smṛteḥ ca atha satyavataḥ kāyāt pāśa baddham vaśam gatam
aṅguṣṭha mātram puruṣam niścakarṣa yamaḥ balāt iti
na hi parameśvaraḥ balāt yamena niṣkraṣṭum śakyaḥ
tena tatra saṃsārī aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ niścitaḥ
saḥ eva iha api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ paramātmā eva ayam aṅguṣṭha mātra parimitaḥ puruṣaḥ bhavitum arhati
kasmāt
śabdāt īśānaḥ bhūta bhavyasya iti
na hi anyaḥ parameśvarāt bhūta bhavyasya niraṅkuśam īśitā
etat vai tat iti ca prakṛtam pṛṣṭam iha anusaṃdadhāti
etat vai tat yat pṛṣṭam brahma iti arthaḥ
pṛṣṭam ca iha brahma anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt anyatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt
anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yat tat paśyasi tadvat vaḥ iti
śabdāt eva iti abhidhāna śruteḥ eva īśānaḥ iti parameśvaraḥ vagamyate iti arthaḥ
katham punar sarva gatasya paramātmanaḥ parimāṇa upadeśaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ
hṛdi apekṣayā tu manuṣya adhikāra tvāt
sarva gatasya api paramātmanaḥ hṛdaye aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam idam ucyate
ākāśasya iva vaṃśa parva apekṣam aratni mātra tvam
na hi añjasā atimātrasya paramātmanaḥ ṅguṣṭha mātra tvam upapadyate
na ca anyaḥ paramātmanaḥ iha grahaṇam arhati īśāna śabda ādibhyaḥ iti uktam
nanu prati prāṇi bhedam hṛdayānām anavasthita tvāt tad apekṣam api aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam na upapadyate iti atas uttaram ucyate manuṣya adhikāra tvāt iti
śāstram hi aviśeṣa pravṛttam api manuṣyān eva adhikaroti
śakta tvāt arthi tvāt aparyudasta tvāt upanayana ādi śāstrāt ca iti varṇitam etat adhikāra lakṣaṇe
manuṣyāṇām ca niyata parimāṇaḥ kāyaḥ
aucityena niyata parimāṇam eva ca eṣām aṅguṣṭha mātram hṛdayam
atas manuṣya adhikāra tvāt śāstrasya manuṣya hṛdaya avasthāna apekṣam aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam upapannam paramātmanaḥ
yat api uktam parimāṇa upadeśāt smṛteḥ ca saṃsārī eva ayam aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ pratyetavyaḥ iti
tat pratyucyate saḥ ātmā tattvam asi ityādi vat saṃsāriṇaḥ eva sataḥ ṅguṣṭha mātrasya brahma tvam idam upadiśyate iti
dvi rūpā hi vedānta vākyānām pravṛttiḥ kvacid paramātma svarūpa nirūpaṇa parā
kvacid vijñānātmanaḥ paramātma ekatva upadeśa parā
tat atra vijñāna ātmanaḥ paramātmanā ekatvam upadiśyate
na aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam kasyacid
etam eva artham pareṇa sphuṭīkariṣyati aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ ntarātmā sadā janānām hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭaḥ
tam svāt śarīrāt pravṛhet muñja ādi vā iṣīkām dhairyeṇa
tam vidyāt śukram amṛtam iti
tad upari api bādarāyaṇaḥ saṃbhavāt
devatā adhikaraṇam
aṅguṣṭha mātra śrutiḥ manuṣya hṛdaya apekṣā manuṣya adhikāra tvāt śāstrasya iti uktam
tad prasaṅgena idam ucyate
bāḍham manuṣyān adhikaroti śāstram
na tu manuṣyān eva iti iha brahma jñāne niyamaḥ sti
teṣām manuṣyāṇām upariṣṭāt ye deva ādayaḥ tān api adhikaroti śāstram iti bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
kasmāt
saṃbhavāt
saṃbhavati hi teṣām api arthi tva ādi adhikāra kāraṇam
tatra arthi tvam tāvat mokṣa viṣayam deva ādīnām api saṃbhavati vikāra viṣaya vibhūti anitya tva ālocanā ādi nimittam
tathā sāmarthyam api teṣām saṃbhavati mantra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa lokebhyaḥ vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt
na ca teṣām kaścid pratiṣedhaḥ sti
na ca upanayana śāstreṇa eṣām adhikāraḥ nivartyeta upanayanasya veda adhyayana artha tvāt teṣām ca svayam pratibhāta veda tvāt
api ca eṣām vidyā grahaṇa artham brahmacarya ādi darśayati ekaśatam ha vai varṣāṇi maghavān prajāpatau brahmacaryam uvāsa bhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ
varuṇam pitaram upasasāra
adhīhi bhagavaḥ brahma ityādi
yat api karmasu anadhikāra kāraṇam uktam na devānām devatā antara abhāvāt iti na ṛṣīṇām ārṣeya antara abhāvāt iti
na tad vidyāsu asti
na hi indra ādīnām vidyāsu adhikriyamāṇānām indra ādi uddeśena kiṃcid kṛtyam asti
na ca bhṛgu ādīnām bhṛgu ādi sagotra tayā
tasmāt deva ādīnām api vidyāsu adhikāraḥ kena vāryate
deva ādi adhikāre pi aṅguṣṭha mātra śrutiḥ sva aṅguṣṭha apekṣayā na virudhyeta
virodhaḥ karmaṇi iti ced na aneka pratipatteḥ darśanāt
syāt etat yadi vigrahavat tva ādi abhyupagamena deva ādīnām vidyāsu adhikāraḥ varṇyeta vigrahavat tvāt ṛtvij ādi vat indra ādīnām api svarūpa saṃnidhānena karma aṅga bhāvaḥ bhyupagamyeta
tadā ca virodhaḥ karmaṇi syāt
na hi indra ādīnām sva rūpa saṃnidhānena yāga aṅga bhāvaḥ dṛśyate
na ca saṃbhavati bahuṣu yāgeṣu yugapad ekasya indrasya sva rūpa saṃnidhāna anupapatteḥ iti ced na ayam asti virodhaḥ
kasmāt
aneka pratipatteḥ
ekasya api devatā ātmanaḥ yugapad aneka svarūpa pratipattiḥ saṃbhavati
katham etat avagamyate
darśanāt
tathā hi kati devāḥ iti upakramya trayaḥ ca trī ca śatā trayaḥ ca trī ca sahasrāḥ iti nirucya katame te iti asyām pṛcchāyām mahimānaḥ eva eṣām ete trayastriṃśat tu eva devāḥ iti bruvatī śrutiḥ ekaikasya devatā ātmanaḥ yugapad aneka rūpa tām darśayati
tathā ṣaṣ ādi antarbhāva krameṇa katamaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ iti prāṇaḥ iti prāṇa eka rūpa tām devānām darśayantī tasya eva ekasya prāṇasya yugapad aneka rūpa tām darśayati
tathā smṛtiḥ api ātmanaḥ vai śarīrāṇi bahūni bharata ṛṣabha
yogī kuryāt balam prāpya taiḥ ca sarvaiḥ mahīm caret
prāpnuyāt viṣayān kaiścid kaiścid ugram tapaḥ caret
saṃkṣipet ca punar tāni sūryaḥ raśmi gaṇān iva iti evaṃjātīyakā prāpta aṇima ādi aiśvaryāṇām yoginām api yugapad aneka śarīra yogam darśayati
kimu vaktavyam ājāna siddhānām devānām
aneka rūpa pratipatti saṃbhavāt ca ekaikā devatā bahubhiḥ rūpaiḥ ātmānam pravibhajya bahuṣu yāgeṣu yugapad aṅga bhāvam gacchati iti
paraiḥ ca na dṛśyate antardhāna ādi śakti yogāt iti upapadyate
aneka pratipatteḥ darśanāt iti asya aparā vyākhyā vigrahavatām api karma aṅga bhāva codanāsu anekā pratipattiḥ dṛśyate
kvacid ekaḥ vigrahavān anekatra yugapad aṅga bhāvam na gacchati yathā bahubhiḥ bhojayadbhiḥ na ekaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ yugapad bhojyate
kvacid ca ekaḥ vigrahavān anekatra yugapad aṅga bhāvam gacchati yathā bahubhiḥ namaskurvāṇaiḥ ekaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ yugapad namaskriyate
tadvat iha uddeśa parityāga ātmaka tvāt yāgasya vigrahavatīm api ekām devatām uddiśya bahavaḥ svam svam dravyam yugapad parityakṣyanti iti vigrahavat tve pi devānām na kiṃcid karmaṇi virudhyate
śabdaḥ iti ced na atas prabhavāt pratyakṣa anumānābhyām
mā nāma vigrahavat tve deva ādīnām abhyupagamyamāne karmaṇi kaścid virodhaḥ prasañji
śabde tu virodhaḥ prasajyeta
katham
autpattikam hi śabdasya arthena saṃbandham āśritya anapekṣa tvāt iti vedasya prāmāṇyam sthāpitam
idānīm tu vigrahavatī devatā abhyupagamyamānā yadi api aiśvarya yogāt yugapad aneka karma saṃbandhīni havīṃṣi bhuñjīta tathā api vigraha yogāt asmat ādi vat janana maraṇavatī sā iti nityasya śabdasya nityena arthena nitye saṃbandhe pratīyamāne yat vaidike śabde prāmāṇyam sthitam tasya virodhaḥ syāt iti ced na ayam api asti virodhaḥ
kasmāt
atas prabhavāt
atas eva hi vaidikāt śabdāt deva ādikam jagat prabhavati
nanu janma ādi asya yatas iti atra brahma prabhava tvam jagataḥ katham iha śabda prabhava tvam ucyate
api ca yadi nāma vaidikāt śabdāt asya prabhavaḥ bhyupagataḥ katham etāvatā virodhaḥ śabde parihṛtaḥ
yāvatā vasavaḥ rudrāḥ ādityāḥ viśvedevāḥ marutaḥ iti ete rthāḥ anityāḥ eva utpattimat tvāt
tad anitya tve ca tad vācinām vaidikānām vasu ādi śabdānām anitya tvam kena nivāryate
prasiddham hi loke devadattasya putre utpanne yajñadattaḥ iti tasya nāma kriyate iti
tasmāt virodhaḥ eva śabdaḥ iti ced na
gavā ādi śabda artha saṃbandha nitya tva darśanāt
na hi gavā ādi vyaktīnām utpattimat tve tad ākṛtīnām api utpattimat tvam syāt
dravya guṇa karmaṇām hi vyaktayaḥ eva utpadyante na ākṛtayaḥ
ākṛtibhiḥ ca śabdānām saṃbandhaḥ na vyaktibhiḥ vyaktīnām ānantyāt saṃbandha grahaṇa anupapatteḥ
vyaktiṣu utpadyamānāsu api ākṛtīnām nitya tvāt na gavādi śabdeṣu kaścid virodhaḥ dṛśyate
tathā deva ādi vyakti prabhava abhyupagame pi ākṛti nitya tvāt na kaścid vasu ādi śabdeṣu virodhaḥ iti draṣṭavyam
ākṛti viśeṣaḥ tu deva ādīnām mantra arthavāda ādibhyaḥ vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt avagantavyaḥ
sthāna viśeṣa saṃbandha nimittāḥ vai indra ādi śabdāḥ senāpati ādi śabda vat
tatas ca yaḥ yaḥ tat tat sthānam adhitiṣṭhati sa saḥ indra ādi śabdaiḥ abhidhīyate iti na doṣaḥ bhavati
na ca idam śabda prabhava tvam brahma prabhava tva vat upādānakāraṇatva abhiprāyeṇa ucyate
katham tarhi sthita vācaka ātmanā nitye śabde nitya artha saṃbandhini śabda vyavahāra yogya artha vyakti niṣpattiḥ atas prabhavaḥ iti ucyate
katham punar avagamyate śabdāt prabhavati jagat iti
pratyakṣa anumānābhyām
pratyakṣam hi śrutiḥ prāmāṇyam pratyanapekṣa tvāt
anumānam smṛtiḥ prāmāṇyam prati sāpekṣa tvāt
te hi śabda pūrvām sṛṣṭim darśayataḥ
ete iti vai prajāpatiḥ devān asṛjata asṛgram iti manuṣyān indavaḥ iti pitṛm stiras pavitram iti grahān āśavaḥ iti stotram viśvāni iti śastram abhi saubhaga iti anyāḥ prajāḥ iti śrutiḥ
tathā anyatra api sa manasā vācam mithunam samabhavat ityādinā tatra tatra śabda pūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ śrāvyate
smṛtiḥ api anādinidhanā nityā vāc utsṛṣṭā svayaṃbhuvā
ādau veda mayī divyā yatas sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ iti
utsargaḥ api ayam vācaḥ saṃpradāya pravartana ātmakaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ anādinidhanāyāḥ anyādṛśasya utsargasya asaṃbhavāt
tathā nāma rūpam ca bhūtānām karmaṇām ca pravartanam
veda śabdebhyaḥ eva ādau nirmame sa maheśvaraḥ iti
sarveṣām tu sa nāmāni karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak
veda śabdebhyaḥ eva ādau pṛthak saṃsthāḥ ca nirmame iti ca
api ca cikīrṣitam artham anutiṣṭhan tasya vācakam śabdam pūrvam smṛtvā paścāt tam artham anutiṣṭhati iti sarveṣām naḥ pratyakṣam etat
tathā prajāpateḥ api sraṣṭuḥ sṛṣṭeḥ pūrvam vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ manasi prādurbabhūvuḥ paścāt tad anugatān arthān sasarja iti gamyate
tathā ca śrutiḥ sa bhūḥ iti vyāharat sa bhūmim asṛjata iti evamādikā bhūḥ ādi śabdebhyaḥ eva manasi prādurbhūtebhyaḥ bhūḥ ādi lokān sṛṣṭān darśayati
kimātmakam punar śabdam abhipretya idam śabda prabhava tvam ucyate
sphoṭam iti āha
varṇa pakṣe hi teṣām utpanna pradhvaṃsi tvāt nityebhyaḥ śabdebhyaḥ deva ādi vyaktīnām prabhavaḥ iti anupapannam syāt
utpanna dhvaṃsinaḥ ca varṇāḥ pratyuccāraṇam anyathā ca anyathā ca pratīyamāna tvāt
tathā hi adṛśyamānaḥ pi puruṣa viśeṣaḥ dhyayana dhvani śravaṇāt eva viśeṣataḥ nirdhāryate devadattaḥ yam adhīte yajñadattaḥ yam adhīte iti
na ca ayam varṇa viṣayaḥ nyathātva pratyayaḥ mithyājñānam bādhaka pratyaya abhāvāt
na ca varṇebhyaḥ rtha avagatiḥ yuktāḥ na hi ekaikaḥ varṇe rtham pratyāyayet vyabhicārāt
na ca varṇa samudāya pratyayaḥ sti krama varti tvāt varṇānām
pūrva pūrva varṇa anubhava janita saṃskāra sahitaḥ ntyaḥ varṇaḥ rtham pratyāyayiṣyati iti yadi ucyeta tat na
saṃbandha grahaṇa apekṣaḥ hi śabdaḥ svayam pratīyamānaḥ rtham pratyāyayet dhūma ādi vat
na ca pūrva pūrva varṇa anubhava janita saṃskāra sahitasya antya varṇasya pratītiḥ asti apratyakṣa tvāt saṃskārāṇām
kārya pratyāyitaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ sahitaḥ ntyaḥ varṇaḥ rtham pratyāyayiṣyati iti ced na
saṃskāra kāryasya api smaraṇasya krama varti tvāt
tasmāt sphoṭaḥ eva śabdaḥ
sa ca ekaika varṇa pratyaya āhita saṃskāra bīje ntya varṇa pratyaya janita paripāke pratyayini eka pratyaya viṣaya tayā jhaṭiti pratyavabhāsate
na ca ayam eka pratyayaḥ varṇa viṣayā smṛtiḥ varṇānām aneka tvāt eka pratyaya viṣaya tva anupapatteḥ
tasya ca pratyuccāraṇam pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt nitya tvam bheda pratyayasya varṇa viṣaya tvāt
tasmāt nityāt śabdāt sphoṭa rūpāt abhidhāyakāt kriyā kāraka phala lakṣaṇam jagat abhidheya bhūtam prabhavati iti
varṇāḥ eva tu śabdaḥ iti bhagavān upavarṣaḥ
nanu utpanna pradhvaṃsi tvam varṇānām uktam
tat na te eva iti pratyabhijñānāt
sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñānam keśa ādiṣu iva iti ced na
pratyabhijñānasya pramāṇa antareṇa bādhā anupapatteḥ
pratyabhijñānam ākṛti nimittam iti ced na
vyakti pratyabhijñānāt
yadi hi pratyuccāraṇam gava ādi vyakti vat anyāḥ anyāḥ varṇa vyaktayaḥ pratīyeran tatas ākṛti nimittam pratyabhijñānam syāt
na tu etat asti
varṇa vyaktayaḥ eva hi pratyuccāraṇam pratyabhijñāyante
dvis go śabdaḥ uccāritaḥ iti hi pratipattiḥ
na tu dvau go śabdau iti
nanu varṇāḥ api uccāraṇa bhedena bhinnāḥ pratīyante devadatta yajñadattayoḥ adhyayana dhvani śravaṇāt eva bheda pratīteḥ iti uktam
atra abhidhīyate sati varṇa viṣaye niścite pratyabhijñāne saṃyoga vibhāga abhivyaṅgya tvāt varṇānām abhivyañjaka vaicitrya nimittaḥ yam varṇa viṣayaḥ vicitraḥ pratyayaḥ na svarūpa nimittaḥ
api ca varṇa vyakti bheda vādinā api pratyabhijñāna siddhaye varṇa ākṛtayaḥ kalpayitavyāḥ
tāsu ca para upādhikaḥ bheda pratyayaḥ iti abhyupagantavyam
tat varam varṇa vyaktiṣu eva para upādhikaḥ bheda pratyayaḥ svarūpa nimittam ca pratyabhijñānam iti kalpanā lāghavam
eṣaḥ eva ca varṇa viṣayasya bheda pratyayasya bādhakaḥ pratyayaḥ yat pratyabhijñānam
katham hi ekasmin kāle bahūnām uccārayatām ekaḥ eva san gakāraḥ yugapad aneka rūpaḥ syāt udāttaḥ ca anudāttaḥ ca svaritaḥ ca sa anunāsikaḥ ca niranunāsikaḥ ca iti
atha vā dhvani kṛtaḥ yam bheda pratyayaḥ na varṇa kṛtaḥ iti adoṣaḥ
kaḥ punar ayam dhvaniḥ nāma
yaḥ dūrāt ākarṇayataḥ varṇa vivekam a pratipadyamānasya karṇa patham avatarati
pratyāsīta atas ca paṭu mṛdu tva ādi bhedam varṇeṣu āsañjayati
tad nibandhanāḥ ca udātta ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ na varṇa svarūpa nibandhanāḥ varṇānām pratyuccāraṇam pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt
evam ca sati sa ālambanāḥ eva ete udātta ādi pratyayāḥ bhaviṣyanti
itarathā hi varṇānām pratyabhijñāyamānānām nirbheda tvāt saṃyoga vibhāga kṛtāḥ udātta ādi viśeṣāḥ kalpyeran
saṃyoga vibhāgānām ca apratyakṣa tvāt na tad āśrayāḥ viśeṣāḥ varṇeṣu adhyavasātum śakyante iti atas nirālambanāḥ eva ete udātta ādi pratyayāḥ syuḥ
api ca na eva etat abhiniveṣṭavyam udātta ādi bhedena varṇānām pratyabhijñāyamānānām bhedaḥ bhavet iti
na hi anyasya bhedena anyasya a bhidyamānasya bhedaḥ bhavitum arhati
na hi vyakti bhedena jātim bhinnām manyante
varṇebhyaḥ ca artha pratīteḥ saṃbhavāt sphoṭa kalpanā anarthikā
na kalpayāmi aham sphoṭam pratyakṣam eva tu enam avagacchāmi ekaika varṇa grahaṇa āhita saṃskārāyāḥ buddhau jhaṭiti pratyavabhāsanāt iti ced na
asyāḥ api buddheḥ varṇa viṣaya tvāt
ekaika varṇa grahaṇa uttara kālā hi iyam ekā buddhiḥ gauḥ iti samasta varṇa viṣayā na artha antara viṣayā
katham etat avagamyate
yatas syām api buddhau gakāra ādayaḥ varṇāḥ anuvartante na tu dakāra ādayaḥ
yadi hi asyāḥ buddheḥ gakāra ādibhyaḥ rtha antaram sphoṭaḥ viṣayaḥ syāt tatas dakāra ādayaḥ iva gakāra ādayaḥ pi asyāḥ buddheḥ vyāvarteran
na tu tathā asti
tasmāt iyam eka buddhiḥ varṇa viṣayā eva smṛtiḥ
nanu aneka tvāt varṇānām na eka buddhi viṣaya tā upapadyate iti uktam tat prati brūmaḥ saṃbhavati anekasya api eka buddhi viṣaya tvam paṅktiḥ vanam senā daśa śatam sahasram ityādi darśanāt
yā tu gauḥ iti ekaḥ yam śabdaḥ iti buddhiḥ sā bahuṣu eva varṇeṣu eka artha avaccheda nibandhanā aupacārikī vana senā ādi buddhi vat eva
atra āha yadi varṇāḥ eva sāmastyena eka buddhi viṣaya tām āpadyamānāḥ padam syuḥ tatas jārāḥ rājā kapiḥ pikaḥ ityādiṣu pada viśeṣa pratipattiḥ na syāt
te eva hi varṇāḥ itaratra itaratra ca pratyavabhāsante iti
atra vadāmaḥ sati api samasta varṇa pratyavamarśe yathā krama anurodhinyaḥ eva pipīlikāḥ paṅkti buddhim ārohanti evam krama anurodhinaḥ eva hi varṇāḥ pada buddhim ārokṣyanti
tatra varṇānām aviśeṣe pi krama viśeṣa kṛtā pada viśeṣa pratipattiḥ na virudhyate
vṛddha vyavahāre ca ime varṇāḥ krama ādi anugṛhītāḥ gṛhīta artha viśeṣa saṃbandhāḥ santaḥ sva vyavahāre pi ekaika varṇa grahaṇa anantaram samasta pratyavamarśinyām buddhau tādṛśāḥ eva pratyavabhāsamānāḥ tam tam artham avyabhicāreṇa pratyāyayiṣyanti iti varṇa vādinaḥ laghīyasī kalpanā
sphoṭa vādinaḥ tu dṛṣṭa hāniḥ adṛṣṭa kalpanā ca
varṇāḥ ca ime krameṇa gṛhyamāṇāḥ sphoṭam vyañjayanti sa sphoṭaḥ rtham vyanakti iti garīyasī kalpanā syāt
atha api nāma pratyuccāraṇam anye nye varṇāḥ syuḥ tathā api pratyabhijñā ālambana bhāvena varṇa sāmānyānām avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt varṇeṣu artha pratipādana prakriyā racitā sā sāmānyeṣu saṃcārayitavyā
tatas ca nityebhyaḥ śabdebhyaḥ deva ādi vyaktīnām prabhavaḥ iti aviruddham
atas eva ca nitya tvam
kartuḥ asmaraṇāt iti sthite vedasya nitya tve deva ādi vyakti prabhava abhyupagamena tasya virodham āśaṅkya atas prabhavāt iti parihṛtya idānīm tat eva veda nitya tvam sthitam draḍhayati atas eva ca nitya tvam iti
atas eva niyata ākṛteḥ deva ādeḥ jagataḥ veda śabda prabhava tvāt veda śabda nitya tvam api pratyetavyam
tathā ca mantravarṇaḥ yajñena vācaḥ padavīyam āyan tām anvavindan ṛṣiṣu praviṣṭām iti sthitām eva vācam anuvinnām darśayati
vedavyāsaḥ ca evam eva smarati yuga ante ntarhitān vedān sa itihāsān mahā ṛṣayaḥ
lebhire tapasā pūrvam anujñātāḥ svayaṃbhuvā iti
samāna nāma rūpa tvāt ca avṛttau api avirodhaḥ darśanāt smṛteḥ ca
atha api syāt yadi paśu ādi vyakti vat deva ādi vyaktayaḥ api saṃtatya evā utpadyeran nirudhyeran ca tatas bhidhāna abhidheya abhidhātṛ vyavahāra avicchedāt saṃbandha nitya tvena virodhaḥ śabde parihriyeta
yadā tu khalu sakalam trailokyam parityakta nāma rūpam nirlepam pralīyate prabhavati ca abhinavam iti śruti smṛti vādāḥ vadanti tadā katham avirodhaḥ iti
tatra idam abhidhīyate samāna nāma rūpa tvāt iti
tadā api saṃsārasya anādi tvam tāvat abhyupagantavyam
pratipādayiṣyati ca ācāryaḥ saṃsārasya anādi tvam upapadyate ca api upalabhyate ca iti
anādau ca saṃsāre yathā svāpa prabodhayoḥ pralaya prabhava śravaṇe pi pūrva prabodha vat uttara prabodhe vyavahārāt na kaścid virodhaḥ evam kalpa antara prabhava pralayayoḥ api iti draṣṭavyam
svāpa prabodhayoḥ ca pralaya prabhavau śrūyete yadā suptaḥ svapnam na kaṃcana paśyati atha asmin prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati tadā enam vāc sarvaiḥ nāmabhiḥ saha api eti cakṣuḥ sarvaiḥ rūpaiḥ saha apyeti śrotram sarvaiḥ śabdaiḥ saha apyeti manaḥ sarvaiḥ dhyānaiḥ saha apyeti sa yadā pratibudhyate yathā agneḥ jvalataḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vipratiṣṭheran evam eva etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ yathāyatanam vipratiṣṭhante prāṇe
syāt etat svāpe puruṣa antara vyavahāra avicchedāt svayam ca suṣupta prabuddhasya pūrva prabodha vyavahāra anusaṃdhāna saṃbhavāt aviruddham
mahāpralaye tu sarva vyavahāra ucchedāt janma antara vyavahāra vat ca kalpa antara vyavahārasya anusaṃdhātum aśakya tvāt vaiṣamyam iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ sati api sarva vyavahāra ucchedini mahāpralaye parameśvara anugrahāt īśvarāṇām hiraṇyagarbha ādīnām kalpa antara vyavahāra anusaṃdhāna upapatteḥ
yadi api prākṛtāḥ prāṇinaḥ na janma antara vyavahāram anusaṃdadhānāḥ dṛśyante iti tathā api na tat prākṛta vat īśvarāṇām bhavitavyam
yathā hi prāṇi tva aviśeṣe manuṣya ādi stamba paryanteṣu jñāna aiśvarya ādi pratibandhaḥ pareṇa pareṇa bhūyān bhavan dṛśyate
tathā manuṣya ādiṣu eva hiraṇyagarbha paryanteṣu jñāna aiśvarya ādi abhivyaktiḥ api pareṇa pareṇa bhūyasī bhavati iti etat śruti smṛti vādeṣu asakṛt eva anukalpa ādau prādurbhavatām pāramaiśvaryam śrūyamāṇam na śakyam na asti iti vaditum
tatas ca atīta kalpa anuṣṭhita prakṛṣṭa jñāna karmaṇām īśvarāṇām hiraṇyagarbha ādīnām vartamāna kalpa ādau prādurbhavatām parameśvara anugṛhītānām supta pratibuddha vat kalpa antara vyavahāra anusaṃdhāna upapattiḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ yaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhāti pūrvam yaḥ vai vaidān ca prahiṇoti tasmai
devam ātma buddhi prakāśam mumukṣuḥ vai śaraṇam aham prapadye iti
smaranti ca śaunaka ādayaḥ madhucchandaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ dāśatayyaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ iti
prativedam ca evam eva kāṇḍa ṛṣi ādayaḥ smaryante
śrutiḥ api ṛṣi jñāna pūrvakam eva mantreṇa anuṣṭhānam darśayati yaḥ ha vai a vidita ārṣeya chandaḥ daivata brāhmaṇena mantreṇa yājayati vā adhyāpayati vā sthāṇum varcchati gartam vā pratipadyate iti upakramya tasmāt etāni mantre mantre vidyāt iti
prāṇinām ca sukha prāptaye dharmaḥ vidhīyate
duḥkha parihārāya ca adharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate
dṛṣṭa ānuśravika sukha duḥkha viṣayau ca rāga dveṣau bhavataḥ na vilakṣaṇa viṣayau iti atas dharma adharma phala bhūta uttarottarā sṛṣṭiḥ niṣpadyamānā pūrva sṛṣṭi sadṛśī eva niṣpadyate
smṛtiḥ ca bhavati teṣām ye yāni karmāṇi prāk sṛṣṭyām pratipedire
tāni eva te prapadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punar punar
hiṃsra ahiṃsre mṛdu krūre dharma adharma āvṛta anṛte
tad bhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāt tat tasya rocate iti
pralīyamānam api ca idam jagat śakti avaśeṣam eva pralīyate
śakti mūlam eva ca prabhavati
itarathā ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt
na ca aneka ākārāḥ śaktayaḥ śakyāḥ kalpayitum
tatas ca vicchidya vicchidya api udbhavatām bhūḥ ādi loka pravāhāṇām deva tiryak manuṣya lakṣaṇānām ca prāṇi nikāya pravāhāṇām varṇa āśrama dharma phala vyavasthānām ca anādau saṃsāre niyata tvam indriya viṣaya saṃbandha niyata tva vat pratyetavyam
na hi indriya viṣaya saṃbandha ādeḥ vyavahārasya pratisargam anyathātvam ṣaṣṭha indriya viṣaya kalpam śakyam utprekṣitum
atas ca sarva kalpānām tulya vyavahāra tvāt kalpa antara vyavahāra anusaṃdhāna kṣama tvāt ca īśvarāṇām samāna nāma rūpāḥ eva pratisargam viśeṣāḥ prādurbhavanti
samāna nāma rūpa tvāt ca avṛttau api mahāsarga mahāpralaya lakṣaṇāyām jagataḥ bhyupagamyamānāyām na kaścid śabda prāmāṇya ādi virodhaḥ
samāna nāma rūpa tām ca śruti smṛtī darśayataḥ sūryācandramasau dhātā yathāpūrvam akalpayat
divam ca pṛthivīm ca antarikṣam atha u suvar iti
yathā pūrvasmin kalpe sūryācandramaḥ prabhṛti jagat klṛptam tathā asmin api kalpe kalpayat iti arthaḥ
tathā agniḥ vai akāmayata
anna ādaḥ devānām asyām iti
saḥ etam agnaye kṛttikābhyaḥ puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam niravapat iti nakṣatreṣṭi vidhau yaḥ agniḥ niravapat yasmai vā agnaye niravapat tayoḥ samāna nāma rūpa tām darśayati iti evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ iha udāhartavyā
smṛtiḥ api ṛṣīṇām nāmadheyāni yāḥ ca vedeṣu dṛṣṭayaḥ
śarvarī ante prasūtānām tāni eva ebhyaḥ dadāti ajaḥ
yathā ṛtuṣu ṛtu liṅgāni nānā rūpāṇi paryaye
dṛśyante tāni tāni eva tathā bhāvāḥ yuga ādiṣu
yathā abhimāninaḥ tītāḥ tulyāḥ te sāṃprataiḥ iha
devāḥ devaiḥ atītaiḥ hi rūpaiḥ nāmabhiḥ eva ca iti evaṃjātīyakā draṣṭavyā
madhu ādiṣu asambhavāt anadhikāram jaiminiḥ
iha deva ādīnām api brahma vidyāyām asti adhikāraḥ iti yat pratijñātam tat paryāvartyate deva ādīnām anadhikāram jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
kasmāt
madhu ādiṣu asaṃbhavāt
brahmavidyāyām adhikāra abhyupagame hi vidyā tva aviśeṣāt madhu ādi vidyāsu api adhikāraḥ bhyupagamyeta
na ca evam saṃbhavati
katham
asau vai ādityaḥ deva madhu iti atra manuṣyāḥ ādityam madhu adhyāsena upāsīran
deva ādiṣu hi upāsakeṣu abhyupagamyamāneṣu ādityaḥ katham anyam ādityam upāsīta
punar ca āditya vyapāśrayāṇi pañca rohita ādīni amṛtāni anukramya vasavaḥ rudrāḥ ādityāḥ marutaḥ sādhyāḥ ca pañca deva gaṇāḥ krameṇa tat tat amṛtam upajīvanti iti upadiśya sa yaḥ etat evam amṛtam veda vasūnām eva ekaḥ bhūtvā agninā eva mukhena etat eva amṛtam dṛṣṭvā tṛpyati iti ādinā vasu ādi upajīvyāni amṛtāni vijānatām vasu ādi mahima prāptim darśayati
vasu ādayaḥ tu kān anyān vasu ādīn amṛta upajīvinaḥ vijānīyuḥ
kam vā anyam vasu ādi mahimānam prepseyuḥ
tathā agniḥ pādaḥ vāyuḥ pādaḥ ādityaḥ pādaḥ diśaḥ pādaḥ vāyuḥ vā saṃvargaḥ ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ ityādiṣu devatā ātma upāsaneṣu na teṣām eva devatā ātmanām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati
tathā imām eva gautama bharadvājau ayam vai gautamaḥ yam bharadvājaḥ ityādiṣu api ṛṣi saṃbandheṣu upāsaneṣu na teṣām eva ṛṣīṇām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati
kutas ca deva ādīnām anadhikāraḥ
jyotiṣi bhāvāt ca
yat idam jyotiḥ maṇḍalam dyu sthānam ahar rātrābhyām bambhramat jagat avabhāsayati tasmin āditya ādayaḥ devatā vacanāḥ śabdāḥ prayujyante
loka prasiddheḥ vākyaśeṣa prasiddheḥ ca
na ca jyotiḥ maṇḍalasya hṛdaya ādinā vigraheṇa cetanatayā arthi tva ādinā vā yogaḥ vagantum śakyate mṛd ādi vat acetana tva avagamāt
etena agni ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ
syāt etat mantra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa lokebhyaḥ deva ādīnām vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced na iti ucyate
na tāvat lokaḥ nāma kiṃcid svatantram pramāṇam asti
pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ eva avyabhicarita viṣayebhyaḥ pramāṇebhyaḥ prasiddhaḥ eva arthaḥ lokāt prasiddhaḥ iti ucyate
na ca atra pratyakṣa ādīnām anyatamam pramāṇam asti
itihāsa purāṇānām api pauruṣeya tvāt pramāṇa antara mūla tām ākāṅkṣati
arthavādāḥ api vidhinā eka vākya tvāt stuti arthāḥ santaḥ na pārthagarthyena deva ādīnām vigraha ādi sadbhāve kāraṇa bhāvam pratipadyante
mantrāḥ api śruti ādi viniyuktāḥ prayoga samavāyinaḥ bhidhāna arthāḥ na kasyacid arthasya pramāṇam iti ācakṣate
tasmāt abhāvaḥ deva ādīnām adhikārasya
bhāvam tu bādarāyaṇaḥ sti hi
tu śabdaḥ pūrvapakṣam vyāvartayati
bādarāyaṇaḥ tu ācāryaḥ bhāvam adhikārasya deva ādīnām api manyate
yadi api madhu ādi vidyāsu devatā ādi vyāmiśrāsu asaṃbhavaḥ dhikārasya tathā api asti hi śuddhāyām brahmavidyāyām saṃbhavaḥ
arthi tva sāmarthya apratiṣedha ādi apekṣa tvāt adhikārasya
na ca kvacid asaṃbhavaḥ iti etāvatā yatra saṃbhavaḥ tatra api adhikāraḥ upodyeta
manuṣyāṇām api na sarveṣām brāhmaṇa ādīnām sarveṣu rājasūya ādiṣu adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati
tatra yaḥ nyāyaḥ saḥ bhaviṣyati
brahma vidyām ca prakṛtya bhavati liṅga darśanam śrautam deva ādi adhikārasya sūcakam tat yaḥ yaḥ devānām pratyabudhyata saḥ eva tat abhavat tathā ṛṣīṇām tathā manuṣyāṇām iti te ha ūcuḥ hanta tam ātmānam anvicchāmaḥ yam ātmānam anviṣya sarvān ca lokān āpnoti sarvān ca kāmān iti indraḥ ha vai devānām abhipravavrāja virocanaḥ surāṇām ityādi ca
smārtam api ca gandharva yājñavalkya saṃvāda ādi
yat api uktam jyotiṣi bhāvāt ca iti atra brūmaḥ jyotiḥ ādi viṣayāḥ api āditya ādayaḥ devatā vacanāḥ śabdāḥ cetanāvantam aiśvarya ādi upetam tam tam devatā ātmānam samarpayanti mantra arthavāda ādiṣu tathā vyavahārāt
asti hi aiśvarya yogāt devatānām jyotiḥ ādi ātmabhiḥ ca avasthātum yathā iṣṭam ca tam tam vigraham grahītum sāmarthyam
tathā hi śrūyate subrahmaṇya arthavāde medhātitheḥ meṣaḥ iti medhātithim ha kāṇvāyanam indraḥ meṣaḥ bhūtvā jahāra iti
smaryate ca ādityaḥ puruṣaḥ bhūtvā kuntīm upajagāma ha iti
mṛd ādiṣu api cetanāḥ adhiṣṭhātāraḥ bhyupagamyante
mṛd abravīt āpaḥ bruvan ityādi darśanāt
jyodiḥ ādeḥ tu bhūtadhātoḥ āditya ādiṣu api acetana tvam abhyupagamyate
cetanāḥ tu adhiṣṭhātāraḥ devatā ātmānaḥ mantra arthavāda ādiṣu vyavahārāt iti uktam
yat api uktam mantra arthavādayoḥ anya artha tvāt na devatā vigraha ādi prakāśana sāmarthyam iti atra brūmaḥ pratyaya apratyayau hi sadbhāva asadbhāvayoḥ kāraṇam
na anya artha tvam ananya artha tvam vā
tathā hi anya artham api prasthitaḥ pathi patitam tṛṇa parṇa ādi asti iti eva pratipadyate
atra āha viṣamaḥ upanyāsaḥ
tatra hi tṛṇa parṇa ādi viṣayam pratyakṣam pravṛttam asti yena tad astitvam pratipadyate
atra punar vidhi uddeśa eka vākya bhāvena stuti arthe rthavāde na pārthagarthyena vṛttānta viṣayā pravṛttiḥ śakyā adhyavasātum
na hi mahāvākye rtha pratyāyake vā antara vākyasya pṛthak pratyāyaka tvam asti
yathā na surām pibet iti nañvati vākye pada traya saṃbandhāt surā pāna pratiṣedhaḥ eva ekaḥ rthaḥ vagamyate
na punar surām pibet iti pada dvaya saṃbandhāt surā pāna vidhiḥ api iti
atra ucyate viṣamaḥ upanyāsaḥ
yuktam yat surā pāna pratiṣedhe pada anvayasya ekatvāt avāntaravākya arthasya agrahaṇam
vidhi uddeśa arthavādayoḥ tu arthavāda sthāni padāni pṛthak anvayam vṛttānta viṣayam pratipadya anantaram kaimarthya vaśena kāmam vidheḥ stāvaka tvam pratipadyante
yathā hi vāyavyam śvetam ālabheta bhūta kāmaḥ iti atra vidhi uddeśa vartinām vāyavya ādi padānām vidhinā saṃbandhaḥ na evam vāyuḥ vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā vāyum eva svena bhāgadheyena upadhāvati saḥ eva enam bhūtim gamayati Maitrāyaṇī Saṃhitā
iti eṣām arthavāda gatānām padānām
na hi bhavati vāyuḥ vai ālabheta iti kṣepiṣṭhāḥ devatāḥ vai ālabheta ityādi
vāyu svabhāva saṃkīrtanena tu avāntaram anvayam pratipadya evam viśiṣṭa daivatyam idam karma iti vidhim stuvanti
tat yatra yaḥ vā antara vākya arthaḥ pramāṇa antara gocaraḥ bhavati tatra tad anuvādena artha vādaḥ pravartate
yatra pramāṇa antara viruddhaḥ tatra guṇa vādena
yatra tu tat ubhayam na asti tatra kim pramāṇa antara abhāvāt guṇa vādaḥ syāt āhostvit pramāṇa antara avirodhāt vidyamāna artha vādaḥ iti pratīti śaraṇaiḥ vidyamāna artha vādaḥ āśrayaṇīyaḥ na guṇa anuvādaḥ
etena mantraḥ vyākhyātaḥ
api ca vidhibhiḥ eva indra ādi daivatyāni havīṃṣi codayadbhiḥ apekṣitam indra ādīnām svarūpam
na hi svarūpa rahitāḥ indra ādayaḥ cetasi āropayitum śakyante
na ca cetasi an ārūḍhāyai tasyai tasyai devatāyai haviḥ pradātum śakyate
śrāvayati ca yasyai devatāyai haviḥ gṛhītam syāt tām dhyāyet vaṣaṭ kariṣyan iti
na ca śabda mātram artha svarūpam saṃbhavati śabda arthayoḥ bhedāt
tatra yādṛśam mantra arthavādayoḥ indra ādīnām svarūpam avagatam na tat tādṛśam śabda pramāṇakena pratyākhyātum yuktam
itihāsa purāṇam api vyākhyātena mārgeṇa saṃbhavat mantra arthavāda mūlaka tvāt prabhavati devatā vigraha ādi sādhayitum
pratyakṣa ādi mūlam api saṃbhavati
bhavati hi asmākam apratyakṣam api ciraṃtanānām pratyakṣam
tathā ca vyāsa ādayaḥ deva ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavaharanti iti smaryate
yaḥ tu brūyāt idānīṃtanānām iva pūrveṣām api na asti deva ādibhiḥ vyavahartum sāmarthyam iti sa jagat vaicitryam pratiṣedhet
idānīm iva ca na anyadā api sārvabhaumaḥ kṣatriyaḥ sti iti brūyāt tatas ca rājasūya ādi codanāḥ uparundhyāt
idānīm iva ca kāla antare pi avyavasthita prāyān varṇa āśrama dharmān pratijānīta tatas ca vyavasthā vidhāyi śāstram anarthakam kuryāt
tasmāt dharma utkarṣa vaśāt ciraṃtanāḥ deva ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavajahnuḥ iti śliṣyate
api ca smaranti svādhyāyāt iṣṭadevatā saṃprayogaḥ ityādi
yogaḥ pi aṇima ādi aiśvarya prāpti phalakaḥ smaryamāṇaḥ na śakyate sāhasa mātreṇa pratyākhyātum
śrutiḥ ca yoga māhātmyam prakhyāpayati pṛthivī ap tejaḥ nilakhe samutthite pañca ātmake yoga guṇe pravṛtte
na tasya rogaḥ na jarā na mṛtyuḥ prāptasya yoga agni mayam śarīram iti
ṛṣīṇām api mantra brāhmaṇa darśinām sāmarthyam na asmadīyena sāmarthyena upamātum yuktam
tasmāt sa mūlam itihāsa purāṇam
loka prasiddhiḥ api na sati saṃbhave nirālambanā adhyavasātum yuktā
tasmāt upapannaḥ mantra ādibhyaḥ deva ādīnām vigrahavat tva ādi avagamaḥ
tatas ca arthi tva ādi saṃbhavāt upapannaḥ deva ādīnām api brahmavidyāyām adhikāraḥ
krama mukti darśanāni api evam eva upapadyante
śugasya tad anādara śravaṇāt tad ādravaṇāt sūcyate hi
apaśūdrā adhikaraṇam
yathā manuṣya adhikāra niyamam apodya deva ādīnām api vidyāsu adhikāraḥ uktaḥ tathā eva dvijāti adhikāra niyama apavādena śūdrasya api adhikāraḥ syāt iti etām āśaṅkām nivartayitum idam adhikaraṇam ārabhyate
tatra śūdrasya api adhikāraḥ syāt iti tāvat prāptam
arthi tva sāmarthyayoḥ saṃbhavāt tasmāt śūdraḥ yajñe navaklṛptaḥ iti vat śūdraḥ vidyāyām anavaklṛptaḥ iti niṣedha aśravaṇāt
yat ca karmasu anadhikāra kāraṇam śūdrasya anagni tvam na tat vidyāsu adhikārasya apavādakam
na hi āhavanīya ādi rahitena vidyā veditum na śakyate
bhavati ca śrautam liṅgam śūdra adhikārasya upodbalakam
saṃvarga vidyāyām hi jānaśrutim pautrāyaṇam śuśrūṣum śūdra śabdena parāmṛśati aha ha āre tvā śūdra tava eva saha gobhiḥ astu iti
vidura prabhṛtayaḥ ca śūdra yoni prabhavāḥ api viśiṣṭa vijñāna saṃpannāḥ smaryante
tasmāt adhikriyate śūdraḥ vidyāsu iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ veda adhyayana abhāvāt
adhīta vedaḥ hi vidita veda arthaḥ veda artheṣu adhikriyate
na ca śūdrasya veda adhyayanam asti
upanayana pūrvaka tvāt veda adhyayanasya upanayanasya ca varṇa traya viṣaya tvāt
yat tu arthi tvam na tat asati sāmarthye dhikāra kāraṇam bhavati
sāmarthyam api na laukikam kevalam adhikāra kāraṇam bhavati
śāstrīye rthe śāstrīyasya sāmarthyasya apekṣita tvāt śāstrīyasya ca sāmarthyasya adhyayana nirākaraṇena nirākṛta tvāt
yat ca idam śūdraḥ yajñe navaklṛptaḥ iti tat nyāya pūrvaka tvāt vidyāyām api anavaklṛpta tvam dyotayati
nyāyasya sādhāraṇa tvāt
yat punar saṃvarga vidyāyām śūdra śabda śravaṇam liṅgam manyase na tat liṅgam
nyāya abhāvāt
nyāya ukte hi liṅga darśanam dyotakam bhavati
na ca atra nyāyaḥ u sti
kāmam ca ayam śūdra śabdaḥ saṃvarga vidyāyām eva ekasyām śūdram adhikuryāt tad viṣaya tvāt
na sarvāsu vidyāsu
arthavāda stha tvāt tu na kvacid api ayam śūdram adhikartum utsahate
śakyate ca ayam śūdra śabdaḥ dhikṛta viṣaye yojayitum
katham iti ucyate kamvaraḥ enam etat santam sayugvānam iva raikvam āttha iti asmāt haṃsa vākyāt ātmanaḥ na ādaram śrutavataḥ jānaśruteḥ pautrāyaṇasya śuc utpede
tām ṛṣiḥ raikvaḥ śūdra śabdena anena sūcayāṃbabhūva ātmanaḥ parokṣa jña tā khyāpanāya iti gamyate jātiśūdrasya anadhikārāt
katham punar śūdra śabdena śuc utpannā sūcyate iti ucyate tadā ādravaṇāt
śucam abhidudrāva śucā vai abhidudruve śucā vā raikvam abhidudrāva iti śūdraḥ
avayava artha saṃbhavāt rūḍhi arthasya ca asaṃbhavāt
dṛśyate ca ayam syām ākhyāyikāyām
kṣatriya tva gateḥ ca uttaratra caitrarathena liṅgāt
itas ca na jātiśūdraḥ jānaśrutiḥ
yatkāraṇam prakaraṇa nirūpaṇena kṣatriya tvam asya uttaratra caitrarathena abhipratāriṇā kṣatriyeṇa samabhivyāhārāt liṅgāt gamyate
uttaratra hi saṃvarga vidyā vākya śeṣe caitrarathiḥ abhipratārī kṣatriyaḥ saṃkīrtyate atha ha śaunakam ca kāpeyam abhipratāriṇam ca kākṣasenim sūdena pariviṣyamāṇau brahmacārī bibhikṣe iti
caitrarathi tvam ca abhipratāriṇaḥ kāpeya yogāt avagantavyam
kāpeya yogaḥ hi citrarathasya avagataḥ etena vai citraratham kāpeyāḥ ayājayan iti
samāna anvayānām ca prāyeṇa samāna anvayāḥ yājakāḥ bhavanti
tasmāt caitrarathiḥ nāma ekaḥ kṣatra patiḥ ajāyata iti ca kṣatra pati tva avagamāt kṣatriya tvam asya avagantavyam
tena kṣatriyeṇa abhipratāriṇā saha samānāyām saṃvarga vidyāyām saṃkīrtanam jānaśruteḥ api kṣatriya tvam sūcayati
samānānām eva hi prāyeṇa samabhivyāhārāḥ bhavanti
kṣattṛ preṣaṇa ādi aiśvarya yogāt ca jānaśruteḥ kṣatriya tva avagatiḥ
atas na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ
saṃskāra parāmarśāt tad abhāva abhilāpāt ca
itas ca na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ yat vidyā pradeśeṣu upanayana ādayaḥ saṃskārāḥ parāmṛśyante tam ha upaninye adhīhi bhagavaḥ iti ha upasasāda brahma parāḥ brahma niṣṭhāḥ param brahma anveṣamāṇāḥ eṣa ha vai tat sarvam vakṣyati iti te ha samidh pāṇayaḥ bhagavantam pippalādam upasannāḥ iti ca
tān ha an upanīya eva iti api pradarśitā eva upanayana prāptiḥ bhavati
śūdrasya ca saṃskāra abhāvaḥ bhilapyate śūdraḥ caturthaḥ varṇaḥ ekajātiḥ iti eka jāti tva smaraṇāt
na śūdre pātakam kiṃcid na ca saṃskāram arhati iti ādibhiḥ ca
tad abhāva nirdhāraṇe ca pravṛtteḥ
itas ca na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ
yat satyavacanena śūdra tva abhāve nirdhārite jābālam gautamaḥ upanetum anuśāsitum ca pravavṛte na etat abrāhmaṇaḥ vivaktum arhati samidham somya āhara upa tvā neṣye na satyāt agāḥ iti śruti liṅgāt
śravaṇa adhyayana artha pratiṣedhāt smṛteḥ ca
itas ca na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ
yat asya smṛteḥ śravaṇa adhyayana artha pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati
veda śravaṇa pratiṣedhaḥ veda adhyayana pratiṣedhaḥ tad artha jñāna anuṣṭhānayoḥ ca pratiṣedhaḥ śūdrasya smaryate
śravaṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tāvat atha ha asya vedam upaśrṛṇvataḥ trapu jatubhyām śrotra pratipūraṇam iti
ha vai etat śamaśānam yat śūdraḥ tasmāt śūdra samīpe na adhyetavyam iti ca
atas eva adhyayana pratiṣedhaḥ
yasya hi samīpe na adhyetavyam bhavati sa katham aśrutam adhīyīta
bhavati ca veda uccāraṇe jihvā chedaḥ dhāraṇe śarīra bhedaḥ iti
atas eva ca arthāt artha jñāna anuṣṭhānayoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati na śūdrāya matim dadyāt iti dvijātīnām adhyayanam ijyā dānam iti ca
yeṣām punar pūrva kṛta saṃskāra vaśāt vidura dharmavyādha prabhṛtīnām jñāna utpattiḥ teṣām na śakyate phala prāptiḥ pratiṣeddhum jñānasya aikāntika phala tvāt
śrāvayet caturaḥ varṇān iti ca itihāsa purāṇa adhigame cāturvarṇyasya adhikāra smaraṇāt
veda pūrvakaḥ tu na asti adhikāraḥ śūdrāṇām iti sthitam
kampanāt
kampanā adhikaraṇam
avasitaḥ prāsaṅgikaḥ dhikāra vicāraḥ
prakṛtām eva idānīm vākya artha vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ
yat idam kiṃca jagat sarvam prāṇaḥ ejati niḥsṛtam
mahat bhayam vajram udyatam ye etat viduḥ amṛtāḥ te bhavanti iti etat vākyam kampane iti dhātvartha anugamāt lakṣitam
asmin vākye sarvam idam jagat prāṇa āśrayam spandate mahat ca kiṃcid bhaya kāraṇam vajra śabditam udyatam tad vijñānāt ca amṛta tva prāptiḥ iti śrūyate
tatra kaḥ sau prāṇaḥ kim tat bhayānakam vajram iti apratipatteḥ vicāre kriyamāṇe prāptam tāvat prasiddheḥ pañca vṛttiḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti
prasiddheḥ eva ca aśaniḥ vajram syāt
vāyoḥ ca idam māhātmyam saṃkīrtyate
katham
sarvam idam jagat pañca vṛttau vāyau prāṇa śabdite pratiṣṭhāya ejati
vāyu nimittam eva ca mahat bhayānakam vajram udyamyate
vāyau hi parjanya bhāvena vivartamāne vidyut stanayitnu vṛṣṭi aśanayaḥ vivartante iti ācakṣate
vāyu vijñānāt eva ca idam amṛta tvam
tathā hi śruti antaram vāyuḥ eva vyaṣṭiḥ vāyuḥ samaṣṭiḥ apa punarmṛtyum jayati yaḥ evam veda iti
tasmāt vāyuḥ ayam iha pratipattavyaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ brahma eva idam iha pratipattavyam
kutas
pūrva uttara ālocanāt
pūrva uttarayoḥ hi grantha bhāgayoḥ brahma eva nirdiśyamānam upalabhāmahe
iha eva katham akasmāt antarāle vāyum nirdiśyamānam pratipadyemahi
pūrvatra tāvat tat eva śukram tat brahma tat eva amṛtam ucyate
tasimant lokāḥ śritāḥ sarve tat u na atyeti kaścana iti brahma nirdiṣṭam
tat eva iha api saṃnidhānāt jagat sarvam prāṇaḥ ejati iti ca loka āśraya tva pratyabhijñānāt nirdiṣṭam iti gamyate
prāṇa śabdaḥ u pi ayam paramātmani eva prayuktaḥ prāṇasya prāṇam iti darśanāt
ejayitṛ tvam api idam paramātmanaḥ eva upapadyate na vāyu mātrasya
tathā ca uktam na prāṇena nā apānena martyaḥ jīvati kaścana
itareṇa tu jīvanti yasmin etau upāśritau iti
uttaratra api bhayāt asya agniḥ tapati bhayāt tapati sūryaḥ
bhayāt indraḥ ca vāyuḥ ca mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti brahmā eva nirdekṣyate na vāyuḥ sa vāyukasya jagataḥ bhaya hetu tva abhidhānāt
tat eva iha api saṃnidhānāt mahat bhayam vajram udyatam iti ca bhaya hetu tvam pratyabhijñānāt nirdiṣṭam iti gamyate
vajra śabdaḥ pi ayam bhaya hetu tva sāmānyāt prayuktaḥ
yathā hi vajram udyatam mama eva śirasi nipatet yadi aham asya śāsanam na kuryām iti anena bhayena janaḥ niyamena rāja ādi śāsane pravartate evam idam agni vāyu sūrya ādikam jagat asmāt eva brahmaṇaḥ bibhyat niyamena sva vyāpāre pravartate iti bhayānakam vajra upamitam brahma
tathā ca brahma viṣayam śruti antaram bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate
bhīṣā udeti sūryaḥ
bhīṣā asmāt agniḥ ca indraḥ ca
mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti
amṛta tva phala śravaṇāt api brahma eva idam iti gamyate
brahma jñānāt hi amṛta tva prāptiḥ tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate yanāyaḥ iti mantra varṇāt
yat tu vāyuvijñānāt kvacid amṛta tvam abhihitam tat āpekṣikam
tatra eva prakaraṇa antara karaṇena paramātmānam abhidhāya atas nyat ārtam iti vāyu ādeḥ ārta tva abhidhānāt
prakaraṇāt api atra paramātma niścayaḥ
anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt anyatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt
anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yat tat paśyasi tat vada iti paramātmanaḥ pṛṣṭa tvāt
jyotiḥ darśanāt
jyotiḥ adhikaraṇam
eṣa saṃprasādaḥ u smāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti śrūyate
tatra saṃśayyate kim jyotiḥ śabdam cakṣuḥ viṣayatama upaham tejaḥ kim vā param brahma iti
kim tāvat prāptam
prasiddham eva tejaḥ jyotiḥ śabdam iti
kutas
jyotiḥ śabdasya rūḍha tvāt
jyotiḥ caraṇa abhidhānāt iti atra hi prakaraṇāt jyotiḥ śabdaḥ sva artham parityajya brahmaṇi vartate
na ca iha tadvat kiṃcid sva artha parityāge kāraṇam dṛśyate
tathā ca nāḍīkhaṇḍe atha yatra etat asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati atha etaiḥ eva raśmibhiḥ ūrdhvam ākramate iti mumukṣoḥ āditya prāptiḥ abhihitā
tasmāt prasiddham eva tejaḥ jyotiḥ śabdam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ param eva brahma jyotiḥ śabdam
kasmāt
darśanāt
tasya hi iha prakaraṇe vaktavya tvena anuvṛttiḥ dṛśyate
yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakasya ātmanaḥ prakaraṇa ādau anveṣṭavya tvena vijijñāsitavya tvena ca pratijñānāt
etam tu eva te bhūyas nuvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca anusaṃdhānāt
aśarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti ca aśarīra tāyai jyotiḥ saṃpatteḥ asya abhidhānāt
brahma bhāvāt ca anyatra aśarīra tā anupapatteḥ
param jyotiḥ saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca viśeṣaṇāt
yat tu uktam mumukṣoḥ āditya prāptiḥ abhihitā iti na asau ātyantikaḥ mokṣaḥ gati utkrānti saṃbandhāt
na hi ātyantike mokṣe gati utkrāntī staḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ
ākāśaḥ
artha antara tva ādi vyapadeśāt
artha antara tva ādi vyapadeśa adhikaraṇam
ākāśaḥ vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yat antarā tat brahma tat amṛtam saḥ ātmā SNM
iti śrūyate
tat kim ākāśa śabdam param brahma kim vā prasiddham eva bhūtākāśam iti vicāre bhūta parigrahaḥ yuktaḥ
ākāśa śabdasya tasmin rūḍha tvāt
nāma rūpa nirvahaṇasya ca avakāśa dāna dvāreṇa tasmin yojayitum śakya tvāt
sraṣṭṛ tva ādeḥ ca spaṣṭasya brahma liṅgasya aśravaṇāt iti evam prāpte idam ucyate param eva brahma iha ākāśa śabdam bhavitum arhati
kasmāt
artha antara tva ādi vyapadeśāt
te yat antarā tat brahma iti hi nāma rūpābhyām artha antara bhūtam ākāśam vyapadiśati
na ca brahmaṇaḥ
anyat nāma rūpābhyām artha antaram saṃbhavati sarvasya vikāra jātasya nāma rūpābhyām eva vyākṛta tvāt
nāma rūpayoḥ api nirvahaṇam niraṅkuśam na
anyatra saṃbhavati anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti brahma kartṛkatva śravaṇāt
nanu jīvasya api pratyakṣam nāma rūpa viṣayam nirvoḍhṛ tvam asti
bāḍham asti
abhedaḥ tu iha vivakṣitaḥ
nāma rūpa nirvahaṇa abhidhānāt eva ca sraṣṭṛ tva ādi brahma liṅgam abhihitam bhavati
tat brahma tat amṛtam saḥ ātmā iti ca brahma vādasya liṅgāni
ākāśaḥ tad liṅgāt iti asya eva ayam prapañcaḥ
suṣupti utkrāntyoḥ bhedena
suṣupti adhikaraṇam
vyapadeśāt iti anuvartate
bṛhadāraṇyake ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake katamaḥ ātmā iti yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ iti upakramya bhūyān ātma viṣayaḥ prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ
tat kim saṃsāri svarūpa mātra anvākhyāna param vākyam uta asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana param iti viśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
saṃsāri svarūpa mātra viṣayam eva iti
kutas
upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām upakrame yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti śārīra liṅgāt
upasaṃhāre ca sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti tad a parityāgāt
madhye buddhānta ādi avasthā upanyāsena tasya eva prapañcanāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvara upadeśa param eva idam vākyam na śārīra mātra anvākhyāna param
kasmāt
suṣuptau utkrāntau ca śārīrāt bhedena parameśvarasya vyapadeśāt
suṣuptau tāvat ayam puruṣaḥ prājñena ātmanā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ na bāhyam kiṃcana veda na antaram iti śārīrāt bhedena parameśvaram vyapadiśati
tatra puruṣaḥ śārīraḥ syāt tasya veditṛ tvāt
bāhya abhyantara vedana prasaṅge sati tad pratiṣedha saṃbhavāt
prājñaḥ parameśvaraḥ sarvajña tva lakṣaṇayā prajñayā nityam aviyogāt
tathā utkrāntau api ayam śārīraḥ ātmā prājñena ātmanā anvārūḍhaḥ utsarjan yāti iti jīvāt bhedena parameśvaram vyapadiśati
tatra api śārīraḥ jīvaḥ syāt śarīra svāmi tvāt
prājñaḥ tu saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ
tasmāt suṣupti utkrāntyoḥ bhedena vyapadeśāt parameśvaraḥ eva atra vivakṣitaḥ iti gamyate
yat uktam ādi anta madhyeṣu śārīra liṅgāt tad para tvam asya vākyasya iti atra brūmaḥ upakrame tāvat yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti na saṃsāri svarūpam vivakṣitam
