kim tarhi anūdya saṃsāri svarūpam pareṇa brahmaṇā asya eka tām vivakṣati
yatas dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti evamādi uttara grantha pravṛttiḥ saṃsāri dharma nirākaraṇa parā lakṣyate
tathā upasaṃhāre pi yathopakramam eva upasaṃharati sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti
yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu saṃsārī lakṣyate sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā parameśvaraḥ eva asmābhiḥ pratipāditaḥ iti arthaḥ
yaḥ tu madhye buddhānta ādi avasthā upanyāsāt saṃsāri svarūpa vivakṣām manyate sa prācīm api diśam prasthāpitaḥ pratīcīm api diśam pratiṣṭheta
yatas na buddhānta ādi avasthā upanyāsena avasthāvattvam saṃsāri tvam vā vivakṣati kim tarhi avasthā rahitatvam asaṃsāri tvam ca
katham etat avagamyate
yat atas ūrdhvam vimokṣāya eva brūhi iti pade pade pṛcchati
yat ca an anvāgataḥ tena bhavati a saṅgaḥ hi ayam puruṣaḥ iti pade pade prativakti
an anvāgatam puṇyena an anvāgatam pāpena tīrṇaḥ hi tadā sarvān śokān hṛdayasya bhavati iti ca
tasmāt asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana param eva etat vākyam iti avagantavyam
pati ādi śabdebhyaḥ
itas ca asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana param eva etat vākyam iti avagantavyam
yat asmin vākye pati ādayaḥ śabdāḥ asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana parāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva pratiṣedhanāḥ ca bhavanti sarvasya vaśī sarvasya īśānaḥ sarvasya adhipatiḥ iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ asaṃsāri svabhāva pratipādana parāḥ
sa na sādhunā karmaṇā bhūyān no eva asādhunā kanīyān iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva pratiṣedhanāḥ
tasmāt asaṃsārī parameśvaraḥ iha uktaḥ iti avagamyate
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ

prathamaḥ dhyāyaḥ
caturthaḥ pādaḥ
ānumānikam api ekeṣām iti ced na śarīra rūpaka vinyasta gṛhīteḥ darśayati ca
ānumānika adhikaraṇam
ānumānikam api anumāna nirūpitam api pradhānam ekeṣām śākhinām śabda vat upalabhyate
kāṭhake hi paṭhyate mahataḥ param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ iti
tatra ye eva yad nāmānaḥ yad kramāḥ ca mahat avyakta puruṣāḥ smṛti prasiddhāḥ te eva iha pratyabhijñāyante
tatra avyaktam iti smṛti prasiddheḥ śabda ādi hīna tvāt ca na vyaktam avyaktam iti vyutpatti saṃbhavāt smṛti prasiddham pradhānam abhidhīyate
atas tasya śabdavat tvāt aśabda tvam anupapannam
tat eva ca jagataḥ kāraṇam śruti smṛti nyāya prasiddhibhyaḥ iti ced na etat evam na hi etat kāṭhaka vākyam smṛti prasiddhayoḥ mahat avyaktayoḥ astitva param
na hi atra yādṛśam smṛti prasiddham svatantram kāraṇam triguṇam pradhānam tādṛśam pratyabhijñāyate
śabda mātram hi atra avyaktam iti pratyabhijñāyate
sa ca śabdaḥ na vyaktam avyaktam iti yaugika tvāt anyasmin api sūkṣme su durlakṣye ca prayujyate
na ca ayam kasmin cit rūḍhaḥ
yā tu pradhāna vādinām rūḍhiḥ sā teṣām eva pāribhāṣikī satī na veda artha nirūpaṇe kāraṇa bhāvam pratipadyate
na ca krama mātra sāmānyāt samāna artha pratipattiḥ bhavati asati tad rūpa pratyabhijñāne
na hyaśca sthāne gām paśyan aśvaḥ yam iti amūḍhaḥ dhī avasyati
prakaraṇa nirūpaṇāyām ca atra na para parikalpitam pradhānam pratīyate śarīra rūpaka vinyasta gṛhīteḥ śarīram hi atra ratha rūpaka vinyastam avyakta śabdena parigṛhyate
kutas
prakaraṇāt pariśeṣāt ca
tathā hi anantara atītaḥ granthaḥ ātma śarīra ādīnām rathi ratha ādi rūpaka klṛptim darśayati ātmānam rathinam viddhi śarīram ratham eva tu
buddhim tu sārathim viddhi manaḥ pragraham eva ca
indriyāṇi hayān āhuḥ viṣayān teṣu gocarān
ātma indriya manaḥ yuktam bhoktā iti āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ iti
taiḥ ca indriya ādibhiḥ asaṃyataiḥ saṃsāram adhigacchati saṃyataiḥ tu adhvanaḥ pāram tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam āpnoti iti kim tat adhvanaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām tebhyaḥ eva prakṛtebhyaḥ indriya ādibhyaḥ paratvena paramātmānam adhvanaḥ pāram tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam darśayati indriyebhyaḥ parāḥ hi arthāḥ arthebhyaḥ ca param manaḥ
manasaḥ tu parā buddhiḥ buddheḥ ātmā mahān paraḥ
mahataḥ param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ
puruṣāt na param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti
tatra ye eva indriya ādayaḥ pūrvasyām ratha rūpaka kalpanāyām aśva ādi bhāvena prakṛtāḥ te eva iha parigṛhyante prakṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriyā parihārāya
tatra indriya manaḥ buddhayaḥ tāvat pūrvatra iha ca samāna śabdāḥ eva
arthāḥ tu ye śabda ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ indriya haya gocara tvena nirdiṣṭāḥ teṣām ca indriyebhyaḥ paratvam indriyāṇām ca graha tvam viṣayāṇām atigraha tvam iti śruti prasiddheḥ
viṣayebhyaḥ ca manasaḥ para tvam manaḥ mūla tvāt viṣaya indriya vyavahārasya
manasaḥ tu parā buddhiḥ buddhim hi āruhya bhogya jātam bhoktāram upasarpati
buddheḥ ātmā mahān paraḥ yaḥ saḥ ātmānam rathinam viddhi iti rathi tvena upakṣiptaḥ
kutas
ātma śabdāt bhoktuḥ ca bhoga upakaraṇāt paratva upapatteḥ
mahat tvam ca asya svāmi tvāt upapannam
athavā manaḥ mahān matiḥ brahmā pūḥ buddhiḥ khyātiḥ īśvaraḥ
prajñā saṃvid citiḥ ca eva smṛtiḥ ca paripaṭhyate iti smṛteḥ yaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhāti pūrvam yaḥ vai vedān ca prahiṇoti tasmai iti ca śruteḥ
yā prathama jasya hiraṇyagarbhasya buddhiḥ sā sarvāsām buddhīnām paramā pratiṣṭhā
sa iha mahān ātmā iti ucyate
sā ca pūrvatra buddhi grahaṇena eva gṛhītā satī hiruk iha upadiśyate tasyāḥ api asmadīyābhyaḥ buddhibhyaḥ paratva upapatteḥ
etasmin tu pakṣe paramātma viṣayeṇa eva pareṇa puruṣa grahaṇena rathinaḥ ātmanaḥ grahaṇam draṣṭavyam paramārthataḥ tu paramātma vijñāna ātmanoḥ bheda abhāvāt
tat evam śarīram eva ekam pariśiṣyate
teṣu itarāṇi indriya ādīni prakṛtāni eva parama pada didarśayiṣayā samanukrāman pariśiṣyamāṇena iha antyena avyakta śabdena pariśiṣyamāṇam prakṛtam śarīram darśayati iti gamyate
śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi viṣaya vedanā saṃyuktasya hi avidyāvataḥ bhoktuḥ śarīra ādīnām ratha ādi rūpaka kalpanayā saṃsāra mokṣa gati nirūpaṇena pratyagātma brahma avagatiḥ iha vivakṣitā
tathā ca eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ tmā na prakāśate
dṛśyate tu agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ iti vaiṣṇavasya parama padasya duravagama tvam uktvā tad avagama artham yogam darśayati yacchet vāc manasī prājñaḥ tat yacchet jñāne ātmani
jñānam ātmani mahati niyacchet tat yacchet śānte ātmani iti
etat uktam bhavati vācam manasi saṃyacchet vāc ādi bāhya indriya vyāpāram utsṛjya manaḥ mātreṇa avatiṣṭheta
manaḥ pi viṣaya vikalpa abhimukham vikalpa doṣa darśanena jñāna śabda uditāyām buddhau adhyavasāya svabhāvāyām dhārayet
tām api buddhim mahati ātmani bhoktari agryāyām vā buddhau sūkṣma tā āpādanena niyacchet
mahāntam tu ātmānam śānte ātmani prakaraṇavati parasmin puruṣe parasyām kāṣṭhāyām pratiṣṭhāpayet iti ca
tat evam pūrva apara ālocanāyām na asti atra para parikalpitasya pradhānasya avakāśaḥ
sūkṣmam tu tad arha tvāt
uktam etat prakaraṇa pariśeṣābhyām śarīram avyakta śabdam na pradhānam iti
idam idānīm āśaṅkyate katham avyakta śabda artha tvam śarīrasya yāvatā sthūla tvāt spaṣṭataram idam śarīram vyakta śabda artham aspaṣṭa vacanaḥ tu avyakta śabdaḥ iti
atas uttaram ucyate sūkṣmam tu iha kāraṇa ātmanā śarīram vivakṣyate sūkṣmasya avyakta śabda artha tvāt
yadi api sthūlam idam śarīram na svayam avyakta śabdam arhati tathā api tasya tu ārambhakam bhūta sūkṣmam avyakta śabdam arhati
prakṛti śabdaḥ ca vikāre dṛṣṭaḥ yathā gobhiḥ śrīṇīta matsaram iti
śrutiḥ ca tat ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt iti idam eva vyākṛta nāma rūpa vibhinnam jagat prāc avasthāyām parityakta vyākṛta nāma rūpam bīja śakti avastham avyakta śabda yogyam darśayati
tad adhīna tvāt arthavat
atra āha yadi jagat idam anabhivyakta nāma rūpam bīja ātmakam prāk avastham avyakta śabda arham abhyupagamyeta tadā ātmanā ca śarīrasya api avyakta śabda arha tvam pratijñāyeta saḥ eva tarhi pradhāna kāraṇa vādaḥ evam sati āpadyeta
asya eva jagataḥ prāk avasthāyāḥ pradhāna tvena abhyupagamāt iti
atrā ucyate yadi vayam svatantrām kāṃcid prāc avasthām jagataḥ kāraṇa tvena abhyupagacchema prasañjayema tadā pradhāna kāraṇa vādam
parameśvara adhīnā tu iyam asmābhiḥ prāc avasthā jagataḥ abhyupagamyate na svatantrā
sā ca avaśya abhyupagantavyā
arthavatī hi sā
na hi tayā vinā parameśvarasya sraṣṭṛ tvam sidhyati śakti rahitasya tasya pravṛtti anupapatteḥ
muktānām ca punar anutpattiḥ
kutas
vidyayā tasyāḥ bīja śakteḥ dāhāt
avidyā ātmikā hi sā bīja śaktiḥ avyakta śabda nirdeśyā parameśvara āśrayā māyā mayī mahāsuṣuptiḥ yasyām sva rūpa pratibodha rahitāḥ śerate saṃsāriṇaḥ jīvāḥ
tat etat avyaktam kvacid ākāśa śabda nirdiṣṭam etasmin u khalu akṣare gārgya ākāśaḥ otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti śruteḥ
kvacid akṣara śabda uditam akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti śruteḥ
kvacid māyā iti sūcitam māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram iti mantra varṇāt
avyaktā hi sā māyā tattva anyatva nirūpaṇasya aśakya tvāt
tat idam mahataḥ param avyaktam iti uktam avyakta prabhava tvāt mahataḥ yadā hairaṇyagarbhī buddhiḥ mahān
yadā tu jīvaḥ mahān
tadā api avyakta adhīna tvāt jīva bhāvasya mahataḥ param avyaktam iti uktam
avidyā hi avyaktam
avidyāvat tvena eva jīvasya sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ saṃtataḥ vartate
tat ca avyakta gatam mahataḥ para tvam abheda upacārāt tad vikāre śarīre parikalpyate
sati api śarīra vat indriya ādīnām tad vikāra tva aviśeṣe śarīrasya eva abheda upacārāt avyakta śabdena grahaṇam indriya ādīnām sva śabdaiḥ eva gṛhīta tvāt pariśiṣṭa tvāt ca śarīrasya
anye tu varṇayanti dvividham hi śarīram sthūlam sūkṣmam ca
sthūlam yat idam upalabhyate
sūkṣmam yat uttaratra vakṣyate tat antara pratipattau raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ praśna nirūpaṇābhyām iti
tat ca ubhayam api śarīram aviśeṣāt pūrvatra ratha tvena saṃkīrtitam
iha tu sūkṣmam avyakta śabdena parigṛhyate sūkṣmasya avyakta śabda arha tvāt
tad adhīna tvāt ca bandha mokṣa vyavahārasya jīvāt tasya paratvam
yathā artha adhīna tvāt indriya vyāpārasya indriyebhyaḥ paratvam arthānām iti
taiḥ tu etat vaktavyam aviśeṣeṇa śarīra dvayasya pūrvatra ratha tvena saṃkīrtita tvāt samānayoḥ prakṛta tva pariśiṣṭa tvayoḥ katham sūkṣmam eva śarīram iha gṛhyate na punar sthūlam api iti
āmnātasya artham pratipattum prabhavāmaḥ na āmnātam paryanuyoktum āmnātam ca avyakta padam sūkṣmam eva pratipādayitum śaknoti na itarat vyakta tvāt tasya iti ced na
eka vākya tā adhīna tvāt arthaṃpratipatteḥ
na hi ime pūrva uttare āmnāte ekavākya tām an āpadya kaṃcid artham pratipādayataḥ
prakṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriyā prasaṅgāt
na ca ākāṅkṣām antareṇa eka vākya tā pratipattiḥ asti
tatra aviśiṣṭāyām śarīra dvayasya grāhya tva ākāṅkṣāyām yathākāṅkṣam saṃbandhe na abhyupagamyamāne ekavākya tā eva bādhitā bhavati kutas āmnātasya arthasya pratipattiḥ
na ca evam mantavyam duḥśodha tvāt sūkṣmasya eva śarīrasya iha grahaṇam sthūlasya tu dṛṣṭa bībhatsa tayā su śodha tvāt agrahaṇam iti
yatas nā evā iha śodhanam kasyacid vivakṣyate
na hi atra śodhana vidhāyi kiṃcid ākhyātam asti
anantara nirdiṣṭa tvāt tu kim tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti idam iha vivakṣyate
tathā hi idam asmāt param idam asmāt param iti uktvā puruṣāt na param kiṃcid iti āha
sarvathā api tu ānumānika nirākaraṇa upapatteḥ tathā nāma astu
na naḥ kiṃcid chidyate
jñeya tva avacanāt ca
jñeya tvena ca sāṃkhyaiḥ pradhānam smaryate guṇa puruṣa antara jñānāt kaivalyam iti vadadbhiḥ na hi guṇa svarūpam a jñātvā guṇebhyaḥ puruṣasya antaram śakyam jñātum iti
kvacid ca vibhūti viśeṣa prāptaye pradhānam jñeyam iti smaranti
na ca idam iha avyaktam jñeya tvena ucyate
pada mātram hi avyakta śabdaḥ na iha avyaktam jñātavyam upāsitavyam ca iti vākyam asti
na ca anupadiṣṭam padārtha jñānam puruṣa artham iti śakyam pratipattum
tasmāt api na avyakta śabdena pradhānam abhidhīyate
asmākam tu ratha rūpaka klṛpta śarīra ādi anusaraṇena viṣṇoḥ eva paramam padam darśayitum ayam upanyāsaḥ iti anavadyam
vadati iti ced na prājñaḥ hi prakaraṇāt
atra āha sāṃkhyaḥ jñeya tva avacanāt iti asiddham
katham
śrūyate hi uttaratra avyakta śabda uditasya pradhānasya jñeya tva vacanam aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam tathā arasam nityam a gandhavat ca yat
anādi anantam mahataḥ param dhruvam nicāyya tam mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti
atra hi yādṛśam śabda ādi hīnam pradhānam mahataḥ param smṛtau nirūpitam tādṛśam eva nicāyya tvena nirdiṣṭam tasmāt pradhānam eva idam
tat eva ca avyakta śabda nirdiṣṭam iti
atra brūmaḥ na iha pradhānam nicāyya tvena nirdiṣṭam
prājñaḥ hi iha paramātmā nicāyya tvena nirdiṣṭaḥ iti gamyate
kutas
prakaraṇāt
prājñasya hi prakaraṇam vitatam vartate puruṣāt na param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ ityādi nirdeśāt eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu guḍhaḥ tmā na prakāśate iti ca durjñāna tva vacanena tasya eva jñeya tva ākāṅkṣaṇāt yacchet vāc manasī prājñaḥ iti ca tad jñānāya eva vāc ādi saṃyamasya vihita tvāt mṛtyu mukha pramokṣaṇa phala tvāt ca
na hi pradhāna mātram nicāyya mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti sāṃkhyaiḥ iṣyate
cetanā ātma vijñānāt hi mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti teṣām abhyupagamaḥ
sarveṣu vedānteṣu prājñasya eva ātmanaḥ śabda ādi dharma tvam abhilapyate
tasmāt na pradhānasya atra jñeya tvam avyakta śabda nirdiṣṭa tvam vā
trayāṇām eva ca evam upanyāsaḥ praśnaḥ ca
itas ca na pradhānasya avyakta śabda vācya tvam jñeya tvam vā
yasmāt trayāṇām eva padārthānām agni jīva paramātmanām asmin granthe kaṭhavallīṣu vara pradāna sāmarthyāt vaktavya tayā upanyāsaḥ dṛśyate
tad viṣayaḥ eva ca praśnaḥ
na atas nyasya praśnaḥ upanyāsaḥ vā asti
tatra tāvat sa tvam agnim svargyam adhyeṣi mṛtyo prabrūhi tam śraddadhānāya mahyam iti agni viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ
yā iyam prete vicikitsā manuṣye sti iti eke na ayam asti iti ca eke
etad vidyām anuśiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti jīva viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ
anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt anyatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt
anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yat tat paśyasi tat vada iti paramātma viṣayaḥ
prativacanam api loka ādim agnim tam uvāca tasmai yāḥ iṣṭakāḥ yāvatīḥ vā yathā vai iti agni viṣayam
hanta te idam pravakṣyāmi guhyam brahma sanātanam
yathā ca maraṇam prāpya ātmā bhavati gautama
yonim anye prapadyante śarīra tvāya dehinaḥ
sthāṇum anye nusaṃyanti yathākarma yathāśrutam iti vyavahitam jīva viṣayam
na jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi bahu prapañcam paramātma viṣayam
na evam pradhāna viṣayaḥ sti
a pṛṣṭa tvāt ca an upanyasanīya tvam tasya iti
atra āha yaḥ yam ātma viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā manuṣye sti iti kim saḥ eva ayam anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt iti punar anukṛṣyate kim vā tatas nyaḥ yam apūrvaḥ praśnaḥ utthāpyate iti
kim ca atas
saḥ eva ayam praśnaḥ punar anukṛṣyate iti yadi ucyeta tadā dvayoḥ ātma viṣayayoḥ praśnayoḥ ekatā āpatteḥ agni viṣayaḥ ātma viṣayaḥ ca dvau eva praśnau iti atas na vaktavyam trayāṇām praśna upanyāsau iti
atha anyaḥ yam apūrvaḥ praśnaḥ utthāpyate iti ucyeta tatas yathā eva vara pradāna vyatirekeṇa praśna kalpanāyām adoṣaḥ
evam praśna vyatirekeṇa api pradhāna upanyāsa kalpanāyām adoṣaḥ syāt iti
atrā ucyate na evam vayam iha vara pradāna vyatirekeṇa praśnam kaṃcid kalpayāmaḥ vākya upakrama sāmarthyāt
vara pradāna upakramā hi mṛtyu naciketaḥ saṃvāda rūpā vākya pravṛttiḥ ā samāpteḥ kaṭha vallīnām lakṣyate
mṛtyuḥ kila naciketase pitrā prahitāya trīn varān pradadau
naciketāḥ kila teṣām prathamena vareṇa pituḥ saumanasyam vavre dvitīyena agni vidyām tṛtīyena ātma vidyām yā iyam prete iti varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti liṅgāt
tatra yadi anyatra dharmāt iti anyaḥ yam apūrvaḥ praśnaḥ utthāpyeta tatas vara pradāna vyatirekeṇa api praśna kalpanāt vākyam bādhyeta
nanu praṣṭavya bhedāt apūrvaḥ yam praśnaḥ bhavitum arhati
apūrvaḥ hi praśnaḥ jīva viṣayaḥ yā iyam prete vicikitsā manuṣye sti na asti iti vicikitsā abhidhānāt
jīvaḥ ca dharma ādi gocara tvāt na anyatra dharmāt iti praśnam arhati
prājñaḥ tu dharma ādi atīta tvāt anyatra dharmāt iti praśnam arhati
praśna chāyā ca na samānā lakṣyate pūrvasya astitva nāstitva viṣaya tvāt uttarasya dharma ādi atīta vastu viṣaya tvāt ca
tasmāt pratyabhijñāna abhāvāt praśna bhedaḥ
na pūrvasya eva uttaratra anukarṣaṇam iti ced na
jīva prājñayoḥ ekatva abhyupagamāt
bhavet praṣṭavya bhedāt praśna bhedaḥ yadi anyaḥ jīvaḥ prājñāt syāt
na tu anya tvam asti tat tvam asi ityādi śruti antarebhyaḥ
iha ca anyatra dharmāt iti asya praśnasya prativacanam na jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit iti janma maraṇa pratiṣedhena pratipādyamānam śārīra parameśvarayoḥ abhedam darśayati
sati hi prasaṅge pratiṣedhaḥ bhāgī bhavati
prasaṅgaḥ ca janma maraṇayoḥ śarīra saṃsparśāt śārīrasya bhavati na parameśvarasya
tathā svapna antam jāgarita antam ca ubhau yena anupaśyati
mahāntam vibhum ātmānam matvā dhīraḥ na śocati iti svapna jāgarita dṛśaḥ jīvasya eva mahat tva vibhu tva viśeṣaṇasya mananena śoka vicchedam darśayan na prājñāt anyaḥ jīvaḥ iti darśayati
prājña vijñānāt hi śoka vicchedaḥ iti vedānta siddhāntaḥ
tathā agre yat eva iha tat amutra yat amutra tat anu iha
mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti jīva prājña bheda dṛṣṭim apavadati
tathā jīva viṣayasya astitva nāstitva praśnasya anantaram anyam varam naciketaḥ vṛṇīṣva iti ārabhya mṛtyunā taiḥ taiḥ kāmaiḥ pralobhyamānaḥ u pi naciketāḥ yadā na cacāla tadā enam mṛtyuḥ abhyudaya niḥśreyasa vibhāga pradarśanena vidyā vidyā vibhāga pradarśanena ca vidyā abhīpsinam naciketasam manye na tvā kāmāḥ bahavaḥ lolupantaḥ iti praśnasya praśnam api tadīyam praśaṃs anyat uvāca tam durdarśam gūḍham anupraviṣṭam guhā hitam gahvar
adhyātma yoga adhigamena devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti iti tena api jīva prājñayoḥ abhedaḥ evā iha vivakṣitaḥ iti gamyate
yat praśna nimittām ca praśaṃsām mahatīm mṛtyoḥ pratyapadyata naciketāḥ yadi tam vihāya praśaṃsā anantaram anyam eva praśnam upakṣipet asthāne eva sā sarvā praśaṃsā prasāritā syāt
tasmāt yā iyam prete iti asya eva praśnasya etat anukarṣaṇam anyatra dharmāt iti
yat tu praśna chāyā vailakṣaṇyam uktam tat adūṣaṇam tadīyasya eva viśeṣasya punar pṛcchyamāna tvāt
pūrvatra hi deha ādi vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ stitvam pṛṣṭam uttaratra tu tasya eva asaṃsāri tvam iti
yāvat hi avidyā na nivartate tāvat dharma ādi gocara tvam jīvasya jīva tvam ca na nivartate tad nivṛttau tu prājñaḥ eva tat tvam asi iti śrutyā pratyāyyate
na ca avidyāvat tve tad apagame ca vastunaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ sti
yathā kaścid sam tamase patitām kāṃcid rajjum ahim manyamānaḥ bhītaḥ vepamānaḥ palāyate tam ca aparaḥ brūyāt mā bhaiṣīḥ na ayam ahiḥ rajjuḥ eva iti sa ca tad upaśrutya ahi kṛtam bhayam utsṛjet vepathum palāyanam ca na tu ahi buddhi kāle tad apagama kāle ca vastunaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ syāt tathā eva etat api draṣṭavyam
tatas ca na jāyate mriyate vā iti evamādi api bhavati astitva nāstitva praśnasya prativacanam
sūtram tu avidyā kalpita jīva prājña bheda apekṣayā yojayitavyam ekatve hi ātma viṣayasya praśnasya prāyaṇa avasthāyām deha vyatirikta astitva mātra vicikitsanāt kartṛ tva ādi saṃsāra svabhāva anapohanāt ca pūrvasya paryāyasya jīva viṣaya tvam utprekṣyate uttarasya tu dharma ādi atyaya saṃkīrtanāt prājña viṣaya tvam iti
tatas ca yuktā agni jīva paramātma kalpanā
pradhāna kalpanāyām tu na vara pradānam na praśnaḥ na prativacanam iti vaiṣamyam
mahadvat ca
yathā mahat śabdaḥ sāṃkhyaiḥ sattā mātre pi prathama je prayuktaḥ na tam eva vaidike pi prayoge bhidhatte buddheḥ ātmā mahān paraḥ mahāntam vibhum ātmānam veda aham etam puruṣam mahāntam iti evamādau ātma śabda prayoga ādibhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ
tathā avyakta śabdaḥ pi na vaidike prayoge pradhānam abhidhātum arhati
atas ca na asti ānumānikasya śabdavat tvam
camasa vat aviśeṣāt
camasa adhikaraṇam
punar api pradhāna vādī aśabda tvam pradhānasya asiddham iti āha
kasmāt
mantra varṇāt ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām vahvīḥ prajāḥ sṛjamānām sarūpāḥ
ajaḥ hi ekaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ nuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ nyaḥ iti
atra hi mantre lohita śukla kṛṣṇa śabdaiḥ rajaḥ sattva tamāṃsi abhidhīyante
lohitam rajaḥ rañjana ātmaka tvāt śuklam sattvam prakāśa ātmaka tvāt
kṛṣṇam tamaḥ āvaraṇa ātmaka tvāt
teṣām sāmya avasthā avayava dharmaiḥ vyapadiśyate lohita śukla kṛṣṇā iti
na jāyate iti ca ajā syāt mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ iti abhyupagamāt
nanu ajā śabdaḥ chāgyām rūḍhaḥ
bāḍham
sā tu rūḍhiḥ iha na āśrayitum śakyā vidyā prakaraṇāt
sā ca bahvīḥ prajāḥ traiguṇya anvitāḥ janayati
tām prakṛtim ajaḥ ekaḥ puruṣaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ prīyamāṇaḥ sevamānaḥ vā anuśetetām eva avidyayā ātma tvena upagamya sukhī duḥkhī mūḍhaḥ ham iti aviveki tayā saṃsarati
anyaḥ punar ajaḥ puruṣaḥ utpanna viveka jñānaḥ viraktaḥ jahāti enām prakṛtim bhukta bhogām kṛta bhoga apavargām parityajati mucyate iti arthaḥ
tasmāt śruti mūlā eva pradhāna ādi kalpanā kāpilānām iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na anena mantreṇa śrutimat tvam sāṃkhya vādasya śakyam āśrayitum
na hi ayam mantraḥ svātantryeṇa kaṃcid api vādam samarthayitum utsahate sarvatra api yayā kayācid kalpanayā ajātu ādi saṃpādana upapatteḥ sāṃkhya vādaḥ evā iha abhipretaḥ iti viśeṣa avadhāraṇa kāraṇa abhāvāt
camasa vat yathā hi arvāc bilaḥ camasaḥ ūrdhva budhnaḥ iti asmin mantre svātantryeṇa ayam nāma asau camasaḥ bhipretaḥ iti na śakyate niyantum sarvatra api yathā kathaṃcid arvāc bila tva ādi kalpanā upapatteḥ evam iha api aviśeṣaḥ ajām ekām iti asya mantrasya
na asmin mantre pradhānam eva ajā abhipretā iti śakyate niyantum
tatra tu idam tat śiraḥ eṣa hi arvāc bilaḥ camasaḥ ūrdhva buddhnaḥ iti vākya śeṣāt camasa viśeṣa pratipattiḥ bhavati
iha punar kā iyam ajā pratipattavyā iti atra brūmaḥ
jyotiḥ upakramā tu tathā hi adhīyate eke
parameśvarāt utpannā jyotiḥ pramukhā tejaḥ banna lakṣaṇā caturvidhasya bhūta grāmasya prakṛti bhūtā iyam ajā pratipattavyā
tu śabdaḥ bhūta traya lakṣaṇā eva iyam ajā vijñeyā na guṇa traya lakṣaṇā
kasmāt
tathā hi eke śākhinaḥ tejaḥ bannānām parameśvarāt utpattim āmnāya teṣām eva rohita ādi rūpa tām āmananti yat agneḥ rohitam rūpam tejasaḥ tat rūpam yat śuklam tat apām yat kṛṣṇam tat annasya iti
tāni eva iha tejaḥ bannāni pratyabhijñāyante rohita ādi śabda sāmānyāt rohita ādīnām ca śabdānām rūpa viśeṣeṣu mukhya tvāt bhākta tvāt ca guṇa viṣaya tvasya
asaṃdigdhena ca saṃdigdhasya nigamanam nyāyyam manyante
tathā iha api brahma vādinaḥ vadanti
kiṃkāraṇam brahma
iti upakramya te dhyāna yoga anugatāḥ apaśyan deva ātma śaktim sva guṇaiḥ nigūḍhām iti pārameśvaryāḥ śakteḥ samasta jagat vidhāyinyāḥ vākya upakrame vagamāt vākyaśeṣe māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram iti yaḥ yonim yonim adhitiṣṭhati ekaḥ iti ca tasyāḥ eva avagamāt na svatantrā kācid prakṛtiḥ pradhānam nāma ajām antreṇa āmnāyate iti śakyate vaktum
prakaraṇāt tu sā eva daivī śaktiḥ avyākṛta nām arūpā nāma rūpayoḥ prāk avasthā anena api mantreṇa āmnāyate iti ucyate
tasyāḥ ca sva vikāra viṣayeṇa trairūpyeṇa trairūpyam uktam
katham punar tejaḥ banna ātmanā trairūpyeṇa tri rūpā ajā pratipattum śakyate yāvatā na tāvat tejaḥ banneṣu aja ākṛtiḥ asti na ca tejaḥ bannānām jāti śravaṇāt a jāti nimittaḥ u pi ajā śabdaḥ saṃbhavati iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
kalpanā upadeśāt ca madhu ādi vat avirodhaḥ
na ayam aja ākṛti nimittaḥ jā śabdaḥ
na api yaugikaḥ
kim tarhi kalpanā upadeśaḥ yam ajā rūpaka klṛptiḥ tejaḥ banna lakṣaṇāyāḥ carācara yoneḥ upadiśyate
yathā hi loke yadṛcchayā kācid ajā rohita śukla kṛṣṇa varṇā syāt bahu barkarā sarūpa barkarā ca tām ca kaścid ajaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ nuśayīta kaścid ca enām bhukta bhogām jahyāt evam iyam api tejaḥ banna lakṣaṇā bhūtaprakṛtiḥ tri varṇā bahu sarūpam carācara lakṣaṇam vikāra jātam janayati a viduṣā ca kṣetrajñena upabhujyate viduṣā ca parityajyate iti
na ca idam āśaṅkitavyam ekaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ nuśete anyaḥ jahāti iti atas kṣetrajña bhedaḥ pāramārthikaḥ pareṣām iṣṭaḥ prāpnoti iti
na hi iyam kṣetrajña bheda pratipipādayiṣā
kiṃtu bandha mokṣa vyavasthā pratipipādayiṣā eva eṣā
prasiddham tu bhedam anūdya bandha mokṣa vyavasthā pratipādyate
bhedaḥ tu upādhi nimittaḥ mithyā jñāna kalpitaḥ
na pāramārthikaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
madhu ādi vat yathā ādityasya a madhunaḥ madhu tvam vācaḥ ca a dhenoḥ dhenu tvam dyu loka ādīnām ca anagnīnām agni tvam iti evaṃjātīyakam kalpyate evam idam anajāyāḥ ajā tvam kalpyate iti arthaḥ
tasmāt avirodhaḥ tejaḥ banneṣu ajā śabda prayogasya
na saṃkhyā upasaṃgrahāt api nānābhāvāt atirekāt ca
saṃkhyā upasaṃgraha adhikaraṇam
evam parihṛte pyajā mantre punar api anyasmāt mantrāt sāṃkhyaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate yasmin pañca pañcajanāḥ ākāśaḥ ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ
tam eva manye ātmānam vidvān brahma amṛtaḥ mṛtam iti
asmin mantre pañca pañcajanāḥ iti pañca saṃkhyā viṣayā aparā pañca saṃkhyā śrūyate pañca śabda dvaya darśanāt
te ete pañca pañcakāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ saṃpadyante
tayā ca pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā yāvantaḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ ākāṅkṣyante tāvanti eva ca tattvāni sāṃkhyaiḥ saṃkhyāyante mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ mahat ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ sapta
ṣoḍaśakaḥ ca vikāraḥ na prakṛtiḥ na vikṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ iti
tayā śruti prasiddhayā pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā teṣām smṛti prasiddhānām pañcaviṃśateḥ tattvānām upasaṃgrahāt prāptam punar śrutimat tvam eva pradhāna ādīnām
tatas brūmaḥ na saṃkhyā upasaṃgrahāt api pradhāna ādīnām śrutimat tvam pratyāśā kartavyā
kasmāt
nānābhāvāt
nānā hi etāni pañcaviṃśatiḥ tattvāni
na eṣām pañcaśas pañcaśas sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ sti yena pañcaviṃśateḥ antarāle parāḥ pañca pañca saṃkhyāḥ niviśeran
na hi eka nibandhanam antareṇa nānā bhūteṣu dvi tva ādikāḥ saṃkhyāḥ niviśante
atha ucyeta pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyā eva iyam avayava dvāreṇa lakṣyate yathā pañca sapta ca varṣāṇi na vavarṣa śatakratuḥ iti dvādaśa vārṣikīm anāvṛṣṭim kathayanti tadvat iti
tat api na upapadyate
ayam eva asmin pakṣe doṣaḥ yat lakṣaṇā āśrayaṇīyā syāt
paraḥ ca atra pañca śabdaḥ jana śabdena samastaḥ pañcajanāḥ iti bhāṣika svareṇa eka pada tva niścayāt
prayoga antare ca pañcānām tvā pañcajanānām iti aikapadya ekasvarya eka vibhaktika tva avagamāt
samasta tvāt ca na vīpsā pañca pañca iti
tena na pañcaka dvaya grahaṇam pañca pañca iti
na ca pañca saṃkhyāyāḥ ekasyāḥ pañca saṃkhyayā parayā viśeṣaṇam pañca pañcakāḥ iti upasarjanasya viśeṣaṇena asaṃyogāt
nanu āpanna pañca saṃkhyākāḥ janāḥ eva punar pañca saṃkhyayā viśeṣyamāṇāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pratyeṣyante yathā pañca pañca pūlyaḥ iti pañcaviṃśatiḥ pūlāḥ pratīyante tadvat
na iti brūmaḥ
yuktam yat pañca pūlī śabdasya samāhāra abhiprāya tvāt kati iti satyām bheda ākāṅkṣāyām pañca pañca pūlyaḥ iti viśeṣaṇam
iha tu pañca janāḥ iti āditas eva bheda upādānāt kati iti asatyām bheda ākāṅkṣāyām na pañca pañcajanāḥ iti viśeṣaṇam bhavet
bhavat api idam viśeṣaṇam pañca saṃkhyāyāḥ eva bhavet
tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ
tasmāt pañca pañcajanāḥ iti na pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam
atirekāt ca na pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam
atirekaḥ hi bhavati ātma ākāśābhyām pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyāyāḥ
ātmā tāvat iha pratiṣṭhām pratyādhāra tvena nirdiṣṭaḥ yasmin iti saptamī sūcitasya tam eva manye ātmānam iti ātma tvena anukarṣaṇāt
ātmā ca cetanaḥ puruṣaḥ
sa ca pañcaviṃśatau antargataḥ eva iti na tasya eva ādhāra tvam ādheya tvam ca yujyeta
artha antara parigrahe vā tattva saṃkhyā atirekaḥ siddhānta viruddhaḥ prasajyeta
tathā ākāśaḥ ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti ākāśasya api pañcaviṃśatau antargatasya na pṛthak upādānam nyāyyam
artha antara parigrahe ca uktam dūṣaṇam
katham ca saṃkhyā mātra śravaṇe satya śrutānām pañcaviṃśati tattvānām upasaṃgrahaḥ pratīyeta
jana śabdasya tattveṣu arūḍha tvāt artha antara upasaṃgrahe pi saṃkhyā upapatteḥ
katham tarhi pañca pañcajanāḥ iti
ucyate diś saṃkhye saṃjñāyām iti viśeṣa smaraṇāt saṃjñāyām eva pañca śabdasya jana śabdena samāsaḥ
tatas ca rūḍha tva abhiprāyeṇa eva kecid pañcajanāḥ nāma vivakṣyante na sāṃkhya tattva abhiprāyeṇa
te kati iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām punar pañca iti prayujyate
pañcajanāḥ nāma ye kecid te ca pañca eva iti arthaḥ saptarṣayaḥ sapta iti yathā
ke punar te pañcajanāḥ nāma iti tat ucyate
prāṇa ādayaḥ vākya śeṣāt
yasmin pañca pañcajanāḥ iti atas uttarasmin mantre brahma svarūpa nirūpaṇāya prāṇa ādayaḥ pañca nirdiṣṭāḥ prāṇasya prāṇam uta cakṣuṣaḥ cakṣuḥ uta śrotrasya śrotram annasya annam manasaḥ ye manaḥ viduḥ iti
te tra vākyaśeṣa gatāḥ saṃnidhānāt pañcajanāḥ vivakṣyante
katham punar prāṇa ādiṣu jana śabda prayogaḥ
tattveṣu vā katham jana śabda prayogaḥ
samāne tu prasiddhi atikrame vākya śeṣa vaśāt prāṇa ādayaḥ eva grahītavyāḥ bhavanti
jana saṃbandhāt ca prāṇa ādayaḥ jana śabda bhājaḥ bhavanti
jana vacanaḥ ca puruṣa śabdaḥ prāṇeṣu prayuktaḥ te vai ete pañca brahma puruṣāḥ iti atra
prāṇaḥ ha pitā prāṇaḥ ha mātā ityādi ca brāhmaṇam
samāsa balāt ca samudāyasya rūḍha tvam aviruddham
katham punar asati prathama prayoge rūḍhiḥ śakyā āśrayitum
śakyāḥ udbhida ādi vat iti āha prasiddha artha saṃnidhāne hi aprasiddha arthaḥ śabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ samabhivyāhārāt tad viṣayaḥ niyamyate
yathā udbhidā yajeta yūpam chinatti vedim karoti iti tathā ayam api pañcajana śabdaḥ samāsa anvākhyānāt avagata saṃjñā bhāvaḥ saṃjñī ākāṅkṣī vākya śeṣa samabhivyāhṛteṣu prāṇa ādiṣu vartiṣyate
kaiścid tu devāḥ pitaraḥ gandharvāḥ asurāḥ rakṣāṃsi ca pañca pañcajanāḥ vyākhyātāḥ
anyaiḥ ca catvāraḥ varṇāḥ niṣāda pañcamāḥ parigṛhītāḥ
kvacid ca yat pāñcajanyayā viśā iti prajā paraḥ prayogaḥ pañcajana śabdasya dṛśyate
tad parigrahe pi iha na kaścid virodhaḥ
ācāryaḥ tu na pañcaviṃśateḥ tattvānām iha pratītiḥ asti iti evaṃpara tayā prāṇa ādayaḥ vākyaśeṣāt iti jagāda
bhaveyuḥ tāvat prāṇa ādayaḥ pañcajanāḥ mādhyaṃdinānām ye nnam prāṇa ādiṣu āmananti
kāṇvānām tu katham prāṇa ādayaḥ pañcajanāḥ bhaveyuḥ ye nnam prāṇa ādiṣu na āmananti iti atas uttaram paṭhati
jyotiṣā ekeṣām asati anne
asati api kāṇvānām anne jyotiṣā teṣām pañca saṃkhyā pūryeta
te pi hi yasmin pañca pañcajanāḥ iti atas pūrvasmin mantre brahma svarūpa nirūpaṇāya eva jyotiḥ adhīyate tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ iti
katham punar ubhayeṣām api tulya vat idam jyotiḥ paṭhyamānam samāna mantra gatayā pañca saṃkhyayā keṣāṃcid gṛhyate keṣāṃcid na iti apekṣā bhedāt iti āha mādhyaṃdinānām hi samāna mantra paṭhita prāṇa ādi pañcajana lābhāt na asmin mantra antara paṭhite jyotiṣi apekṣā bhavati
tad alābhāt tu kāṇvānām bhavati apekṣā
apekṣā bhedāt ca samāne pi mantre jyotiṣaḥ grahaṇa agrahaṇe
yathā samāne pi atirātre vacana bhedāt ṣoḍaśinaḥ grahaṇa agrahaṇe tadvat
tat evam na tāvat śruti prasiddhiḥ kācid pradhāna viṣayā asti
smṛti nyāya prasiddhī tu parihariṣyete
kāraṇa tvena ca ākāśa ādiṣu yathā vyapadiṣṭa ukteḥ
kāraṇatva adhikaraṇam
pratipāditam brahmaṇaḥ lakṣaṇam
pratipāditam brahma viṣayam gati sāmānyam vedānta vākyānām
pratipāditam ca pradhānasya a śabda tvam
tatra idam aparam āśaṅkyate na janma ādi kāraṇatvam brahmaṇaḥ brahma viṣayam vā gati sāmānyam vedānta vākyānām pratipādayitum śakyam
kasmāt
vigāna darśanāt
prati veda antam hi anyā anyā sṛṣṭiḥ upalabhyate krama ādi vaicitryāt
tathā hi kvacid ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti ākāśa ādikā sṛṣṭiḥ āmnāyate
kvacid tejaḥ ādikā tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti
kvacid prāṇa ādikā sa prāṇam asṛjata prāṇāt śraddhām iti
kvacid akrameṇa eva lokānām utpattiḥ āmnāyate saḥ imān lokān asṛjata
ambhaḥ marīcīḥ maramā apaḥ iti
tathā kvacid asat pūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ paṭhyate asat vai idam agre āsīt tatas vai sat ajāyata iti asat eva idam agre āsīt tat sat āsīt tat samabhavat iti ca
kvacid asat vāda nirākaraṇena sat pūrvikā prakriyā pratijñāyate tat ha eke āhuḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti upakramya kutas tu khalu somya evam syāt iti ha uvāca katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti sattu eva somya idam agre āsīt iti
kvacid svayam kartṛkā eva vyākriyā jagataḥ nigadyate tat ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt tat nāma rūpābhyām eva vyākriyate iti
evam anekadhā vipratipatteḥ vastuni ca vikalpasya anupapatteḥ na vedānta vākyānām jagat kāraṇa avadhāraṇa para tā nyāyyā
smṛti nyāya prasiddhibhyām tu kāraṇa antara parigrahaḥ nyāyyaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ sati api prati vedāntam sṛjyamāneṣu ākāśa ādiṣu krama ādi dvārake vigāne na sraṣṭari kiṃcid vigānam asti
kutas
yathā vyapadiṣṭa ukteḥ yathābhūtaḥ hi ekasmin vedānte sarvajñaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ sarva ātmā ekaḥ dvitīyaḥ kāraṇa tvena vyapadiṣṭaḥ tathābhūtaḥ eva vedānta antareṣu api vyapadiśyate
tat yathā satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti
atra tāvat jñāna śabdena pareṇa ca tad viṣayeṇa kāmayitṛ tva vacanena cetanam brahma nyarūpayat
apara prayojya tvena īśvaram kāraṇam abravīt
tad viṣayeṇa eva pareṇa ātma śabdena śarīra ādi kośa paramparayā ca antar anupraveśanena sarveṣām antar pratyagātmānam niradhārayat
bahu syām prajāyeya iti ca ātma viṣayeṇa bahu bhavana anuśaṃsanena sṛjyamānānām vikārāṇām sraṣṭuḥ abhedam abhāṣata
tathā idam sarvam asṛjata
yat idam kim ca iti samasta jagat sṛṣṭi nirdeśena prāk sṛṣṭeḥ advitīyam sraṣṭāram ācaṣṭe
tat atra yat lakṣaṇam brahma kāraṇa tvena vijñātam
tad lakṣaṇam eva anyatra api vijñāyate sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti
tathā ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt na anyat kiṃcana miṣat
saḥ īkṣata lokān nu sṛjai iti ca evaṃjātīyakasya kāraṇa svarūpa nirūpaṇa parasya vākya jātasya prati vedāntam avigīta artha tvāt
kārya viṣayam tu vigānam dṛśyate kvacid ākāśa ādikā sṛṣṭiḥ kvacid tejaḥ ādikā iti evaṃjātīyakam
na ca kārya viṣayeṇa vigānena kāraṇam api brahma sarva vedānteṣu avigītam adhigamyamānam avivakṣitam bhavitum arhati iti śakyate vaktum atiprasaṅgāt
samādhāsyati ca ācāryaḥ kārya viṣayam api vigānam na viyat aśruteḥ iti ārabhya
bhavet api kāryasya vigīta tvam apratipādya tvāt
na hi ayam sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcaḥ
na hi tad pratibaddhaḥ kaścid puruṣa arthaḥ dṛśyate śrūyate vā
na ca kalpayitum śakyate upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām tatra tatra brahma viṣayaiḥ vākyaiḥ sākam eka vākya tāyāḥ gamyamāna tvāt
darśayati ca sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcasya brahma pratipatti artha tām annena somya śuṅgena apaḥ mūlam anviccha adbhiḥ somya śuṅgena tejaḥ mūlam anviccha tejasā somya śuṅgena sat mūlam anviccha iti
mṛd ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ ca kāryasya kāraṇena abhedam vaditum sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcaḥ śrāvyate iti gamyate
tathā ca saṃpradāya vidaḥ vadanti mṛd loha visphuliṅga ādyaiḥ sṛṣṭiḥ yā ca uditā anyathā
upāyaḥ saḥ vatārāya na asti bhedaḥ kathaṃcana iti
brahma pratipatti pratibaddham tu phalam śrūyate brahma vid āpnoti param tarati śokam ātma vid tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti iti
pratyakṣa avagamam ca idam phalam tat tvam asi iti a saṃsāri ātma tva pratipattau satyām saṃsāri ātma tva vyāvṛtteḥ
yat punar kāraṇa viṣayam vigānam darśitam asat vai idam agre āsīt ityādi tat parihartavyam
atrā ucyate
samākarṣāt
asat vai idam agre āsīt iti na atra asat nirātmakam kāraṇa tvena śrāvyate
yatas a san eva sa bhavati
asat brahma iti veda ced
asti brahma iti ced veda
santam enam tatas viduḥ iti asadvāda apavādena astitva lakṣaṇam brahma anna maya ādi kośa paramparayā pratyagātmānam nirdhārya saḥ kāmayate iti tam eva prakṛtam samākṛṣya sa prapañcām sṛṣṭim tasmāt śrāvayitvā tat satyam iti ācakṣate iti ca upasaṃhṛtya tat api eṣa ślokaḥ bhavati iti tasmin eva prakṛte rthe ślokam imam udāharati asat vai idam agre āsīt iti
yadi tu asat nirātmakam asmin śloke bhipreyeta tatas nya sama ākarṣaṇe nyasya udāharaṇāt asaṃbaddham vākyam āpadyeta
tasmāt nāma rūpa vyākṛta vastu viṣayaḥ prāyeṇa sat śabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ iti tad vyākaraṇa abhāva apekṣayā prāk utpatteḥ sat eva brahma asat iva āsīt iti upacaryate
eṣā eva asat eva idam agre āsīt iti atra api yojanā tat sat āsīt iti samākarṣaṇāt
atyanta abhāva abhyupagame hi tat sadā āsīt iti kim samākṛṣyeta
tat ha eke āhuḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti atra api na śruti antara abhiprāyeṇa ayam ekīya mata upanyāsaḥ kriyāyām iva vastuni vikalpasya asaṃbhavāt
tasmāt śruti parigṛhīta sat pakṣa dārḍhyāya eva ayam manda mati parikalpitasya asat pakṣasya upanyasya nirāsaḥ iti draṣṭavyam
tat ha idam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt iti atra api na niradhyakṣasya jagataḥ vyākaraṇam kathyate saḥ eṣaḥ iha praviṣṭaḥ ā nakha agrebhyaḥ iti adhyakṣasya vyākṛta kārya anupraveśi tvena samākarṣāt
niradhyakṣe vyākaraṇa abhyupagame hi anantareṇa prakṛta avalambinā saḥ iti anena sarvanāmnā kaḥ kārya anupraveśi tvena samākṛṣyeta
cetanasya ca ayam ātmanaḥ śarīre nupraveśaḥ śrūyate anupraviṣṭasya cetana tva śravaṇāt paśyan cakṣuḥ śrṛṇvan śrotram manvānaḥ manaḥ iti
api ca yādṛśam idam adya tve nāma rūpābhyām vyākriyamāṇam jagat sādhyakṣam vyākriyate evam ādisarge pi iti gamyate dṛṣṭa viparīta kalpanā anupapatteḥ
śruti antaram api anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti sa adhyakṣām eva jagataḥ vyākriyām darśayati
vyākriyatam iti api karma kartari lakāraḥ sati eva parameśvare vyākartari saukaryam apekṣya draṣṭavyaḥ yathā lūyate kedāraḥ svayam eva iti sati eva pūrṇake lavitari
yat vā karmaṇi eva eṣa lakāraḥ rtha ākṣiptam kartṛ antaram apekṣya draṣṭavyaḥ yathā gamyate grāmaḥ iti
jagat vāci tvāt
bālākī adhikaraṇam
kauṣītaki brāhmaṇe bālākī ajātaśatru saṃvāde śrūyate yaḥ vai bālākaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā yasya vā etat karma sa vai veditavyaḥ iti
tatra kim jīvaḥ veditavya tvena upadiśyate uta mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ uta paramātmā iti viśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
prāṇe iti
kutas
yasya vā etat karma iti śravaṇāt parispanda lakṣaṇasya ca karmaṇaḥ prāṇa āśraya tvāt
vākya śeṣe ca atha asmin prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati iti prāṇa śabda śravaṇāt prāṇa śabdasya ca mukhye prāṇe prasiddha tvāt
ye ca ete purastāt bālākinā āditye puruṣaḥ candramasi puruṣaḥ iti evamādayaḥ puruṣāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ teṣām api bhavati prāṇaḥ kartā prāṇa avasthā viśeṣa tvāt āditya ādi devatā ātmanām katamaḥ ekaḥ devaḥ iti prāṇaḥ iti sa brahma tyad iti ācakṣate iti śruti antara prasiddheḥ
jīvaḥ vā ayam iha veditavya tayā upadiśyate
tasya api dharma adharma lakṣaṇam karma śakyate śrāvayitum yasya vā etat karma iti
saḥ pi bhoktṛ tvāt bhoga upakaraṇa bhūtānām eteṣām puruṣāṇām ca kartā upapadyate
vākyaśeṣe jīva liṅgam avagamyate yatkāraṇam veditavyatayā upanyastasya puruṣāṇām kartuḥ vedanāya upetam bālākim prati bubodhayiṣuḥ ajātaśatruḥ suptam puruṣam āmantrya āmantraṇa śabda aśravaṇāt prāṇa ādīnām abhoktṛ tvam pratibodhya yaṣṭi ghāta utthāpanāt prāṇa ādi vyatiriktam jīvam bhoktāram pratibodhayati
tathā parastāt api jīva liṅgam avagamyate tat yathā śreṣṭhī svaiḥ bhuṅkte yathā vā svāḥ śreṣṭhinam bhuñjanti evam eva eṣa prajñā ātmā etaiḥ ātmabhiḥ bhuṅkte evam eva ete ātmānaḥ etam ātmānam bhuñjanti iti
prāṇabhṛt tvāt ca jīvasya upapannam prāṇa śabda tvam
tasmāt jīva mukhya prāṇayoḥ anyataraḥ iha grahaṇīyaḥ na parameśvaraḥ tad liṅga anavagamāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvaraḥ eva ayam eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā syāt
kasmāt
upakrama sāmarthyāt
iha hi bālākiḥ ajātaśatruṇā saha  brahma te SD bravāṇi SPr1Su
iti saṃvaditum upacakrame
sa ca katicid āditya ādi adhikaraṇān puruṣān amukhya brahma dṛṣṭi bhājaḥ uktvā tūṣṇīm babhūva
tam ajātaśatruḥ mṛṣā vai khalu mā saṃvadiṣṭhāḥ brahma te bravāṇi iti a mukhya brahma vādi tayā apodya tad kartāram anyam veditavya tayā upacikṣepa
yadi saḥ u pi amukhya brahma dṛṣṭi bhāj syāt upakramaḥ bādhyeta
tasmāt parameśvaraḥ eva ayam bhavitum arhati
kartṛ tvam ca eteṣām puruṣāṇām na parameśvarāt anyasya svātantryeṇa avakalpate
yasya vā etat karma iti api na ayam parispanda lakṣaṇasya dharma adharma lakṣaṇasya vā karmaṇaḥ nirdeśaḥ tayoḥ anyatarasya api aprakṛta tvāt asaṃśabdita tvāt ca
na api puruṣāṇām ayam nirdeśaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā iti eva teṣām nirdiṣṭa tvāt liṅga vacana vigānāt ca
nā api puruṣa viṣayasya karoti arthasya kriyā phalasya vā ayam nirdeśaḥ kartṛ śabdena eva tayoḥ upātta tvāt
pāriśeṣyāt pratyakṣa saṃnihitam jagat sarvanāmnā etad śabdena nirdiśyate
kriyate iti ca tat eva jagat karma
nanu jagat api aprakṛtam asaṃśabditam ca
satyam etat
tathā api asati viśeṣa upādāne sādhāraṇena arthena saṃnidhānena saṃnihita vastu mātrasya ayam nirdeśaḥ iti gamyate na viśiṣṭasya viśeṣa saṃnidhāna abhāvāt
pūrvatra ca jagat eka deśa bhūtānām puruṣāṇām viśeṣa upādānāt aviśeṣitam jagat eva iha upādīyate iti gamyate
etat uktam bhavati yaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām jagat eka deśa bhūtānām kartā kim anena viśeṣeṇa
yasya vā kṛtsnam eva jagat aviśeṣitam karma iti vā śabdaḥ eka deśa avacchinna kartṛ tva vyāvṛtti arthaḥ
ye bālākinā brahma tva abhimatāḥ puruṣāḥ kīrtitāḥ teṣām abrahma tva khyāpanāya viśeṣa upādānam
evam brāhmaṇa parivrājaka nyāyena sāmānya viśeṣābhyām jagataḥ kartā veditavya tayā upadiśyate
parameśvaraḥ ca sarva jagataḥ kartā sarva vedānteṣu avadhāritaḥ
jīva mukhya prāṇa liṅgat na iti ced tat vyākhyātam
atha yat uktam vākyaśeṣa gatāt jīva liṅgāt mukhya prāṇa liṅgāt ca tayoḥ eva anyatarasya iha grahaṇam nyāyyam na parameśvarasya iti tat parihartavyam
atrā ucyate parihṛtam ca etat na upāsā traividhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt iti atra
trividham hi atra upāsanam evam sati prasajyeta jīva upāsanam mukhya prāṇa upāsanam brahma upāsanam ca iti
na ca etat nyāyyam
upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām hi brahma viṣaya tvam asya vākyasya avagamyate
tatra upakramasya tāvat brahma viṣaya tvam darśitam
upasaṃhārasya api niratiśaya phala śravaṇāt brahma viṣaya tvam dṛśyate sarvān pāpmanaḥ upahatya sarveṣām ca bhūtānām śraiṣṭhyam svārājyam ādhipatyam paryeti yaḥ evam veda iti
nanu evam sati pratardana vākya nirṇayena evā idam api vākyam nirṇīyeta
na nirṇīyate yasya vā etat karma ityasya brahma viṣaya tvena tatra anirdhārita tvāt
tasmāt atra jīva mukhya prāṇa śaṅkā punar utpadyamānā nivartyate
prāṇa śabdaḥ api brahma viṣayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ prāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ iti atra
jīva liṅgam api upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ brahma viṣaya tvāt abheda abhiprāyeṇa yojayitavyam
anya artham tu jaiminiḥ praśna vyākhyānābhyām api ca evam eke
api ca na eva atra vivaditavyam jīva pradhānam vā idam vākyam syāt brahma pradhānam vā iti
yatas jīva parāmarśam brahma pratipatti artham asmin vākye jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
kasmāt
praśna vyākhyānābhyām
praśnaḥ tāvat suṣupta puruṣa pratibodhanena prāṇa ādi vyatirikte jīve pratibodhite punar jīva vyatirikta viṣayaḥ dṛśyate kva eṣa etat bālāke śayiṣṭa kva vā etat abhūt kutas etat āgāt iti
prativacanam api yadā suptaḥ svapnam na kaṃcana paśyati atha asmin prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati ityādi etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ yathāyatanam vipratiṣṭhante prāṇebhyaḥ devāḥ devebhyaḥ lokāḥ iti ca suṣupti kāle ca pareṇa brahmaṇā jīvaḥ ekatām gacchati
parasmāt ca brahmaṇaḥ prāṇa ādikam jagat jāyate iti vedānta maryādā
tasmāt yatra asya jīvasya niḥsaṃbodha svastha tā rūpaḥ svāpaḥ upādhi janita viśeṣa vijñāna rahitam svarūpam yatas tat bhraṃśa rūpam āgamanam saḥ u tra paramātmā veditavya tayā śrāvitaḥ iti gamyate
api ca evam eke śākhinaḥ vājasaneyinaḥ smin eva bālākya jātaśatru saṃvāde spaṣṭam vijñāna maya śabdena jīvam āmnāya tad vyatiriktam paramātmānam āmananti yaḥ eṣa vijñāna mayaḥ puruṣaḥ kva eṣa tadā abhūt kutas etat āgāt iti praśne
prativacane pi yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete iti
ākāśa śabdaḥ ca paramātmani prayuktaḥ daharaḥ smin antarākāśaḥ iti atra
sarve ete ātmānaḥ vyuccaranti iti ca upādhimatām ātmanām anyatas vyuccaraṇam āmanantaḥ paramātmānam eva kāraṇa tvena āmananti iti gamyate
prāṇa nirākaraṇasya api suṣupta puruṣa utthāpanena prāṇa ādi vyatirikta upadeśaḥ abhyuccayaḥ
vākya anvayāt
vākya anvaya adhikaraṇam
brṛhadāraṇyake maitreyībrāhmaṇe bhidhīyate na vai are patyuḥ kāmāya iti upakramya na vai are sarvasya kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ maitreyi ātmanaḥ vai are darśanena śravaṇena matyā vijñānena idam sarvam viditam iti
tatra etat vicikitsyate kim vijñāna ātmā eva ayam draṣṭavya śrotavya tva ādi rūpeṇa upadiśyate āhosvit paramātmā iti
kutas punar eṣā vicikitsā
priya saṃsūcitena ātmanā bhoktrā upakramāt vijñāna ātma upadeśaḥ iti pratibhāti
tathā ātma vijñānena sarva vijñāna upadeśāt paramātma upadeśaḥ iti
kim tāvat prāptam
vijñāna ātma upadeśaḥ iti
kasmāt
upakrama sāmarthyāt
pati jāyā putra vitta ādikam hi bhogya bhūtam sarvam jagat ātma artha tayā priyam bhavati iti priya saṃsūcitam bhoktāram ātmānam upakramya anantaram idam ātmanaḥ darśana ādi upadiśyamānam kasya anyasya ātmanaḥ syāt
madhye pi idam mahat bhūtam anantam apāram vijñāna ghane eva etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni eva anuvinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti prakṛtasya eva mahataḥ bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ samutthānam vijñāna ātma bhāvena bruvan vijñāna ātmanaḥ eva idam draṣṭavya tvam darśayati
tathā vijñātāram are kena vijānīyāt iti kartṛ vacanena śabdena upasaṃharan vijñāna ātmānam eva iha upadiṣṭam darśayati
tasmāt ātma vijñānena sarva vijñāna vacanam bhoktṛ artha tvāt bhogya jātasya aupacārikam draṣṭavyam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ paramātma upadeśaḥ eva ayam
kasmāt
vākya anvayāt
vākyam hi idam paurvāparyeṇa avekṣyamāṇam paramātmānam pratyanvita avayavam lakṣyate
katham iti tat upapādyate amṛta tvasya tu na āśā asti vittena iti yājñavalkyāt upaśrutya yena aham na amṛtā syām kim aham tena kuryām yat eva bhagavān veda tat eva me brūhi iti amṛta tvam āśāsānāyai maitreyyai yājñavalkyaḥ ātma vijñānam upadiśati
na ca anyatra paramātma vijñānāt amṛta tvam asti iti śruti smṛti vādāḥ vadanti
tathā ca ātma vijñānena sarva vijñānam ucyamānam na anyatra parama kāraṇa vijñānāt mukhyam avakalpate
na ca etat aupacārikam āśrayitum śakyam yatkāraṇam ātma vijñānena sarva vijñānam pratijñāya anantareṇa granthena tat eva upapādayati brahma tam parādāt yaḥ nyatra ātmanaḥ brahma veda ityādinā
yaḥ hi brahma kṣatra ādikam jagat ātmanaḥ nyatra svātantryeṇa labdha sadbhāvam paśyati tam mithyādarśinam tat eva mithyādṛṣṭam brahma kṣatra ādikam jagat parākaroti iti bheda dṛṣṭim apodya idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti sarvasya vastu jātasya ātma avyatirekam avatārayati
dundubhi ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ ca tam eva avyatirekam draḍhayati
asya mahataḥ bhūtasya niḥśvasitam etat yat ṛgvedaḥ ityādinā ca prakṛtasya ātmanaḥ nāma rūpa karma prapañca kāraṇatām vyācakṣāṇaḥ paramātmānam eva enam gamayati
tathā eva ekāyana prakriyāyām api sa viṣayasya sa indriyasya sa antaḥkaraṇasya prapañcasya ekāyanam anantaram abāhyam kṛtsnam prajñāna ghanam vyācakṣāṇaḥ paramātmānam eva enam gamayati
tasmāt paramātmanaḥ eva ayam darśana ādi upadeśaḥ iti gamyate
yat punar uktam priya saṃsūcita upakramāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ eva ayam darśana ādi upadeśaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ
pratijñā siddheḥ liṅgam āśmarathyaḥ
asti atra pratijñā ātmani vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti ca
tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcayati etat liṅgam yat priya saṃsūcitasya ātmanaḥ draṣṭavyā tva ādi saṃkīrtanam
yadi hi vijñāna ātmā paramātmanaḥ nyaḥ syāt tatas paramātma vijñāne vijñāna ātmā na vijñāyate iti eka vijñānena sarva vijñānam yat pratijñātam tat hīyeta
tasmāt pratijñā siddhi artham vijñānātma paramātmanoḥ abheda aṃśena upakramaṇam iti āśmarathyaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
utkramiṣyate evambhāvāt iti auḍulomiḥ
vijñāna ātmanaḥ eva deha indriya manaḥ buddhi saṃghāta upādhi saṃparkāt kaluṣībhūtasya jñāna dhyāna ādi sādhana anuṣṭhānāt saṃprasannasya deha ādi saṃghātāt utkramiṣyataḥ paramātmanā aikya upapatteḥ idam abhedena upakramaṇam iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
śrutiḥ ca evam bhavati eṣa saṃprasādaḥ u smāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti
kvacid ca jīva āśrayam api nāma rūpam nadī nidarśanena jñāpayati yathā nadyaḥ syandamānāḥ samudre nāma rūpe vihāya
tathā vidvān nāma rūpāt vimuktaḥ parāt param puruṣam upaiti divyam iti
yathā loke nadyaḥ sva āśrayam eva nāma rūpam vihāya samudram upayanti evam sva āśrayam eva nāma rūpam vihāya param puruṣam upaiti iti hi tatra arthaḥ pratīyate dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭāntikayoḥ tulya tāyai
avasthiteḥ iti kāśakṛtsnaḥ
asya eva paramātmanaḥ nena api vijñāna ātma bhāvena avasthānāt upapannam idam abhedena upakramaṇam iti kāśakṛtsnaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
tathā ca brāhmaṇam anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti evaṃjātīyakam parasya eva ātmanaḥ jīva bhāvena avasthānam darśayati
mantravarṇaḥ ca sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīraḥ nāmāni kṛtvā abhivadan yat āste
iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ
na ca tejaḥ prabhṛtīnām sṛṣṭau jīvasya pṛthak sṛṣṭiḥ śrutā yena parasmāt ātmanaḥ nyasta dvikāraḥ jīvaḥ syāt
kāśakṛtsnasya ācāryasya avikṛtaḥ parameśvaraḥ jīvaḥ na anyaḥ iti matam
āśmarathyasya tu yadi api jīvasya parasmāt ananya tvam abhipretam tathā api pratijñā siddheḥ iti sāpekṣa tva abhidhānāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kiyān api abhipretaḥ iti gamyate
auḍulomi pakṣe punar spaṣṭam eva avasthā antara apekṣau bheda abhedau gamyete
tatra kāśakṛtsnīyam matam śruti anusāri iti gamyate pratipipādayiṣita artha anusārāt tat tvam asi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
evam ca sati tad jñānāt amṛta tvam avakalpate
vikāra ātmaka tve hi jīvasya abhyupagamyamāne vikārasya prakṛti saṃbandhe pralaya prasaṅgāt na tad jñānāt amṛta tvam avakalpeta
atas ca sva āśrayasya nāma rūpasya asaṃbhavāt upādhi āśrayam nāma rūpam jīve upacaryate
atas eva utpattiḥ api jīvasya kvacid agni visphuliṅga udāharaṇena śrāvyamāṇā upādhi āśrayā eva veditavyā
yat api uktam prakṛtasya eva mahataḥ bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ samutthānam vijñāna ātma bhāvena darśayan vijñāna ātmanaḥ eva idam draṣṭavya tvam darśayati iti tatra api iyam eva tri sūtrī yojayitavyā
pratijñā siddheḥ liṅgam āśmarathyaḥ idam atra pratijñātam ātmani vidite sarvam idam viditam bhavati idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā iti ca
upapāditam ca sarvasya nāma rūpa karma prapañcasya eka prasava tvāt eka pralaya tvāt ca dundubhi ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ a vyatireka pratipādanāt
tasyāḥ eva pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcayati etat liṅgam yat mahataḥ bhūtasya bhūtebhyaḥ samutthānam vijñāna ātma bhāvena kathitam iti āśmarathyaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate abhede hi sati eka vijñānena sarva vijñānam pratijñātam avakalpate iti
utkramiṣyataḥ evaṃbhāvāt iti auḍulomiḥ utkramiṣyataḥ vijñāna ātmanaḥ jñāna dhyāna ādi sāmarthyāt saṃprasannasya pareṇa ātmanā aikya saṃbhavāt idam abheda abhidhānam iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
avasthiteḥ iti kāśakṛtsnaḥ asya eva paramātmanaḥ nena api vijñāna ātma bhāvena avasthānāt upapannam idam abheda abhidhānam iti kāśakṛtsnaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
nanu uccheda abhidhānam etat etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni eva anuvinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti
katham etat abheda abhidhānam
na eṣa doṣaḥ
viśeṣa vijñāna vināśa abhiprāyam etat vināśa abhidhānam na ātma uccheda abhiprāyam
atra eva mā bhagavān amūmuhat na pretya saṃjñā asti iti paryanuyujya svayam eva śrutyā artha antarasya darśita tvāt na vai are ham moham bravīmi avināśī vai are yam ātmā an ucchitti dharmā mātrā saṃsargaḥ tu asya bhavati iti
etat uktam bhavati kūṭastha nityaḥ eva ayam vijñāna ghanaḥ ātmā
na asya uccheda prasaṅgaḥ sti
mātrābhiḥ tu asya bhūta indriya lakṣaṇābhiḥ avidyā kṛtābhiḥ a saṃsargaḥ vidyayā bhavati
saṃsarga abhāve ca tad kṛtasya viśeṣa vijñānasya abhāvāt na pretya saṃjñā asti iti uktam iti
yat api uktam vijñātāram are kena vijānīyāt iti kartṛ vacanena śabdena upasaṃhārāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ eva idam draṣṭavyam iti tat api kāśakṛtsnīyena eva darśanena pariharaṇīyam
api ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati iti ārabhya avidyā viṣaye tasya eva darśana ādi lakṣaṇam viśeṣa vijñānam prapañcya yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet ityādinā vidyā viṣaye tasya eva darśana ādi lakṣaṇasya viśeṣa vijñānasya abhāvam abhidadhāti
punar ca viṣaya abhāve pi ātmānam vijānīyāt iti āśaṅkya vijñātāram are kena vijānīyāt iti āha
tatas ca viśeṣa vijñāna abhāva upapādana para tvāt vākyasya vijñāna dhātuḥ eva kevalaḥ san bhūta pūrva gatyā kartṛ vacanena tṛcāḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ iti gamyate
darśitam tu purastāt kāśakṛtsnīyasya pakṣasya śrutimat tvam
atas ca vijñāna ātma paramātmanoḥ avidyā pratyupasthāpita nāma rūpa racita deha ādi upādhi nimittaḥ bhedaḥ na pāramārthikaḥ iti eṣaḥ rthaḥ sarvaiḥ vedānta vādibhiḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam ātmā eva idam sarvam brahmā eva idam sarvam idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā na anyaḥ atas sti draṣṭā na anyat atas sti draṣṭṛ iti evaṃrūpābhyaḥ śrutibhyaḥ
smṛtibhyaḥ ca vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi sarva kṣetreṣu bhārata samam sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantam parameśvaram iti evaṃrūpābhyaḥ
bheda darśana apavādāt ca anyaḥ sau anyaḥ ham asmi iti na sa veda yathā paśuḥ mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti evaṃjātīyakāt
sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ bhayaḥ brahma iti ca ātmani sarva vikriyā pratiṣedhāt
anyathā ca mumukṣūṇām nirapavāda vijñāna anupapatteḥ su niścita artha tva anupapatteḥ ca
nirapavādam hi vijñānam sarva ākāṅkṣā nivartakam ātma viṣayam iṣyate vedānta vijñāna su niścita arthāḥ
iti ca śruteḥ
tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam anupaśyataḥ iti ca
sthita prajña lakṣaṇa smṛteḥ ca
sthite ca kṣetrajña param ātma eka tva viṣaye samyak darśane kṣetrajñaḥ paramātmā iti nāma mātra bhedāt kṣetrajñaḥ yam paramātmanaḥ bhinnaḥ paramātmā ayam kṣetrajñāt bhinnaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ ātma bheda viṣayaḥ yam nirbandhaḥ nirarthakaḥ ekaḥ hi ayam ātmā nāma mātra bhedena bahudhā abhidhīyate iti
na hi satyam jñānam anantam brahma
yaḥ veda nihitam guhāyām iti kāṃcid eva ekām guhām adhikṛtya etat uktam
na ca brahmaṇaḥ nyaḥ guhāyām nihitaḥ sti tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva anuprāviśat iti sraṣṭuḥ eva praveśa śravaṇāt
ye tu nirbandham kurvanti te vedānta artham bādhamānāḥ śreyaḥ uddhāram samyak darśanam eva bādhante
kṛtakam anityam ca mokṣam kalpayanti
nyāyena ca na saṃgacchante iti
prakṛtiḥ ca pratijñā dṛṣṭānta an uparodhāt
prakṛti adhikaraṇam
yathā abhyudaya hetu tvāt dharmaḥ jijñāsyaḥ evam niḥśreyasa hetu tvāt brahma api jijñāsyam iti uktam
brahma ca janmādyasya yatas iti lakṣitam
tat ca lakṣaṇam ghaṭa rucaka ādīnām mṛd suvarṇa ādi vat prakṛti tve kulāla suvarṇakāra ādi vat nimitta tve ca samānam iti atas bhavati vimarśaḥ kimātmakam punar brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇatvam syāt iti
tatra nimitta kāraṇam eva tāvat kevalam syāt iti pratibhāti
kasmāt
īkṣā pūrvaka kartṛ tva śravaṇāt īkṣā pūrvakam hi brahmaṇaḥ kartṛ tvam avagamyate saḥ īkṣāṃcakre sa prāṇam asṛjata ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
īkṣā pūrvakam ca kartṛ tvam nimitta kāraṇeṣu eva kulāla ādiṣu dṛṣṭam
aneka kāraka pūrvikā ca kriyā phala siddhiḥ loke dṛṣṭā
sa ca nyāyaḥ ādi kartari api yuktaḥ saṃkramayitum
īśvara tva prasiddheḥ ca īśvarāṇām hi rāja vaivasvata ādīnām nimitta kāraṇa tvam eva kevalam pratīyate
tadvat parameśvarasya api nimitta kāraṇa tvam eva yuktam pratipattum
kāryam ca idam jagat sa avayavam acetanam aśuddham ca dṛśyate kāraṇena api tasya tādṛśena eva bhavitavyam kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya darśanāt
brahma ca an evaṃlakṣaṇam avagamyate niṣkalam niṣkriyam śāntam niravadyam nirañjanam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
pāriśeṣyāt brahmaṇaḥ nyat upādānakāraṇam aśuddhi ādi guṇakam smṛti prasiddham abhyupagantavyam brahma kāraṇatva śruteḥ nimitta tva mātre paryavasānāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ prakṛtiḥ ca upādānakāraṇam ca brahma abhyupagantavyam nimitta kāraṇam ca
na kevalam nimitta kāraṇam eva
kasmāt
pratijñā dṛṣṭānta an uparodhāt
evam hi pratijñā dṛṣṭāntau śrautau na upurudhyete
pratijñā tāvat uta tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ yena a śrutam śrutam bhavati a matam matam a vijñātam vijñātam iti
tatra ca ekena vijñātena sarvam anyat avijñātam api vijñātam bhavati iti pratīyate
tat ca upādāna kāraṇa vijñāne sarva vijñānam saṃbhavati upādāna kāraṇa avyatirekāt kāryasya
nimitta kāraṇa a vyatirekaḥ tu kāryasya na asti loke takṣṇaḥ prāsāda vyatireka darśanāt
dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā somya ekena mṛd piṇḍena sarvam mṛd mayam vijñātam syāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti upādāna kāraṇa gocaraḥ eva āmnāyate
tathā ekena loha maṇinā sarvam loha mayam vijñātam syāt ekena nakha nikṛntanena sarvam kārṣṇāyasam vijñātam syāt iti ca
tathā anyatra api kasmin nu bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti pratijñā
yathā pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavanti iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ
tathā ātmani khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idam sarvam viditam iti pratijñā
sa yathā dundubheḥ hanyamānasya na bāhyān śabdān śaknuyāt grahaṇāya dundubheḥ tu grahaṇena dundubhi āghātasya vā śabdaḥ gṛhītaḥ iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ
evam yathāsaṃbhavam prati vedāntam pratijñā dṛṣṭāntau prakṛti tva sādhanau pratyetavyau
yatas iti iyam api pañcamī yatas vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti atra jani kartuḥ prakṛtiḥ iti viśeṣa smaraṇāt prakṛti lakṣaṇe eva apādāne draṣṭavyā
nimitta tvam tu adhiṣṭhātṛ antara abhāvāt adhigantavyam
yathā hi loke mṛd suvarṇa ādikam upādānakāraṇam kulāla suvarṇakāra ādīn adhiṣṭhātṛn apekṣya pravartate na evam brahmaṇaḥ upādānakāraṇasya sataḥ nyaḥ dhiṣṭhātā apekṣyaḥ sti prāk utpatteḥ ekam eva advitīyam iti avadhāraṇāt
adhiṣṭhātṛ antara abhāvaḥ veditavyaḥ adhiṣṭhātari hi upādānāt anyasmin abhyupagamyamāne punar api eka vijñānena sarva vijñānasya asaṃbhavāt pratijñā dṛṣṭānta uparodhaḥ eva syāt
tasmāt adhiṣṭhātṛ antara abhāvāt ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam upādāna antara abhāvāt ca prakṛti tvam
kutas ca ātmanaḥ kartṛ tva prakṛti tve
abhidhyā upadeśāt ca
abhidhyā upadeśaḥ ca ātmanaḥ kartṛ tva prakṛti tve gamayati saḥ kāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti ca
tatra abhidhyāna pūrvikāyāḥ svātantrya pravṛtteḥ kartā iti gamyate
bahu syām iti pratyagātma viṣaya tvāt bahu bhavana abhidhyānasya prakṛtiḥ iti api gamyate
sākṣāt ca ubhaya āmnānāt
prakṛti tvasya ayam abhyuccayaḥ
itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yatkāraṇam sākṣāt brahma eva kāraṇam upādāya ubhau prabhava pralayau āmnāyete sarvāṇi ha vai imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante
ākāśam pratyastam yanti iti
yat hi yasmāt prabhavati yasmin ca pralīyate tat tasya upādānam prasiddham yathā vrīhi yava ādīnām pṛthivī
sākṣāt iti ca upādāna antara anupādānam sūcayati ākāśāt eva iti
pratyastamayaḥ ca na upādānāt anyatra kāryasya dṛṣṭaḥ
ātma kṛteḥ pariṇāmāt
itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yatkāraṇam brahma prakriyāyām tadā ātmānam svayam akuruta iti ātmanaḥ karma tvam kartṛ tvam ca darśayati ātmānam iti karma tvam svayam akuruta iti kartṛ tvam
katham punar pūrva siddhasya sataḥ kartṛ tvena vyavasthitasya kriyamāṇa tvam śakyam saṃpādayitum
pariṇāmāt iti brūmaḥ pūrva siddhaḥ api hi sanna ātmā viśeṣeṇa vikāra ātmanā pariṇamayāmāsa ātmānam iti
vikāra ātmanā ca pariṇāmaḥ mṛd ādyāsu prakṛtiṣu upalabdhaḥ
svayam iti ca viśeṣaṇāt nimitta antara anapekṣa tvam api pratīyate
pariṇāmāt iti vā pṛthak sūtram
tasya eṣaḥ rthaḥ itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yatkāraṇam brahmaṇaḥ eva vikāra ātmanā ca pariṇāmaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena āmnāyate sat ca tyad ca abhavat niruktam ca aniruktam ca ityādinā iti
yoniḥ ca hi gīyate
itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yatkāraṇam brahma yoniḥ iti api paṭhyate vedānteṣu kartāram īśam puruṣam brahma yonim iti yat bhūtayonim paripaśyanti dhīrāḥ iti ca
yoni śabdaḥ ca prakṛti vacanaḥ samadhigataḥ loke pṛthivī yoniḥ oṣadhi vanaspatīnām iti
strī yoneḥ api asti eva avayava dvāreṇa garbham prati upādāna kāraṇa tvam
kvacid sthāna vacanā u pi yoni śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ indra niṣade akāri iti
vākyaśeṣāt tu atra prakṛti vacana tā parigṛhyate yathā ūrṇanābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate ca iti evaṃjātīyakāt
tat evam prakṛti tvam brahmaṇaḥ prasiddham
yat punar idam uktam īkṣā pūrvakam kartṛ tvam nimitta kāraṇeṣu eva kulāla ādiṣu loke dṛṣṭam na upādāneṣu ityādi tat pratyucyate na loka vat iha bhavitavyam
na hi ayam anumāna gamyaḥ rthaḥ
śabda gamya tvāt tu asya arthasya yathāśabdam iha bhavitavyam
śabdaḥ ca īkṣituḥ īśvarasya prakṛti tvam pratipādayati iti avocāma
punar ca etat sarvam vistareṇa prativakṣyāmaḥ
etena sarve vyākhyātāḥ vyākhyātāḥ
sarva vyākhyāna adhikaraṇam
īkṣateḥ na a śabdam iti ārabhya pradhāna kāraṇa vādaḥ sūtraiḥ eva punar punar āśaṅkya nirākṛtaḥ tasya hi pakṣasya upodbalakāni kānicid liṅga ābhāsāni vedānteṣu āpātena manda matīn prati bhānti iti
sa ca kārya kāraṇa ananyatva abhyupagamāt pratyāsannaḥ vedānta vādasya devala prabhṛtibhiḥ ca kaiścid dharmasūtra kāraiḥ sva grantheṣu āśritaḥ tena tad pratiṣedhe eva tīva kṛtaḥ na aṇu ādi kāraṇa vāda pratiṣedhe
te pi tu brahma kāraṇa vāda pakṣasya pratipakṣa tvāt pratiṣeddhavyāḥ
teṣām api upodbalakam vaidikam kiṃcid liṅgam āpātena manda matīn prati bhāyāt iti atas pradhāna malla nibarhaṇa nyāyena atidiśati etena pradhāna kāraṇa vāda pratiṣedha nyāya kalāpena sarve ṇu ādi kāraṇa vādāḥ api pratiṣiddha tayā vyākhyātāḥ veditavyāḥ teṣām api pradhāna vat aśabda tvāt śabda virodhi tvāt ca iti
vyākhyātāḥ vyākhyātāḥ iti pada abhyāsaḥ dhyāya parisamāptim dyotayati
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye prathamaḥ dhyāyaḥ

tāsu hi acetanam pradhānam svatantram jagataḥ kāraṇam upanibadhyate

tathā puruṣa arthān catur varṇa āśrama dharmān nānāvidhān vidadhati

tathā idam api jagat acetanam sukha dukha moha anvitam sat acetanasya eva sukha duḥkha moha ātmakasya kāraṇasya kāryam bhavitum arhati na vilakṣaṇasya brahmaṇaḥ
brahma vilakṣaṇa tvam ca asya jagataḥ śuddhi acetana tva darśanāt avagantavyam aśuddham hi idam jagat sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tayā pratīyate prīti paritāpa viṣāda ādi hetutvāt svarga naraka ādi uccāvaca prapañca tvāt ca
acetanam ca idam jagat cetanam prati kārya kāraṇa bhāvena upakaraṇa bhāva upagamāt
na hi sāmye sati upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ bhavati
na hi pradīpau parasparasya upakurutaḥ
nanu cetanam api kārya kāraṇam svāmi bhṛtya nyāyena bhoktuḥ upakariṣyati
na svāmi bhṛtyayoḥ api acetana aṃśasya eva cetanam pratyupakāraka tvāt
yaḥ hi ekasya cetanasya parigrahaḥ buddhi ādiḥ acetana bhāgaḥ saḥ eva anyasya cetanasya upakaroti na tu svayam eva cetanaḥ cetanā antarasya upakaroti apakaroti vā
niratiśayāḥ hi akartāraḥ cetanāḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ manyante
tasmāt acetanam kāryakāraṇam
na ca kāṣṭha loṣṭa ādīnām cetana tve kiṃcid pramāṇam asti
prasiddhaḥ ca ayam cetana acetana vibhāgaḥ loke
tasmāt brahma vilakṣaṇa tvāt na idam jagat tad prakṛtikam
yaḥ pi kaścid ācakṣīta śrutyā jagataḥ cetana prakṛtikatām tad balena eva samastam jagat cetanam avagamiṣyāmi prakṛti rūpasya vikāre nvaya darśanāt
avibhāvanam tu caitanyasya pariṇāma viśeṣāt bhaviṣyati
yathā spaṣṭa caitanyānām api ātmanām svāpa mūrchā ādi avasthāsu caitanyam na vibhāvyate evam kāṣṭha loṣṭa ādīnām api caitanyam na vibhāvayiṣyate
etasmāt eva ca vibhāvita tva a vibhāvita tva kṛtāt viśeṣāt rūpa ādi bhāva abhāvābhyām ca kārya kāraṇānām ātmanām ca cetana tva aviśeṣe guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ na virotsyate
yathā ca pārthiva tva aviśeṣe māṃsa sūpa odana ādīnām pratyātma vartinaḥ viśeṣāt paraspara upakāri tvam bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati
pravibhāga prasiddhiḥ api atas eva na virotsyate iti tena api kathaṃcid cetana tva acetana tva lakṣaṇam vilakṣaṇa tvam parihriyeta
śuddhi aśuddhi tva lakṣaṇam tu vilakṣaṇa tvam nā eva parihriyate
na ca itarat api vilakṣaṇa tvam parihartum śakyate iti āha tathātvam ca śabdāt iti
an avagamyamānam eva hi idam loke samastasya vastunaḥ cetana tvam cetana prakṛtika tva śravaṇāt śabda śaraṇa tayā kevalayā utprekṣeta
tat ca śabdena eva virudhyate yatas śabdāt api tathātvam avagamyate
tathātvam iti prakṛti vilakṣaṇa tvam kathayati
śabdaḥ eva vijñānam ca a vijñānam ca iti kasyacid vibhāgasya acetana tām śrāvayan cetanāt brahmaṇaḥ vilakṣaṇam acetanam jagat śrāvayati
nanu cetanatvam api kvacid acetana tva abhimatānām bhūta indriyāṇām śrūyate yathā mṛd abravīt āpaḥ bruvan iti tat tejaḥ aikṣata tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣanta iti ca evamādyā bhūta viṣayā cetana tva śrutiḥ
indriya viṣayāḥ api te ha ime prāṇāḥ ahaṃśreyase vivadamānāḥ brahma jagmuḥ iti te ha vācam ūcuḥ tvam naḥ udgāya iti iti evamādyā indriya viṣayā iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
abhimāni vyapadeśaḥ tu viśeṣa anugatibhyām
tu śabdaḥ āśaṅkām apanudati
na khalu mṛd abravīt iti evaṃjātīyakayā śrutyā bhūta indriyāṇām cetana tvam āśaṅkanīyam yatas bhimāni vyapadeśaḥ eṣaḥ
mṛd ādi abhimāninyaḥ vāc ādi abhimāninyaḥ ca cetanā devatāḥ vadana saṃvadana ādiṣu cetanā uciteṣu vyavahāreṣu vyapadiśyante na bhūta indriya mātram
kasmāt
viśeṣa anugatibhyām viśeṣaḥ hi bhoktṛṇām bhūta indriyāṇām ca cetana acetana pravibhāga lakṣaṇaḥ prāk abhihitaḥ
sarva cetana tāyām ca asau na upapadyeta
api ca kauṣītakinaḥ prāṇa saṃvāde karaṇa mātra āśaṅkā vinivṛttaye dhiṣṭhātṛ cetana parigrahāya devatā śabdena viśiṣanti etāḥ ha vai devatāḥ ahaṃśreyase vivadamānāḥ iti tāḥ vai etāḥ sarvāḥ devatāḥ prāṇe niḥśreyasam viditvā iti ca
anugatāḥ ca sarvatra abhimāninyaḥ cetanāḥ devatāḥ mantra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa ādibhyaḥ vagamyante agniḥ vāc bhūtvā mukham prāviśat iti evamādikā ca śrutiḥ karaṇeṣu anugrāhikām devatām anugatām darśayati
prāṇa saṃvāda vākya śeṣe ca te ha prāṇāḥ prajāpatim pitaram etya ūcuḥ iti śreṣṭha tva nirdhāraṇāya prajāpati gamanam tad vacanāt ca ekaika utkramaṇena anvaya vyatirekābhyām prāṇa śraiṣṭhya pratipattiḥ tasmai bali haraṇam iti ca evaṃjātīyakaḥ smat ādiṣu iva vyavahāraḥ nugamyamānaḥ bhimāni vyapadeśam draḍhayati
tat tejaḥ aikṣata iti api parasyāḥ eva devatāyāḥ adhiṣṭhātryāḥ sva vikāreṣu anugatāyāḥ iyam īkṣā vyapadiśyate iti draṣṭavyam
tasmāt vilakṣaṇam eva idam brahmaṇaḥ jagat
vilakṣaṇa tvāt ca na brahma prakṛtikam iti ākṣipte pratividhatte
dṛśyate tu
tu śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati
yat uktam vilakṣaṇa tvāt na idam jagat brahma prakṛtikam iti na ayam ekāntaḥ
dṛśyate hi loke cetana tvena prasiddhebhyaḥ puruṣa ādibhyaḥ vilakṣaṇānām keśa nakha ādīnām utpattiḥ acetana tvena ca prasiddhebhyaḥ gomaya ādibhyaḥ vṛścika ādīnām
nanu acetanāni eva puruṣa ādi śarīrāṇi acetanānām keśa nakha ādīnām kāraṇāni acetanāni eva ca vṛścika ādi śarīrāṇi acetanānām gomaya ādīnām kāryāṇi iti
ucyate evam api kiṃcid acetanam cetanasya āyatana bhāvam upagacchati kiṃcid na iti asti eva vailakṣaṇyam
mahān ca ayam pāriṇāmikaḥ svabhāva viprakarṣaḥ puruṣa ādīnām keśa nakha ādīnām ca rūpa ādi bhedāt tathā gomaya ādīnām vṛścika ādīnām ca
atyanta sārūpye ca prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ eva pralīyeta
atha ucyeta asti kaścid pārthiva tva ādi svabhāvaḥ puruṣa ādīnām keśa nakha ādiṣu anuvartamānaḥ gomaya ādīnām ca vṛścika ādiṣu iti
brahmaṇaḥ pi tarhi sattā lakṣaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ ākāśa ādiṣu anuvartamānaḥ dṛśyate
vilakṣaṇa tvena ca kāraṇena brahma prakṛtika tvam jagataḥ dūṣayatā kim aśeṣasya brahma svabhāvasya ananuvartanam vilakṣaṇa tvam abhipreyate uta yasya kasyacid
atha caitanyasya iti vaktavyam

na hi asati atiśaye prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ iti bhavati
dvitīye ca asiddha tvam
dṛśyate hi sattā lakṣaṇaḥ brahma svabhāvaḥ ākāśa ādiṣu anuvartamānaḥ iti uktam
tṛtīye tu dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ
kim hi yat caitanyena ananvitam tat abrahma prakṛtikam dṛṣṭam iti brahma kāraṇa vādinam pratyudāhriyeta samastasya asya vastu jātasya brahma prakṛtika tva abhyupagamāt
āgama virodhaḥ tu prasiddhaḥ eva cetanam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti āgama tātparyasya prasādhita tvāt
yat tu uktam pariniṣpanna tvāt brahmaṇi pramāṇa antarāṇi saṃbhaveyuḥ iti tat api manoratha mātram
rūpa ādi abhāvāt hi na ayam arthaḥ pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ
liṅga ādi abhāvāt ca na anumāna ādīnām
āgama mātra samadhigamyaḥ eva tu ayam arthaḥ dharma vat
tathā ca śrutiḥ na eṣā tarkeṇa matiḥ āpaneyā proktā anyena eva su jñānāya preṣṭhaḥ iti
kaḥ addhā veda kaḥ iha pravocat iyam visṛṣṭiḥ yatas ābabhūva iti ca ete ṛcau nija siddhānām api īśvarāṇām durbodhatām jagat kāraṇasya darśayataḥ
smṛtiḥ api bhavati acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ na tān tarkeṇa yojayet iti avyaktaḥ yam acintyaḥ yam avikāryaḥ yam ucyate iti ca na me viduḥ sura gaṇāḥ prabhavam na mahā ṛṣayaḥ
aham ādiḥ hi devānām mahā ṛṣīṇām ca sarvaśas iti ca evaṃjātīyakā
yat api śravaṇa vyatirekeṇa mananam vidadhat śabdaḥ eva tarkam api ādartavyam darśayati iti uktam na anena miṣeṇa śuṣka tarkasya atra ātmalābhaḥ saṃbhavati
śruti anugṛhītaḥ eva hi atra tarkaḥ nubhava aṅgatvena āśrīyate svapnānta buddhāntayoḥ ubhayoḥ itaretara vyabhicārāt ātmanaḥ nanu āgata tvam saṃprasāde ca prapañca parityāgena sat ātmanā saṃpatteḥ niṣprapañca sat ātmaka tvam prapañcasya brahma prabhava tvāt kārya kāraṇa ananyatva nyāyena brahma avyatirekaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ
tarka apratiṣṭhānāt iti ca kevalasya tarkasya vipralambhaka tvam darśayiṣyati
yaḥ u pi cetana kāraṇa śravaṇa balena eva samastasya jagataḥ cetana tām utprekṣeta tasya api vijñānam ca a vijñānam ca iti cetana acetana vibhāga śravaṇam vibhāvanā a vibhāvanābhyām caitanyasya śakyate eva yojayitum
parasya eva tu idam api vibhāga śravaṇam na yujyate
katham
parama kāraṇasya hi atra samasta jagat ātmanā samavasthānam śrāvyate vijñānam ca a vijñānam ca abhavat iti
tatra yathā cetanasya acetana bhāvaḥ nā upapadyate vilakṣaṇa tvāt evam acetanasya api cetana bhāvaḥ nā upapadyate
pratyukta tvāt tu vilakṣaṇa tvasya yathā śrutyā eva cetanam kāraṇam grahītavyam bhavati
asat iti ced na pratiṣedha mātra tvāt
yadi cetanam śuddham śabda ādi hīnam ca brahma tad viparītasya acetanasya aśuddhasya śabda ādimataḥ ca kāryasya kāraṇam iṣyeta asat tarhi kāryam prāk utpatteḥ iti prasajyeta
aniṣṭam ca etat satkārya vādinaḥ tava iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ pratiṣedha mātra tvāt
pratiṣedha mātram hi idam
na asya pratiṣedhasya pratiṣedhyam asti
na hi ayam pratiṣedhaḥ prāk utpatteḥ sattvam kāryasya pratiṣeddhum śaknoti
katham
yathā eva hi idānīm api idam kāryam kāraṇa ātmanā sat evam prāk utpatteḥ api iti gamyate
na hi idānīm api idam kāryam kāraṇa ātmānam antareṇa svatantram eva asti sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ nyatra ātmanaḥ sarvam veda ityādi śravaṇāt
kāraṇa ātmanā tu sattvam kāryasya prāc utpatteḥ aviśiṣṭam
nanu śabda ādi hīnam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam bāḍham na tu śabda ādimat kāryam kāraṇa ātmanā hīnam prāk utpatteḥ idānīm vā asti
tena na śakyate vaktum prāk utpatteḥ asatkāryam iti
vistareṇa ca etat kārya kāraṇa ananyatva vāde vakṣyāmaḥ
apītau tadvat prasaṅgāt asamañjasam
atra āha yadi sthaulya sāvayavat tva acetana tva paricchinna tva aśuddhi ādi dharmakam kāryam brahma kāraṇakam abhyupagamyeta tadā api itau pralaye pratisaṃsṛjyamānam kāryam kāraṇa avibhāgam āpadyamānam kāraṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa dūṣayet iti api itau kāraṇasya api brahmaṇaḥ kāryasya iva aśuddhi ādi rūpatā prasaṅgāt sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam iti asamañjasam idam aupaniṣadam darśanam
api ca samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ punar utpattau niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt bhoktṛ bhogya ādi vibhāgena utpattiḥ na prāpnoti iti asamañjasam
api ca bhoktṛṇām pareṇa brahmaṇā avibhāgam gatānām karma ādi nimitta pralaye pi punarutpattau abhyupagamyamānāyām muktānām api punarutpatti prasaṅgāt asamañjasam
atha idam jagat apītau api vibhaktam eva pareṇa brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta evam api apītiḥ ca na saṃbhavati kāraṇa a vyatiriktam ca kāryam na saṃbhavati iti asamañjasam eva iti
atrā ucyate
na tu dṛṣṭānta bhāvāt
na eva asmadīye darśane kiṃcid asāmañjasyam asti
yat tāvat abhihitam kāraṇam api gacchat kāryam kāraṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa dūṣayet iti na tat dūṣaṇam
kasmāt
dṛṣṭānta bhāvāt santi hi dṛṣṭāntāḥ yathā kāraṇam apigacchat kāryam kāraṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa na dūṣayati
tat yathā śarāva ādayaḥ mṛd prakṛtikāḥ vikārāḥ vibhāga avasthāyām uccāvaca madhyama prabhedāḥ santaḥ punar prakṛtim apigacchantaḥ na tām ātmīyena dharmeṇa saṃsṛjanti
rucaka ādayaḥ ca suvarṇa vikārāḥ apītau na punar suvarṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa saṃsṛjanti
pṛthivī vikāraḥ caturvidhaḥ bhūta grāmaḥ na pṛthivīm api itau ātmīyena dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati
tvad pakṣasya tu na kaścid dṛṣṭāntaḥ sti
apītiḥ eva hi na saṃbhavet yadi kāraṇe kāryam svadharmeṇa eva avatiṣṭheta
ananya tve pi kārya kāraṇayoḥ kāryasya kāraṇa ātmatvam na tu kāraṇasya kārya ātmatvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti atra vakṣyāmaḥ
ati alpam ca idam ucyate kāryam apītau ātmīyena dharmeṇa kāraṇam saṃsṛjet iti
sthitau api hi samānaḥ yam prasaṅgaḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ ananyatva abhyupagamāt
idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā ātmā eva idam sarvam brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt sarvam khalu idam brahma iti evamādyābhiḥ hi śrutibhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa triṣu api kāleṣu kāryasya kāraṇāt ananya tvam śrāvyate
tatra yaḥ parihāraḥ kāryasya tad dharmāṇām ca avidyā adhyāropita tvāt na taiḥ kāraṇam saṃsṛjyate iti api itau api sa samānaḥ
asti ca ayam aparaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā svayam prasāritayā māyayā māyāvī triṣu api kāleṣu na saṃspṛśyate avastu tvāt evam paramātmā api saṃsāra māyayā na saṃspṛśyate iti
yathā ca svapna dṛś ekaḥ svapna darśana māyayā na saṃspṛśyate prabodha saṃprasādayoḥ an anvāgata tvāt evam avasthā traya sākṣī ekaḥ vyabhicārī avasthā trayeṇa vyabhicāriṇā na saṃspṛśyate
māyā mātram hi etat yat paramātmanaḥ vasthā traya ātmanā avabhāsanam rajjvā iva sarpa ādi bhāvena iti
atra uktam vedānta artha saṃpradāya vidbhiḥ ācāryaiḥ anādi māyayā suptaḥ yadā jīvaḥ prabudhyate
ajam anidram asvapnam advaitam budhyate tadā iti
tatra yat uktam apītau kāraṇasya api kāryasya iva sthaulya ādi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti etat ayuktam
yat punar etat uktam samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ punar vibhāgena utpattau niyama kāraṇam na upapadyate iti ayam api adoṣaḥ dṛṣṭānta bhāvāt eva yathā hi suṣupti samādhi ādau api satyām svābhāvikyām avibhāga prāptau mithyājñānasya anapodita tvāt pūrvavat punar prabodhe vibhāgaḥ bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati
śrutiḥ ca atra bhavati imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ sati saṃpadya na viduḥ sati saṃpadyāmahe iti te iha vyāghraḥ vā siṃhaḥ vā vṛkaḥ vā varāhaḥ vā kīṭaḥ vā pataṅgaḥ vā daṃśaḥ vā maśakaḥ vā yat yat bhavanti tadā bhavanti iti
yathā hi avibhāge pi paramātmani mithyājñāna pratibaddhaḥ vibhāga vyavahāraḥ svapna vat avyāhataḥ sthitau dṛśyate evam apītau api mithyājñāna pratibaddhā eva vibhāga śaktiḥ anumāsyate
etena muktānām punarutpatti prasaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ samyak jñānena mithyājñānasya apodita tvāt
yaḥ punar ayam ante paraḥ vikalpaḥ utprekṣitaḥ atha idam jagat apītau api vibhaktam eva pareṇa brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta iti saḥ u pi anabhyupagamāt eva pratiṣiddhaḥ
tasmāt samañjasam idam aupaniṣadam darśanam
sva pakṣa doṣāt ca
sva pakṣe ca ete prativādinaḥ sādhāraṇāḥ doṣāḥ prāduḥṣyuḥ
katham iti ucyate yat tāvat abhihitam vilakṣaṇa tvāt na idam jagat brahma prakṛtikam iti pradhāna prakṛtikatāyām api samānam etat śabda ādi hīnāt pradhānāt śabda ādimataḥ jagataḥ utpatti abhyupagamāt
atas eva ca vilakṣaṇa kārya utpatti abhyupagamāt samānaḥ prāk utpatteḥ asatkārya vāda prasaṅgaḥ
tathā api ītau kāryasya kāraṇa avibhāga abhyupagamāt tadvat prasaṅgaḥ pi samānaḥ
tathā mṛdita sarva viśeṣeṣu vikāreṣu apītau avibhāga ātma tām gateṣu idam asya puruṣasya upādānam idam asya iti prāk pralayāt pratipuruṣam ye niyatāḥ bhedāḥ na te tathā eva punarutpattau niyantum śakyante kāraṇa abhāvāt
vinā eva ca kāraṇena niyame bhyupagamyamāne kāraṇa abhāva sāmyāt muktānām api punar bandha prasaṅgaḥ
atha kecid bhedāḥ api itau avibhāgam āpadyante kecid na iti ced ye na āpadyante teṣām pradhāna kārya tvam na prāpnoti iti evam ete doṣāḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt na anyatarasmin pakṣe codayitavyāḥ bhavanti iti adoṣa tām eva eṣām draḍhayati avaśya āśrayitavya tvāt
tarka apratiṣṭhānāt api anyathā numeyam iti ced evam api avimokṣa prasaṅgaḥ
itas ca na āgama gamye rthe kevalena tarkeṇa pratyavasthātavyam
yasmāt nirāgamāḥ puruṣa utprekṣā mātra nibandhanāḥ tarkāḥ apratiṣṭhitāḥ bhavanti utprekṣāyāḥ niraṅkuśa tvāt
tathā hi kaiḥ cit abhiyuktaiḥ yatnena utprekṣitāḥ tarkāḥ abhiyuktataraiḥ anyaiḥ ābhāsyamānāḥ dṛśyante
taiḥ api utprekṣitāḥ santaḥ tatas nyaiḥ ābhāsyante iti na pratiṣṭhita tvam tarkāṇām śakyam āśrayitum puruṣam ati vairūpyāt
atha kasyacid prasiddha māhātmyasya kapilasya anyasya vā saṃmataḥ tarkaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti āśrīyeta evam api apratiṣṭhita tvam eva prasiddha māhātmya abhimatānām api tīrthakarāṇām kapila kaṇabhuj prabhṛtīnām paraspara vipratipatti darśanāt
atha ucyeta anyathā vayam anumāsyāmahe yathā na a pratiṣṭhā doṣaḥ bhaviṣyati
na hi pratiṣṭhitaḥ tarkaḥ eva na asti iti śakyate vaktum
etat api hi tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tvam tarkeṇa eva pratiṣṭhāpyate keṣāṃcid tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tva darśanena anyeṣām api tad jātīyakānām tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tva kalpanāt
sarva tarka apratiṣṭhāyām ca lokavyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgaḥ
atīta vartamāna adhva sāmyena hi anāgate pi adhvani sukha duḥkha prāpti parihārāya pravartamānaḥ lokaḥ dṛśyate
śruti artha vipratipattau ca artha ābhāsa nirākaraṇena samyak artha nirdhāraṇam tarkeṇa eva vākya vṛtti nirūpaṇa rūpeṇa kriyate
manuḥ api ca evam eva manyate pratyakṣam anumānam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam
trayam su viditam kāryam dharma śuddhim abhīpsatā iti
ārṣam dharma upadeśam ca veda śāstra avirodhinā

bruvan
ayam eva ca tarkasya alaṃkāraḥ yat apratiṣṭhita tvam nāma
evam hi sāvadya tarka parityāgena niravadyaḥ tarkaḥ pratipattavyaḥ bhavati
na hi pūrvajaḥ mūḍhaḥ āsīt iti ātmanā api mūḍhena bhavitavyam iti kiṃcid asti pramāṇam
tasmāt na tarka apratiṣṭhānam doṣaḥ iti ced evam api avimokṣa prasaṅgaḥ
yadi api kvacid viṣaye tarkasya pratiṣṭhita tvam upalakṣyate tathā api prakṛte tāvat viṣaye prasajyate eva apratiṣṭhita tva doṣāt anirmokṣaḥ tarkasya
na hi idam ati gambhīram bhāva yāthātmyam mukti nibandhanam āgamam antareṇa utprekṣitum api śakyam
rūpa ādi abhāvāt hi na ayam arthaḥ pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ liṅga ādi abhāvāt ca na anumāna ādīnām iti ca avocāma
api ca samyak jñānāt mokṣaḥ iti sarveṣām mokṣa vādinām abhyupagamaḥ
tat ca samyak jñānam eka rūpam vastu tantra tvāt
eka rūpeṇa hi avasthitaḥ yaḥ rthaḥ sa paramārthaḥ
loke tad viṣayam jñānam samyak jñānam iti ucyate yathā agniḥ uṣṇaḥ iti
tatra evam sati samyak jñāne puruṣāṇām vipratipattiḥ anupapannā
tarka jñānānām tu anyonya virodhāt prasiddhā vipratipattiḥ
yat hi kenacid tārkikeṇa idam eva samyak jñānam iti pratiṣṭhāpitam tad apareṇa vyutthāpyate
tena api pratiṣṭhāpitam pareṇa vyutthāpyate iti ca prasiddham loke
katham eka rūpa anavasthita viṣayam tarka prabhavam samyak jñānam bhavet
na ca pradhāna vādī tarka vidām uttamaḥ iti sarvaiḥ tārkikaiḥ parigṛhītaḥ yena tadīyam matam samyak jñānam iti pratipadyemahi
na ca śakyante tīta anāgata vartamānāḥ tārkikāḥ ekasmin deśe kāle ca samāhartum yena tad matiḥ eka rūpa eka artha viṣayā samyak matiḥ iti syāt
vedasya tu nitya tve vijñāna utpatti hetu tve ca sati vyavasthita artha viṣaya tva upapatteḥ tad janitasya jñānasya samyaktvam atīta anāgata vartamānaiḥ sarvaiḥ api tārkikaiḥ apahnotum aśakyam
atas siddham asya eva aupaniṣadasya jñānasya samyak jñāna tvam
atas nyatra samyak jñāna tva anupapatteḥ saṃsāra avimokṣaḥ eva prasajyeta
atas āgama vaśena āgama anusāri tarka vaśena ca cetanam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti sthitam
etena śiṣṭa a parigrahāḥ api vyākhyātāḥ
śiṣṭa aparigraha adhikaraṇam
vaidikasya darśanasya pratyāsanna tvāt gurutara tarka bala upeta tvāt veda anusāribhiḥ ca kaiścid śiṣṭaiḥ kenacid aṃśena parigṛhīta tvāt pradhāna kāraṇa vādam tāvat vyapāśritya yaḥ tarka nimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ vedānta vākyeṣu udbhāvitaḥ sa parihṛtaḥ
idānīm aṇu ādi vāda vyapāśrayeṇa api kaiścid manda matibhiḥ vedānta vākyeṣu punar tarka nimittaḥ ākṣepaḥ āśaṅkyate iti atas pradhāna malla nibarhaṇa nyāyena atidiśati parigṛhyante iti parigrahāḥ
na parigrahāḥ aparigrahāḥ
śiṣṭānām aparigrahāḥ śiṣṭa aparigrahāḥ
etena prakṛtena pradhāna kāraṇa vāda nirākaraṇa kāraṇena
śiṣṭaiḥ manu vyāsa prabhṛtibhiḥ kenacid api aṃśena a parigṛhītāḥ ye ṇu ādi kāraṇa vādāḥ te pi pratiṣiddha tayā vyākhyātāḥ nirākṛtāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ
tulya tvāt nirākaraṇa kāraṇasya na atra punar āśaṅkitavyam kiṃcid asti
tulyam atrā api parama gambhīrasya jagat kāraṇasya tarka anavagāhya tvam tarkasya ca apratiṣṭhita tvam anyathā anumāne pi avimokṣaḥ āgama virodhaḥ ca iti evaṃjātīyakam nirākaraṇa kāraṇam

bhoktṛ āpatti adhikaraṇam
anyathā punar brahma kāraṇa vādaḥ tarka balena eva ākṣipyate
yadi api śrutiḥ pramāṇam sva viṣaye bhavati tathā api pramāṇa antareṇa viṣaya apahāre nyaparā bhavitum arhati yathā mantra arthavādau
tarkaḥ pi sva viṣayāt anyatra apratiṣṭhitaḥ syāt yathā dharma adharmayoḥ
kim atas yadi evam
atas idam ayuktam yat pramāṇa antara prasiddha artha bādhanam śruteḥ
katham punar pramāṇa antara prasiddhaḥ rthaḥ śrutyā bādhyate iti atra ucyate prasiddhaḥ hi ayam bhoktṛ bhogya vibhāgaḥ loke bhoktā cetanaḥ śārīraḥ bhogyāḥ śabda ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ iti
yathā bhoktā devadattaḥ bhogya odana iti
tasya ca vibhāgasya abhāvaḥ prasajyeta yadi bhoktā bhogya bhāvam āpadyeta bhogyam vā bhoktṛ bhāvam āpadyeta
tayoḥ ca itaretarabhāva āpattiḥ parama kāraṇāt brahmaṇaḥ na anyatvāt prasajyeta
na ca asya prasiddhasya vibhāgasya bādhanam yuktam
yathā tu adyatve bhoktṛ bhogyayoḥ vibhāgaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā atīta anāgatayoḥ api kalpayitavyaḥ
tasmāt prasiddhasya asya bhoktṛ bhogya vibhāgasya abhāva prasaṅgāt ayuktam idam brahma kāraṇatā avadhāraṇam iti ced kaścid codayet tam prati brūyāt syāt loka vat iti
upapadyate eva ayam asmad pakṣe vibhāgaḥ evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt
tathā hi samudrāt udaka ātmanaḥ na anya tve tad vikārāṇām phena vīcī taraṅga budbuda ādīnām itaretara vibhāgaḥ itaretara asaṃśleṣa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ ca vyavahāraḥ upalabhyate
na ca samudrāt udaka ātmanaḥ na anyatve tad vikārāṇām phena taraṅga ādīnām itaretarabhāva āpattiḥ bhavati
na ca teṣām itaretara bhāvānām pattau api samudra ātmanaḥ bhavati
evam iha api na bhoktṛ bhogyayoḥ itaretarabhāva āpattiḥ na ca parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ bhaviṣyati
yadi api bhoktā na brahmaṇaḥ vikāraḥ tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva anuprāviśat iti sraṣṭuḥ eva avikṛtasya kārya anupraveśena bhoktṛ tva śravaṇāt tathā api kāryam anupraviṣṭasya asti upādhi nimittaḥ vibhāgaḥ ākāśasya iva ghaṭa ādi upādhi nimittaḥ iti atas parama kāraṇāt brahmaṇaḥ nanyatve pi upapadyate bhoktṛ bhogya lakṣaṇaḥ vibhāgaḥ samudra taraṅga ādi nyāyena iti uktam

ārambhaṇa adhikaraṇam

na tu ayam vibhāgaḥ paramārthataḥ sti yasmāt tayoḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ ananyatvam avagamyate

etat uktam bhavati ekena mṛd piṇḍena paramārthataḥ mṛd ātmanā vijñātena sarvam mṛd mayam ghaṭa śarāva udañcana ādikam mṛd ātmaka tva aviśeṣāt vijñātam bhavet
yatas vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam vācā eva kevalam asti iti ārabhyate vikāraḥ ghaṭaḥ śarāvaḥ udañcanam ca iti
na tu vastu vṛttena vikāraḥ nāma kaścid asti
