bādhite ca śārīra ātma tve tad āśrayaḥ samastaḥ svābhāvikaḥ vyavahāraḥ bādhitaḥ bhavati yat prasiddhaye paraḥ brahmaṇaḥ kalpyeta
darśayati ca yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet ityādinā brahma ātma tva darśinam prati samastasya kriyā kāraka phala lakṣaṇasya vyavahārasya abhāvam
na ca ayam vyavahāra abhāvaḥ vasthā viśeṣa nibaddhaḥ bhidhīyate iti yuktam vaktum tat tvam asi iti brahma ātma bhāvasya anavasthā viśeṣa nibandhana tvāt
taskara dṛṣṭāntena ca anṛta abhisaṃdhasya bandhanam satya abhisaṃdhasya ca mokṣam darśayan ekatvam eva ekam pāramārthikam darśayati mithyājñāna vijṛmbhitam ca nānātvam
ubhaya satyatāyām hi katham vyavahāra gocaraḥ jantuḥ anṛta abhisaṃdhaḥ iti ucyate
mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti ca bheda dṛṣṭim apavadan etat eva darśayati
na ca asmin darśane jñānāt mokṣaḥ iti upapadyate samyak jñāna apanodyasya kasyacid mithyājñānasya saṃsāra kāraṇa tvena anabhyupagamāt
ubhaya satyatāyām hi katham ekatva jñānena nānātva jñānam apanudyate iti ucyate

kūṭasthasya iti viśeṣaṇāt
na hi kūṭasthasya brahmaṇaḥ sthiti gati vat aneka dharma āśraya tvam saṃbhavati
kūṭastham ca nityam brahma sarva vikriyā pratiṣedhāt iti avocāma
na ca yathā brahmaṇaḥ ātma eka tva darśanam mokṣa sādhanam evam jagat ākāra pariṇāmi tva darśanam api svatantram eva kasmaicid phalāya abhipreyate pramāṇa abhāvāt
kūṭastha brahma ātma ekatva vijñānāt eva hi phalam darśayati śāstram saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmā iti upakramya abhayam vai janaka iti evaṃjātīyakam
tatra etat siddham bhavati brahma prakaraṇe sarva dharma viśeṣa rahita brahma darśanāt eva phala siddhau satyām yat tatra aphalam śrūyate brahmaṇaḥ jagat ākāra pariṇāmi tva ādi tat brahma darśana upāya tvena eva viniyujyate phalavat saṃnidhau aphalam tat aṅgam itivat
na tu svatantram phalāya kalpyate iti
na hi pariṇāmavat tva vijñānāt pariṇāmavat tvam ātmanaḥ phalam syāt iti vaktum yuktam kūṭastha nitya tvāt mokṣasya
nanu kūṭastha brahma ātma vādinaḥ ekatva aikāntyāt īśitṛ īśitavya abhāve īśvara kāraṇa pratijñā virodhaḥ iti ced na
avidyā ātmaka nāma rūpa bīja vyākaraṇa apekṣa tvāt sarvajña tvasya
tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityādi vākyebhyaḥ nitya śuddha buddha mukta svarūpāt sarvajñāt sarva śakteḥ īśvarāt jagat jani sthiti pralayāḥ na acetanāt pradhānāt anyasmāt vā iti eṣaḥ rthaḥ pratijñātaḥ janma ādi asya yatas iti
sā pratijñā tad avasthā eva na tad viruddhaḥ rthaḥ punar iha ucyate
katham nā ucyate atyantam ātmanaḥ ekatvam advitīya tvam ca bruvatā
śṛṇu yathā nā ucyate sarvajñasya īśvarasya ātma bhūte iva avidyā kalpite nāma rūpe tattva anya tvābhyām anirvacanīye saṃsāra prapañca bīja bhūte sarvajñasya īśvarasya māyā śaktiḥ prakṛtiḥ iti na śruti smṛtyoḥ abhilapyete
tābhyām anyaḥ sarvajñaḥ īśvaraḥ ākāśaḥ vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yat antarā tat brahma
iti  śruteḥ nāmarūpe vyākaravāṇi SPr1Im 
sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīraḥ nāmāni kṛtvā abhivadanyadā āste
oḥ Taiā
ekam bījam bahudhā yaḥ karoti śvet
ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca
evam avidyā kṛta nāma rūpa upādhi anurodhi īśvaraḥ bhavati vyomā iva ghaṭa karaka ādi upādhi anurodhi
sa ca sva ātma bhūtān eva ghaṭa ākāśa sthānīyān avidyā pratyupasthāpita nāma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa saṃghāta anurodhinaḥ jīva ākhyān vijñāna ātmanaḥ pratīṣṭe vyavahāra viṣaye
tat evam avidyā ātmaka upādhi pariccheda apekṣam eva īśvarasya īśvara tvam sarvajña tvam sarva śakti tvam ca na paramārthataḥ vidyayā apāsta sarva upādhi svarūpe ātmani īśitṛ īśitavya sarvajña tva ādi vyavahāraḥ upapadyate
tathā ca uktam yatra na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anyat vijānāti sa bhūmā iti
yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet ityādinā ca
evam paramārtha avasthāyām sarva vyavahāra abhāvam vadanti vedāntāḥ sarve
tathā īśvaragītāsu api na kartṛ tvam na karmāṇi lokasya sṛjati prabhuḥ
na karma phala saṃyogam svabhāvaḥ tu pravartate na ādatte kasyacid pāpam na ca eva sukṛtam vibhuḥ
ajñānena āvṛtam jñānam tena muhyanti jantavaḥ PNM
iti paramārtha avasthāyām īśitṛ īśitavya ādi vyavahāra abhāvaḥ pradarśyate
vyavahāra avasthāyām tu  uktaḥ śrutau api īśvara ādi vyavahāraḥ eṣa sarva īśvaraḥ SNM eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ eṣa bhūta pālaḥ eṣa setuḥ vidharaṇaḥ eṣām lokānām a  sambhedāya SDM
iti
tathā ca īśvaragītāsu api īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe rjuna tiṣṭhati

iti mahā samudra ādi sthānīya tām brahmaṇaḥ kathayati a pratyākhyāya eva kārya prapañcam pariṇāma prakriyām ca āśrayati sa guṇeṣu upāsaneṣu upayokṣyate iti
bhāve ca upalabdheḥ
itas ca kāraṇāt ananya tvam kāryasya yat kāraṇam bhāvaḥ eva kāraṇasya kāryam upalabhyate na abhāve
tat yathā satyām mṛdi ghaṭaḥ upalabhyate satsu ca tantuṣu paṭaḥ
na ca niyamena anya bhāve nyasya upalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭā
na hi aśvaḥ goḥ anyaḥ san goḥ bhāvaḥ eva upalabhyate
na ca kulāla bhāve eva ghaṭaḥ upalabhyate sati api nimitta naimittika bhāve
nanu anyasya bhāve pi anyasya upalabdhiḥ niyatā dṛśyate yathā agni bhāve dhūmasya iti
na iti ucyate udvāpite pi agnau gopāla ghuṭikā ādi dhāritasya dhūmasya dṛśyamāna tvāt
atha dhūmam kayācid avasthayā viśiṃṣyāt īdṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ na asati agnau bhavati iti na evam api kaścid doṣaḥ
tad bhāva anuraktām hi buddhim kārya kāraṇayoḥ ananyatve hetum vayam vadāmaḥ
na ca asau agni dhūmayoḥ vidyate
bhāvāt ca upalabdheḥ iti vā sūtram
na kevalam śabdāt eva kārya kāraṇayoḥ ananyatvam pratyakṣa upalabdhi bhāvāt ca tayoḥ ananyatvam iti arthaḥ
bhavati hi pratyakṣa upalabdhiḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ ananyatve
tat yathā tantu saṃsthāne paṭe tantu vyatirekeṇa paṭaḥ nāma kāryam na eva upalabhyate kevalāḥ tu tantavaḥ ātāna vitānavantaḥ pratyakṣam upalabhyante tathā tantuṣu aṃśavaḥ aṃśuṣu tad avayavāḥ
anayā pratyakṣa upalabdhyā lohita śukla kṛṣṇāni trīṇi rūpāṇi tatas vāyu mātram ākāśa mātram ca iti anumeyam tatas param brahma ekam eva advitīyam
tatra sarva pramāṇānām niṣṭhām avocāma
sattvāt ca avarasya
itas ca kāraṇāt kāryasya ananya tvam yat kāraṇam prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa ātmanā eva kāraṇe sattvam avara kālīnasya kāryasya śrūyate sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt ityādau idam śabda gṛhītasya kāryasya kāraṇena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt
yat ca yat ātmanā yatra na vartate na tat tatas utpadyate yathā sikatābhyaḥ tailam
tasmāt prāk utpatteḥ ananyatvāt utpannam api ananyat eva kāraṇāt kāryam iti avagamyate
yathā ca kāraṇam brahma triṣu kāleṣu sattvam na vyabhicarati evam kāryam api jagatī traṣu kāleṣu sattvam na vyabhicarati
ekam ca punar sattvam
atas pi ananya tvam kāraṇāt kāryasya
asat vyapadeśāt na iti ced na dharma antareṇa vākyaśeṣāt
nanu kvacid asattvam api prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya vyapadiśati śrutiḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti asat vai idam agre āsīt iti ca
tasmāt asat vyapadeśāt na prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya sattvam iti ced nā iti brūmaḥ
na hi ayam atyanta asattva abhiprāyeṇa prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya asat vyapadeśaḥ
kim tarhi vyākṛta nāma rūpa tvāt dharmāt avyākṛta nāma rūpa tvam dharma antaram tena dharma antareṇa ayam asat vyapadeśaḥ prāk utpatteḥ sataḥ eva kāryasya kāraṇa rūpeṇa ananyasya
katham etat avagamyate
vākya śeṣāt
yad upakrame saṃdigdha artham vākyam tat śeṣāt niścīyate
iha ca tāvat asat eva idam agre āsīt iti asat śabdena upakrame nirdiṣṭam yat tat eva punar tad śabdena parāmṛśya sat iti viśinaṣṭi tat sat āsīt iti asataḥ ca pūrva apara kāla asaṃbandhāt āsīt śabda anupapatteḥ ca
asat vai idam agre āsīt iti atra api tadā ātmānam svayam akuruta iti vākyaśeṣe viśeṣaṇāt na atyanta asattvam
tasmāt dharma antareṇa eva ayam asat vyapadeśaḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya
nāma rūpa vyākṛtam hi vastu sat śabda arham loke prasiddham
atas prak nāma rūpa vyākaraṇāt asat iva āsīt iti upacaryate
yukteḥ śabda antarāt ca
yukteḥ ca prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya sattvam ananya tvam ca kāraṇāt avagamyate śabda antarāt ca
yuktiḥ tāvat varṇyate dadhi ghaṭa rucaka ādi arthibhiḥ pratiniyatāni kāraṇāni kṣīra mṛttikā suvarṇa ādīni upādīyamānāni loke dṛśyante
na hi dadhi arthibhiḥ mṛttikā upādīyate na ghaṭa arthibhiḥ kṣīram
tat asatkārya vāde na upapadyeta
aviśiṣṭe hi prāk utpatteḥ sarvasya sarvatra asattve kasmāt kṣīrāt eva dadhi utpadyate na mṛttikāyāḥ
mṛttikāyāḥ eva ca ghaṭaḥ utpadyate na kṣīrāt
atha aviśiṣṭe pi prāk asattve kṣīre eva dadhnaḥ kaścid atiśayaḥ na mṛttikāyām mṛttikāyām eva ca ghaṭasya kaścid atiśayaḥ na kṣīre iti ucyeta atas tarhi atiśayavat tvāt prāk avasthāyāḥ asatkārya vāda hāniḥ satkārya vāda siddhiḥ ca
śaktiḥ ca kāraṇasya kārya niyama arthā kalpyamānā na anyā asatī vā kāryam niyacchet asattva aviśeṣāt anya tva aviśeṣāt ca
tasmāt kāraṇasya ātma bhūtā śaktiḥ śakteḥ ca ātma bhūtam kāryam
api ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ dravya guṇa ādīnām ca aśva mahiṣa vat bheda buddhi abhāvāt tādātmyam abhyupagantavyam
samavāya kalpanāyām api samavāyasya samavāyibhiḥ saṃbandhe bhyupagamyamāne tasya tasya anyonyaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ iti anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ anabhyupagamyamāne ca viccheda prasaṅgaḥ
atha samavāyaḥ svayam saṃbandha rūpa tvāt an apekṣya eva aparam saṃbandham saṃbadhyeta saṃyogaḥ pi tarhi svayam saṃbandha rūpa tvāt an apekṣya eva aparam samavāyam saṃbadhyeta
tādātmya pratīteḥ ca dravya guṇa ādīnām samavāya kalpanā ānarthakyam
katham ca kāryam avayavi dravyam kāraṇeṣu avayava dravyeṣu vartamānam vartate
kim samasteṣu avayaveṣu varteta uta pratyavayavam
yadi tāvat samasteṣu varteta tatas vayavi anupalabdhiḥ prasajyeta samasta avayava saṃnikarṣasya aśakya tvāt
na hi bahu tvam samasteṣu āśrayeṣu vartamānam vyasta āśraya grahaṇena gṛhyate
atha avayavaśas samasteṣu varteta tadā api ārambhaka avayava vyatirekeṇa avayavinaḥ vayavāḥ kalpyeran yaiḥ ārambhakeṣu avayaveṣu avayavaśas vayavī varteta
kośa avayava vyatiriktaiḥ hi avayavaiḥ asiḥ kośam vyāpnoti
anavasthā ca evam prasajyeta teṣu teṣu avayaveṣu vartayitum anyeṣām anyeṣām avayavānām kalpanīya tvāt
atha pratyavayavam varteta tadā ekatra vyāpāre nyatra avyāpāraḥ syāt
na hi devadattaḥ srughne saṃnidhīyamānaḥ tat ahar eva pāṭaliputre saṃnidhīyate
yugapad anekatra vṛttau aneka tva prasaṅgaḥ syāt devadatta yajñadattayoḥ iva srughna pāṭaliputra nivāsinoḥ
go tva ādi vat pratyekam parisamāpteḥ na doṣaḥ iti ced na
tathā pratīti abhāvāt
yadi go tva ādi vat pratyekam parisamāptaḥ vayavī syāt yathā go tvam prati vyakti pratyakṣam gṛhyate evam avayavī api pratyavayavam pratyakṣam gṛhyeta
na ca evam niyatam gṛhyate
pratyeka parisamāptau ca avayavinaḥ kāryeṇa adhikārāt tasya ca ekatvāt śṛṅgeṇa api stana kāryam kuryāt urasā ca pṛṣṭha kāryam
na ca evam dṛśyate
prāk utpatteḥ ca kāryasya asattve utpattiḥ akartṛkā nirātmikā ca syāt
utpattiḥ ca nāma kriyā sā sa kartṛkā eva bhavitum arhati gati ādi vat
kriyā ca nāma syāt akartṛkā ca iti vipratiṣidhyeta
ghaṭasya ca utpattiḥ ucyamānā ca ghaṭa kartṛkā kiṃtarhi anya kartṛkā iti kalpyā syāt
tathā kapāla ādīnām api utpattiḥ ucyamānāni akartṛkā eva kalpyeta
tathā ca sati ghaṭaḥ utpadyate id yukte kulāla ādīni kāraṇāni utpadyante iti uktam syāt
na ca loke ghaṭa utpattiḥ iti ukte kulāla ādīnām api utpadyamāna tā pratīyate utpanna tā pratīteḥ
atha sva kāraṇa sattā saṃbandhe evā utpattiḥ ātma lābhaḥ ca kāryasya iti ced katham alabdha ātmakam saṃbadhyeta iti vaktavyam
satoḥ hi dvayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃbhavati na sat asatoḥ asatoḥ vā
abhāvasya ca nirupākhya tvāt prāk utpatteḥ iti maryādā karaṇam anupapannam
satām hi loke kṣetra gṛha ādīnām maryādā dṛṣṭā na abhāvasya
na hi vandhyāputraḥ rājā babhūva prāk pūrṇavarmaṇaḥ bhiṣekāt iti evaṃjātīyakena maryādā karaṇena nirupākhyaḥ vandhyāputraḥ rājā babhūva bhavati bhaviṣyati iti vā viśeṣyate
yadi ca kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam abhaviṣyat tatas idam api upāpatsyata kārya bhāvaḥ pi kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam bhaviṣyati iti
vayam tu paśyāmaḥ vandhyā putrasya kārya abhāvasya ca abhāva tva aviśeṣāt yathā bandhyā putraḥ kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam na bhaviṣyati evam kārya abhāvaḥ api kāraka vyāpārāt ūrdhvam na bhaviṣyati iti
nanu evam sati kāraka vyāpāraḥ narthakaḥ prasajyeta
yathā eva hi prāk siddha tvāt kāraṇa svarūpa siddhaye na kaścid vyāpriyate evam prāk siddha tvāt tad ananyatvāt ca kāryasya svarūpa siddhaye na kaścid vyāpriyeta
vyāpriyate ca
atas kāraka vyāpāra arthavat tvāya manyāmahe prāk utpatteḥ abhāvaḥ kāryasya iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ
yatas kāryākāreṇa kāraṇam vyavasthāpayataḥ kāraka vyāpārasya arthavat tvam upapadyate
kārya ākāraḥ pi kāraṇasya ātma bhūtaḥ eva anātma bhūtasya an ārabhya tvāt iti abhāṇi
na ca viśeṣa darśana mātreṇa vastu anya tvam bhavati
na hi devadattaḥ saṃkucita hasta pādaḥ prasārita hasta pādaḥ ca viśeṣeṇa dṛśyamānaḥ u pi vastu anya tvam gacchati saḥ eva iti pratyabhijñānāt
tathā pratidinam aneka saṃsthānānām api pitṛ ādīnām na vastu anya tvam bhavati mama pitā mama bhrātā mama putraḥ iti pratyabhijñānāt
janma uccheda anantarita tvāt tatra yuktam na anyatra iti ced na
kṣīra ādīnām api dadhi ādi ākāra saṃsthānasya pratyakṣa tvāt
adṛśyamānānām api vaṭa dhānā ādīnām samāna jātīya avayava antara upacitānām aṅkura ādi bhāvena darśana gocara tā āpattau janma saṃjñā
teṣām eva avayavānām apacaya vaśāt adarśana āpattau uccheda saṃjñā
tatra īdṛś janma uccheda antarita tvāt ced asataḥ sattva āpattiḥ sataḥ ca asattva āpattiḥ tathā sati garbha vāsinaḥ uttānaśāyinaḥ ca bheda prasaṅgaḥ
tathā ca bālya yauvana sthāvireṣu api bheda prasaṅgaḥ pitṛ ādi vyavahāra lopa prasaṅagaḥ ca
etena kṣaṇabhaṅga vādaḥ prativaditavyaḥ
yasya tu punar prāk utpatteḥ asat kāryam tasya nirviṣayaḥ kāraka vyāpāraḥ syāt abhāvasya viṣaya tva anupapatteḥ ākāśa hanana prayojana khaṅga ādi aneka āyudha prayukti vat
samavāyi kāraṇa viṣayaḥ kāraka vyāpāraḥ syāt iti ced na
anya viṣayeṇa kāraka vyāpāreṇa anya niṣpatteḥ atiprasaṅgāt
samavāyi kāraṇasya eva ātma atiśayaḥ kāryam iti ced na
satkārya tā āpatteḥ
tasmāt kṣīra ādīni eva dravyāṇi dadhi ādi bhāvena avatiṣṭhamānāni kārya ākhyām labhante iti na kāraṇāt anyat kāryam varṣa śatena api śakyam kalpayitum
tathā mūlakāraṇam eva ā antyāt kāryāt tena tena kārya ākāreṇa naṭa vat sarva vyavahāra āspada tvam pratipadyate
evam yukteḥ kāryasya prāc utpatteḥ sattvam ananya tvam ca kāraṇāt avagamyate
śabda antarāt ca etat avagamyate pūrva sūtre sat vyapadeśinaḥ śabdasya udāhṛta tvāt tatas nyaḥ sat vyapadeśī śabdaḥ śabda antaram sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam ityādi
tat ha eke āhuḥ asat eva idam agre āsīt iti ca asat pakṣam upakṣipya katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti ākṣipya sat eva somya idam agre āsīt iti avadhārayati
tatra idam śabda vācyasya kāryasya prāk utpatteḥ sat śabda vācyena kāraṇena sāmānādhikaraṇyasya śrūyamāṇa tvāt sattva ananyatve prasidhyataḥ
yadi tu prāk utpatteḥ asat kāryam syāt paścāt ca utpadyamānam kāraṇe samaveyāt tat anyat kāraṇāt syāt tatra yena aśrutam śrutam bhavati iti iyam pratijñā pīḍyeta
sattva ananyatva avagateḥ tu iyam pratijñā samarthyate
paṭa vat ca
yathā ca saṃveṣṭitaḥ paṭaḥ na vyaktam gṛhyate kim ayam paṭaḥ kim vā anyat dravyam iti
saḥ eva prasāritaḥ yat saṃveṣṭitam dravyam tat paṭaḥ eva iti prasāraṇena abhivyaktaḥ gṛhyate
yathā ca saṃveṣṭana samaye paṭaḥ iti gṛhyamāṇaḥ na viśiṣṭa āyāma vistāraḥ gṛhyate
saḥ eva prasāraṇa samaye viśiṣṭa āyāma vistāraḥ gṛhyate na saṃveṣṭita rūpāt anyaḥ yam bhinnaḥ paṭaḥ iti evam tantu ādi kāraṇa avastham paṭa ādi kāryam aspaṣṭam sat turī vema kuvinda ādi kāraka vyāpāra abhivyaktam spaṣṭam gṛhyate
atas saṃveṣṭita prasārita paṭa nyāyena eva ananyat kāraṇāt kāryam iti arthaḥ
yathā ca prāṇa ādi
yathā ca loke prāṇa apāna ādiṣu prāṇa bhedeṣu prāṇāyāmena niruddheṣu kāraṇa mātreṇa rūpeṇa vartamāneṣu jīvana mātram kāryam nirvartyate na ākuñcana prasāraṇa ādikam kārya antaram
teṣu eva prāṇabhedeṣu punar pravṛtteṣu jīvanāt adhikam ākuñcana prasāraṇa ādikam api kārya antaram nirvartyate
na ca prāṇa bhedānām prabhedavataḥ prāṇāt anya tvam samīraṇa svabhāva aviśeṣāt evam kāryasya kāraṇāt ananya tvam
atas ca kṛtsnasya jagataḥ brahma kārya tvāt tad ananya tvāt ca siddhā eṣā śrautī pratijñā yena a śrutam śrutam bhavati a matam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti
itara vyapadeśāt
itara vyapadeśa adhikaraṇam
anyathā punar cetana kāraṇa vādaḥ ākṣipyate cetanāt hi jagat prakriyāyām āśrīyamāṇāyām hita akaraṇa ādayaḥ doṣāḥ prasajyante
kutas
itara vyapadeśāt
itarasya śārīrasya brahma ātmatvam vyapadiśati śrutiḥ saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti pratibodhanāt
yat vai itarasya ca brahmaṇaḥ śārīra ātma tvam vyapadiśati tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva anuprāviśat iti sraṣṭuḥ eva avikṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ kārya anupraveśena śārīra ātma tva darśanāt
anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti ca parā devatā jīvam ātma śabdena vyapadiśantī na brahmaṇaḥ bhinnaḥ śārīraḥ iti darśayati
tasmāt yat brahmaṇaḥ sraṣṭṛ tvam tat śārīrasya eva iti
atas ca svatantraḥ kartā san hitam eva ātmanaḥ saumanasya karam kuryāt na ahitam janma maraṇa jarā roga ādi aneka anartha jālam
na hi kaścid aparatantraḥ bandhanāgāram ātmanaḥ kṛtvā anupraviśati
na ca svayam atyanta nirmalaḥ san atyanta malinam deham ātma tvena upeyāt
kṛtam api kathaṃcid yat duḥkha karam tat icchayā jahyāt
sukha karam ca upādadīta
smaret ca mayā idam jagat bimbam vicitram viracitam iti
sarvaḥ hi lokaḥ spaṣṭam kāryam kṛtvā smarati mayā idam kṛtam iti
yathā ca māyāvī svayam prasāritām māyām icchayā anāyāsena eva upasaṃharati evam śārīraḥ pi imām sṛṣṭim upasaṃharet
svakīyam api tāvat śarīram śārīraḥ na śaknoti anāyāsena upasaṃhartum
evam hita kriyā ādi adarśanāt anyāyyā cetanāt jagat prakriyā iti gamyate
adhikam tu bheda nirdeśāt
tu śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati
yat sarvajñam sarva śakti brahma nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam śārīrāt adhikam anyat tat vayam jagataḥ sraṣṭṛ brūmaḥ
na tasmin hita akaraṇa ādayaḥ doṣāḥ prasajyante
na hi tasya hitam kiṃcid kartavyam asti ahitam vā parihartavyam nitya mukta svabhāva tvāt
na ca tasya jñāna pratibandhaḥ śakti pratibandhaḥ vā kvacid api asti sarvajña tvāt sarva śakti tvāt ca
śārīraḥ tu anevaṃvidhaḥ
tasmin prasajyante hita akaraṇa ādayaḥ doṣāḥ
na tu tam vayam jagataḥ sraṣṭāram brūmaḥ
kutas etat
bheda nirdeśāt ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ saḥ nveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati śārīraḥ ātmā prājñena ātmanā anvārūḍhaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ kartṛ karma ādi bheda nirdeśaḥ jīvāt adhikam brahma darśayati
nanu abheda nirdeśaḥ api darśitaḥ tattvam asi iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ
katham bheda abhedau viruddhau saṃbhaveyātām
na eṣa doṣaḥ mahākāśa ghaṭa ākāśa nyāyena ubhaya saṃbhavasya tatra tatra pratiṣṭhāpita tvāt
api ca yadā tat tvam asi iti evaṃjātīyakena abheda nirdeśena abhedaḥ pratibodhitaḥ bhavati apagatam bhavati tadā jīvasya saṃsāri tvam brahmaṇaḥ ca sraṣṭṛ tvam samastasya mithyā jñāna vijṛmbhitasya bheda vyavahārasya samyak jñānena bādhita tvāt
tatra kutas eva sṛṣṭiḥ
kutas vā hita akaraṇa ādayaḥ doṣāḥ
avidyā pratyupasthāpita nāma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa saṃghāta upādhya viveka kṛtā hi bhrāntiḥ hita akaraṇa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ saṃsāraḥ na tu paramārthataḥ sti iti asakṛt avocāma janma maraṇa chedana bhedana ādi abhimāna vat
abādhite tu bheda vyavahāre saḥ nveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakena bheda nirdeśena avagamyamānam brahmaṇaḥ dhika tvam hita akaraṇa ādi doṣa prasaktim niruṇaddhi
aśma ādi vat ca tad anupapattiḥ
yathā ca loke pṛthivī tva sāmānya anvitānām api aśmanām kecid mahārhāḥ maṇayaḥ vajra vaiḍūrya ādayaḥ anye madhyama vīryāḥ sūryakānta ādayaḥ anye prahīṇāḥ śvāyasa prakṣepaṇa arhāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ iti anekavidham vaicitryam dṛśyate
yathā ca eka pṛthivī vyapāśrayāṇām api bījānām bahuvidham patra puṣpa phala gandha rasa ādi vaicitryam candana kiṃpāka campaka ādiṣu upalakṣyate
yathā ca ekasya api anna rasasya lohita ādīni keśa loma ādīni ca vicitrāṇi kāryāṇi bhavanti evam ekasya api brahmaṇaḥ jīva prājña pṛthaktvam kārya vaicitryam ca upapadyate iti atas tad anupapattiḥ para parikalpita doṣa anupapattiḥ iti arthaḥ
śruteḥ ca prāmāṇyāt vikārasya ca vācā ārambhaṇa mātra tvāt svapna dṛśya bhāva vaicitrya vat ca iti abhyuccayaḥ
upasaṃhāra darśanāt na iti ced na kṣīravat hi
upasaṃhāra darśana adhika ramam
cetanam brahma ekam advitīyam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti yat uktam tat na upapadyate
kasmāt
upasaṃhāra darśanāt
iha hi loke kulāla ādayaḥ ghaṭa paṭa ādīnām kartāraḥ mṛd daṇḍa cakra sūtra salila ādi aneka kāraka upasaṃhāreṇa saṃgṛhīta sādhanāḥ santaḥ tat tat kāryam kurvāṇāḥ dṛśyante
brahma ca asahāyam tava abhipretam
tasya sādhana antara an upasaṃgrahe sati katham sraṣṭṛ tvam upapadyeta
tasmāt na brahma jagat kāraṇam iti ced nā eṣa doṣaḥ
yatas kṣīra vat dravya svabhāva viśeṣāt upapadyate yathā hi loke kṣīram jalam vā svayam eva dadhi hima karaka ādi bhāvena pariṇamate na apekṣya bāhyam sādhanam tathā iha api bhaviṣyati
nanu kṣīra ādi api dadhi ādi bhāvena pariṇamamānam apekṣate eva bāhyam sādhanam auṣṇya ādikam
katham ucyate kṣīravat hi iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ
svayam api hi kṣīram yām ca yāvatīm ca pariṇāma mātrām anubhavati tāvatī eva tu āryate tu auṣṇya ādinā dadhi bhāvāya
yadi ca svayam dadhi bhāva śīla tā na syāt na eva auṣṇya ādinā api balāt dadhi bhāvam āpadyeta
na hi vāyuḥ ākāśaḥ vai auṣṇya ādinā balāt dadhi bhāvam āpadyate
sādhana sāmagryā ca tasya pūrṇa tā saṃpādyate
paripūrṇa śaktikam tu brahma
na tasya anyena kenacid pūrṇa tā saṃpādayitavyā
śrutiḥ ca bhavati na tasya kāryam karaṇam ca vidyate na tad samaḥ ca abhyadhikaḥ ca dṛśyate
parā asya śaktiḥ vividhā eva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñāna bala kriyā ca iti
tasmāt ekasya api brahmaṇaḥ vicitra śakti yogāt kṣīra ādi vat vicitra pariṇāmaḥ upapadyate
deva ādi vat api loke
syāt etat upapadyate kṣīra ādīnām acetanānām an apekṣya api bāhyam sādhanam dadhi ādi bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt
cetanāḥ punar kulāla ādayaḥ sādhana sāmagrīm apekṣya eva tasmai tasmai kāryāya pravartamānāḥ dṛśyante
katham brahma cetanam sat asahāyam pravarteta iti deva ādi vat iti brūmaḥ yathā loke devāḥ pitaraḥ ṛṣayaḥ iti evamādayaḥ mahā prabhāvāḥ cetanāḥ api santaḥ na apekṣya eva kiṃcid bāhyam sādhanam aiśvarya viśeṣa yogāt abhidhyāna mātreṇa svatas eva bahūni nānā saṃsthānāni śarīrāṇi prāsāda ādīni ratha ādīni ca nirmimāṇāḥ upalabhyante mantra arthavāda itihāsa purāṇa prāmāṇyāt
tantunābhaḥ ca svatas eva tantūn sṛjati
balākā ca antareṇa eva śukram garbham dhatte
padminī ca an apekṣya kiṃcid prasthāna sādhanam saraḥ ntarāt saraḥ ntaram pratiṣṭhate evam cetanam api brahma an apekṣya eva bāhyam sādhanam svatas eva jagat srakṣyati
sa yadi brūyāt ye ete deva ādayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ dṛṣṭāntāḥ upāttāḥ te dārṣṭāntikena brahmaṇā na samānāḥ bhavanti
śarīram eva hi acetanam deva ādīnām śarīra antara ādi vibhūti utpādane upādānam na tu cetanaḥ ātmā
tantunābhasya ca kṣudratara jantu bhakṣaṇāt lālā kaṭhina tām āpadyamānā tantuḥ bhavati
balākā ca stanayitnu rava śravaṇāt garbham dhatte
padminī ca cetana prayuktā satī acetanena eva śarīreṇa saraḥ ntarāt saraḥ ntaram upasarpati vallī iva vṛkṣam na tu svayam evā acetanā saraḥ ntara upasarpaṇe vyāpriyate
tasmāt na ete brahmaṇaḥ dṛṣṭāntāḥ iti tam prati brūyāt na ayam doṣaḥ
kulāla ādi dṛṣṭānta vailakṣaṇya mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt iti yathā hi kulāla ādīnām deva ādīnām ca samāne cetana tve kulāla ādayaḥ kārya ārambhe bāhyam sādhanam apekṣante na deva ādayaḥ
tathā brahma cetanam api na bāhyam sādhanam apekṣiṣyate iti etāvat vayam deva ādi udāharaṇena vivakṣāmaḥ
tasmāt yathā ekasya sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam tathā sarveṣām eva bhavitum arhati iti na asti ekānte iti abhiprāyaḥ
kṛtsna prasaktiḥ niravayava tva śabda kopaḥ vā
kṛtsna prasakti adhikaraṇam
cetanam ekam advitīyam brahma kṣīra ādi vat deva ādi vat ca an apekṣya bāhyam sādhanam svayam pariṇamamānam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti sthitam
śāstra artha pariśuddhaye tu punar ākṣipati
kṛtsna prasaktiḥ kṛtsnasya brahmaṇaḥ kārya rūpeṇa pariṇāmaḥ prāpnoti niravayava tvāt yadi brahma pṛthivī ādi vat sa avayavam abhaviṣyat tatas sya eka deśaḥ paryaṇaṃsyat eka deśaḥ ca avasthāsyata
niravayavam tu brahma śrutibhyaḥ vagamyate niṣkalam niṣkriyam śāntam niravadyam nirañjanam divyaḥ hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sa bāhya abhyantaraḥ hi ajaḥ idam mahat bhūtam anantam apāram vijñāna ghanaḥ eva saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmā a sthūlam an aṇu ityādyābhyaḥ sarva viśeṣa pratiṣedhinībhyaḥ
tatas ca eka deśa pariṇāma asaṃbhavāt kṛtsna pariṇāma prasaktau satyām mūla ucchedaḥ prasajyeta
draṣṭavya tā upadeśa ānarthakyam ca āpadyeta ayatna dṛṣṭa tvāt kāryasya tad vyatiriktasya ca brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavāt
aja tva ādi śabda vyākopaḥ ca
atha etad doṣa parijihīrṣayā sāvayavam eva brahma abhyupagamyeta tathā api ye niravayava tvasya pratipādakāḥ śabdāḥ udāhṛtāḥ te prakupyeyuḥ
sāvayava tve ca anitya tva prasaṅgaḥ iti sarvathā ayam pakṣaḥ na ghaṭayitum śakyate iti ākṣipati
śruteḥ tu śabda mūla tvāt
tu śabdena ākṣepam pariharati
na khalu asmad pakṣe kaścid api doṣaḥ sti
na tāvat kṛtsna prasaktiḥ asti
kutas
śruteḥ yathā eva hi brahmaṇaḥ jagat utpattiḥ śrūyate evam vikāra vyatirekeṇa api brahmaṇaḥ śrūyate prakṛti vikārayoḥ bhedena vyapadeśāt sā iyam devatā aikṣata hanta aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti tāvān asya mahimā tatas jyāyāḥ ca pūruṣaḥ
pādaḥ u sya viśvā bhūtāni tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti ca evaṃjātīyakāt
tathā hṛdaya āyatana tva vacanāt
sat saṃpatti vacanāt ca yadi ca kṛtsnam brahma kārya bhāvena upayuktam syāt satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati iti suṣupti gatam viśeṣaṇam anupapannam syāt vikṛtena brahmaṇā nitya saṃpanna tvāt avikṛtasya ca brahmaṇaḥ bhāvāt
tathā indriya gocara tva pratiṣedhāt brahmaṇaḥ vikārasya ca indriya gocara tva upapatteḥ
tasmāt asti avikṛtam brahma
na ca niravayava tva śabda vyākopaḥ sti śrūyamāṇa tvāt eva niravayava tvasya api abhyupagamyamāna tvāt
śabda mūlam ca brahma śabda pramāṇakam na indriya ādi pramāṇakam
tat yathāśabdam abhyupagantavyam
śabdaḥ ca ubhayam api brahmaṇaḥ pratipādayati akṛtsna prasaktim niravayava tvam ca
laukikānām api maṇi mantra oṣadhi prabhṛtīnām deśa kāla nimitta vaicitrya vaśāt śaktayaḥ viruddha aneka kārya viṣayāḥ dṛśyante
tāḥ api tāvat na upadeśam antareṇa kevalena tarkeṇa avagantum śakyante asya vastunaḥ etāvatyaḥ etad sahāyāḥ etad viṣayāḥ etad prayojanāḥ ca śaktayaḥ iti
kim uta acintya svabhāvasya brahmaṇaḥ rūpam vinā śabdena na nirūpyeta
tathā ca āhuḥ paurāṇikāḥ acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ na tān tarkeṇa yojayet
prakṛtibhyaḥ param yat ca tat acintyasya lakṣaṇam iti
tasmāt śabda mūlaḥ eva atīndriya artha yāthātmya adhigamaḥ
nanu śabdena api na śakyate viruddhaḥ rthaḥ pratyāyayitum niravayavam ca brahma pariṇamate na ca kṛtsnam iti
yadi niravayavam brahma syāt na eva pariṇameta kṛtsnam eva vā pariṇameta
atha kenacid rūpeṇa pariṇameta kenacid ca avatiṣṭheta iti rūpa bheda kalpanāt sa avayavam eva prasajyeta
kriyā viṣaye hi atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti na atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti iti evaṃjātīyakāyām virodha pratītau api vikalpa āśrayaṇam virodha a parihāra kāraṇam bhavati puruṣa tantra tvāt ca anuṣṭhānasya
iha tu vikalpa āśrayaṇena api na virodha parihāraḥ saṃbhavati a puruṣa tantra tvāt vastunaḥ
tasmāt durghaṭam etat iti na eṣa doṣaḥ avidyā kalpita rūpa bheda abhyupagamāt
na hi avidyā kalpitena rūpa bhedena sa avayavam vastu saṃpadyate
na hi timira upahata nayanena anekaḥ iva candramāḥ dṛśyamānaḥ nekaḥ eva bhavati
avidyā kalpitena ca nāma rūpa lakṣaṇena rūpa bhedena vyākṛta avyākṛta ātmakena tattva anya tvābhyām anirvacanīyena brahma pariṇāma ādi sarva vyavahāra āspada tvam pratipadyate
pāramārthikena ca rūpeṇa sarva vyavahāra atītam apariṇatam avatiṣṭhate vācā ārambhaṇa mātra tvāt ca avidyā kalpitasya nāma rūpa bhedasya iti na niravayava tvam brahmaṇaḥ kupyati
na ca iyam pariṇāma śrutiḥ pariṇāma pratipādana arthā tad pratipattau phala anavagamāt
sarva vyavahāra hīna brahma ātma bhāva pratipādana arthā tu eṣā tad pratipattau phala avagamāt
saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmā iti upakramya āha abhayam vai janaka prāptaḥ si iti
tasmāt asmad pakṣe na kaścid api doṣa prasaṅgaḥ sti
ātmani ca iva vicitrāḥ ca hi
api ca na eva atra vivaditavyam katham ekasmin brahmaṇi svarūpa anupamardena eva aneka ākārā sṛṣṭiḥ syāt iti
yatas ātmani api ekasmin svapna dṛśi sva rūpa anupamardena eva aneka ākārā sṛṣṭiḥ paṭhyate na tatra rathāḥ na ratha yogāḥ na panthānaḥ bhavanti atha rathān ratha yogān pathaḥ sṛjate ityādinā
loke pi deva ādiṣu māyāvi ādiṣu ca sva rūpa an upamardena eva vicitrāḥ hasti aśva ādi sṛṣṭayaḥ dṛśyante
tathā ekasmin api brahmaṇi svarūpa anupamardena eva aneka ākārā sṛṣṭiḥ bhaviṣyati iti
sva pakṣa doṣāt ca
pareṣām api eṣa samānaḥ sva pakṣa doṣaḥ pradhāna vādinaḥ hi niravayavam aparicchinnam śabda ādi hīnam pradhānam sa avayavasya paricchinnasya śabda ādimataḥ kāryasya kāraṇam iti sva pakṣaḥ
tatra api kṛtsna prasaktiḥ niravayava tvāt pradhānasya prāpnoti niravayava tva abhyupagama kopaḥ vā
nanu nā eva taiḥ niravayavam pradhānam abhyupagamyate
sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi hi trayaḥ guṇāḥ
teṣām sāmya avasthā pradhānam
taiḥ eva avayavaiḥ tat sāvayavam iti na evaṃjātīyakena sāvayava tvena prakṛtaḥ doṣaḥ parihartum pāryate yatas sattva rajaḥ tamasām api ekaikasya samānam niravayava tvam ekaikam eva ca itara dvaya anugṛhītam sajātīyasya prapañcasya upādānam iti samāna tvāt sva pakṣa doṣa prasaṅgasya
tarka apratiṣṭhānāt sāvayavatvam eva iti ced evam api anitya tva ādi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ
atha śaktayaḥ eva kārya vaicitrya sūcitāḥ avayavāḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tāḥ tu aviśiṣṭāḥ
tathā aṇu vādinaḥ u pi aṇuḥ aṇu antareṇa saṃyujyamānaḥ niravayava tvāt yadi kārtsnyena saṃyujyeta tatas prathima anupapatteḥ aṇu mātra tva prasaṅgaḥ
atha eka deśena saṃyujyeta tathā api niravayava tva abhyupagama kopaḥ iti sva pakṣe samānaḥ eṣa doṣaḥ
samāna tvāt ca na anyatarasmin eva pakṣe upakṣeptavyaḥ bhavati
parihṛtaḥ tu brahma vādinā sva pakṣe doṣaḥ
sarva upetā ca tad darśanāt
sarva upeta adhikaraṇam
ekasya api brahmaṇaḥ vicitra śakti yogāt upapadyate vicitraḥ vikāra prapañcaḥ iti uktam
tat punar katham avagamyate vicitra śakti yuktam param brahma iti
tat ucyate sarva upetā ca tad darśanāt
sarva śakti yuktā ca parā devatā iti abhyupagantavyam
kutas
tad darśanāt
tathā hi darśayati śrutiḥ sarva śakti yogam parasyāḥ devatāyāḥ sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ sarva rasaḥ sarvam idam abhyāttaḥ vāki anādaraḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ iti evaṃjātīyakā
vikaraṇa tvāt na iti ced tat uktam
syāt etat vikaraṇām parām devatām śāsti śāstram acakṣuṣkam aśrotram avāgamanāḥ iti evaṃjātīyakam
katham sā sarva śakti yuktā api satī kāryāya prabhavet
deva ādayaḥ hi cetanāḥ sarva śakti yuktāḥ api santaḥ ādhyātmika kārya karaṇa saṃpannāḥ eva tasmai tasmai kāryāya prabhavantaḥ vijñāyante
katham ca na iti na iti iti pratiṣiddha sarva viśeṣāyāḥ devatāyāḥ sarva śakti yogaḥ saṃbhavet iti ced yat atra vaktavyam tat purastāt eva uktam
śruti avagāhyam eva idam ati gambhīram brahma na tarka avagāhyam
na ca yathā ekasya sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam tathā anyasya api sāmarthyena bhavitavyam iti niyamaḥ u sti iti
pratiṣiddha sarve viśeṣasya api brahmaṇaḥ sarva śakti yogaḥ saṃbhavati iti etat api avidyā kalpita rūpa bheda upanyāsena uktam eva
tathā ca śāstram a pāṇi pādaḥ javanaḥ grahītā paśyati a cakṣuḥ sa śrṛṇoti a karṇaḥ iti brahmaṇaḥ sarva sāmarthya yogam darśayati
na prayojanavat tvāt
prayojanavat tva adhikaraṇam
anyathā punar cetana kartṛ tvam jagataḥ ākṣipati na khalu cetanaḥ paramātmā idam jagat bimbam viracayitum arhati
kutas
prayojanavat tvāt pravṛttīnām
cetanaḥ hi loke buddhi pūrva kārī puruṣaḥ pravartamānaḥ na manda upakramām api tāvat pravṛttim ātma prayojana anupayoginīm ārabhamāṇaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim uta gurutara saṃrambhām
bhavati ca loka prasiddhi anuvādinī śrutiḥ na vai are sarvasya kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati iti
gurutara saṃrambhā ca iyam pravṛttiḥ yat uccāvaca prapañcam jagat bimbam viracayitavyam
yadi iyam api pravṛttiḥ cetanasya paramātmanaḥ ātma prayojana upayoginī parikalpyeta paritṛpta tvam paramātmanaḥ śrūyamāṇam bādhyeta
prayojana abhāve vā pravṛtti abhāvaḥ syāt
atha san unmattaḥ buddhi aparādhāt antareṇa eva ātma prayojanam pravartamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā paramātmā api pravartiṣyate iti ucyeta tathā sati sarvajña tvam paramātmanaḥ śrūyamāṇam bādhyeta
tasmāt aśliṣṭā cetanāt sṛṣṭiḥ iti
loka vat tu līlā kaivalyam
tu śabdena ākṣepam pariharati
yathā loke kasyacid āpta eṣaṇasya rājñaḥ rāja amātyasya vā vyatiriktam kiṃcid prayojanam an abhisaṃdhāya kevalam līlā rūpāḥ pravṛttayaḥ krīḍā vihāreṣu bhavanti
yathā ca ucchvāsa praśvāsa ādayaḥ na abhisaṃdhāya bāhyam kiṃcid prayojanam svabhāvāt eva saṃbhavanti
evam īśvarasya api an apekṣya kiṃcid prayojana antaram svabhāvāt eva kevalam līlā rūpā pravṛttiḥ bhaviṣyati
na hi īśvarasya prayojana antaram nirūpyamāṇam nyāyataḥ śrutitaḥ vā saṃbhavati
na ca svabhāvaḥ paryanuyoktum śakyate
yadi api asmākam iyam jagat bimba viracanā gurutara saṃrambhā iva ābhāti tathā api parameśvarasya līlā eva kevalā iyam aparimita śakti tvāt
yadi nāma loke līlāsu api kiṃcid sūkṣmam prayojanam utprekṣyeta tathā api nā eva atra kiṃcid prayojanam utprekṣitum śakyate āpta kāma śruteḥ
na api apravṛttiḥ unmatta pravṛttiḥ vā sṛṣṭi śruteḥ sarvajña śruteḥ ca
na ca iyam parama artha viṣayā sṛṣṭi śrutiḥ
avidyā kalpita nāma rūpa vyavahāra gocara tvāt brahma ātma bhāva pratipādana para tvāt ca iti etat api nā eva vismartavyam
vaiṣamya nairghṛṇye na sāpekṣa tvāt tathā hi darśayati
vaiṣamya nairghṛṇya adhikaraṇam
punar ca jagat janma ādi hetu tvam īśvarasya ākṣipyate sthūṇā nikhanana nyāyena pratijñātasya arthasya dṛḍhīkaraṇāya
na īśvaraḥ jagataḥ kāraṇam upapadyate
kutas
vaiṣamya nairghṛṇya prasaṅgāt kāṃścid atyanta sukha bhājaḥ karoti deva ādīn kāṃścid atyanta duḥkha bhājaḥ paśu ādīn kāṃścid madhyama bhoga bhājaḥ manuṣya ādīn iti evam viṣamām sṛṣṭim nirmimāṇasya īśvarasya pṛthagjanasya iva rāga dveṣa upapatteḥ śruti smṛti avadhārita svaccha tvāt īśvara svabhāva vilopaḥ prasajyeta
tathā khala janaiḥ api jugupsitam nirghṛṇa tvam ati krūra tvam duḥkha yoga vidhānāt sarva prajā upasaṃhārāt ca prasajyeta
tasmāt vaiṣamya nairghṛṇya prasaṅgāt na īśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vaiṣamya nairghṛṇye na īśvarasya prasajyete
kasmāt
sāpekṣa tvāt
yadi hi nirapekṣaḥ kevalaḥ īśvaraḥ viṣamām sṛṣṭim nirmimīte syātām etau doṣau vaiṣamyam nairghṛṇyam ca
na tu nirapekṣasya nirmātṛ tvam asti
sāpekṣaḥ hi īśvaraḥ viṣamām sṛṣṭim nirmimīte
kim apekṣate iti ced dharma adharmau apekṣate iti vadāmaḥ
atas sṛjyamāna prāṇi dharma adharma apekṣā viṣamā sṛṣṭiḥ iti na ayam īśvarasya aparādhaḥ
īśvaraḥ tu parjanya vat draṣṭavyaḥ yathā hi parjanyaḥ vrīhi yava ādi sṛṣṭau sādhāraṇam kāraṇam bhavati vrīhi yava ādi vaiṣamye tu tad tad bīja gatāni eva asādhāraṇāni sāmarthyāni kāraṇāni bhavanti evam īśvaraḥ deva manuṣya ādi sṛṣṭau sādhāraṇam kāraṇam bhavati deva manuṣya ādi vaiṣamye tu tad tad jīva gatāni eva asādhāraṇāni karmāṇi kāraṇāni bhavanti
evam īśvaraḥ sāpekṣa tvāt na vaiṣamya nairghṛṇyābhyām duṣyati
katham punar avagamyate sa apekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ nīca madhyama uttamam saṃsāram nirmimīte iti
tathā hi darśayati śrutiḥ eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ unninīṣate eṣaḥ u eva asādhu karma kārayati tam yam adhas ninīṣate

na karma avibhāgāt iti ced na anādi tvāt
sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti prāk sṛṣṭeḥ avibhāga avadhāraṇāt na asti karma yat apekṣya viṣamā sṛṣṭiḥ syāt
sṛṣṭi uttara kālam hi śarīra ādi vibhāga apekṣam karma karma apekṣaḥ ca śarīra ādi vibhāgaḥ iti itaretara āśraya tvam prasajyeta
atas vibhāgāt ūrdhvam karma apekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ pravartatām nāma
prāk vibhāgāt vaicitrya nimittasya karmaṇaḥ bhāvāt tulyā eva ādyā sṛṣṭiḥ prāpnoti iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ
anādi tvāt saṃsārasya
bhavet eṣa doṣaḥ yadi ādimān ayam saṃsāraḥ syāt
anādau tu saṃsāre bīja aṅkura vat hetu hetumat bhāvena karmaṇaḥ sarga vaiṣamyasya ca pravṛttiḥ na virudhyate
katham punar avagamyate anādiḥ eṣa saṃsāraḥ iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
upapadyate ca api upalabhyate ca
upapadyate ca saṃsārasya anādi tvam ādimat tve hi saṃsārasya akasmāt udbhūteḥ muktānām api punar saṃsāra udbhūti prasaṅgaḥ akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśa prasaṅgaḥ ca sukha duḥkha ādi vaiṣamyasya nirnimitta tvāt
na ca īśvaraḥ vaiṣamya hetuḥ iti uktam
na ca avidyā kevalā vaiṣamyasya kāraṇam eka rūpa tvāt
rāga ādi kleśa vāsanā ākṣipta karma apekṣā tu avidyā vaiṣamya karī syāt
na ca karma antareṇa śarīram saṃbhavati na ca śarīram antareṇa karma saṃbhavati iti itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgaḥ
anādi tve tu bīja aṅkura nyāyena upapatteḥ na kaścid doṣaḥ bhavati
upalabhyate ca saṃsārasya anādi tvam śruti smṛtyoḥ

ādimattve tu prāk anavadhārita prāṇaḥ san katham prāṇa dhāraṇa nimittena jīva śabdena sarga pramukhe bhilapyeta

sarva dharma upapatteḥ ca
sarva dharma upapatti adhikaraṇam
cetanam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti asmin avadhārite veda arthe paraiḥ upakṣiptān vilakṣaṇa tva ādīn doṣān paryahārṣīt ācāryaḥ
idānīm parapakṣa pratiṣedha pradhānam prakaraṇam prāripsamāṇaḥ sva pakṣa parigraha pradhānam prakaraṇam upasaṃharati
yasmāt asmin brahmaṇi kāraṇe parigṛhyamāṇe pradarśitena prakāreṇa sarve kāraṇa dharmāḥ upapadyante sarvajñam sarva śakti mahā māyam ca brahma iti tasmāt an atiśaṅkanīyam idam aupaniṣadam darśanam iti
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ
dvitīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ
racanā anupapatteḥ ca na anumānam
racanā anupapatti adhikaraṇam
yadi api idam vedānta vākyānām aidaṃparyam nirūpayitum śāstram pravṛttam na tarka śāstra vat kevalābhiḥ yuktibhiḥ kaṃcid siddhāntam sādhayitum dūṣayitum vā pravṛttam
tathā api vedānta vākyāni vyācakṣāṇaiḥ samyak darśana pratipakṣa bhūtāni sāṃkhya ādi darśanāni nirākaraṇīyāni iti tad arthaḥ paraḥ pādaḥ pravartate
vedānta artha nirṇayasya ca samyak darśana artha tvāt tad nirṇayena sva pakṣa sthāpanam prathamam kṛtam tat vyabhyarhitam para pakṣa pratyākhyānāt iti
nanu mumukṣūṇām mokṣa sādhana tvena samyak darśana nirūpaṇāya sva pakṣa sthāpanam eva kevalam kartum yuktam kim para pakṣa nirākaraṇena para dveṣa karaṇena
bāḍham evam
tathā api mahājana parigṛhītāni mahānti sāṃkhya ādi tantrāṇi samyak darśana apadeśena pravṛttāni upalabhya bhavet keṣāṃcid manda matīnām etāni api samyak darśanāya upādeyāni iti apekṣā
tathā yukti gāḍha tva saṃbhavena sarvajña bhāṣita tvāt ca śraddhā ca teḥ iti atas tad asāra tā upapādanāya prayatyate

iti ca pūrvatra api sāṃkhya ādi pakṣa pratikṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ kim punar kṛata karaṇena iti
tat ucyate sāṃkhya ādayaḥ sva pakṣa sthāpanāya vedānta vākyāni api udāhṛtya sva pakṣa ānuguṇyena eva yojayantaḥ vyācakṣate teṣām yat vyākhyānam tat vyākhyāna ābhāsam na samyak vyākhyānam iti etāvat pūrvam kṛtam iha tu vākya nirapekṣaḥ svatantraḥ tad yukti pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate iti eṣa viśeṣaḥ
tatra sāṃkhyāḥ manyante yathā ghaṭa śarāva ādayaḥ bhedāḥ mṛd ātma tayā anvīyamānāḥ mṛd ātmaka sāmānya pūrvakāḥ loke dṛṣṭāḥ tathā sarve eva bāhya ādhyātmikāḥ bhedāḥ sukha duḥkha moha ātma tayā anvīyamānāḥ sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka sāmānya pūrvakāḥ bhavitum arhanti
yat sukha duḥkha moha ātmakam sāmānyam tat triguṇam pradhānam mṛd vat acetanam cetanasya puruṣasya artham sādhayitum svabhāvena eva vicitreṇa vikāra ātmanā pravartate iti
tathā parimāṇa ādibhiḥ api liṅgaiḥ tat eva pradhānam anumimate
tatra vadāmaḥ yadi dṛṣṭānta balena eva etat nirūpyeta na acetanam loke cetanā anadhiṣṭhitam svatantram kiṃcid viśiṣṭa puruṣa artha nirvartana samarthān vikārān viracayat dṛṣṭam
geha prāsāda śayana āsana vihāra bhūmi ādayaḥ hi loke prajñāvadbhiḥ śilpibhiḥ yathākālam sukha duḥkha prāpti parihāra yogyāḥ racitāḥ dṛśyante
tathā idam jagat akhilam pṛthivī ādi nānā karma phala upabhoga yogyam bāhyam ādhyātmikam ca śarīra ādi nānā jāti anvitam pratiniyata avayava vinyāsam aneka karma phala anubhava adhiṣṭhānam dṛśyamānam prajñāvadbhiḥ saṃbhāvitatamaiḥ śilpibhiḥ manasā api ālocayitum aśakyam sat katham acetanam pradhānam racayet
loṣṭa pāṣāṇa ādiṣu adṛṣṭa tvāt
mṛd ādiṣu api kumbhakāra ādi adhiṣṭhiteṣu viśiṣṭa ākārā racanā dṛśyate tadvat pradhānasya api cetanā antara dhiṣṭhita tva prasaṅgaḥ
na ca mṛd ādi upādāna svarūpa vyapāśrayeṇa eva dharmeṇa mūla kāraṇam avadhāraṇīyam na bāhya kumbhakāra ādi vyapāśrayeṇa iti kiṃcid niyāmakam asti
na ca evam sati kiṃcid virudhyate pratyuta śrutiḥ anugṛhyate cetana kāraṇa samarpaṇāt
atas racanā anupapatteḥ ca hetoḥ na acetanam jagat kāraṇam anumātavyam bhavati
anvaya ādi anupapatteḥ ca iti ca śabdena hetoḥ asiddhim samuccinoti
na hi bāhya ādhyātmikānām bhedānām sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tayā anvayaḥ upapadyate sukha ādīnām ca antara tva pratīteḥ śabda ādīnām ca a tad rūpa tva pratīteḥ tad nimitta tva pratīteḥ ca śabda ādi aviśeṣe ca bhāvanā viśeṣāt sukha ādi viśeṣa upalabdheḥ
tathā parimitānām bhedānām mūla aṅkura ādīnām saṃsarga pūrvaka tvam dṛṣṭvā bāhya ādhyātmikānām bhedānām parimita tvāt saṃsarga pūrvaka tvam anumimānasya sattva rajaḥ tamasām api saṃsarga pūrvaka tva prasaṅgaḥ parimita tva aviśeṣāt
kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tu prekṣā pūrvaka nirmitānām śayana āsana ādīnām dṛṣṭaḥ iti na kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt bāhya ādhyātmikānām bhedānām acetana pūrvaka tvam śakyam kalpayitum
pravṛtteḥ ca
āstām tāvat iyam racanā
tad siddhi arthāḥ yā pravṛttiḥ sāmya avasthānāt pracyutiḥ sattva rajaḥ tamasām aṅga aṅgi bhāva rūpa āpattiḥ viśiṣṭa kārya abhimukha pravṛtti tā sā api nā acetanasya pradhānasya svatantrasya upapadyate mṛd ādiṣu adarśanāt ratha ādiṣu ca
na hi mṛd ādayaḥ ratha ādayaḥ vā svayam acetanāḥ santaḥ cetanaiḥ kulāla ādibhiḥ aśva ādibhiḥ vā anadhiṣṭhitāḥ viśiṣṭa kārya abhimukha pravṛttayaḥ dṛśyante
dṛṣṭāt ca adṛṣṭa siddhiḥ
atas pravṛtti anupapatteḥ api hetoḥ na acetanam jagat kāraṇam anumātavyam bhavati
nanu cetanasya api pravṛttiḥ kevalasya na dṛṣṭā satyam etat tathā api cetana saṃyuktasya ratha ādeḥ acetanasya pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā
na tu acetana saṃyuktasya cetanasya pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā
kim punar atra yuktam yasmin pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā tasya sā uta yat saṃprayuktasya dṛṣṭā tasya eva sā iti
nanu yasmin dṛśyate pravṛttiḥ tasya eva sā iti yuktam ubhayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt
na tu pravṛtti āśraya tvena kevalaḥ cetanaḥ ratha ādi vat pratyakṣaḥ
pravṛtti āśraya deha ādi saṃyuktasya eva tu cetanasya sadbhāva siddhiḥ kevala acetana ratha ādi vailakṣaṇyam jīvat dehasya dṛṣṭam iti
atas eva ca pratyakṣe dehe sati caitanyasya darśanāt asati ca adarśanāt dehasya eva caitanyam api iti lokāyatikāḥ pratipannāḥ
tasmāt acetanasya eva pravṛttiḥ iti
tat abhidhīyate na brūmaḥ yasmin acetane pravṛttiḥ dṛśyate na tasya sā iti
bhavatu tasya eva sā
sā tu cetanāt bhavati iti brūmaḥ tad bhāve bhāvāt tad abhāve ca abhāvāt yathā kāṣṭha ādi vyapāśrayā api dāha prakāśa ādi lakṣaṇā vikriyā anupalabhyamānā api ca kevale jvalane jvalanāt eva bhavati tad saṃyoge darśanāt tad viyoge ca adarśanāt tadvat
lokāyatikānām api cetanaḥ eva cetanānām ratha ādīnām pravartakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti avipratiṣiddham cetanasya pravartaka tvam
nanu tava deha ādi saṃyuktasya api ātmanaḥ vijñāna sva rūpa mātra vyatirekeṇa pravṛtti anupapatteḥ anupapannam pravartaka tvam iti ced na
ayaskānta vat rūpa ādi vat ca pravṛtti rahitasya api pravartaka tva upapatteḥ
yathā ayaskāntaḥ maṇiḥ svayam pravṛtti rahitaḥ u pi ayasaḥ pravartakaḥ bhavati yathā ca rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ svayam pravṛtti rahitāḥ api cakṣuḥ ādīnām pravartakāḥ bhavanti evam pravṛtti rahitaḥ u pi īśvaraḥ sarva gataḥ sarva ātmā sarvajñaḥ sarva śaktiḥ ca san sarvam pravartayet iti upapannam
ekatvāt pravartya abhāve pravartaka tva anupapattiḥ iti ced na
avidyā pratyupasthāpita nāma rūpa māyā āveśa vaśena asakṛt pratyukta tvāt
tasmāt saṃbhavati pravṛttiḥ sarvajña kāraṇa tve na tu acetana kāraṇa tve
payaḥ mbu vat ced tatra api
syāt etat yathā kṣīram acetanam svabhāvena eva vatsa vivṛddhi artham pravartate yathā ca jalam acetanam svabhāvena eva loka upakārāya syandate evam pradhānam api acetanam svabhāvena eva puruṣa artha siddhaye pravartiṣyate iti
na etat sādhu ucyate yatas tatra api payaḥ mbunoḥ cetanā dhiṣṭhitayoḥ eva pravṛttiḥ iti anumimīmahe ubhaya vādi prasiddhe ratha ādau acetane kevale pravṛtti adarśanāt
śāstram ca yaḥ u psu tiṣṭhan yaḥ u paḥ ntaraḥ yamayati etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi prācyaḥ nyāḥ nadyaḥ syandante iti evaṃjātīyakam samastasya loka parispanditasya īśvara dhiṣṭhita tām śrāvayati
tasmāt sādhya pakṣa nikṣipta tvāt payaḥ mbu vat iti anupanyāsaḥ cetanāyāḥ ca dhenvāḥ sneha icchayā payasaḥ pravartaka tva upapatteḥ vatsa coṣaṇena ca payasaḥ ākṛṣyamāṇa tvāt
na ca ambunā u pi atyantam anapekṣā nimna bhūmi ādi apekṣa tvāt syandanasya
cetanā apekṣa tvam tu sarvatra upadarśitam
upasaṃhāra darśanāt na iti ced na kṣīravat hi iti atra tu bāhya nimitta nirapekṣam api sva āśrayam kāryam bhavati iti etat loka dṛṣṭyā nidarśitam
śāstra dṛṣṭyā punar sarvatra eva īśvara apekṣa tvam āpadyamānam na parāṇudyate
vyatireka anavasthiteḥ ca anapekṣa tvāt
sāṃkhyānām trayaḥ guṇāḥ sāmyena avatiṣṭhamānāḥ pradhānam
na tu tad vyatirekeṇa pradhānasya pravartakam nivartakam vā kiṃcid bāhyam apekṣyam avasthitam asti
puruṣaḥ tu udāsīnaḥ na pravartakaḥ na nivartakaḥ iti atas napekṣam pradhānam
anapekṣa tvāt ca kadācid pradhānam mahat ādi ākāreṇa pariṇamate kadācid na pariṇamate iti etat ayuktam
īśvarasya tu sarvajña tvāt sarva śakti tvāt mahāmāya tvāt ca pravṛtti apravṛttī na virudhyete
anyatra abhāvāt ca ca tṛṇa ādi vat
syāt etat yathā tṛṇa pallava udaka ādi nimitta antara nirapekṣam svabhāvāt eva kṣīra ādi ākāreṇa pariṇamate evam pradhānam api mahat ādi ākāreṇa pariṇaṃsyate iti
katham ca nimitta antara nirapekṣam tṛṇa ādi iti gamyate
nimitta antara anupalambhāt
yadi hi kiṃcid nimitta antaram upalabhemahi tatas yathākāmam tena tena nimittena tṛṇa ādi upādāya kṣīram saṃpādayemahi
na tu saṃpādayāmahe
tasmāt svābhāvikaḥ tṛṇa ādeḥ pariṇāmaḥ
tathā pradhānasya api syāt iti
atrā ucyate bhavet tṛṇa ādi vat svābhāvikaḥ pradhānasya api pariṇāmaḥ yadi tṛṇa ādeḥ api svābhāvikaḥ pariṇāmaḥ bhyupagamyeta
na tu abhyupagamyate nimitta antara upalabdheḥ
katham nimitta antara upalabdhiḥ
anyatra abhāvāt
dhenvā eva hi upabhuktam tṛṇa ādi kṣīrībhavati na prahīṇam anaḍuha ādi upabhuktam vā
yadi hi nirnimittam etat syāt dhenu śarīra saṃbandhāt anyatra api tṛṇa ādi kṣīrībhavet
na ca yathākāmam mānuṣaiḥ na śakyam saṃpādayitum iti etāvatā nirnimittam bhavati
bhavati hi kiṃcid kāryam mānuṣa saṃpādyam kiṃcid daiva saṃpādyam manuṣyāḥ api śaknuvanti eva svocitena upāyena tṛṇa ādi upādāya kṣīram saṃpādayitum
prabhūtam hi kṣīram kāmayamānāḥ prabhūtam ghāsam dhenum cārayanti
tatas ca prabhūtam kṣīram labhante
tasmāt na tṛṇa ādi vat svābhāvikaḥ pradhānasya pariṇāmaḥ
abhyupagame pi artha abhāvāt
svābhāvikī pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ na bhavati iti sthāpitam
atha api nāma bhavataḥ śraddhām anurudhyamānāḥ svābhāvikīm eva pradhānasya pravṛttim abhyupagacchema tathā api doṣaḥ nuṣajyeta eva
kutas
artha abhāvāt
yadi tāvat svābhāvikī pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ na kiṃcid anyat iha apekṣate iti ucyeta tatas yathā eva sahakāri kiṃcid na apekṣate evam prayojanam api kiṃcid na apekṣiṣyate iti atas pradhānam puruṣasya artham sādhayitum pravartate iti iyam pratijñā hīyeta
sa yadi brūyāt sahakārī eva kevalam na apekṣate na prayojanam api iti
tathā api pradhāna pravṛtteḥ prayojanam vivektavyam bhogaḥ vā syāt apavargaḥ vā ubhayam vā iti
bhogaḥ ced kīdṛśaḥ na ādheya atiśayasya puruṣasya bhogaḥ bhavet
anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca
apavargaḥ ced prāk api pravṛtteḥ apavargasya siddha tvāt pravṛttiḥ anarthikā syāt śabda ādi anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ ca
ubhaya arthatā abhyupagame pi bhoktavyānām pradhāna mātrāṇām ānantyāt anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ eva
na ca autsukya nivṛtti arthā pravṛttiḥ
na hi pradhānasya acetanasya autsukyam saṃbhavati
na ca puruṣasya nirmalasya
dṛkśakti sarga śakti vaiyarthya bhayāt ced pravṛttiḥ tarhi dṛkśakti anuccheda vat sarga śakti anucchedāt saṃsāra anucchedāt anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ eva
tasmāt pradhānasya puruṣa arthā pravṛttiḥ iti etat ayuktam
puruṣa aśma vat iti ced tathā pi
syāt etat yathā kaścid puruṣaḥ dṛkśakti saṃpannaḥ pravṛtti śakti vihīnaḥ paṅguḥ aparam puruṣam pravṛtti śakti saṃpannam dṛkśakti vihīnam andham adhiṣṭhāya pravartayati yathā vā ayaskāntaḥ śmā svayam a pravartamānaḥ pi ayaḥ pravartayati evam puruṣaḥ pradhānam pravartayiṣyati iti dṛṣṭānta pratyayena punar pratyavasthānam
atrā ucyate tathā api nā eva doṣāt nirmokṣaḥ sti
abhyupeta hānam tāvat doṣaḥ āpatati pradhānasya svatantrasya pravṛtti abhyupagamāt puruṣasya ca pravartaka tva anabhyupagamāt
katham ca udāsīnaḥ puruṣaḥ pradhānam pravartayet
paṅguḥ api hi andham puruṣam vāc ādibhiḥ pravartayati
na evam puruṣasya kaścid api pravartana vyāpāraḥ sti niṣkriya tvāt nirguṇa tvāt ca
na api ayaskānta vat saṃnidhi mātreṇa pravartayet saṃnidhi nitya tvena pravṛtti nitya tva prasaṅgāt
ayaskāntasya tu anitya saṃnidheḥ asti sva vyāpāraḥ saṃnidhiḥ parimārjana ādi apekṣā ca asya asti iti anupanyāsaḥ puruṣa aśma vat iti
tathā pradhānasya acaitanyāt puruṣasya ca audāsīnyāt tṛtīyasya ca tayoḥ saṃbandhayituḥ abhāvāt saṃbandha anupapattiḥ
yogyatā nimitte ca saṃbandhe yogyatā anucchedāt anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ
pūrvavat ca iha api artha abhāvaḥ vikalpayitavyaḥ
paramātmanaḥ tu svarūpa vyapāśrayam audāsīnyam māyā vyapāśrayam ca pravartaka tvam iti asti atiśayaḥ
aṅgi tva anupapatteḥ ca
itas ca na pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ avakalpate yat hi sattva rajaḥ tamasām anyonya guṇa pradhāna bhāvam utsṛjya sāmyena sva rūpa mātreṇa avasthānam sā pradhāna avasthā
tasyām avasthāyām anapekṣa svarūpāṇām sva rūpa praṇāśa bhayāt parasparam pratyaṅga aṅgi bhāva anupapatteḥ bāhyasya ca kasyacid kṣobhayituḥ abhāvāt guṇa vaiṣamya nimittaḥ mahat ādi utpādaḥ na syāt
anyathā numitau ca jña śakti viyogāt
atha api syāt anyathā vayam anumimīmahe yathā na ayam anantaraḥ doṣaḥ prasajyeta
na hi anapekṣa svabhāvāḥ kūṭasthāḥ ca asmābhiḥ guṇāḥ abhyupagamyante pramāṇa abhāvāt
kārya vaśena tu guṇānām svabhāvaḥ bhyupagamyate
yathā yathā kārya utpādaḥ upapadyate tathā tathā eteṣām svabhāvaḥ bhyupagantavyaḥ
calam cala SNNe guṇa Cp vṛttam SNPaNe
iti ca asti abhyupagamaḥ
tasmāt sāmya avasthāyām api vaiṣamya upagama yogyāḥ eva guṇāḥ avatiṣṭhante iti
evam api pradhānasya jña śakti viyogāt racanā anupapatti ādayaḥ pūrva uktāḥ doṣāḥ tad avasthāḥ eva
jña śaktim api tu anumimānaḥ prativādi tvāt nivarteta cetanam ekam aneka prapañcasya jagataḥ upādānam iti brahma vāda prasaṅgāt
vaiṣamya upagama yogyāḥ api guṇāḥ sāmya avasthāyām nimitta abhāvāt nā eva vaiṣamyam bhajeran bhajamānāḥ vā nimitta abhāva aviśeṣāt sarvadā eva vaiṣamyam bhajeran iti prasajyate eva ayam doṣaḥ
vipratiṣedhāt ca asamañjasam
paraspara viruddhaḥ ca ayam sāṃkhyānām abhyupagamaḥ kvacid sapta indriyāṇi anukrāmanti kvacid ekādaśa
tathā kvacid mahataḥ tanmātra sargam upadiśanti kvacid ahaṃkārāt
tathā kvacid trīṇi antaḥkaraṇāni varṇayanti kvacid ekam iti
prasiddhaḥ eva tu śrutyā īśvara kāraṇa vādinyāḥ virodhaḥ tad anuvartinyā ca smṛtyā
tasmāt api asamañjasam sāṃkhyānām darśanam iti
atra āha nanu aupaniṣadānām api asamañjasam eva darśanam tapya tāpakayoḥ jāti antara bhāva anabhyupagamāt
ekam hi brahma sarva ātmakam sarvasya prapañcasya kāraṇam abhyupagacchatām ekasya eva ātmanaḥ viśeṣau tapya tāpakau na jāti antara bhūtau iti abhyupagantavyam syāt
yadi ca etau tapya tāpakau ekasya ātmanaḥ viśeṣau syātām sa tābhyām tapya tāpakābhyām na nirmucyeta iti tāpa upaśāntaye samyak darśanam upadiśat śāstram anarthakam syāt
na hi auṣṇya prakāśa dharmasya pradīpasya tad avasthasya eva tābhyām nirmokṣaḥ upapadyate
yaḥ pi jala taraṅga vīcī phena ādi upanyāsaḥ tatra api jala ātmanaḥ ekasya vīci ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāva rūpeṇa nityāḥ eva iti samānaḥ jala ātmanaḥ vīci ādibhiḥ anirmokṣaḥ
prasiddhaḥ ca ayam tapya tāpakayoḥ jāti antara bhāvaḥ loke
tathā hi arthī ca arthaḥ ca anyonya bhinnau lakṣyete
yadi arthinaḥ svatas nyaḥ rthaḥ na syāt yasya arthinaḥ yad viṣayam arthi tvam sa tasya arthaḥ nitya siddhaḥ eva iti na tasya tad viṣayam arthi tvam syāt yathā prakāśa ātmanaḥ pradīpasya prakāśa ākhyaḥ rthaḥ nitya siddhaḥ eva iti na tasya tad viṣayam arthi tvam bhavati aprāpte hi arthe rthinaḥ rthi tvam syāt iti
tathā arthasya api artha tvam na syāt
yadi syāt svārtha tvam eva syāt
na ca etat asti
saṃbandhi śabdau hi etau arthī ca arthaḥ ca iti
dvayoḥ ca saṃbandhinoḥ saṃbandhaḥ syāt na ekasya eva
tasmāt bhinnau etau artha arthinau
tathā anartha anarthinau api
arthinaḥ nukūlaḥ arthaḥ pratikūlaḥ anarthaḥ
tābhyām ekaḥ paryāyeṇa ubhābhyām saṃbadhyate
tatra arthasya alpīyaḥ tvāt bhūyaḥ tvāt ca anarthasya ubhau api artha anarthau anarthaḥ eva iti tāpakaḥ saḥ ucyate
tapyaḥ tu puruṣaḥ yaḥ ekaḥ paryāyeṇa ubhābhyām saṃbadhyate iti tayoḥ tapya tāpakayoḥ eka ātmatāyām mokṣa anupapattiḥ
jāti antara bhāve tu tad saṃyoga hetu parihārāt syāt api kadācid mokṣa upapattiḥ iti
atrā ucyate na eka tvāt eva tapya tāpaka bhāva anupapatteḥ bhavet eṣa doṣaḥ yadi eka ātma tāyām tapya tāpakau anyonyasya viṣaya viṣayi bhāvam pratipadyeyātām
na tu etat asti ekatvāt eva
na hi agniḥ ekaḥ san svam ātmānam dahati prakāśayati vā sati api auṣṇya prakāśa ādi dharma bhede pariṇāmi tve ca
kim u kūṭasthe brahmaṇi ekasmin tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ saṃbhavet
kva punar ayam tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ syāt iti
ucyate kim na paśyasi karma bhūtaḥ jīvat dehaḥ tapyaḥ tāpakaḥ savitā iti
nanu taptiḥ nāma duḥkham
sā cetayituḥ
na acetanasya dehasya
yadi hi dehasya eva taptiḥ syāt sā deha nāśe svayam eva naśyati iti tad nāśāya sādhanam nā eṣitavyam syāt iti
ucyate deha abhāve pi kevalasya cetanasya taptiḥ na dṛṣṭā
na ca tvayā api taptiḥ nāma vikriyā cetayituḥ kevalasya iṣyate
nā api deha cetanayoḥ saṃhata tvam aśuddhi ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt
na ca tapteḥ eva taptim abhyupagacchasi
katham tava api tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ
sattvam tapyam tāpakam rajaḥ iti ced na
tābhyām cetanasya saṃhata tva anupapatteḥ
sattva anurodhi tvāt cetanā u pi tapyate iva iti ced paramārthataḥ tarhi nā eva tapyate iti āpatati iva śabda prayogāt
na ced tapyate na iva śabdaḥ doṣāya
na hi ḍuṇḍubhaḥ sarpaḥ iva iti etāvatā sa viṣaḥ bhavati sarpaḥ vai ḍuṇḍubha sarpaḥ iva iti etāvatā nirviṣaḥ bhavati
atas ca avidyā kṛtaḥ yam tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ na pāramārthikaḥ iti abhyupagantavyam iti na evam sati mama api kiṃcid duṣyati
atha pāramārthikam eva cetanasya tapya tvam abhyupagacchasi tava eva sutarām anirmokṣaḥ prasajyeta nitya tva abhyupagamāt ca tāpakasya
tapya tāpaka śaktyoḥ nitya tve pi sa nimitta saṃyoga apekṣa tvāt tapteḥ saṃyoga nimitta adarśana nivṛttau ātyantikaḥ saṃyoga uparamaḥ tatas ca ātyantikaḥ mokṣaḥ upapannaḥ iti ced na
adarśanasya tamasaḥ nitya tva abhyupagamāt
guṇānām ca udbhava abhibhavayoḥ aniyata tvāt aniyataḥ saṃyoga nimitta uparamaḥ iti viyogasya api aniyata tvāt sāṃkhyasya eva anirmokṣaḥ parihāryaḥ syāt
aupaniṣadasya tu ātma eka tva abhyupagamāt ekasya ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāva anupapatteḥ vikāra bhedasya ca vācā ārambhaṇa mātra tva śravaṇāt anirmokṣa śaṅkā svapne na upajāyante
vyavahāre tu yatra yathā dṛṣṭaḥ tapya tāpaka bhāvaḥ tatra tathā eva saḥ iti na codayitavyaḥ parihartavyaḥ vā bhavati
pradhāna kāraṇa vādaḥ nirākṛtaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ idānīm nirākartavyaḥ
tatra ādau tāvat yaḥ ṇu vādinā brahma vādini doṣaḥ utprekṣyate sa pratisamādhīyate
tatra ayam vaiśeṣikāṇām abhyupagamaḥ kāraṇa dravya samavāyinaḥ guṇāḥ kārya dravye samāna jātīyam guṇa antaram ārabhante śuklebhyaḥ tantubhyaḥ śuklasya paṭasya prasava darśanāt tad viparyaya adarśanāt ca
tasmāt cetanasya brahmaṇaḥ jagat kāraṇatve bhyupagamyamāne kārye jagati caitanyam samaveyāt
tad adarśanāt tu na cetanam brahma jagat kāraṇam bhavitum arhati iti
imam abhyupagamam tadīyayā eva prakriyayā vyabhicārayati
mahat dīrgha vat vā hrasva parimaṇḍalābhyām
mahat dīrgha adhikaraṇam
eṣā teṣām prakriyā paramāṇavaḥ kila kaṃcid kālam anārabdha kāryāḥ yathāyogam rūpa ādimantaḥ pārimāṇḍalya parimāṇāḥ ca tiṣṭhanti
te ca paścāt adṛṣṭa ādi puraḥsarāḥ saṃyoga sacivāḥ ca santaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa kṛtsnam kārya jātam ārabhante kāraṇa guṇāḥ ca kārye guṇa antaram
yadā dvau paramāṇū dvyaṇukam ārabhete tadā paramāṇu gatāḥ rūpa ādi guṇa viśeṣāḥ śukla ādayaḥ dvyaṇuke śukla ādīn aparān ārabhante
paramāṇu guṇa viśeṣaḥ tu pārimāṇḍalyam na dvyaṇuke pārimāṇḍalyam aparam ārabhate dvyaṇukasya parimāṇa antara yoga abhyupagamāt
aṇu tva hrasva tve hi dvi aṇuka vartinī parimāṇe varṇayanti
yadā api dve dvi aṇuke catur aṇukam ārabhete tadā api samānam dvi aṇuka samavāyinām śukla ādīnām ārambhaka tvam
aṇu tva hrasva tve tu dvyaṇuka samavāyinī api na eva ārabhete catur aṇukasya mahat tva dīrgha tva parimāṇa yoga abhyupagamāt
yadā api bahavaḥ paramāṇavaḥ bahūni vā dvyaṇukāni dvyaṇuka sahitaḥ vā paramāṇuḥ kāryam ārabhate tadā api samānā eṣā yojanā
tat evam yathā paramāṇoḥ parimaṇḍalāt sataḥ hrasvam ca dvyaṇukam jāyate mahat dīrgham ca tryaṇuka ādi na parimaṇḍalam
yathā vā dvi aṇukāt aṇoḥ hrasvāt ca sataḥ mahat dīrgham ca tryaṇukam jāyate na aṇu no hrasvam
evam cetanāt brahmaṇaḥ cetanam jagat janiṣyate iti abhyupagame kim tava chinnam
atha manyase virodhinā parimāṇa antareṇa ākrāntam kārya dravyam dvi aṇuka ādi iti atas na ārambhakāṇi kāraṇa gatāni pārimāṇḍalī ādīni iti abhyupagacchāmi
na tu cetanā virodhinā guṇa antareṇa jagataḥ ākrānta tvam asti yena kāraṇa gatā cetanā kārye cetanā antaram na ārabheta
na hi acetanā nāma cetanā virodhī kaścid guṇaḥ sti cetanā pratiṣedha mātra tvāt
tasmāt pārimāṇḍalya ādi vaiṣamyāt prāpnoti cetanāyāḥ ārambhaka tvam iti
mā evam maṃsthāḥ yathā kāraṇe vidyamānānām api pārimāṇḍalī ādīnām anārambhaka tvam evam caitanyasya api iti asya aṃśasya samāna tvāt
na ca parimāṇa antara ākrānta tvam pārimāṇḍalī ādīnām anārambhaka tve kāraṇam prāk parimāṇa antara ārambhāt pārimāṇḍalī ādīnām ārambhaka tva upapatteḥ ārabdham api kārya dravyam prāk guṇa ārambhāt kṣaṇa mātram aguṇam tiṣṭhati iti abhyupagamāt
na ca parimāṇa antara ārambhe vyagrāṇi pārimāṇḍalī ādīni iti atas sva samāna jātīyam parimāṇa antaram na ārabhante parimāṇa antarasya anya hetu tva abhyupagamāt
kāraṇa bahu tvāt kāraṇa mahā tvāt pracaya viśeṣāt ca mahat tad viparītam aṇu etena dīrgha tva hrasva tve vyākhyāte iti hi kāṇabhujāni sūtrāṇi
na ca saṃnidhāna viśeṣāt kutaścid kāraṇa bahu tva ādīni eva ārabhante na pārimāṇḍalya ādīni iti ucyeta dravya antare guṇa antare vā ārabhyamāṇe sarveṣām eva kāraṇa guṇānām sva āśraya samavāya aviśeṣāt
tasmāt svabhāvāt eva pārimāṇḍalī ādīnām anārambhaka tvam tathā cetanāyāḥ api iti draṣṭavyam
saṃyogāt ca dravya ādīnām vilakṣaṇānām utpatti darśanāt samāna jātīya utpatti vyabhicāraḥ
dravye prakṛte guṇa udāharaṇam ayuktam iti ced na
dṛṣṭāntena vilakṣaṇa ārambha mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt
na ca dravyasya dravyam eva udāhartavyam guṇasya vā guṇaḥ eva iti kaścid niyame hetuḥ asti
sūtrakāraḥ pi bhavatām dravyasya guṇam udājahāra pratyakṣa apratyakṣāṇām apratyakṣa tvāt saṃyogasya pañca ātmakam na vidyate
Candrānand iti yathā pratyakṣa apratyakṣayoḥ bhūmi ākāśayoḥ samavayan saṃyogo pratyakṣaḥ evam pratyakṣa apratyakṣeṣu pañcasu bhūteṣu samavayat śarīram apratyakṣam syāt
pratyakṣam hi śarīram tasmāt na pāñcabhautikam iti etat uktam bhavati guṇaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ dravyam śarīram
dṛśyate tu iti ca atra api vilakṣaṇa utpattiḥ prapañcitā
nanu evam sati tena eva etat gatam
na iti brūmaḥ tat sāṃkhyam pratyuktam etat tu vaiśeṣikam prati
nanu atideśaḥ api samāna nyāya tayā kṛtaḥ etena śiṣṭa aparigrahāḥ api vyākhyātāḥ iti
satyam etat
tasya eva tu ayam vaiśeṣika parīkṣā ārambhe tat prakriyā anugatena nidarśanena prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ
ubhayathā na karma atas tad abhāvaḥ
paramāṇu jagat akāraṇa tva adhikaraṇam
idānīm paramāṇu kāraṇa vādam nirākaroti
sa ca vādaḥ ittham samuttiṣṭhati paṭa ādīni hi loke sa avayavāni dravyāṇi sva anugataiḥ eva saṃyoga sacivaiḥ tantu ādibhiḥ dravyaiḥ ārabhyamāṇāni dṛṣṭāni
tad sāmānyena yāvat kiṃcid sa avayavam tat sarvam sva anugataiḥ eva saṃyoga sacivaiḥ taiḥ taiḥ dravyaiḥ ārabdham iti gamyate
sa ca ayam avayava avayavi vibhāgaḥ yatas nivartate saḥ upakarṣa paryanta gataḥ paramāṇuḥ
sarvam ca idam giri samudra ādikam jagat sa avayavam
sa a vaya tvāt ca ādi anta vat
na ca akāraṇena kāryeṇa bhavitavyam iti atas paramāṇavaḥ jagataḥ kāraṇam iti kaṇabhuj abhiprāyaḥ
tāni imāni catvāri bhūtāni bhūmi udaka tejaḥ pavana ākhyāni sa avayavāni upalabhya caturvidhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ parikalpyante
teṣām ca apakarṣa paryanta gata tvena paratas vibhāga asaṃbhavāt vinaśyatām pṛthivī ādīnām paramāṇu paryantaḥ vibhāgaḥ bhavati
sa pralaya kālaḥ
tatas sarga kāle ca vāyavīyeṣu aṇuṣu adṛṣṭa apekṣam karma utpadyate
tat karma sva āśrayam aṇum aṇu antareṇa saṃyunakti
tatas dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa vāyuḥ utpadyate
evam agniḥ
evam āpaḥ
evam pṛthivī
evam eva śarīram sa indriyam iti evam sarvam idam jagat aṇubhyaḥ saṃbhavati
aṇu gatebhyaḥ ca rūpa ādibhyaḥ dvyaṇuka ādi gatāni rūpa ādīni saṃbhavanti tantu paṭa nyāyena iti kāṇādāḥ manyante
tatra idam abhidhīyate vibhāga avasthānām tāvat aṇūnām saṃyogaḥ karma apekṣaḥ bhyupagantavyaḥ karmavatām tantu ādīnām saṃyoga darśanāt
karmaṇaḥ ca kārya tvāt nimittam kim api abhyupagantavyam
an abhyupagame nimitta abhāvāt na aṇuṣu ādyam karma syāt
abhyupagame yadi prayatnaḥ bhighāta ādiḥ vā yathā dṛṣṭam kim api karmaṇaḥ nimittam abhyupagamyeta tasya asaṃbhavāt na eva aṇuṣu ādyam karma syāt
na hi tasyām avasthāyām ātma guṇaḥ prayatnaḥ saṃbhavati śarīra abhāvāt
śarīra pratiṣṭhe hi manasi ātmanaḥ saṃyoge sati ātma guṇaḥ prayatnaḥ jāyate
etena abhighāta ādi api dṛṣṭam nimittam pratyākhyātavyam
sarga uttara kālam hi tat sarvam na ādyasya karmaṇaḥ nimittam saṃbhavati
atha adṛṣṭam ādyasya karmaṇaḥ nimittam iti ucyeta tat punar ātma samavāyi vā syāt
aṇu samavāyi vā
ubhayathā api na adṛṣṭa nimittam aṇuṣu karma avakalpeta adṛṣṭasya acetana tvāt
na hi acetanam cetanena anadhiṣṭhitam svatantram pravartate pravartayati vā iti sāṃkhya parīkṣāyām abhihitam
ātmanaḥ ca anutpanna caitanyasya tasyām avasthāyām acetana tvāt
ātma samavāyi tva abhyupagamāt ca na adṛṣṭam aṇuṣu karmaṇaḥ nimittam syāt asaṃbandhāt
a dṛṣṭavatā puruṣeṇa asti aṇūnām saṃbandhaḥ iti ced saṃbandha sātatyāt pravṛtti sātatya prasaṅgaḥ niyāmaka antara abhāvāt
tat evam niyatasya kasyacid karma nimittasya abhāvāt na aṇuṣu ādyam karma syāt
karma abhāvāt tad nibandhanaḥ saṃyogaḥ na syāt
saṃyoga abhāvāt ca tad nibandhanam dvi auṇaka ādi kārya jātam na syāt
saṃyogaḥ ca aṇoḥ aṇu antareṇa sarva ātmanā vā syāt
eka deśena vā
sarva ātmanā ced upacaya anupapatteḥ aṇu mātra tva prasaṅgaḥ dṛṣṭa viparyaya prasaṅgaḥ ca pradeśavataḥ dravyasya pradeśavatā dravya antareṇa saṃyogasya dṛṣṭa tvāt
eka deśena ced sāvayava tva prasaṅgaḥ
paramāṇūnām kalpitāḥ pradeśāḥ syuḥ iti ced kalpitānām avastu tvāt avastu eva saṃyogaḥ iti vastunaḥ kāryasya asamavāyi kāraṇam na syāt
asati ca asamavāyi kāraṇe dvi aṇuka ādi kārya dravyam na utpadyeta
yathā ca ādisarge nimitta abhāvāt saṃyoga utpatti artham karma na aṇūnām saṃbhavati evam mahāpralaye pi vibhāga utpatti artham karma na eva aṇūnām saṃbhavet
na hi tatra api kiṃcid niyatam tad nimittam dṛṣṭam asti
adṛṣṭam api bhoga prasiddhi artham na pralaya prasiddhi artham iti atas nimitta abhāvāt na syāt aṇūnām saṃyoga utpatti artham vibhāga utpatti artham vā karma
atas ca saṃyoga vibhāga abhāvāt tad āyattayoḥ sarga pralayayoḥ abhāvaḥ prasajyeta
tasmāt anupapannaḥ yam paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ
samavāya abhyupagamāt ca sāmyāt anavasthiteḥ
samavāya abhyupagamāt ca tad abhāvaḥ iti prakṛtena aṇu vāda nirākaraṇena saṃbadhyate
dvābhyām ca aṇubhyām dvyaṇukam utpadyamānam atyanta bhinnam aṇubhyām aṇvoḥ samavaiti iti abhyupagamyate bhavatā
na ca evam abhyupagacchatā śakyate ṇu kāraṇa tā samarthayitum
kutas
sāmyāt anavasthiteḥ yathā eva hi aṇubhyām atyanta bhinnam sat dvyaṇukam samavāya lakṣaṇena saṃbandhena tābhyām saṃbadhyate evam samavāyaḥ api samavāyibhyaḥ tyanta bhinnaḥ san samavāya lakṣaṇena anyena eva saṃbandhena samavāyibhiḥ saṃbadhyeta atyanta bheda sāmyāt
tatas ca tasya tasya anyaḥ nyaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ iti anavasthā eva prasajyeta
nanu iha pratyaya grāhyaḥ samavāyaḥ nitya saṃbaddhaḥ eva samavāyibhiḥ gṛhyate na asaṃbaddhaḥ saṃbandha antara apekṣaḥ vā
tatas ca na tasya anyaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ yena anavasthā prasajyeta iti
na iti ucyate
saṃyogaḥ pi evam sati saṃyogibhiḥ nitya saṃbaddhaḥ eva iti samavāya vat na anyam saṃbandham apekṣeta
atha artha antara tvāt saṃyogaḥ saṃbandha antaram apekṣeta samavāyaḥ u pi tarhi artha antara tvāt saṃbandha antaram apekṣeta
na ca guṇa tvāt saṃyogaḥ saṃbandha antaram apekṣate na samavāyaḥ aguṇa tvāt iti yujyate vaktum
apekṣā kāraṇasya tulya tvāt guṇa paribhāṣāyāḥ ca atantra tvāt
tasmāt artha antaram samavāyam abhyupagacchataḥ prasajyeta eva anavasthā
prasajyamānāyām ca anavasthāyām eka asiddhau sarva asiddheḥ dvābhyām aṇubhyām dvyaṇukam na eva utpadyeta
tasmāt api anupapannaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ
nityam eva ca bhāvāt
api ca aṇavaḥ pravṛtti svabhāvāḥ vā nivṛtti svabhāvāḥ vā ubhaya svabhāvāḥ vā anubhaya svabhāvāḥ vā abhyupagamyante gati antara abhāvāt
caturdhā api nā upapadyate pravṛtti svabhāva tve nityam eva pravṛtteḥ bhāvāt pralaya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ
nivṛtti svabhāva tve pi nityam eva nivṛtteḥ bhāvāt sarga abhāva prasaṅgaḥ
ubhaya svabhāva tvam ca virodhāt asamañjasam
anubhaya svabhāva tve tu nimitta vaśāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ abhyupagamyamānayoḥ adṛṣṭa ādeḥ nimittasya nitya saṃnidhānāt nitya pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ atantra tve pi adṛṣṭa ādeḥ nitya apravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ
tasmāt api anupapannaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ
rūpa ādimat tvāt ca viparyayaḥ darśanāt
sa avayavānām dravyāṇām avayavaśas vibhajyamānānām yatas paraḥ vibhāgaḥ na saṃbhavati te caturvidhāḥ rūpa ādimantaḥ paramāṇavaḥ caturvidhasya rūpa ādimataḥ bhūta bhautikasya ārambhakāḥ nityāḥ ca iti yat vaiśeṣikāḥ abhyupagacchanti sa teṣām abhyupagamaḥ nirālambanaḥ eva
yatas rūpa ādimat tvāt paramāṇūnām aṇu tva nitya tva viparyayaḥ prasajyeta
parama kāraṇa apekṣayā sthūla tvam anitya tvam ca teṣām abhipreta viparītam āpadyeta iti arthaḥ
kutas
evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt yat hi loke rūpa ādimat vastu tat sva kāraṇa apekṣayā sthūlam anityam ca dṛṣṭam
tat yathā paṭaḥ tantūn apekṣya sthūlaḥ nityaḥ ca bhavati
tantavaḥ ca aṃśūn apekṣya sthūlāḥ anityāḥ ca bhavanti tathā ca amī paramāṇavaḥ rūpa ādimantaḥ taiḥ abhyupagamyante
tasmāt te pi kāraṇavantaḥ tad apekṣayā sthūlāḥ anityāḥ ca prāpnuvanti
yat ca nitya tve kāraṇam taiḥ uktam sat akāraṇavat nityam iti tat api evam sati aṇuṣu na saṃbhavati uktena prakāreṇa aṇūnām api kāraṇavat tva upapatteḥ
yat api nitya tve dvitīyam kāraṇam uktam anityam iti ca viśeṣataḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ iti tat api na avaśyam paramāṇūnām nitya tvam sādhayati
asati hi yasmin kasmin cit nitye vastuni nitya śabdena nañaḥ samāsaḥ nā upapadyate
na punar paramāṇu nitya tvam eva apekṣyate
tat ca asti eva nityam parama kāraṇam brahma
na ca śabda artha vyavahāra mātreṇa kasyacid arthasya prasiddhiḥ bhavati pramāṇa antara siddhayoḥ śabda arthayoḥ vyavahāra avatārāt
yat api nitya tve tṛtīyam kāraṇam uktam avidyā ca iti tat yadi evam satām paridṛśyamāna kāryāṇām kāraṇānām pratyakṣeṇa agrahaṇam avidyā iti tatas dvi aṇuka nitya tā api āpadyeta
atha a dravya tve sati iti viśeṣyeta tathā api akāraṇavat tvam eva nitya tā nimittam āpadyeta tasya ca prāk eva ukta tvāt avidyā ca iti punaruktam syāt
atha api kāraṇa vibhāgāt kāraṇa vināśāt ca anyasya tṛtīyasya vināśa hetoḥ asaṃbhavaḥ vidyā sā paramāṇūnām nitya tvam khyāpayati iti vyākhyāyeta na avaśyam vinaśyat vastu dvābhyām eva hetubhyām vinaṣṭum arhati iti
saṃyoga sacive hi anekasmin ca dravye dravya antarasya ārambhake bhyupagamyamāne etat evam syāt
yadā tu apāsta viśeṣam sāmānya ātmakam kāraṇam viśeṣa vat avasthā antaram āpadyamānam ārambhakam abhyupagamyate tadā ghṛta kāṭhinya vilayana vat mūrti avasthā vilayanena api vināśaḥ upapadyate
tasmāt rūpa ādimat tvāt syāt abhipreta viparyayaḥ paramāṇūnām
tasmāt api anupapannaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ
ubhayathā ca doṣāt
gandha rasa rūpa sparśa guṇā sthūlā pṛthivī rūpa rasa sparśa guṇāḥ sūkṣmāḥ āpaḥ rūpa sparśa guṇam sūkṣmataram tejaḥ sparśa guṇaḥ sūkṣmatamaḥ vāyuḥ iti evam etāni catvāri bhūtāni upacita apacita guṇāni sthūla sūkṣma sūkṣmatara sūkṣmatama tāratamya upetāni ca loke lakṣyante
tadvat paramāṇavaḥ pi upacita apacita guṇāḥ kalperan na vā
ubhayathā api ca doṣa anuṣaṅgaḥ parihāryaḥ eva syāt
kalpyamāne tāvat upacita apacita guṇa tve upacita guṇānām mūrti upacayāt aparamāṇu tva prasaṅgaḥ
na ca antareṇa api mūrti upacayam guṇa upacayaḥ bhavati iti ucyeta kāryeṣu bhūteṣu guṇa upacaye mūrti upacaya darśanāt
a kalpyamāne tu upacita apacita guṇa tve paramāṇu tva sāmya prasiddhaye yadi tāvat sarve ekaika guṇāḥ eva kalpyeran tatas tejasi sparśasya upalabdhiḥ na syāt apsu rūpa sparśayoḥ pṛthivyām ca rasa rūpa sparśānām kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvāt kārya guṇānām
atha sarve caturguṇāḥ eva kalpyeran tatas u psu api gandhasya upalabdhiḥ syāt tejasi gandha rasayoḥ vāyau ca gandha rūpa rasānām
na ca evam dṛśyate
tasmāt api anupapannaḥ paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ
aparigrahāt ca atyantam anapekṣā
pradhāna kāraṇa vādaḥ veda vidbhiḥ api kaiścid manu ādibhiḥ satkārya tva ādi aṃśa upajīvana abhiprāyeṇa upanibaddhaḥ
ayam tu paramāṇu kāraṇa vādaḥ na kaiścid api śiṣṭaiḥ kenacid api aṃśena parigṛhītaḥ iti atyantam eva an ādaraṇīyaḥ veda vādibhiḥ
api ca vaiśeṣikāḥ tantra artha bhūtān ṣaṣ padārthān dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya ākhyān atyanta bhinnān bhinna lakṣaṇān abhyupagacchanti yathā śvas śaśaḥ iti
tathātvam ca abhyupagamya tad viruddham dravya adhīna tvam śeṣāṇām abhyupagacchanti
tat na upapadyate
katham
yathā hi loke śaśa kuśa palāśa prabhṛtīnām atyanta bhinnānām satām na itaretara adhīna tvam bhavati evam dravya ādīnām api atyanta bhinna tvāt na eva dravya adhīna tvam guṇa ādīnām bhavitum arhati
atha bhavati dravya adhīna tvam guṇa ādīnām tatas dravya bhāve bhāvāt dravya abhāve bhāvāt dravyam eva saṃsthāna ādi bhedāt aneka śabda pratyaya bhāj bhavati yathā devadattaḥ ekaḥ eva san avasthā antara yogāt aneka śabda pratyaya bhāj bhavati tadvat
tathā sati sāṃkhya siddhānta prasaṅgaḥ sva siddhānta virodhaḥ ca āpadyeyātām
nanu agneḥ anyasya api sataḥ dhūmasya agni adhīna tvam dṛśyate
satyam dṛśyate
bheda pratīteḥ tu tatra agni dhūmayoḥ anya tvam niścīyate
iha tu śuklaḥ kambalaḥ rohiṇī dhenuḥ nīlam utpalam iti dravyasya eva tasya tasya tena tena viśeṣaṇena pratīyamāna tvāt na eva dravya guṇayoḥ agni dhūmayoḥ iva bheda pratītiḥ asti
tasmāt dravya ātmaka tā guṇasya
etena karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām dravya ātmaka tā vyākhyātā
guṇānām dravya adhīna tvam dravya guṇayoḥ ayuta siddha tvāt iti yadi ucyeta tat punar ayuta siddha tvam apṛthak deśa tvam vā syāt apṛthak kāla tvam vā apṛthak svabhāva tvam vā
sarvathā api na upapadyate
apṛthak deśa tve tāvat sva abhyupagamaḥ virudhyeta
katham
tantu ārabdhaḥ hi paṭaḥ tantu deśaḥ bhyupagamyate na paṭa deśaḥ
paṭasya tu guṇāḥ śukla tva ādayaḥ paṭa deśāḥ abhyupagamyante na tantu deśāḥ
tathā ca āhuḥ dravyāṇi dravya antaram ārabhante guṇāḥ ca guṇa antaram
iti
tantavaḥ hi kāraṇa dravyāṇi kārya dravyam paṭam ārabhante tantu gatāḥ ca guṇāḥ śukla ādayaḥ kārya dravye paṭe śukla ādi guṇa antaram ārabhante iti hi te bhyupagacchanti
saḥ bhyupagamaḥ dravya guṇayoḥ apṛthak deśa tve bhyupagamyamāne bādhyeta
atha apṛthak kāla tvam ayuta siddha tvam ucyeta savya dakṣiṇayoḥ api go viṣāṇayoḥ ayuta siddha tvam prasajyeta
tathā apṛthak svabhāva tve tu ayuta siddha tve na dravya guṇayoḥ ātma bhedaḥ saṃbhavati tasya tādātmyena eva pratīyamāna tvāt
yuta siddhayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃyogaḥ ayuta siddhayoḥ tu samavāyaḥ iti ayam abhyupagamaḥ mṛṣā eva teṣām prāk siddhasya kāryāt kāraṇasya ayuta siddha tva anupapatteḥ
atha anyatara apekṣaḥ eva ayam abhyupagamaḥ syāt ayuta siddhasya kāryasya kāraṇena saṃbandhaḥ samavāyaḥ iti evam api prāk asiddhasya alabdha ātmakasya kāryasya kāraṇena saṃbandhaḥ na upapadyate dvaya āyatta tvāt saṃbandhasya
siddham bhūtvā saṃbadhyate iti ced prāk kāraṇa saṃbandhāt kāryasya siddhau abhyupagamyamānāyām ayuta siddhi abhāvāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ saṃyoga vibhāgau na vidyete DuPr3InPv
oḥ iti idam uktam duruktam syāt
yathā ca utpanna mātrasya akriyasya kārya dravyasya vibhubhiḥ ākāśa ādibhiḥ dravya antaraiḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃyogaḥ eva abhyupagamyate na samavāyaḥ evam kāraṇa dravyeṇa api saṃbandhaḥ saṃyogaḥ eva syāt na samavāyaḥ
nā api saṃyogasya samavāyasya vā saṃbandhasya saṃbandhi vyatirekeṇa astitve kiṃcid pramāṇam asti
saṃbandhi śabda pratyaya vyatirekeṇa saṃyoga samavāya śabda pratyaya darśanāt tayoḥ astitvam iti ced na
eka tve pi svarūpa bāhya rūpa apekṣayā aneka śabda pratyaya darśanāt
yathā ekaḥ pi san devadattaḥ loke sva rūpam saṃbandhi rūpam ca apekṣya aneka śabda pratyaya bhāj bhavati manuṣyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ śrotriyaḥ vadānyaḥ bālaḥ yuvā sthaviraḥ pitā putraḥ pautraḥ bhrātā jāmātā iti yathā ca ekā api satī rekhā sthāna anya tvena niviśamānā eka daśa śata sahasra ādi śabda pratyaya bhedam anubhavati tathā saṃbandhinoḥ eva saṃbandhi śabda pratyaya vyatirekeṇa saṃyoga samavāya śabda pratyaya arha tvam na vyatirikta vastu as
nā api saṃbandhi viṣaya tve saṃbandha śabda pratyayayoḥ saṃtata bhāva prasaṅgaḥ
svarūpa bāhya rūpa apekṣayā iti ukta uttara tvāt
tathā aṇu ātma manasām apradeśa tvāt na saṃyogaḥ saṃbhavati pradeśavataḥ dravyasya pradeśavatā dravya antareṇa saṃyoga darśanāt
kalpitāḥ pradeśāḥ aṇu ātma manasām bhaviṣyanti iti ced na
avidyamāna artha kalpanāyām sarva artha siddhi prasaṅgāt iyān eva avidyamānaḥ viruddhaḥ viruddhaḥ vā arthaḥ kalpanīyaḥ na atas dhikaḥ iti niyama hetu abhāvāt kalpanāyāḥ ca sva āyatta tvāt prabhūta tva saṃbhavāt ca na ca vaiśeṣikaiḥ kalpitebhyaḥ ṣaḍbhyaḥ padārthebhyaḥ nye dhikāḥ śatam sahasram vā arthāḥ na kalpayitavyāḥ iti nivārakaḥ hetuḥ asti
tasmāt yasmai yasmai yat yat rocate tat tat sidhyet
kaścid kṛpāluḥ prāṇinām duḥkha bahulaḥ saṃsāraḥ eva mā bhūt iti kalpayet
anyaḥ vā vyasanī muktānām api punar utpattim kalpayet
kaḥ tayoḥ nivārakaḥ syāt
kiṃca anyat dvābhyām paramāṇubhyām niravayavābhyām sa avayavasya dvyaṇukasya ākāśena iva saṃśleṣa anupapattiḥ
na hi ākāśasya pṛthivī ādīnām ca jatu kāṣṭha vat saṃśleṣaḥ sti
kārya kāraṇa dravyayoḥ āśrita āśraya bhāvaḥ nyathā na upapadyate iti avaśyam kalpyaḥ samavāyaḥ iti ced na
itaretara āśraya tvāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ hi bheda siddhau āśrita āśraya bhāva siddhiḥ āśrita āśraya bhāva siddhau ca tayoḥ bheda siddhiḥ kuṇḍa badara vat iti itaretara āśraya tā syāt
na hi kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhedaḥ āśrita āśraya bhāvaḥ vā vedāntavādibhiḥ abhyupagamyate kāraṇasya eva saṃsthāna mātram kāryam iti abhyupagamāt
kiṃca anyat paramāṇūnām paricchinna tvāt yāvatyaḥ diśaḥ ṣaḍ aṣṭau daśa vā tāvadbhiḥ avayavaiḥ sa avayavāḥ te syuḥ sāvayava tvāt anityāḥ ca iti nitya tva niravayava tva abhyupagamaḥ bādhyeta
yān tvam diś bheda bhedinaḥ vayavān kalpayasi te eva paramāṇavaḥ iti ced na
sthūla sūkṣma tāratamya krameṇa parama kāraṇāt vināśa upapatteḥ yathā pṛthivī dvyaṇuka ādi apekṣayā sthūlatamā vastu bhūtā api vinaśyati tatas sūkṣmam sūkṣmataram ca pṛthivī eka jātīyakam vinaśyati tatas dvyaṇukam tathā paramāṇavaḥ pi pṛthivī eka jātīyaka tvāt vinaśyeyuḥ
vinaśyantaḥ api avayava vibhāgena eva vinaśyanti iti ced na ayam doṣaḥ
yatas ghṛta kāṭhinya vilayana vat api vināśa upapattim avocāma yathā hi ghṛta suvarṇa ādīnām avibhajyamāna avayavānām api agni saṃyogāt drava bhāva āpattyā kāṭhinya vināśaḥ bhavati evam paramāṇūnām api parama kāraṇa bhāva āpattyā mūrti ādi vināśaḥ bhaviṣyati
tathā kārya ārambhaḥ u pi na avayava saṃyogena eva kevalena bhavati kṣīra jala ādīnām antareṇa api avayava saṃyoga antaram dadhi hima ādi kārya ārambha darśanāt
tat evam asāratara tarka saṃdṛbdha tvāt īśvara kāraṇa śruti viruddha tvāt śruti pravaṇaiḥ ca śiṣṭaiḥ manu ādibhiḥ a parigṛhīta tvāt atyantam eva anapekṣā asmin paramāṇu kāraṇa vāde kāryā āryaiḥ śreyaḥ orthibhiḥ iti vākyaśeṣaḥ
samudāye ubhaya hetuke tad aprāptiḥ
samudāya adhikaraṇam
vaiśeṣika rāddhāntaḥ duryukti yogāt veda virodhāt śiṣṭa aparigrahāt ca na apekṣitavyaḥ iti uktam
saḥ ūrdhva vaināśikaḥ iti vaināśika tva sāmyāt sarva vaināśika rāddhāntaḥ natarām apekṣitavyaḥ iti idam idānīm upapādayāmaḥ
sa ca bahu prakāraḥ pratipatti bhedāt vineya bhedāt vā
tatra ete trayaḥ vādinaḥ bhavanti kecid sarva astitva vādinaḥ
kecid vijñāna astitva mātra vādinaḥ
anye punar sarva śūnyatva vādinaḥ iti
tatra ye sarva astitva vādinaḥ bāhyam āntaram ca vastu abhyupagacchanti bhūtam bhautikam ca cittam caittam ca tān tāvat pratibrūmaḥ
tatra bhūtam pṛthivī dhātu ādayaḥ bhautikam rūpa ādayaḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ ca catuṣṭaye ca pṛthivī ādi paramāṇavaḥ khara sneha uṣṇa īraṇa svabhāvāḥ te pṛthivī ādi bhāvena saṃhanyante iti manyante
tathā rūpa vijñāna vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra saṃjñakāḥ pañca kandhāḥ te pi ādhyātmam sarva vyavahāra āspada bhāvena saṃhanyante iti manyante
tatra idam abhidhīyate yaḥ yam ubhaya hetukaḥ ubhaya prakāraḥ samudāyaḥ pareṣām abhipretaḥ aṇu hetukaḥ ca bhūta bhautika saṃhati rūpaḥ skandha hetukaḥ ca pañca skandhī rūpaḥ tasmin ubhaya hetuke samudāye bhipreyamāṇe tad aprāptiḥ syāt samudāya aprāptiḥ samudāya bhāva anupapattiḥ iti arthaḥ
kutas
samudāyinām acetana tvāt citta abhijvalanasya ca samudāya siddhi adhīna tvāt anyasya ca kasyacid cetanasya bhoktuḥ praśāsituḥ vā sthirasya saṃhantuḥ anabhyupagamāt nirapekṣa pravṛtti abhyupagame ca pravṛtti anuparama prasaṅgāt āśayasya api anyatva ananyatvābhyām anirūpya tvāt kṣaṇikatva abhyupagamāt ca nirvyāpāra tvāt pravṛtti anupapatteḥ
tasmāt samudāya anupapattiḥ
samudāya anupapattau ca tad āśrayā lokayātrā lupyeta
itaretara pratyaya tvāt iti ced na utpatti mātra nimitta tvāt
yadi api bhoktā praśāsitā vā kaścid cetanaḥ saṃhantā sthiraḥ nā abhyupagamyate tathā api avidyā ādīnām itaretara kāraṇa tvāt upapadyate lokayātrā
tasyām ca upapadyamānāyām na kiṃcid aparam apekṣitavyam asti
te ca avidyā ādayaḥ avidyā saṃskāraḥ vijñānam nāma rūpam ṣaṣ āyatanam sparśaḥ vedanā tṛṣṇā upādānam bhavaḥ jātiḥ jarā maraṇam śokaḥ paridevanā duḥkham durmanas tā iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ itaretara hetukāḥ saugate samaye kvacid saṃkṣiptāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ kvacid prapañcitāḥ
sarveṣām api ayam pratyākhyeyaḥ
tat evam avidyā ādi kalāpe paraspara nimitta naimittika bhāvena ghaṭīyantra vat aniśam āvartamāne rtha ākṣiptaḥ upapannaḥ saṃghātaḥ iti ced tat na
kasmāt
utpatti mātra nimitta tvāt bhavet upapannaḥ saṃghātaḥ yadi saṃghātasya kiṃcid nimittam avagamyeta
na tu avagamyate
yatas itaretara pratyaya tve pi avidyā ādīnām pūrva pūrvam uttara uttarasya utpatti mātra nimittam bhavat bhavet na tu saṃghāta utpatteḥ kiṃcid nimittam saṃbhavati
nanu avidyā ādibhiḥ arthāt ākṣipyate saṃghātaḥ iti uktam
atrā ucyate yadi tāvat ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā ādayaḥ saṃghātam antareṇa ātmānam alabhamānāḥ apekṣante saṃghātam iti tatas tasya saṃghātasya kiṃcid nimittam vaktavyam
tat ca nityeṣu api aṇuṣu abhyugamyamāneṣu āśraya āśrayi bhūteṣu ca bhoktṛṣu satsu na saṃbhavati iti uktam vaiśeṣika parīkṣāyām
kim aṅga punar kṣaṇikeṣu api aṇuṣu bhoktṛ rahiteṣu āśraya āśrayi śūnyeṣu vā abhyupagamyamāneṣu saṃbhavet
atha ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā ādayaḥ eva saṃghātasya nimittam iti katham tam eva āśritya ātmānam labhamānāḥ tasya eva nimittam syuḥ
atha manyase saṃghātāḥ eva anādau saṃsāre saṃtatya anuvartante tad āśrayāḥ ca avidyā ādayaḥ iti tadā api saṃghātāt saṃghāta antaram utpadyamānam niyamena vā sadṛśam eva utpadyeta aniyamena vā sadṛśam visadṛśam vā utpadyeta
niyama abhyupagame manuṣya pudgalasya deva tiryagyoni nāraka prāpti abhāvaḥ prāpnuyāt
aniyama abhyupagame manuṣya pudgalaḥ kadācid kṣaṇena hastī bhūtvā devaḥ vā punar manuṣyaḥ vā bhavet iti prāpnuyāt
ubhayam api abhyupagama viruddham
api ca yad bhoga arthaḥ saṃghātaḥ syāt sa jīvaḥ nā asti sthiraḥ bhoktā iti tava abhyupagamaḥ
tatas ca bhogaḥ bhoga arthaḥ eva sa na anyena prārthanīyaḥ
tathā mokṣaḥ mokṣa arthaḥ eva iti mumukṣuṇā na anyena bhavitavyam
anyena ced prārthyeta ubhayam bhoga mokṣa kāla avasthāyinā tena bhavitavyam

tasmāt itaretara utpatti mātra nimitta tvam avidyā ādīnām yadi bhavet bhavatu nāma
na tu saṃghātaḥ sidhyet bhoktṛ abhāvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ
uttara utpāde ca pūrva nirodhāt
uktam etat avidyā ādīnām utpatti mātra nimitta tvāt na saṃghāta siddhiḥ asti iti
tat api tu utpatti mātra nimitta tvam na saṃbhavati iti idam idānīm upapādyate
kṣaṇabhaṅga vādinaḥ yam abhyupagamaḥ uttarasmin kṣaṇe utpadyamāne pūrvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ nirudhyate iti
na ca evam abhyupagacchatā pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ hetu phala bhāvaḥ śakyate saṃpādayitum nirudhyamānasya niruddhasya vā pūrva kṣaṇasya abhāva grasta tvāt uttara kṣaṇa hetu tva anupapatteḥ
atha bhāva bhūtaḥ pariniṣpanna avasthaḥ pūrva kṣaṇaḥ uttara kṣaṇasya hetuḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā api nā upapadyate bhāva bhūtasya punar vyāpāra kalpanāyām kṣaṇa antara saṃbandha prasaṅgāt
atha bhāvaḥ eva asya vyāpāraḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā api nā evā upapadyate hetu svabhāva an uparaktasya phalasya utpatti asaṃbhavāt
svabhāva uparāga abhyupagame ca hetu svabhāvasya phala kāla avasthāyi tve sati kṣaṇa bhaṅga abhyupagama tyāga prasaṅgaḥ
vinā eva vā svabhāva uparāgeṇa hetu phala bhāvam abhyupagacchataḥ sarvatra tad prāpteḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ
api ca utpāda nirodhau nāma vastunaḥ svarūpam eva vā syātām avasthā antaram vā vastu antaram eva vā sarvathā api nā upapadyate
yadi tāvat vastunaḥ svarūpam eva utpāda nirodhau syātām tatas vastu śabdaḥ utpāda nirodha śabdau ca paryāyāḥ prāpnuyuḥ
atha asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti manyeta utpāda nirodha śabdābhyām madhya vartinaḥ vastunaḥ ādi anta ākhye avasthe abhilapyete iti evam api ādi anta madhya kṣaṇa traya saṃbandhi tvāt vastunaḥ kṣaṇika tva abhyupagama hāniḥ
atha atyanta vyatiriktau evā utpāda nirodhau vastunaḥ syātām aśva mahiṣa vat tatas vastu utpāda nirodhābhyām a saṃspṛṣṭam iti vastunaḥ śāśvata tva prasaṅgaḥ
yadi ca darśana adarśane vastunaḥ utpāda nirodhau syātām evam api draṣṭṛ dharmau tau na vastu dharmau iti vastunaḥ śāśvata tva prasaṅgaḥ eva
tasmāt api asaṃgatam saugatam matam
asati pratijñā uparodhaḥ yaugapadyam anyathā
kṣaṇabhaṅga vāde pūrva kṣaṇaḥ nirodha grasta tvāt na uttarasya kṣaṇasya hetuḥ bhavati iti uktam
