atha asati eva hetau phala utpattim brūyāt tatas pratijñā uparodhaḥ syāt caturvidhān hetūn pratītya citta caittāḥ utpadyante iti iyam pratijñā hīyeta
nirhetukāyām ca utpattau apratibandhāt sarvam sarvatra utpadyeta
atha uttara kṣaṇa utpattiḥ yāvat tāvat avatiṣṭhate pūrva kṣaṇe iti brūyāt tatas yaugapadyam hetu phalayoḥ syāt
tathā api pratijñā uparodhaḥ eva syāt kṣaṇikāḥ sarve saṃskārāḥ iti iyam pratijñā uparudhyeta
pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā nirodha aprāptiḥ avicchedāt
api ca vaināśikāḥ kalpayanti buddhi bodhyam trayāt anyat saṃskṛtam kṣaṇikam ca iti
tat api ca trayam pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā nirodhau ākāśam ca iti ācakṣate
trayam api ca etat avastu abhāva mātram nirupākhyam iti manyante
buddhi pūrvakaḥ kila vināśaḥ bhāvānām pratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ nāma bhāṣyate
tad viparītaḥ pratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ
āvaraṇa abhāva mātram ākāśam iti
teṣām ākāśam parastāt pratyākhyāsyati
nirodha dvayam idānīm pratyācaṣṭe pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā nirodhayoḥ aprāptiḥ asaṃbhavaḥ iti arthaḥ
kasmāt
avicchedāt etau hi pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā nirodhau saṃtāna gocarau vā syātām bhāva gocarau vā
na tāvat saṃtāna gocarau saṃbhavataḥ sarveṣu api saṃtāneṣu saṃtāninām avicchinnena hetu phala bhāvena saṃtāna vicchedasya asaṃbhavāt
na api bhāva gocarau saṃbhavataḥ na hi bhāvānām niranvayaḥ nirupākhyaḥ vināśaḥ saṃbhavati sarvāsu api avasthāsu pratyabhijñāna balena anvayi aviccheda darśanāt aspaṣṭa pratyabhijñānāsu api avasthāsu kvacid dṛṣṭena anvayi avicchedena anyatra api tad anumānāt
tasmāt para parikalpitasya nirodha dvayasya anupapattiḥ
ubhayathā ca doṣāt
yaḥ yama vidyā ādi nirodhaḥ pratisaṃkhyā nirodha antaḥpātī para parikalpitaḥ sa samyak jñānāt vā sa parikarāt syāt
svayam eva vā pūrvasmin vikalpe nirhetuka vināśa abhyupagama hāni prasaṅgaḥ
uttarasmin tu mārga upadeśa ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ
evam ubhayathā api doṣa prasaṅgāt asamañjasam idam darśanam
ākāśe ca aviśeṣāt
yat ca teṣām eva abhipretam nirodha dvayam ākāśam ca nirupākhyam iti tatra nirodha dvayasya nirupākhya tvam purastāt nirākṛtam
ākāśasya idānīm nirākriyate
ākāśe ca ayuktaḥ nirupākhya tva abhyupagamaḥ pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā nirodhayoḥ iva vastu tva pratipatteḥ aviśeṣāt
āgama prāmāṇyāt tāvat ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ākāśasya ca vastu tva prasiddhiḥ
vipratipannān prati tu śabda guṇa anumeya tvam vaktavyam gandha ādīnām guṇānām pṛthivī ādi vastu āśraya tva darśanāt
api ca āvaraṇa abhāva mātram ākāśam icchatām ekasmin suparṇe patati āvaraṇasya vidyamāna tvāt suparṇa antarasya utpitsataḥ na avakāśa tva prasaṅgaḥ
yatra āvaraṇa abhāvaḥ tatra patiṣyati iti ced yena āvaraṇa abhāvaḥ viśeṣyate tat tarhi vastu bhūtam eva ākāśam syāt na āvaraṇa abhāva mātram
api ca āvaraṇa abhāva mātram ākaśam manyamānasya saugatasya sva abhyupagama virodhaḥ prasajyeta
saugate hi samaye pṛthivī bhagavan kiṃsaṃniśrayā iti asmin praśna prativacana pravāhe pṛthivī ādīnām ante vāyuḥ kiṃsaṃniśrayaḥ iti asya praśnasya prativacanam bhavati vāyuḥ ākāśa saṃniśrayaḥ iti
tat ākāśasya a vastu tve na samañjasam syāt
tasmāt api ayuktam ākāśasya avastu tvam
api ca nirodha dvayam ākāśam ca trayam api etat nirupākhyam avastu nityam ca iti vipratiṣiddham
na hi avastunaḥ nitya tvam anitya tvam vā saṃbhavati vastu āśraya tvāt dharma dharmi vyavahārasya
dharma dharmi bhāve hi ghaṭa ādi vat vastu tvam eva syāt na nirupākhya tvam
anusmṛteḥ ca
api ca vaināśikaḥ sarvasya vastunaḥ kṣaṇikatām abhyupayan upalabdhuḥ api kṣaṇikatām abhyupeyāt
na ca sā saṃbhavati
anusmṛteḥ anubhavam upalabdhim anūtpadyamānam smaraṇam eva anusmṛtiḥ
sā ca upalabdhi eka kartṛkā satī saṃbhavati puruṣa antara upalabdhi viṣaye puruṣa antarasya smṛti adarśanāt
katham hi aham adaḥ drākṣam idam idānīm paśyāmi iti ca pūrva uttara darśini ekasmin asati pratyayaḥ syāt
api ca darśana smaraṇayoḥ kartari ekasmin pratyakṣaḥ pratyabhijñā pratyayaḥ sarvasya lokasya prasiddhaḥ aham adaḥ drākṣam idam paśyāmi iti
yadi hi tayoḥ bhinnaḥ kartā syāt tatas aham smarāmi adrākṣīt anyaḥ iti pratīyāt
na tu evam pratyeti kaścid
yatra evam pratyayaḥ tatra darśana smaraṇayoḥ bhinnam eva kartāram sarva lokaḥ vagacchati smarāmi aham asau adaḥ drākṣīt iti
iha tu aham adaḥ drākṣam iti darśana smaraṇayoḥ vaināśikaḥ pi ātmānam eva ekam kartāram avagacchati
na na aham iti ātmanaḥ darśanam nirvṛttam nihnute yathā agniḥ an uṣṇaḥ prakāśaḥ iti vā
tatra evam sati ekasya darśana smaraṇa lakṣaṇa kṣaṇa dvaya saṃbandhe kṣaṇikatva abhyupagama hāniḥ aparihāryā vaināśikasya syāt
tathā anantarām anantarām ātmanaḥ eva pratipattim pratyabhijānan eka kartṛkām ā uttamāt ucchvāsāt atītāḥ ca pratipattīḥ janmanaḥ ātma eka kartṛkāḥ pratisaṃdadhānaḥ katham kṣaṇabhaṅga vādī vaināśikaḥ na apatrapeta
sa yadi brūyāt sādṛśyāt etat saṃpatsyate iti tam pratibrūyāt tena idam sadṛśam iti dvaya āyatta tvāt sādṛśyasya kṣaṇabhaṅga vādinaḥ sadṛśayoḥ dvayoḥ vastunoḥ grahītuḥ ekasya abhāvāt sādṛśya nimittam pratisaṃdhānam iti mithyāpralāpaḥ eva syāt
syāt ced pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ sādṛśyasya grahītā ekaḥ tathā sati ekasya kṣaṇa dvaya avasthānāt kṣaṇika tva pratijñā pīḍyeta
tena idam sadṛśam iti pratyaya antaram eva idam na pūrva uttara kṣaṇa dvaya grahaṇa nimittam iti ced na
tena idam iti bhinna padārtha upādānāt
pratyaya antaram eva ced sādṛśya viṣayam syāt tena idam sadṛśam iti vākya prayogaḥ narthakaḥ syāt sādṛśyam iti eva prayogaḥ prāpnuyāt
yadā hi loke prasiddhaḥ padārthaḥ parīkṣakaiḥ na parigṛhyate tadā sva pakṣa siddhiḥ para pakṣa doṣaḥ vā ubhayam api ucyamānam parīkṣakāṇām ātmanaḥ ca yathārtha tvena na buddhi saṃtānam ārohati
evam eva eṣaḥ rthaḥ iti niścitam yat tat eva vaktavyam
tatas bahu pralāpi tvam ātmanaḥ kevalam prakhyāpayet
na ca ayam sādṛśyāt saṃvyavahāraḥ yuktaḥ
tad bhāva avagamāt tad sadṛśa bhāva anavagamāt ca
bhavet api kadācid bāhya vastuni vipralambha saṃbhavāt tat eva idam syāt tat sadṛśam vā iti saṃdehaḥ
upalabdhari tu na kadācid bhavati saḥ eva aham syām tad sadṛśaḥ vā iti yaḥ eva aham pūrvedyus adrākṣam saḥ eva aham adya smarāmi iti niścita tad bhāva upalambhāt
tasmāt api anupapannaḥ vaināśika samayaḥ
na asataḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt
itas ca anupapannaḥ vaināśika samayaḥ yatas sthiram anuyāyi kāraṇam an abhyupagacchatām abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ iti etat āpadyeta
darśayanti ca abhāvāt bhāva utpattim na an upamṛdya prādurbhāvāt iti
vinaṣṭāt hi kila bījāt aṅkuraḥ utpadyate tathā vinaṣṭāt kṣīrāt dadhi mṛd piṇḍāt ca ghaṭaḥ
kūṭasthāt ced kāraṇāt kāryam utpadyeta aviśeṣāt sarvam sarvatas utpadyeta
tasmāt abhāva grastebhyaḥ bīja ādibhyaḥ ṅkura ādīnām utpadyamāna tvāt abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ iti manyante
tatra idam ucyate na asataḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt iti
na abhāvāt bhāvaḥ utpadyate
yadi abhāvāt bhāvaḥ utpadyeta abhāva tva aviśeṣāt kāraṇa viśeṣa abhyupagamaḥ narthakaḥ syāt
na hi bīja ādīnām upamṛditānām yaḥ bhāvaḥ tasya abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇa ādīnām ca niḥsvabhāva tva aviśeṣāt abhāva tve kaścid viśeṣaḥ sti
yena bījāt eva aṅkuraḥ jāyate kṣīrāt eva dadhi iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ kāraṇa viśeṣa abhyupagamaḥ rthavān syāt
nirviśeṣasya tu abhāvasya kāraṇa tva abhyupagame śaśaviṣāṇa ādibhyaḥ pi aṅkura ādayaḥ jāyeran
na ca evam dṛśyate
yadi punar abhāvasya api viśeṣaḥ bhyupagamyeta utpala ādīnām iva nīla tva ādiḥ tatas viśeṣavat tvāt eva abhāvasya bhāva tvam utpala ādi vat prasajyeta
nā api abhāvaḥ kasyacid utpatti hetuḥ syāt abhāva tvāt eva śaśaviṣāṇa ādi vat
abhāvāt ca bhāva utpattau abhāva anvitam eva sarvam kāryam syāt
na ca evam dṛśyate sarvasya ca vastunaḥ svena svena rūpeṇa bhāva ātmanā eva upalabhyamāna tvāt
na ca mṛd anvitāḥ śarāva ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ tantu ādi vikārāḥ kenacid abhyupagamyante
mṛd vikārān eva tu mṛd anvitān bhāvān lokaḥ pratyeti
yat tu uktam sva rūpa upamardam antareṇa kasyacid kūṭasthasya vastunaḥ kāraṇa tva anupapatteḥ abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ bhavitum arhati iti tat duruktam sthira svabhāvānām eva suvarṇa ādīnām pratyabhijñāyamānānām rucaka ādi kāraṇa bhāva darśanāt
yeṣu api bīja ādiṣu sva rūpa upamardaḥ lakṣyate teṣu api na asau upamṛdyamānā pūrva avasthā uttara avasthāyāḥ kāraṇam abhyupagamyate an upamṛdyamānānām eva anuyāyinām bīja ādi avayavānām aṅkura ādi kāraṇa bhāva abhyupagamāt
tasmāt asadbhyaḥ śaśaviṣāṇa ādibhyaḥ sat utpatti adarśanāt sadbhyaḥ ca suvarṇa ādibhyaḥ sat utpatti darśanāt anupapannaḥ yam abhāvāt bhāva utpatti abhyupagamaḥ
api ca caturbhiḥ citta caittāḥ utpadyante paramāṇubhyaḥ ca bhūta bhautika lakṣaṇaḥ samudāyaḥ utpadyate iti abhyupagamya punar abhāvāt bhāva utpattim kalpayadbhiḥ abhyupagamam apahnuvānaiḥ vaināśikaiḥ sarvaḥ lokaḥ ākulīkriyate
udīsīnānām api ca evam siddhiḥ
yadi ca abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ abhyupagamyeta evam sati udāsīnānām anīhamānānām api janānām abhimata siddhiḥ syāt abhāvasya sulabha tvāt
kṛṣīvalasya kṣetra karmaṇi aprayatamānasya api sasya niṣpattiḥ syāt
kulālasya ca mṛd saṃskriyāyām aprayatamānasya api amatra utpattiḥ
tantuvāyasya api tantūn a tanvānasya api tanvānasya iva vastra lābhaḥ
svarga apavargayoḥ ca na kaścid kathaṃcid samīheta
na ca etat yujyate abhyupagamyate vā kenacid
tasmāt anupapannaḥ yam abhāvāt bhāva utpatti abhyupagamaḥ
na abhāvaḥ upalabdheḥ
na abhāva adhikaraṇam
evam bāhya artha vādam āśritya samudāya aprāpti ādiṣu dūṣaṇeṣu udbhāviteṣu vijñāna vādī bauddhaḥ idānīm pratyavatiṣṭhate keṣāṃcid kila vineyānām bāhye vastuni abhiniveśam ālakṣya tad anurodhena bāhya artha vāda prakriyā iyam viracitā
na asau sugata abhiprāyaḥ
tasya tu vijñāna eka skandha vādaḥ eva abhipretaḥ
tasmin ca vijñāna vāde buddhi ārūḍhena rūpeṇa antasthaḥ eva pramāṇa prameya phala vyavahāraḥ sarvaḥ upapadyate sati api bāhya arthe buddhi āroham antareṇa pramāṇa ādi vyavahāra anavatārāt
katham punar avagamyate antasthaḥ eva ayam sarva vyavahāraḥ na vijñāna vyatiriktaḥ bāhyaḥ rthaḥ asti iti
tad asaṃbhavāt iti āha sa hi bāhyaḥ rthaḥ bhyupagamyamānaḥ paramāṇavaḥ vā syuḥ tad samūhāḥ vā stambha ādayaḥ syuḥ
tatra na tāvat paramāṇavaḥ stambha ādi pratyaya paricchedyāḥ bhavitum arhanti paramāṇu ābhāsa jñāna anupapatteḥ
na api tad samūhāḥ stambha ādayaḥ teṣām paramāṇubhyaḥ nya tva ananya tvābhyām nirūpayitum aśakya tvāt
evam jāti ādīn api pratyācakṣīta
api ca anubhava mātreṇa sādhāraṇa ātmanaḥ jñānasya jāyamānasya yaḥ yam prati viṣayam pakṣapātaḥ stambha jñānam kuḍya jñānam ghaṭa jñānam paṭa jñānam iti na asau jñāna gata viśeṣam antareṇa upapadyate iti avaśyam viṣaya sārūpyam jñānasya aṅgīkartavyam
aṅgīkṛte ca tasmin viṣaya ākārasya jñānena eva avaruddha tvāt apārthikā bāhya artha sadbhāva kalpanā
api ca saha upalambha niyamāt abhedaḥ viṣaya vijñānayoḥ āpatati
na hi anayoḥ ekasya anupalambhe nyasya upalambhaḥ sti
na ca etat svabhāva viveke yuktam pratibandha kāraṇa abhāvāt
tasmāt api artha abhāvaḥ
svapna ādi vat ca idam draṣṭavyam yathā hi svapna māyā marīci udaka gandharvanagara ādi pratyayāḥ vinā eva bāhyena arthena grāhya grāhaka ākārāḥ bhavanti
evam jāgarita gocarāḥ api stambha ādi pratyayāḥ bhavitum arhanti iti avagamyate pratyaya tva aviśeṣāt
katham punar asati bāhya arthe pratyaya vaicitryam upapadyate
vāsanā vaicitryāt iti āha anādau hi saṃsāre bīja aṅkura vat vijñānānām vāsanānām ca anyonya nimitta naimittika bhāvena vaicitryam na vipratiṣidhyate
api ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām vāsanā nimittam eva jñāna vaicitryam iti avagamyate svapna ādiṣu antareṇa api artham vāsanā nimittasya jñāna vaicitryasya ubhābhyām api āvābhyām abhyupagamyamāna tvāt antareṇa tu vāsanām artha nimittasya jñāna vaicitryasya mayā an abhyupagamyamāna tvāt
tasmāt api abhāvaḥ bāhya arthasya iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ
na abhāvaḥ upalabdheḥ iti
na khalu abhāvaḥ bāhyasya arthasya adhyavasātum śakyate
kasmāt
upalabdheḥ upalabhyate hi prati pratyayam bāhyaḥ rthaḥ stambhaḥ kuḍyam ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ iti
na ca upalabhyamānasya eva abhāvaḥ bhavitum arhati
yathā hi kaścid bhuñjānaḥ sādhyāyām tṛptau svayam anubhūyamānāyām evam brūyāt na aham bhuñje na vā tṛpyāmi iti tadvat indriya saṃnikarṣeṇa svayam upalabhamānaḥ eva bāhyam artham na aham upalabhe na ca saḥ sti iti bruvan katham upādeya vacanaḥ syāt
nanu na aham evam bravīmi na kaṃcid artham upalabhe iti
kim tu upalabdhi vyatiriktam na upalabhe iti bravīmi
bāḍham evam bravīṣi niraṅkuśa tvāt te tuṇḍasya na tu yukti upetam bravīṣi yatas upalabdhi vyatirekaḥ balāt arthasya abhyupagantavyaḥ upalabdheḥ eva
na hi kaścid upalabdhim eva stambhaḥ kuḍyam ca iti upalabhate
upalabdhi viṣaya tvena eva tu stambha kuḍya ādīn sarve laukikāḥ upalabhante
atas ca evam eva sarve laukikāḥ upalabhante
yat pratyācakṣāṇāḥ api bāhyam artham evam ācakṣate yat antar jñeya rūpam tat bahis vat avabhāsate iti te hi sarva loka prasiddhām bahis avabhāsamānām saṃvidam pratilabhamānāḥ pratyākhyātu kāmāḥ ca bāhyam artham bahis vat iti vatkāram kurvanti
itarathā hi kasmāt bahirvat iti brūyuḥ
na hi viṣṇu mitraḥ vandhyā putra vat avabhāsate iti kaścid ācakṣīta
tasmāt yathānubhavam tattvam abhyupagacchadbhiḥ bahis eva avabhāsate iti yuktam abhyupagantum na tu bahis vat avabhāsate iti
nanu bāhyasya arthasya asaṃbhavāt bahis vat avabhāsate iti adhyavasitam
na ayam sādhuḥ adhyavasāyaḥ yatas pramāṇa pravṛtti apravṛtti pūrvakau saṃbhava asaṃbhavau avadhāryete na punar saṃbhava asaṃbhava pūrvake pramāṇa pravṛtti apravṛttī
yat hi pratyakṣa ādīnām anyatamena api pramāṇena upalabhyate tat saṃbhavati
yat tu na kenacid api pramāṇena upalabhyate tat na saṃbhavati
iha tu yathāsvam sarvaiḥ eva pramāṇaiḥ bāhyaḥ rthaḥ upalabhyamānaḥ katham vyatireka avyatireka ādi vikalpaiḥ na saṃbhavati iti ucyeta upalabdheḥ eva
na ca jñānasya viṣaya sārūpyāt viṣaya nāśaḥ bhavati asati viṣaye viṣaya sārūpya anupapatteḥ bahis upalabdheḥ ca viṣayasya
atas eva saha upalambha niyamaḥ api pratyaya viṣayayoḥ upāya upeya bhāva hetukaḥ na abheda hetukaḥ iti abhyupagantavyam
api ca ghaṭa jñānam paṭa jñānam iti viśeṣaṇayoḥ ghaṭa paṭayoḥ bhedaḥ na viśeṣyasya jñānasya yathā śuklaḥ gauḥ kṛṣṇaḥ gauḥ iti śauklya kārṣṇyayoḥ eva bhedaḥ na go tvasya
dvābhyām ca bhedaḥ ekasya siddhaḥ bhavati ekasmāt ca dvayoḥ
tasmāt artha jñānayoḥ bhedaḥ
tathā ghaṭa darśanam ghaṭa smaraṇam iti atra api pratipattavyam
atra api hi viśeṣyayoḥ eva darśana smaraṇayoḥ bhedaḥ na viśeṣaṇasya ghaṭasya yathā kṣīra gandhaḥ kṣīra rasaḥ iti viśeṣyayoḥ eva gandha rasayoḥ bhedaḥ na viśeṣaṇasya kṣīrasya tadvat
api ca dvayoḥ vijñānayoḥ pūrva uttara kālayoḥ sva saṃvedanena eva upakṣīṇayoḥ itaretara grāhya grāhaka tva anupapattiḥ
tatas ca vijñāna bheda pratijñā kṣaṇika tva ādi dharma pratijñā sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇa vāsya vāsaka tva avidyā upaplava sat asat dharma bandha mokṣa ādi pratijñāḥ ca sva śāstra gatāḥ tāḥ hīyeran
kiṃca anyat vijñānam vijñānam iti abhyupagacchatā bāhya arthaḥ stambhaḥ kuḍyam iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ kasmāt na abhyupagamyate iti vaktavyam
vijñānam anubhūyate iti ced arthaḥ nubhūyate eva iti yuktam abhyupagantum
atha vijñānam prakāśa ātmaka tvāt pradīpa vat svayam evā anubhūyate na tathā arthaḥ iti ced atyanta viruddhām svātmani kriyām abhyupagacchasi agniḥ ātmānam dahati itivat
aviruddham tu loka prasiddham sva ātma vyatiriktena vijñānena bāhya arthaḥ nubhūyate iti nā icchasi
aho pāṇḍityam mahat darśitam
na ca artha vyatiriktam api vijñānam svayam evā anubhūyate sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt eva
nanu vijñānasya svarūpa vyatirikta grāhya tve tat api anyena grāhyam tat api anyena iti anavasthā prāpnoti
api ca pradīpa vat avabhāsa ātmaka tvāt jñānasya jñāna antaram kalpayataḥ sama tvāt avabhāsya avabhāsaka bhāva anupapatteḥ kalpanā ānarthakyam iti tat ubhayam api asat vijñāna grahaṇa mātre eva vijñāna sākṣiṇaḥ grahaṇa ākāṅkṣā anutpādāt anavasthā śaṅkā anupapatteḥ sākṣi pratyayayoḥ ca svabhāva vaiṣamyāt upalabdhṛ upalabhya bhāva upapatteḥ svayaṃsiddhasya ca sākṣiṇaḥ pratyākhyeya tvāt
kiṃca anyat pradīpavat vijñānam avabhāsaka antara nirapekṣam svayam eva prathate iti bruvatā a pramāṇa gamyam vijñānam an avagantṛkam iti uktam syāt śilāghana madhya stha pradīpa sahasra prathana vat
bāḍham evam anubhava rūpa tvāt tu vijñānasya iṣṭaḥ naḥ pakṣaḥ tvayā anujñāyate iti ced na
anyasya avagantuḥ cakṣuḥ sādhanasya pradīpa ādi prathana darśanāt
atas vijñānasya api avabhāsya tva aviśeṣāt sati eva anyasmin avagantari prathanam pradīpa vat iti avagamyate
sākṣiṇaḥ vagantuḥ svayam siddha tām upakṣipatā svayam prathate vijñānam iti eṣaḥ eva mama pakṣaḥ tvayā vācoyukti antareṇa āśritaḥ iti ced na
vijñānasya utpatti pradhvaṃsa aneka tva ādi viśeṣavat tva abhyupagamāt
atas pradīpa vat vijñānasya api vyatirikta avagamya tvam asmābhiḥ prasādhitam
vaidharmyāt ca na svapna ādi vat
yat uktam bāhya artha apalāpinā svapna ādi pratyaya vat jāgarita gocarāḥ api stambha ādi pratyayāḥ vinā eva bāhyena arthena bhaveyuḥ pratyaya tva aviśeṣāt iti tat prativaktavyam
atra ucyate na svapna ādi pratyaya vat jāgrat pratyayāḥ bhavitum arhanti
kasmāt
vaidharmyāt vaidharmyam hi bhavati svapna jāgaritayoḥ
kim punar vaidharmyam
bādhā bādhau iti brūmaḥ bādhyate hi svapna upalabdham vastu pratibuddhasya mithyā mayā upalabdhaḥ mahājana samāgamaḥ iti na hi asti mama mahājana samāgamaḥ nidrā glānam tu me manaḥ babhūva tena eṣā bhrāntiḥ udbabhūva iti
evam māyā ādiṣu api bhavati yathāyatham bādhaḥ
na evam jāgarita upalabdham vastu stambha ādikam kasyāṃcid api avasthāyām bādhyate
api ca smṛtiḥ eṣā yat svapna darśanam
upalabdhiḥ tu jāgarita darśanam
smṛti upalabdhyoḥ ca pratyakṣam antaram svayam anubhūyate artha viprayoga saṃprayoga ātmakam iṣṭam putram smarāmi na upalabhe upalabdhum icchāmi iti
tatra evam sati na śakyate vaktum mithyā jāgarita upalabdhiḥ upalabdhi tvāt svapna upalabdhi vat iti ubhayoḥ antaram svayam anubhavatā
na ca sva anubhava apalāpaḥ prājña mānibhiḥ yuktaḥ kartum
api ca anubhava virodha prasaṅgāt jāgarita pratyayānām svatas nirālambana tām vaktum aśaknuvatā svapna pratyaya sādharmyāt vaktum iṣyate
na ca yaḥ yasya svatas dharmaḥ na saṃbhavati saḥ nyasya sādharmyāt tasya saṃbhaviṣyati
na hi agniḥ uṣṇaḥ nubhūyamānaḥ udaka sādharmyāt śītaḥ bhaviṣyati
darśitam tu vaidharmyam svapna jāgaritayoḥ
na bhāvaḥ n upalabdheḥ
yat api uktam vinā api arthena jñāna vaicitryam vāsanā vaicitryāt eva avakalpate iti tat prativaktavyam
atrā ucyate na bhāvaḥ vāsanānām upapadyate tvad pakṣe n upalabdheḥ bāhyānām arthānām
artha upalabdhi nimittāḥ hi pratyartham nānā rūpāḥ vāsanāḥ bhavanti
an upalabhyamāneṣu tu artheṣu kiṃnimittāḥ vicitrāḥ vāsanāḥ bhaveyuḥ
anādi tve pi andha paraṃparā nyāyena apratiṣṭhā evā anavasthā vyavahāra lopinī syāt nā abhiprāya siddhiḥ
yau api anvaya vyatirekau artha apalāpinā upanyastau vāsanā nimittam eva idam jñāna jātam na artha nimittam iti tau api evam sati pratyuktau draṣṭavyau vinā artha upalabdhyā vāsanā anupapatteḥ
api ca vinā api vāsanābhiḥ artha upalabdhi upagamāt vinā tu artha upalabdhyā vāsanā utpatti anabhyupagamāt artha sadbhāvam eva anvaya vyatirekau api pratiṣṭhāpayataḥ
api ca vāsanāḥ nāma saṃskāra viśeṣāḥ
saṃskārāḥ ca na āśrayam antareṇa avakalpante evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt
na ca tava vāsanā āśrayaḥ kaścid asti pramāṇataḥ n upalabdheḥ
kṣaṇika tvāt ca
yat api ālayavijñānam nāma vāsanā āśraya tvena parikalpitam tat api kṣaṇika tva abhyupagamāt anavasthita svarūpam sat pravṛtti vijñāna vat na vāsanānām adhikaraṇam bhavitum arhati
na hi kāla traya saṃbandhini ekasmin anvayini asati kūṭasthe vā sarva artha darśini deśa kāla nimitta apekṣa vāsanā adhīna smṛti pratisaṃdhāna ādi vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati
sthira svarūpa tve tu ālayavijñānasya siddhānta hāniḥ
api ca vijñāna vāde pi kṣaṇikatva abhyupagamasya samāna tvāt yāni bāhya artha vāde kṣaṇikatva nibandhanāni dūṣaṇāni udbhāvitāni uttara utpāde ca pūrva nirodhāt iti evamādīni tāni iha api anusaṃdhātavyāni
evam etau dvau api vaināśika pakṣau nirākṛtau bāhya artha vādi pakṣaḥ vijñāna vādi pakṣaḥ ca
śūnyavādi pakṣaḥ tu sarva pramāṇa vipratiṣiddhaḥ iti tad nirākaraṇāya na ādaraḥ kriyate
na hi ayam sarva pramāṇa siddhaḥ lokavyavahāraḥ nyat tattvam an adhigamya śakyate pahnotum apavāda abhāve utsarga prasiddheḥ
sarvathā nupapatteḥ ca
kim bahunā
sarva prakāreṇa yathā yathā ayam vaināśika samayaḥ upapattimat tvāya parīkṣyate tathā tathā sikatā kūpa vat vidīryate eva
na kāṃcid api atra upapattim paśyāmaḥ
atas ca anupapannaḥ vaināśika tantra vyavahāraḥ
api ca bāhya artha vijñāna śūnya vāda trayam itaretara viruddham upadiśatā sugatena spaṣṭīkṛtam saṃbaddha pralāpi tvam pradveṣaḥ vā prajāsu viruddha artha pratipattyā vimuhyeyuḥ imāḥ prajāḥ iti
sarvathā api an ādaraṇīyaḥ yam sugata samayaḥ śreyaskāmaiḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ
na ekasmin asambhavāt
ekasmin asaṃbhava adhikaraṇam
nirastaḥ sugata samayaḥ
vivasana samayaḥ idānīm nirasyate
sapta ca eṣām padārthāḥ saṃmatāḥ jīva ajīva āsrava saṃvara nirjara bandha mokṣāḥ nāma
saṃkṣepataḥ tu dvau eva padārthau jīva ajīva ākhyau yathāyogam tayoḥ eva itara antarbhāvāt iti manyante
tayoḥ imam aparam prapañcam ācakṣate pañca astikāyāḥ nāma jīva astikāyaḥ pudgala astikāyaḥ dharma astikāyaḥ dharma astikāyaḥ ākāśa astikāyaḥ ca iti
sarveṣām api eṣām avāntarabhedān bahuvidhān sva samaya parikalpitān varṇayanti
sarvatra ca imam saptabhaṅgīnayam nāma nyāyam avatārayanti syāt asti syāt na asti syāt asti ca na asti ca syāt avaktavyaḥ syāt asti ca avaktavyaḥ ca syāt na asti ca avaktavyaḥ ca syāt asti ca na asti ca avaktavyaḥ ca iti
evam eva ekatva nitya tva ādiṣu api imam sapta bhaṅgī nayam yojayanti
atra ācakṣmahe na ayam abhyupagamaḥ yuktaḥ iti
kutas
ekasmin asaṃbhavāt
na hi ekasmin dharmiṇi yugapad sat asat tva ādi viruddha dharma samāveśaḥ saṃbhavati śīta uṣṇa vat
ye ete sapta padārthāḥ nirdhāritāḥ etāvantaḥ evaṃrūpāḥ ca iti te tathā eva vā syuḥ na eva vā tathā syuḥ
itarathā hi tathā vā syuḥ atathā vā iti anirdhārita rūpam jñānam saṃśaya jñāna vat apramāṇam eva syāt
nanu aneka ātmakam vastu iti nirdhārita rūpam eva jñānam utpadyamānam saṃśaya jñāna vat na apramāṇam bhavitum arhati
na iti brūmaḥ niraṅkuśam hi anekānta tvam sarva vastuṣu pratijānānasya nirdhāraṇasya api vastu tva aviśeṣāt syāt asti syāt na asti ityādi vikalpa upanipātāt anirdhāraṇa ātmaka tā eva syāt
evam nirdhārayituḥ nirdhāraṇa phalasya ca syāt pakṣe stitā syāt ca pakṣe nāstitā iti
evam sati katham pramāṇa bhūtaḥ san tīrthakaraḥ pramāṇa prameya pramātṛ pramitiṣu anirdhāritāsu upadeṣṭum śaknuyāt
katham vā tad abhiprāya anusāriṇaḥ tad upadiṣṭe rthe nirdhārita rūpe pravarteran
aikāntika phalatva nirdhāraṇe hi sati tad sādhana anuṣṭhānāya sarvaḥ lokaḥ na ākulaḥ pravartate na anyathā
atas ca anirdhārita artham śāstram praṇayan matta unmatta vat anupādeya vacanaḥ syāt
tathā pañcānām astikāyānām pañcatva saṃkhyā asti vā na asti vā iti vikalpyamānā syāt tāvat ekasmin pakṣe pakṣa antare tu na syāt iti atas nyūna saṃkhyā tvam adhika saṃkhyā tvam vā prāpnuyāt
na ca eṣām padārthānām avaktavya tvam saṃbhavati
a vaktavyāḥ ced na ucyeran
ucyante ca avaktavyāḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham
ucyamānāḥ ca tathā eva avadhāryante na avadhāryante iti ca
tathā tad avadhāraṇa phalam samyak darśanam asti vā na asti vā evam tad viparītam asamyak darśanam api asti vā na asti vā iti pralapan matta unmatta pakṣasya eva pakṣaḥ syāt na pratyayitavya pakṣasya
svarga apavargayoḥ ca pakṣe bhāvaḥ pakṣe ca abhāvaḥ tathā pakṣe nitya tā pakṣe ca anitya tā iti anavadhāraṇāyām pravṛtti anupapattiḥ
anādisiddha jīva prabhṛtīnām ca sva śāstra avadhṛta svabhāvānām ayathā avadhṛta svabhāva tva prasaṅgaḥ
evam jīva ādiṣu padārtheṣu ekasmin dharmiṇi sattva asattvayoḥ viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ asaṃbhavāt sattve ca ekasmin dharme sattvasya dharma antarasya asaṃbhavāt asattve ca evam sattvasya asaṃbhavāt asaṃgatam idam ārhatam matam

yat tu pudgala saṃjñakebhyaḥ ṇubhyaḥ saṃghātāḥ saṃbhavanti iti kalpayanti tat pūrveṇa eva aṇu vāda nirākaraṇena nirākṛtam bhavati iti atas na pṛthak tad nirākaraṇāya prayatyate
evam ca ātma akārtsnyam
yathā ekasmin dharmiṇi viruddha dharma asaṃbhavaḥ doṣaḥ syāt vāde prasaktaḥ evam ātmanaḥ api jīvasya akārtsnyam aparaḥ doṣaḥ prasajyeta
katham
śarīra parimāṇaḥ hi jīvaḥ iti ārhatāḥ manyante
śarīra parimāṇa tāyām ca satyām akṛtsnaḥ sarva gataḥ paricchinnaḥ ātmā iti atas ghaṭa ādi vat anitya tvam ātmanaḥ prasajyeta
śarīrāṇām ca anavasthita parimāṇa tvāt manuṣya jīvaḥ manuṣya śarīra parimāṇaḥ bhūtvā punar kenacid karma vipākena hasti janma prāpnuvan na kṛtsnam hasti śarīram vyāpnuyāt
puttikā janma ca prāpnuvan na kṛtsnaḥ puttikā śarīre saṃmīyeta
samānaḥ eṣaḥ ekasmin api janmani kaumāra yauvana sthāvireṣu doṣaḥ
syāt etat ananta avayavaḥ jīvaḥ
tasya te eva avayavāḥ alpe śarīre saṃkuceyuḥ
mahati ca vikaseyuḥ iti
teṣām punar anantānām jīva avayavānām samāna deśa tvam prativihanyate vā na vā iti vaktavyam
pratighāte tāvat na ananta avayavāḥ paricchinne deśe saṃmīyeran
apratighāte pi eka avayava deśa tva upapatteḥ sarveṣām avayavānām prathima anupapatteḥ jīvasya aṇu mātra tva prasaṅgaḥ syāt
api ca śarīra mātra paricchinnānām jīva avayavānām ānantyam na utprekṣitum api śakyam
atha paryāyeṇa bṛhat śarīra pratipattau kecid jīva avayavāḥ upagacchanti tanu śarīra pratipattau ca kecid apagacchanti iti ucyeta
tatra api ucyate
na ca paryāyāt api avirodhaḥ vikāra ādibhyaḥ
na ca paryāyeṇa api avayava upagama apagamābhyām etat deha parimāṇa tvam jīvasya avirodhena upapādayitum śakyate
kutas
vikāra ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt avayava upagama apagamābhyām hi aniśam āpūryamāṇasya apakṣīyamāṇasya ca jīvasya vikriyāvat tvam tāvat aparihāryam
vikriyāvat tve ca carma ādi vat anitya tvam prasajyeta
tatas ca bandha mokṣa abhyupagamaḥ bādhyeta karma aṣṭaka pariveṣṭitasya jīvasya alābū vat saṃsāra sāgare nimagnasya bandhana ucchedāt ūrdhvagāmi tvam bhavati iti
kiṃca anyat āgacchatām apagacchatām ca avayavānām āgama apāya dharmavat tvāt eva anātma tvam śarīra ādi vat
tatas ca avasthitaḥ kaścid avayavaḥ ātmā iti syāt
na ca sa nirūpayitum śakyate ayam asau iti
kiṃca anyat āgacchantaḥ ca ete jīva avayavāḥ kutas prādurbhavanti apagacchantaḥ ca kva vā līyante iti vaktavyam
na hi bhūtebhyaḥ prādurbhaveyuḥ bhūteṣu ca nilīyeran abhautika tvāt jīvasya
nā api kaścid anyaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ vā jīvānām avayava ādhāraḥ nirūpyate pramāṇa abhāvāt
kiṃca anyat an avadhṛta sva rūpaḥ ca evam sati ātmā syāt āgacchatām apagacchatām ca avayavānām aniyata parimāṇa tvāt
atas evamādi doṣa prasaṅgāt na paryāyeṇa api avayava upagama apagamau ātmanaḥ āśrayitum śakyete
athavā pūrveṇa sūtreṇa śarīra parimāṇasya ātmanaḥ upacita apacita śarīra antara pratipattau akārtsnya prasañjana dvāreṇa anitya tāyām coditāyām punar paryāyeṇa parimāṇa anavasthāne srotaḥ saṃtāna nityatā nyāyena ātmanaḥ nitya tā syāt yathā rakta paṭānām vijñāna anavasthāne tad saṃtāna nityatā tadvat visicām api iti āśaṅkya anena sūtreṇa uttaram ucyate saṃtānasya tāvat avastu tve nairātmya vāda prasaṅgaḥ vastu tve pi ātmanaḥ vikār
antya avasthiteḥ ca ubhaya nitya tvāt aviśeṣaḥ
api ca antyasya mokṣa avasthā bhāvinaḥ jīva parimāṇasya nitya tvam iṣyate jainaiḥ
tadvat pūrvayoḥ api ādya madhyamayoḥ jīva parimāṇayoḥ nitya tva prasaṅgāt aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ syāt
eka śarīra parimāṇa tā eva syāt na upacita apacita śarīra antara prāptiḥ
athavā antyasya jīva parimāṇasya avasthita tvāt pūrvayoḥ api avasthayoḥ avasthita parimāṇaḥ eva jīvaḥ syāt
tatas ca aviśeṣeṇa sarvadā eva aṇuḥ mahān vā jīvaḥ bhyupagantavyaḥ na śarīra parimāṇaḥ
atas ca saugata vat ārhatam api matam asaṃgatam iti upekṣitavyam
patyuḥ asāmañjasyāt
pati adhikaraṇam
idānīm kevala adhiṣṭhātṛ īśvara kāraṇa vādaḥ pratiṣidhyate
tat katham avagamyate
prakṛtiḥ ca pratijñā dṛṣṭānta an uparodhāt abhidhyā upadeśāt ca iti atra prakṛti bhāvena adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāvena ca ubhaya svabhāvasya īśvarasya svayam eva ācāryeṇa pratiṣṭhāpita tvāt
yadi punar aviśeṣeṇa īśvara kāraṇa vāda mātram iha pratiṣidhyeta pūrva uttara virodhāt vyāhata abhivyāhāraḥ sūtrakāraḥ iti etat āpadyeta
tasmāt aprakṛtiḥ adhiṣṭhātā kevalam nimitta kāraṇam īśvaraḥ iti eṣa pakṣaḥ vedānta vihita brahma ekatva pratipakṣa tvāt yatnena atra pratiṣidhyate
sā ca iyam veda bāhya īśvara kalpanā aneka prakārā kecid tāvat sāṃkhya yoga vyapāśrayāḥ kalpayanti pradhāna puruṣayoḥ adhiṣṭhātā kevalam nimitta kāraṇam īśvaraḥ
itaretara vilakṣaṇāḥ pradhāna puruṣa īśvarāḥ iti
māheśvarāḥ tu manyante kārya kāraṇa yoga vidhi duḥkhāntāḥ pañca padārthāḥ paśupatinā īśvareṇa paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇāya upadiṣṭāḥ
paśupatiḥ īśvaraḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti
tathā vaiśeṣika ādayaḥ api kecid kathaṃcid sva prakriyā anusāreṇa nimitta kāraṇam īśvaram iti
atas uttaram ucyate patyuḥ asāmañjasyāt iti
patyuḥ īśvarasya pradhāna puruṣayoḥ adhiṣṭhātṛ tvena jagat kāraṇatvam na upapadyate
kasmāt
asāmañjasyāt
kim punar asāmañjasyam
hīna madhyama uttama bhāvena hi prāṇi bhedān vidadhataḥ īśvarasya rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa prasakteḥ asmat ādi vat anīśvara tvam prasajyeta
prāṇi karma apekṣita tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na

na anādi tvāt iti ced na
vartamāna kāla vat atīteṣu api kāleṣu itaretara āśraya doṣa aviśeṣāt andha paraṃparā nyāya āpatteḥ
api  ca  pravartanā Cp lakṣaṇāḥ PNM doṣāḥ PNM
iti nyāya vid samayaḥ
na hi kaścid adoṣa prayuktaḥ sva arthe para arthe vā pravartamānaḥ dṛśyate
sva artha prayuktaḥ eva ca sarvaḥ janaḥ para arthe pravartate iti evam api asāmañjasyam sva arthavat tvāt īśvarasya anīśvara tva prasaṅgāt
puruṣa viśeṣa tva abhyupagamāt ca īśvarasya puruṣasya ca audāsīnya abhyupagamāt asāmañjasyam
sambandha anupapatteḥ ca
punar api asāmañjasyam eva na hi pradhāna puruṣa vyatiriktaḥ īśvaraḥ ntareṇa saṃbandham pradhāna puruṣayoḥ īśitā
na tāvat saṃyoga lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ saṃbhavati pradhāna puruṣa īśvarāṇām sarvagata tvāt niravayava tvāt ca
nā api samavāya lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ āśraya āśrayi bhāva anirūpaṇāt
nā api anyaḥ kaścid kārya gamyaḥ saṃbandhaḥ śakyate kalpayitum kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya eva adya api asiddha tvāt
brahma vādinaḥ katham iti ced na
tasya tādātmya lakṣaṇa saṃbandha upapatteḥ
api ca āgama balena brahma vādī kāraṇa ādi svarūpam nirūpayati iti na avaśyam tasya yathādṛṣṭam eva sarvam abhyupagantavyam iti
parasya tu dṛṣṭānta balena kāraṇa ādi svarūpam nirūpayataḥ yathādṛṣṭam eva sarvam abhyupagantavyam iti ayam asti atiśayaḥ
parasya api sarvajña praṇīta āgama sadbhāvāt samānam āgama balam iti ced na
itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt āgama pratyayāt sarvajña tva siddhiḥ sarvajña tva pratyayāt ca āgama siddhiḥ iti
tasmāt anupapannā sāṃkhya yoga vādinām īśvara kalpanā
evam anyāsu api veda bāhyāsu īśvara kalpanāsu yathāsaṃbhavam asāmañjasyam yojayitavyam
adhiṣṭhāna anupapatteḥ ca
itas ca anupapattiḥ tārkika parikalpitasya īśvarasya sa hi parikalpyamānaḥ kumbhakāraḥ iva mṛd ādīni pradhāna ādīni adhiṣṭhāya pravartayet
na ca evam upapadyate
na hi apratyakṣam rūpa ādi hīnam ca pradhānam īśvarasya adhiṣṭheyam saṃbhavati mṛd ādi vailakṣaṇyāt
karaṇavat ced na bhoga ādibhyaḥ
syāt etat yathā karaṇa grāmam cakṣuḥ ādikam apratyakṣam rūpa ādi hīnam ca puruṣaḥ dhitiṣṭhati evam pradhānam īśvaraḥ dhiṣṭhāsyati iti
tathā api na upapadyate
bhoga ādi darśanāt hi karaṇa grāmasya adhiṣṭhita tvam gamyate
na ca atra bhoga ādayaḥ dṛśyante
karaṇa grāma sāmye ca abhyupagamyamāne saṃsāriṇām iva īśvarasya api bhoga ādayaḥ prasajyeran
anyathā vā sūtra dvayam vyākhyāyate adhiṣṭhāna anupapatteḥ ca itas ca anupapattiḥ tārkika parikalpitasya īśvarasya
sa adhiṣṭhānaḥ hi loke sa śarīraḥ rājā rāṣṭrasya īśvaraḥ dṛśyate
na niradhiṣṭhānaḥ
atas ca tad dṛṣṭānta vaśena adṛṣṭam īśvaram kalpayitum icchataḥ īśvarasya api kiṃcid śarīram karaṇa āyatanam varṇayitavyam syāt
na ca tat varṇayitum śakyate sṛṣṭi uttara kāla bhāvi tvāt śarīrasya prāk sṛṣṭeḥ tad anupapatteḥ
niradhiṣṭhāna tve ca īśvarasya pravartaka tva anupapattiḥ evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt
karaṇa vat ced na bhoga ādibhyaḥ atha loka darśana anusāreṇa īśvarasya api kiṃcid karaṇānām āyatanam śarīram kāmena kalpyeta evam api nā upapadyate
sa śarīra tve hi sati saṃsāri vat bhoga ādi prasaṅgāt īśvarasya api anīśvara tvam prasajyeta
antavat tvam asarvajña tā vā
itas ca anupapattiḥ tārkika parikalpitasya īśvarasya sa hi sarvajñaḥ taiḥ abhyupagamyate nantaḥ ca
anantam ca pradhānam anantāḥ ca puruṣāḥ mithas bhinnāḥ abhyupagamyante
tatra sarvajñena īśvareṇa pradhānasya puruṣāṇām ātmanaḥ ca iyattā paricchidyeta vā na vā paricchidyeta
ubhayathā api doṣaḥ nuṣaktaḥ eva
katham
pūrvasmin tāvat vikalpe iyat tā paricchinna tvāt pradhāna puruṣa īśvarāṇām antavat tvam avaśyaṃbhāvi evam loke dṛṣṭa tvāt
yat hi loke iyattā paricchinnam vastu ghaṭa ādi tat antavat dṛṣṭam tathā pradhāna puruṣa īśvara trayam api iyattā paricchinna tvāt antavat syāt
saṃkhyā parimāṇam tāvat pradhāna puruṣa īśvara traya rūpeṇa paricchinnam
sva rūpa parimāṇam api tad gatam īśvareṇa paricchidyeta puruṣa gatā ca mahā saṃkhyā
tatas ca iyattā paricchinnānām madhye ye saṃsārāt mucyante teṣām saṃsāraḥ ntavān saṃsāri tvam ca teṣām antavat
evam itareṣu api krameṇa mucyamāneṣu saṃsārasya saṃsāriṇām ca antavat tvam syāt
pradhānam ca sa vikāram puruṣa artham īśvarasya adhiṣṭheyam saṃsāra tvena abhimatam
tad śūnyatāyām īśvaraḥ kim adhitiṣṭhet
kiṃviṣaye vā sarvajña tā īśvara te syātām
pradhāna puruṣa īśvarāṇām ca evam antavat tve sati ādimat tva prasaṅgaḥ
ādi antavat tve ca śūnyavāda prasaṅgaḥ
atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti uttaraḥ vikalpaḥ bhyupagamyeta na pradhānasya puruṣāṇām ātmanaḥ ca iyat tā īśvareṇa paricchidyate iti
tatas īśvarasya sarvajña tva abhyupagama hāniḥ aparaḥ doṣaḥ prasajyeta
tasmāt api asaṃgataḥ tārkika parigṛhītaḥ īśvara kāraṇa vādaḥ
utpatti asambhavāt
utpatti asaṃbhava adhikaraṇam
yeṣām aprakṛtiḥ adhiṣṭhātā kevala nimitta kāraṇam īśvaraḥ bhimataḥ teṣām pakṣaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ
yeṣām punar prakṛtiḥ ca adhiṣṭhātā ca ubhaya ātmakam kāraṇam īśvaraḥ bhimataḥ teṣām pakṣaḥ pratyākhyāyate
nanu śruti samāśrayaṇena api evaṃrūpaḥ eva īśvaraḥ prāk nirdhāritaḥ prakṛtiḥ ca adhiṣṭhātā ca iti
śruti anusāriṇī ca smṛtiḥ pramāṇam iti sthitiḥ
tat kasya hetoḥ eṣa pakṣaḥ pratyācikhyāsitaḥ iti ucyate yadi api evaṃjātīyakaḥ ūm śaḥ samāna tvāt na visaṃvāda gocaraḥ bhavati asti tu aṃśa antaram visaṃvāda sthānam iti atas tad pratyākhyānāya ārambhaḥ
tatra bhāgavatāḥ manyate bhagavān eva ekaḥ vāsudevaḥ nirañjana jñāna svarūpaḥ paramārtha tattvam
sa caturdhā ātmānam pravibhajya pratiṣṭhitaḥ vāsudeva vyūha rūpeṇa saṃkarṣaṇa vyūha rūpeṇa pradyumna vyūha rūpeṇa aniruddha vyūha rūpeṇa ca
vāsudevaḥ nāma paramātmā ucyate
saṃkarṣaṇaḥ nāma jīvaḥ
pradyumnaḥ nāma manaḥ
aniruddhaḥ nāma ahaṃkāraḥ
teṣām vāsudevaḥ parā prakṛtiḥ itare saṃkarṣaṇa ādayaḥ kāryam
tam itthaṃbhūtam parameśvaram bhagavantam abhigamana upādāna ijyā svādhyāya yogaiḥ varṣa śatam iṣṭvā kṣīṇa kleśaḥ bhagavantam eva pratipadyate iti
tatra yat tāvat ucyate saḥ au nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ vyaktāt prasiddhaḥ paramātmā sarvātmā saḥ ātmanā ātmānam anekadhā vyūhya avasthitaḥ iti tat na nirākriyate saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ paramātmanaḥ nekadhā bhāvasya adhigata tvāt
yat api tasya bhagavataḥ bhigamana ādi lakṣaṇam ārādhanam ajasram ananya cittatayā abhipreyate tat api na pratiṣidhyate śruti smṛtyoḥ īśvara praṇidhānasya prasiddha tvāt
yat punar idam ucyate vāsudevāt saṃkarṣaṇaḥ utpadyate saṃkarṣaṇāt ca pradyumnaḥ pradyumnāt ca aniruddhaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na vāsudeva saṃjñakāt paramātmanaḥ saṃkarṣaṇa saṃjñakasya jīvasya utpattiḥ saṃbhavati anitya tva ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt
utpattimat tve hi jīvasya anitya tva ādayaḥ doṣāḥ prasajyeran
tatas ca nā eva asya bhagavat prāptiḥ mokṣaḥ syāt kāraṇa prāptau kāryasya pravilaya prasaṅgāt
pratiṣedhiṣyati ca ācāryaḥ jīvasya utpattim na ātmā aśruteḥ nitya tvāt ca tābhyaḥ iti
tasmāt asaṃgatā eṣā kalpanā
na ca kartuḥ karaṇam
itas ca asaṃgatā eṣā kalpanā yasmāt na hi loke kartuḥ devadatta ādeḥ karaṇam paraśu ādi utpadyamānam dṛśyate
varṇayanti ca bhāgavatāḥ kartuḥ jīvāt saṃkarṣaṇa saṃjñakāt karaṇam manaḥ pradyumna saṃjñakam utpadyate kartṛ jāt ca tasmāt aniruddha saṃjñakaḥ haṃkāraḥ utpadyate iti
na ca etat dṛṣṭāntam antareṇa adhyavasātum śaknumaḥ
na ca evaṃbhūtām śrutim upalabhāmahe
vijñāna ādi bhāve vā tad apratiṣedhaḥ
atha api syāt na ca ete saṃkarṣaṇa ādayaḥ jīva ādi bhāvena abhipreyante
kim tarhi īśvarāḥ eva ete sarve jñāna aiśvarya śakti bala vīrya tejobhiḥ aiśvarya dharmaiḥ anvitāḥ abhyupagamyante vāsudevāḥ eva ete sarve nirdoṣāḥ niradhiṣṭhānāḥ niravadyāḥ ca iti
tasmāt na ayam yathā varṇitaḥ utpatti asaṃbhavaḥ doṣaḥ prāpnoti iti
atrā ucyate evam api tad apratiṣedhaḥ utpatti asaṃbhavasya apratiṣedhaḥ prāpnoti eva ayam utpatti asaṃbhavaḥ doṣaḥ prakāra antareṇa iti abhiprāyaḥ
katham
yadi tāvat ayam abhiprāyaḥ paraspara bhinnāḥ eva ete vāsudeva ādayaḥ catvāraḥ īśvarāḥ tulya dharmāṇaḥ na eṣām eka ātmaka tvam asti iti tatas neka īśvara kalpanā ānarthakyam ekena eva īśvareṇa īśvara kārya siddheḥ
siddhānta hāniḥ ca bhagavān eva ekaḥ vāsudevaḥ paramārtha tattvam iti abhyupagamāt
atha ayam abhiprāyaḥ ekasya eva bhagavataḥ ete catvāraḥ vyūhāḥ tulya dharmāṇaḥ iti tathā api tad avasthaḥ evā utpatti asaṃbhavaḥ
na hi vāsudevāt saṃkarṣaṇasya utpattiḥ saṃbhavati saṃkarṣaṇāt ca pradyumnasya pradyumnāt ca aniruddhasya atiśaya abhāvāt
bhavitavyam hi kārya kāraṇayoḥ atiśayena yathā mṛd haṭayoḥ
na hi asati atiśaye kāryam kāraṇam iti avakalpate
na ca pañcarātra siddhāntibhiḥ vāsudeva ādiṣu ekasmin sarveṣu vā jñāna aiśvarya ādi tāratamya kṛtaḥ kaścid bhedaḥ bhyupagamyate
vāsudevāḥ eva hi sarve vyūhāḥ nirviśeṣāḥ iṣyante
na ca ete bhagavat vyūhāḥ catur saṃkhyāyām eva avatiṣṭheran brahma ādi stamba paryantasya samastasya eva jagataḥ bhagavat vyūha tva avagamāt
vipratiṣedhāt ca
vipratiṣedhaḥ ca asmin śāstre bahuvidhaḥ upalabhyate guṇa guṇi tva kalpanā ādi lakṣaṇaḥ
jñāna aiśvarya śakti bala vīrya tejāṃsi guṇāḥ ātmānaḥ eva ete bhagavantaḥ vāsudevāḥ ityādi darśanāt
veda vipratiṣedhaḥ ca bhavati caturṣu vedeṣu param śreyaḥ labdhvā śāṇḍilyaḥ idam śāstram adhigatavān ityādi veda nindā darśanāt
tasmāt asaṃgatā eṣā kalpanā iti siddham
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ

dvitīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
na viyat aśruteḥ
viyat adhikaraṇam
kim asya ākāśasya utpattiḥ asti uta na asti iti
tatra tāvat pratipadyate na viyat aśruteḥ iti
na khalu ākāśam utpadyate
kasmāt
aśruteḥ na hi asya utpatti prakaraṇe śravaṇam asti
chāndogye hi sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti sat śabda vācyam brahma prakṛtya tat aikṣata tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti ca pañcānām mahābhūtānām madhyamam tejaḥ ādi kṛtvā trayāṇām tejaḥ bannānām utpattiḥ śrāvyate
śrutiḥ ca naḥ pramāṇam atīndriya artha vijñāna utpattau
na ca atra śrutiḥ asti ākāśasya utpatti pratipādinī
tasmāt na ākāśasya utpattiḥ iti
asti tu
tuśabdaḥ pakṣa antara parigrahe
mā nāma ākāśasya chāndogye bhūt utpattiḥ
śruti antare tu asti
taittirīyakāḥ hi samāmananti satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti prakṛtya tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti
tatas ca śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ kvacid tejaḥ pramukhā sṛṣṭiḥ kvacid ākāśa pramukhā iti
nanu eka vākya tā anayoḥ śrutyoḥ yuktā
satyam sā yuktā na tu sā avagantum śakyate
kutas
tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvayena saṃbandha anupapatteḥ tat tejaḥ sṛjata tat ākāśam asṛjata iti
nanu sakṛt śrutasya api kartuḥ kartavya dvayena saṃbandhaḥ dṛśyate yathā saḥ sūpam paktvā odanam pacati iti evam tat ākāśam sṛṣṭvā tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti yojayiṣyāmi
na evam yujyate
prathama ja tvam hi chāndogye tejasaḥ vagamyate
taittirīyake ca ākāśasya
na ca ubhayoḥ prathama ja tvam saṃbhavati
etena itara śruti akṣara virodhaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti atra api tasmāt ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ tasmāt tejaḥ saṃbhūtam iti sakṛt śrutasya apādānasya saṃbhavanasya ca viyat tejobhyām yugapad saṃbandha anupapatteḥ vāyoḥ agniḥ iti ca pṛthak āmnānāt
asmin vipratiṣedhe kaścid āha
goṇī asambhavāt
na asti viyataḥ utpattiḥ aśruteḥ eva
yā tu itarā viyat utpatti vādinī śrutiḥ udāhṛtā sā gauṇī bhavitum arhati
kasmāt
asaṃbhavāt
na hi ākāśasya utpattiḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyā śrīmat kaṇabhuj abhiprāya anusāripu jīvatsu
te hi kāraṇa sāmagrī asaṃbhavāt ākāśasya utpattim vārayanti
samavāyi asamavāyi nimitta kāraṇebhyaḥ hi kila sarvam utpadyamānam samutpadyate
dravyasya ca eka jātīyakam anekam ca dravyam samavāyi kāraṇam bhavati
na ca ākāśasya eka jātīyakam anekam ca dravyam ārambhakam asti
yasmin samavāyi kāraṇe sati asamavāyi kāraṇe ca tad saṃyoge ākāśaḥ utpadyeta
tad abhāvāt tu tad anugraha pravṛttam nimitta kāraṇam dūra apetam eva ākāśasya bhavati
utpattimatām ca tejaḥ prabhṛtīnām pūrva uttara kālayoḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvyate prāk utpatteḥ prakāśa ādi kāryam na babhūva paścāt ca bhavati iti
ākāśasya punar na pūrva uttara kālayoḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyate
kim hi prāk utpatteḥ anavakāśam a suṣiram acchidram babhūva iti śakyate dhī avasātum
pṛthivī ādi vaidharmyāt ca vibhu tva ādi lakṣaṇāt ākāśasya aja tva siddhiḥ
tasmāt yathā loke ākāśam kuru ākāśaḥ jātaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ gauṇaḥ prayogaḥ bhavati yathā ca ghaṭa ākāśaḥ karaka ākāśaḥ gṛha ākāśaḥ iti ekasya api ākāśasya evaṃjātīyakaḥ bheda vyapadeśaḥ gauṇaḥ bhavati vede pi āraṇyān ākāśeṣu ālabheran iti
evam utpatti śrutiḥ api gauṇī draṣṭavyā
śabdāt ca
śabdaḥ khalu api ākāśasya aja tvam khyāpayati yatas āha vāyuḥ ca antarikṣam ca etat amṛtam iti
na hi amṛtasya utpattiḥ upapadyate
ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ iti ca ākāśena brahma sarva gata tva nitya tvābhyām dharmābhyām upamimānaḥ ākāśasya api tau dharmau sūcayati
na ca tādṛśasya utpattiḥ upapadyate
sa yathā anantaḥ yam ākāśaḥ evam anantaḥ ātmā veditavyaḥ iti ca udāharan ākāśa śarīram brahma ākāśaḥ ātmā iti ca
na hi ākāśasya utpattimat tve brahmaṇaḥ tena viśeṣaṇam saṃbhavati nīlena iva utpalasya
tasmāt nityam eva ākāśena sādhāraṇam brahma iti gamyate
syāt ca ekasya brahma śabda vat
idam pada uttaram sūtram
syāt etat
katham punar ekasya saṃbhūta śabdasya tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti asmin adhikāre pareṣu tejaḥ prabhṛtiṣu anuvartamānasya mukhya tvam saṃbhavati ākāśe ca gauṇa tvam iti
atas uttaram ucyate syāt ca ekasya api saṃbhūta śabdasya viṣaya viśeṣa vaśāt gauṇaḥ mukhyaḥ ca prayogaḥ brahma śabda vat
yathā ekasya api brahma śabdasya tapasā brahma vijijñāsasva tapaḥ brahma iti asmin adhikāre nna ādiṣu gauṇaḥ prayogaḥ ānande ca mukhyaḥ
yathā ca tapasi brahma vijñāna sādhane brahma śabdaḥ bhaktyā prayujyate añjasā tu vijñeye brahmaṇi tadvat
katham punar anutpattau nabhasaḥ ekam eva advitīyam iti iyam pratijñā samarthyate
nanu nabhasā dvitīyena sa dvitīyam brahma prāpnoti
katham ca brahmaṇi vidite sarvam viditam syāt iti tat ucyate ekam eva iti tāvat sva kārya apekṣayā upapadyate
yathā loke kaścid kumbhakāra kule pūrvedyus mṛd daṇḍa cakra ādīni ca upalabhya aparedyus ca nānāvidhāni amatrāṇi prasāritāni upalabhya brūyāt mṛd eva ekākinī pūrvedyus āsīt iti sa ca tayā avadhāraṇayā mṛd kārya jātam eva pūrvedyus na āsīt iti abhipreyāt na daṇḍa cakra ādi tadvat advitīya śrutiḥ adhiṣṭhātṛ antaram vārayati yathā mṛdaḥ matra prakṛteḥ kumbhakāraḥ dhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate na evam brahmaṇaḥ jagat prakṛteḥ anyaḥ dh
na ca nabhasā api dvitīyena sa dvitīyam brahma prasajyate
lakṣaṇa anyatva nimittam hi nānātvam
na ca prāk utpatteḥ brahma nabhasoḥ lakṣaṇa anyatvam asti kṣīra udakayoḥ iva saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ vyāpi tva amūrta tva ādi dharma sāmānyāt
sarga kāle tu brahma jagat utpādayitum yatate stimitam itarat tiṣṭhati tena anya tvam avasīyate
tathā ca ākāśa śarīram brahma ityādi śrutibhyaḥ pi brahma ākāśayoḥ abheda upacāra siddhiḥ
atas eva ca brahma vijñānena sarva vijñāna siddhiḥ
api ca sarvam kāryam utpadyamānam ākāśena a vyatirikta deśa kālam eva utpadyate brahmaṇā ca a vyatirikta deśa kālam eva ākāśam bhavati iti atas brahmaṇā tad kāryeṇa ca vijñātena saha vijñātam eva ākāśam bhavati yathā kṣīra pūrṇe ghaṭe katicid ap bindavaḥ prakṣiptāḥ santaḥ kṣīra grahaṇena eva gṛhītāḥ bhavanti
na hi kṣīra grahaṇāt ap bindu grahaṇam pariśiṣyate
evam brahmaṇā tad kāryaiḥ ca avyatirikta deśa kāla tvāt gṛhītam eva brahma grahaṇena nabhaḥ bhavati
tasmāt bhāktam nabhasaḥ saṃbhava śravaṇam iti
evam prāpte idam āha
pratijñā hāniḥ avyatirekāt śabdebhyaḥ
yena a śruta a śrutam bhavati a matam matam a vijñātam vijñātam iti ātmani khalu are dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idam sarvam viditam iti kasmin nu bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti na kācana mat bahirdhā vidyā asti iti ca evaṃrūpā prati vedāntam pratijñā vijñāyate
tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ evam ahāniḥ an uparodhaḥ syāt yadi a vyatirekaḥ kṛtsnasya vastu jātasya vijñeyāt brahmaṇaḥ syāt
vyatireke hi sati eka vijñānā anena sarvam vijñāyate iti iyam pratijñā hīyeta
sa ca avyatirekaḥ evam upapadyate yadi kṛtsnam vastu jātam ekasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpadyeta
śabdebhyaḥ ca prakṛti vikāra avyatireka nyāyena eva pratijñā siddhiḥ avagamyate
tathā hi yena aśruta aśrutam bhavati iti pratijñāya mṛd ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ kārya kāraṇa abheda pratipādana paraiḥ pratijñā eṣā samarthyate
tad sādhanāya eva ca uttare śabdāḥ sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam tat aikṣata tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti evam kārya jātam brahmaṇaḥ pradarśya a vyatirekam pradarśayanti aitadātmyam idam sarvam iti ārabhya ā prapāṭhaka parisamāpteḥ
tat yadi ākāśam na brahma kāryam syāt na brahmaṇi vijñāte ākāśam vijñāyeta
tatas ca pratijñāhāniḥ syāt
na ca pratijñā hānyā vedasya aprāmāṇyam yuktam kartum
tathā hi prati veda antam te te śabdāḥ tena tena dṛṣṭāntena tām eva pratijñām jñāpayanti idam sarvam yat ayam ātmā brahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt iti evamādayaḥ
tasmāt jvalana ādi vat eva gaganam api utpadyate
yat uktam aśruteḥ na viyat utpadyate iti tat ayuktam viyat utpatti viṣaya śruti antarasya darśita tvāt tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti
satyam darśitam viruddham tu tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti anena śruti antareṇa
na eka vākya tvāt sarva śrutīnām
bhavatu eka vākya tvam aviruddhānām
iha tu virodhaḥ uktaḥ sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvaya saṃbandha asaṃbhavāt dvayoḥ ca prathama ja tva asaṃbhavāt vikalpa asaṃbhavāt ca iti na eṣa doṣaḥ tejaḥ sargasya taittirīyake tṛtīya tva śravaṇāt tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agniḥ iti
aśakyā hi iyam śrutiḥ anyathā pariṇetum
śakyā tu pariṇetum chāndogya śrutiḥ tat ākāśam vāyum ca sṛṣṭvā tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti
na hi iyam śrutiḥ tejaḥ jani pradhānā satī śruti antara prasiddhām ākāśasya utpattim vārayitum śaknoti ekasya vākyasya vyāpāra dvaya asaṃbhavāt
sraṣṭā tu ekaḥ api krameṇa anekam sraṣṭavyam sṛjet iti eka vākya tva kalpanāyām saṃbhavantyām na viruddha artha tvena śrutiḥ hātavyā
na ca asmābhiḥ sakṛt śrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavya dvaya saṃbandhaḥ bhipreyate śruti antara vaśena sraṣṭavya antara upasaṃgrahāt
yathā ca sarvam khalu idam brahma tat jalān iti atra sākṣāt eva sarvasya vastu jātasya brahma ja tvam śrūyamāṇam na pradeśa antara vihitam tejaḥ pramukham utpatti kramam vārayati evam tejasaḥ api brahma ja tvam śrūyamāṇam na śruti antara vihitam nabhaḥ pramukham utpatti kramam vārayitum arhati
nanu śama vidhāna artham etat vākyam tad jalān iti śāntaḥ upāsīta iti śruteḥ
na etat sṛṣṭi vākyam
tasmāt etat na pradeśa antara prasiddham kramam anuroddhum arhati iti
tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti etat sṛṣṭi vākyam
tasmāt atra yathāśruti kramaḥ grahītavyaḥ iti
na iti ucyate
na hi tejaḥ prāthamya anurodhena śruti antara prasiddhaḥ viyat padārthaḥ parityaktavyaḥ bhavati padārtha dharma tvāt kramasya
api ca tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti na atra kramasya vācakaḥ sti
arthāt tu kramaḥ gamyate
sa ca vāyoḥ agniḥ iti anena śruti antara prasiddhena krameṇa nivāryate
vikalpa samuccayau tu viyat tejasoḥ prathama ja tva viṣayau asaṃbhava anabhyupagamābhyām nivāritaḥ
tasmāt na asti śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ
api ca chāndogye yena a śrutam śrutam bhavati iti etām pratijñām vākya upakrame śrutām samarthayitum a samāmnātam api viyat utpattau upasaṃkhyātavyam
kim aṅga punar taittirīyake samāmnātam nabhaḥ na saṃgṛhyate
yat ca uktam ākāśasya sarveṇa an anya deśa kāla tvāt brahmaṇā tad kāryaiḥ ca saha viditam eva tat bhavati
atas na pratijñā hīyate
na ca ekam eva advitīyam iti śruti kopaḥ bhavati kṣīrodaka vat brahma nabhasoḥ avyatireka upapatteḥ iti
atra ucyate na kṣīra udaka nyāyena idam eka vijñānena sarva vijñānam netavyam
mṛd ādi dṛṣṭānta praṇayanāt hi prakṛti vikāra nyāyena eva idam sarva vijñānam netavyam iti gamyate
kṣīrodaka nyāyena ca sarva vijñānam kalpyamānam na samyak vijñānam syāt
na hi kṣīra jñāna gṛhītasya udakasya samyak vijñāna gṛhīta tvam asti
na ca vedasya puruṣāṇām iva māyā alīka vañcana ādibhiḥ artha avadhāraṇam upapadyate
sa avadhāraṇā ca iyam ekam eva advitīyam iti śrutiḥ kṣīra udaka nyāyena nīyamānā pīḍyeta
na ca sva kārya apekṣayā idam vastu eka deśa viṣayam sarva vijñānam eva advitīya tā avadhāraṇam ca iti nyāyyam mṛd ādiṣu api hi tad saṃbhavāt na tat apūrva vat upanyasitavyam bhavati śvetaketo yat nu somya idam mahāmanāḥ anūcāna mānī stabdhaḥ syuta tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ yena a śrutam śrutam bhavati ityādinā
tasmāt aśeṣa vastu viṣayam eva idam sarva vijñānam sarvasya brahma kārya tā apekṣayā upanyasyate iti draṣṭavyam
yat punar etat uktam asaṃbhavāt gauṇī gaganasya utpatti śrutiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ
yāvadvikāram tu vibhāgaḥ loka vat
tu śabdaḥ saṃbhava āśaṅkā vyāvṛtti arthaḥ
na khalu ākāśa utpattau asaṃbhava āśaṅkā kartavyā
yatas yāvat kiṃcid vikāra jātam dṛśyate ghaṭa ghaṭikā udañcana ādi vā kaṭaka keyūra kuṇḍala ādi vā sūcī nārāca nistriṃśa ādi vā tāvān eva vibhāgaḥ loke lakṣyate
na tu avikṛtam kiṃcid kutaścid vibhaktam upalabhyate
vibhāgaḥ ca ākāśasya pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ vagamyate
tasmāt saḥ pi vikāraḥ bhavitum arhati
etena diś kāla manaḥ paramāṇu ādīnām kārya tvam vyākhyātam
nanu ātmā api ākāśa ādibhyaḥ vibhaktaḥ iti tasya api kārya tvam ghaṭa ādi vat prāpnoti
na ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti śruteḥ
yadi hi ātmā api vikāraḥ syāt tasmāt param anyat na śrutam iti ākāśa ādi sarvam kāryam nirātmakam ātmanaḥ kārya tve syāt
tathā ca śūnyavādaḥ prasajyeta
ātma tvāt ca ātmanaḥ nirākaraṇa śaṅkā anupapattiḥ na hi ātma āgantukaḥ kasyacid svayam siddha tvāt
na hi ātmā ātmanaḥ pramāṇam apekṣya sidhyati
tasya hi pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni asiddha prameya siddhaye upādīyante
na hi ākāśa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramāṇa nirapekṣāḥ svayam siddhāḥ kenacid abhyupagamyante
ātmā tu pramāṇa ādi vyavahāra āśraya tvāt prāk eva pramāṇa ādi vyavahārāt sidhyati
na ca īdṛśasya nirākaraṇam saṃbhavati
āgantukam hi vastu nirākriyate na svarūpam
yaḥ eva hi nirākartā tat eva tasya svarūpam
na hi agneḥ auṣṇyam agninā nirākriyate
tathā aham eva idānīm jānāmi vartamānam vastu aham eva atītam atītataram ca ajñāsiṣam aham eva anāgatam anāgatataram ca jñāsyāmi iti atīta anāgata vartamāna bhāvena anyathā bhavati api jñātavye na jñātuḥ anyathābhāvaḥ sti sarvadā vartamāna svabhāva tvāt
tathā bhasmībhavati api dehe na ātmanaḥ ucchedaḥ
vartamāna svabhāvāt anya svabhāva tvam vā na saṃbhāvayitum śakyam
evam apratyākhyeya svabhāva tvāt akārya tvam ātmānaḥ kārya tvam ca ākāśasya
yat tu uktam samāna jātīyam anekam kāraṇa dravyam vyomnaḥ na asti iti tat pratyucyate na tāvat samāna jātīyam eva ārabhate na bhinna jātīyam iti
na hi tantūnām tad saṃyogānām ca samāna jātīya tvam asti dravya guṇa tva abhyupagamāt
na ca nimitta kāraṇānām api turī vema ādīnām samāna jātīya tva niyamaḥ sti
syāt etat samavāyi kāraṇa viṣaye eva samāna jātīya tva abhyupagamaḥ na kāraṇa antara viṣayaḥ iti
tat api anaikāntikam
sūtra go vālaiḥ hi aneka jātīyaiḥ ekā rajjuḥ sṛjyamānā dṛśyate
tathā sūtraiḥ ūrṇā ādibhiḥ ca vicitrān kambalān vitanvate
sattva dravya tva ādi apekṣayā vā samāna jātīya tve kalpyamāne niyama ānarthakyam sarvasya sarveṇa samāna jātīyaka tvāt
na api anekam eva ārabhate na ekam iti niyamaḥ sti
aṇu manasoḥ ādya karma ārambha abhyupagamāt
ekaikaḥ hi paramāṇuḥ manaḥ ca ādyam karma ārabhate na dravya antaraiḥ saṃhatya iti abhyupagamyate
dravya ārambhe eva aneka ārambhaka tva niyamaḥ iti ced na
pariṇāma abhyupagamāt
bhavet eṣa niyamaḥ yadi saṃyoga sacivam dravyam dravya antarasya ārambhakam abhyupagamyeta
tat eva tu dravyam viśeṣa vat avasthā antaram āpadyamānam kāryam nāma abhyupagamyate
tat ca kvacid anekam pariṇamate mṛd bīja ādi aṅkura ādi bhāvena
kvacid ekam pariṇamate kṣīra ādi dadhi ādi bhāvena
na īśvara śāsanam iti anekam eva kāraṇam kāryam janayati iti
atas śruti prāmāṇyāt ekasmāt brahmaṇaḥ ākāśa ādi mahābhūta utpatti krameṇa jagat jātam iti niścīyate
tathā ca uktam upasaṃhāra darśanāt na iti ced na kṣīravat hi iti
yat ca uktam ākāśasya utpattau na pūrva uttara kālayoḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvayitum śakyate iti tat ayuktam
yena eva viśeṣeṇa pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ vyatiricyamānam nabhaḥ sva rūpa vat idānīm adhyavasīyate saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ prāk utpatteḥ na āsīt iti gamyate
yathā ca brahma na sthūla ādibhiḥ pṛthivī ādi svabhāvaiḥ svabhāvavat a sthūlam an aṇu ityādi śrutibhyaḥ evam ākāśa svabhāvena api na svabhāvavat anākāśam iti śruteḥ avagamyate
tasmāt prāk utpatteḥ an ākāśam iti sthitam
yat api uktam pṛthivī ādi vaidharmyāt ākāśasya aja tvam iti tat api asat śruti virodhe sati utpatti asaṃbhava anumānasya ābhāsa tva upapatteḥ utpatti anumānasya ca darśita tvāt
anityam ākāśam anitya guṇa āśraya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat ityādi prayoga saṃbhavāt ca
ātmani anaikāntikam iti ced na
tasya aupaniṣadam prati anitya guṇa āśraya tva asiddheḥ
vibhu tva ādīnām ca ākāśasya utpatti vādinam prati asiddha tvāt
yat ca uktam etat śabdāt ca iti tatra amṛta tva śrutiḥ tāvat viyati amṛtāḥ divaukasaḥ iti vat draṣṭavyā
utpatti pralayayoḥ upapādita tvāt
ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ iti api prasiddha mahat tvena ākāśa upamānam kriyate niratiśaya mahat tvāya na ākāśa sama tvāya yathā iṣuḥ iva savitā dhāvati iti kṣipra gati tvāya ucyate na iṣu tulya gati tvāya tadvat
etena ananta tva upamāna śrutiḥ vyākhyātā
jyāyān ākāśāt ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca brahmaṇaḥ sakāśāt ākāśasya ūna parimāṇa tva siddhiḥ na tasya pratimā asti iti ca brahmaṇaḥ darśayati
atas nyat ārtam iti ca brahmaṇaḥ nyeṣām ākāśa ādīnām ārta tvam darśayati
tapasi brahma śabda vat ākāśasya janma śruteḥ gauṇa tvam iti etat ākāśa saṃbhava śruti anumānābhyām parihṛtam
tasmāt brahma kāryam viyat iti siddham
etena mātariśvā vyākhyātaḥ
mātariśva adhikaraṇam
atideśaḥ yam
etena viyat vyākhyānena mātariśvā api viyat āśrayaḥ vāyuḥ vyākhyātaḥ
tatra api ete yathāyogam pakṣāḥ racayitavyāḥ na vāyuḥ utpadyate chandogānām utpatti prakaraṇe na āmnānāt iti ekaḥ pakṣaḥ asti tu taittirīyāṇām utpatti prakaraṇe āmnānam ākāśāt vāyuḥ iti pakṣa antaram
tatas ca śrutyoḥ vipratiṣedhe sati gauṇī vāyoḥ utpatti śrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti aparaḥ bhiprāyaḥ
asaṃbhavaḥ ca sā eṣā an astamitā devatā yat vāyuḥ iti astamaya pratiṣedhāt amṛta tva ādi śravaṇāt ca
pratijñā an uparodhāt yāvadvikāram ca vibhāga abhyupagamāt utpadyate vāyuḥ iti siddhāntaḥ
astamaya pratiṣedhaḥ para vidyā viṣayaḥ āpekṣikaḥ agni ādīnām iva vāyoḥ astamaya abhāvāt
kṛta pratividhānam ca amṛta tva ādi śravaṇam
nanu vāyoḥ ākāśasya ca tulyayoḥ utpatti prakaraṇe śravaṇa aśravaṇayoḥ ekam eva adhikaraṇam ubhaya viṣayam astu kim atideśena asati viśeṣaḥ iti ucyate satyam evam etat
tathā api manda dhiyām śabda mātra kṛta āśaṅkā nivṛtti arthaḥ yam atideśaḥ kriyate saṃvarga vidyā ādiṣu hi upāsyata vāyoḥ mahābhāga tva śravaṇāt astamaya pratiṣedha ādibhyaḥ ca bhavati nitya tva āśaṅkā kasyacid iti
asambhavaḥ tu sataḥ nupapatteḥ
asaṃbhava adhikaraṇam
viyat pavanayoḥ asaṃbhāvyamāna janmanoḥ api utpattim upaśrutya brahmaṇaḥ pi bhavet kutaścid utpattiḥ iti syāt kasyacid matiḥ
tathā vikārebhyaḥ eva ākāśa ādibhyaḥ uttareṣām vikārāṇām utpattim upaśrutya ākāśasya api vikārāt eva brahmaṇaḥ utpattiḥ iti kaścid manyeta
tām āśaṅkām apanetum idam sūtram asaṃbhavaḥ tu iti
na khalu brahmaṇaḥ sat ātmakasya kutaścid anyatas saṃbhave utpattiḥ āśaṅkitavyā
kasmāt
anupapatteḥ
sat mātram hi brahma
na tasya sat mātrāt evā utpattiḥ saṃbhavati asati atiśaye prakṛti vikāra bhāva anupapatteḥ
na api sat viśeṣāt dṛṣṭa viparyayāt sāmānyāt viśeṣāḥ utpadyamānāḥ dṛśyante mṛd ādeḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ na tu viśeṣebhyaḥ sāmānyam
na api asataḥ nirātmaka tvāt
katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti ca ākṣepa śravaṇāt
sa kāraṇam karaṇa adhipa adhipaḥ na ca asya kaścid janitā na ca adhipaḥ iti ca brahmaṇaḥ janayitāram vārayati
viyat pavanayoḥ punarutpattiḥ pradarśitā na tu brahmaṇaḥ sā asti iti vaiṣamyam
na ca vikārebhyaḥ vikāra antara utpatti darśanāt brahmaṇaḥ vikāra tvam bhavitum arhati mūlaprakṛti anabhyupagame navasthā prasaṅgāt
yā mūlaprakṛtiḥ abhyupagamyate tat eva ca naḥ brahma iti avirodhaḥ
tejaḥ taḥ tathā hi āha
tejaḥ dhi karaṇam
chāndogye sat mūla tvam tejasaḥ śrāvitam taittirīyake tu vāyu mūla tvam
tatra tejaḥ yonim prati śruti vipratipattau satyām prāptam tāvat brahma yonikam tejaḥ iti
kutas
sa devaḥ iti upakramya tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti upadeśāt
sarva vijñāna pratijñāyāḥ ca brahma prabhava tve sarvasya saṃbhavāt
tad jalān iti ca aviśeṣa śruteḥ
etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ iti ca upakramya śruti antare sarvasya aviśeṣeṇa brahma ja tva upadeśāt
taittirīyake ca sa tapaḥ taptvā
idam sarvam asṛjata
yat idam kiṃca iti aviśeṣa śravaṇāt
tasmāt vāyoḥ agniḥ iti krama upadeśaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ vāyoḥ anantaram agniḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti evam prāpte ucyate tejaḥ atas mātariśvanaḥ jāyate iti
kasmāt
tathā hi āha vāyoḥ agniḥ iti
avyavahite hi tejasaḥ brahma ja tve sati asati vāyu ja tve vāyoḥ agniḥ iti iyam śrutiḥ kadarthitā syāt
nanu krama arthā eṣā bhaviṣyati iti uktam
na iti brūmaḥ tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti purastāt saṃbhavati apādānasya ātmanaḥ pañcamī nirdeśāt tasya eva ca saṃbhavateḥ iha adhikārāt parastāt api tad adhikāre pṛthivyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ iti apādāna pañcamī darśanāt vāyoḥ agniḥ iti apādāna pañcamī eva eṣā iti gamyate
api ca vāyoḥ ūrdhvam agniḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti kalpyaḥ upapadārtha yogaḥ klṛptaḥ tu kāraka artha yogaḥ vāyoḥ agniḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti
tasmāt eṣā śrutiḥ vāyu yoni tvam tejasaḥ vagamayati
nanu itarā api śrutiḥ brahma yoni tvam tejasaḥ vagamayati tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti
na tasyāḥ pāraṃparya ja tve pi avirodhāt
yadā api hi ākāśam vāyum ca sṛṣṭvā vāyu bhāva āpannam brahma tejaḥ sṛjata iti kalpyate tadā api brahma ja tvam tejasaḥ na virudhyate yathā tasyāḥ śrṛtam tasyāḥ dadhi tasyāḥ āmikṣā ityādi
darśayati ca brahmaṇaḥ vikāra ātmanā avasthānam iti
tathā ca īśvara smaraṇam bhavati buddhiḥ jñānam asaṃmohaḥ ityādi anukramya bhavanti bhāvāḥ bhūtānām mattaḥ eva pṛthagvidhāḥ iti
yadi api buddhi ādayaḥ sva kāraṇebhyaḥ pratyakṣam bhavantaḥ dṛśyante tathā api sarvasya bhāva jātasya sākṣāt praṇāḍyā vā īśvara vaṃśya tvāt
etena akrama sṛṣṭi vādinyaḥ śrutayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ tāsām sarvathā upapatteḥ kramavat sṛṣṭi vādinīnām tu anyathā anupapatteḥ
pratijñā api sat vaṃśya tva mātram apekṣate na avyavahita janya tvam iti avirodhaḥ
āpaḥ
ap adhikaraṇam
atas tathā hi āha iti anuvartate
āpaḥ ataḥ tejasaḥ jāyante
kasmāt
tathā hi āha tat apaḥ sṛjate iti agneḥ āpaḥ iti ca
sati vacane na asti saṃśayaḥ
tejasaḥ tu sṛṣṭim vyākhyāya pṛthivyāḥ vyākhyāsyan apaḥ ntariyām iti āpaḥ iti sūtrayāṃbabhūva
pṛthivī adhikāra rūpa śabda antarebhyaḥ
pṛthivī adhikāra adhikaraṇam
tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣanta bahvyaḥ syāma prajāyemahi iti tāḥ annam asṛjanta iti śrūyate
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim anena anna śabdena vrīhi yava ādi abhyavahāryam vai odana ādi ucyate kim vā pṛthivī iti
tatra prāptam tāvat vrīhi yava ādi odana ādi vā parigrahītavyam iti
tatra hi anna śabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ loke
vākya śeṣaḥ u pi etam artham upodbalayati tasmāt yatra kvacana varṣati tat eva bhūyiṣṭham annam bhavati iti vrīhi yava ādi eva hi sati varṣaṇe bahu bhavati na pṛthivī iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ pṛthivī eva iyam anna śabdena adbhyaḥ jāyamānā vivakṣyate iti
kasmāt
adhikārāt rūpāt śabda antarāt ca
adhikāraḥ tāvat tat tejaḥ sṛjata tat apaḥ sṛjata iti mahābhūta viṣayaḥ vartate
tatra krama prāptām pṛthivīm mahābhūtam vilaṅghya na akasmāt vrīhi ādi parigrahaḥ nyāyyaḥ
tathā rūpam api vākya śeṣe pṛthivī anuguṇam dṛśyate yat kṛṣṇam tat annasya iti
na hi odana ādeḥ abhyavahāryasya kṛṣṇa tva niyamaḥ u sti na api vrīhi ādīnām
nanu pṛthivyāḥ api nā eva kṛṣṇa tva niyamaḥ sti payaḥ pāṇḍurasya aṅgāra rohitasya ca kṣetrasya darśanāt
na ayam doṣaḥ bāhulya apekṣa tvāt
bhūyiṣṭham hi pṛthivyāḥ kṛṣṇam rūpam na tathā śveta rohite
paurāṇikāḥ api pṛthivī chāyām śarvarīm upadiśanti sā ca kṛṣṇa ābhāsā iti atas kṛṣṇam rūpam pṛthivyāḥ iti śliṣyate
śruti antaram api samāna adhikāram adabhyaḥ pṛthivī iti bhavati tat yat apām śaraḥ āsīt tat samahanyata sā pṛthivī abhavat iti ca
pṛthivyāḥ tu vrīhi ādeḥ utpattim darśayati pṛthivyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ oṣadhībhyaḥ annam iti ca
evam adhikāra ādiṣu pṛthivyāḥ pratipādakeṣu satsu kutas vrīhi ādi pratipattiḥ
prasiddhiḥ api adhikāra ādibhiḥ eva bādhyate
vākya śeṣaḥ u pi pārthiva tvāt annādi asya tad dvāreṇa pṛthivyāḥ eva adbhyaḥ prabhava tvam sūcayati iti draṣṭavyam
tasmāt pṛthivīyam anna śabdaḥ iti
tad abhidhyānāt eva tu tad liṅgāt saḥ
tad abhidhyāna adhikaraṇam
kim imāni viyat ādīni bhūtāni svayam eva sva vikārān sṛjanti āhosvit parameśvaraḥ eva tena tena ātmanā avatiṣṭhamānaḥ bhidhyāyan tam tam vikāram sṛjati iti saṃdehe sati prāptam tāvat svayam eva sṛjanti iti
kutas
ākāśāt vāyuḥ vāyoḥ agniḥ ityādi svātantrya śravaṇāt
nanu acetanānām svatantrāṇām pravṛttiḥ pratiṣiddhā
na eṣa doṣaḥ tat tejaḥ aikṣata tāḥ āpaḥ aikṣanta iti ca bhūtānām api cetana tva śravaṇāt iti
evam prāpte abhidhīyate saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ tena tena ātmanā avatiṣṭhamānaḥ bhidhyāyan tam tam vikāram sṛjati iti
kutas
tad liṅgāt
tathā hi śāstram yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan yaḥ pṛthivyāḥ antaraḥ yam pṛthivī na veda yasya pṛthivī śarīram yaḥ pṛthivīm antaraḥ yamayati iti evaṃjātīyakam sādhyakṣāṇām eva bhūtānām pravṛttim darśayati
tathā sā u kāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti prastutya sat ca tyat ca abhavat tat ātmānam svayam akuruta iti ca tasya eva ca sarva ātma bhāvam darśayati
yat tu īkṣaṇa śravaṇam ap tejasoḥ tat parameśvara āveśa vaśāt eva draṣṭavyam sti draṣṭā iti īkṣitṛ antara pratiṣedhāt prakṛta tvāt ca sataḥ īkṣituḥ tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti iti atra
viparyayeṇa tu te upapadyate ca
viparyaya adhikaraṇam
bhūtānām utpatti kramaḥ cintitaḥ
atha idānīm apyaya kramaḥ cintyate kim aniyatena krameṇa apyayaḥ uta utpatti krameṇa athavā tad viparītena iti
trayaḥ pi ca utpatti sthiti pralayāḥ bhūtānām brahma āyattāḥ śrūyante yatas vai imāni bhūtāni jāyante
yena jātāni jīvanti
yat prayanti abhisaṃviśanti iti
tatra aniyamaḥ viśeṣāt iti prāptam
athavā utpatteḥ kramasya śruta tvāt pralayasya api krama ākāṅkṣiṇaḥ saḥ eva kramaḥ syāt iti
evam prāptam tatas brūmaḥ viparyayeṇa tu pralaya kramaḥ atas utpatti kramāt bhavitum arhati
tathā hi loke dṛśyate yena krameṇa sopānam ārūḍhaḥ tatas viparītena krameṇa avarohati iti
api ca dṛśyate mṛdaḥ jātam ghaṭa śarāva ādi apyaya kāle mṛd bhāvam apyeti adbhyaḥ ca jātam himakaraka ādi ap bhāvam apyeti iti
atas ca upapadyate etat yat pṛthivī adbhyaḥ jātā satī sthiti kāla vyatikrāntau apaḥ apīyāt
āpaḥ ca tejasaḥ jātāḥ satyaḥ tejaḥ apīyuḥ
evam krameṇa sūkṣmam sūkṣmataram ca anantaram anantarataram kāraṇam apītya sarvam kārya jātam parama kāraṇam parama sūkṣmam ca brahma apyeti iti veditavyam
na hi sva kāraṇa vyatikrameṇa kāraṇa kāraṇe kārya apyayaḥ nyāyyaḥ
smṛtau api utpatti krama viparyayeṇa eva apyaya kramaḥ tatra tatra darśitaḥ jagat pratiṣṭhā devarṣe pṛthivī apsu pralīyate
jyotiṣi āpaḥ pralīyante jyotiḥ vāyau pralīyate iti evamādau
utpatti kramaḥ tu utpattau eva śruta tvāt na apyaye bhavitum arhati
na ca asau ayogya tvāt apyayena ākāṅkṣyate
na hi kārye dhriyamāṇe kāraṇasya apyayaḥ yuktaḥ kāraṇa apyaye kāryasya avasthāna anupapatteḥ
kārya apyaye tu kāraṇasya avasthānam yuktam mṛd ādiṣu evam dṛṣṭa tvāt
antarā vijñāna manasī krameṇa tad liṅgāt iti ced na aviśeṣāt
antarā vijñāna adhikaraṇam
bhūtānām utpatti pralayau anuloma pratiloma kramābhyām bhavataḥ iti uktam
ātma ādiḥ utpattiḥ pralayaḥ ca ātma antaḥ iti api uktam
sa indriyasya tu manasaḥ buddheḥ ca sadbhāvaḥ prasiddhaḥ śruti smṛtyoḥ buddhim tu sārathim viddhi manaḥ pragraham eva ca
indriyāṇi hayān āhuḥ ityādi liṅgebhyaḥ
tayoḥ api kasmiṃścid antarāle krameṇa utpatti pralayau upasaṃgrāhyau sarvasya vastu jātasya brahma ja tva abhyupagamāt
api ca ātharvaṇe utpatti prakaraṇe bhūtānām ātmanaḥ ca antarāle karaṇāni anukramyante etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca
kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇī iti
tasmāt pūrva ukta utpatti pralaya krama bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ bhūtānām iti ced na
aviśeṣāt yadi tāvat bhautikāni karaṇāni tatas bhūta utpatti pralayābhyām eva eṣām utpatti pralayau bhavataḥ iti na etayoḥ krama antaram mṛgyam
bhavati ca bhautika tve liṅgam karaṇānām anna mayam hi somya manaḥ āpaḥ mayaḥ prāṇaḥ tejaḥ mayī vāc iti evaṃjātīyakam
vyapadeśaḥ pi kvacid bhūtānām karaṇānām ca brāhmaṇa parivrājaka nyāyena netavyaḥ
atha tu abhautikāni karaṇāni tathā api bhūta utpatti kramaḥ na karaṇaiḥ viśiṣyate prathamam karaṇāni utpadyante caramam bhūtāni prathamam vā bhūtāni utpadyante caramam karaṇāni iti
ātharvaṇe tu samāmnāya krama mātram karaṇānām bhūtānām ca na tatra utpatti kramaḥ ucyate
tathā anyatra api pṛthak eva bhūta kramāt karaṇa kramaḥ āmnāyate prajāpatiḥ vai idam agre āsīt saḥ ātmānam aikṣata sa manaḥ sṛjata tat manaḥ eva āsīt tat ātmānam aikṣata tat vācam asṛjata ityādinā
tasmāt nā asti bhūta utpatti kramasya bhaṅgaḥ
carācara vyapāśrayaḥ tu syāt tad vyapadeśaḥ bhāktaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt
carācara vyapāśraya adhikaraṇam
staḥ jīvasya api utpatti pralayau jātaḥ devadattaḥ mṛtaḥ devadattaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakāt laukika vyapadeśāt jātakarma ādi saṃskāra vidhānāt ca iti syāt kasyacid bhrāntiḥ
tām apanudāmaḥ
na jīvasya utpatti pralayau staḥ śāstra phala saṃbandha upapatteḥ
śarīra anuvināśini hi jīve śarīra antara gata iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra arthau vidhi pratiṣedhau anarthakau syātām
śrūyate ca jīva apetam vāva kila idam mriyate na jīvaḥ mriyate iti
nanu laukikaḥ janma maraṇa vyapadeśaḥ jīvasya darśitaḥ
satyam darśitaḥ
bhāktaḥ tu eṣa jīvasya janma maraṇa vyapadeśaḥ
kimāśrayaḥ punar ayam mukhyaḥ yad apekṣayā bhāktaḥ iti
ucyate carācara vyapāśrayaḥ
sthāvara jaṅgama śarīra viṣayau janma maraṇa śabdau
sthāvara jaṅgamāni hi bhūtāni jāyante ca mriyante ca
atas tad viṣayau janma maraṇa śabdau mukhyau santau tad sthe jīvātmani upacaryete tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt śarīra prādurbhāva tirobhāvayoḥ hi satoḥ janma maraṇa śabdau bhavataḥ na asatoḥ
na hi śarīra saṃbandhāt anyatra jīvaḥ jātaḥ mṛtaḥ vā kenacid lakṣyate
sa vai ayam puruṣaḥ jāyamānaḥ śarīram abhisaṃpadyamānaḥ saḥ utkrāman mriyamāṇaḥ iti ca śarīra saṃyoga viyoga nimittau eva janma maraṇa śabdau darśayati
jātakarma ādi vidhānam api deha prādurbhāva apekṣam eva draṣṭavyam abhāvāt jīva prādurbhāvasya
jīvasya parasmāt ātmanaḥ utpattiḥ viyat ādīnām iva asti na asti vā iti etat uttareṇa sūtreṇa vakṣyati
deha āśrayau tāvat jīvasya sthūlau utpatti pralayau na staḥ iti etat anena sūtreṇa avocat
na ātmā śruteḥ nitya tvāt ca tābhyaḥ
ātma adhikaraṇam
asti ātmā jīva ākhyaḥ śarīra indriya pañjara adhyakṣaḥ karma phala saṃbandhī
sa kim vyoma ādi vat utpadyate brahmaṇaḥ āhosvit brahma vat eva na utpadyate iti śruti vipratipatteḥ viśayaḥ
kāsucid śrutiṣu agni visphuliṅga ādi nidarśanaiḥ rjīvātmanaḥ parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpattiḥ āmnāyate
kāsucid tu avikṛtasya eva parasya brahmaṇaḥ kārya praveśena jīva bhāvaḥ vijñāyate na ca utpattiḥ āmnāyate iti
tatra prāptam tāvat utpadyate jīvaḥ iti
kutas
pratijñā an uparodhāt eva
ekasmin vidite sarvam idam viditam iti iyam pratijñā sarvasya vastu jātasya brahma prabhava tve sati nā uparudhyeta tattva antara tve tu jīvasya pratijñā iyam uparudhyeta
na ca avikṛtaḥ paramātmā eva jīvaḥ iti śakyate vijñātum lakṣaṇa bhedāt apahata pāpma tva ādi dharmakaḥ hi paramātmā tad viparītaḥ hi jīvaḥ
vibhāgāt ca asya vikāra tva siddhiḥ yāvān hi ākāśa ādiḥ pravibhaktaḥ sa sarvaḥ vikāraḥ
tasya ca ākāśa ādeḥ utpattiḥ samadhigatā
jīvātmā api puṇya apuṇya karmā sukha duḥkha yuj pratiśarīram pravibhaktaḥ iti tasya api prapañca utpatti avasare utpattiḥ bhavitum arhati
api ca yathā agneḥ kṣudrāḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vyuccaranti evam eva asmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ iti prāṇa ādeḥ bhogya jātasya sṛṣṭim śiṣṭvā sarve ete ātmānaḥ vyuccaranti iti bhoktṛṇām ātmanām pṛthak sṛṣṭim śāsti
yathā su dīptāt pāvakāt visphuliṅgāḥ sahasraśas prabhavante sarūpāḥ
tathā akṣarāt vividhāḥ somya bhāvāḥ prajāyante tatra ca eva apiyanti iti ca jīvātmanām utpatti pralayau ucyete sarūpa vacanāt jīvātmānaḥ hi paramātmanā sarūpāḥ bhavanti caitanya yogāt
na ca kvacid aśravaṇam anyatra śrutam vārayitum arhati śruti antara gatasya api aviruddhasya adhikasya arthasya sarvatra upasaṃhartavya tvāt
praveśa śrutiḥ api evam sati vikāra bhāva āpattyā eva vyākhyātavyā tat ātmānam svayam akuruta ityādi vat
tasmāt utpadyate jīvaḥ iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ na ātmā jīvaḥ utpadyate iti
kasmāt
aśruteḥ
na hi asya utpatti prakaraṇe śravaṇam asti bhūyaḥsu pradeśeṣu
nanu kvacid aśravaṇam anyatra śrutam na vārayati iti uktam
satyam uktam
utpattiḥ eva tu asya na saṃbhavati iti vadāmaḥ
kasmāt
nitya tvāt ca tābhyaḥ ca śabdāt aja tva ādibhyaḥ ca nitya tvam hi asya śrutibhyaḥ vagamyate tathā aja tvam avikāri tvam avikṛtasya eva brahmaṇaḥ jīva ātmanā avasthānam brahma ātmanā ca iti
na ca evaṃrūpasya utpattiḥ upapadyate
tāḥ kāḥ śrutayaḥ
na jīvaḥ mriyate sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ bhayaḥ brahma na jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ajaḥ nityaḥ śāśvataḥ yam purāṇaḥ tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva anuprāviśat anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi saḥ eṣaḥ iha praviṣṭaḥ ā nakha agrebhyaḥ tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi ayam ātmā brahma sarva anubhūḥ iti evamādyāḥ nitya tva vādinyaḥ satyaḥ jīvasya utpattim pratibadhnanti
nanu pravibhakta tvāt vikāraḥ vikāra tvāt ca utpadyate iti uktam
atra ucyate na asya pravibhāgaḥ svatas sti ekaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā iti śruteḥ
buddhi ādi upādhi nimittam tu asya pravibhāga pratibhānam ākāśasya iva ghaṭa ādi saṃbandha nimittam
tathā ca śāstram sa vai ayam ātmā brahma vijñāna mayaḥ manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ cakṣuḥ mayaḥ śrotra mayaḥ iti evamādi brahmaṇaḥ eva avikṛtasya sataḥ sya ekasya aneka buddhi ādi maya tvam darśayati
tad maya tvam ca asya tad vivikta svarūpa anabhivyaktyā tad uparakta svarūpa tvam strī mayaḥ jālmaḥ ityādi vat draṣṭavyam
yat api kvacid asya utpatti pralaya śravaṇam tat api atas eva upādhi saṃbandhāt netavyam upādhi utpattyā asya utpattiḥ tad pralayena ca pralayaḥ iti
tathā ca darśayati prajñāna ghanaḥ eva etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni eva anu vinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti
tathā upādhi pralayaḥ eva ayam na ātma vilayaḥ iti etat api atra eva mā bhagavān moha antam āpīpadat na vai aham imam vijānāmi na pretya saṃjñā asti iti praśna pūrvakam pratipādayati na vai are ham moham bravīmi avināśī vai are yam ātmā an ucchitti dharmā mātrā saṃsargaḥ tu asya bhavati iti
pratijñā an uparodhaḥ pi avikṛtasya eva brahmaṇaḥ jīva bhāva abhyupagamāt
lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ pi anayoḥ upādhi nimittaḥ eva atas ūrdhvam vimokṣāya eva brūhi iti ca prakṛtasya eva vijñāna mayasya ātmanaḥ sarva saṃsāra dharma pratyākhyānena paramātma bhāva pratipādanāt
tasmāt na eva ātmā utpadyate pravilīyate ca iti
jñaḥ taḥ eva
jñā adhikaraṇam
sa kim kāṇabhujānām iva āgantuka caitanyaḥ svatas cetanaḥ āhosvit sāṃkhyānām iva nitya caitanya svarūpaḥ eva iti vādi vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
āgantukam ātmanaḥ caitanyam ātma manaḥ saṃyoga jam agni ghaṭa saṃyoga ja rohita ādi guṇavat iti prāptam
nitya caitanya tve hi supta mūrchita graha āviṣṭānām api caitanyam syāt
te pṛṣṭāḥ santaḥ na kiṃcid vayam cetayemahi iti jalpanti
svasthāḥ ca cetayamānāḥ dṛśyante
atas kādācitka caitanya tvāt āgantuka caitanyaḥ ātmā iti
evam prāpte abhidhīyate jñaḥ nitya caitanyaḥ yam ātmā atas eva yasmāt eva na utpadyate param eva brahma avikṛtam upādhi saṃparkāt jīva bhāvena avatiṣṭhate
parasya hi brahmaṇaḥ caitanya svarūpa tvam āmnātam vijñānam ānandam brahma satyam jñānam anantam brahma anantaraḥ bāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ prajñāna ghanaḥ eva ityādiṣu śrutiṣu
tat eva ced param brahma jīvaḥ tasmāt jīvasya api nitya caitanya svarūpa tvam agni auṣṇya prakāśa vat iti gamyate
vijñāna maya prakriyāyām ca śrutayaḥ bhavanti a suptaḥ suptān abhicākaśīti atra ayam puruṣaḥ svayam jyotiḥ bhavati iti na hi vijñātuḥ vijñāteḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate iti evaṃrūpāḥ
atha yaḥ veda idam jighrāṇi iti saḥ ātmā iti ca sarvaiḥ karaṇa dvāraiḥ idam veda idam veda iti vijñānena anusaṃdhānāt tad rūpa tva siddhiḥ
nitya caitanya svarūpa tve ghrāṇa ādi ānarthakyam iti ced na gandha ādi viṣaya viśeṣa pariccheda ārthatvāt
tathā hi darśayati gandhāya ghrāṇam ityādi
yat tu supta ādayaḥ na cetayante iti tasya śrutyā eva parihāraḥ bhihitaḥ suṣuptam prakṛtya yat vai tat na paśyati paśyan vai tat na paśyati
na hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate vināśi tvāt
na tu tad dvitīyam asti tatas yat paśyet ityādinā
etat uktam bhavati viṣaya abhāvāt iyam acetayamānatā na caitanya abhāvāt iti yathā viyat āśrayasya prakāśasya prakāśya abhāvāt anabhivyaktiḥ na svarūpa abhāvāt tadvat
vaiśeṣika ādi tarkaḥ ca śruti virodhaḥ ābhāsībhavati
tasmāt nitya caitanya svarūpaḥ eva ātmā iti niścinumaḥ
utkrānti gati āgatīnām
utkrānti gati adhikaraṇam
idānīm tu kiṃparimāṇaḥ jīvaḥ iti cintyate kim aṇu parimāṇaḥ uta madhyama parimāṇaḥ āhosvit mahā parimāṇaḥ iti
nanu ca na ātmā utpadyate nitya caitanyaḥ ca ayam iti uktam
atas ca paraḥ eva ātmā jīvaḥ iti āpatati
parasya ca ātmanaḥ nanta tvam āmnātam
tatra kutas jīvasya parimāṇa cintā avatāraḥ iti
ucyate satyam etat
utkrānti gati āgati śravaṇāni tu jīvasya paricchedam prāpayanti
sva śabdena ca asya kvacid aṇu parimāṇa tvam āmnāyate
tasya sarvasya an ākula tva upapādanāya ayam ārambhaḥ
tatra prāptam tāvat utkrānti gati āgatīnām śravaṇāt paricchinnaḥ ṇu parimāṇaḥ jīvaḥ iti
utkrāntiḥ tāvat sa yadā asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati saha eva etaiḥ sarvaiḥ utkrāmati iti
gatiḥ api ye vai ke ca asmāt lokāt prayanti candramasam eva te sarve gacchanti iti
āgatiḥ api tasmāt lokāt punar aiti asmai lokāya karmaṇe iti
āsām utkrānti gatyāgatīnām śravaṇāt paricchinnaḥ tāvat jīvaḥ iti prāpnoti na hi vibhoḥ calanam avakalpate iti
sati paricchede śarīra parimāṇa tvasya ārhata parīkṣāyām nirasta tvāt aṇuḥ ātmā iti gamyate
sva ātmanā ca uttarayoḥ
utkrāntiḥ grāma svāmya nivṛtti vat deha svāmya nivṛttyā karma kṣayeṇa avakalpeta
uttare tu gati āgatī na acalataḥ saṃbhavataḥ
sva ātmanā hi tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ bhavati gameḥ kartṛ stha kriyā tvāt
amadhyama parimāṇasya ca gati āgatī aṇu tve eva saṃbhavataḥ
satyoḥ ca gati āgatyoḥ utkrāntiḥ api apasṛptiḥ eva dehāt iti pratīyate
na hi an apasṛptasya dehāt gati āgatī syātām deha pradeśānām ca utkrāntau apādāna tva vacanāt cakṣuṣṭas vā mūrdhnaḥ vā anyebhyaḥ vā śaḥ īra deśebhyaḥ iti
saḥ etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyādadānaḥ hṛdayam eva anvavakrāmati śukram ādāya punar aiti sthānam iti ca antare śarīre śārīrasya gati āgatī bhavataḥ
tasmāt api asya aṇu tva siddhiḥ
na aṇuḥ a tad śruteḥ iti ced na itara adhikārāt
atha api syāt na aṇuḥ ayam ātmā
kasmāt
a tad śruteḥ
aṇu tva viparīta parimāṇa śravaṇāt iti arthaḥ
sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti evaṃjātīyakā hi śrutiḥ ātmanaḥ ṇu tve vipratiṣidhyeta iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ
kasmāt
itara adhikārāt parasya hi ātmanaḥ prakriyāyām eṣā parimāṇa antara śrutiḥ parasya eva ātmanaḥ prādhānyena vedānteṣu veditavya tvena prakṛta tvāt virajaḥ paras ākāśāt iti evaṃvidhāt ca parasya eva ātmanaḥ tatra tatra viśeṣa adhikārāt
nanu yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti śārīre eva mahat tva saṃbandhi tvena pratinirdiśyate śāstra dṛṣṭyā tu eṣa nirdeśaḥ vāmadeva vat draṣṭavyaḥ
tasmāt prājña viṣaya tvāt parimāṇa antara śravaṇasya na jīvasya aṇu tvam virudhyate
sva śabda unmānābhyām ca
itas ca aṇuḥ ātmā yatas sākṣāt eva asya aṇu tva vācī śabdaḥ śrūyate eṣaḥ ṇuḥ ātmā cetasā veditavyaḥ yasmin prāṇaḥ pañcadhā saṃviveśa iti
prāṇa saṃbandhāt ca jīvaḥ eva ayam aṇuḥ abhihitaḥ iti gamyate
tathā unmānam api jīvasya aṇimānam gamayati vāla agra śata bhāgasya śatadhā kalpitasya ca
bhāgaḥ jīvaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ iti
ārā agra mātraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti ca unmāna antaram
nanu aṇu tve sati eka deśa sthasya sakala deha gata upalabdhiḥ virudhyate
dṛśyate ca jāhnavī hrada nimagnānām sarva aṅga śaitya upalabdhiḥ nidāgha samaye ca sakala śarīra paritāpa upalabdhiḥ iti atas uttaram paṭhati
avirodhaḥ candana vat
yathā hi haricandana binduḥ śarīra eka deśa saṃbaddhaḥ san sakala deha vyāpinam āhlādam karoti evam ātmā api deha eka deśa sthaḥ sakala deha vyāpinīm upalabdhim kariṣyati
tvak saṃbandhāt ca asya sakala śarīra gatā vedanā na virudhyate
tvac ātmanoḥ hi saṃbandhaḥ kṛtsnāyām tvaci vartate
tvac ca kṛtsna śarīra vyāpinī iti
avasthiti vaiśeṣyāt iti ced nā abhyupagamāt hṛdi hi
atra āha yat uktam avirodhaḥ candana vat iti tat ayuktam dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭāntikayoḥ atulya tvāt
siddhe hi ātmanaḥ deha eka deśa stha tve candana dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavati pratyakṣam tu candanasya avasthiti vaiśeṣyam eka deśa stha tvam sakala deha āhlādanam ca
ātmanaḥ punar sakala deha upalabdhi mātram pratyakṣam na eka deśa varti tvam
anumeyam tu tat iti yat api ucyeta na ca atra anumānam saṃbhavati kim ātmanaḥ sakala śarīra gatā vedanā tvac indriyasya iva sakala deha vyāpinaḥ sataḥ kim vā vibhoḥ nabhasaḥ iva āhosvit candana bindoḥ iva aṇoḥ eka deśa sthasya iti saṃśaya anativṛtteḥ iti
atra ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ
kasmāt
abhyupagamāt
abhyupagamyate hi candanasya iva deha eka deśa vṛtti tvam avasthiti vaiśeṣyam
katham iti ucyate hṛdi hi eṣaḥ ātmā paṭhyate vedānteṣu hṛdi hi eṣaḥ ātmā sa vai eṣaḥ ātmā hṛdi katamaḥ ātmā iti yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ ityādi upadeśebhyaḥ
tasmāt dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭāntikayoḥ avaiṣamyāt yuktam eva etat avirodhaḥ candana vat iti
guṇāt vā loka vat
caitanya guṇa vyāpteḥ vā aṇoḥ api sataḥ jīvasya sakala deha vyāpi kāryam na virudhyate yathā loke maṇi pradīpa prabhṛtīnām apavaraka eka deśa vartinām api prabhā apavaraka vyāpinī satī kṛtsne pavarake kāryam karoti tadvat
syāt kadācid candanasya sāvayava tvāt sūkṣma avayava visarpaṇena api sakala dehe āhlādayitṛ tvam
na tu aṇoḥ jīvasya avayavāḥ santi yaiḥ ayam sakala deham visarpet iti āśaṅkya guṇāt vā loka vat iti uktam
katham punar guṇaḥ guṇi vyatirekeṇa anyatra varteta
na hi paṭasya śuklaḥ guṇaḥ paṭa vyatirekeṇa anyatra vartamānaḥ dṛśyate
pradīpa prabhā vat bhavet iti ced na
tasyāḥ api dravya tva abhyupagamāt nibiḍa avayavam hi tejaḥ dravyam pradīpaḥ pravirala avayavam tu tejaḥ dravyam eva prabhā iti atas uttaram paṭhati
vyatirekaḥ gandha vat
yathā guṇasya api sataḥ gandhasya gandhavat dravya vyatirekeṇa vṛttiḥ bhavati aprāpteṣu api kusuma ādiṣu gandhavatsu kusuma gandha upalabdheḥ
evam aṇoḥ api sataḥ jīvasya caitanya guṇa vyatirekaḥ bhaviṣyati
atas ca anaikāntikam etat guṇa tvāt rūpa ādi vat āśraya viśleṣa anupapattiḥ iti guṇasya eva sataḥ gandhasya āśraya viśleṣa darśanāt
gandhasya api saha eva āśrayeṇa viśleṣaḥ iti ced na
yasmāt mūla dravyāt viśleṣaḥ tasya kṣaya prasaṅgāt
a kṣīyamāṇam api tat pūrva avasthātaḥ gamyate
anyathā tad pūrva avasthaiḥ guru tva ādibhiḥ hīyeta
syāt etat gandha āśrayāṇām viśliṣṭānām avayavānām alpa tvāt san api viśleṣaḥ na upalakṣyate
sūkṣmāḥ hi gandha paramāṇavaḥ sarvatas viprasṛtāḥ gandha buddhim utpādayanti nāsikāpuṭam anupraviśantaḥ iti ced na
atīndriya tvāt paramāṇūnām sphuṭa gandha upalabdheḥ ca nāgakesara ādiṣu
na ca loke pratītiḥ gandhavat dravyam āghrātam iti
gandhaḥ eva āghrātaḥ iti tu laukikāḥ pratiyanti
rūpa ādiṣu āśraya vyatireka anupalabdheḥ gandhasya api ayuktaḥ āśraya vyatirekaḥ iti ced na
pratyakṣa tvāt anumāna apravṛtteḥ
tasmāt yat yathā loke dṛṣṭam tat tathā eva anumantavyam nirūpakaiḥ na anyathā
na hi rasaḥ guṇaḥ jihvayā upalabhyate iti atas rūpa ādayaḥ pi guṇāḥ jihvayā eva upalabhyeran iti niyantum śakyate
tathā ca darśayati
hṛdaya āyatana tvam aṇu parimāṇa tvam ca ātmanaḥ abhidhāya tasya eva ā lomabhyaḥ ā nakha agrebhyaḥ iti caitanyena guṇena samasta śarīra vyāpi tvam darśayati
pṛthak upadeśāt
prajñayā śarīram samāruhya iti ca ātma prajñayoḥ kartṛ karaṇa bhāvena pṛthak upadeśāt caitanya guṇena eva asya śarīra vyāpi tā gamyate
tat eṣām prāṇānām vijñānena vijñānam ādāya iti ca kartuḥ śārīrāt pṛthak vijñānasya upadeśaḥ etam eva abhiprāyam upodbalayati
tasmāt aṇuḥ ātmā iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ
tad guṇa sāra tvāt tu tad vyapadeśaḥ prājña vat
tu śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati
na etat asti aṇuḥ ātmā iti
utpatti aśravaṇāt parasya eva tu brahmaṇaḥ praveśa śravaṇāt tādātmya upadeśāt ca param eva brahma jīvaḥ iti uktam
param eva ced brahma jīvaḥ tasmāt yāvat param brahma tāvān eva jīvaḥ bhavitum arhati
parasya ca brahmaṇaḥ vibhu tvam āmnātam
tasmāt vibhuḥ jīvaḥ
tathā ca sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ jīva viṣayāḥ vibhu tva vādāḥ śrautāḥ smārtāḥ ca samarthitāḥ bhavanti
na ca aṇoḥ jīvasya sakala śarīra gatā vedanā upapadyate
tvak saṃbandhāt syāt iti ced na
kaṇṭaka todane sakala śarīra gatā eva vedanā prasajyeta tvac kaṇṭakayoḥ hi saṃyogaḥ kṛtsnāyām tvaci vartate tvac ca kṛtsna śarīra vyāpinī iti
pāda tale eva tu kaṇṭaka nunnaḥ vedanām pratilabhate
na ca aṇoḥ guṇa vyāptiḥ upapadyate guṇasya guṇi deśa tvāt
guṇa tvam eva hi guṇinam an āśritya guṇasya hīyeta
pradīpa prabhāyāḥ ca dravya antara tvam vyākhyātam
gandhaḥ pi guṇa tva abhyupagamāt sa āśrayaḥ eva saṃcaritum arhati anyathā guṇa tva hāni prasaṅgāt
tathā ca uktam bhagavatā dvaipāyanena upalabhya apsu ced gandham kecid brūyuḥ anaipuṇāḥ
pṛthivyām eva tam vidyāt apaḥ vāyum ca saṃśritam iti
yadi ca caitanyam jīvasya samasta śarīram vyāpnuyāt na aṇuḥ jīvaḥ syāt
caitanyam eva hi asya svarūpam agneḥ iva auṣṇya prakāśau na atra guṇa guṇi vibhāgaḥ vidyate iti
śarīra parimāṇa tvam ca pratyākhyātam
pariśeṣāt vibhuḥ jīvaḥ
katham tarhi aṇu tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ iti atas āha tad guṇa sāra tvāt tu tad vyapadeśaḥ iti
tasyāḥ buddheḥ guṇāḥ tad guṇāḥ icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham iti evamādayaḥ tad guṇāḥ sāraḥ pradhānam yasya ātmanaḥ saṃsāri tve saṃbhavati sa tad guṇa sāraḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tad guṇa sāra tvam
na hi buddheḥ guṇaiḥ vinā kevalasya ātmanaḥ saṃsāri tvam asti
