buddhi upādhi dharma adhyāsa nimittam hi kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva ādi lakṣaṇam saṃsāri tvam akartuḥ abhoktuḥ ca asaṃsāriṇaḥ nitya muktasya sataḥ ātmanaḥ
tasmāt tad guṇa sāra tvāt buddhi parimāṇena asya parimāṇa vyapadeśaḥ tad utkrānti ādibhiḥ ca asya utkrānti ādi vyapadeśaḥ na svatas
tathā ca vālāgra śata bhāgasya śatadhā kalpitasya ca
bhāgaḥ jīvaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sa ca ānantyāya kalpate iti aṇu tvam jīvasya uktvā tasya eva punar ānantyam āha
tat ca evam eva samañjasam syāt yadi aupacārikam aṇu tvam jīvasya bhavet pāramārthikam ca ānantyam
na hi ubhayam mukhyam avakalpeta
na ca ānantyam aupacārikam iti śakyam vijñātum sarva upaniṣatsu brahma ātma bhāvasya pratipipādayiṣita tvāt
tathā itarasmin api unmāne buddheḥ guṇena ātma guṇena ca eva ārā agra mātraḥ hi avaraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti ca buddhi guṇa saṃbandhena eva ārā agra mātra tām śāsti na svena eva ātmanā
eṣaḥ ṇuḥ ātmā cetasā veditavyaḥ iti atra api na jīvasya aṇu parimāṇa tvam śiṣyate parasya eva ātmanaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi anavagrāhya tvena jñāna prasāda gamya tvena ca prakṛta tvāt jīvasya api ca mukhya aṇu parimāṇa tva anupapatteḥ
tasmāt durjñāna tva abhiprāyam idam aṇu tva vacanam upādhi abhiprāyam vā draṣṭavyam
tathā prajñayā śarīram samāruhya iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu api bheda upadeśeṣu buddhyā eva upādhi bhūtayā jīvaḥ śarīram samāruhya iti evam yojayitavyam vyapadeśa mātram vā śilāputrakasya śarīram ityādi vat
na hi atra guṇa guṇi vibhāgaḥ vidyate iti uktam
hṛdaya āyatana tva vacanam api buddheḥ eva tad āyatana tvāt
tathā utkrānti ādīnām api upādhyāyattatām darśayati kasmin nu aham utkrāntaḥ utkrāntaḥ bhaviṣyāmi kasmin vā pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmi iti sa prāṇam asṛjata iti
utkrānti abhāve hi gati agatyoḥ api abhāvaḥ vijñāyate
na hi an apasṛptasya dehāt gatya āgatī syātām
evam upādhi guṇa sāra tvāt jīvasya aṇu tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ prājña vat
yathā prājñasya paramātmanaḥ saguṇeṣu upāsaneṣu upādhi guṇa sāra tvāt aṇīyaḥ tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ aṇīyān vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ sarva gandhaḥ sarva rasaḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evaṃprakāraḥ tadvat
syāt etat yadi buddhi guṇa sāra tvāt ātmanaḥ saṃsāri tvam kalpyeta tatas buddhi ātmanoḥ bhinnayoḥ saṃyoga avasānam avaśyaṃbhāvi iti atas buddhi viyoge sati ātmanaḥ vibhaktasya anālakṣya tvāt asattvam asaṃsāri tvam vā prasajyeta iti atas uttaram paṭhati
yāvadātmabhāvi tvāt ca na doṣaḥ tad darśanāt
na iyam anantara nirdiṣṭa doṣa prāptiḥ āśaṅkanīyā
kasmāt
yāvat ātma bhāvi tvāt buddhi saṃyogasya yāvat ayam ātmā saṃsārī bhavati yāvat asya samyak darśanena saṃsāri tvam na nivartate tāvat asya buddhyā saṃyogaḥ na śāmyati
yāvat eva ca ayam buddhi upādhi saṃbandhaḥ tāvat eva asya jīva tvam saṃsāri tvam ca
paramārthataḥ tu na jīvaḥ nāma buddhi upādhi parikalpita svarūpa vyatirekeṇa asti
na hi nitya mukta svarūpāt sarvajñāt īśvarāt anyaḥ cetanaḥ dhātuḥ dvitīyaḥ vedānta artha nirūpaṇāyām upalabhyate sti draṣṭā śrotā mantā vijñātā na anyat atas sti draṣṭṛ śrotṛ mantṛ vijñātṛ tattvam asi aham brahma asmi ityādi śruti śatebhyaḥ
katham punar avagamyate yāvat ātma bhāvī buddhi saṃyogaḥ iti
tad darśanāt iti āha
tathā hi śāstram darśayati yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ sa samānaḥ san ubhau lokau anusaṃcarati dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva ityādi
tatra vijñāna mayaḥ iti buddhi mayaḥ iti etat uktam bhavati pradeśa antare vijñāna mayaḥ manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ cakṣuḥ mayaḥ śrotra mayaḥ iti vijñāna mayasya manaḥ ādibhiḥ saha pāṭhāt
buddhi maya tvam ca tad guṇa sāra tvam eva abhipreyate yathā loke strī mayaḥ devadattaḥ iti strī rāga ādi pradhānaḥ bhidhīyate tadvat
sa samānaḥ san ubhau lokau anusaṃcarati iti ca loka antara gamane pi aviyogam buddhyā darśayati
kena samānaḥ
tayā eva buddhyā iti gamyate saṃnidhānāt
tat ca darśayati dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti
etat uktam bhavati na ayam svatas dhyāyati na api calati dhyāyantyām buddhau dhyāyati iva calantyām buddhau calati iva iti
api ca mithyā jñāna puraḥsaraḥ yam ātmanaḥ buddhi upādhi saṃbandhaḥ
na ca mithyājñānasya samyak jñānāt anyatra nivṛttiḥ asti iti atas yāvat brahma ātma tā anavabodhaḥ tāvat ayam buddhi upādhi saṃbandhaḥ na śāmyati
darśayati ca veda aham etam puruṣam mahāntam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt
tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate yanāyaḥ iti
nanu suṣupta pralayayoḥ na śakyate buddhi saṃbandhaḥ ātmanaḥ bhyupagantum satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati svam api itas bhavati iti vacanāt kṛtsna vikāra pralaya abhyupagamāt ca
tat katham yāvadātmabhāvitvam buddhi saṃbandhasya iti atrā ucyate
puṃstva ādivat tvasya sataḥ abhivyakti yogāt
yathā loke puṃstva ādīni bīja ātmanā vidyamānāni eva bālya ādiṣu anupalabhyamānāni avidyamāna vat abhipreyamāṇāni yauvana ādiṣu āvirbhavanti
na avidyamānāni utpadyante ṣaṇḍa ādīnām api tad utpatti prasaṅgāt evam ayam api buddhi saṃbandhaḥ śakti ātmanā vidyamānaḥ eva suṣupta pralayayoḥ punar prabodha prasavayoḥ āvirbhavati
evam hi etat yujyate
na hi ākasmikī kasyacid utpattiḥ saṃbhavati atiprasaṅgāt
darśayati ca suṣuptāt utthānam avidyā ātmaka bīja sadbhāva kāritam sati saṃpadya na viduḥ sati saṃpadyāmahe iti te iha vyāghraḥ vā siṃhaḥ vā ityādinā
tasmāt siddham etat yāvat ātma bhāvī buddhi ādi upādhi saṃbandhaḥ iti
nitya upalabdhi anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ nyatara niyamaḥ vā nyathā
tat ca ātmanaḥ upādhi bhūtam antaḥkaraṇam manaḥ buddhiḥ vijñānam cittam iti ca anekadhā tatra tatra abhilapyate
kvacid ca vṛtti vibhāgena saṃśaya ādi vṛttikam manaḥ iti ucyate niścaya ādi vṛttikam buddhiḥ iti
tat ca evam bhūtam antaḥkaraṇam avaśyam asti iti abhyupagantavyam anyathā hi anabhyupagamyamāne tasmin nitya upalabdhi anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ syāt ātma indriya viṣayāṇām upalabdhi sādhanānām saṃnidhāne sati nityam eva upalabdhiḥ prasajyeta
atha sati api hetu samavadhāne phala abhāvaḥ tatas nityam evā anupalabdhiḥ prasajyeta
na ca evam dṛśyate
athavā anyatarasya ātmanaḥ indriyasya vā śakti pratibandhaḥ bhyupagantavyaḥ
na ca ātmanaḥ śakti pratibandhaḥ saṃbhavati avikriya tvāt
na api indriyasya
na hi tasya pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ apratibaddha śaktikasya sataḥ kasmāt śaktiḥ pratibadhyeta
tasmāt yasya avadhāna anavadhānābhyām upalabdhi anupalabdhī bhavataḥ tat manaḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ anyatramanāḥ abhūvam na adarśam anyatramanāḥ abhūvam na aśrauṣam iti manasā hi eva paśyati manasā śrṛṇoti iti ca
kāma ādayaḥ ca asya vṛttayaḥ iti darśayati kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ vicikitsā śraddhā aśraddhā dhṛtiḥ adhṛtiḥ hrīḥ dhīḥ bhīḥ iti etat sarvam manaḥ eva iti
tasmāt yuktam etat tad guṇa sāra tvāt tad vyapadeśaḥ iti
kartā śāstra arthavat tvāt
kartṛ adhikaraṇam
tad guṇa sāra tva adhikāreṇa eva aparaḥ jīva dharmaḥ prapañcyate
kartā ca ayam jīvaḥ syāt
kasmāt
śāstra arthavat tvāt evam ca yajeta juhuyāt dadyāt iti evaṃvidham vidhi śāstram arthavat
vihāra upadeśāt
itas ca jīvasya kartṛ tvam yat jīva prakriyāyām saṃdhye sthāne vihāram upadiśati saḥ īyate mṛtaḥ yatra kāmam iti sve śarīre yathākāmam parivartate iti ca
upādānāt
itas ca asya kartṛ tvam yat jīva prakriyāyām eva karaṇānām upādānam saṃkīrtayati tat eṣām prāṇānām vijñānena vijñānam ādāya iti prāṇān gṛhītvā iti ca
vyapadeśāt ca kriyāyām na ced nirdeśa viparyayaḥ
itas ca jīvasya kartṛ tvam yat asya laukikīṣu vaidikīṣu ca kriyāsu kartṛ tvam vyapadiśati śāstram vijñānam yajñam tanute karmāṇi tanute ca iti
nanu vijñāna śabdaḥ buddhau samadhigataḥ katham anena jīvasya kartṛ tvam sūcyate iti na iti ucyate jīvasya eva eṣa nirdeśaḥ na buddheḥ
na ced jīvasya syāt nirdeśa viparyayaḥ syāt vijñānena iti evam niradekṣyat
tathā hi anyatra buddhi vivakṣāyām vijñāna śabdasya karaṇa vibhakti nirdeśaḥ dṛśyate tat eṣām prāṇānām vijñānena vijñānam ādāya iti
iha tu vijñānam yajñam tanute iti kartṛ sāmānādhikaraṇya nirdeśāt buddhi vyatiriktasya eva ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam sūcyate iti adoṣaḥ
atra āha yadi buddhi vyatiriktaḥ jīvaḥ kartā syāt sa svatantraḥ san priyam hitam ca eva ātmanaḥ niyamena saṃpādayet na viparītam
viparītam api tu saṃpādayan upalabhyate
na ca svatantrasya ātmanaḥ īdṛśī pravṛttiḥ aniyamena upapadyate iti atas uttaram paṭhati
upalabdhi vat aniyamaḥ
yathā ayam ātma upalabdhim prati svatantraḥ aniyamena iṣṭam aniṣṭam ca upalabhate evam aniyamena eva iṣṭam aniṣṭam ca saṃpādayiṣyati
upalabdhau api asvātantryam upalabdhi hetu upādāna upalambhāt iti ced na viṣaya prakalpanā mātra prayojana tvāt upalabdhi hetūnām
upalabdhau tu an anya apekṣa tvam ātmanaḥ caitanya yogāt
api ca arthakriyāyām api na atyantam ātmanaḥ svātantryam asti deśa kāla nimitta viśeṣa apekṣa tvāt
na ca sahāya apekṣasya kartuḥ kartṛ tvam nivartate
bhavati hi edha udaka ādi apekṣasya api paktuḥ paktṛ tvam
sahakāri vaicitryāt ca iṣṭa aniṣṭa arthakriyāyām aniyamena pravṛttiḥ ātmanaḥ na virudhyate
śakti viparyayāt
itas ca vijñāna vyatiriktaḥ jīvaḥ kartā bhavitum arhati
yadi punar vijñāna śabda vācyā buddhiḥ eva kartrī syāt tatas śakti viparyayaḥ syāt karaṇa śaktiḥ buddheḥ hīyeta kartṛ śaktiḥ ca āpadyeta
satyām ca buddheḥ kartṛ śaktau tasyāḥ eva ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tvam abhyupagantavyam ahaṃkāra pūrvikāyāḥ eva pravṛtteḥ sarvatra darśanāt aham gacchāmi aham āgacchāmi aham bhuñje aham pibāmi iti ca
tasyāḥ ca kartṛ śakti yuktāyāḥ sarva artha kāri karaṇam anyat kalpayitavyam
śaktaḥ u pi hi san kartā karaṇam upādāya kriyāsu pravartamānaḥ dṛśyate
tatas ca saṃjñā mātre vivādaḥ syāt na vastu bhedaḥ kaścid karaṇa vyatiriktasya kartṛ tva abhyupagamāt
samādhi abhāvāt ca
yaḥ u pi ayam aupaniṣada ātma pratipatti prayojanaḥ samādhiḥ upadiṣṭaḥ vedānteṣu ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ saḥ nveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ om iti evam dhyāyatha ātmānam iti evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ saḥ u pi asati ātmanaḥ kartṛ tve na upapadyeta
tasmāt api asya kartṛ tva siddhiḥ
yathā ca takṣa ubhayathā
takṣa adhikaraṇam
evam tāvat śāstra arthavat tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ kartṛ tvam śārīrasya pradarśitam
tat punar svābhāvikam vā syāt upādhi nimittam vā iti cintyate
tatra etaiḥ eva śāstra arthavat tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ svābhāvikam kartṛ tvam apavāda hetu abhāvāt iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ na svābhāvikam kartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ saṃbhavati anirmokṣa prasaṅgāt
kartṛ tva svabhāva tve hi ātmanaḥ na kartṛ tvāt nirmokṣaḥ saṃbhavati agneḥ iva auṣṇyāt
na ca kartṛ tvāt anirmuktasya asti puruṣa artha siddhiḥ kartṛ tvasya duḥkha rūpa tvāt
nanu sthitāyām api kartṛ tva śaktau kartṛ tva kārya parihārāt puruṣa arthaḥ setsyati
tad parihāraḥ ca nimitta parihārāt yathā agneḥ dahana śakti yuktasya api kāṣṭha viyogāt dahana kārya abhāvaḥ tadvat na nimittānām api śakti lakṣaṇena saṃbandhena saṃbaddhānām atyanta parihāra asaṃbhāvāt
nanu mokṣa sādhana vidhānāt mokṣaḥ setsyati na sādhana āyattasya anitya tvāt
api ca nitya śuddha mukta ātma pratipādanāt mokṣa siddhiḥ abhimatā
tādṛś ātma pratipādanam ca na svābhāvike kartṛ tve
tasmāt upādhi dharma adhyāsena eva ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam na svābhāvikam
tathā ca śrutiḥ dhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti ātma indriya manaḥ yuktam bhoktā iti āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ iti ca upādhi saṃpṛktasya eva ātmanaḥ bhoktṛ tva ādi viśeṣa lābham darśayati
na hi vivekinām parasmāt anyaḥ jīvaḥ nāma kartā bhoktā vā vidyate draṣṭā ityādi śravaṇāt
paraḥ eva tarhi saṃsārī kartā bhoktā ca prasajyeta
parasmāt anyaḥ ced citimān jīvaḥ kartā buddhi ādi saṃghāta vyatiriktaḥ na syāt na avidyā pratyupasthāpita tvāt kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tvayoḥ
tathā ca śāstram yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tat itaraḥ itaram paśyati iti avidyā avasthāyām kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve darśayitvā vidyā avasthāyām te eva kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve nivārayati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet iti
tathā svapna jāgaritayoḥ ātmanaḥ upādhi saṃparka kṛtam śramam śyenasya iva ākāśe viparipatataḥ śrāvayitvā tad abhāvam suṣuptau prājñena ātmanā saṃpariṣvaktasya śrāvayati tat vai asya etat āpta kāmam ātma kāmam akāmam rūpam śoka antaram iti ārabhya eṣā asya paramā gatiḥ eṣā asya paramā saṃpad eṣā u sya paramaḥ lokaḥ eṣā u sya paramaḥ ānandaḥ iti upasaṃhārāt
tat etat āha ācāryaḥ yathā ca takṣobhayathāḥ iti
tu arthe ca ayam caḥ paṭhitaḥ
na evam mantavyam svābhāvikam eva ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam agneḥ iva auṣṇyam iti
yathā tu takṣā loke vāsi ādi karaṇa hastaḥ kartā duḥkhī bhavati saḥ eva sva gṛham prāptaḥ vimukta vāsi ādi karaṇaḥ svasthaḥ nirvṛtaḥ nirvyāpāraḥ sukhī bhavati evam avidyā pratyupasthāpita dvaita saṃpṛktaḥ ātmā svapna jāgarita avasthayoḥ kartā duḥkhī bhavati saḥ tad śrama apanuttaye svam ātmānam param brahma praviśya vimukta kārya karaṇa saṃghātaḥ kartā sukhī bhavati saṃprasāda avasthāyām tathā mukti avasthāyām api avidyā dhvānt
takṣa dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca etāvatā aṃśena draṣṭavyaḥ takṣā hi viśiṣṭeṣu takṣaṇa ādi vyāpāreṣu apekṣya eva pratiniyatāni karaṇāni kartā bhavati sva śarīreṇa tu akartā eva
evam ayam ātmā sarva vyāpāreṣu apekṣya eva manaḥ ādīni karaṇāni kartā bhavati sva ātmanā tu kartā eva iti
na tu ātmanaḥ takṣṇaḥ iva avayavāḥ santi yaiḥ hasta ādibhiḥ iva vāsi ādīni takṣā manaḥ ādīni karaṇāni ātmā upādadīta nyasyet vā
yat tu uktam śāstra arthavat tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ svābhāvikam ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam iti tat na vidhi śāstram tāvat yathāprāptam kartṛ tvam upādāya kartavya viśeṣam upadiśati na kartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ pratipādayati
na ca svābhāvikam asya kartṛ tvam asti brahma ātmatva upadeśāt iti avocāma
tasmāt avidyā kṛtam kartṛ tvam upādāya vidhi śāstram pravartiṣyate
kartā vijñāna ātmā puruṣaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakam api śāstram anuvāda rūpatvāt yathāprāptam eva avidyā kṛtam kartṛ tvam anuvadiṣyati
etena vihāra upādāne parihṛte tayoḥ api anuvāda rūpa tvāt
nanu saṃdhye sthāne prasupteṣu karaṇeṣu sve śarīre yathākāmam parivartate iti vihāraḥ upadiśyamānaḥ kevalasya ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam āvahati
tathā upādāne pi tat eṣām prāṇānām vijñānena vijñānam ādāya iti karaṇeṣu karma karaṇa vibhaktī śrūyamāṇe kevalasya ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam gamayataḥ iti
atrā ucyate na tāvat saṃdhye sthāne tyantam ātmanaḥ karaṇa viramaṇam asti sa dhīḥ svapnaḥ bhūtvā imam lokam atikrāmati iti tatra api dhī saṃbandha śravaṇāt
tathā ca smaranti indriyāṇām uparame manaḥ nu uparatam yadi
sevate viṣayān eva tat vidyāt svapna darśanam iti
kāma ādayaḥ ca manasaḥ vṛttayaḥ iti śrutiḥ
tāḥ ca svapne dṛśyante
tasmāt samanāḥ eva svapte viharati
vihāraḥ pi ca tatratyaḥ vāsanā mayaḥ eva na tu pāramārthikaḥ sti
tathā ca śrutiḥ ivakāra anubaddham eva svapna vyāpāram varṇayati uta iva strībhiḥ saha modamānaḥ jakṣat uta iva api bhayāni paśyan iti
laukikāḥ api tathā eva svapnam kathayanti ārukṣam iva giri śrṛṅgam adrākṣam iva vana rājim iti
tathā upādāne pi yadi api karaṇeṣu karma karaṇa vibhakti nirdeśaḥ tathā api tad saṃpṛktasya eva ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam draṣṭavyam kevale kartṛ tva asaṃbhavasya darśita tvāt
bhavati ca loke neka prakārā vivakṣā yodhāḥ yudhyante yodhaiḥ rājā yudhyate iti
api ca asmin upādāne karaṇa vyāpāra uparama mātram vivakṣyate na svātantryam kasyacid abuddhi pūrvakasya api svāpe karaṇa vyāpāra uparam asya dṛṣṭa tvāt
yaḥ tu ayam vyapadeśaḥ darśitaḥ vijñānam yajñam tanute iti sa buddheḥ eva kartṛ tvam prāpayati vijñāna śabdasya tatra prasiddha tvāt manaḥ nantaram pāṭhāt ca tasya śraddhā eva śiraḥ iti ca vijñāna mayasya ātmanaḥ śraddhā ādi avayava tva saṃkīrtanāt śraddhā ādīnām ca buddhi dharma tva prasiddheḥ vijñānam devāḥ sarve brahma jyeṣṭham upāsate iti ca vākya śeṣāt jyeṣṭha tvasya ca prathama ja tvasya buddhau prasiddha tvāt saḥ eṣa vācaḥ c
na ca buddheḥ śakti viparyayaḥ karaṇānām kartṛ tva abhyupagame bhavati sarva kārakāṇām eva sva sva vyāpāreṣu kartṛ tvasya avaśyaṃbhāvi tvāt
upalabdhi apekṣam tu eṣām karaṇānām karaṇa tvam
sā ca ātmanaḥ
na ca tasyām api asya kartṛ tvam asti nitya upalabdhi svarūpa tvāt
ahaṃkāra pūrvakam api kartṛ tvam na upalabdhuḥ bhavitum arhati ahaṃkārasya api upalabhyamāna tvāt
na ca evam sati karaṇa antara kalpanā prasaṅgaḥ buddheḥ karaṇa tva abhyupagamāt
samādhi abhāvaḥ tu śāstra arthavat tvena eva parihṛtaḥ yathāprāptam eva kartṛ tvam upādāya samādhi vidhānāt
tasmāt kartṛ tvam api ātmanaḥ upādhi nimittam eva iti sthitam
parāt tu tad śruteḥ
parāyatta adhikaraṇam
yat idam avidyā avasthāyām upādhi nibandhanam kartṛ tvam jīvasya abhihitam tat kim an apekṣya īśvaram bhavati āhosvit īśvara apekṣam iti bhavati vicāraṇā
tatra prāptam tāvat na īśvaram apekṣate jīvaḥ kartṛ tve iti
kasmāt
apekṣā prayojana abhāvāt
ayam hi jīvaḥ svayam eva rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa prayuktaḥ kāraka antara sāmagrī saṃpannaḥ kartṛ tvam anubhavitum śaknoti
tasya kim īśvaraḥ kariṣyati
na ca loke kṛṣi ādikāsu kriyāsu anaḍuha ādi vat iti
kleśa ātmakena ca kartṛ tvena jantūn saṃsṛjataḥ īśvarasya nairghṛṇyam prasajyeta
viṣama phalam ca eṣām kartṛ tvam vidadhataḥ vaiṣamyam
nanu vaiṣamya nairghṛṇye na sāpekṣa tvāt iti uktam satyam uktam sati tu īśvarasya sāpekṣa tva saṃbhave
sāpekṣa tvam ca īśvarasya saṃbhavati satoḥ jantūnām dharma adharmayoḥ
tayoḥ ca sadbhāvaḥ sati jīvasya kartṛ tve
tat eva ced kartṛ tvam īśvara apekṣam syāt kiṃviṣayam īśvarasya sāpekṣa tvam ucyeta
a kṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca evam jīvasya prasajyeta
tasmāt svatas eva asya kartṛ tvam iti etām prāptim tu śabdena vyāvartya pratijānīte parāt iti
avidyā avasthāyām kārya karaṇa saṃghāta aviveka darśinaḥ jīvasya avidyā timira andhasya sataḥ parasmāt ātmanaḥ karma adhyakṣāt sarva bhūta adhivāsāt sākṣiṇaḥ cetayituḥ īśvarāt tad anujñayā kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva lakṣaṇasya saṃsārasya siddhiḥ
tad anugraha hetukena eva ca vijñānena mokṣa siddhiḥ bhavitum arhati
kutas
tad śruteḥ
yadi api doṣa prayuktaḥ sāmagrī saṃpannaḥ ca jīvaḥ yadi api ca loke kṛṣi ādiṣu karmasu na īśvara kāraṇa tvam prasiddham tathā api sarvāsu eva pravṛttiṣu īśvaraḥ hetu kartā iti śruteḥ avasīyate
tathā hi śrutiḥ bhavati eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ unninīṣate
eṣa hi eva asādhu karma kārayati tam yam adhas ninīṣate iti yaḥ ātmani tiṣṭhan ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati iti ca evaṃjātīyakā
nanu evam īśvarasya kārayitṛ tve sati vaiṣamya nairghṛṇye syātām akṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca jīvasya iti
na iti ucyata
kṛta prayatna apekṣaḥ tu vihita pratiṣiddha a vaiyarthya ādibhyaḥ
tu śabdaḥ codita doṣa vyāvartana arthaḥ
kṛtaḥ yaḥ prayatnaḥ jīvasya dharma adharma lakṣaṇaḥ tad apekṣaḥ eva enam īśvaraḥ kārayati
atas ca ete coditāḥ doṣāḥ na prasajyante jīva kṛta dharma adharma vaiṣamya apekṣaḥ eva tat tat phalāni viṣamam vibhajet parjanya vat īśvaraḥ nimitta tva mātreṇa yathā loke nānāvidhānām guccha gulma ādīnām vrīhi yava ādīnām ca asādhāraṇebhyaḥ sva sva bījebhyaḥ jāyamānānām sādhāraṇam nimittam bhavati parjanyaḥ na hi asati parjanye rasa puṣpa phala palāśa ādi vaiṣamyam teṣām jāyate na api asatsu sva sva bījeṣu evam jīva kṛta prayatna ap
nanu kṛta prayatna apekṣa tvam eva jīvasya parāyatte kartṛ tve nā upapadyate nā eṣa doṣaḥ
parāyatte hi kartṛ tve karoti eva jīvaḥ kurvantam hi tam īśvaraḥ kārayati
api ca pūrva prayatnam apekṣya idānīm kārayati pūrvataram ca prayatnam apekṣya pūrvam akārayat iti anādi tvāt saṃsārasya iti anavadyam
katham punar avagamyate kṛta prayatna apekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ iti
vihita pratiṣiddha a vaiyarthya ādibhyaḥ iti āha
evam hi svarga kāmaḥ yajeta brāhmaṇaḥ na hantavyaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakasya vihitasya pratiṣiddhasya ca avaiyarthyam bhavati
anyathā tat anarthakam syāt
īśvaraḥ eva vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ niyujyeta atyanta paratantra tvāt jīvasya
tathā vihita kāriṇam api anarthena saṃsṛjet pratiṣiddha kāriṇam api arthena
tatas ca prāmāṇyam vedasya astam iyāt
īśvarasya ca atyanta anapekṣa tve laukikasya api puruṣakārasya vaiyarthyam tathā deśa kāla nimittānām
pūrva ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca iti evaṃjātīyakam doṣa jātam ādi grahaṇena darśayati
aṃśaḥ nānā vyapadeśāt anyathā ca api dāśakitavādi tvam adhīyate eke
aśā adhikaraṇam
jīva īśvarayoḥ upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ uktaḥ
sa ca saṃbaddhayoḥ eva loke dṛṣṭaḥ yathā svāmi bhṛtyayoḥ yathā vā agni visphuliṅgayoḥ
tatas ca jīva īśvarayoḥ api upakārya upakāraka bhāva abhyupagamāt kim svāmi bhṛtya vat saṃbandhaḥ āhosvit agni visphuliṅga vat
iti asyām vicikitsāyām aniyamaḥ vā prāpnoti
athavā svāmi bhṛtya prakāreṣu eva īśitṛ īśitavya bhāvasya prasiddha tvāt tadvidhaḥ eva saṃbandhaḥ iti prāpnoti
atas bravīti aṃśaḥ iti
jīvaḥ īśvarasya aṃśaḥ bhavitum arhati yathā agneḥ visphuliṅgaḥ
aṃśaḥ iva aṃśaḥ
na hi niravayavasya mukhyaḥ ūm śaḥ saṃbhavati
kasmāt punar niravayava tvāt saḥ eva na bhavati
nānā vyapadeśāt
saḥ nveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ etam eva viditvā muniḥ bhavati yaḥ ātmani tiṣṭhan ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati iti ca evaṃjātīyakaḥ bheda nirdeśaḥ na asati bhede yujyate
nanu ca ayam nānā vyapadeśaḥ sutarām svāmi bhṛtya sārūpye yujyate iti atas āha anyathā ca api iti
na ca nānā vyapadeśāt eva kevalāt aṃśa tva pratipattiḥ
kim tarhi anyathā ca api vyapadeśaḥ bhavati anānātvasya pratipādakaḥ
tathā hi eke śākhinaḥ dāśa kitava ādi bhāvam brahmaṇaḥ āmananti ātharvaṇikāḥ brahmasūkte brahma dāśāḥ brahma dāsāḥ brahma eva ime kitavāḥ ityādinā
dāśāḥ ye ete kaivartāḥ prasiddhāḥ ye ca amīdāsāḥ svāmiṣu ātmānam upakṣapayanti ye ca anye kitavāḥ dyūta kṛtaḥ te sarve brahmā eva iti hīna jantu udāharaṇena sarveṣām eva nāma rūpa kṛta kārya karaṇa saṃghāta praviṣṭānām jīvānām brahmatvam āha
tathā anyatra api brahma prakriyāyām eva ayam arthaḥ prapañcyate tvam strī tvam pumān asi tvam kumāraḥ uta vā kumārī
tvam jīrṇaḥ daṇḍena vañcasi tvam jātaḥ bhavati viśvatomukhaḥ iti sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīraḥ nāmāni kṛtvā abhivadanyat āste iti ca
draṣṭā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca asya arthasya siddhiḥ
caitanyam ca aviśiṣṭam jīva īśvarayoḥ yathā agni visphuliṅgayoḥ auṣṇyam
atas bheda abheda avagamābhyām aṃśa tva avagamaḥ
kutas ca aṃśa tva avagamaḥ
mantra varṇāt ca
mantra varṇaḥ ca etam artham avagamayati tāvān asya mahimā
tatas jyāyāḥ ca puruṣaḥ
pādaḥ sya sarvā bhūtāni
tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti
atra bhūta śabdena jīva pradhānāni sthāvara jaṅgamāni nirdiśati a hiṃsan sarva bhūtāni anyatra tīrthebhyaḥ iti prayogāt
aṃśaḥ pādaḥ bhāgaḥ iti anarthāntaram
tasmāt api aṃśa tva avagamaḥ
kutas ca aṃśa tva avagamaḥ
api ca smaryate
īśvaragītāsu api ca īśvara aṃśa tvam jīvasya smaryate mama eva aṃśaḥ jīva loke jīva bhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ iti
tasmāt api aṃśa tva avagamaḥ
yat tu uktam svāmi bhṛtya ādiṣu eva īśitṛ īśitavya bhāvaḥ loke prasiddhaḥ iti yadi api eṣā loke prasiddhiḥ tathā api śāstrāt tu atra aṃśa aṃśi tvam īśitṛ īśitavya bhāvaḥ ca niścīyate
niratiśaya upādhi saṃpannaḥ ca īśvaraḥ nihīna upādhi saṃpannān jīvān praśāsti iti na kiṃcid vipratiṣidhyate
atra āha nanu jīvasya īśvara aṃśa tva abhyupagame tadīyena saṃsāra duḥkha upabhogena aṃśinaḥ īśvarasya api duḥkhi tvam syāt yathā loke duḥkhena aṅginaḥ devadattasya duḥkhi tvam tadvat
tatas ca tad prāptānām mahattaram duḥkham prāpnuyāt
atas varam pūrva avasthaḥ saṃsāraḥ eva astu iti samyak darśana ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ syāt iti
atrā ucyate
prakāśa ādi vat na evam paraḥ
yathā jīvaḥ saṃsāra duḥkham a nubhavati na evam paraḥ īśvaraḥ nubhavati iti pratijānīmahe
jīvaḥ hi avidyā āveśa vaśāt deha ādi ātma bhāvam iva gatvā tad kṛtena duḥkhena duḥkhī aham iti avidyayā kṛtam duḥkha upabhogam abhimanyate
na evam parameśvarasya deha ādi ātmabhāvaḥ duḥkha abhimānaḥ vā asti
jīvasya api avidyā kṛta nāma rūpa nirvṛtta deha indriya ādi upādhya viveka bhrama nimittaḥ eva duḥkha abhimānaḥ na tu pāramārthikaḥ sti
yathā ca sva deha gata dāha cheda ādi nimittam duḥkham tad abhimāna bhrāntyā anubhavati tathā putra mitra ādi gocaram api duḥkham tad abhimāna bhrāntyā eva anubhavati aham eva putraḥ aham eva mitram iti evam sneha vaśena putra mitra ādiṣu abhiniviśamānaḥ
tatas ca niścitam etat avagamyate mithyā abhimāna bhrama nimittaḥ eva duḥkha anubhavaḥ iti
vyatireka darśanāt ca evam avagamyate
tathā hi putra mitra ādimatsu bahuṣu upaviṣṭeṣu tad saṃbandha abhimāniṣu itareṣu ca putraḥ mṛtaḥ mitram mṛtam iti evam āghoṣite yeṣām eva putra mitra ādimat tva abhimānaḥ teṣām eva tad nimittam duḥkham utpadyate na abhimāna hīnānām parivrājaka ādīnām
atas ca laukikasya api puṃsaḥ samyak daśana arthavat tvam dṛṣṭam kim uta viṣaya śūnyāt ātmanaḥ nyat vastu antaram apaśyataḥ nitya caitanya mātra svarūpasya iti
tasmāt nā asti samyak darśana ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ
prakāśa ādi vat iti nidarśana upanyāsaḥ prakāśaḥ sauraḥ cāndramasaḥ vā viyat vyāpya avatiṣṭhamānaḥ aṅguli ādi upādhi saṃbandhāt teṣu ṛju vakra ādi bhāvam pratipadyamāneṣu tat tad bhāvam iva pratipadyamānaḥ u pi na paramārthataḥ tad bhāvam pratipadyate yathā ca ākāśaḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu gacchatsu gacchan iva vibhāvyamānaḥ u pi na paramārthataḥ gacchati yathā ca uda śarāva ādi kampanāt tad gate sūrya pratibimbe kampamāne pi na tadvān sūrya
jīvasya api duḥkha prāptiḥ avidyā nimittā eva iti uktam
tathā ca avidyā nimitta jīva bhāva vyudāsena brahma bhāvam eva jīvasya pratipādayanti vedāntāḥ tat tvam asi iti evamādayaḥ
tasmāt nā asti jaivena duḥkhena paramātmanaḥ duḥkhi tva prasaṅgaḥ
smaranti ca
smaranti ca vyāsa ādayaḥ yathā jaivena duḥkhena na paramātmā duḥkhāyate iti
tatra yaḥ paramātmā hi sa nityaḥ nirguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
na lipyate phalaiḥ ca api padma patram iva ambhasā
karma ātmā tu aparaḥ sau mokṣa bandhaiḥ sa yujyate
sa saptadaśakena api rāśinā yujyate punar iti
ca śabdāt samāmananti ca iti vākya śeṣaḥ tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādvatti an aśnan anyaḥ abhicākaśīti iti ekaḥ tathā sarva bhūta antarātmā na lipyate loka duḥkhena bāhyaḥ iti ca
atra āha yadi tarhi ekaḥ eva sarveṣām bhūtānām antarātmā syāt katham anujñā parihārau syātām laukikau vaidikau ca iti
nanu ca aṃśaḥ jīvaḥ īśvarasya iti uktam
tad bhedāt ca anujñā parihārau tad āśrayau avyatikīrṇau upapadyete
kim atra codyate iti ucyate na etat evam
an aṃśa tvam api hi jīvasya abheda vādinyaḥ śrutayaḥ pratipādayanti tat sṛṣṭvā tat eva anuprāviśat sti draṣṭā mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati tattvam asi aham brahma asmi iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ
nanu bheda abheda avagamābhyām aṃśa tvam sidhyati iti uktam syāt etat evam yadi ubhau api bheda abhedau pratipipādayiṣitau syātām
abhedaḥ eva tu atra brahma ātmatva pratipattau puruṣa artha siddheḥ
svabhāva prāptaḥ tu bhedaḥ nu udyate
na ca niravayavasya brahmaṇaḥ mukhyaḥ ūm śaḥ jīvaḥ saṃbhavati iti uktam
tasmāt paraḥ eva ekaḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām antarātmā jīva bhāvena avasthitaḥ iti atas vaktavyā anujñā parihāra upapattiḥ
tām brūmaḥ
anujñā parihārau deha sambandhāt jyotiḥ ādi vat
ṛtau bhāryām upeyāt iti anujñā guru aṅganām na upagacchet iti parihāraḥ
tathā agnīṣomīyam paśum saṃjñapayet iti anujñā na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni iti parihāraḥ
evam loke mitram upasevitavyam iti anujñā śatruḥ parihartavyaḥ iti parihāraḥ evaṃprakārau anujñā parihārau ekatve pi ātmanaḥ deha saṃbandhāt syāt
dehaiḥ saṃbandhaḥ deha saṃbandhaḥ
kaḥ punar deha saṃbandhaḥ
deha ādiḥ ayam saṃghātaḥ ham eva iti ātmani viparīta pratyaya utpattiḥ
dṛṣṭā ca sā sarva prāṇinām aham gacchāmi aham āgacchāmi aham andhaḥ aham an andhaḥ aham mūḍhaḥ aham a mūḍhaḥ iti evam ātmikā
na hi asyāḥ samyagdarśanāt anyat nivārakam asti
prāk tu samyak darśanāt pratatā eṣā bhrāntiḥ sarva jantuṣu
tat evam avidyā nimitta deha ādi upādhi saṃbandha kṛtāt viśeṣāt aikātmya abhyupagame pi anujñā parihārau avakalpete
samyak darśinaḥ tarhi anujñā parihāra ānarthakyam prāptam na tasya kṛtārtha tvāt niyojya tva anupapatteḥ heya upādeyayoḥ hi niyojyaḥ niyoktavyaḥ syāt
ātmanaḥ tu atiriktam heyam upādeyam vā vastu a paśyan katham niyujyeta
na ca ātmā ātmani eva niyojyaḥ syāt
śarīra vyatireka darśinaḥ eva niyojya tvam iti ced na
tad saṃhata tva abhimānāt satyam vyatireka darśinaḥ niyojya tvam
tathā api vyoma ādi vat deha ādi asaṃhata tvam a paśyataḥ eva ātmanaḥ niyojya tva abhimānaḥ
na hi deha ādi asaṃhata tva darśinaḥ kasyacid api niyogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim uta aikātmya darśinaḥ
na ca niyoga abhāvāt samyak darśinaḥ yatheṣṭa ceṣṭā prasaṅgaḥ sarvatra abhimānasya eva pravartaka tvāt abhimāna abhāvāt ca samyak darśinaḥ
tasmāt deha saṃbandhāt eva anujñā parihārau jyotiḥ ādi vat yathā jyotiṣaḥ ekatve pi agniḥ kravyād parihriyate na itaraḥ
yathā ca prakāśaḥ ekasya api savituḥ amedhya deśa saṃbaddhaḥ parihriyate na itaraḥ śuci bhūmiṣṭhaḥ
tathā bhaumāḥ pradeśāḥ vajra vaiḍūrya ādayaḥ upādīyante bhaumāḥ api santaḥ naraka lebara ādayaḥ parihriyante
tathā mūtra purīṣam gavām pavitra tayā parigṛhyate tat eva jāti antare parivarjyate tadvat
a santateḥ ca a vyatikaraḥ
syātām nāma anujñā parihārau ekasya ātmanaḥ deha viśeṣa yogāt
yaḥ tu ayam karma phala saṃbandhaḥ sa ca aikātmya abhyupagame vyatikīryeta svāmī ekatvāt iti ced na etat evam asaṃtateḥ
na hi kartuḥ bhoktuḥ ca ātmanaḥ saṃtataḥ sarvaiḥ śarīraiḥ saṃbandhaḥ sti
upādhi tantraḥ hi jīvaḥ iti uktam
upādhya saṃtānāt ca nā asti jīva saṃtānaḥ tatas ca karma vyatikaraḥ phala vyatikaraḥ vā na bhaviṣyati
ābhāsaḥ eva ca
ābhāsaḥ eva ca eṣa jīvaḥ parasya ātmanaḥ jala sūryaka ādi vat pratipattavyaḥ na saḥ eva sākṣāt nā api vastu antaram
atas ca yathā na ekasmin jala sūryake kampamāne jala sūryaka antaram kampate evam na ekasmin jīve karma phala saṃbandhini jīva antarasya tad saṃbandhaḥ
evam avyatikare eva karma phalayoḥ
ābhāsasya ca avidyā kṛta tvāt tad āśrayasya saṃsārasya avidyā kṛta tva upapattiḥ iti tad vyudāsena ca pāramārthikasya brahma ātma bhāvasya upadeśa upapattiḥ
yeṣām tu bahavaḥ ātmānaḥ te ca sarve sarva gatāḥ teṣām eva eṣa vyatikaraḥ prāpnoti
katham
bahavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca ātmānaḥ caitanya mātra svarūpāḥ nirguṇāḥ niratiśayāḥ ca
tad artham sādhāraṇam pradhānam
tad nimittā eṣām bhoga apavarga siddhiḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ
sati bahu tve vibhu tve ca ghaṭa kuḍya ādi samānāḥ dravya mātra svarūpāḥ svatas
acetanāḥ ātmānaḥ tad upakaraṇāni ca aṇūni manāṃsi acetanāni tatra ātma dravyāṇām manaḥ dravyāṇām ca saṃyogāt nava icchā ādayaḥ vaiśeṣikāḥ ātma guṇāḥ utpadyante te ca avyatirekeṇa pratyekam ātmasu samavayanti sa saṃsāraḥ
teṣām navānām ātma guṇānām atyanta anutpādaḥ mokṣaḥ iti kāṇādāḥ
tatra sāṃkhyānām tāvat caitanya svarūpa tvāt sarva ātmanām saṃnidhāna ādya viśeṣāt ca ekasya sukha duḥkha saṃbandhe sarveṣām sukha duḥkha saṃbandhaḥ prāpnoti
syāt etat pradhāna pravṛtteḥ puruṣa kaivalya artha tvāt vyavasthā bhaviṣyati
anyathā hi sva vibhūti khyāpana arthā pradhāna pravṛttiḥ syāt
tathā ca anirmokṣaḥ prasajyeta iti na etat sāram na hi abhilaṣita siddhi nibandhanā vyavasthā śakyā vijñātum
upapattyā tu kayācid vyavasthā ucyeta
asatyām punar upapattau kāmam mā bhūt abhilaṣitam puruṣa kaivalyam
prāpnoti tu vyavasthā hetu abhāvāt vyatikaraḥ
kāṇādānām api yadā ekena ātmanā manaḥ saṃyujyate tadā ātma antaraiḥ api nāntarīyakaḥ saṃyogaḥ syāt saṃnidhāna ādi aviśeṣāt
tatas ca hetu aviśeṣāt phala aviśeṣaḥ iti ekasya ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkha yoge sarva ātmanām api samānam sukha duḥkhi tvam prasajyeta
syāt etat adṛṣṭa nimittaḥ niyamaḥ bhaviṣyati iti
na iti āha
adṛṣṭa aniyamāt
bahuṣu ātmasu ākāśa vat sarva gateṣu pratiśarīram bāhya abhyantara aviśeṣeṇa saṃnihiteṣu manaḥ vāc kāyaiḥ dharma adharma lakṣaṇam adṛṣṭam upārjyate
sāṃkhyānām tāvat tat anātma samavāyi pradhāna varti
pradhāna sādhāraṇyāt na pratyātmam sukha duḥkha upabhogasya niyāmakam upapadyate
kāṇādānām api pūrvavat sādhāraṇena ātma manaḥ saṃyogena nirvartitasya adṛṣṭasya api asya eva ātmanaḥ idam adṛṣṭam iti niyame hetu abhāvāt eṣaḥ eva doṣaḥ
syāt etat aham idam phalam prāpnavāni idam pariharāṇi ittham prayatai ittham karavāṇi iti evaṃvidhāḥ abhisaṃdhyā ādayaḥ pratyātmam pravartamānāḥ adṛṣṭasya ātmanām ca sva svāmi bhāvam niyaṃsyanti iti
na iti āha
abhisandhyā ādiṣu api ca evam
ami saṃdhi ādīnām api sādhāraṇena eva ātma manaḥ saṃyogena sarva ātma saṃnidhau kriyamāṇānām niyama hetu tva anupapatteḥ ukta doṣa anuṣaṅgaḥ eva
pradeśāt iti ced na antarbhāvāt
atha ucyeta vibhu tve pi ātmanaḥ śarīra pratiṣṭhena manasā saṃyogaḥ śarīra avacchinnaḥ eva ātma pradeśe bhaviṣyati
atas pradeśa kṛtāḥ vyavasthāḥ abhisaṃdhyā ādīnām adṛṣṭasya sukha duḥkhayoḥ ca bhaviṣyati iti tat api na upapadyate
kasmāt
antarbhāvāt
vibhu tva aviśeṣāt hi sarve eva ātmānaḥ sarva śarīreṣu antarbhavanti
tatra na vaiśeṣikaiḥ śarīra avacchinnaḥ pi ātmanaḥ pradeśaḥ kalpayitum śakyaḥ
kalpyamānaḥ u pi ayam niṣpradeśasya ātmanaḥ pradeśaḥ kālpanika tvāt eva na pāramārthikam kāryam niyantum śaknoti
śarīram api sarva ātma saṃnidhau utpadyamānam asya eva ātmanaḥ na itareṣām iti na niyantum śakyam
pradeśa viśeṣa abhyupagame ca dvayoḥ ātmanoḥ samāna sukha duḥkha bhājoḥ kadācid ekena eva tāvat śarīreṇa upabhoga siddhiḥ syāt samāna pradeśasya api dvayoḥ ātmanoḥ adṛṣṭasya saṃbhavāt
tathā hi devadattaḥ yasmin pradeśe sukha duḥkham anvabhūt tasmāt pradeśāt apakrānte tad śarīre yajñadatta śarīre ca tam pradeśam anuprāpte tasya api itareṇa samānaḥ sukha duḥkha anubhavaḥ dṛśyate
sa na syāt yadi devadatta yajñadattayoḥ samāna pradeśam adṛṣṭam na syāt
svarga ādi an upabhoga prasaṅgaḥ ca pradeśavādinaḥ syāt brāhmaṇa ādi śarīra pradeśeṣu adṛṣṭa niṣpatteḥ pradeśa antara varti tvāt ca svarga ādi upabhogasya
sarvagata tva anupapattiḥ ca bahūnām ātmanām dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt
vada tāvat tvam ke bahavaḥ samāna deśāḥ ca iti
rūpa ādayaḥ iti ced na
teṣām api dharmi aṃśena abhedāt lakṣaṇa bhedāt ca na tu bahūnām ātmanām lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ sti
antya viśeṣa vaśāt bheda upapattiḥ iti ced na
bheda kalpanāyāḥ antya viśeṣa kalpanāyāḥ ca itaretara āśraya tvāt
ākāśa ādīnām api vibhu tvam brahma vādinaḥ siddham kāryatva abhyupagamāt
tasmāt ātma ekatva pakṣaḥ eva sarva doṣa abhāvaḥ iti siddham
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ

dvitīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ
caturthaḥ pādaḥ
tathā prāṇāḥ
prāṇa utpatti adhikaraṇam
tathā prāṇāḥ iti
katham punar atra tathā iti akṣara ānulomyam prakṛta upamāna abhāvāt sarvagata ātma bahutva vādi dūṣaṇam atīta anantara pādānte prakṛtam
tat tāvat na upamānam saṃbhavati sādṛśya abhāvāt
sādṛśye hi sati upamānam syāt yathā siṃhaḥ tathā balavarmā iti
adṛṣṭa sāmya pratipādana artham iti yadi ucyeta yathā adṛṣṭasya sarva ātma saṃnidhau utpadyamānasya aniyata tvam evam prāṇānām api sarva ātmanaḥ prati aniyata tvam iti tat api deha aniyamena eva ukta tvāt punar uktam bhavet
na ca jīvena prāṇāḥ upamīyeran siddhānta virodhāt jīvasya hi anutpattiḥ ākhyātā prāṇānām tu utpattiḥ ācikhyāsitā
tasmāt tathā iti asaṃbaddham iva pratibhāti na udāharaṇa upāttena api upamānena saṃbandha upapatteḥ atra prāṇa utpatti vādi vākya jātam udāharaṇam etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ sarve lokāḥ sarve devāḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni vyuccaranti iti evaṃjātīyakam
tatra yathā loka ādayaḥ parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ utpadyante tathā prāṇāḥ api iti arthaḥ
tathā etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca
kham vāyuḥ jyotiḥ āpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇī iti evamādiṣu api kha ādi vat prāṇānām utpattiḥ iti draṣṭavyam
athavā pāna vyāpad ca tadvat iti evamādiṣu vyavahita upamāna saṃbandhasya api āśrita tvāt yathā atīta anantara pāda ādau uktāḥ viyat ādayaḥ parasya brahmaṇaḥ vikārāḥ samadhigatāḥ tathā prāṇāḥ api parasya brahmaṇaḥ vikārāḥ iti yojayitavyam
kaḥ punar prāṇānām vikāra tve hetuḥ
śruta tvam eva
nanu keṣucid pradeśeṣu na prāṇānām utpattiḥ śrūyate iti uktam tat ayuktam pradeśa antareṣu śravaṇāt
na hi kvacid aśravaṇam anyatra śrutam nivārayitum utsahate
tasmāt śruta tva aviśeṣāt ākāśa ādi vat prāṇāḥ api utpadyante iti sūktam
gauṇī asambhavāt
yat punar uktam prāk utpatteḥ sadbhāva śravaṇāt gauṇī prāṇānām utpatti śrutiḥ iti tat pratyāha gauṇī asaṃbhavāt iti
gauṇyāḥ asaṃbhavaḥ gauṇī asaṃbhavaḥ na hi prāṇānām utpatti śrutiḥ gauṇī saṃbhavati pratijñā hāni prasaṅgāt kasmin nu bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti hi eka vijñānena sarva vijñānam pratijñāya tad sādhanāya idam āmnāyate etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ ityādi
sā ca pratijñā prāṇa ādeḥ samastasya jagataḥ brahma vikāra tve sati prakṛti vyatirekeṇa vikāra abhāvāt sidhyati
gauṇyām tu prāṇānām utpatti śrutau pratijñā iyam hīyeta
tathā ca pratijñāta artham upasaṃharati puruṣaḥ eva idam viśvam karma tapaḥ brahma para amṛtam iti brahma eva idam viśvam idam variṣṭham iti ca
tathā ātmanaḥ vai are darśanena śravaṇena matyā vijñānena idam sarvam viditam iti evaṃjātīyakāsu śrutiṣu eṣā eva pratijñā yojayitavyā
katham punar prāk utpatteḥ prāṇānām sadbhāva śravaṇam
na etat mūlaprakṛti viṣayam a prāṇaḥ hi amanāḥ śubhraḥ hi akṣarāt paratas paraḥ iti mūlaprakṛteḥ prāṇa ādi samasta viśeṣa rahita tva avadhāraṇāt
avāntaraprakṛti viṣayam tu etat sva vikāra apekṣam prāk utpatteḥ prāṇānām sadbhāva avadhāraṇam iti draṣṭavyam vyākṛta viṣayāṇām api bhūyasīnām avasthānām śruti smṛtyoḥ prakṛti vikāra bhāva prasiddheḥ
viyat adhikaraṇe hi gauṇī asaṃbhavāt iti pūrvapakṣa sūtra tvāt gauṇī janma śrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātam
pratijñā hānyā ca tatra siddhāntaḥ bhihitaḥ
iha tu siddhānta sūtra tvāt gauṇyāḥ janma śruteḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātam
tad anurodhena tu iha api gauṇī janma śrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyācakṣāṇaiḥ pratijñā hāniḥ upekṣitā syāt
tad prāk śruteḥ ca
itas ca ākāśa ādīnām iva prāṇānām api mukhyā eva janma śrutiḥ yat jāyate iti ekam janma vāci padam prāṇeṣu prāk śrutam sat uttareṣu ākāśa ādiṣu anuvartate etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ iti atra
ākāśa ādiṣu mukhyam janma iti pratiṣṭhāpitam
tad sāmānyāt prāṇeṣu api mukhyam eva janma bhavitum arhati
na hi ekasmin prakaraṇe ekasmin ca vākye ekaḥ śabdaḥ sakṛt uccaritaḥ bahubhiḥ saṃbadhyamānaḥ kvacid mukhyaḥ kvacid gauṇaḥ iti adhyavasātum śakyam vairūpya prasaṅgāt
tathā sa prāṇam asṛjata prāṇāt śraddhām iti atra api prāṇeṣu śrutaḥ sṛjatiḥ pareṣu api utpattimatsu śraddhā ādiṣu anuṣajyate
yatra api paścāt śrutaḥ utpatti vacanaḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaiḥ saṃbadhyate tatra api eṣaḥ eva nyāyaḥ yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni vyuccaranti iti ayam ante paṭhitaḥ vyuccaranti śabdaḥ pūrvaiḥ api prāṇa ādibhiḥ saṃbadhyate
tad pūrvaka tvāt vācaḥ
yadi api tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti etasmin prakaraṇe prāṇānām utpattiḥ na paṭhyate tejaḥ bannānām eva trayāṇām bhūtānām utpatti śravaṇāt
tathā api brahma prakṛtika tejaḥ banna pūrvakatva abhidhānāt vāc prāṇa manasām tad sāmānyāt ca sarveṣām eva prāṇānām brahma prabhava tvam siddham bhavati
tathā hi asmin eva prakaraṇe tejaḥ banna pūrvaka tvam vāc prāṇa manasām āmnāyate anna mayam hi somya manaḥ āpaḥ mayaḥ prāṇaḥ tejaḥ mayī vāc iti
tatra yadi tāvat mukhyam eva eṣām annāda maya tvam tatas vartate eva brahma prabhava tvam
atha bhāktam tathā api brahma kartṛkāyām nāma rūpa vyākriyāyām śravaṇāt yena aśrutam śrutam bhavati iti ca upakramāt aitadātmyam idam sarvam iti ca upasaṃhārāt śruti antara prasiddheḥ ca brahma kārya tva prapañcana artham eva manaḥ ādīnām anna ādi maya tva vacanam iti gamyate
tasmāt api prāṇānām brahma vikāra tva siddhiḥ
sapta gateḥ viśeṣita tvāt ca
sapta gati adhikaraṇam
utpatti viṣayaḥ śruti vipratiṣedhaḥ prāṇānām parihṛtaḥ
saṃkhyā viṣayaḥ idānīm parihriyate
tatra mukhyam prāṇam upariṣṭāt vakṣyati
saṃprati tu kati itare prāṇāḥ iti saṃpradhārayati
śruti vipratipatteḥ ca atra viśayaḥ kvacid sapta prāṇāḥ saṃkīrtyante sapta prāṇāḥ prabhavanti tasmāt iti
kvacid aṣṭau prāṇāḥ graha tvena guṇena saṃkīrtyante aṣṭau grahāḥ aṣṭau atigrahāḥ iti
kvacid nava sapta vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ dvau avāñcau iti
kvacid daśa nava vai puruṣe prāṇāḥ nābhiḥ daśamī iti
kvacid ekādaśa daśa ime puruṣe prāṇāḥ ātmā ekādaśaḥ iti
kvacid dvādaśa sarveṣām sparśānām tvac ekāyanam iti atra
kvacid trayodaśa cakṣuḥ ca draṣṭavyam ca iti atra evam hi vipratipannāḥ prāṇa iyattām prati śrutayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
sapta eva prāṇāḥ iti
kutas
gateḥ
yatas tāvantaḥ vagamyante sapta prāṇāḥ prabhavanti tasmāt iti evaṃvidhāsu śrutiṣu viśeṣitāḥ ca ete sapta vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ iti atra
nanu prāṇāḥ guhā āśayāḥ nihitāḥ sapta sapta iti vīpsā śrūyate
sā saptabhyaḥ tiriktān prāṇān gamayati iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
puruṣa bheda abhiprāyā iyam vīpsā pratipuruṣam sapta sapta prāṇāḥ iti
na tattva bheda abhiprāyā sapta sapta anye nye prāṇāḥ iti
nanu aṣṭa tva ādikā api saṃkhyā prāṇeṣu udāhṛtā
katham sapta eva syuḥ
satyam udāhṛtā
virodhāt tu anyatamā saṃkhyā adhyavasātavyā
tatra stoka kalpanā anurodhāt sapta saṃkhyā adhyavasānam
vṛtti bheda apekṣam ca saṃkhyā antara śravaṇam iti manyate
atrā ucyate
hasta ādayaḥ tu sthite taḥ na evam
hasta ādayaḥ tu apare prāṇāḥ śrūyante hastaḥ vai grahaḥ sa karmaṇā atigraheṇa gṛhītaḥ hastābhyām hi karma karoti iti evamādyāsu śrutiṣu
sthite ca sapta tva atireke sapta tvam antarbhāvāt śakyate saṃbhāvayitum
hīna adhika saṃkhyā vipratipattau hi adhikā saṃkhyā saṃgrāhyā bhavati
tasyām hīnā antarbhavati na tu hīnāyām adhikā
atas ca nā evam mantavyam stoka kalpanā anurodhāt sapta eva prāṇāḥ syuḥ iti
uttara saṃkhyā anurodhāt tu ekādaśā eva te prāṇāḥ syuḥ
tathā ca udāhṛtā śrutiḥ daśa ime puruṣe prāṇāḥ ātmā ekādaśaḥ iti
ātma śabdena ca atra antaḥkaraṇam parigṛhyate karaṇa adhikārāt
nanu ekādaśa tvāt api adhike dvādaśa trayodaśa tve udāhṛte satyam udāhṛte
na tu ekādaśabhyaḥ kārya jātebhyaḥ dhikam kārya jātam asti yad artham adhikam karaṇam kalpyeta
śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandha viṣayāḥ pañca buddhi bhedāḥ tad arthāni pañca buddhīndriyāṇi
vacana ādāna viharaṇa utsarga ānandāḥ pañca karma bhedāḥ tad arthāni ca pañca karmendriyāṇi
sarva artha viṣayam traikālya vṛtti manaḥ tu ekam aneka vṛttikam
tat eva vṛtti bhedāt kvacid bhinna vat vyapadiśyate manaḥ buddhiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ cittam ca iti
tathā ca śrutiḥ kāma ādyāḥ nānāvidhāḥ vṛttīḥ anukramya āha etat sarvam manaḥ eva iti
api ca sapta eva śīrṣaṇyān prāṇān abhimanyamānasya catvāraḥ eva prāṇāḥ abhimatāḥ syuḥ
sthāna bhedāt hi ete catvāraḥ santaḥ sapta gaṇyante dve śrotre dve cakṣuṣī dve nāsike ekā vāc iti
na ca tāvatām eva vṛtti bhedāḥ itare prāṇāḥ iti śakyate vaktum hasta ādi vṛttīnām atyanta vijātīya tvāt
tathā nava vai puruṣe prāṇāḥ nābhiḥ daśamī iti atra api deha chidra bheda abhiprāyeṇa eva daśa prāṇāḥ ucyante na prāṇa tattva bheda abhiprāyeṇa nābhiḥ daśamī iti vacanāt
na hi nābhiḥ nāma kaścid prāṇaḥ prasiddhaḥ sti
mukhyasya tu prāṇasya bhavati nābhiḥ api ekam viśeṣa āyatanam iti atas nābhiḥ daśamī iti ucyate
kvacid upāsana artham katicid prāṇāḥ gaṇyante kvacid pradarśana artham
tat evam vicitre prāṇa iyattā mnāne sati kva kim param āmnānam iti vivektavyam
kārya jāta vaśāt tu ekādaśa tva āmnānam prāṇa viṣayam pramāṇam iti sthitam
iyam aparā sūtra dvaya yojanā sapta eva prāṇāḥ syuḥ yatas saptānām eva gatiḥ śrūyate tam utkrāmantam prāṇaḥ nu utkrāmati prāṇam anūtkrāmantam sarve prāṇāḥ anūtkrāmanti iti atra
nanu sarva śabdaḥ u tra paṭhyate tat katham saptānām eva gatiḥ pratijñāyate iti
viśeṣita tvāt iti āha sapta eva hi prāṇāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ tvac paryantāḥ viśeṣitāḥ iha prakṛtāḥ sa yatra eva cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ parāṅ paryāvartate thārūpa jñaḥ bhavati ekībhavati na paśyati iti āhuḥ iti evamādinā anukramaṇena
prakṛta gāmī ca sarva śabdaḥ bhavati
yathā sarve brāhmaṇāḥ bhojayitavyāḥ iti ye nimantritāḥ prakṛtāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ te eva sarva śabdena ucyante na anye evam iha api ye prakṛtāḥ sapta prāṇāḥ te eva sarva śabdena ucyante na anye iti
nanu atra vijñānam aṣṭamam anukrāntam
katham saptānām eva anukramaṇam
na eṣa doṣaḥ
manaḥ vijñānayoḥ tattva abhedāt vṛtti bhede pi sapta tva upapatteḥ
tasmāt sapta eva prāṇāḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ hasta ādayaḥ tu apare saptabhyaḥ tiriktāḥ prāṇāḥ pratīyante hastaḥ vai grahaḥ ityādi śrutiṣu
graha tvam ca bandhana bhāvaḥ gṛhyate badhyate kṣetrajñaḥ anena graha saṃjñakena bandhanena iti
sa ca kṣetrajñaḥ na ekasmin eva śarīre badhyate śarīra antareṣu api tulya tvāt bandhanasya
tasmāt śarīra antara saṃcāri idam graha saṃjñakam bandhanam iti arthāt uktam bhavati
tathā ca smṛtiḥ puryaṣṭakena liṅgena prāṇa ādyena sa yujyate
tena baddhasya vai bandhaḥ mokṣaḥ muktasya tena ca iti prāk mokṣāt graha saṃjñakena bandhanena aviyogam darśayati
ātharvaṇe ca viṣaya indriya anukramaṇe cakṣuḥ ca draṣṭavyam ca iti atra tulya vat hasta ādīni indriyāṇi sa viṣayāṇi anukrāmati hastau ca ādātavyam ca upasthaḥ ca ānandayitavyam ca pāyuḥ ca visarjayitavyam ca pādau ca gantavyam ca iti
tathā daśa ime puruṣe prāṇāḥ ātmā ekādaśaḥ te yadā asmāt śarīrāt martyāt utkrāmanti atha rodayanti iti ekādaśānām prāṇānām utkrāntim darśayati
sarva śabdaḥ pi ca prāṇa śabdena saṃbadhyamānaḥ śeṣān prāṇān abhidadhānaḥ na prakaraṇa vaśena saptasu eva avasthāpayitum śakyate prakaraṇāt śabdasya balīyaḥ tvāt
sarve brāhmaṇāḥ bhojayitavyāḥ iti atra api sarveṣām eva avanivartinām brāhmaṇānām grahaṇam nyāyyam sarva śabda sāmarthyāt
sarva bhojana asaṃbhavāt tu tatra nimantrita mātra viṣayā sarva śabdasya vṛttiḥ āśritā
iha tu na kiṃcid sarva śabda artha saṃkocane kāraṇam asti
tasmāt sarva śabdena atra aśeṣāṇām prāṇānām parigrahaḥ
pradarśana artham ca saptānām anukramaṇam iti anavadyam
tasmāt ekādaśa eva prāṇāḥ śabdataḥ kāryataḥ ca iti siddham
aṇavaḥ ca
prāṇa aṇu tva adhikaraṇam
adhunā prāṇānām eva svabhāva antaram abhyuccinoti
aṇavaḥ ca ete prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ pratipattavyāḥ
aṇu tvam ca eṣām saukṣmya paricchedau na paramāṇu tulya tvam kṛtsna deha vyāpi kārya anupapatti prasaṅgāt sūkṣmāḥ ete prāṇāḥ sthūlāḥ ced syuḥ maraṇa kāle śarīrāt nirgacchantaḥ bilāt ahiḥ iva upalabhyeran mriyamāṇasya pārśva sthaiḥ
paricchinnāḥ ca ete prāṇāḥ sarva gatāḥ ced syuḥ utkrānti gati āgati śruti vyākopaḥ syāt tad guṇa sāra tvam ca jīvasya na sidhyet
sarvagatānām api vṛtti lābhaḥ śarīra deśe syāt iti ced na vṛtti mātrasya karaṇa tva upapatteḥ
yat eva hi upalabdhi sādhanam vṛttiḥ anyat vā tasya eva naḥ karaṇa tvam saṃjñā mātre vivādaḥ iti karaṇānām vyāpi tva kalpanā nirarthikā
tasmāt sūkṣmāḥ paricchinnāḥ ca prāṇāḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ
śreṣṭhaḥ ca
prāṇa śraiṣṭhya adhikaraṇam
mukhyaḥ ca prāṇaḥ itara prāṇa vat brahma vikāraḥ iti atidiśati
tat ca aviśeṣeṇa eva sarva prāṇānām brahma vikāra tvam ākhyātam etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca iti sa indriya manaḥ vyatirekeṇa prāṇasya utpatti śravaṇāt sa prāṇam asṛjata ityādi śravaṇebhyaḥ ca
kimarthaḥ punar atideśaḥ
adhika āśaṅkā vāraṇa arthaḥ nāsadāsīye hi brahma pradhāne sūkte mantra varṇaḥ bhavati na mṛtyuḥ āsīt amṛtam na tarhi na rātryāḥ ahnaḥ āsīt praketaḥ
ānīt avātam svadhayā tat ekam tasmāt ha anyat aparaḥ kiṃcana asaḥ iti
ānīt iti prāṇa karma upādānāt prāk utpatteḥ santam iva prāṇam sūcayati
tasmāt ajaḥ prāṇaḥ iti jāyate kasyacid matiḥ
tām atideśena apanudati
ānīt śabdaḥ api na prāk utpatteḥ prāṇa sadbhāvam sūcayati avātam iti viśeṣaṇāt aprāṇaḥ hi amanāḥ śubhraḥ iti ca mūlaprakṛteḥ prāṇa ādi samasta viśeṣa rahita tvasya darśita tvāt
tasmāt kāraṇa sadbhāva pradarśana arthaḥ eva ayam ānīt śabdaḥ iti
śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca mukhyam prāṇam abhidadhāti prāṇaḥ vāva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca iti śruti nirdeśāt
jyeṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇaḥ śukra niṣeka kālāt ārabhya tasya vṛttilābhāt na ced tasya tadānīm vṛttilābhaḥ syāt yonau niṣiktam śukram pūyeta na saṃbhavet vā
śrotra ādīnām tu karṇa śaṣkulī ādi sthāna vibhāga niṣpattau vṛtti lābhāt na jyeṣṭha tvam
śreṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇaḥ guṇa ādhikyāt na vai śakṣyāmaḥ tvat ṛte jīvitum iti śruteḥ
na vā āyu kriye pṛthak upadeśāt
vāyu kriyā adhikaraṇam
sa punar mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ kiṃsvarūpaḥ iti idānīm jijñāsyate
tatra prāptam tāvat śruteḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti
evam hi śrūyate yaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ saḥ eṣa vāyuḥ pañcavidhaḥ prāṇa u pānaḥ vyānaḥ udānaḥ samānaḥ iti
athavā tantra antarīya abhiprāyāt samasta karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇaḥ iti prāptam
evam hi tantra antarīyāḥ ācakṣate sāmānyā karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ pañca iti
atra ucyate na vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ na api karaṇa vyāpāraḥ
kutas
pṛthak upadeśāt
vāyoḥ tāvat prāṇasya pṛthak upadeśaḥ bhavati prāṇaḥ eva brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ sa vāyunā jyotiṣā bhāti ca tapati ca iti
na hi vāyuḥ eva san vāyoḥ pṛthak upadiśyeta
tathā karaṇa vṛtteḥ api pṛthak upadeśaḥ bhavati vāc ādīni karaṇāni anukramya tatra tatra pṛthak prāṇasya anukramaṇāt vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ abhedāt
na hi karaṇa vyāpāraḥ eva san karaṇebhyaḥ pṛthak upadiśyeta
tathā etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca
kham vāyuḥ iti evamādayaḥ vāyoḥ karaṇebhyaḥ ca prāṇasya pṛthak upadeśāḥ anusartavyāḥ
na ca samastānām karaṇānām ekā vṛttiḥ saṃbhavati pratyekam eka eka vṛtti tvāt samudāyasya ca akāraka tvāt
nanu pañjara cālana nyāyena etat bhaviṣyati yathā eka pañjara vartinaḥ ekādaśa pakṣiṇaḥ pratyekam pratiniyata vyāpārāḥ santaḥ saṃbhūya ekam pañjaram cālayanti evam eka śarīra vartinaḥ ekādaśa prāṇāḥ pratyekam pratiniyata vṛttayaḥ santaḥ saṃbhūya ekām prāṇa ākhyām vṛttim pratilapsyante iti
na iti ucyate yuktam tatra pratyeka vṛttibhiḥ avāntara vyāpāraiḥ pañjara cālana anurūpaiḥ eva upetāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃbhūya ekam pañjaram cālayeyuḥ iti tathā dṛṣṭa tvāt
iha tu śravaṇa ādi avāntara vyāpāra upetāḥ prāṇāḥ na saṃbhūya prāṇyuḥ iti yuktam pramāṇa abhāvāt atyanta vijātīya tvāt ca śravaṇa ādibhyaḥ prāṇanasya
tathā prāṇasya śreṣṭha tvāt yuddha ūṣaṇam guṇa bhāva upagamaḥ ca tam prati vāc ādīnām na karaṇa vṛtti mātre prāṇe
tasmāt anyaḥ vāyu kriyābhyām prāṇaḥ
katham tarhi iyam śrutiḥ yaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti
ucyate vāyuḥ eva ayam adhyātmam āpannaḥ pañca vyūhaḥ viśeṣa ātmanā avatiṣṭhamānaḥ prāṇaḥ nāma bhaṇyate na tattva antaram nā api vāyu mātram
atas ca ubhe api bheda abheda śrutī na virudhyete
syāt etat tarhi jīva vat asmin śarīre svātantryam prāpnoti śreṣṭha tvāt guṇa bhāva upagamāt ca tam prati vāc ādīnām indriyāṇām
tathā hi anekavidhā vibhūtiḥ prāṇasya śrāvyate supteṣu vāc ādiṣu prāṇaḥ eva ekaḥ jāgarti prāṇaḥ eva ekaḥ mṛtyunā an āptaḥ prāṇaḥ saṃvargaḥ vāc ādīn saṃvṛṅkte prāṇaḥ itarān prāṇān rakṣati mātā iva putrān iti
tasmāt prāṇasya api jīva vat svātantrya prasaṅgaḥ
tam pariharati
cakṣuḥ ādi vat tu tad saha śiṣṭi ādibhyaḥ
tu śabdaḥ prāṇasya jīva vat svātantryam vyāvartayati
yathā cakṣuḥ ādīni rāja prakṛti vat jīvasya kartṛ tvam bhoktṛ tvam ca prati upakaraṇāni na svatantrāṇi
tathā mukhyaḥ pi prāṇaḥ rāja mantri vat jīvasya sarva arthakara tvena upakaraṇa bhūtaḥ na svatantraḥ
kutas
tad saha śiṣṭi ādibhyaḥ
taiḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ saha eva prāṇaḥ śiṣyate prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu
samāna dharmaṇām ca saha śāsanam yuktam bṛhat rathaṃtara ādi vat
ādi śabdena saṃhata tva acetana tva ādīn prāṇasya svātantrya nirākaraṇa hetūn darśayati
syāt etat yadi cakṣuḥ ādi vat prāṇasya jīvam prati karaṇa bhāvaḥ bhyupagamyeta viṣaya antaram rūpa ādi vat prasajyeta rūpa ālocanā ādibhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ yathāsvam cakṣuḥ ādīnām jīvam prati karaṇa bhāvaḥ bhavati
api ca ekādaśa eva kārya jātāni rūpa ālocanā ādīni parigaṇitāni yad artham ekādaśa prāṇāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ
na tu dvādaśam aparam kārya jātam avagamyate yad artham ayam dvādaśaḥ prāṇaḥ pratijñāyate iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
akaraṇa tvāt ca na doṣaḥ tathā hi darśayati
na tāvat viṣaya antara prasaṅgaḥ doṣaḥ akaraṇa tvāt prāṇasya
na hi cakṣuḥ ādi vat prāṇasya viṣaya paricchedena karaṇa tvam abhyupagamyate
na ca asya etāvatā kārya abhāvaḥ eva
kasmāt
tathā hi śrutiḥ prāṇa antareṣu asaṃbhāvyamānam mukhyaprāṇasya vaiśeṣikam kāryam darśayati prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu atha ha prāṇāḥ aham śreyasi vyūdire iti upakramya yasmin vaḥ utkrānte śarīram pāpiṣṭhataram iva dṛśyeta sa vaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca upanyasya pratyekam vāc ādi utkramaṇena tad vṛtti mātra hīnam yathāpūrvam jīvanam darśayitvā prāṇa uccikramiṣāyām vāc ādi śaithilya āpattim śarīrapāta prasaṅgam ca darśayantī śrutiḥ
tān variṣṭhaḥ prāṇaḥ uvāca mā moham āpat yathā aham eva etat pañcadhā ātmānam pravibhajya etat bāṇam avaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi iti ca etam eva artham śrutiḥ āha
prāṇena rakṣan avaram kulāyam iti ca supteṣu cakṣuḥ ādiṣu prāṇa nimittām śarīra rakṣām darśayati
yasmāt kasmāt ca aṅgāt prāṇaḥ utkrāmati tat eva tat śuṣyati iti tena yat aśnāti yat pibati tena itarān prāṇān avati iti ca prāṇa nimittām śarīra indriya puṣṭim darśayati
kasmin vaham utkrāntaḥ utkrāntaḥ bhaviṣyāmi kasmin vā pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmi iti sa prāṇam asṛjata
iti ca prāṇa nimitte jīvasya utkrānti pratiṣṭhe darśayati
pañca vṛttiḥ manaḥ vat vyapadiśyate
itas ca asti mukhyasya prāṇasya vaiśeṣikam kāryam yatkāraṇam pañca vṛttiḥ ayam vyapadiśyate śrutiṣu prāṇa u pānaḥ vyānaḥ udānaḥ samānaḥ iti
vṛtti bhedaḥ ca ayam kārya bheda apekṣaḥ prāṇaḥ prāc vṛttiḥ ucchvāsa ādi karmā apānaḥ avāc vṛttiḥ niśvāsa ādi karmā vyānaḥ tayoḥ saṃdhau vartamānaḥ vīryavat karma hetuḥ udānaḥ ūrdhva vṛttiḥ utkrānti ādi hetuḥ samānaḥ samam sarveṣu aṅgeṣu yaḥ nna rasān nayati iti evam pañca vṛttiḥ prāṇaḥ manaḥ vat yathā manasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ evam prāṇasya api iti arthaḥ
śrotra ādi nimittāḥ śabda ādi viṣayāḥ manasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ prasiddhāḥ
na tu kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ
bṛ
u
ityādyāḥ paripaṭhitāḥ gṛhyeran pañca saṃkhyā atirekāt
nanu atra api śrotra ādi nirapekṣā bhūta bhaviṣyat ādi viṣayā aparā manasaḥ vṛttiḥ asti iti samānaḥ pañca saṃkhyā atirekaḥ
evam tarhi para matam apratiṣiddham anumatam bhavati iti nyāyāt iha api yoga śāstra prasiddhāḥ manasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ parigṛhyante pramāṇa viparyaya vikalpa nidrā smṛtayaḥ nāma
bahu vṛtti tva mātreṇa vā manaḥ prāṇasya nidarśanam iti draṣṭavyam
jīva upakaraṇa tvam api prāṇasya pañcavṛtti tvāt manovat iti vā yojayitavyam
aṇuḥ ca
śreṣṭha aṇu tva adhikaraṇam
aṇuḥ ca ayam mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ pratyetavyaḥ itara prāṇa vat
aṇu tvam ca iha api saukṣmya paricchedau na paramāṇu tulya tvam pañcabhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ kṛtsna śarīra vyāpi tvāt
sūkṣmaḥ prāṇaḥ utkrāntau pārśva sthena anupalabhyamāna tvāt
paricchinnaḥ ca utkrānti gati āgati śrutibhyaḥ
nanu vibhu tvam api prāṇasya samāmnāyate samaḥ pluṣiṇā samaḥ maśakena samaḥ nāgena samaḥ ebhiḥ tribhiḥ lokaiḥ samaḥ nena sarveṇa iti evamādiṣu pradeśeṣu
tat ucyate ādhidaivikena samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpeṇa hairaṇyagarbheṇa prāṇa ātmanā eva etat vibhu tvam āmnāyate na ādhyātmikena
api ca samaḥ pluṣiṇā ityādinā sāmya vacanena pratiprāṇi vartinaḥ prāṇasya paricchedaḥ eva pradarśyate
tasmāt adoṣaḥ
jyotiḥ ādi adhiṣṭhānam tu tad āmananāt
jyotiḥ ādi adhikaraṇam
te punar prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ kim sva mahimnā eva svasmai svasmai kāryāya prabhavanti āhosvit devatā dhiṣṭhitāḥ prabhavanti iti vicāryate
tatra prāptam tāvat yathāsvam kārya śakti yogāt sva mahimnā eva prāṇāḥ pravarteran iti
api ca devatā dhiṣṭhitānām prāṇānām pravṛttau abhyugamyamānāyām tāsām eva adhiṣṭhātrīṇām devatānām bhoktṛ tva prasaṅgāt śārīrasya bhoktṛ tvam pralīyeta
atas sva mahimnā eva eṣām pravṛttiḥ iti
evam prāpte idam ucyate jyotiḥ ādi adhiṣṭhānam tu iti
tu śabdena pūrvapakṣaḥ vyāvartyate
jyotiḥ ādibhiḥ agni ādi abhimāninībhiḥ devatābhiḥ adhiṣṭhitam vāc ādi karaṇa jātam sva kāryeṣu pravartate iti pratijānīte
hetum ca vyācaṣṭhe tad āmananāt iti
tathā hi āmananti agniḥ vāc bhūtvā mukham prāviśat ityādi
agneḥ ca ayam vāc bhāvaḥ mukha praveśaḥ ca devatā ātmanā adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam aṅgīkṛtya ucyate
na hi devatā saṃbandham pratyākhyāya agneḥ vāci mukhe vā kaścid viśeṣa saṃbandhaḥ dṛśyate
tathā vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ bhūtvā nāsike prāviśat iti evamādi api yojayitavyam
tathā anyatra api vāc eva brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ saḥ gninā jyotiṣā bhāti ca tapati ca iti evamādinā vāc ādīnām agni ādi jyotiṣṭva ādi vacanena etam eva artham draḍhayati
sa vai vācam eva prathamām atyavahat sā yadā mṛtyum atyamucyata saḥ gniḥ abhavat iti ca evamādinā vāc ādīnām agni ādi bhāva āpatti vacanena etam eva artham dyotayati
sarvatra ca adhyātma adhidaivata vibhāgena vāc ādi agni ādi anukramaṇam anayā eva pratyāsattyā bhavati
smṛtau api vāc adhyātmam iti prāhuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tattva darśinaḥ
vaktavyam adhibhūtam tu vahniḥ tatra adhidaivatam ityādinā vāc ādīnām agni ādi devatā adhiṣṭhita tvam sa prapañcam pradarśitam
yat uktam sva kārya śakti yogāt sva mahimnā eva prāṇāḥ pravarteran iti tat ayuktam śaktānām api śakaṭa ādīnām anaḍuha ādi adhiṣṭhitānām pravṛtti darśanāt
ubhayathā upapattau ca āgamāt vāc ādīnām devatā dhiṣṭhita tvam eva niścīyate
yat api uktam devatānām eva adhiṣṭhātrīṇām bhoktṛ tva prasaṅgaḥ na śārīrasya iti tat parihriyate
prāṇavatā śabdāt
satīṣu api prāṇānām adhiṣṭhātrīṣu devatāsu prāṇavatā kārya karaṇa saṃghāta svāminā śārīreṇa eva eṣām prāṇānām saṃbandhaḥ śruteḥ avagamyate
tathā hi śrutiḥ atha yatra etat ākāśam anuviṣaṇṇam cakṣuḥ sa cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ darśanāya cakṣuḥ atha yaḥ veda idam jighrāṇi iti saḥ ātmā gandhāya ghrāṇam iti evaṃjātīyakā śārīreṇa eva prāṇānām saṃbandham śrāvayati
api ca aneka tvāt pratikaraṇam adhiṣṭhātrīṇām devatānām na bhoktṛ tvam asmin śarīre vakalpate
ekaḥ hi ayam asmin śarīre śārīraḥ bhoktā pratisaṃdhāna ādi saṃbhavāt avagamyate
tasya ca nitya tvāt
tasya ca śārīrasya asmin śarīre bhoktṛ tvena nitya tvam puṇya pāpa upalepa saṃbhavāt sukha duḥkha upabhoga saṃbhavāt ca na devatānām
tāḥ hi parasmin aiśvarye pade vatiṣṭhamānāḥ na hīne smin śarīre bhoktṛ tvam pratilabdhum arhanti
śrutiḥ ca bhavati puṇyam eva amum gacchati na ha vai devān pāpam gacchati iti
śārīreṇa eva ca nityaḥ prāṇānām saṃbandhaḥ utkrānti ādiṣu tad anuvṛtti darśanāt tam utkrāmantam prāṇaḥ nu utkrāmati prāṇam anūtkrāmantam sarve prāṇāḥ anūtkrāmanti ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
tasmāt satīṣu api karaṇānām niyantrīṣu devatāsu na śārīrasya bhoktṛ tvam apagacchati
karaṇa pakṣasya eva hi devatā na bhoktṛ pakṣasya iti
te indriyāṇi tad vyapadeśāt anyatra śreṣṭhāt
indriya adhikaraṇam
mukhyaḥ ca ekaḥ itare ca ekādaśa prāṇāḥ anukrāntāḥ
tatra idam a param saṃdihyate kim mukhyasya eva prāṇasya vṛtti bhedāḥ itare prāṇāḥ āhosvit tattva antarāṇi iti
kim tāvat prāptam mukhyasya eva itare vṛtti bhedāḥ iti
kutas
śruteḥ
tathā hi śrutiḥ mukhyam itarān ca prāṇān saṃnidhāpya mukhya ātma tām itareṣām khyāpayati hanta asya eva sarve rūpam asāma iti te etasya eva sarve rūpam abhavan iti
prāṇa eka śabda tvāt ca eka tva adhyavasāyaḥ
itarathā hi anyāyyam aneka artha tvam prāṇa śabdasya prasajyeta ekatra vā mukhyasya itaratra lākṣaṇika tvam āpadyeta
tasmāt yathā ekasya eva prāṇasya prāṇa ādyāḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ evam vāc ādyāḥ api ekādaśa iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ tattva antarāṇi eva prāṇāt vāc ādīni iti
kutas
vyapadeśa bhedāt
kaḥ yam vyapadeśa bhedaḥ
te prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ śreṣṭham varjayitvā avaśiṣṭāḥ ekādaśa indriyāṇi iti ucyante śrutau evam vyapadeśa bheda darśanāt etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca iti hi evaṃjātīyakeṣu pradeśeṣu pṛthak prāṇaḥ vyapadiśyate pṛthak ca indriyāṇi
nanu manasaḥ api evam sati varjanam indriya tvena prāṇa vat syāt manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca iti pṛthak vyapadeśa darśanāt
satyam etat smṛtau tu ekādaśa indriyāṇi iti manaḥ pi indriya tvena śrotra ādi vat saṃgṛhyate
prāṇasya tu indriya tvam na śrutau smṛtau vā prasiddham asti
vyapadeśa bhedaḥ ca ayam tattva bheda pakṣe upapadyate
tattva ekatve tu saḥ eva ekaḥ san prāṇe indriya vyapadeśam labhate na labhate ca iti vipratiṣiddham
tasmāt tattva antara bhūtāḥ mukhyāt itare
kutas ca tattva antara bhūtāḥ
bheda śruteḥ
bhedena vāc ādibhyaḥ prāṇaḥ sarvatra śrūyate te ha vācam ūcuḥ iti upakramya vāc ādīn asura pāpma vidhvastān upanyasya upasaṃhṛtya vāc ādi prakaraṇam atha ha imam āsanyam prāṇam ūcuḥ iti asura vidhvaṃsinaḥ mukhyasya prāṇasya pṛthak upakramaṇāt
tathā manaḥ vācam prāṇam tāni ātmane kurute iti evamādyāḥ api bheda śrutayaḥ udāhartavyāḥ
tasmāt api tattva antara bhūtāḥ mukhyāt itare
kutas ca tattva antara bhūtāḥ
vailakṣaṇyāt ca
vailakṣaṇyam ca bhavati mukhyasya itareṣām ca supteṣu vāc ādiṣu mukhyaḥ ekaḥ jāgarti
saḥ eva ca ekaḥ mṛtyunā anāptaḥ āptāḥ tu itare tasya eva ca sthiti utkrāntibhyām deha dhāraṇa patana hetu tvam na indriyāṇām
viṣaya ālocana hetu tvam ca indriyāṇām na prāṇasya iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyān lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ prāṇa indriyāṇām
tasmāt api eṣām tattva antara bhāva siddhiḥ
yat uktam te etasya eva sarve rūpam abhavan iti śruteḥ prāṇaḥ eva indriyāṇi iti tat ayuktam tatra api paurvāparya ālocanāt bheda pratīteḥ
tathā hi vadiṣyāmi eva aham iti vāc dadhre iti vāc ādīni indriyāṇi anukramya tāni mṛtyuḥ śramaḥ bhūtvā upayeme tasmāt śrāmyati eva vāc iti ca śrama rūpeṇa mṛtyunā grasta tvam vāc ādīnām abhidhāya atha imam eva na āpnodyaḥ yam madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ iti pṛthak prāṇam mṛtyunā an abhibhūtam tam anukrāmati
ayam vai naḥ śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca śreṣṭha tām asya avadhārayati tasmāt tad avirodhena vāc ādiṣu parispanda lābhasya prāṇa āyatta tvam tad rūpa bhavanam vāc ādīnām iti mantavyam na tu tādātmyam
atas eva ca prāṇa śabdasya indriyeṣu lākṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ te etasya eva sarve rūpam abhavan
tasmāt ete etena ākhyāyante prāṇāḥ iti mukhya prāṇa viṣayasya eva prāṇa śabdasya indriyeṣu lākṣaṇikīm vṛttim darśayati
tasmāt tattva antarāṇi prāṇāt vāc ādīni indriyāṇi iti
saṃjñā mūrti klṛptiḥ tu trivṛt kurvataḥ upadeśāt
saṃjñā mūrti klṛpti adhikaraṇam
sat prakriyāyām tejaḥ bannānām sṛṣṭim abhidhāya upadiśyate sā iyam devatā aikṣata hanta aham imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti
tāsām trivṛtam trivṛtam ekaikām karavāṇi iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim jīva kartṛkam idam nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam āhosvit parameśvara kartṛkam iti
tatra prāptam tāvat jīva kartṛkam eva idam nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam iti
kutas
anena jīvena ātmanā iti viśeṣaṇāt yathā loke cāreṇa aham para sainyam anupraviśya saṃkalayāni iti evaṃjātīyake prayoge cāra kartṛkam eva sat sainya saṃkalanam hetu kartṛ tvāt rājā ātmani adhyāropayati saṃkalayāni iti uttama puruṣa prayogeṇa
evam jīva kartṛkam eva sat nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam hetu kartṛ tvāt devatāḥ ātmani adhyāropayati vyākaravāṇi iti uttamapuruṣa prayogeṇa
api ca ḍittha ḍavittha ādiṣu nāmasu ghaṭa śarāva ādiṣu ca rūpeṣu jīvasya eva vyākartṛ tvam dṛṣṭam
tasmāt jīva kartṛkam eva idam nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam iti evam prāpte abhidhatte saṃjñā mūrti klṛptiḥ tu iti
tu śabdena pakṣam vyāvartayati
saṃjñā mūrti klṛptiḥ iti nāma rūpa vyākriyā iti etat
trivṛt kurvataḥ iti parameśvaram lakṣayati trivṛt karaṇe tasya nirapavāda kartṛ tva nirdeśāt yā iyam saṃjñā klṛptiḥ mūrti klṛptiḥ ca agniḥ ādityaḥ candramāḥ vidyut iti tathā kuśa kāśa palāśa ādiṣu paśu mṛga manuṣya ādiṣu ca pratyākṛti prativyakti ca aneka prakārā sā khalu parameśvarasya eva tejaḥ bannānām nirmātuḥ kṛtiḥ bhavitum arhati
kutas
upadeśāt
tathā hi sā iyam devatā iti upakramya vyākaravāṇi iti uttamapuruṣa prayogeṇa parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ vyākartṛ tvam iha upadiśyate
nanu jīvena iti viśeṣaṇāt jīva kṛrtṛka tvam vyākaraṇasya adhyavasitam na etat evam
jīvena iti etat anupraviśya iti anena saṃbadhyate ānantaryāt
na vyākaravāṇi iti anena tena hi saṃbandhe vyākaravāṇi iti ayam devatā viṣaye uttama puruṣaḥ aupacārikaḥ kalpyeta
na ca giri nadī samudra ādiṣu nānāvidheṣu nāma rūpeṣu anīśvarasya jīvasya vyākaraṇa sāmarthyam asti
yeṣu api ca asti sāmarthyam teṣu api parameśvara āyattam eva tat
na ca jīvaḥ nāma parameśvarāt atyanta bhinnaḥ cāraḥ iva rājñaḥ ātmanā iti viśeṣaṇāt upādhi mātra nibandhana tvāt ca jīva bhāvasya
tena tat kṛtam api nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam parameśvara kṛtam eva bhavati
parameśvaraḥ eva ca nāma rūpayoḥ vyākartā iti sarva upaniṣad siddhāntaḥ ākāśaḥ ha vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
tasmāt parameśvarasya eva trivṛt kurvataḥ karma nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam
trivṛtkaraṇa pūrvakam eva idam iha nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam vivakṣyate pratyekam nāma rūpa vyākaraṇasya tejaḥ banna utpatti vacanena eva ukta tvāt
tat ca trivṛtkaraṇam agni āditya candra vidyutsu śrutiḥ darśayati yat agneḥ rohitam rūpam tejasaḥ tat rūpam yat śuklam tat apām yat kṛṣṇam tat annasya ityādinā
tatra agniḥ iti idam rūpam vyākriyate sati ca rūpa vyākaraṇe viṣaya pratilambhāt agniḥ iti idam nāma vyākriyate
evam eva āditya candra vidyutsu api draṣṭavyam
anena ca agni ādi udāharaṇena bhauma ambhasa taijaseṣu triṣu api dravyeṣu aviśeṣeṇa trivṛtkaraṇam uktam bhavati upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt
tathā hi aviśeṣeṇa eva upakramaḥ imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ trivṛt itravṛt ekaikā bhavati iti aviśeṣeṇa eva ca upasaṃhāraḥ yat u rohitam iva abhūt iti tejasaḥ tat rūpam iti evamādiḥ yat u avijñātam iva abhūt iti etāsām eva devatānām samāsaḥ iti evamantaḥ
tāsām tisṛṇām devatānām bahis trivṛt kṛtānām satīnām adhyātmam aparam trivṛt karaṇam uktam imāḥ tisraḥ devatāḥ puruṣam prāpya trivṛt itravṛt ekaikā bhavati iti
tat idānīm ācāryaḥ yathāśrutyā iva upadarśayati āśaṅkitam kaṃcid doṣam parihariṣyan
māṃsa ādi bhaumam yathāśabdam itarayoḥ ca
bhūmeḥ trivṛtkṛtāyāḥ puruṣeṇa upabhujyamānāyāḥ māṃsa ādi kāryam yathāśabdam niṣpadyate
tathā hi śrutiḥ annam aśitam tredhā vidhīyate tasya yaḥ sthaviṣṭhaḥ dhātuḥ tat purīṣam bhavati yaḥ madhyamaḥ tat māṃsam yaḥ ṇiṣṭhaḥ tat manaḥ iti
trivṛtkṛtā bhūmiḥ eva eṣā vrīhi yava ādi anna rūpeṇa adyate iti abhiprāyaḥ
tasyāḥ ca sthaviṣṭham rūpam purīṣa bhāvena bahis nirgacchati
madhyamam adhyātmam māṃsam vardhayati
aṇiṣṭham tu manaḥ
evam itarayoḥ ap tejasoḥ yathāśabdam kāryam avagantavyam mūtram lohitam prāṇaḥ ca apām kāryam asthi majjā vāc tejasaḥ iti
atra āha yadi sarvam eva trivṛt kṛtam bhūta bhautikam a viśeṣa śruteḥ tāsām trivṛtam trivṛtam ekaikām akarot iti kim kṛtaḥ tarhi ayam viśeṣa vyapadeśaḥ idam tejaḥ imāḥ āpaḥ idam annam iti
tathā adhyātmam idam annasya aśitasya kāryam māṃsa ādi idam apām pītānām kāryam lohita ādi idam tejasaḥ u śitasya kāryam asthi ādi iti
atrā ucyate
vaiśeṣyāt tu tad vādaḥ tad vādaḥ
tu śabdena coditam doṣam apanudati
viśeṣasya bhāvaḥ vaiśeṣyam bhūyaḥ tvam iti yāvat
sati api trivṛtkaraṇe kvacid kasyacid bhūta dhātoḥ bhūyaḥ tvam upalabhyate agneḥ tejaḥ bhūyaḥ tvam udakasya ap bhūyaḥ tvam pṛthivyāḥ anna bhūyaḥ tvam iti
vyavahāra prasiddhi artham ca idam trivṛtkaraṇam
vyavahāraḥ ca trivṛtkṛta rajju vat eka tva āpattau satyām na bhedena bhūta traya gocaraḥ lokasya prasidhyet
tasmāt sati api trivṛtkaraṇe vaiśeṣyāt eva tejaḥ banna viśeṣa vādaḥ bhūta bhautika viṣayaḥ upapadyate
tad vādaḥ tad vādaḥ iti pada abhyāsaḥ adhyāya parisamāptim dyotayati
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye dvitīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ

tṛtīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ
prathamaḥ pādaḥ
tad antara pratipattau raṃhati sampariṣvaktaḥ praśna nirūpaṇābhyām
tad antara pratipatti adhikaraṇam
dvitīye
adhyāye smṛti nyāya virodhaḥ vedānta vihite brahma darśane parihṛtaḥ
parapakṣāṇām ca anapekṣa tvam prapañcitam
śruti vipratiṣedhaḥ ca parihṛtaḥ
tatra ca jīva vyatiriktāni tattvāni jīva upakaraṇāni brahmaṇaḥ jāyante iti uktam
atha idānīm upakaraṇa upahitasya jīvasya saṃsāra gati prakāraḥ tad avasthā antarāṇi brahma tattvam vidyā bheda abhedau guṇa upasaṃhāra anupasaṃhārau samyak darśanāt puruṣa artha siddhaḥ samyak darśana upāya vidhi prabhedaḥ mukti phala aniyamaḥ ca iti etad artha jātam tṛtīye
adhyāye nirūpayiṣyate prasaṅga āgatam ca kim api anyat
tatra prathame tāvat pāde pañcāgni vidyām āśritya saṃsāra gati prabhedaḥ pradarśyate vairāgya hetoḥ
tasmāt jugupset iti ca ante śravaṇāt
jīvaḥ mukhya prāṇa sacivaḥ sa indriyaḥ sa manaḥ kaḥ
avidyā karma pūrva prajñā parigrahaḥ pūrva deham vihāya deha antaram pratipadyate iti etat avagatam
atha enam ete prāṇāḥ abhisamāyanti iti evamādeḥ anyan avataram kalyāṇataram rūpam kurute
iti evama antāt saṃsāra prakaraṇa sthāt śabdāt dharma adharma phala upabhoga saṃbhavāt ca
sa kim deha bījaiḥ bhūta sūkṣmaiḥ a saṃpariṣvaktaḥ gacchati āhosvit saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti cintyate
kim tāvat prāptam
a saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti
kutas
karaṇa upādāna vat bhūta upādānasya a śruta tvāt
saḥ etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyādadānaḥ SNPaPrM
iti hi atra tejaḥ mātrā śabdena karaṇānām upādānam saṃkīrtayati
vākya śeṣe cakṣuḥ ādi saṃkīrtanāt
na evam bhūtamātra upādāna saṃkīrtanam asti
sulabhāḥ ca sarvatra bhūtamātrāḥ
yatra eva dehaḥ ārabdhavyaḥ tatra eva santi tatas ca tāsām nayanam niṣprayojanam
tasmāt a saṃpariṣvaktaḥ yāti iti
evam prāpte paṭhati ācāryaḥ tad antara pratipattau raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti
tad antara pratipattau deha antara pratipattau deha bījaiḥ bhūta sūkṣmaiḥ saṃpariṣvaktaḥ raṃhati gacchati iti avagantavyam
kutas
praśna nirūpaṇābhyām
tathā hi praśnaḥ vettha yathā pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavanti iti
nirūpaṇam ca prativacanam dyu parjanya pṛthivī puruṣa yoṣitsu pañcasu agniṣu śraddhā soma vṛṣṭi anna retaḥ rūpāḥ pañca āhutīḥ darśayitvā iti tu pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavanti iti
tasmāt adbhiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ jīvaḥ raṃhati vrajati iti gamyate
nanu anyā śrutiḥ jalūkā vat pūrva deham na muñcati yāvat na deha antaram ākramati iti darśayati tat yathā tṛṇajalāyukāḥ iti
tatra api ap pariveṣṭitasya eva jīvasya karma upasthāpita pratipattavya deha viṣaya bhāvanā dīrghībhāva mātram jalūkayā upamīyate iti avirodhaḥ
evam śruti ukte deha antara pratipatti prakāre sati yāḥ puruṣam ati prabhavāḥ kalpanāḥ vyāpinām karaṇānām ātmanaḥ ca deha antara pratipattau karma vaśāt vṛtti lābhaḥ tatra bhavati kevalasya eva ātmanaḥ vṛtti lābhaḥ tatra bhavati indriyāṇi tu deha vat abhinavāni eva tatra tatra bhogasthāne utpadyante manaḥ eva vā kevalam bhogasthānam abhipratiṣṭhate jīvaḥ eva vā utplutya dehāt deha antaram pratipadyate śukaḥ iva vṛkṣāt vṛkṣa antaram iti evam
nanu udāhṛtābhyām praśna prativacanābhyām kevalābhiḥ adbhiḥ saṃpariṣvaktaḥ raṃhati iti prāpnoti ap śabda śravaṇa sāmarthyāt
tatra katham sāmānyena pratijñāyate sarvaiḥ eva bhūta sūkṣmaiḥ saṃpariṣvaktaḥ raṃhati iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
tri ātmaka tvāt tu bhūyaḥ tvāt
tu śabdena ca uditām āśaṅkām ucchinatti
tri ātmikāḥ hi āpaḥ trivṛtkaraṇa śruteḥ
tāsu ārambhikāsu abhyupagatāsu itarat api bhūta dvayam avaśyam abhyupagantavyam bhavati
tri ātmakaḥ ca dehaḥ trayāṇām api tejaḥ bannānām tasmin kārya upalabdheḥ
punar ca tri ātmakaḥ tri dhātu tvāt tribhiḥ vāta pitta śleṣmabhiḥ
na sa bhūta antarāṇi pratyākhyāya kevalābhiḥ adbhiḥ ārabdhum śakyate
tasmāt bhūyastva apekṣaḥ yam āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ iti praśna prativacanayoḥ ap śabdaḥ na kaivalya apekṣaḥ
sarva deheṣu hi rasa lohita ādi drava bhūyaḥ tvam dṛśyate
nanu pārthivaḥ dhātuḥ bhūyiṣṭhaḥ deheṣu upalabhyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ itara apekṣayā apām bāhulyam bhaviṣyati
dṛśyate ca śukra śoṇita lakṣaṇe deha bīje drava bāhulyam
karma ca nimitta kāraṇam deha antara ārambhe
karmāṇi ca agnihotra ādīni soma ājya payaḥ prabhṛti drava dravya vyapāśrayāṇi
karma samavāyinyaḥ ca āpaḥ śraddhā śabda uditāḥ saha karmabhiḥ dyu loka ākhye gnau hūyante iti vakṣyati
tasmāt api apām bāhulya prasiddhiḥ
bāhulyāt ca ap śabdena sarveṣām eva deha bījānām bhūta sūkṣmāṇām upādānam iti niravadyam
prāṇa gateḥ ca
prāṇānām ca deha antara pratipattau gatiḥ śrāvyate tam utkrāmantam prāṇaḥ nu utkrāmati prāṇam anūtkrāmantam sarve prāṇāḥ anūtkrāmanti ityādi śrutibhiḥ
sā ca prāṇānām gatiḥ na āśrayam antareṇa saṃbhavati iti atas prāṇa gati prayuktā tad āśraya bhūtānām apām api bhūta antara upasṛṣṭānām gatiḥ arthāt avagamyate
na hi nirāśrayāḥ prāṇāḥ kvacid gacchanti tiṣṭhanti vā jīvataḥ darśanāt
aṃgni ādi gati śruteḥ iti ced na bhākta tvāt
syāt etat na eva prāṇāḥ deha antara pratipattau saha jīvena gacchanti agni ādi gati śruteḥ
tathā hi śrutiḥ maraṇa kāle vāc ādayaḥ prāṇāḥ agni ādīn devān gacchanti iti darśayati yatra asya puruṣasya mṛtasya agnim vāc apyeti vātam prāṇaḥ ityādinā iti ced na bhākta tvāt
vāc ādīnām agni ādi gati śrutiḥ gauṇī lomasu keśeṣu ca adarśanāt oṣadhīḥ lomāni vanaspatīn keśāḥ iti hi tatra āmnāyate na hi lomāni keśāḥ ca utplutya oṣadhīḥ vanaspatīn ca gacchanti iti saṃbhavati
na ca jīvasya prāṇa upādhi pratyākhyāne gamanam avakalpate
nā api prāṇaiḥ vinā deha antare upabhogaḥ upapadyate
vispaṣṭam ca prāṇānām saha jīvena gamanam anyatra śrāvitam
atas vāc ādi adhiṣṭhātrīṇām agni ādi devatānām vāc ādi upakāriṇīnām maraṇa kāle upakāra nivṛtti mātram apekṣya vāc ādayaḥ gni ādīn gacchanti iti upacaryate
prathame śravaṇāt iti ced na tāḥ eva hi upapatteḥ
syāt etat katham punar pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavanti iti etat nirdhārayitum pāryate yāvatā na eva prathame gnau apām śravaṇam asti
iha hi dyu loka prabhṛtayaḥ pañca agnyaḥ pañcānām āhutīnām ādhāra tvena adhītāḥ
teṣām ca pramukhe asau vāva lokaḥ gautama agniḥ iti upanyasya tasmin etasmin agnau devāḥ śraddhām juhvati iti śraddhā homya dravya tvena āveditā
na tatra āpaḥ homya dravya tayā śrutāḥ
yadi nāma parjanya ādiṣu uttareṣu caturṣu agniṣu apām homya dravya tā parikalpyeta parikalpyatām nāma teṣu hotavya tayā upāttānām soma ādīnām ap bahula tva upapatteḥ
prathame tu agnau śrutām śraddhām parityajya a śrutāḥ āpaḥ parikalpyante iti sāhasam etat
śraddhā ca nāma pratyaya viśeṣaḥ prasiddhi sāmarthyāt
tasmāt ayuktaḥ pañcamyām āhutau apām puruṣa bhāvaḥ iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ
hi yatas tatra api prathame gnau tāḥ eva āpaḥ śraddhā śabdena abhipreyante
kutas
upapatteḥ
evam hi ādi madhya avasāna saṃgānāt an ākulam etat eka vākyam upapadyate
itarathā punar pañcamyām āhutau apām puruṣa vacaḥ tva prakāre pṛṣṭe prativacana avasare prathama āhuti sthāne yadi an apaḥ homya dravyam śraddhām nāma avatārayet tatas anyathā praśnaḥ nyathā prativacanam iti ekavākya tā na syāt
iti tu pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavanti iti ca upasaṃharan etat eva darśayati
śraddhā kāryam ca soma vṛṣṭi ādi sthūlībhavat ap bahulam lakṣyate
sā ca śraddhāyāḥ ap tve yuktiḥ
kāraṇa anurūpam hi kāryam bhavati
na ca śraddhā ākhyaḥ pratyayaḥ manasaḥ jīvasya vā dharmaḥ san dharmiṇaḥ niṣkṛṣya homāya upādātum śakyate paśu ādibhyaḥ iva hṛdaya ādīni iti āpaḥ eva śraddhā śabdāḥ bhaveyuḥ
śraddhā śabdaḥ ca apsu upapadyate vaidika prayoga darśanāt śraddhā vai āpaḥ iti
tanu tvam śraddhā sārūpyam gacchanti āpaḥ deha bīja bhūtāḥ iti atas śraddhā śabdāḥ syuḥ yathā siṃha parākramaḥ naraḥ siṃha śabdaḥ bhavati
śraddhā pūrvaka karma samavāyāt ca apsu śraddhā śabdaḥ upapadyate mañca śabdaḥ iva puruṣeṣu
śraddhā hetu tvāt ca śraddhā śabda upapattiḥ āpaḥ ha asmai śraddhām saṃnamante puṇyāya karmaṇe iti śruteḥ
aśruta tvāt iti ced na iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām pratīteḥ
atha api syāt praśna prativacanābhyām nāma āpaḥ śraddhā ādi krameṇa pañcamyām āhutau puruṣa ākāram pratipadyeran
na tu tad saṃpariṣvaktāḥ jīvāḥ raṃheyuḥ a śruta tvāt na hi atra apām iva jīvānām śrāvayitā kaścid śabdaḥ sti
tasmāt raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti ayuktam iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ
kutas
iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām pratīteḥ atha ye ime grāme iṣṭāpūrte dattam iti upāsate te dhūmam abhisaṃbhavanti iti upakramya iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām dhūma ādinā pitṛyāṇena pathā candra prāptim kathayati ākāśāt candramasam eṣa somaḥ rājā iti
te eva iha api pratīyante tasmin etasmin agnau devāḥ śraddhām juhvati tasyāḥ āhuteḥ somaḥ rājā saṃbhavati iti śruti sāmānyāt
teṣām ca agnihotra darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi karma sādhana bhūtāḥ dadhi payaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ drava dravya bhūyaḥ tvāt pratyakṣam eva āpaḥ santi
tāḥ āhavanīye hutāḥ sūkṣmāḥ pūrva rūpāḥ satyaḥ tān iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ āśrayanti teṣām ca śarīram naidhanena vidhānena antye gnau ṛtvijaḥ juhvati asau svargāya lokāya svāhā iti
tatas tāḥ śraddhā pūrvaka karma samavāyinyaḥ āhuti mayyaḥ āpaḥ pūrva rūpāḥ satyaḥ tān iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ jīvān pariveṣṭya amum lokam phala dānāya nayanti iti yat tat atra juhotinā abhidhīyate śraddhām juhvati iti
tathā ca agnihotre ṣaṭpraśnī nirvacana rūpeṇa vākyaśeṣeṇa te vai ete āhutī hute utkrāmataḥ iti evamādinā agnihotra āhutyoḥ phala ārambhāya loka antara prāptiḥ darśitā
tasmāt āhutī mayībhiḥ adbhiḥ saṃpariṣvaktāḥ jīvāḥ raṃhanti sva karma phala upabhogāya iti śliṣyate
katham punar idam iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām sva karma phala upabhogāya raṃhaṇam pratijñāyate yāvatā teṣām dhūma pratīkena vartmanā candramasam adhirūḍhānām anna bhāvam darśayati eṣa somaḥ rājā tat devānām annam tam bhakṣayanti iti te candram prāpya annam bhavanti tān tatra devāḥ yathā somam rājānam āpyāyasva apakṣīyasva iti evam etān tatra bhakṣayanti iti ca samāna viṣayam śruti antaram
na ca vyāghra ādibhiḥ iva devaiḥ bhakṣyamāṇānām upabhogaḥ saṃbhavati iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
bhāktam vā an ātma vid tvāt tathā hi darśayati
vā śabdaḥ codita doṣa vyāvartana arthaḥ
bhāktam eṣām anna tvam na mukhyam
mukhye hi anna tve svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti evaṃjātīyaka adhikāra śrutiḥ uparudhyeta
candra maṇḍale ced iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām upabhogaḥ na syāt kimartham adhikāriṇaḥ iṣṭa ādi āyāsa bahulam karma kuryuḥ
anna śabdaḥ ca upabhoga hetu tva sāmānyāt an anne pi upacaryamāṇaḥ dṛśyate yathā viśaḥ nnam rājñām paśavaḥ nnam viśām iti
tasmāt iṣṭa strī putra mitra bhṛtya ādibhiḥ iva guṇa bhāva upagataiḥ iṣṭa ādi kāribhiḥ yat sukha viharaṇam devānām tat eva eṣām bhakṣaṇam abhipretam na modaka ādi vat carvaṇam nigaraṇam vā
na ha vai devāḥ aśnanti na pibanti etat eva amṛtam dṛṣṭvā tṛpyanti iti ca devānām carvaṇā ādi vyāpāram vārayati
teṣām ca iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām devān prati guṇa bhāva upagatānām api upabhogaḥ upapadyate rāja upajīvinām iva parijanānām
anātma vid tvāt ca iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām deva upabhogya bhāvaḥ upapadyate
tathā hi śrutiḥ anātma vidām deva upabhogya tām darśayati atha yaḥ nyām devatām upāste saḥ anyaḥ ham asmi iti na sa veda yathā paśuḥ evam sa devānām iti
sa ca asmin api loke iṣṭa ādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ prīṇayan paśu vat devānām upakaroti amuṣmin api loke tad upajīvī tad ādiṣṭam phalam upabhuñjānaḥ paśu vat eva devānām upakaroti iti gamyate
anātma vid tvāt tathā hi darśayati iti asya aparā vyākhyā anātma vidaḥ hi ete kevala karmiṇaḥ iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ na jñāna karma samuccaya anuṣṭhāyinaḥ pañcāgni vidyām iha ātma vidyā iti upacaranti prakaraṇāt
pañcāgni vidyā vihīna tvāt ca idam iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām guṇa vādena anna tvam udbhāvyate pañcāgni vijñāna praśaṃsāyai
pañcāgni vidyā iha vidhitsitā vākya tātparya avagamāt
tathā hi śruti antaram candra maṇḍale bhoga sadbhāvam darśayati sa soma loke vibhūtim anubhūya punar āvartate iti
tathā anyat api śruti antaram atha ye śatam pitṛṇām jita lokānām ānandāḥ saḥ ekaḥ karma devānām ānandaḥ ye karmaṇā deva tvam abhisaṃpadyante iti iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām devaiḥ saha saṃvasatām bhoga prāptim darśayati
evam bhākta tvāt anna bhāva vacanasya iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ jīvāḥ raṃhanti iti pratīyate
tasmāt raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti yuktam eva uktam
kṛta atyaye dṛṣṭa smṛtibhyām ca
kṛta atyaya adhikaraṇam
iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām dhūma ādinā vartmanā candra maṇḍalam adhirūḍhānām bhukta bhogānām tatas pratyavarohaḥ āmnāyate tasmin yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā atha etam eva adhvānam punar nivartante yathetam iti ārabhya yāvat ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ brāhmaṇa ādi yonim āpadyante kapūya caraṇāḥ śva ādi yonim iti
tatra idam vicāryate kim niranuśayāḥ bhukta kṛtsna karmāṇaḥ varohanti āhosvit sa anuśayāḥ iti
kim tāvat prāptam
niranuśayāḥ iti
kutas
yāvat saṃpātam iti viśeṣaṇāt saṃpāta śabdena atra karma āśayaḥ ucyate saṃpatanti anena asmāt lokāt amum lokam phala upabhogāya iti
yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā iti ca kṛtsnasya tasya kṛtasya tatra eva bhukta tām darśayati
teṣām yadā tat paryavaiti iti ca śruti antareṇa eva eva arthaḥ pradarśyate
syāt etat yāvat amuṣmin loke upabhoktavyam karma tāvat upabhuṅkte iti kalpayiṣyāmi iti
na evam kalpayitum śakyate yat kiṃca iti anyatra parāmarśāt prāpya antam karmaṇaḥ tasya yat kiṃca iha karoti ayam
tasmāt lokāt punar aiti asmai lokāya karmaṇe iti hi aparā śrutiḥ yat kiṃca iti a viśeṣa parāmarśena kṛtsnasya iha kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ tatra kṣayita tām darśayati
api ca prāyaṇam an ārabdha phalasya karmaṇaḥ bhivyañjakam
prāk prāyaṇāt ārabdha phalena karmaṇā pratibaddhasya abhivyakti anupapatteḥ
tat ca aviśeṣāt yāvat kiṃcid anārabdha phalam tasya sarvasya abhivyañjakam
na hi sādhāraṇe nimitte naimittikam asādhāraṇam bhavitum arhati
na hi aviśiṣṭe pradīpa saṃnidhau ghaṭaḥ bhivyajyate na paṭaḥ iti upapadyate
tasmāt niranuśayāḥ avarohanti iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ kṛta atyaye iti
yena karma bṛndena candramasam ārūḍhāḥ phala upabhogāya tasmin upabhogena kṣayite teṣām yat am mayam śarīram candramasi upabhogāya ārabdham tat upabhoga kṣaya darśana śoka agni saṃparkāt pravilīyate savitṛ kiraṇa saṃparka ādi vahima karakāḥ hutabhuj arciḥ saṃparkāt iva ca ghṛta kāṭhinyam
tatas kṛta atyaye kṛtasya iṣṭa ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ phala upabhogena upakṣaye sati sa anuśayāḥ eva imam avarohanti
kena hetunā
dṛṣṭa smṛtibhyām iti āha
tathā hi pratyakṣā śrutiḥ sa anuśayānām avaroham darśayati tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ abhyāśaḥ ha yat te ramaṇīyām yonim āpadyeran brāhmaṇa yonim vā kṣatriya yonim vā vaiśya yonim vā atha ye iha kapūya caraṇāḥ abhyāśaḥ ha yat te kapūyām yonim āpadyeran śva yonim vā sūkara yonim vā cāṇḍāla yonim vā iti
caraṇa śabdena anuśayaḥ sūcyate iti varṇayiṣyati
dṛṣṭaḥ ca ayam janmanā eva prati prāṇi uccāvaca rūpaḥ upabhogaḥ pravibhajyamānaḥ ākasmika tva asaṃbhavāt anuśaya sadbhāvam sūcayati abhyudaya pratyavāyayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛta hetu tvasya sāmānyatas śāstreṇa avagamita tvāt
smṛtiḥ api varṇāḥ āśramāḥ ca sva karma niṣṭhāḥ pretya karma phalam anubhūya tatas śeṣeṇa viśiṣṭa deśa jāti kula rūpa āyuḥ śruta vṛtta vitta sukha medhasaḥ janma pratipadyante iti sa anuśayānām eva avaroham darśayati
kaḥ punar anuśayaḥ nāma iti kecid tāvat āhuḥ svarga arthasya karmaṇaḥ bhukta phalasya avaśeṣaḥ kaścid anuśayaḥ nāma bhāṇḍa anusāri sneha vat yathā hi sneha bhāṇḍam ricyamānam na sarva ātmanā ricyate bhāṇḍa anusāri eva kaścid sneha śeṣaḥ vatiṣṭhate tathā anuśayaḥ u pi iti
nanu kārya virodhi tvāt adṛṣṭasya na bhukta phalasya avaśeṣa avasthānam nyāyyam
na ayam doṣaḥ
na hi sarva ātmanā bhukta phala tvam karmaṇaḥ pratijānīmahe
nanu niravaśeṣa karma phala upabhogāya candra maṇḍalam ārūḍhāḥ
bāḍham tathā api su alpa karma avaśeṣa mātreṇa tatra avasthānam na labhyate
yathā kila kaścid sevakaḥ sakalaiḥ sevā upakaraṇaiḥ rājakulam upasṛptaḥ cira pravāsāt parikṣīṇa bahu upakaraṇaḥ chatra pādukā ādi mātra avaśeṣaḥ na rājakule vasthātum śaknoti evam anuśaya mātra parigrahaḥ na candra maṇḍale vasthātum śaknoti iti
na ca etat yuktam iva eva
na hi svarga arthasya karmaṇaḥ bhukta phalasya avaśeṣa anuvṛttiḥ upapadyate kārya virodhi tvāt iti uktam
nanu etat api uktam na svarga phalasya karmaṇaḥ nikhilasya bhukta phala tvam bhaviṣyati iti
tat etat apeśalam svarga artham kila karma svarga sthasya eva svarga phalam nikhilam na janayati svarga cyutasya api kaṃcid phala leśam janayati iti
na śabdapramāṇakānām īdṛśī kalpanā avakalpate
sneha bhāṇḍe tu sneha leśa anuvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt upapadyate
tathā sevakasya upakaraṇa leśa anuvṛttiḥ ca dṛśyate
na tu iha tathā svarga phalasya karmaṇaḥ leśa anuvṛttiḥ dṛśyate
na api kalpayitum śakyate svarga phala tva śāstra virodhāt
avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam na svarga phalasya iṣṭa ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ bhāṇḍa anusāri sneha vat eka deśaḥ nuvartamānaḥ nuśayaḥ iti
yadi hi yena su kṛtena karmaṇā iṣṭa ādinā svargam anvabhūvan tasya eva kaścid eka deśaḥ nuśayaḥ kalpyeta tatas ramaṇīyaḥ eva ekaḥ nuśayaḥ syāt na viparītaḥ
tatra iyam anuśaya vibhāga śrutiḥ uparudhyeta tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ
atha ye iha kapūya caraṇāḥ iti
