tasmāt āmuṣmika phale karma jāte upabhukte aihika phalam karma antara jātam anuśayaḥ tadvantaḥ varohanti iti
yat uktam yat kiṃca iti a viśeṣa parāmarśāt sarvasya iha kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phala upabhogena antam prāpya niranuśayāḥ avarohanti iti na etat evam
anuśaya sadbhāvasya avagamita tvāt yat kiṃcid iha kṛtam āmuṣmika phalam karma ārabdha bhogam tat sarvam phala upabhogena kṣapayitvā iti gamyate
yat api uktam prāyaṇam aviśeṣāt anārabdha phalam kṛtsnam eva karma abhivyanakti
tatra kenacid phalam ārabhyate kenacid asmin iti ayam vibhāgaḥ na saṃbhavati iti tat api anuśaya sadbhāva pratipādanena eva pratyuktam
api ca kena hetunā prāyaṇam anārabdha phalasya karmaṇaḥ bhivyañjakam pratijñāyate iti vaktavyam
ārabdha phalena karmaṇā pratibaddhasya itarasya vṛtti udbhava anupapatteḥ tad upaśamāt prāyaṇa kāle vṛtti udbhavaḥ bhavati iti yadi ucyeta tatas vaktavyam yathā eva tarhi pāk prāyaṇāt ārabdha phalena karmaṇā pratibaddhasya itarasya vṛtti udbhava anupapattiḥ evam prāyaṇa kāle pi viruddha phalasya anekasya karmaṇaḥ yugapad phala ārambha asaṃbhavāt balavatā pratibaddhasya durbalasya vṛtti udbhava anupapattiḥ iti
na hi anārabdha phalatva sāmānyena jāti antara upabhogya phalam api anekam karma ekasmin prāyaṇe yugapad abhivyaktam sat ekām jātim ārabhate iti śakyam vaktum pratiniyata phalatva virodhāt
nā api kasyacid karmaṇaḥ prāyaṇe bhivyaktiḥ kasyacid ucchedaḥ iti śakyate vaktum aikāntika phala tva virodhāt
na hi prāyaścitta ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ vinā karmaṇām ucchedaḥ saṃbhāvyate
smṛtiḥ api viruddha phalena karmaṇā pratibaddhasya karma antarasya ciram avasthānam darśayati kadācid su kṛtam karma kūṭastham iha tiṣṭhati
majjamānasya saṃsāre yāvat duḥkhāt vimucyate iti evaṃjātīyākā
yadi ca kṛtsnam anārabdha phalam karma ekasmin prāyaṇe bhivyaktam sat ekām jātim ārabheta tatas svarga naraka tiryagyoniṣu adhikāra anavagamāt dharma adharma anutpattau nimitta abhāvāt na uttarā jātiḥ upapadyeta brahmahatyā ādīnām ca ekaikasya karmaṇaḥ neka janma nimitta tvam smaryamāṇam uparudhyeta
na ca dharma adharmayoḥ svarūpa phala sādhana ādi samadhigame śāstrāt atiriktam kāraṇam śakyam saṃbhāvayitum
na ca dṛṣṭa phalasya karmaṇaḥ kārīrī ādeḥ prāyaṇam abhivyañjakam saṃbhavati iti avyāpikā api iyam prāyaṇasya abhivyañjaka tva kalpanā
pradīpa upanyāsaḥ u pi karma bala abala pradarśanena eva pratinītaḥ
sthūla sūkṣma rūpa abhivyakti vat ca idam draṣṭavyam yathā hi pradīpaḥ samāne saṃnidhāne sthūlam rūpam abhivyanakti na sūkṣmam evam prāyaṇam samāne pi anārabdha phalasya karma jātasya prāpta avasara tve balavataḥ karmaṇaḥ vṛttim udbhāvayati na durbalasya iti
tasmāt śruti smṛti nyāya virodhāt aśliṣṭaḥ yama śeṣa karma abhivyakti abhyupagamaḥ
śeṣa karma sadbhāve nirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti ayam api asthāne saṃbhramaḥ samyak darśanāt aśeṣa karma kṣaya śruteḥ
tasmāt sthitam etat eva anuśayavantaḥ varohanti iti
te ca avarohantaḥ yathetam anevam ca avarohanti
yathetam iti yathāgatam iti arthaḥ
anevam iti tad viparyayeṇa iti arthaḥ
dhūma ākāśayoḥ pitṛyāṇe dhvani upāttayoḥ avarohe saṃkīrtanāt yathetam śabdāt ca yathāgatam iti pratīyate
rātri ādi a saṃkīrtanāt abhra ādi upasaṃkhyānāt ca viparyayaḥ pi pratīyate
caraṇāt iti ced na upalakṣaṇa arthā iti kārṣṇājiniḥ
atha api syāt yā śrutiḥ anuśaya sadbhāva pratipādanāya udāhṛtā tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ iti sā khalu caraṇāt yoni āpattim darśayati na anuśayāt
anyat caraṇam anyaḥ nuśayaḥ caraṇam cāritram ācāraḥ śīlam iti anartha antaram anuśayaḥ tu bhukta phalāt karmaṇaḥ tiriktam karma abhipretam
śrutiḥ ca karma caraṇe bhedena vyapadiśati yathā kārī yathā cārī tathā bhavati iti yāni anavadyāni karmāṇi tāni sevitavyāni no itarāṇi yāni asmākäsu caritāni tāni tvayā upāsyāni iti ca
tasmāt caraṇāt yoni āpatti śruteḥ na anuśaya siddhiḥ iti ced nā eṣa doṣaḥ yatas nuśaya upalakṣaṇa arthā eva eṣā caraṇa śrutiḥ iti kārṣṇājiniḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
ānarthakyam iti ced na tat apekṣa tvāt
syāt etat kasmāt punar caraṇa śabdena śrautam śīlam vihāya lākṣaṇikaḥ anuśayaḥ pratyāyyate
nanu śīlasya eva śrautasya vihita pratiṣiddhasya sādhu asādhu rūpasya śubha aśubha yoni āpattiḥ phalam bhaviṣyati
avaśyam ca śīlasya api kiṃcid phalam abhyupagantavyam anyathā hi ānarthakyam eva śīlasya prasajyeta iti ced nā eṣa doṣaḥ
kutas
tad apekṣa tvāt
iṣṭa ādi hi karma jātam caraṇa apekṣam
na hi sat ācāra hīnaḥ kaścid adhikṛtaḥ syāt ācāra hīnam na punanti vedāḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ
puruṣa artha tve pi ācārasya na ānarthakyam
iṣṭa ādau hi karma jāte phalam ārabhamāṇe tad apekṣaḥ eva ācāraḥ tatra eva kaṃcid atiśayam ārapsyate
karma ca sarva artha kāri iti śruti smṛti prasiddhiḥ
tasmāt karma eva śīla upalakṣitam anuśaya bhūtam yoni āpattau kāraṇam iti kārṣṇājineḥ matam
na hi karmaṇi saṃbhavati śīlāt yoni āpattiḥ yuktā
na hi padbhyām palāyitum pārayamāṇaḥ jānubhyām raṃhitum arhati iti
sukṛta duṣkṛte eva iti tu bādariḥ
bādariḥ tu ācāryaḥ sukṛta duṣkṛte eva caraṇa śabdena pratyāyyete iti manyate
caraṇam anuṣṭhāna karma iti anartha antaram
tathā hi aviśeṣeṇa karma mātre caratiḥ prayujyamānaḥ dṛśyate yaḥ hi iṣṭa ādi lakṣaṇam puṇyam karma karoti tam laukikāḥ ācakṣate dharmam carati eṣa mahātmā iti
ācāraḥ ca dharma viśeṣaḥ eva
bheda vyapadeśaḥ tu karma caraṇayoḥ brāhmaṇa parivrājaka nyāyena api upapadyate
tasmāt ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ praśasta karmāṇaḥ kapūya caraṇāḥ nindita karmāṇaḥ iti nirṇayaḥ
aniṣṭa ādi kāriṇām api ca śrutam
aniṣṭa ādi kāri adhikaraṇam
iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ candramasam gacchanti iti uktam
ye tu itare niṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ te kim candramasam gacchanti uta na gacchanti iti cintyate
tatra tāvat āha iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ eva candramasam gacchanti iti etat na
kasmāt
yatas niṣṭa ādi kāriṇām api candra maṇḍalam gantavya tvena śrutam
tathā hi aviśeṣeṇa kauṣītakinaḥ samāmananti ye vai ke ca asmāt lokāt prayanti candramasam eva te sarve gacchanti iti
ca punar jāyamānānām na antareṇa candra prāptim avakalpate pañcamyām āhutau iti āhuti saṃkhyā niyamāt
tasmāt sarve eva candramasam āsīdeyuḥ
iṣṭa ādi kāriṇām itareṣām ca samāna gati tvam na yuktam iti ced na itareṣām candra maṇḍale bhoga abhāvāt
saṃyamane tu anubhūya itareṣām āroha avarohau tad gati darśanāt
tu śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati
na etat asti sarve candramasam gacchanti iti
kasmāt
bhogāya eva hi candra ārohaṇam na niṣprayojanam
na api pratyavarohāya eva yathā kaścid vṛkṣam ārohati puṣpa phala upādānāya na niṣprayojanam na api patanāya eva
bhogaḥ ca aniṣṭa ādi kāriṇām candramasi na asti iti uktam
tasmāt iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ eva candramasam ārohanti na itare
te tu saṃyamanam yama ālayam avagāhya sva duṣkṛta anurūpāḥ yāmīḥ yātanāḥ anubhūya punar eva imam lokam pratyavarohanti
evaṃbhūtau teṣām āroha avarohau bhavataḥ
kutas
tad gati darśanāt
tathā hi yama vacana sarūpā śrutiḥ prayatām aniṣṭa ādi kāriṇām yama vaśya tām darśayati na sāṃparāyaḥ pratibhāti bālam pramādyantam vitta mohena mūḍham
ayam lokaḥ na asti paraḥ iti mānī punar punar vaśam āpadyate me iti
vaivasvatam saṃgamanam janānām iti evaṃjātīyakam ca bahu eva yama vaśya tā prāpti liṅgam bhavati
smaranti ca
api ca manu vyāsa prabhṛtayaḥ śiṣṭāḥ saṃyamane pure yama āyattam kapūya karma vipākam smaranti nāciketa upākhyāna ādiṣu
api ca sapta
api ca sapta narakāḥ raurava pramukhāḥ duṣkṛta phala upabhoga bhūmi tvena smaryante paurāṇikaiḥ
tān aniṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ prāpnuvanti
kutas te candram prāpnuyuḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ
nanu viruddham idam yama āyattāḥ yātanāḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ nubhavanti iti yāvatā teṣu raurava ādiṣu anye citragupta ādayaḥ nānā adhiṣṭhātāraḥ smaryante iti
na iti āha
tatra api ca tad vyāpārāt avirodhaḥ
teṣu api saptasu narakeṣu tasya eva yamasya adhiṣṭhātṛ tva vyāpāra abhyupagamāt avirodhaḥ
yama prayuktāḥ eva hi te citragupta ādayaḥ dhiṣṭhātāraḥ smaryante
vidyā karmaṇoḥ iti tu prakṛta tvāt
pañcāgni vidyāyām vettha yathā asau lokaḥ na saṃpūryate iti asya praśnasya prativacana avasare śrūyate atha etayoḥ pathoḥ na katareṇa cana tāni imāni kṣudrāṇi asakṛt āvartīni bhūtāni bhavanti
jāyasva mriyastvā iti etat tṛtīyam sthānam tena asau loke na saṃpūryate iti
tatra etayoḥ pathoḥ iti vidyā karmaṇoḥ iti etat
kasmāt
prakṛta tvāt
vidyā karmaṇī hi deva yāna pitṛyāṇayoḥ pathoḥ pratipade prakṛte tat ye ittham viduḥ iti vidyā tayā pratipattavyaḥ deva yānaḥ panthāḥ prakīrtitaḥ
iṣṭāpūrte dattam iti karma tena pratipattavyaḥ pitṛyāṇaḥ panthāḥ prakīrtitaḥ tad prakriyāyām atha etayoḥ pathoḥ na katareṇa cana iti śrutam
etat uktam bhavati ye na vidyā sādhanena deva yāne pathi adhikṛtāḥ na api karmaṇā pitṛyāṇe teṣām eṣa sakṛdāvartī tṛtīyaḥ panthāḥ bhavati iti
tasmāt api na aniṣṭa ādi kāribhiḥ candramāḥ prāpyate
syāt etat te candra bimbam āruhya tatas varuhya kṣudra jantu tvam pratipatsyante iti
tat api na asti āroha ānarthakyāt
api ca sarveṣu prayatsu candra lokam prāpnuvatsu asau lokaḥ prayadbhiḥ saṃpūryeta iti atas praśna viruddham prativacanam prasajyeta
tathā hi prativacanam dātavyam yathā asau lokaḥ na saṃpūryate
avaroha abhyupagamāt asaṃpūraṇa upapattiḥ iti ced na aśruta tvāt
satyam avarohāt api a saṃpūraṇam upapadyate
śrutiḥ tu tṛtīya sthāna saṃkīrtanena asaṃpūraṇam darśayati etat tṛtīyam sthānam tena asau lokaḥ na saṃpūryate iti
tena anārohāt eva asaṃpūraṇam iti yuktam
avarohasya iṣṭa ādi kāriṣu api aviśiṣṭa tve sati tṛtīya sthāna ukti ānarthakya prasaṅgāt
tu śabdaḥ tu śākhā antarīya vākya prabhavām aśeṣa gamana āśaṅkām ucchinatti
evam sati adhikṛta apekṣaḥ śākhāntarīye vākye sarva śabdaḥ vatiṣṭhate ye vai kecid adhikṛtāḥ asmāt lokāt prayanti candramasam eva te sarve gacchanti iti
yat punar uktam deha lābha upapattaye sarve candramasam gantum arhanti pañcamyām āhutau
iti āhuti saṃkhyā niyamāt iti tat pratyucyate
na tṛtīye tathā upalabdheḥ
na tṛtīye sthāne deha lābhāya pañca saṃkhyā niyamaḥ āhutīnām ādartavyaḥ
kutas
tathā upalabdheḥ
tathā hi antareṇa eva āhuti saṃkhyā niyamam varṇitena prakāreṇa tṛtīya sthāna prāptiḥ upalabhyate jāyasva mriyasva iti etat tṛtīyam sthānam iti
api ca pañcamyām āhutau āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavanti iti manuṣya śarīra hetu tvena āhuti saṃkhyā kīrtyate na kīṭa pataṅga ādi śarīra hetu tvena puruṣa śabdasya manuṣya jāti vacana tvāt
api ca pañcamyām āhutau apām puruṣavacaḥ tvam upadiśyate na a pañcamyām āhutau puruṣavacaḥ tvam pratiṣidhyate vākyasya dvi artha tā doṣāt
tatra yeṣām āroha avarohau saṃbhavataḥ teṣām pañcamyām āhutau dehaḥ udbhaviṣyati
anyeṣām tu vinā eva āhuti saṃkhyayā bhūta antara upasṛṣṭābhiḥ adbhiḥ dehaḥ ārapsyate
smaryate pi ca loke
api ca smaryate loke droṇa dhṛṣṭadyumna prabhṛtīnām sītā draupadī prabhṛtīnām ca a yoni ja tvam
tatra droṇa ādīnām yoṣit viṣayā ekā āhutiḥ na asti
dhṛṣṭadyumna ādīnām tu yoṣit puruṣa viṣaye dve api āhutī na staḥ
yathā ca tatra āhuti saṃkhyā niyama an ādaraḥ bhavati evam anyatra api bhaviṣyati
balākā api antareṇa eva retaḥ sekam garbham dhatte iti loka rūḍhiḥ
darśanāt ca
api ca caturvidhe bhūta grāme jarāyu ja aṇḍa ja sveda ja udbhid ja lakṣaṇe sveda ja udbhid jayoḥ antareṇa eva grāmya dharmam utpatti darśanāt āhuti saṃkhyāna ādaraḥ bhavati
evam anyatra api bhaviṣyati
nanu teṣām khalu eṣām bhūtānām trīṇi eva bījāni bhavanti āṇḍa jam jīva jam udbhijjam iti atra trividhaḥ eva bhūta grāmaḥ śrūyate
katham caturvidha tvam bhūta grāmasya pratijñātam iti atra ucyate
tṛtīya śabda avarodhaḥ saṃśoka jasya
āṇḍa jam jīva jam udbhijjam iti atra tṛtīyena udbhijja śabdena eva sveda ja upasaṃgrahaḥ kṛtaḥ pratyetavyaḥ ubhayoḥ api sveda ja udbhijjayoḥ bhūmi udaka udbheda prabhava tvasya tulya tvāt
sthāvara udbhedāt tu vilakṣaṇaḥ jaṅgama udbhedaḥ iti anyatra sveda ja udbhid jayoḥ bheda vādaḥ iti avirodhaḥ
sābhāvya āpattiḥ upapatteḥ
sābhāvya āpatti adhikaraṇam
iṣṭa ādi kāriṇaḥ candramasam āruhya tasmin yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā tatas sa anuśayāḥ avarohanti iti uktam
atha avaroha prakāraḥ parīkṣyate
tatra iyam avaroha śrutiḥ bhavati atha etam eva adhvānam punar nivartante yathetam ākāśam ākāśāt vāyum vāyuḥ bhūtvā dhūmaḥ bhavati dhūmaḥ bhūtvā abhram bhavati abhram bhūtvā meghaḥ bhavati meghaḥ bhūtvā pravarṣati iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ākāśa ādi svarūpam eva avarohantaḥ pratipadyante kim vā ākāśa ādi sāmyam iti
tatra prāptam tāvat ākāśa ādi sva rūpam eva pratipadyante iti
kutas
evam hi śrutiḥ bhavati
itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt
śruti lakṣaṇā viśaye ca śrutiḥ nyāyyā na lakṣaṇā
tathā ca vāyuḥ bhūtvā dhūmaḥ bhavati iti evamādīni akṣaraṇi tad tad svarūpa āpattau āñjasyena avakalpante
tasmāt ākāśa ādi svarūpa pratipattiḥ iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ ākāśa ādi sāmyam pratipadyante iti
candra maṇḍale yat am mayam śarīram upabhoga artham ārabdham tat upabhoga kṣaye sati pravilīyamānam sūkṣmam ākāśa samam bhavati
tatas vāyoḥ vaśam eti
tatas dhūma ādibhiḥ saṃpṛcyate iti
tat etat ucyate yathā itam ākāśam ākāśāt vāyum iti evamādinā
kutas etat
upapatteḥ
evam hi etat upapadyate
na hi anyasya anya bhāvaḥ mukhyaḥ upapadyate
ākāśa svarūpa pratipattau ca vāyu ādi krameṇa avarohaḥ na upapadyate
vibhu tvāt ca ākāśena nitya saṃbaddha tvāt na tad sādṛśya āpatteḥ anyaḥ tad saṃbandhaḥ ghaṭate
śruti asaṃbhave ca lakṣaṇa āśrayaṇam nyāyyam eva
atas ākāśa ādi tulya tā āpattiḥ eva atra ākāśa ādi bhāvaḥ iti upacaryate
na ati cireṇa viśeṣāt
na ati cira adhikaraṇam
tatra akāśa ādi pratipattau prāk vrīhi ādi bhāva āpatteḥ bhavati viśayaḥ kim dīrgham dīrgham kālam pūrva pūrva sādṛśyena avasthāya uttara uttara sādṛśyam gacchanti uta alpam alpam iti
tatra aniyamaḥ niyama kāriṇaḥ śāstrasya abhāvāt iti evam prāpte idam āha na aticireṇa iti
alpam alpam kālam ākāśa ādi bhāvena avasthāya varṣa dhārābhiḥ saha imām bhuvam āpatanti
kutas etat
viśeṣa darśanāt
tathā hi vrīhi ādi bhāva āpatteḥ anantaram viśinaṣṭi atas vai khalu durniṣprapataram iti
takāraḥ ekaḥ chāndasyām prakriyāyām luptaḥ mantavyaḥ
dus niṣprapatataram dus niṣkramataram duḥkhataram asmāt vrīhi ādi bhāvāt niḥsaraṇam bhavati iti arthaḥ
tat atra duḥkham niṣprapatanam pradarśayan pūrveṣu sukham niṣprapatanam darśayati
sukha duḥkha tā viśeṣaḥ ca ayam niṣprapatanasya kāla alpatva dīrgha tva nimittaḥ tasmin avadhau śarīra aniṣpatteḥ upabhoga asaṃbhavāt
tasmāt vrīhi ādi bhāva āpatteḥ prāk alpena eva kālena avarohaḥ syāt iti
anya dhiṣṭhiteṣu pūrvavat abhilāpāt
anya adhiṣṭhita adhikaraṇam
tasmin eva avarohe pravarṣaṇa anantaram paṭhyate te iha vrīhi yavāḥ oṣadhi vanaspatayaḥ tila māṣāḥ iti jāyante iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim asmin avadhau sthāvara jāti āpannāḥ sthāvara sukha duḥkha bhājaḥ nuśayinaḥ bhavanti āhosvit kṣetrajña antara dhiṣṭhiteṣu sthāvara śarīreṣu saṃśleṣa mātram gacchanti iti
kim tāvat prāptam
sthāvara jāti āpannāḥ tad sukha duḥkha bhājaḥ nuśayinaḥ bhavanti iti
kutas etat
janeḥ mukhya artha tva upapatteḥ sthāvara bhāvasya ca śruti smṛtyoḥ upabhoga sthāna tva prasiddheḥ paśu hiṃsā ādi yogāt ca iṣṭa ādeḥ karma jātasya aniṣṭa phala tva upapatteḥ
tasmāt mukhyam eva idam anuśayinām vrīhi ādi janma śva ādi janma vat yathā śva yonim vā sūkara yonim vā cāṇḍāla yonim vā iti mukhyam eva anuśayinām śva ādi janma tat sukha duḥkha anvitam bhavati evam vrīhi ādi janma api iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ anyaiḥ jīvaiḥ adhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhi ādiṣu saṃsarga mātram anuśayinaḥ pratipadyante na tad sukha duḥkha bhājaḥ bhavanti pūrvavat yathā vāyu dhūma ādi bhāvaḥ nuśayinām tad saṃśleṣa mātram evam vrīhi ādi bhāvaḥ jāti sthāvaraiḥ saṃśleṣa mātram
kutas etat
tadvat eva iha api abhilāpāt
kaḥ abhilāpasya tadvat bhāvaḥ
karma vyāpāram antareṇa saṃkīrtanam yathā ākāśa ādiṣu pravarṣaṇa anteṣu na kiṃcid karma vyāpāram parāmṛśati evam vrīhi ādi janmani api
tasmāt na asti atra sukha duḥkha bhāktvam anuśayinām
yatra tu sukha duḥkha bhāktvam abhipraiti parāmṛśati tatra karma vyāpāram ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ
kapūya caraṇāḥ iti
api ca mukhye nuśayinām vrīhi ādi janmani vrīhi ādiṣu lūyamāneṣu kaṇḍyamāneṣu pacyamāneṣu bhakṣyamāṇeṣu ca tad abhimāninaḥ nuśayinaḥ pravaseyuḥ
yaḥ hi jīvaḥ yat śarīram abhimanyate sa tasmin pīḍyamāne pravasati iti prasiddham
tatra vrīhi ādi bhāvāt retaḥ sic bhāvaḥ nuśayinām na abhilapyeta
atas saṃsarga mātram anuśayinām anya dhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhi ādiṣu bhavati
etena janeḥ mukhya artha tvam pratibrūyāt upabhoga sthāna tvam ca sthāvara bhāvasya
na ca vayam upabhoga sthāna tvam sthāvara bhāvasya avajānīmahe
bhavatu anyeṣām jantūnām apuṇya sāmarthyena sthāvara bhāvam upagatānām etat upabhoga sthānam
candramasaḥ tu avarohantaḥ nuśayinaḥ na sthāvara bhāvam upabhuñjate iti ācakṣmahe
aśuddham iti ced na śabdāt
yat punar uktam paśu hiṃsā ādi yogāt aśuddham ādhvarikam karma tasya aniṣṭam api phalam avakalpate iti atas mukhyam eva anuśayinām vrīhi ādi janma astu
tatra gauṇī kalpanā anarthikā iti tat parihriyate na śāstra hetu tvāt dharma adharma vijñānasya
ayam dharmaḥ ayam adharmaḥ iti śāstram eva vijñāne kāraṇam atīndriya tvāt tayoḥ
aniyata deśa kāla nimitta tvāt ca yasmin deśe kāle nimitte ca yaḥ dharmaḥ nuṣṭhīyate saḥ eva deśa kāla nimitta antareṣu adharmaḥ bhavati
tena na śāstrāt ṛte dharma adharma viṣayam vijñānam kasyacid asti
śāstrāt ca hiṃsā anugraha ādi ātmakaḥ jyotiṣṭomaḥ dharmaḥ iti avadhāritaḥ sa katham aśuddhaḥ iti śakyate vaktum
nanu na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni iti śāstram eva bhūta viṣayām hiṃsām adharmaḥ iti avagamayati
bāḍham utsargaḥ tu saḥ
apavādaḥ yam ca agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabheta iti
utsarga apavādayoḥ ca vyavasthita viṣaya tvam
tasmāt viśuddham karma vaidikam śiṣṭaiḥ anuṣṭhīyamāna tvāt a nindyamāna tvāt ca
tena na tasya pratirūpam phalam jāti sthāvara tvam
na ca śva ādi janma vat api vrīhi ādi janma bhavitum arhati
tat hi kapūya caraṇa an adhikṛtyaḥ ucyate
na evam iha vaiśeṣikaḥ kaścid adhikāraḥ sti
atas khalitānām anuśayinām vrīhi ādi saṃśleṣa mātram tad bhāvaḥ iti upacaryate
retaḥ sic yogaḥ tha
itas ca vrīhi ādi saṃśleṣa mātram tad bhāvaḥ yat kāraṇam vrīhi ādi bhāvasya anantaram anuśayinām retaḥ sic bhāvaḥ āmnāyate yaḥ yaḥ hi annam atti yaḥ retaḥ siñcati tat bhūyaḥ eva bhavati iti
na ca atra mukhyaḥ retaḥ sigbhāvaḥ saṃbhavati
cira jātaḥ hi prāpta yauvanaḥ retaḥsic bhavati
katham iva an upacaritam tad bhāvam adyamāna anna anugataḥ nuśayī pratipadyate
tatra tāvat avaśyam retaḥ sic yogaḥ eva retaḥ sic bhāvaḥ bhyupagantavyaḥ
tadvat vrīhi ādi bhāvaḥ vrīhi ādi yogaḥ eva iti avirodhaḥ
yoneḥ śarīram
atha retaḥ sigbhāvasya anantaram yonau niṣikte retasi yoneḥ adhi śarīram anuśayinām anuśaya phala upabhogāya jāyate iti āha śāstram tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ ityādi
tasmāt api avagamyate na avarohe brāhya ādi bhāva avasare tat śarīram eva sukha duḥkha anvitam bhavati iti
tasmāt vrīhi ādi saṃśleṣa mātram anuśayinām tat janma iti siddham
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ

tṛtīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ
sandhye sṛṣṭiḥ āha hi
saṃdhyā adhikaraṇam
saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ iti
saṃdhyam iti svapna sthānam ācaṣṭe vede prayoga darśanāt saṃdhyam iti
dvayoḥ loka sthānayoḥ prabodha saṃprasāda sthānayoḥ vā saṃdhau bhavati iti saṃdhyam
tasmin saṃdhye sthāne tathya rūpā eva sṛṣṭiḥ bhavitum arhati
kutas
yatas pramāṇa bhūtā śrutiḥ evam āha atha rathān natha yogān pathaḥ sṛjate ityādi
sa hi kartā iti ca upasaṃhārāt evam eva avagamyate
nirmātāram ca eke putra ādayaḥ ca
api ca eke śākhinaḥ asmin eva saṃdhye sthāne kāmānām nirmātāram ātmānam āmananti yaḥ eṣa supteṣu jāgarti kāmam kāmam puruṣaḥ nirmimāṇaḥ iti
putra ādayaḥ ca tatra kāmāḥ abhipreyante kāmyante iti
nanu kāma śabdena icchā viśeṣaḥ eva ucyeran
na śata āyuṣaḥ putra pautrān vṛṇīṣva iti prakṛtya ante kāmānām tvā kāma bhājam karomi iti prakṛteṣu tatra tatra putra ādiṣu kāma śabdasya prayukta tvāt
prājñam ca enam nirmātāram prakaraṇa vākyaśeṣābhyām pratīmaḥ prājñasya hi idam prakaraṇam anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt ityādi
tad viṣayaḥ eva ca tat eva śukram tat brahma tat eva amṛtam ucyate
tasimant lokāḥ śritāḥ sarve tat u na atyeti kaścana iti
prājña kartṛkā ca sṛṣṭiḥ tathya rūpā samadhigatā jāgarita āśrayā tathā svapna āśrayā api sṛṣṭiḥ bhavitum arhati
tathā ca śrutiḥ atha u khalu āhuḥ jāgarita deśe eva asya eṣa iti yāni eva jāgrat paśyati tāni suptaḥ iti svapna jāgaritayoḥ samāna nyāya tām śrāvayati
tasmāt tathya rūpā eva saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ iti
evam prāpte pratyāha
māyā mātram tu kārtsnyena anabhivyakta svarūpa tvāt
tu śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati
na etat asti yat uktam saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ pāramārthikī iti
māyā eva sṛṣṭiḥ na paramārtha gandhaḥ u pi asti
kutas
kārtsnyena anabhivyakta svarūpa tvāt na hi kārtsnyena paramārtha vastu dharmeṇa abhivyakta svarūpaḥ svapnaḥ
kim punar atra kārtsnyam abhipretam
deśa kāla nimitta saṃpattiḥ abādhaḥ ca
na hi paramārtha vastu viṣayāṇi deśa kāla nimittāni abādhaḥ ca svapne saṃbhāvyante na tāvat svapne ratha ādīnām ucitaḥ deśaḥ saṃbhavati
na hi saṃvṛte deha deśe ratha ādayaḥ vakāśam labheran
syāt etat bahis dehāt svapnam drakṣyati deśa antarita dravya grahaṇāt
darśayati ca śrutiḥ bahis dehāt svapnam bahis kulāyāt amṛtaḥ caritvā
saḥ īyate mṛtaḥ yatra kāmam iti
sthiti gati pratyaya bhedaḥ ca na a niṣkrānte jantau sāmañjasyam aśnuvīta iti
na iti ucyate na hi suptasya jantoḥ kṣaṇa mātreṇa yojana śata antaritam deśam paryetum viparyetum ca tatas sāmarthyam saṃbhāvyate
kvacid ca pratyāgamana varjitam svapnam śrāvayati kuruṣu aham adya śayānaḥ nidrayā abhiplutaḥ svapne pañcālān abhigataḥ ca asmin pratibuddhaḥ ca iti
dehāt ced apeyāt pañcāleṣu eva pratibudhyeta
tān asau abhigataḥ iti
kuruṣu eva tu pratibudhyate
yena ca ayam dehena deśa antaram aśnuvānaḥ manyate tam anye pārśva sthāḥ śayana deśe eva paśyanti
yathābhūtāni ca ayam deśa antarāṇi svapne paśyati na tāni tathābhūtāni eva bhavanti
paridhāvan ced paśyet jāgrat vat vastu bhūtam artham ākalayet
darśayati ca śrutiḥ antar eva dehe svapnam sa yatra etat svapnyayā carati iti upakramya sve śarīre yathākāmam parivartate iti
atas ca śruti upapatti virodhāt bahis kulāya śrutiḥ gauṇī vyākhyātavyā bahis iva kulāyāt amṛtaḥ caritvā iti yaḥ hi vasan api śarīre na tena prayojanam karoti sa bahis iva śarīrāt bhavati iti
sthiti gati pratyaya bhedaḥ pi evam sati vipralambhaḥ eva abhyupagantavyaḥ
kāla visaṃvādaḥ ca svapne bhavati rajanyām suptaḥ vāsaram bhārate varṣe manyate
tathā muhūrta mātra vartini svapne kadācid bahūn varṣa pūgān ativāhayati
nimittāni api ca svapne na buddhaye karmaṇe vā ucitāni vidyante
karaṇa upasaṃhārāt hi na asya aśva ratha ādi grahaṇāya cakṣuḥ ādīni santi
ratha ādi nirvartane nimeṣa mātreṇa sāmarthyam dārūṇi vā
bādhyante ca ete ratha aśva ādayaḥ svapna dṛṣṭāḥ prabodhe
svapne eva ca ete sulabha bādhāḥ bhavanti ādi antayoḥ vyabhicāra darśanāt rathaḥ yam iti hi kadācid svapne nirdhāritaḥ kṣaṇena manuṣyaḥ saṃpadyate manuṣyaḥ yam iti nirdhāritaḥ kṣaṇena vṛkṣaḥ
spaṣṭam ca abhāvam ratha ādīnām svapne śrāvayati śāstram na tatra rathāḥ na ratha yogāḥ na panthānaḥ bhavanti ityādi
tasmāt māyā mātram svapna darśanam
sūcakaḥ ca hi śruteḥ ācakṣate ca tad vidaḥ
māyā mātra tvāt tarhi na kaścid svapne paramārtha gandhaḥ u sti iti na iti ucyate sūcakaḥ ca hi svapnaḥ bhavati bhaviṣyatoḥ sādhu asādhunoḥ
tathā hi śrūyate yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu striyam svapneṣu paśyati
samṛddhim tatra jānīyāt tasmin svapna nidarśane iti
tathā puruṣam kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇa dantam paśyati saḥ enam hanti iti evamādibhiḥ svapnaiḥ acirajīvi tvam āvedyate iti śrāvayati
ācakṣate ca svapnādhyāya vidaḥ kuñjara ārohaṇa ādīni svapne dhanyāni khara yāna ādīni adhanyāni iti
mantra devatā dravya viśeṣa nimittāḥ ca kecid svapnāḥ satya artha gandhinaḥ bhavanti iti manyante
tatra api bhavatu nāma sūcyamānasya vastunaḥ satya tvam
sūcakasya tu strī darśana ādeḥ bhavati eva vaitathyam bādhyamāna tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ
tasmāt upapannam svapnasya māyā mātra tvam
yat uktam āha hi iti tat evam sati bhāktam vyākhyātavyam yathā lāṅgalam gavādīn udvahati iti nimitta mātra tvāt evam ucyate na tu pratyakṣam eva lāṅgalam gavādīn udvahati
evam nimitta mātra tvāt suptaḥ ratha ādīn sṛjate sa hi kartā iti ca ucyate
na tu pratyakṣam eva suptaḥ ratha ādīn sṛjati
nimitta tvam tu asya ratha ādi pratibhāna nimitta moda trāsa ādi darśanāt tad nimitta bhūtayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ kartṛ tvena iti vaktavyam
api ca jāgarite viṣaya indriya saṃyogāt āditya ādi jyotiḥ vyatikarāt ca ātmanaḥ svayam jyotiḥ tvam durvivecanam iti tad vivecanāya svapnaḥ upanyastaḥ
tatra yadi ratha ādi sṛṣṭi vacanam śrutyā nīyeta tatas svayaṃjyotiṣṭvam na nirṇītam syāt
tasmāt ratha ādi abhāva vacanam śrutyā ratha ādi sṛṣṭi vacanam tu bhaktyā iti vyākhyeyam
etena nirmāṇa śravaṇam vyākhyātam
yat api uktam prājñam enam nirmātāram āmananti iti tat api asat śruti antare svayam vihatya svayam nirmāya svena bhāsā svena jyotiṣā prasvapiti iti jīva vyāpāra śravaṇāt
iha api yaḥ eṣa supteṣu jāgarti iti prasiddha anuvādāt jīvaḥ eva ayam kāmānām nirmātā saṃkīrtyate
tasya tu vākyaśeṣeṇa tat eva śukram tat brahma iti jīva bhāvam vyāvartya brahma bhāvaḥ upadiśyate tat tvam asi ityādi vat iti na brahma prakaraṇam virudhyate
na ca asmābhiḥ svapne prājña vyāpāraḥ pratiṣidhyate tasya sarva īśvara tvāt sarvāsu api avasthāsu adhiṣṭhātṛ tva upapatteḥ
pāramārthikaḥ tu na ayam saṃdhyā āśrayaḥ sargaḥ viyat ādi sarga vat iti etāvat pratipādyate
na ca viyat ādi sargasya api ātyantikam satya tvam asti
pratipāditam hi tad ananyatvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti atra samastasya prapañcasya māyā mātra tvam
prāk tu brahma ātmatva darśanāt viyat ādi prapañcaḥ vyavasthita rūpaḥ bhavati
saṃdhyā āśrayaḥ tu prapañcaḥ pratidinam bādhyate iti atas vaiśeṣikam idam saṃdhyasya māyā mātra tvam uditam
para abhidhyānāt tu tirohitam tatas hi asya bandha viparyayau
atha api syāt parasya eva tāvat ātmanaḥ ūm śaḥ jīvaḥ agneḥ iva visphuliṅgaḥ
tatra evam sati yathā agni visphuliṅgayoḥ samāne dahana prakāśana śaktī bhavataḥ evam jīva īśvarayoḥ api jñāna aiśvarya śaktī
tatas ca jīvasya jñāna aiśvarya vaśāt sāṃkalpikī svapne ratha ādi sṛṣṭiḥ bhaviṣyati iti
atrā ucyate sati api jīva īśvarayoḥ aṃśa aṃśi bhāve pratyakṣam eva jīvasya īśvara viparīta dharma tvam
kim punar jīvasya īśvara samāna dharma tvam na asti eva
na na asti eva
vidyamānam api tat tirohitam avidyā ādi vyavadhānāt
tat punar tirohitam sat parameśvaram abhidhyāyataḥ yatamānasya jantoḥ vidhūta dhvāntasya timira tiraskṛtā iva dṛkśaktiḥ auṣadha vīryāt īśvara prasādāt saṃsiddhasya kasyacid eva āvirbhavati na svabhāvataḥ eva sarveṣām jantūnām
kutas
tatas hi īśvarāt hetoḥ asya jīvasya bandha mokṣau bhavataḥ īśvara svarūpa aparijñānāt bandhaḥ tad svarūpa parijñānāt tu mokṣaḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ jñātvā devam sarva pāśa apahāniḥ kṣīṇaiḥ kleśaiḥ janma mṛtyu prahāṇiḥ
tasya abhidhyānāt tṛtīyam dehabhede viśva aiśvaryam kevalaḥ āpta kāmaḥ iti evamādyā
deha yogāt vā saḥ pi
kasmāt punar jīvaḥ paramātma aṃśaḥ eva san tiraskṛta jñāna aiśvaryaḥ bhavati
yuktam tu jñāna aiśvaryayoḥ a tiraskṛta tvam visphuliṅgasya iva dahana prakāśanayoḥ iti
ucyate satyam eva etat
saḥ pi tu jīvasya jñāna aiśvarya tirobhāvaḥ deha yogāt deha indriya manaḥ buddhi viṣaya vedanā ādi yogāt bhavati
asti ca atra upamā yathā agneḥ dahana prakāśana saṃpannasya api araṇi gatasya dahana prakāśane tirohite bhavataḥ yathā vā bhasma channasya evam avidyā pratyupasthāpita nāma rūpa kṛta deha ādi upādhi yogāt tad aviveka bhrama kṛtaḥ jīvasya jñāna aiśvarya tirobhāvaḥ
vā śabdaḥ jīvasya īśvarāt anyatva śaṅkā vyāvṛtti arthaḥ
nanu anyaḥ eva jīvaḥ īśvarāt astu tiraskṛta jñāna aiśvarya tvāt
kim deha yoga kalpanayā
na iti ucyate na hi anya tvam jīvasya īśvarāt upapadyate sā iyam devatā aikṣata iti upakramya anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya iti ātma śabdena jīvasya parāmarśāt
tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti ca jīvāya upadiśati īśvara ātma tvam
atas ananyaḥ eva īśvarāt jīvaḥ san deha yogāt tirohita jñāna aiśvaryaḥ bhavati
atas ca na sāṃkalpikī jīvasya svapne ratha ādi sṛṣṭiḥ ghaṭate
yadi ca sāṃkalpikī svapne ratha ādi sṛṣṭiḥ syāt na eva aniṣṭam kaścid svapnam paśyet na hi kaścid aniṣṭam saṃkalpayate
yat punar uktam jāgarita deśa śrutiḥ svapnasya satya tvam khyāpayati iti na tat sāmya vacanam satya tva abhiprāyam svayaṃjyotiṣṭva virodhāt śrutyā eva ca svapne ratha ādi abhāvasya darśita tvāt
jāgarita prabhava vāsanā nirmita tvāt tu svapnasya tad tulya nirbhāsa tva abhiprāyam tat
tasmāt upapannam svapnasya māyā mātra tvam
tad abhāvaḥ nāḍīṣu tad śruteḥ ātmani ca
tad abhāva adhikaraṇam
svapna avasthā parīkṣitā
suṣupta avasthā idānīm parīkṣyate
tatra etāḥ suṣupta viṣayāḥ śrutayaḥ bhavanti
kvacid śrūyate tat yatra etat suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasannaḥ svapnam na vijānāti āsu tadā nāḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati iti
anyatra tu nāḍīḥ eva anukramya śrūyate tābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete iti
tathā anyatra nāḍīḥ eva anukramya tāsu tadā bhavati yadā suptaḥ svapnam na kaṃcana paśyati atha asmin prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati iti
tathā anyatra yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete iti
tathā anyatra satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati svam api itas bhavati iti
tathā prājñena ātmanā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ na bāhyam kiṃcana veda na antaram iti ca
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim etāni nāḍī ādīni paraspara nirapekṣa tayā bhinnāni suṣupti sthānāni āhosvit paraspara apekṣa tayā ekam suṣupti sthānam iti
kim tāvat prāptam
bhinnāni iti
kutas
eka artha tvāt na hi eka arthānām kvacid paraspara apekṣa tvam dṛśyate vrīhi yava ādīnām
nāḍī ādīnām ca eka artha tā suṣuptau dṛśyate nāḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati purītati śete iti ca tatra tatra saptamī nirdeśasya tulya tvāt
nanu na evam sati saptamī nirdeśaḥ dṛśyate satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ tatra api saptamī arthasya gamyamāna tvāt vākya śeṣaḥ hi tatra āyatana eṣī jīvaḥ sat upasarpati iti āha anyatra āyatanam a labdhvā prāṇam eva upaśrayate iti
prāṇa śabdena tatra prakṛtasya sataḥ upādānāt
āyatanam ca saptamī arthaḥ saptamī nirdeśaḥ tatra vākyaśeṣe dṛśyate sati saṃpadya na viduḥ sati saṃpadyāmahe iti
sarvatra ca viśeṣa vijñāna uparama lakṣaṇam suṣuptam na viśiṣyate
tasmāt eka artha tvāt nāḍī ādīnām vikalpena kadācid kiṃcid sthānam svāpāya upasarpati iti
evam prāpte pratipādyate tad abhāvaḥ nāḍīṣu ātmani ca iti
tad abhāvaḥ iti tasya prakṛtasya svapna darśanasya abhāvaḥ suṣuptam iti arthaḥ
nāḍīṣu ātmani ca iti samuccayena etāni nāḍī ādīni svāpāya upasarpati na vikalpena iti arthaḥ
kutas
tad śruteḥ
tathā hi sarveṣām eva nāḍī ādīnām tatra tatra suṣupti sthāna tvam śrūyate
tat ca samuccaye saṃgṛhītam bhavati
vikalpe hi eṣām pakṣe bādhaḥ syāt
nanu eka artha tvāt vikalpaḥ nāḍī ādīnām vrīhi yava ādi vat iti uktam
na iti ucyate na hi eka vibhakti nirdeśa mātreṇa eka artha tvam vikalpaḥ ca āpatati nānā artha tva samuccayayoḥ api eka vibhakti nirdeśa darśanāt prāsāde śete paryaṅke śete iti evamādiṣu tathā iha api nāḍīṣu purītati brahmaṇi ca svapiti iti upapadyate samuccayaḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ tāsu tadā bhavati yadā suptaḥ svapnam na kaṃcana paśyati atha asmin prāṇaḥ eva ekadhā bhavati iti samuccayam nāḍīnām prāṇasya ca suṣuptau śrāvayati eka vākya upādānāt
prāṇasya ca brahmatvam samadhigatam prāṇaḥ tathā anugamāt iti atra
yatra api nirapekṣāḥ iva nāḍīḥ suṣupti sthāna tvena śrāvayati āsu tadā nāḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati iti tatra api pradeśa antara prasiddhasya brahmaṇaḥ pratiṣedhāt nāḍī dvāreṇa brahmaṇi eva avatiṣṭhate iti pratīyate
na ca evam api nāḍīṣu saptamī virudhyate nāḍībhiḥ api brahmā upasarpan sṛptaḥ eva nāḍīṣu bhavati yaḥ hi gaṅgayā sāgaram gacchati gataḥ eva sa gaṅgāyām bhavati
bhavati ca atra raśmi nāḍī dvāra ātmakasya brahmaloka mārgasya vivakṣita tvāt nāḍī stuti artham sṛpti saṃkīrtanam nāḍīṣu sṛptaḥ bhavati iti uktvā tam na kaścana pāpmā spṛśati iti bruvan nāḍīḥ praśaṃsati
bravīti ca pāpma sparśa abhāve hetum tejasā hi tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati iti tejasā nāḍī gatena pitta ākhyena abhivyāpta karaṇaḥ na bāhyān viṣayān īkṣate iti arthaḥ
athavā tejasā iti brahmaṇaḥ eva ayam nirdeśaḥ śruti antare brahma eva tejaḥ eva iti tejaḥ śabdasya brahmaṇi prayukta tvāt
brahmaṇā hi tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati nāḍī dvāreṇa atas tam na kaścana pāpmā spṛśati iti arthaḥ brahma saṃpattiḥ ca pāpma sparśa abhāve hetuḥ samadhigataḥ sarve pāpmānaḥ tasmāt nivartante pahata pāpmā hi eṣa brahma lokaḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
evam ca sati pradeśa antara prasiddhena brahmaṇā suṣupti sthānena anugataḥ nāḍīnām samuccayaḥ samadhigataḥ bhavati
tathā brahma prakriyāyām saṃkīrtanāt tad anuguṇam eva suṣupti sthāna tvam jñāyate yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete iti hṛdaya ākāśe suṣupti sthāne prakṛte idam ucyate purītati śete iti
purītat iti hṛdaya pariveṣṭanam ucyate
tad antarvartini api hṛdaya ākāśe śayānaḥ śakyate purītati śete iti vaktum prākāra parikṣipte hi pure vartamānaḥ prākāre vartate iti ucyate
hṛdaya ākāśasya ca brahmatvam samadhigatam dahara uttarebhyaḥ iti atra
tathā nāḍī purītat samuccayaḥ tābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete iti eka vākya upādānāt avagamyate
sat prājñayoḥ ca prasiddham eva brahmatvam
evam etāsu śrutiṣu trīṇi eva suṣupti sthānāni saṃkīrtitāni nāḍyaḥ purītat brahma ca iti
tatra api dvāra mātram nāḍyaḥ purītat ca brahmā eva tu ekam anapāyi suṣupti sthānam
api ca nāḍyaḥ purītat vā jīvasya upādhi ādhāraḥ eva bhavati tatra asya karaṇāni vartante iti
na hi upādhi saṃbandham antareṇa svatas eva jīvasya ādhāraḥ kaścid saṃbhavati brahma avyatirekeṇa sva mahima pratiṣṭhita tvāt
brahma ādhāra tvam api asya suṣupte na eva ādhāra ādheya bheda abhiprāyeṇa ucyate katham tarhi
tādātmya abhiprāyeṇa
yatas āha satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati svam api itas bhavati iti sva śabdena ātmā abhilapyate sva rūpam āpannaḥ suptaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ
api ca na kadācid jīvasya brahmaṇā saṃpattiḥ na asti svarūpasya anapāyi tvāt
svapna jāgaritayoḥ tu upādhi saṃparka vaśāt para rūpa āpattim iva apekṣya tad upaśamāt suṣupteḥ sva rūpa āpattiḥ vivakṣyate svam api itas bhavati iti
atas ca supta avasthāyām kadācid satā saṃpadyate kadācid na saṃpadyate iti ayuktam
api ca sthāna vikalpa abhyupagame viśeṣa vijñāna upaśama lakṣaṇam tāvat suṣuptam na kvacid viśiṣyate
tatra sati saṃpannaḥ tāvat eka tvāt na vijānāti iti yuktam tat kena kam vijānīyāt iti śruteḥ
nāḍīṣu purītati ca śayānasya na kiṃcid avijñāne kāraṇam śakyam vijñātum bheda viṣaya tvāt yatra vai anyat iva syāt tatra anyaḥ nyat paśyet iti śruteḥ
nanu bheda viṣayasya api ati dūra ādi kāraṇam avijñāne syāt
bāḍham evam syāt yadi jīvaḥ svataḥ paricchinnaḥ abhyupagamyeta yathā viṣṇumitraḥ pravāsī sva gṛhān na paśyati iti
na tu jīvasya upādhi vyatirekeṇa paricchedaḥ vidyate
upādhi gatam eva ati dūra ādi kāraṇam avijñāne iti yadi ucyeta tathā api upādheḥ upaśānta tvāt sati eva saṃpannaḥ na vijānāti iti yuktam
na ca vayam iha tulya vat nāḍī ādi samuccayam pratipādayāmaḥ
na hi nāḍyaḥ supti sthānam purītat ca iti anena vijñānena kiṃcid prayojanam asti
na hi etat vijñāna pratibaddham kiṃcid phalam śrūyate
na api etat vijñānam phalavataḥ kasyacid aṅgam upadiśyate
brahma tu anapāyi supti sthānam iti etat pratipādayāmaḥ
tena tu vijñānena prayojanam asti jīvasya brahma ātma tva avadhāraṇam svapna jāgarita vyavahāra vimukta tva avadhāraṇam ca
tasmāt ātmā eva supti sthānam
atas prabodhaḥ u smāt
yasmāt ca ātmā eva supti sthānam atas eva ca kāraṇāt nitya vat eva asmāt ātmanaḥ prabodhaḥ svāpa adhikāre śiṣyate kutas etat āgāt iti asya praśnasya prativacana avasare yathā agneḥ kṣudrāḥ visphuliṅgāḥ vyuccaranti evam eva asmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ ityādinā sataḥ āgamya na viduḥ sataḥ āgacchāmahe
iti ca
vikalpyamāneṣu tu suṣupti sthāneṣu kadācid nāḍībhyaḥ pratibudhyate kadācid purītataḥ kadācid ātmanaḥ iti aśāsiṣyat
tasmāt api ātmā eva supti sthānam iti
saḥ eva tu karma anusmṛti śabda vidhibhyaḥ
karma anusmṛti śabda vidhi adhikaraṇam
tasyāḥ punar sat saṃpatteḥ pratibudhyamānaḥ kim yaḥ eva sat saṃpannaḥ saḥ eva pratibudhyate uta sa vai anyaḥ vā iti cintyate
tatra prāptam tāvat aniyamaḥ iti
kutas
yadā hi jala rāśau kaścid jala binduḥ prakṣipyate jala rāśiḥ eva sa tadā bhavati punar uddharaṇe ca saḥ eva jala binduḥ bhavati iti duḥsaṃpādam tadvat suptaḥ pareṇa ekatvam āpannaḥ saṃprasīdati iti na saḥ eva punar utthātum arhati
tasmāt saḥ eva īśvaraḥ vā anyaḥ vā jīvaḥ pratibudhyate iti
evam prāpte idam āha saḥ eva tu jīvaḥ suptaḥ svāsthyam gataḥ punar uttiṣṭhati na anyaḥ
kasmāt
karma anusmṛti śabda vidhibhyaḥ
vibhajya hetum darśayiṣyāmi karma śeṣa anuṣṭhāna darśanāt tāvat saḥ eva utthātum arhati na anyaḥ
tathā hi pūrvedyus anuṣṭhitasya karmaṇaḥ aparedyus śeṣam anutiṣṭhan dṛśyate
na ca anyena sāmi kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ anyaḥ śeṣa kriyāyām pravartitum utsahate atiprasaṅgāt
tasmāt ekaḥ eva pūrvedyus aparedyus ca ekasya karmaṇaḥ kartā iti gamyate
itas ca saḥ eva uttiṣṭhati yatkāraṇam atīte hani aham adaḥ drākṣam iti pūrva anubhūtasya paścāt smaraṇam anyasya utthāne na upapadyate
na hi anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ nusmartum arhati
saḥ ham asmi iti ca ātma anusmaraṇam ātma antara utthāne na avakalpate
śabdebhyaḥ ca tasya eva utthānam avagamyate
tathā hi punar pratinyāyam pratiyoni ādravati buddha antāya eva imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ aharahar gacchantyaḥ etam brahma lokam na vindanti te iha vyāghraḥ vā siṃhaḥ vā vṛkaḥ vā varāhaḥ vā kīṭaḥ vā pataṅgaḥ vā daṃśaḥ vā maśakaḥ vā yat yat bhavanti tadā bhavanti iti evamādayaḥ śabdāḥ svāpa prabodha adhikāra paṭhitāḥ na ātma antara utthāne sāmañjasyam īyuḥ
karma vidyā vidhibhyaḥ ca evam eva avagamyate
anyathā hi karma vidyā vidhayaḥ narthakāḥ syuḥ
anya utthāna pakṣe hi supta mātraḥ mucyate iti āpadyeta
evam ced syāt vada kim kāla antara phalena karmaṇā vidyayā vā kṛtam syāt
api ca anya utthāna pakṣe yadi tāvat śarīra antare vyavaharamāṇaḥ jīvaḥ uttiṣṭhet tatratya vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ syāt
atha tatra suptaḥ uttiṣṭhet kalpanā ānarthakyam syāt yaḥ hi yasmin śarīre suptaḥ saḥ tasmin na uttiṣṭhati anyasmin śarīre suptaḥ anyasmin uttiṣṭhati iti kaḥ syām kalpanāyām lābhaḥ syāt
atha muktaḥ uttiṣṭhet antavān mokṣaḥ āpadyeta
nivṛtta avidyasya ca punarutthānam anupapannam
etena īśvarasya utthānam pratyuktam nitya nivṛtta avidya tvāt
akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśau ca durnivārau anya utthāna pakṣe syātām
tasmāt saḥ eva uttiṣṭhati na anyaḥ iti
yat punar uktam yathā jala rāśau prakṣiptaḥ jala binduḥ na uddhartum śakyate evam sati saṃpannaḥ jīvaḥ na utpatitum arhati iti tat parihriyate yuktam tatra viveka kāraṇa abhāvāt jala bindoḥ anuddharaṇam iha tu vidyate viveka kāraṇam karma ca avidyā ca iti vaiṣamyam
dṛśyate ca durvivecayoḥ api asmad jātīyaiḥ kṣīra udakayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ haṃsena vivecanam
api ca na jīvaḥ nāma kaścid parasmāt anyaḥ vidyate yaḥ jala binduḥ iva jalarāśeḥ sataḥ vivicyeta
sat eva tu upādhi saṃparkāt jīvaḥ iti upacaryate iti asakṛt prapañcitam
evam sati yāvat eka upādhi gatā bandha anuvṛttiḥ tāvat eka jīva vyavahāraḥ
upādhi antara gatāyām tu bandha anuvṛttau jīva antara vyavahāraḥ
saḥ eva ayam upādhiḥ svāpa prabodhayoḥ bīja aṅkura nyāyena iti atas saḥ eva jīvaḥ pratibudhyate iti yuktam
mugdheḥ ṛdh sampattiḥ pariśeṣāt
mugdhādhikaraṇam
asti mugdhaḥ nāma yam mūrchitaḥ iti laukikāḥ kathayanti
sa tu kimavasthaḥ iti parīkṣāyām ucyate tisraḥ tāvat avasthāḥ śarīra sthasya jīvasya prasiddhāḥ jāgaritam svapnaḥ suṣuptam iti
caturthī śarīrāt apasṛptiḥ
na tu pañcamī kācid avasthā jīvasya śrutau smṛtau vā prasiddhā asti
tasmāt catasṛṇām eva avasthānām anyatamā avasthā mūrchā iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ na tāvat mugdhaḥ jāgarita avasthaḥ bhavitum arhati
na hi ayam indriyaiḥ viṣayān īkṣate
syāt etat iṣukāra nyāyena mugdhaḥ bhaviṣyati yathā iṣukāraḥ jāgrat api iṣu āsakta manaḥ tayā na anyān viṣayān īkṣate evam mugdhaḥ musala saṃpāta ādi janita duḥkha anubhava vyagra manaḥ tayā jāgrat api na anyāḥ nu iṣayān īkṣate iti
na a cetayamāna tvāt
iṣukāraḥ hi vyāpṛta manāḥ bravīti iṣum eva aham etāvantam kālam upalabhamānaḥ bhūvam iti mugdhaḥ tu labdha saṃjñaḥ bravīti andhe tamasi aham etāvantam kālam prakṣiptaḥ bhūvam na kiṃcid mayā cetitam iti
jāgrataḥ ca eka viṣaya viṣakta cetasaḥ pi dehaḥ vidhriyate
mugdhasya tu dehaḥ dharaṇyām patati
tasmāt na jāgarti
na api svapnān paśyati niḥsaṃjñaka tvāt
na api mṛtaḥ prāṇa ūṣmaṇoḥ bhāvāt mugdhe hi jantau mṛtaḥ yam syāt na vā mṛtaḥ iti saṃśayānāḥ ūṣmā asti nā asti iti hṛdaya deśam ālabhante niścaya artham prāṇaḥ u sti nā asti iti ca nāsikā deśam
yadi prāṇa ūṣmaṇoḥ astitvam na avagacchanti tatas mṛtaḥ yam iti adhyavasāya dahanāya araṇyam nayanti
atha tu prāṇam ūṣmāṇam vā pratipadyante tatas na ayam mṛtaḥ iti adhyavasāya saṃjñā lābhāya bhiṣajyanti
punar utthānāt ca na diṣṭam gataḥ
na hi yamam gataḥ yama rāṣṭrāt pratyāgacchati
astu tarhi suṣuptaḥ niḥsaṃjña tvāt amṛta tvāt ca
na vailakṣaṇyāt mugdhaḥ kadācid ciram api na ucchvasiti sa vepathuḥ asya dehaḥ bhavati bhayānakam ca vadanam visphārite netre
suṣuptaḥ tu prasanna vadanaḥ tulya kālam punar punar ucchvasiti nimīlite asya netre bhavataḥ na ca asya dehaḥ vepate
pāṇi peṣaṇa mātreṇa ca suṣuptam utthāpayanti na tu mugdham mudgara ghātena api
nimitta bhedaḥ ca bhavati moha svāpayoḥ musala saṃpāta ādi nimitta tvāt mohasya śrama nimitta tvāt ca svāpasya
na ca loke sti prasiddhiḥ mugdhaḥ suptaḥ iti
pariśeṣāt ardha saṃpattiḥ mugdha tā iti avagacchāmaḥ niḥsaṃjña tvāt saṃpannaḥ itarasmāt ca vailakṣaṇyāt asaṃpannaḥ iti
katham punar ardha saṃpattiḥ mugdha tā iti śakyate vaktum
yāvatā suptam prati tāvat uktam śrutyā satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati iti atra stenaḥ stenaḥ bhavati na etam setum ahar rātre tarataḥ na jarā na mṛtyuḥ na śokaḥ na sukṛtam na duṣkṛtam ityādi
jīve hi sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ prāptiḥ sukhi tva duḥkhi tva pratyaya utpādanena bhavati
na ca sukhi tva pratyayaḥ duḥkhi tva pratyayaḥ vā suṣupte vidyate
mugdhe pi tau pratyayau na eva vidyete
tasmāt upādhi upaśamāt suṣupta vat mugdhe pi kṛtsna saṃpattiḥ eva bhavitum arhati na ardha saṃpattiḥ iti
atra ucyate na brūmaḥ mugdheḥ ṛdha saṃpattiḥ jīvasya brahmaṇā bhavati iti
kim tarhi ardhena suṣupta pakṣasya bhavati mugdha tvam ardhena avasthā antara pakṣasya iti brūmaḥ
darśite ca mohasya svāpena sāmya vaiṣamye
dvāram ca etat maraṇasya
yadā asya sa avaśeṣam karma bhavati tadā vāc manase pratyāgacchataḥ
yadā tu niravaśeṣam karma bhavati tadā prāṇa ūṣmāṇau apagacchataḥ
tasmāt ardha saṃpattim brahma vidaḥ icchanti
yat tu uktam na pañcamī kācid avasthā prasiddhā asti iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
kādācitkīyam avasthā iti na prasiddhā syāt
prasiddhā ca eṣā loka āyurvedayoḥ
ardha saṃpatti abhyupagamāt ca na pañcamī gaṇyate iti anavadyam
na parasya ubhaya liṅgam sarvatra hi
ubhaya liṅga adhikaraṇam
yena brahmaṇā suṣupti ādiṣu jīvaḥ upādhi upaśamāt saṃpadyate tasya idānīm svarūpam śruti vaśena nirdhāryate
santi ubhaya liṅgāḥ śrutayaḥ brahma viṣayāḥ sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ sarva gandhaḥ sarva rasaḥ iti evamādyāḥ sa viśeṣa liṅgāḥ
a sthūlam an aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham iti evamādyāḥ ca nirviśeṣa liṅgāḥ
kim āsu śrutiṣu ubhaya liṅgam brahma pratipattavyam
yadā api anyatara liṅgam tadā api sa viśeṣam uta nirviśeṣam iti mīmāṃsyate
tatra ubhaya liṅga śruti anugrahāt ubhaya liṅgam eva brahma iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na tāvat svatas eva parasya brahmaṇaḥ ubhaya liṅga tvam upapadyate
na hi ekam vastu svatas eva rūpa ādi viśeṣa upetam tad viparītam ca iti avadhārayitum śakyam virodhāt
astu tarhi sthānataḥ pṛthivī ādi upādhi yogāt iti
tat api nā upapadyate na hi upādhi yogāt api anyādṛśasya vastunaḥ nyādṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati
na hi svacchaḥ san sphaṭikaḥ alaktaka ādi upādhi yogāt asvacchaḥ bhavati bhrama mātra tvāt asvaccha tā abhiniveśasya
upādhīnām ca avidyā pratyupasthāpita tvāt
atas ca anyatara liṅga parigrahe samasta viśeṣa rahitam nirvikalpakam eva brahma pratipattavyam na tad viparītam
sarvatra hi brahma svarūpa pratipādana pareṣu vākyeṣu aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam iti evamādiṣu apāsta samasta viśeṣam eva brahma upadiśyate
na bhedāt iti ced na pratyekam a tad vacanāt
atha api syāt yat uktam nirvikalpam eka liṅgam eva brahma na asya svatas sthānataḥ vā ubhaya liṅga tvam asti iti tat na upapadyate
kasmāt
bhedāt
bhinnāḥ hi pratividyam brahmaṇaḥ ākārāḥ upadiśyante catuṣpād brahma ṣoḍaśa kalam brahma vāmanī tva ādi lakṣaṇam brahma trailokya śarīra vaiśvānara śabda uditam brahma iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ
tasmāt sa viśeṣa tvam api brahmaṇaḥ bhyupagantavyam
nanu uktam na ubhaya liṅga tvam brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavati iti
ayam api avirodhaḥ upādhi kṛta tvāt ākāra bhedasya
anyathā hi nirviṣayam eva bheda śāstram prasajyeta iti ced na iti brūmaḥ
kasmāt
pratyekam a tad vacanāt
pratyupādhi bhedam hi abhedam eva brahmaṇaḥ śrāvayati śāstram yaḥ ca ayam asyām pṛthivyām tejaḥ mayaḥ mṛta mayaḥ puruṣaḥ yaḥ ca ayam adhyātmam śārīraḥ tejaḥ mayaḥ mṛta mayaḥ puruṣaḥ yam eva sa yaḥ yam ātmā ityādi
atas ca na bhinna ākāra yogaḥ brahmaṇaḥ śāstrīyaḥ iti śakyate vaktum bhedasya upāsana artha tvāt abhede tātparyāt
api ca evam eke
api ca evam bheda darśana nindā pūrvakam abheda darśanam eva eke śākhinaḥ samāmananti manasā eva idam āptavyam na iha nānā asti kiṃcana
mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti
tathā anye bhoktā bhogyam preritāram ca matvā sarvam proktam trividham brahma me tat iti samastasya bhogya bhoktṛ niyantṛ lakṣaṇasya prapañcasya brahma eka svabhāva tām adhīyate
katham punar ākāra vat upadeśinīṣu an ākāra upadeśinīṣu ca brahma viṣayāsu śrutiṣu satīṣu anākāram eva brahma avadhāryate na punar viparītam
iti atas uttaram paṭhati
a rūpavat eva hi tat pradhāna tvāt
rūpa ādi ākāra rahitam eva hi brahma avadhārayitavyam na rūpa ādimat
kasmāt
tad pradhāna tvāt
a sthūlam an aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham a śabdam a sparśam arūpam avyayam ākāśaḥ vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yat antarā tat brahma divyaḥ hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sa bāhya abhyantaraḥ hi ajaḥ tat etat brahma apūrvam anaparam anantaram abāhyam ayam ātmā brahma sarva anubhūḥ iti evamādīni vākyāni niṣprapañca brahma ātma tattva pradhānāni na artha antara pradhānāni iti etat pratiṣṭhāpitam tat tu samanvayāt iti atra
tasmāt evaṃjātīyakeṣu vākyeṣu yathāśrutam nirākāram eva brahma avadhārayitavyam
itarāṇi tu ākāravat brahma viṣayāṇi vākyāni na tad pradhānāni
upāsanā vidhi pradhānāni hi tāni
teṣu asati virodhe yathāśrutam āśrayitavyam
sati tu virodhe tad pradhānāni a tad pradhānebhyaḥ balīyāṃsi bhavanti iti eṣa vinigamanāyām hetuḥ yena ubhayīṣu api śrutiṣu satīṣu anākāram eva brahma avadhāryate na punar viparītam iti
kā tarhi ākāravat viṣayāṇām śrutīnām gatiḥ
iti atas āha
prakāśa vat ca a vaiyarthyāt
yathā prakāśaḥ sauraḥ cāndramasaḥ vā viyat vyāpya avatiṣṭhamānaḥ aṅguli ādi upādhi saṃbandhāt teṣu ṛju vakra ādi bhāvam pratipadyamāneṣu tad bhāvam iva pratipadyate evam brahmā api pṛthivī ādi upādhi saṃbandhāt tad ākāra tām iva pratipadyate
tad ālambanaḥ brahmaṇaḥ ākāra viśeṣa upadeśaḥ upāsana arthaḥ na virudhyate
evam avaiyarthyam ākāra vat brahma viṣayāṇām api vākyānām bhaviṣyati
na hi veda vākyānām kasyacid arthavat tvam kasyacid anarthavat tvam iti yuktam pratipattum pramāṇa tva aviśeṣāt
nanu evam api yat purastāt pratijñātam na upādhi yogāt api ubhaya liṅga tvam brahmaṇaḥ sti iti tat virudhyate
na iti brūmaḥ upādhi nimittasya vastu dharma tva anupapatteḥ
upādhīnām ca avidyā pratyupasthāpita tvāt
satyām eva ca naisargikyām avidyāyām loka veda vyavahāra avatāraḥ iti tatra tatra avocāma
āha ca tanmātram
āha ca śrutiḥ caitanya mātram vilakṣaṇa rūpa antara rahitam nirviśeṣam brahma sa yathā saindhava ghanaḥ nantaraḥ bāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ rasa ghanaḥ eva evam vai are yam ātmā anantaraḥ bāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ prajñāna ghanaḥ eva iti
etat uktam bhavati na asya ātmanaḥ ntar bahis vā caitanyāt anyat rūpam asti caitanyam eva tu nirantaram asya svarūpam yathā saindhava ghanasya antar bahis ca lavaṇa rasaḥ eva nirantaraḥ bhavati na rasa antaram tathā eva iti
darśayati ca atha u api smaryate
darśayati ca śrutiḥ para rūpa pratiṣedhena eva brahma nirviśeṣa tvāt atha atas ādeśaḥ na iti na iti anyat eva tat viditāt atha u a viditāt adhi yatas vācaḥ nivartante a prāpya manasā saha iti evamādyā
bāṣkalinā ca bādhvaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ san avacanena eva brahma provāca iti śrūyate sa ha uvāca adhīhi bho iti sa tūṣṇīm babhūva tam ha dvitīye tṛtīye vā vacane uvāca brūmaḥ khalu tvam tu na vijānāsi
upaśāntaḥ yama ātmā iti
tathā smṛtiṣu api para pratiṣedhena evā upadiśyate jñeyam yat tat pravakṣyāmi yat jñātvā amṛtam aśnute
anādimat param brahma na sat tat na asat ucyate iti evamādyāsu
tathā viśva rūpa dharaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ nāradam uvāca iti smaryate māyā hi eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yat mām paśyasi nārada
sarva bhūta guṇaiḥ yuktam na evam mām jñātum arhasi iti
atas eva ca upamā sūryaka ādi vat
yatas eva ca ayam ātmā caitanya rūpaḥ nirviśeṣaḥ vāc manasā atītaḥ para pratiṣedha upadeśyaḥ atas eva ca asya upādhi nimittām apāramārthikīm viśeṣavat tām abhipretya jala sūryaka ādi vat iti upamā upādīyate mokṣa śāstreṣu yathā hi ayam jyotiḥ ātmā vivasvān apaḥ bhinnāḥ bahudhā ekaḥ nugacchan
upādhinā kriyate bheda rūpaḥ devaḥ kṣetreṣu evam ajaḥ yama ātmā iti
ekaḥ eva hi bhūtātmā bhūte bhūte vyavasthitaḥ
ekadhā bahudhā ca eva dṛśyate jala candra vat iti ca evamādiṣu
atra pratyavasthīyate
ambu vat agrahaṇāt tu na tathātvam
na jala sūryaka ādi tulya tvam iha upapadyate tadvat agrahaṇāt
sūrya ādibhyaḥ hi mūrtebhyaḥ pṛthak bhūtam viprakṛṣṭa deśam mūrtam jalam gṛhyate
tatra yuktaḥ sūrya ādi pratibimba udayaḥ
na tu ātmā mūrtaḥ na ca asmāt pṛthak bhūtāḥ viprakṛṣṭa deśāḥ ca upādhayaḥ sarvagata tvāt sarva ananyatvāt ca
tasmāt ayuktaḥ yam dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti
atra pratividhīyate
vṛddhi hrāsa bhāj tvam antarbhāvāt ubhaya sāmañjasyāt evam
yuktaḥ eva tu ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ vivakṣita aṃśa saṃbhavāt
na hi dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭāntikayoḥ kvacid kaṃcid vivakṣitam aṃśam muktvā sarva sārūpyam kenacid darśayitum śakyate
sarva sārūpye hi dṛ
darśanāt ca
darśayati ca śrutiḥ parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ deha ādiṣu upādhiṣu antar anupraveśam puras cakre dvipadaḥ puras cakre catuṣpadaḥ
puras sa pakṣī bhūtvā puras puruṣa āviśat iti
anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya iti ca
tasmāt yuktam etat atas eva ca upamā sūryaka ādi vat iti
tasmāt nirvikalpaka eka liṅgam eva brahma na ubhaya liṅgam viparīta liṅgam vā iti siddham
atra kecid dve adhikaraṇe kalpayanti prathamam tāvat kim pratyastamita aśeṣa prapañcam eka ākāram brahma uta prapañca vat aneka ākāra upetam iti
dvitīyam tu pratyastam ita prapañca tve kim sat lakṣaṇam brahma uta bodha lakṣaṇam uta ubhaya lakṣaṇam iti
atra vayam vadāmaḥ sarvathā api ānarthakyam adhikaraṇa antara ārambhasya iti
yadi tāvat aneka liṅga tvam parasya brahmaṇaḥ nirākartavyam iti ayam prayāsaḥ tat pūrveṇa eva na iti anena adhikaraṇena nirākṛtam iti uttaram adhikaraṇam prakāśavat ca iti etat vyartham eva bhavet
na ca sat lakṣaṇam eva brahma na bodha lakṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum vijñāna ghanaḥ eva ityādi śruti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt
katham vā nirasta caitanyam brahma cetanasya jīvasya ātma tvena upadiśyeta
nā api bodha lakṣaṇam eva brahma na sat lakṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum asti iti eva upalabdhavyaḥ ityādi śruti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt
katham vā nirasta sattākaḥ bodhaḥ bhyupagamyeta
nā api ubhaya lakṣaṇam eva brahma iti śakyam vaktum pūrva abhyupagama virodha prasaṅgāt
sattā vyāvṛttena ca bodhena bodha vyāvṛttayā ca sattayā upetam brahma pratijānānasya tat eva pūrva adhikaraṇa pratiṣiddham sa prapañca tvam prasajyeta
śruta tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na ekasya aneka svabhāva tva anupapatteḥ
atha sattā eṣa bodhaḥ bodhaḥ eva ca sattā na anayoḥ paraspara vyāvṛttiḥ asti iti yadi ucyeta tathā api kim sat lakṣaṇam brahma uta bodha lakṣaṇam uta ubhaya lakṣaṇam iti ayam vikalpaḥ nirālambanaḥ eva syāt
sūtrāṇi tu eka adhikaraṇa tvena eva asmābhiḥ nītāni
api ca brahma viṣayāsu śrutiṣu ākāra vat anākāra pratipādanena vipratipannāsu anākāre brahmaṇi parigṛhīte avaśyam vaktavyā itarāsām śrutīnām gatiḥ
tādarthyena prakāśa vat ca ityādīni sūtrāṇi arthavattarāṇi saṃpadyante
yat api āhuḥ ākāra vādinyaḥ pi śrutayaḥ prapañca vilaya mukhena anākāra pratipatti arthāḥ eva na pṛthak arthāḥ iti tat api na samīcīnam iva lakṣyate
katham
ye hi paravidyā adhikāre kecid prapañcāḥ ucyante yathā yuktāḥ hi asya harayaḥ śatāḥ daśa iti ayam vai harayaḥ yam vai daśa ca sahasrāṇi bahūni ca anantāni ca iti evamādayaḥ te bhavantu pravilaya arthāḥ
tat etat brahma apūrvam anaparam anantaram abāhyam iti upasaṃhārāt
ye punar upāsanā vidhāna adhikāre prapañcāḥ ucyante yathā manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ iti evamādayaḥ na teṣām pravilaya artha tvam nyāyyam
sa kratum kurvīta iti evaṃjātīyakena prakṛtena eva upāsana vidhinā teṣām saṃbandhāt
śrutyā ca evaṃjātīyakānām guṇānām upāsana artha tve na lakṣaṇayā pravilaya artha tvam avakalpate
sarveṣām ca sādhāraṇe pravilaya artha tve sati arūpavat eva hi tad pradhāna tvāt iti vinigamana kāraṇa vacanam anavakāśam syāt
phalam api eṣām yathopadeśam kvacid durita kṣayaḥ kvacid aiśvairya prāptiḥ kvacid krama muktiḥ iti avagamyate eva iti atas pārthagarthyam eva upāsanā vākyānām brahma vākyānām ca nyāyyam na eka vākya tvam
katham ca eṣām eka vākyatā utprekṣyate iti vaktavyam eka niyoga pratīteḥ prayāja darśa pūrṇamāsa vākya vat iti ced na brahma vākyeṣu niyoga abhāvāt vastu mātra paryavasāyīni hi brahma vākyāni na niyoga upadeśīni iti etat vistareṇa pratiṣṭhāpitam tat tu samanvayāt iti atra
kiṃviṣayaḥ ca atra niyogaḥ bhipreyate iti vaktavyam
puruṣaḥ hi niyujyamānaḥ kuru iti sva vyāpāre kasmiṃścid niyujyate
nanu dvaita prapañca pravilayaḥ niyoga viṣayaḥ bhaviṣyati apravilāpite hi dvaita prapañce brahma tattva ābodhaḥ na bhavati iti atas brahma tattva avabodha pratyanīka bhūtaḥ dvaita prapañcaḥ pravilāpyaḥ yathā svarga kāmasya yāgaḥ nuṣṭhātavyaḥ upadiśyate evam apavarga kāmasya prapañca pravilayaḥ
yathā ca tamasi vyavasthitam ghaṭa ādi tattvam avabubhutsamānena tad pratyanīka bhūtam tamaḥ pravilāpyate evam brahma tattvam avabubhutsamānena tad pratyanīka bhūtaḥ prapañcaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ brahma svabhāvaḥ hi prapañcaḥ na prapañca svabhāvam brahma
tena nāma rūpa prapañca pravilāpanena brahma tattva avabodhaḥ bhavati iti
atra vayam pṛcchāmaḥ kaḥ yam prapañca pravilayaḥ nāma
kim agni pratāpa saṃparkāt ghṛta kāṭhinya pravilayaḥ iva prapañca pravilayaḥ kartavyaḥ āhosvit ekasmin candre timira kṛta aneka candra prapañca vat avidyā kṛtaḥ brahmaṇi nāma rūpa prapañcaḥ vidyayā pravilāpayitavyaḥ iti
tatra yadi tāvat vidyamānaḥ yam prapañcaḥ deha ādi lakṣaṇaḥ ādhyātmikaḥ bāhyaḥ ca pṛthivī ādi lakṣaṇaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ iti ucyeta sa puruṣa mātreṇa aśakyaḥ pravilāpayitum iti tad pravilaya upadeśaḥ śakya viṣayaḥ eva syāt
ekena ca ādi muktena pṛthivī ādi pravilayaḥ kṛtaḥ iti idānīm pṛthivī ādi śūnyam jagat abhaviṣyat
atha avidyā adhyastaḥ brahmaṇi ekasmin ayam prapañcaḥ vidyayā pravilāpyate iti brūyāt tatas brahma eva avidyā adhyasta prapañca pratyākhyānena āvedayitavyam ekam eva advitīyam brahma tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti tasmin āvedite vidyā svayam eva utpadyate
tayā ca avidyā bādhyate tatas ca avidyā adhyastaḥ sakalaḥ yam nāma rūpa prapañcaḥ svapna prapañca vat pravilīyate an āvedite tu brahmaṇi brahma vijñānam kuru prapañca pravilayam ca iti śata kṛtvā u pi ukte na brahma vijñānam prapañca pravilayaḥ vā jāyeta
nanu āvedite brahmaṇi tad vijñāna viṣayaḥ prapañca vilaya viṣayaḥ vā niyogaḥ syāt
na niṣprapañca brahma ātma tva āvedanena eva ubhaya siddheḥ rajju sva rūpa prakāśanena eva hi tat sva rūpa vijñānam avidyā adhyasta sarpa ādi prapañca pravilayaḥ ca bhavati
na ca kṛtam eva punar kriyate
ca prapañca avasthāyām yaḥ avagamyate jīvaḥ nāma sa prapañca pakṣasya eva vā syāt brahma pakṣasya eva vā prathame vikalpe niṣprapañca brahma tattva pratipādanena pṛthivī ādi vat jīvasya api pravilāpita tvāt kasya prapañca vilaye niyogaḥ ucyeta
kasya vā niyoga niṣṭha tayā mokṣaḥ vāptavyaḥ ucyeta
dvitīye pi brahma eva aniyojya svabhāvam jīvasya svarūpam jīva tvam tu avidyā kṛtam eva iti pratipādite brahmaṇi niyojya abhāvāt niyoga abhāvaḥ eva
draṣṭavya ādi śabdāḥ api paravidyā adhikāra paṭhitāḥ tattva abhimukhīkaraṇa pradhānāḥ na tattva avabodha vidhi pradhānāḥ bhavanti
loke pi idam paśya idam ākarṇaya iti ca evaṃjātīyakeṣu nirdeśeṣu praṇidhāna mātram kuru iti ucyate na sākṣāt jñānam eva kuru iti
jñeya abhimukhasya api jñānam kadācid jāyate kadācid na jāyate
tasmāt tam prati jñāna viṣayaḥ eva darśayitavyaḥ jñāpayitu kāmena
tasmin darśite svayam eva yathāviṣayam yathāpramāṇam ca jñānam utpadyate
na ca pramāṇa antareṇa anyathā prasiddhe rthe anyathā jñānam niyuktasya api upapadyate
yadi punar niyuktaḥ ham iti anyathā jñānam kuryāt na tu tat jñānam kim tarhi mānasī sā kriyā
svayam eva ced anyathā utpadyeta bhrāntiḥ eva syāt
jñānam tu pramāṇa janyam yathā bhūta viṣayam ca
na tat niyoga śatena api kārayitum śakyate na ca pratiṣedha śatena api vārayitum śakyate
na hi tat puruṣa tantram vastu tantram eva hi tat
atas pi niyoga abhāvaḥ
kiṃca anyat niyoga niṣṭhatayā eva paryavasyati āmnāye yat abhyupagatam a niyojya brahma ātmatvam jīvasya tat apramāṇakam eva syāt
atha śāstram eva aniyojya brahma ātmatvam ācakṣīta tad avabodhe ca puruṣam niyuñjīta tatas brahmaśāstrasya ekasya dvi artha para tā viruddha artha para tā ca prasajyeyātām
niyoga para tāyām ca śruta hāniḥ aśruta kalpanā karma phala vat mokṣasya adṛṣṭa phala tvam anitya tvam ca iti evamādayaḥ doṣāḥ na kenacid parihartum śakyāḥ
tasmāt avagati niṣṭhāni eva brahma vākyāni na niyoga niṣṭhāni
atas ca eka niyoga pratīteḥ eka vākya tā iti ayuktam
abhyupagamyamāne ca brahma vākyeṣu niyoga sadbhāve tad eka tvam niṣprapañca upadeśeṣu sa prapañca upadeśeṣu ca asiddham
na hi śabda antara ādibhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ niyoga bhede vagamyamāne sarvatra ekaḥ niyogaḥ iti śakyam āśrayitum
prayāja darśa pūrṇamāsa vākyeṣu tu adhikāra aṃśena abhedāt yuktam eka tvam
na tu iha saguṇa nirguṇa codanāsu kaścid ekatva kara oṃśaḥ sti
na hi bhā rūpa tva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ prapañca pravilaya upakāriṇaḥ na api prapañca vilayaḥ bhā rūpa tva ādi guṇa upakārī paraspara virodhi tvāt
na hi kṛtsna prapañca pravilāpanam prapañca eka deśa apekṣaṇam ca ekasmin dharmiṇi yuktam samāveśayitum
tasmāt asmad uktaḥ eva vibhāgaḥ ākāra vat anākāra upadeśānām yuktataraḥ iti
prakṛtā etāvat tvam hi pratiṣedhati tatas bravīti ca bhūyas
prakṛta etāvat tva adhikaraṇam
dve vāva brahmaṇaḥ rūpe mūrtam ca eva amūrtam ca iti upakramya pañca mahābhūtāni dvairāśyena pravibhajya amūrta rasasya ca puruṣa śabda uditasya māhārajana ādīni rūpāṇi darśayitvā punar paṭhyate atha atas ādeśaḥ na iti na iti na hi etasmāt iti na iti anyat param asti iti
tatra kaḥ sya pratiṣedhasya viṣayaḥ iti jijñāsāmahe
na hi atra idam tat iti viśeṣitam kiṃcid pratiṣedhyam upalabhyate
iti śabdena tu atra pratiṣedhyam kim api samarpyate na iti na iti iti iti paratvāt nañ prayogasya
iti śabdaḥ ca ayam saṃnihita ālambanaḥ evaṃśabda samāna vṛttiḥ prayujyamānaḥ dṛśyate iti ha sma upādhyāyaḥ kathayati iti evamādiṣu
saṃnihitam ca atra prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt rūpa dvayam sa prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ tat ca brahma yasya te dve rūpe
tatra naḥ saṃśayaḥ upajāyate kim ayam pratiṣedhaḥ rūpe rūpavat ca ubhayam api pratiṣedhati āhosvit ekataram
yadā api ekataram tadā api kim brahma pratiṣedhati rūpe pariśinaṣṭi āhosvit rūpe pratiṣedhati brahma pariśinaṣṭi iti
tatra prakṛta tva aviśeṣāt ubhayam api pratiṣedhati iti āśaṅkāmahe dvau ca etau pratiṣedhau dvis na iti śabda prayogāt
tayoḥ ekena sa prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam pratiṣidhyate apareṇa rūpavat brahma iti bhavati matiḥ
athavā brahma eva rūpavat pratiṣidhyate
tat hi vāc manasā atīta tvāt asaṃbhāvyamāna sadbhāvam pratiṣedha arham
na tu rūpa prapañcaḥ pratyakṣa ādi gocara tvāt pratiṣedha arhaḥ
abhyāsaḥ tu ādara arthaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na tāvat ubhaya pratiṣedhaḥ upapadyate śūnyavāda prasaṅgāt kaṃcid hi paramārtham ālambya aparamārthaḥ pratiṣidhyate yathā rajju ādiṣu sarpa ādayaḥ
tat ca pariśiṣyamāṇe kasmiṃścid bhāve avakalpate
kṛtsna pratiṣedhe tu kaḥ nyaḥ bhāvaḥ pariśiṣyeta
a pariśiṣyamāṇe ca anyasmin yaḥ itaraḥ pratiṣeddhum ārabhyate pratiṣeddhum aśakya tvāt tasya eva parama artha tva āpatteḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ
nā api brahma pratiṣedhaḥ upapadyate brahma te bravāṇi ityādi upakrama virodhāt asannā eva sa bhavati
asat brahma iti veda ced ityādi nindā virodhāt asti iti eva upalabdhavyaḥ ityādi avadhāraṇa virodhāt sarva vedānta vyākopa prasaṅgāt ca
vāc manasā atīta tvam api brahmaṇaḥ na abhāva abhiprāyeṇa abhidhīyate
na hi mahatā parikara bandhena brahma vidā āpnoti param satyam jñānam anantam brahma iti evamādinā vedānteṣu brahma pratipādya tasya eva punar abhāvaḥ bhilapyeta
prakṣālanāt hi paṅkasya dūrāt asparśanam varam iti hi nyāyaḥ
pratipādana prakriyā tu eṣā yatas vācaḥ nivartante
a prāpya manasā saha iti
etat uktam bhavati vāc manasā atītam aviṣaya antaḥpāti pratyagātma bhūtam nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam brahma iti
tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ rūpa prapañcam pratiṣedhati pariśinaṣṭi brahma iti avagantavyam
tat etat ucyate prakṛtā etāvat tvam hi pratiṣedhati iti
prakṛtam yat etāvat iyat tā paricchinnam mūrta amūrta lakṣaṇam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam tat eṣa śabdaḥ pratiṣedhati
tat hi prakṛtam prapañcitam ca pūrvasmin granthe adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca
tad janitam eva ca vāsanā lakṣaṇam aparam rūpam amūrta rasa bhūtam puruṣa śabda uditam liṅga ātma vyapāśrayam māhārajana ādi upamābhiḥ darśitam amūrta rasasya puruṣasya cakṣuḥ grāhya rūpa yogi tva anupapatteḥ
tat etat sa prapañcam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam saṃnihita ālambanena iti karaṇena pratiṣedhakam nañam prati upanīyate iti gamyate
brahma tu rūpa viśeṣaṇa tvena ṣaṣṭhyā nirdiṣṭam pūrvasmin granthe na sva pradhāna tvena
prapañcite ca tadīye rūpa dvaye rūpavataḥ svarūpa jijñāsāyām idam upakrāntam atha atas ādeśaḥ na iti na iti iti
tatra kalpita rūpa pratyākhyānena brahmaṇaḥ svarūpa āvedanam iti nirṇīyate
tad āspadam hi idam samastam kāryam na iti na iti iti pratiṣiddham
yuktam ca kāryasya vācā ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ sattvam iti na iti na iti iti pratiṣedhanam
na tu brahmaṇaḥ sarva kalpanā mūla tvāt
na ca atra iyam āśaṅkā kartavyā katham hi śāstram svayam eva brahmaṇaḥ rūpa dvayam darśayitvā svayam eva punar pratiṣedhati prakṣālanāt hi paṅkasya dūrāt asparśanam varam iti yatas na idam śāstram pratipādya tvena brahmaṇaḥ rūpa dvayam nirdiśati loka prasiddham tu idam rūpa dvayam brahmaṇi kalpitam parāmṛśati pratiṣedhya tvāya śuddha brahma svarūpa pratipādanāya ca iti niravadyam
dvau ca etau pratiṣedhau yathā saṃkhya nyāyena dve api mūrta amūrte pratiṣedhataḥ
yat vā pūrvaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ bhūta rāśim pratiṣedhati uttaraḥ vāsanā rāśim
athavā na iti na iti iti vīpsā iyam iti iti yāvat kiṃcid utprekṣyate tat sarvam na bhavati iti arthaḥ parigaṇita pratiṣedhe hi kriyamāṇe yadi na etat brahma kim anyat brahma bhavet iti jijñāsā syāt
vīpsāyām tu satyām samastasya viṣaya jātasya pratiṣedhāt aviṣayaḥ pratyagātmā brahma iti jijñāsā nivartate
tasmāt prapañcam eva brahmaṇi kalpitam pratiṣedhati pariśinaṣṭi brahma iti nirṇayaḥ
itas ca eṣaḥ eva nirṇayaḥ yatas tatas prapañca pratiṣedhāt bhūyas brahma bravīti anyat param asti iti
abhāva avasāne hi pratiṣedhe kriyamāṇe kim anyat param asti iti brūyāt
tatra eṣā akṣara yojanā na iti na iti iti brahma ādiśya tam eva ādeśam punar nirvakti na iti na iti iti asya kaḥ rthaḥ
na hi etasmāt brahmaṇaḥ vyatiriktam asti iti atas na iti na iti iti ucyate na punar svayam eva na asti iti arthaḥ
tat ca darśayati anyat param apratiṣiddham brahma asti iti
yadā punar evam akṣarāṇi yojyante na hi etasmāt iti na iti na iti prapañca pratiṣedha rūpāt ādeśanāt anyat param ādeśanam brahmaṇaḥ asti iti tadā tatas bravīti ca bhūyas iti etat nāmadheya viṣayam yojayitavyam atha nāmadheya asatyasya satyam iti prāṇāḥ vai satyam teṣām eṣa satyam iti hi bravīti iti
tat ca brahma avasāne pratiṣedhe samañjasam bhavati
abhāva avasāne tu pratiṣedhe kim satyasya satyam iti ucyeta
tasmāt brahma avasānaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ na abhāva avasānaḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ
tat avyaktam āha hi
yat tat pratiṣiddhāt prapañca jātāt anyat param brahma tat asti ced kasmāt na gṛhyate iti ucyate tat avyaktam an indriya grāhyam sarva dṛśya sākṣi tvāt
āha hi evam śrutiḥ na cakṣuṣā gṛhyate na api vācā na anyaiḥ devaiḥ tapasā karmaṇā vā saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmā a gṛhyaḥ na hi gṛhyate yat tat a dreśyam a grāhyam yadā hi eva eṣa etasmin adṛśye na ātmye nirukte nilayane ityādyā
smṛtiḥ api avyaktaḥ yam acintyaḥ yam avikāryaḥ yam ucyate ityādyā
api ca saṃrādhane pratyakṣa anumānābhyām
api ca enam ātmānam nirasta samasta prapañcam avyaktam saṃrādhana kāle paśyanti yoganaḥ
saṃrādhanam ca bhakti dhyāna praṇidhāna ādi anuṣṭhānam
katham punar avagamyate saṃrādhana kāle paśyanti iti
pratyakṣa anumānābhyām śruti smṛtibhyām iti arthaḥ
tathā hi śrutiḥ parāñci khāni vyatṛṇat svayaṃbhūḥ tasmāt parāṅ paśyati na antarātman
kaścid dhīraḥ pratyagātmānam aikṣat āvṛtta cakṣuḥ amṛta tvam icchan iti jñāna prasādena viśuddha sattvaḥ tatas tu tam paśyate niṣkalam dhyāyamānaḥ iti ca evamādyā
smṛtiḥ api ye vinidrā jita śvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ
jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāḥ tasmai yoga ātmane namaḥ
yoginaḥ tam prapaśyanti bhagavantam sanātanam iti ca evamādyā
nanu saṃrādhya saṃrādhaka bhāva abhyupagamāt para apara ātmanoḥ anya tvam syāt iti
na iti ucyate
prakāśa ādi vat ca a vaiśeṣyam prakāśaḥ ca karmaṇi abhyāsāt
yathā prakāśa ākāśa savitṛ prabhṛtayaḥ aṅguli karaka udaka prabhṛtiṣu karmasu upādhi bhūteṣu sa viśeṣāḥ iva avabhāsante na ca svābhāvikīm aviśeṣa ātmatām jahati
evam upādhi nimittaḥ eva ayam ātma bhedaḥ svatas tu aikātmyam eva
tathā hi vedānteṣu abhyāsena asakṛt jīva prājñayoḥ abhedaḥ pratipādyate
atas na antena tathā hi liṅgam
atas ca svābhāvika tvāt abhedasya avidyā kṛta tvāt ca bhedasya vidyayā avidyām vidhūya jīvaḥ pareṇa anantena prājñena ātmanā ekatām gacchati
tathā hi liṅgam sa yaḥ ha vai tat paramam brahma veda brahma eva bhavati brahma eva san brahma apyeti ityādi
ubhaya vyapadeśāt tu ahi kuṇḍala vat
tasmin eva saṃrādhya saṃrādhaka bhāve mata antaram upanyasyati sva mata viśuddhaye
kvacid jīva prājñayoḥ bhedaḥ vyapadiśyate tatas tu tam paśyate niṣkalam dhyāyamānaḥ iti dhyātṛ dhyātavya tvena draṣṭṛ draṣṭavya tvena ca
parātparam puruṣam upaiti divyam iti gantṛ gantavya tvena
yaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni antaraḥ yamayati iti niyantṛ niyantavya tvena ca
kvacid tu tayoḥ eva abhedaḥ vyapadiśyate tat tvam asi aham brahma asmi eṣa te ātmā sarva antaraḥ eṣa te ātmā antaryāmī amṛtaḥ iti
tatra evam ubhaya vyapadeśe sati yadi abhedaḥ eva ekāntataḥ gṛhyate bheda vyapadeśaḥ nirālambanaḥ eva syāt
atas ubhaya vyapadeśa darśanāt ahi kuṇḍala vat atra tattvam bhavitum arhati yathā ahiḥ iti abhedaḥ kuṇḍala ābhoga prāṃśu tva ādīni iti ca bhedaḥ evam iha api iti
prakāśa āśrayavat vā tejaḥ tvāt
athavā prakāśa āśraya vat etat pratipattavyam yathā prakāśaḥ sāvitraḥ tad āśrayaḥ ca savitā na atyanta bhinnau ubhayoḥ api tejaḥ tva aviśeṣāt
atha ca bheda vyapadeśa bhājau bhavataḥ evam iha api iti
pūrvavat vā
yathā vā pūrvam upanyastam prakāśa ādi vat ca a vaiśeṣyam iti tathā eva etat bhavitum arhati
tathā hi avidyā kṛta tvāt bandhasya vidyayā mokṣaḥ upapadyate
yadi punar paramārthataḥ eva baddhaḥ kaścid ātmā ahi kuṇḍala nyāyena parasya ātmanaḥ saṃsthāna bhūtaḥ prakāśa āśraya nyāyena ca eka deśa bhūtaḥ bhyupagamyeta
tatas pāramārthikasya bandhasya tiraskartum aśakya tvāt mokṣa śāstra vaiyarthyam prasajyeta
na ca atra ubhau api bheda abhedau śrutiḥ tulya vat vyapadiśati
abhedam eva hi pratipādya tvena nirdiśati bhedam tu pūrva prasiddham eva anuvadati artha antara vivakṣayā
tasmāt prakāśa ādi vat ca avaiśeṣyam iti eṣaḥ eva siddhāntaḥ
pratiṣedhāt ca
itas ca eṣaḥ eva siddhāntaḥ yatkāraṇam parasmāt ātmanaḥ cetanam pratiṣedhati śāstram draṣṭā iti evamādi
atha atas ādeśaḥ na iti na iti tat etat brahma apūrvam anaparam anantaram abāhyam iti ca brahma vyatirikta prapañca nirākaraṇāt brahma mātra pariśeṣāt ca eṣaḥ eva siddhāntaḥ iti gamyate
yat etat nirasta samasta prapañcam brahma nirdhāritam asmāt param anyat tattvam asti na asti iti śruti vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ
kānicid hi vākyāni āpātena eva pratibhāsamānāni param anyat tattvam pratipādayanti iva
teṣām hi parihāram abhidhātum ayam upakramaḥ kriyate
paramatas setu unmāna sambandha bheda vyapadeśebhyaḥ
param atas brahmaṇaḥ anyat tattvam bhavitum arhati
kutas
setu vyapadeśāt unmāna vyapadeśāt saṃbandha vyapadeśāt bheda vyapadeśāt ca
setu vyapadeśaḥ tāvat atha yaḥ ātmā sa setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ iti ātma śabda abhihitasya brahmaṇaḥ setu tvam saṃkīrtayati
setu śabdaḥ ca hi loke jala saṃtāna viccheda kare mṛd dārva ādi pracaye prasiddhaḥ
iha ca setu śabdaḥ ātmani prayuktaḥ iti laukika setoḥ iva ātma setoḥ anyasya vastunaḥ stitvam gamayati
setu tītrvā iti ca tarati śabda prayogāt yathā laukikam setum tītrvā jāṅgalam a setum prāpnoti evam ātmānam setum tītrvā anātmānam a setum prāpnoti iti gamyate
unmāna vyapadeśaḥ ca bhavati tat etat brahma catuṣpād aṣṭāśapham ṣoḍaśa kalam iti
yat ca loke unmitam etāvat idam iti paricchinnam kārṣāpaṇa ādi tatas nyat vastu asti iti prasiddham
tathā brahmaṇaḥ pi unmānāt tatas nyena vastunā bhavitavyam iti gamyate
tathā saṃbandha vyapadeśaḥ bhavati satā somya tadā saṃpannaḥ bhavati iti śārīraḥ ātmā prājñena ātmanā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti ca
mitānām ca mitena saṃbandhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā narāṇām nagareṇa
jīvānām ca brahmaṇā saṃbandham vyapadiśati suṣuptau
atas tatas param anyat amitam asti iti gamyate
bheda vyapadeśaḥ ca enam artham gamayati
tathā hi atha yaḥ eṣaḥ ntarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti āditya ādhāram īśvaram vyapadiśya tatas bhedena akṣi ādhāram īśvaram vyapadiśati atha yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti
atideśam ca asya amunā rūpa ādiṣu karoti tasya etasya tat eva rūpam yat amuṣya rūpam yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau yat nāma tat nāma iti
ca īśvara tvam ubhayoḥ vyapadiśati ye ca amuṣmāt parāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca iṣṭe deva kāmānām ca iti ekasya ye ca etasmāt arvāñcaḥ lokāḥ teṣām ca iṣṭe manuṣya kāmānām ca iti ekasya yathā idam māgadhasya rājyam idam vaidehasya iti
evam etebhyaḥ setu ādi vyapadeśebhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ param asti iti
evam prāpte pratipādyate
sāmānyāt tu
tu śabdena pradarśitām prāptim niruṇaddhi
na brahmaṇaḥ nyat kiṃcid bhavitum arhati pramāṇa abhāvāt na hi anyasya astitve kiṃcid pramāṇam upalabhāmahe
sarvasya hi janimataḥ vastu jātasya janma ādi brahmaṇaḥ bhavati iti nirdhāritam ananya tvam ca kāraṇāt kāryasya
na ca brahma vyatiriktam kiṃcid ajam saṃbhavati sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti avadhāraṇāt
eka vijñānena ca sarva vijñāna pratijñānāt na brahma vyatirikta vastu astitvam avakalpate
nanu setu ādi vyapadeśāḥ brahma vyatiriktam tattvam sūcayanti iti uktam
na iti ucyate setu vyapadeśaḥ tāvat na brahmaṇaḥ bāhyasya sadbhāvam pratipādayitum kṣamate
setuḥ ātmā iti hi āha na atas param asti iti
tatra parasmin asati setu tvam na avakalpate iti param kim api kalpyeta
na ca etat nyāyyam
haṭhaḥ hi aprasiddha kalpanā
api ca setu vyapadeśāt ātmanaḥ laukika setu nidarśanena sa bāhya vastu tām prasañjayatā mṛd dāru maya tā api prāsaṅkṣyata
na ca etat nyāyyam aja tva ādi śruti virodhāt
setu sāmānyāt tu setu śabdaḥ ātmani prayuktaḥ iti śliṣyate
jagataḥ tad maryādānām ca vidhāraka tvam setu sāmānyam ātmanaḥ
atas setuḥ iva setuḥ iti prakṛtaḥ ātmā stūyate
setum tītrvā iti api taratiḥ atikrama asaṃbhavāt prāpnoti arthaḥ eva vartate yathā vyākaraṇam tīrṇaḥ iti prāptaḥ ucyate na atikrāntaḥ tadvat
buddhi arthaḥ pāda vat
yat api uktam unmāna vyapadeśāt asti param iti tatra abhidhīyate unmāna vyapadeśaḥ u pi na brahma vyatirikta vastu astitva pratipatti arthaḥ
kimarthaḥ tarhi
buddhi arthaḥ upāsana arthaḥ iti yāvat
catuṣpād aṣṭāśapham ṣoḍaśa kalam iti evaṃrūpā buddhiḥ katham nu nāma brahmaṇi sthirā syāt iti vikāra dvāreṇa brahmaṇaḥ unmāna kalpanā eva kriyate
na hi avikāre nante brahmaṇi sarvaiḥ puṃbhiḥ śakyā buddhiḥ sthāpayitum manda madhyama uttama buddhi tvāt puṃsām iti
pāda vat yathā manaḥ ākāśayoḥ adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca brahma pratīkayoḥ āmnātayoḥ catvāraḥ vāc ādayaḥ manaḥ saṃbandhinaḥ pādāḥ kalpyante catvāraḥ ca agni ādayaḥ ākāśa saṃbandhinaḥ ādhyānāya tadvat
athavā pāda vat iti yathā kārṣāpaṇe pāda vibhāgaḥ vyavahāra prācuryāya kalpyate na hi sakalena eva kārṣāpaṇena sarvadā sarve janāḥ vyavahartum īśate kraya vikraye parimāṇa aniyamāt tadvat iti arthaḥ
sthāna viśeṣāt prakāśa ādi vat
iha sūtre dvayoḥ api saṃbandha bheda vyapadeśayoḥ parihāraḥ abhidhīyate
yat api uktam saṃbandha vyapadeśāt bheda vyapadeśāt ca paramatas syāt iti tat api asat
yatas ekasya api sthāna viśeṣa apekṣayā etau vyapadeśau upapadyete
saṃbandha vyapadeśe tāvat ayam arthaḥ buddhi ādi upādhi sthāna viśeṣa yogāt udbhūtasya viśeṣa vijñānasya upādhi upaśame yaḥ upaśamaḥ sa paramātmanā saṃbandhaḥ iti upādhi apekṣayā upacaryate na parimita tva apekṣayā
tathā bheda vyapadeśaḥ u pi brahmaṇaḥ upādhi bheda apekṣayā eva upacaryate na svarūpa bheda apekṣayā
prakāśa ādi vat iti upamā upādānam yathā ekasya prakāśasya sauryasya cāndramasasya vā upādhi yogāt upajāta viśeṣasya upādhi upaśamāt saṃbandha vyapadeśaḥ bhavati upādhi bhedāt ca bheda vyapadeśaḥ
yathā vā sūcī pāśa ākāśa ādiṣu upādhi apekṣayā eva etau saṃbandha bheda vyapadeśau bhavataḥ tadvat
upapatteḥ ca
upapadyate ca atra īdṛśaḥ eva saṃbandhaḥ na anyādṛśaḥ svam api itas bhavati iti hi sva rūpa saṃbandham enam āmananti
sva rūpasya ca anapāyi tvāt na nara nagara nyāyena saṃbandhaḥ ghaṭate
upādhi kṛta svarūpa tirobhāvāt tu svam api itas bhavati iti upapadyate
tathā bhedaḥ u pi nā anyādṛśaḥ saṃbhavati bahutara śruti prasiddha eka īśvara tva virodhāt
tathā ca śrutiḥ ekasya api ākāśasya sthāna kṛtam bheda vyapadeśam upapādayati yaḥ yam bahirdhā puruṣāt ākāśaḥ yaḥ yam antar puruṣe ākāśaḥ yaḥ yam antar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ iti
tathā anya pratiṣedhāt
evam setu ādi vyapadeśān parapakṣa hetūn unmathya saṃprati sva pakṣam hetu antareṇa upasaṃharati
tathā anya pratiṣedhā api na brahmaṇaḥ param vastu antaram asti iti gamyate
tathā hi saḥ eva adhastāt
aham eva adhastāt ātmā eva adhastāt sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ nyatra ātmanaḥ sarvam veda brahma eva idam sarvam ātmā eva idam sarvam na iha nānā asti kiṃcana yasmāt param na aparam asti kiṃcid tat etat brahma apūrvam anaparam anantaram abāhyam iti evamādīni vākyāni sva prakaraṇa sthāni anya artha tvena pariṇetum aśakyāni brahma vyatiriktam vastu antaram vārayanti
sarva antara śruteḥ ca na paramātmanaḥ nyaḥ antarātmā asti iti avagamyate
anena sarvagata tvam āyāma śabda ādibhyaḥ
anena setu ādi vyapadeśa nirākaraṇena anya pratiṣedha samāśrayaṇena ca sarvagata tvam api ātmanaḥ siddham bhavati
anyathā hi tat na sidhyet
setu ādi vyapadeśeṣu hi mukhyeṣu aṅgīkriyamāṇeṣu paricchedaḥ ātmanaḥ prasajyeta setu ādīnām evam ātmaka tvāt
tathā anya pratiṣedhe pi asati vastu vastu antarāt vyāvartate iti paricchedaḥ eva ātmanaḥ prasajyeta
sarva gata tvam ca asya āyāma śabda ādibhyaḥ vagamyate
āyāma śabdaḥ vyāpti vacanaḥ śabdaḥ
yāvān vai ayam ākāśaḥ tāvān eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ jyāyān divaḥ jyāyān ākāśāt nityaḥ sarva gataḥ sthāṇuḥ acalaḥ yam sanātanaḥ iti evamādayaḥ hi śruti smṛti nyāyāḥ sarva gata tvam ātmanaḥ vabodhayanti
phalam atas upapatteḥ
phala adhikaraṇam
tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ vyāvahārikyām īśitṛ īśitavya vibhāga avasthāyām ayam anyaḥ svabhāvaḥ varṇyate
yat etat iṣṭa aniṣṭa vyāmiśra lakṣaṇam karma phalam saṃsāra gocaram trividham prasiddham jantūnām kim etat karmaṇaḥ bhavati āhosvit īśvarāt iti bhavati vicāraṇā
tatra tāvat pratipādyate phalam atas īśvarāt bhavitum arhati
kutas
upapatteḥ
sa hi sarva adhyakṣaḥ sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhārān vicitrān vidadhat deśa kāla viśeṣa abhijña tvāt karmiṇām karma anurūpam phalam saṃpādayati iti upapadyate
karmaṇaḥ tu anu kṣaṇa vināśinaḥ kāla antara bhāvi phalam bhavati iti anupapannam abhāvāt bhāva anutpatteḥ
syāt etat karma vinaśyat sva kālam eva sva anurūpam phalam janayitvā vinaśyati tat phalam kāla antaritam kartrā bhokṣyate iti
tat api na pariśudhyati prāk bhoktṛ saṃbandhāt phalatva anupapatteḥ yatkālam hi yat sukham duḥkham vā ātmanā bhujyate tasya eva loke phala tvam prasiddham
na hi asaṃbaddhasya ātmanā sukhasya duḥkhasya vā phala tvam pratiyanti laukikāḥ
atha ucyeta mā bhūt karma anantaram phala utpādaḥ karma kāryāt apūrvāt phalam utpatsyate iti tat api nā upapadyate apūrvasya acetanasya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samasya cetanena a pravartitasya pravṛtti anupapatteḥ tad astitve eva pramāṇa abhāvāt
arthāpattiḥ pramāṇam iti ced na īśvara siddheḥ arthāpatti kṣayāt
śruta tvāt ca
na kevalam upapatteḥ eva īśvaram phala hetum kalpayāmaḥ kim tarhi śrutatvāt api īśvaram eva phala hetum manyāmahe tathā ca śrutiḥ bhavati sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā anna ādaḥ vasu dānaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakā
dharmam jaiminiḥ atas eva
jaiminiḥ tu ācāryaḥ dharmam phalasya dātāram manyate atas eva hetoḥ śruteḥ upapatteḥ ca
śrūyate tāvat ayam arthaḥ svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti evamādiṣu vākyeṣu
tatra ca vidhi śruteḥ viṣaya bhāva upagamāt yāgaḥ svargasya utpādakaḥ iti gamyate
anyathā hi an anuṣṭhātṛkaḥ yāgaḥ āpadyeta
tatra asya upadeśa vaiyarthyam syāt
nanu anu kṣaṇa vināśinaḥ karmaṇaḥ phalam na upapadyate iti parityaktaḥ yam pakṣaḥ
na eṣa doṣaḥ śruti prāmāṇyāt śrutiḥ ced pramāṇam yathā ayam karma phala saṃbandhaḥ śrutaḥ upapadyate tathā kalpayitavyaḥ
na ca an utpādya kim api apūrvam karma vinaśyat kāla antaritam phalam dātum śaknoti
atas karmaṇaḥ vā sūkṣmā kācid uttara avasthā phalasya vā pūrva avasthā apūrvam nāma asti iti tarkyate
upapadyate ca ayam artham uktena prakāreṇa
īśvaraḥ tu phalam dadāti iti anupapannam avicitrasya kāraṇasya vicitra kārya anupapatteḥ vaiṣamya nairghṛṇya prasaṅgāt tad anuṣṭhāna vaiyarthya āpatteḥ ca
tasmāt dharmāt eva phalam iti
pūrvam tu bādarāyaṇaḥ hetu vyapadeśāt
bādarāyaṇaḥ tu ācāryaḥ pūrva uktam eva īśvaram phala hetum manyate
kevalāt karmaṇaḥ apūrvāt vā kevalāt phalam iti ayam pakṣaḥ tuśabdena vyāvartyate
karma apekṣāt apūrva apekṣāt vā yathā tathā astu īśvarāt phalam iti siddhāntaḥ
kutas
hetu vyapadeśāt
dharma adharmayoḥ api hi kārayitṛ tvena īśvaraḥ hetuḥ vyapadiśyate phalasya ca dātṛ tvena eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yam ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ unninīṣate
eṣaḥ u eva asādhu karma kārayati tam yam adhas ninīṣate iti
smaryate ca ayam arthaḥ bhagavadgītāsu yaḥ yaḥ yām yām tanum bhaktaḥ śraddhayā arcitum icchati
tasya tasya acalām śraddhām tām eva vidadhāmi aham
sa tayā śraddhayā yuktaḥ tasya ārādhanam īhate
labhate ca tatas kāmān mayā eva vihitān hitān iti
sarva vedānteṣu ca īśvara hetukāḥ eva sṛṣṭayaḥ vyapadiśyante
tat eva ca īśvarasya phala hetu tvam yat sva karma anurūpāḥ prajāḥ sṛjati
vicitra kārya anupapatti ādayaḥ api doṣāḥ kṛta prayatna apekṣa tvāt īśvarasya na prasajyante
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
sarva vedānta pratyayam codana ādi aviśeṣāt
sarva vedānta pratyaya adhikaraṇam
sarva vedānta pratyayāni vijñānāni tasmin tasmin vedānte tāni tāni eva bhavitum arhanti
kutas
codanā ādi aviśeṣāt
ādi grahaṇena śākhā antara adhikaraṇa siddhānta sūtra uditāḥ abheda hetavaḥ iha ākṛṣyante saṃyoga rūpa codana ākhyā viśeṣāt iti arthaḥ
yathā ekasmin agnihotre śākhā bhede pi puruṣa prayatnaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva codyate juhuyāt iti evam yaḥ ha vai jyeṣṭham ca śreṣṭham ca veda iti vājasaneyinām chandogānām ca tādṛśī eva codanā
prayojana saṃyogaḥ u pi a viśiṣṭaḥ eva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca svānām bhavati iti
rūpam api ubhayatra tat eva vijñānasya yat uta jyeṣṭha śreṣṭha ādi viśeṣaṇa anvitam prāṇa tattvam yathā ca dravya devate yāgasya rūpam evam vijñeyam rūpam vijñānasya
tena hi tat rūpyate
samākhyā api sā eva prāṇa vidyā iti
tasmāt sarva vedānta pratyaya tvam vijñānānām
evam pañca agni vidyāḥ vaiśvānara vidyā śāṇḍilya vidyā iti evamādiṣu api yojayitavyam
ye tu nāma rūpa ādayaḥ bheda hetvābhāsāḥ te prathame eva kāṇḍe na nāmnā syāt acodana abhidhāna tvāt iti ārabhya parihṛtāḥ
iha api kaṃcid viśeṣam āśaṅkya pariharati
bhedāt na iti ced na ekasyām api
syāt etat sarva vedānta pratyaya tvam vijñānānām guṇa bhedāt na upapadyate
tathā hi vājasaneyinaḥ pañcāgni vidyām prastutya ṣaṣṭham aparam agnim āmananti tasya agniḥ eva agniḥ bhavati ityādinā
chandogāḥ tu tam naḥ āmananti pañca saṃkhyayā eva ca te upasaṃharanti atha ha yaḥ etān evam pañca agnīn veda iti
yeṣām ca sa guṇaḥ sti yeṣām ca na asti katham ubhayeṣām ekā vidyā upapadyeta
na ca atra guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ śakyate pratyetum pañca saṃkhyā virodhāt
tathā prāṇa saṃvāde śreṣṭhāt anyān caturaḥ prāṇān vāc cakṣuḥ śrotra manāṃsi chandogāḥ āmananti
vājasaneyinaḥ tu pañcamam api āmananti retaḥ vai prajāpatiḥ prajāyate ha prajayā paśubhiḥ yaḥ evam veda iti
āvāpa udvāpa bhedāt ca vedya bhedaḥ bhavati vedya bhedāt ca vidyā bhedaḥ dravya devatā bheda ādiva yāgasya iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ
yatas ekasyām api vidyāyām evaṃjātīyakaḥ guṇa bhedaḥ upapadyate
yadi api ṣaṣṭhasya agneḥ upasaṃhāraḥ na saṃbhavati tathā api dyu prabhṛtīnām pañcānām agnīnām ubhayatra pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt na vidyā bhedaḥ bhavitum arhati
na hi ṣoḍaśi grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ atirātraḥ bhidyate
paṭhyate ca ṣaṣṭhaḥ gniḥ chandogaiḥ tam pretam diṣṭam itas gnayaḥ eva haranti iti
vājasaneyinaḥ tu sāṃpādikeṣu pañcasu agniṣu anuvṛttāyāḥ samidh dhūma ādi kalpanāyāḥ nivṛttaye tasya agniḥ eva agniḥ bhavati samidh samidh ityādi samāmananti
sa nitya anuvādaḥ
atha api upāsana arthaḥ eṣa vādaḥ tathā api sa guṇaḥ śakyate chandogaiḥ api upasaṃhartum
na ca atra pañca saṃkhyā virodhaḥ āśaṅkyaḥ
sāṃpādikā agni abhiprāyā hi eṣā pañca saṃkhyā nitya anuvāda bhūtā na vidhi samavāyinī iti adoṣaḥ
evam prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu api adhikasya guṇasya itaratra upasaṃhāraḥ na virudhyate
na ca āvāpa udvāpa bhedāt vedya bhedaḥ vidyā bhedaḥ ca āśaṅkyaḥ kasyacid vedya aṃśasya āvāpa udvāpayoḥ api bhūyasaḥ vedya rāśeḥ abheda avagamāt
tasmāt aikavidyam eva
svādhyāyasya tathā tvena hi samācāre dhikārāt ca sava vat ca tad niyamaḥ
yat api uktam ātharvaṇikānām vidyām prati śiraḥ vrata ādi apekṣaṇāt anyeṣām ca tad anapekṣaṇāt vidyā bhedaḥ iti tat pratyucyate
svādhyāyasya eṣa dharmaḥ na vidyāyāḥ
katham idam avagamyate
yatas tathātvena svādhyāya dharma tvena samācāre veda vrata upadeśa pare granthe ātharvaṇikāḥ idam api veda vrata tvena vyākhyātam iti samāmananti
na etat acīrṇa vrataḥ dhīte iti ca adhikṛta viṣayāt etad śabdāt adhyayana śabdāt ca sva upaniṣad adhyayana dharmaḥ eva eṣaḥ iti nirdhāryate
