nanu teṣām eva etām brahma vidyām vadeta śirovratam vidhivat yaiḥ tu cīrṇam iti brahma vidyā saṃyoga śravaṇāt ekā eva sarvatra brahma vidyā iti saṃkīryeta eṣa dharmaḥ na tatra api etām iti prakṛta pratyavamarśāt
prakṛta tvam ca brahma vidyāyāḥ grantha viśeṣa apekṣam iti grantha viśeṣa saṃyogī eva eṣa dharmaḥ
sava vat ca tad niyamaḥ iti nidarśana nirdeśaḥ yathā ca savāḥ sapta saurya ādayaḥ śataudana paryantāḥ veda antara udita tretāgni anabhisaṃbandhāt ātharvaṇa udita ekāgni abhisaṃbandhāt ca ātharvaṇikānām eva niyamyante tathā eva ayam api dharmaḥ svādhyāya viśeṣa saṃbandhāt tatra eva niyamyate
tasmāt api anavadyam vidyā ekatvam
darśayati ca
darśayati ca vidyā eka tvam sarva vedānteṣu vedya eka tva upadeśāt sarve vedāḥ yat padam āmananti iti tathā etam hi eva bahvṛcāḥ mahati ukthe mīmāṃsante etam agnau adhvaryavaḥ etam mahāvrate chandogāḥ iti ca
tathā mahat bhayam vajram udyatam iti kāṭhake uktasya īśvara guṇasya bhaya hetu tvasya taittirīyake bheda darśana nindāyai parāmarśaḥ dṛśyate yadā hi eva eṣa etasmin udaram antaram kurute
atha tasya bhayam bhavati
tat tu eva bhayam viduṣaḥ manvānasya iti
tathā vājasaneyake prādeśa mātra saṃpāditasya vaiśvānarasya chāndogye siddha vat upādānam yaḥ tu etam evam prādeśa mātram abhivimānam ātmānam vaiśvānaram upāste iti
tathā sarva vedānta pratyaya tvena anyatra vihitānām uktha ādīnām anyatra upāsana vidhānāya upādānāt prāya darśana nyāyena upāsanānām api sarva vedānta pratyaya tva siddhiḥ
upasaṃhāraḥ rtha abhedāt vidhi śeṣa vat samāne ca
upasaṃhāra adhikaraṇam
idam prayojana sūtram
sthite ca evam sarva vedānta pratyaya tve sarva vijñānānām anyatra uditānām vijñāna guṇānām anyatra api samāne vijñāne upasaṃhāraḥ bhavati
artha abhedāt yaḥ eva hi teṣām guṇānām ekatra arthaḥ viśiṣṭa vijñāna upakāraḥ saḥ eva anyatra api
ubhayatra api hi tat eva ekam vijñānam
tasmāt upasaṃhāraḥ
vidhi śeṣa vat yathā vidhi śeṣāṇām agnihotra ādi dharmāṇām tat eva ekam agnihotra ādi karma sarvatra iti artha abhedāt upasaṃharaṇam
evam iha api
yadi hi vijñāna bhedaḥ bhavet tatas vijñāna antara nibaddha tvāt guṇānām prakṛti vikṛti bhāva abhāvāt ca na syāt upasaṃhāraḥ
vijñāna eka tve tu na evam iti
asya eva tu prayojana sūtrasya prapañcaḥ sarva abhedāt iti ārabhya bhaviṣyati
anyathātvam śabdāt iti ced na aviśeṣāt
anyathātva adhikaraṇam
vājasaneyake te ha devāḥ ūcuḥ hanta asurān yajñe udgīthena atyayāma iti te ha vācam ūcuḥ tvam naḥ udgāye iti prakramya vāc ādīn prāṇān asura pāpma viddha tvena ninditvā mukhya prāṇa parigrahaḥ paṭhyate atha ha imam āsanyam prāṇam ūcuḥ tvam naḥ udgāya iti tathā iti tebhyaḥ eṣa prāṇaḥ udagāyat iti
tathā chāndogye pi tat ha devāḥ udgītham ājahruḥ anena enān abhibhaviṣyāmaḥ iti prakramya itarān prāṇān asura pāpma viddha tvena ninditvā tathā eva mukhya prāṇa parigrahaḥ paṭhyate atha ha yaḥ eva ayam mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ tam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti
ubhayatra api ca prāṇa praśaṃsayā prāṇa vidyā vidhiḥ adhyavasīyate
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim atra vidyā bhedaḥ syāt āhosvit vidyā eka tvam iti
kim tāvat prāptam pūrveṇa nyāyena vidyā ekatvam iti
nanu na yuktam vidyā eka tvam prakrama bhedāt
anyathā hi prakramante vājasaneyinaḥ anyathā chandogāḥ tvam naḥ udgāye iti vājasaneyinaḥ udgīthasya kartṛ tvena prāṇam āmananti chandogāḥ tu udgītha tvena tam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti tat katham vidyā ekatvam syāt iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ
na hi etāvatā viśeṣeṇa vidyā eka tvam apagacchati aviśeṣasya api bahutarasya pratīyamāna tvāt
tathā hi deva asura saṃgrāma upakrama tvam asura atyaya abhiprāyaḥ udgītha upanyāsaḥ vāc ādi saṃkīrtanam tad nindayā mukhya prāṇa vyapāśrayaḥ tad vīryāt ca asura vidhvaṃsanam aśma loṣṭa nidarśanena iti evam bahavaḥ rthāḥ ubhayatra api aviśiṣṭāḥ pratīyante
vājasaneyake ca udgītha sāmānādhikaraṇyam prāṇasya śrutam eṣaḥ u vai udgīthaḥ iti
tasmāt chāndogye pi kartṛ tvam lakṣayitavyam
tasmāt ca vidyā eka tvam iti
na vā prakaraṇa bhedāt paraḥ varīyaḥ tva ādi vat
na vā vidyā eka tvam atra nyāyyam
vidyā bhedaḥ eva atra nyāyyaḥ
kasmāt
prakaraṇa bhedāt prakrama bhedāt iti arthaḥ
tathā hi iha prakrama bhedaḥ dṛśyate chāndogye tāvat om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti evam udgītha avayavasya oṃkārasya upāsya tvam prastutya rasatama tva ādi guṇa upavyākhyānam tatra kṛtvā atha khalu etasya eva akṣarasya upavyākhyānam bhavati iti punar api tam eva udgītha avayavam oṃkāram anuvartya deva asura ākhyāyikā dvāreṇa tam prāṇam udgītham upāsāṃcakrire iti āha
tatra yadi udgītha śabdena sakalā bhaktiḥ abhipreyeta tasyāḥ ca kartā udgātā ṛtvij tatas upakramaḥ ca uparudhyeta lakṣaṇā ca prasajyeta
upakrama tantreṇa ca ekasmin vākye upasaṃhāreṇa bhavitavyam
tasmāt atra tāvat udgītha avayave oṃkāre prāṇa dṛṣṭiḥ upadiśyate vājasaneyake tu udgītha śabdena avayava grahaṇe kāraṇa abhāvāt sakalā eva bhaktiḥ āvedyate
tvam naḥ udgāye iti api tasyāḥ kartā udgātā ṛtvij prāṇa tvena nirūpyate iti prasthāna antaram
yat api tatra udgītha sāmānādhikaraṇyam prāṇasya tat api udgātṛ tvena eva didarśayiṣitasya prāṇasya sarva ātma tva pratipādana artham iti na vidyā ekatvam āvahati
sakala bhakti viṣayaḥ eva ca tatra api udgītha śabdaḥ iti vaiṣamyam
na ca prāṇasya udgātṛ tvam asaṃbhavena hetunā parityajyate udgītha bhāva vat udgātṛ bhāvasya api upāsana artha tvena upadiśyamāna tvāt
prāṇa vīryeṇa eva ca udgātā audgātram karoti iti na asti asaṃbhavaḥ
tathā ca tatra eva śrāvitam vācā ca hi eva sa prāṇena ca udagāyat iti
na ca vivakṣita artha bhede vagamyamāne vākya chāyā anukāra mātreṇa samāna artha tvam adhyavasātum yuktam
tathā hi abhyudaya vākye paśu kāma vākye ca tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet ye madhyamāḥ syuḥ tān agnaye dātre puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam kuryāt ityādi nirdeśa sāmye upakrama bhedāt abhyudaya vākye devatā apanayaḥ dhī avasitaḥ paśu kāma vākye tu yāga vidhiḥ tathā iha api upakrama bhedāt vidyā bhedaḥ
parovarīyaḥ tva ādi vat yathā paramātma dṛṣṭi adhyāsa sāmye ākāśaḥ hi eva ebhyaḥ jyāyān ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam saḥ eṣa paraḥ varīyān udgīthaḥ saḥ eṣaḥ nantaḥ iti paraḥ varīyaḥ tva guṇa viśiṣṭam udgītha upāsanam akṣi āditya ādi gata hiraṇya śmaśru tva ādi guṇa viśiṣṭa udgītha upāsanāt bhinnam
na ca itaretara guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ekasyām api śākhāyām tadvat śākhā antara stheṣu api evaṃjātīyakeṣu upāsaneṣu iti
saṃjñātaḥ ced tat uktam asti tu tat api
athā ucyeta saṃjñā eka tvāt vidyā eka tvam atra nyāyyam ekā saṃjñā iti tat api nā upapadyate
uktam hi  etat na  vā  prakaraṇa Cp bhedāt SBM paras  varīyaḥ Cp tva Cp ādi Cp vat
iti
tat eva ca atra nyāyyataram śruti akṣara anugatam hi
tat saṃjñā eka tvam tu śruti akṣara bāhyam udgītha śabda mātra yogāt laukikaiḥ vyavahartṛbhiḥ upacaryate
asti ca etat saṃjñā eka tvam prasiddha bhedeṣu api paraḥ varīyaḥ tva ādi upāsaneṣu udgītha vidyā iti
tathā prasiddha bhedānām api agnihotra darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīnām kāṭhaka eka grantha paripaṭhitānām kāṭhaka saṃjñā eka tvam dṛśyate tathā iha api bhaviṣyati
yatra tu na asti kaścid evaṃjātīyakaḥ bheda hetuḥ tatra bhavatu saṃjñā eka tvāt vidyā eka tvam yathā saṃvarga vidyā ādiṣu
vyāpteḥ ca samañjasam
vyāptyā adhikaraṇam
om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti atra akṣara udgītha śabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇye śrūyamāṇe adhyāsa apavāda eka tva viśeṣaṇa pakṣāṇām pratibhāsanāt katamaḥ u tra pakṣaḥ nyāyyaḥ syāt iti vicāraḥ
tatra adhyāsaḥ nāma dvayoḥ vastunoḥ anivartitāyām eva anyatara buddhau anyatara buddhiḥ adhyasyate
yasmin itara buddhiḥ adhyasyate anuvartate eva tasmin tad buddhiḥ adhyasta itara buddhau api yathā nāmni brahma buddhau adhyasyamānāyām api anuvartate eva nāma buddhiḥ na brahma buddhyāḥ nivartate yathā vā pratimā ādiṣu viṣṇu ādi buddhi adhyāsaḥ evam iha api akṣare udgītha buddhiḥ adhyasyeta udgīthe vā akṣara buddhiḥ iti
apavādaḥ nāma yatra kasmiṃścid vastuni pūrva niviṣṭāyām mithyā buddhau niścitāyām paścāt upajāyamānā yathārthā buddhiḥ pūrva niviṣṭāyāḥ mithyā buddheḥ nivartikā bhavati yathā deha indriya saṃghāte ātma buddhiḥ ātmani eva ātma buddhyā paścāt bhāvinyā tat tvam asi iti anayā yathārtha buddhyā nivartyate yathā vā diś bhrānti buddhiḥ diś yāthātmya buddhyā nivartyate evam iha api akṣara buddhyā udgītha buddhiḥ nivartyeta udgītha buddhyā v
eka tvam tu akṣara udgītha śabdayoḥ anatirikta artha vṛtti tvam yathā dvijottamaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhūmidevaḥ iti
viśeṣaṇam punar sarva veda vyāpinaḥ om iti etasya akṣarasya grahaṇa prasaṅge audgātra viśeṣasya samarpaṇam yathā nīlam yat utpalam tat ānaya iti evam iha api udgīthaḥ yaḥ oṃkāraḥ tam upāsīta iti
evam etasmin sāmānādhikaraṇya vākye vimṛśyamāne ete pakṣāḥ pratibhānti
tatra anyatama nirdhāraṇa kāraṇa abhāvāt anirdhāraṇa prāptau idam ucyate vyāpteḥ ca samañjasam iti
ca śabdaḥ yam tuśabda sthāna niveśī pakṣa traya vyāvartana prayojanaḥ
tat iha trayaḥ pakṣāḥ sāvadyāḥ iti paryudasyante
viśeṣaṇa pakṣaḥ eva ekaḥ niravadyaḥ iti upādīyate
tatra adhyāse tāvat yā buddhiḥ itaratra adhyasyate tad śabdasya lakṣaṇa āvṛtti tvam prasajyeta tad phalam ca kalpyeta
śrūyate eva phalam āpayitā ha vai kāmānām bhavati ityādi iti ced tat na tasya anya phala tvāt
āpti ādi dṛṣṭi phalam hi tat na udgītha adhyāsa phalam
apavāde pi samānaḥ phala abhāvaḥ
mithyājñāna nivṛttiḥ phalam iti ced na
puruṣa artha upayoga anavagamāt
na ca kadācid api oṃkārāt okāra buddhiḥ nivarteta udgīthāt vā udgītha buddhiḥ
na ca idam vākyam vastu tattva pratipādana param upāsanā vidhi paratvāt
na api ekatva pakṣaḥ saṃgacchate
niṣprayojanam hi tadā śabda dvaya uccāraṇam syāt ekena eva vivakṣita artha samarpaṇāt
na ca hautra viṣaye ādhvaryava viṣaye vā akṣare oṃkāra śabda vācye udgītha śabda prasiddhiḥ asti nā api sakalāyām sāmnaḥ dvitīyāyām bhaktau udgītha śabda vācyāyām oṃkāra śabda prasiddhiḥ yena anatirikta artha tā syāt
pariśeṣāt viśeṣaṇa pakṣaḥ parigṛhyate vyāpteḥ sarva veda sādhāraṇyāt
sarva vyāpi akṣaram iha mā prasañji iti atas udgītha śabdena akṣaram viśeṣyate katham nāma udgītha avayava bhūtaḥ oṃkāraḥ gṛhyeta iti
nanu asmin api pakṣe samānā lakṣaṇā udgītha śabdasya avayava lakṣaṇa artha tvāt
satyam evam etat
lakṣaṇāyām api tu saṃnikarṣa viprakarṣau bhavataḥ eva
adhyāsa pakṣe hi artha antara buddhiḥ artha antare nikṣipyate iti viprakṛṣṭā lakṣaṇā viśeṣaṇa pakṣe tu avayavi vacanena śabdena avayavaḥ samarpyate iti saṃnikṛṣṭā
samudāyeṣu hi pravṛttāḥ śabdāḥ avayaveṣu api vartamānāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ paṭa grāma ādiṣu
atas ca vyāpteḥ hetoḥ om iti etat akṣaram iti etasya udgītham iti etat viśeṣaṇam iti samañjasam etat niravadyam iti arthaḥ
sarva abhedāt anyatra ime
sarva abheda adhikaraṇam
vājinām chandogānām ca prāṇa saṃvāde śraiṣṭhya guṇa anvitasya prāṇasya upāsya tvam uktam
vāc ādayaḥ pi hi tatra vasiṣṭha tva ādi guṇa anvitāḥ uktāḥ
te ca guṇāḥ prāṇe punar pratyarpitāḥ yat vai aham vasiṣṭha asmi tvam tat vasiṣṭhaḥ u si ityādinā
anyeṣām api tu śākhinām koṣītaki prabhṛtīnām prāṇa saṃvādeṣu atha atas niḥśreyasa ādānam etāḥ ha vai devatāḥ ahaṃśreyase vivadamānāḥ iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu prāṇasya śraiṣṭhyam uktam na tu ime guṇāḥ uktāḥ
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ime vasiṣṭha tva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ anyatra api asyeran uta na asyeran iti
tatra prāptam tāvat na āsyeran iti
kutas
evam śabda saṃyogāt
atha u yaḥ evam vidvān prāṇe niḥśreyasam viditvā iti hi tatra tatra evam śabdena vedyam vastu nivedyate
evam śabdaḥ ca saṃnihita avalambanaḥ na śākhā antara paripaṭhitam evaṃjātīyakam guṇa jātam śaknoti nivedayitum
tasmāt sva prakaraṇa sthaiḥ eva guṇaiḥ nirākāṅkṣatvam iti evam prāpte pratyāha asyeran ime guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ vasiṣṭha tva ādayaḥ anyatra api
kutas
sarva abhedāt sarvatra eva tat eva ekam prāṇa vijñānam abhinnam pratyabhijñāyate prāṇa saṃvāda ādi sārūpyāt
abhede ca vijñānasya katham ime guṇāḥ kvacid uktāḥ anyatra na asyeran
nanu evam śabdaḥ tatra tatra bhedena evaṃjātīyakam guṇa jātam vedya tvāya samarpayati iti uktam
atra ucyate yadi api kauṣītaki brāhmaṇa gatena evam śabdena vājasaneyi brāhmaṇa gatam guṇa jātam a saṃśabditam a saṃnihita tvāt tathā api tasmin eva vijñāne vājasaneyi brāhmaṇa gatena evam śabdena tat saṃśabditam iti na para śākhā gatam api abhinna vijñāna avabaddham guṇa jātam sva śākhā gatāt viśiṣyate
na ca evam sati śruta hāniḥ aśruta kalpanā vā bhavati
ekasyām api hi śākhāyām śrutāḥ guṇāḥ śrutāḥ eva sarvatra bhavanti guṇavataḥ bheda abhāvāt
na hi devadattaḥ śaurya ādi guṇa tvena sva deśe prasiddhaḥ deśa antaram gataḥ tad deśyaiḥ avibhāvita śaurya ādi guṇaḥ a pi a tad guṇaḥ bhavati
yathā ca tatra paricaya viśeṣāt deśa antare pi devadatta guṇāḥ vibhāvyante evam abhiyoga viśeṣāt śākhā antare pi upāsyāḥ guṇāḥ śākhā antare pi asyeran
tasmāt eka pradhāna saṃbaddhāḥ dharmāḥ ekatra api ucyamānāḥ sarvatra eva upasaṃhartavyāḥ iti
ānanda ādayaḥ pradhānasya
ānanda ādi adhikaraṇam
brahma svarūpa pratipādana parāsu śrutiṣu ānanda rūpa tvam vijñāna ghana tvam sarvagata tvam sarva ātma tvam iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ brahmaṇaḥ dharmāḥ kvacid kecid śrūyante
teṣu saṃśayaḥ kim ānanda ādayaḥ brahma dharmāḥ yatra yāvantaḥ śrūyante tāvantaḥ eva tatra pratipattavyāḥ kim vā sarve sarvatra iti
tatra yathāśruti vibhāgam dharma pratipattau prāptāyām idam ucyate ānanda ādayaḥ pradhānasya brahmaṇaḥ dharmāḥ sarve sarvatra pratipattavyāḥ
kasmāt
sarva abhedāt eva sarvatra hi tat eva ekam pradhānam viśeṣyam brahma na bhidyate
tasmāt sārvatrika tvam brahma dharmāṇām tena eva pūrva adhikaraṇa uditena devadatta śaurya ādi nidarśanena
nanu evam sati priya śiraḥ tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ sarve sarvatra saṃkīryeran
tathā hi taittirīyake ānanda mayam ātmānam prakramya āmnāyate tasya priyam eva śiraḥ
modaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ
pramodaḥ uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ
ānandaḥ ātmā
brahma puccham pratiṣṭhāḥ iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
priya śiraḥ tva ādi aprāptiḥ upacaya apacayau hi bhede
priyaśiraḥ tva ādīnām dharmāṇām taittirīyake āmnātānām na asti anyatra prāptiḥ yatkāraṇam priyam modaḥ pramodaḥ ānandaḥ iti ete paraspara apekṣayā bhoktṛ antara apekṣayā ca upacita apacita rūpāḥ upalabhyante
upacaya apacayau ca sati bhede saṃbhavataḥ
nirbhedam tu brahma ekam eva advitīyam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
na ca ete priya śiraḥ tva ādayaḥ brahma dharmāḥ
kośa dharmāḥ tu ete iti upadiṣṭam asmābhiḥ ānanda mayaḥ bhyāsāt iti atra
api ca parasmin brahmaṇi cittāvatāra upāya mātra tvena ete parikalpyante na draṣṭavya tvena
evam api sutarām anyatra aprāptiḥ priya śiraḥ tva ādīnām
brahma dharmān tu etān kṛtvā nyāya mātram idam ācāryeṇa pradarśitam priyaśiraḥ tva ādi aprāptiḥ iti
sa ca nyāyaḥ anyeṣu niściteṣu brahma dharmeṣu upāsanāya upadiśyamāneṣu netavyaḥ saṃyat vāma tva ādiṣu satya kāma tva ādiṣu ca
teṣu hi sati api upāsyasya brahmaṇaḥ eka tve prakrama bhedāt upāsanā bhede sati na anyonya dharmāṇām anyonyatra prāptiḥ
yathā ca dve nāryau ekam nṛpatim upāsāte chatreṇa anyā cāmareṇa anyā tatra upāsya eka tve upāsana bhedaḥ dharma vyavasthā ca bhavati evam iha api iti
upacita apacita guṇa tvam hi sati bheda vyavahāre saguṇe brahmaṇi upapadyate na nirguṇe parasmin brahmaṇi
atas na satya kāma tva ādīnām dharmāṇām kvacid śrutānām sarvatra prāptiḥ iti arthaḥ
itare tu artha sāmānyāt
itare tu ānanda ādayaḥ dharmāḥ brahma svarūpa pratipādanāya eva ucyamānāḥ artha sāmānyāt pratipādyasya brahmaṇaḥ dharmiṇaḥ ekatvāt sarve sarvatra pratīyeran iti vaiṣamyam pratipatti mātra prayojanāḥ hi te iti
ādhyānāya prayojana abhāvāt
ādhyāna adhikaraṇam
kāṭhake hi paṭhyate indriyebhyaḥ parāḥ hi arthāḥ arthebhyaḥ ca param manaḥ
manasaḥ tu parā buddhiḥ iti ārabhya puruṣāt na param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ime sarve eva artha ādayaḥ tatas tatas paratvena pratipādyante uta puruṣaḥ eva ebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ paraḥ pratipādyate iti
tatra tāvat sarveṣām eva eṣām para tvena pratipādanam iti bhavati matiḥ
tathā hi śrūyate idam asmāt param idam asmāt param iti
nanu bahuṣu artheṣu paratvena vākya bhedaḥ syāt
na eṣa doṣaḥ vākya bahutva upapatteḥ
bahūni eva hi etāni vākyāni prabhavanti bahūn arthān paratva upetān pratipādayitum
tasmāt pratyekam eṣām paratva pratipādanam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ puruṣaḥ eva hi ebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ paraḥ pratipādyate iti yuktam na pratyekam eṣām paratva pratipādanam
kasmāt
prayojana abhāvāt
na hi itareṣu paratvena pratipanneṣu kiṃcid prayojanam dṛśyate śrūyate vā
puruṣe tu indriya ādibhyaḥ parasmin sarva anartha vrāta atīte pratipanne dṛśyate prayojanam mokṣa siddhiḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ nicāyya tat mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti
api ca para pratiṣedhena kāṣṭhā śabdena ca puruṣa viṣayam ādaram darśayan puruṣa pratipatti arthā eva pūrva apara pravāha uktiḥ iti darśayati
ādhyānāya iti ādhyāna pūrvakāya samyak darśanāya iti arthaḥ
samyak darśana artham eva hi iha ādhyānam upadiśyate na tu ādhyānam eva svapradhānam
ātma śabdāt ca
itas ca puruṣa pratipatti arthā eva iyam indriya ādi pravāha uktiḥ yatkāraṇam eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍha utmā na prakāśate
dṛśyate tu agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ iti prakṛtam puruṣam ātmā iti āha
atas ca anātma tvam itareṣām vivakṣitam iti gamyate
tasya eva ca durvijñāna tām saṃskṛta mati gamya tām ca darśayati
tad vijñānāya eva ca yacchet vāc manasī prājñaḥ iti ādhyānam vidadhāti
tat vyākhyātam ānumānikam api ekeṣām iti atra
evam aneka prakāraḥ āśaya atiśayaḥ śruteḥ puruṣe lakṣyate na itareṣu
api ca saḥ dhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti ukte kim tat adhvanaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām indriya ādi anukramaṇāt parama pada pratipatti arthaḥ eva ayam āmnāyaḥ iti avasīyate
ātma gṛhītiḥ itaravat uttarāt
ātma gṛhī iti adhikaraṇam
aitareyake śrūyate ātmā vai idam ekaḥ eva agre āsīt na anyat kiṃcana miṣat saḥ īkṣata lokān nu sṛjai iti saḥ imān lokān asṛjata ambhaḥ marīcīḥ maramā apaḥ ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim paraḥ eva ātmā iha ātma śabdena abhilapyate uta anyaḥ kaścid iti
kim tāvat prāptam
na paramātmā iha ātma śabda abhilapyaḥ bhavitum arhati iti
kasmāt
vākya anvaya darśanāt
nanu vākya anvayaḥ sutarām paramātma viṣayaḥ dṛśyate prāk utpatteḥ ātma ekatva avadhāraṇāt īkṣaṇa pūrvaka sraṣṭṛ tva vacanāt ca
na iti ucyate loka sṛṣṭi vacanāt paramātmani hi sraṣṭari parigṛhyamāṇe mahābhūta sṛṣṭiḥ ādau vaktavyā
loka sṛṣṭiḥ tu iha ādau ucyate
lokāḥ ca mahābhūta saṃniveśa viśeṣāḥ
tathā ca ambhaḥ prabhṛtīn loka tvena eva nirbravīti adaḥ mbhaḥ pareṇa divam ityādinā
loka sṛṣṭiḥ ca parameśvara dhiṣṭhitena apareṇa kenacid īśvareṇa kriyate iti śruti smṛtyoḥ upalabhyate
tathā hi śrutiḥ bhavati ātmā eva idam agre āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ ityādyā
smṛtiḥ api sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣaḥ ucyate
ādikartā sa bhūtānām brahma agre samavartata iti
aitareyiṇaḥ pi atha atas retasaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ prajāpateḥ retaḥ devāḥ iti atra pūrvasmin prakaraṇe prajāpati kartṛkām vicitrām sṛṣṭim āmananti
ātma śabdaḥ u pi tasmin prayujyamānaḥ dṛśyate ātmā eva idam agre āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ iti atra
ekatva avadhāraṇam api prāk utpatteḥ sva vikāra apekṣam upapadyate
īkṣaṇam api tasya cetana tva abhyupagamāt upapannam
api ca tābhyaḥ gām ānayat tābhyaḥ śvam ānayat tābhyaḥ puruṣam ānayat tāḥ abruvan iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyān vyāpāra viśeṣaḥ laukikeṣu viśeṣavatsu ātmasu prasiddhaḥ iha anugamyate
tasmāt viśeṣavān eva kaścid iha ātmā syāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ paraḥ eva ātmā iha ātma śabdena gṛhyate
itaravat yathā itareṣu sṛṣṭi śravaṇeṣu tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti evamādiṣu parasya ātmanaḥ grahaṇam yathā ca itarasmin laukika ātma śabda prayoge pratyagātmā eva mukhyaḥ ātma śabdena gṛhyate tathā iha api bhavitum arhati
yatra tu ātmā eva idam agre āsīt iti evamādau puruṣavidhaḥ iti evamādi viśeṣaṇa antaram śrūyate bhavet tatra viśeṣavataḥ ātmanaḥ grahaṇam
atra punar paramātma grahaṇa anuguṇam eva viśeṣaṇam api uttaram upalabhyate saḥ īkṣata lokān nu sṛjai iti saḥ imān lokān asṛjata iti evamādi
tasmāt tasya eva grahaṇam iti nyāyyam
anvayāt iti ced syāt avadhāraṇāt
vākya anvaya darśanāt na paramātma grahaṇam iti punar yat uktam tat parihartavyam iti atra ucyate syāt avadhāraṇāt iti
bhavet upapannam paramātmanaḥ grahaṇam
kasmāt
avadhāraṇāt
paramātma grahaṇe hi prāk utpatteḥ ātma ekatva avadhāraṇam āñjasam avakalpate
anyathā hi anāñjasam tat parikalpyeta
loka sṛṣṭi vacanam tu śruti antara prasiddha mahābhūta sṛṣṭi anantaram iti yojayiṣyāmi
yathā tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti etat śruti antara prasiddha viyat vāyu sṛṣṭi anantaram iti ayūyujam evam iha api
śruti antara prasiddhaḥ hi samāna viṣayaḥ viśeṣaḥ śruti antareṣu upasaṃhartavyaḥ bhavati
yaḥ pi ayam vyāpāra viśeṣa anugamaḥ tābhyaḥ gām ānayat iti evamādiḥ saḥ pi vivakṣita artha avadhāraṇa ānuguṇyena eva grahītavyaḥ
na hi ayam sakalaḥ kathā prabandhaḥ vivakṣitaḥ iti śakyate vaktum tad pratipattau puruṣa artha abhāvāt
brahma ātmatvam tu iha vivakṣitam
tathā hi ambhaḥ prabhṛtīnām lokānām lokapālānām ca agni ādīnām sṛṣṭim śiṣṭvā karaṇāni karaṇa āyatanam ca śarīram upadiśya saḥ eva sraṣṭā katham nu idam mat ṛte syāt iti vīkṣya idam śarīram praviveśa iti darśayati saḥ etam eva sīmānam vidārya etayā dvārā prāpadyate iti
punar ca yadi vācā abhivyāhṛtam yadi prāṇena abhiprāṇitam iti evamādinā karaṇa vyāpāra vivecana pūrvakam atha kaḥ ham iti vīkṣya saḥ etam eva puruṣam brahma tatamam apaśyat iti brahma ātmatva darśanam avadhārayati
tathā upariṣṭāt eṣa brahma eṣaḥ indraḥ ityādinā samastam bheda jātam saha mahābhūtaiḥ anukramya sarvam tat prajñā netram prajñāne pratiṣṭhitam prajñā netraḥ lokaḥ prajñā pratiṣṭhā prajñānam brahma iti brahma ātmatva darśanam eva avadhārayati
tasmāt iha ātma gṛhītiḥ iti anapavādam
aparā yojanā ātma gṛhītiḥ itaravat uttarāt
vājasaneyake katamaḥ ātmā iti yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ iti ātma śabdena upakramya tasya eva sarva saṅga vinirmukta tva pratipādanena brahma ātmatām avadhārayati
tathā hi upasaṃharati sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ bhayaḥ brahma iti
chāndogye tu sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti antareṇa eva ātma śabdam upakramya udarke saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti tādātmyam upadiśati
tatra saṃśayaḥ tulya ārtha tvam kim anayoḥ āmnānayoḥ syāt atulya ārtha tvam vā iti
atulya artha tvam iti tāvat prāptam atulya tvāt āmnānayoḥ
na hi āmnāna vaiṣamye sati artha sāmyam yuktam pratipattum āmnāna tantra tvāt artha parigrahasya
vājasaneyake ca ātma śabda upakramāt ātma tattva upadeśaḥ iti gamyate
chāndogye tu upakrama viparyayāt upadeśa viparyayaḥ
nanu chandogānām api asti udarke tādātmya upadeśaḥ iti uktam
satyam uktam upakrama tantra tvāt upasaṃhārasya tādātmya saṃpattiḥ sā iti manyate
tathā prāpte abhidhīyate ātma gṛhītiḥ sat eva somya idam agre āsīt iti atra chandogānām api bhavitum arhati
itaravat yathā katamaḥ ātmā iti atra vājasaneyinām ātma gṛhītiḥ tathā eva
kasmāt
uttarāt tādātmya upadeśāt
anvayāt iti ced avadhāraṇāt yat uktam upakrama anvayāt upakrame ca ātma śabda śravaṇa abhāvāt na ātma gṛhītiḥ iti tasya kaḥ parihāraḥ iti ced saḥ abhidhīyate syāt avadhāraṇāt iti
bhavet upapannā iha ātma gṛhītiḥ avadhāraṇāt
tathā hi yena a śrutam śrutam bhavati a matam matam a vijñātam vijñātam iti eka vijñānena sarva vijñānam avadhārya tad saṃpipādayiṣayā sa devaḥ iti āha
tat ca ātma gṛhītau satyām saṃpadyate
anyathā hi yaḥ yam mukhyaḥ ātmā sa na vijñātaḥ iti na eva sarva vijñānam saṃpadyeta
tathā prāk utpatteḥ ekatva ādhāraṇam jīvasya ca ātma śabdena parāmarśaḥ svāpa avasthāyām ca tad svabhāva saṃpatti kathanam paricodanā pūrvakam ca punar punar tattvam asi iti avadhāraṇam iti ca sarvam etat tādātmya pratipādanāyām eva avakalpate na tādātmya saṃpādanāyām
na ca atra upakrama tantra tva upanyāsaḥ nyāyyaḥ
na hi upakrame ātmatva saṃkīrtanam anātmatva saṃkīrtanam vā asti
sāmānya upakramaḥ ca na vākyaśeṣa gatena viśeṣeṇa virudhyate viśeṣa ākaṅkṣi tvāt sāmānyasya
sat śabda arthaḥ ca paryālocyamānaḥ na mukhyāt ātmanaḥ nyaḥ saṃbhavati atas nyasya vastu jātasya ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ
āmnāna vaiṣamyam api na avaśyam artha vaiṣamyam āvahati āhara pātram pātram āhara iti evamādiṣu artha sāmye tad darśanāt
tasmāt evaṃjātīyakeṣu vākyeṣu pratipādana prakāra bhede pi pratipādya artha abhedaḥ iti siddham
kārya ākhyānāt apūrvam
kārya ākhyāna adhikaraṇam
chandogāḥ vājasaneyinaḥ ca prāṇa saṃvāde śva ādi maryādam prāṇasya annam āmnāya tasya eva āpaḥ vāsaḥ āmananti
anantaram ca chandogāḥ āmananti tasmāt vai etat a śiṣyantaḥ purastāt ca upariṣṭāt ca adbhiḥ paridadhati iti
vājasaneyinaḥ ca āmananti tad vidvāṃsaḥ śrotriyāḥ a śiṣyantaḥ ācāmanti aśitvā ca ācāmanti etam eva tat anam anagnam kurvantaḥ manyante tasmāt evaṃvid a śiṣyan ācāmet aśitvā ca ācāmet etam eva tat anam anagnam kurute iti
tatra ca ācamanam anagna tā cintanam ca prāṇasya pratīyate
tat kim ubhayam api vidhīyate uta ācamanam eva anagna tā cintanam eva iti vicāryate
kim tāvat prāptam
ubhayam api vidhīyate iti
kutas
ubhayasya api avagamyamāna tvāt
ubhayam api ca etat apūrva tvāt vidhi arham
athavā ācamanam eva vidhīyate
vispaṣṭā hi tasmin vidhi vibhaktiḥ tasmāt evaṃvid aśiṣyan ācāmet aśitvā ca ācāmet iti
tasya eva stuti artham anagna tā saṃkīrtanam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na ācamanasya vidheya tvam upapadyate kārya ākhyānāt prāptam eva hi idam kārya tvena ācamanam prāyatyā artham smṛti prasiddham anvākhyāyate
nanu iyam śrutiḥ tasyāḥ smṛteḥ mūlam syāt
na iti ucyate viṣaya nānātvāt
sāmānya viṣayā hi smṛtiḥ puruṣa mātra saṃbaddham prāyatyā artham ācamanam prāpayati
śrutiḥ tu prāṇa vidyā prakaraṇa paṭhitā tad viṣayam eva ācamanam vidadhatī vidadhyāt
na ca bhinna viṣayayoḥ śruti smṛtyoḥ mūla mūli bhāvaḥ
na ca iyam śrutiḥ prāṇa vidyā saṃyogi apūrvam ācamanam vidhāsyati iti śakyam āśrayitum pūrvasya eva puruṣa mātra saṃyoginaḥ ācamanasya iha pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt
atas eva ca na ubhaya vidhānam
ubhaya vidhāne ca vākyam bhidyeta
tasmāt prāptam eva ca ubhayatas ācamanam anūdya etam eva tat anam anagnam kurvantaḥ manyante iti prāṇasya anagna tā karaṇa saṃkalpaḥ anena vākyena ācamanīyāsu apsu prāṇa vidyā saṃbandhi tvena apūrvaḥ upadiśyate
na ca ayam anagna tā vādaḥ ācamana stuti arthaḥ iti nyāyyam ācamanasya avidheya tvāt
svayam ca anagna tā saṃkalpasya vidheya tva pratīteḥ
na ca evam sati ekasya ācamanasya ubhaya artha tā abhyupagatā bhavati prāyatya artha tā paridhāna artha tā ca iti kriyā antara tva abhyupagamāt kriyā antaram eva hi ācamanam nāma prāyatya artham puruṣasya abhyupagamyate
tadīyāsu tu apsu vāsaḥ saṃkalpanam nāma kriyā antaram eva paridhāna artham prāṇasya abhyupagamyate iti anavadyam
api ca yat idam kiṃca śvabhyaḥ ā kṛmibhyaḥ ā kīṭa pataṃgebhyaḥ tat te nnam iti atra tāvat na sarva anna abhyavahāraḥ codyate iti śakyam vaktum aśabda tvāt aśakya tvāt ca
sarvam tu prāṇasya annam iti iyam anna dṛṣṭiḥ codyate
tad sāhacaryāt ca āpaḥ vāsaḥ iti atra api na apām ācamanam codyate
prasiddhāsu eva tu ācamanīyāsu apsu paridhāna dṛṣṭiḥ ca udyate iti yuktam
na hi ardhavaiśasam saṃbhavati
api ca ācāmanti iti vartamāna apadeśi tvāt na ayam śabdaḥ vidhi kṣamaḥ
nanu manyante iti api samānam vartamāna apadeśi tvam
satyam eva tat
avaśya vidheye tu anyatarasmin vāsaḥ kārya ākhyānāt apām vāsaḥ saṃkalpanam eva apūrvam vidhīyate
na ācamanam
pūrvavat hi tat iti upapāditam
yat api uktam vispaṣṭā ca ācamane vidhi vibhaktiḥ iti tat api pūrvavat tvena eva ācamanasya pratyuktam
atas eva ācamanasya a vidhitsita tvāt etam eva tad anam anagnam kurvantaḥ manyante iti atra eva kāṇvāḥ paryavasyanti na āmananti tasmāt evaṃvid ityādi
tasmāt mādhyaṃdinānām api pāṭhe ācamana anuvādena evaṃvid tvam eva prakṛta prāṇa vāsaḥ vid tvam vidhīyate iti pratipattavyam
yaḥ u pi ayam abhyupagamaḥ kvacid ācamanam vidhīyatām kvacid vāsaḥ vijñānam iti saḥ u pi na sādhuḥ āpaḥ vāsaḥ iti ādikāyāḥ vākya pravṛtteḥ sarvatra aikarūpyāt
tasmāt vāsaḥ vijñānam eva iha vidhīyate na ācamanam iti nyāyyam
samānaḥ evam ca abhedāt
samāna adhikaraṇam
vājasaneyi śākhāyām agnirahasye śāṇḍilya nāma aṅkitā vidyā vijñātā
tatra ca guṇāḥ śrūyante saḥ ātmānam upāsīta manaḥ mayam prāṇa śarīram bhā rūpam iti evamādayaḥ
tasyām eva śākhāyām bṛhadāraṇyake punar paṭhyate manaḥ mayaḥ yam puruṣaḥ bhās satyaḥ tasmin antar hṛdaye yathā vrīhiḥ vā yavaḥ vā saḥ eṣa sarvasya īśānaḥ sarvasya adhipatiḥ sarvam idam praśāsti yat idam kiṃca iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iyam ekā vidyā agni rahasya bṛhat āraṇyakayoḥ guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ca uta dve ime vidye guṇa anupasaṃhāraḥ ca iti
kim tāvat prāptam
vidyā bhedaḥ guṇa vyavasthā ca iti
kutas
paunaruktya prasaṅgāt bhinnāsu hi śākhāsu adhyetṛ veditṛ bhedāt paunaruktya parihāram ālocya vidyā ekatvam adhyavasāya ekatra atiriktāḥ guṇāḥ itaratra upasaṃhriyante prāṇa saṃvāda ādiṣu iti uktam
ekasyām punar śākhāyām adhyetṛ veditṛ bheda abhāvāt aśakya parihāre paunaruktye na viprakraṣṭa deśa sthā ekā vidyā bhavitum arhati
na ca atra ekam āmnānam vidyā vidhāna artham aparam guṇa vidhāna artham iti vibhāgaḥ saṃbhavati
tadā hi atiriktāḥ eva guṇāḥ itaratra itaratra ca āmnāyeran na samānāḥ
samānāḥ api tu ubhayatra āmnāyante manaḥ maya tva ādayaḥ
tasmāt na anyonya guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ iti evam prāpte brūmahe yathā bhinnāsu śākhāsu vidyā ekatvam guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ca bhavati evam ekasyām api śākhāyām bhavitum arhati upāsya abhedāt
tat eva hi brahma manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇakam ubhayatra api upāsyam abhinnam pratyabhijānīmaḥ
upāsyam ca rūpam vidyāyāḥ
na ca vidyamāne rūpa abhede vidyā bhedam adhyavasātum śaknumaḥ
na api vidyā bhede guṇa vyavasthānam
nanu paunaruktya prasaṅgāt vidyā bhedaḥ dhī avasitaḥ
na iti ucyate artha vibhāga upapatteḥ ekam hi āmnānam vidyā vidhāna artham aparam guṇa vidhāna artham iti na kiṃcid na upapadyate
nanu evam sati yat apaṭhitam agnirahasye tat eva bṛhadāraṇyake paṭhitavyam saḥ eṣa sarvasya īśānaḥ ityādi
yat tu paṭhitam eva manaḥ mayaḥ ityādi tat na paṭhitavyam na eṣa doṣaḥ tad balena eva pradeśa antara paṭhita vidyā pratyabhijñānāt
samāna guṇa āmnānena hi viprakṛṣṭa deśām śāṇḍilya vidyām pratyabhijñāpya tasyām īśāna tva ādi upadiśyate
anyathā hi katham tasyām ayam guṇa vidhiḥ abhidhīyate
api ca aprāpta aṃśa upadeśena arthavati vākye saṃjāte prāpta aṃśa parāmarśasya nitya anuvāda tayā api upapadyamāna tvāt na tad balena pratyabhijñā upekṣitum śakyate
tasmāt atra samānāyām api śākhāyām vidyā eka tvam guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ ca iti upapannam
sambandhāt evam anyatra api
saṃbandha adhikaraṇam
bṛhadāraṇyake satyam brahma iti upakramya tat yat tat satyam asau saḥ ādityaḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ yaḥ ca ayam dakṣiṇe kṣan puruṣaḥ iti tasya eva satyasya brahmaṇaḥ adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca āyatana viśeṣam upadiśya vyāhṛti śarīra tvam ca saṃpādya dve upaniṣadau ādiśyete tasya upaniṣad ahar iti adhidaivatam tasya upaniṣad aham iti adhyātmam
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim avibhāgena eva ubhe api upaniṣadau ubhayatra anusaṃdhātavye uta vibhāgena ekā adhidaivatam ekā adhyātmam iti
tatra sūtreṇa eva upakramate yathā śāṇḍilya vidyāyām vibhāgena api adhītāyām guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ uktaḥ evam anyatra api evaṃjātīyake viṣaye bhavitum arhati eka vidyā abhisaṃbandhāt ekā hi iyam satya vidyā adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca adhītā upakrama abhedāt vyatiṣakta pāṭhāt ca
katham tasyām uditaḥ dharmaḥ tasyām eva na syāt
yaḥ hi ācārye kaścid anugamana ādiḥ ācāraḥ coditaḥ sa grāma gate raṇya gate ca tulya vat eva bhavati
tasmāt ubhayoḥ api upaniṣadoḥ ubhayatra prāptiḥ iti
evam prāpte pratividhatte
na vā viśeṣāt
na eva ubhayoḥ ubhayatra prāptiḥ
kasmāt
viśeṣāt upāsana sthāna viśeṣa upanibandhāt iti arthaḥ
katham sthāna viśeṣa upanibandhaḥ iti ucyate yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ iti hi ādhidaivikam puruṣam prakṛtya tasya upaniṣad ahar iti śrāvayati
yaḥ yam dakṣiṇe kṣan puruṣaḥ iti ca ādhyātmikam puruṣam prakṛtya tasya upaniṣad aham iti
tasya iti ca etat saṃnihita avalambanam sarvanāma
tasmāt āyatana viśeṣa vyapāśrayeṇa eva ete upaniṣadau upadiśyete
kutas ubhayoḥ ubhayatra prāptiḥ
nanu ekaḥ eva ayam adhidaivatam adhyātmam ca puruṣaḥ ekasya eva satyasya brahmaṇaḥ āyatana dvaya pratipādanāt
satyam evam etat
ekasya api tu avasthā viśeṣa upādānena eva upaniṣad viśeṣa upadeśāt tad avasthasya eva sā bhavitum arhati
asti ca ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ sati api ācārya svarūpa anapāye yat ācāryasya āsīnasya anuvartanam uktam na tat tiṣṭhataḥ bhavati
yat ca tiṣṭhataḥ uktam na tat āsīnasya iti
grāma araṇyayoḥ tu ācārya sva rūpa anapāyāt tad sva rūpa anubaddhasya ca dharmasya grāma araṇya kṛta viśeṣa abhāvāt ubhayatra tulyavat bhāvaḥ iti adṛṣṭāntaḥ saḥ
tasmāt vyavasthā anayoḥ upaniṣadoḥ
darśayati ca
api ca evaṃjātīyakānām dharmāṇām vyavasthā iti liṅga darśanam bhavati tasya etasya tat eva rūpam yat amuṣya rūpam yau amuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau yat nāma tat nāma iti
katham asya liṅga tvam iti tat ucyate akṣi āditya sthāna bheda bhinnān dharmān anyonyasmin anupasaṃhāryān paśyan iha atideśena āditya puruṣa gatān rūpa ādīn akṣi puruṣe upasaṃharati tasya etasya tat eva rūpam ityādinā
tasmāt vyavatiṣṭhete eva ete upaniṣadau iti nirṇayaḥ
sambhṛti dyu vyāpti api ca atas
saṃbhṛti adhikaraṇam
brahma jyeṣṭhā vīryā saṃbhṛtāni brahma agre jyeṣṭham divam ātatāna iti evam rāṇāyanīyānām khileṣu vīrya saṃbhṛti dyuniveśa prabhṛtayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ vibhūtayaḥ paṭhyante
teṣām eva ca upaniṣadi śāṇḍilya vidyā prabhṛtayaḥ brahma vidyāḥ paṭhyante
tāsu brahma vidyāsu tāḥ brahma vibhūtayaḥ upasaṃhriyeran na vā iti vicāraṇāyām brahma saṃbandhāt upasaṃhāra prāptau evam paṭhati
saṃbhṛti dyu vyāpti prabhṛtayaḥ vibhūtayaḥ śāṇḍilya vidyā prabhṛtiṣu na upasaṃhartavyāḥ atas eva ca āyatana viśeṣa yogāt
tathā hi śāṇḍilya vidyāyām hṛdaya āyatana tvam brahmaṇaḥ uktam eṣa me ātmā antar hṛdaye iti
tadvat eva dahara vidyāyām api daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma daharaḥ smin antar ākāśaḥ iti
upakosala vidyāyām tu akṣi āyatana tvam yaḥ eṣaḥ u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti
evam tatra tatra tat tat ādhyātmikam āyatanam etāsu vidyāsu pratīyate
ādhidaivikyaḥ tu etāḥ vibhūtayaḥ saṃbhṛti dyu vyāpti prabhṛtayaḥ
tāsām kutas etāsu prāptiḥ
nanu etāsu api ādhidaivikyaḥ vibhūtayaḥ śrūyante jyāyān divaḥ jyāyān ebhyaḥ lokebhyaḥ eṣaḥ u eva bhāmanīḥ eṣa hi sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti yāvān vā ayam ākāśaḥ tāvān eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśe ubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī antar eva samāhite iti evamādyāḥ
santi ca anyāḥ āyatana viśeṣa hīnāḥ api iha brahma vidyāḥ ṣoḍaśa kalā ādyāḥ satyam evam etat
tathā api atra vidyate viśeṣaḥ saṃbhṛti ādi anupasaṃhāra hetuḥ samāna guṇa āmnānena hi pratyupasthāpitāsu viprakṛṣṭa deśāsu api vidyāsu viprakṛṣṭa deśa guṇāḥ upasaṃhriyeran iti yuktam
saṃbhṛti ādayaḥ tu śāṇḍilya ādi vākya gocarāḥ ca guṇāḥ paraspara vyāvṛtta svarūpa tvāt na pradeśa antara varti vidyā pratyupasthāpana kṣamāḥ
na ca brahma saṃbandha mātreṇa pradeśa antara varti vidyā pratyupasthāpanam iti ucyate vidyā bhede pi tad upapatteḥ
ekam api hi brahma vibhūti bhedaiḥ anekadhā upāsyate iti sthitiḥ paraḥ varīyaḥ tva ādi vat bheda darśanāt
tasmāt vīryasaṃbhṛti ādīnām śāṇḍilyavidyā ādiṣu anupasaṃhāraḥ iti
puruṣa vidyāyām iva ca itareṣām an āmnānāt
puruṣa vidyā adhikaraṇam
asti tāṇḍinām paiṅginām ca rahasyabrāhmaṇe puruṣa vidyā
tatra puruṣaḥ yajñaḥ kalpitaḥ
tadīyam āyuḥ tredhā vibhajya savana trayam kalpitam
aśiśiṣa ādīni ca dīkṣā ādi bhāvena kalpitāni
anye ca dharmāḥ tatra samadhigatāḥ āśīḥ mantra prayoga ādayaḥ
taittirīyakāḥ api kaṃcid puruṣa yajñam kalpayanti tasya evaṃviduṣaḥ yajñasya ātmā yajamānaḥ śraddhā patnī iti etena anuvākena
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim itaratra uktāḥ puruṣa yajñasya dharmāḥ taittirīyakeṣu upasaṃhartavyāḥ kim vā na upasaṃhartavyāḥ iti
puruṣa yajña tva aviśeṣāt upasaṃhāra prāptau ācakṣmahe na upasaṃhartavyāḥ iti
kasmāt
tad rūpa pratyabhijñāna abhāvāt
tat āha ācāryaḥ puruṣa vidyāyām iva iti yathā ekeṣām śākhinām tāṇḍinām paiṅginām ca puruṣa vidyāyām āmnānam na evam itareṣām taittirīyāṇām āmnānam asti
teṣām hi itara vilakṣaṇam eva yajña saṃpādanam dṛśyate patnī yajamāna vedi veda barhiḥ yūpa ājya paśu ṛtvij ādi anukramaṇāt
yat api savana saṃpādanam tat api itara vilakṣaṇam eva yat prātar madhyaṃdina sāyam ca tāni iti
yat api kiṃcid maraṇa avabhṛtha tva ādi sāmānyam tat api alpīyaḥ tvāt bhūyasā vailakṣaṇyena abhibhūyamānam na pratyabhijñāpana kṣamam
na ca taittirīyake puruṣasya yajña tvam śrūyate
viduṣaḥ yajñasya iti hi na ca ete samāna adhikaraṇe ṣaṣṭhyau vidvān eva yaḥ yajñaḥ tasya iti
na hi puruṣasya mukhyam yajña tvam asti
vyadhikaraṇe tu ete ṣaṣṭhyau viduṣaḥ yaḥ yajñaḥ tasya iti
bhavati hi puruṣasya mukhyaḥ yajña saṃbandhaḥ
satyām ca gatau mukhyaḥ eva arthaḥ āśrayitavyaḥ na bhāktaḥ
ātmā yajamānaḥ iti ca yajamāna tvam puruṣasya nirbruvan vaiyadhikaraṇyena eva asya yajña saṃbandham darśayati
api ca tasya evaṃviduṣaḥ iti siddha vat anuvāda śrutau satyām puruṣasya yajña bhāvam ātma ādīnām ca yajamāna ādi bhāvam pratipitsamānasya vākya bhedaḥ syāt
api ca sa saṃnyāsām ātma vidyām purastāt upadiśya anantaram tasya evaṃviduṣaḥ ityādi anukramaṇam paśyantaḥ pūrva śeṣaḥ eva eṣaḥ āmnāyaḥ na svatantraḥ iti pratīmaḥ
tathā ca ekam eva phalam ubhayoḥ api anuvākayoḥ upalabhāmahe brahmaṇaḥ mahimānam āpnoti iti
itareṣām tu an anya śeṣaḥ puruṣa vidyā āmnāyaḥ
āyuḥ abhivṛddhi phalaḥ hi asau ṣoḍaśam varṣa śatam jīvati yaḥ evam veda iti samabhivyāhārāt
tasmāt śākhā antara adhītānām puruṣa vidyā dharmāṇām āśīḥ mantra ādīnām aprāptiḥ taittirīyake
vedha ādi artha bhedāt
vedha ādi adhikaraṇam
asti ātharvaṇikānām upaniṣad ārambhe mantra samāmnāyaḥ sarvam pravidhya hṛdayam pravidhya dhamanīḥ pravṛjya śiraḥ bhipravṛjya tridhā vipṛktaḥ ityādiḥ
tāṇḍinām deva savitar prasuva yajñam ityādiḥ
śāṭyāyaninām śveta aśvaḥ harita nīlaḥ si iti ādiḥ
kaṭhānām taittirīyāṇām ca śam naḥ mitraḥ śam varuṇaḥ ityādiḥ
vājasaneyinām tu upaniṣad ārambhe pravargya brāhmaṇam paṭhyate devāḥ ha vai satram niṣeduḥ ityādi
kauṣītakinām api agniṣṭoma brāhmaṇam brahma vai agniṣṭomaḥ brahma eva tat ahar brahmaṇā eva te brahma upayanti te mṛta tvam āpnuvanti ye etat ahar upayanti iti
kim ime sarve pravidhi ādayaḥ mantrāḥ pravargya ādīni ca karmāṇi vidyāsu upasaṃhriyeran kim vā na upasaṃhriyeran iti mīmāṃsāmahe
kim tāvat naḥ pratibhāti
upasaṃhāraḥ eva eṣām vidyāsu iti
kutas
vidyā pradhānānām upaniṣad granthānām samīpe pāṭhāt
nanu eṣām vidyā artha tayā vidhānam na upalabhāmahe bāḍham an upalabhamānāḥ api tu anumāsyāmahe saṃnidhi sāmarthyāt
na hi saṃnidheḥ arthavat tve saṃbhavati akasmāt asau an āśrayitum yuktaḥ
nanu na eṣām mantrāṇām vidyā viṣayam kiṃcid sāmarthyam paśyāmaḥ
katham ca pravargya ādīni karmāṇi anya artha tvena eva viniyuktāni santi vidyā artha tvena api pratipadyemahi iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
sāmarthyam tāvat mantrāṇām vidyā viṣayam api kiṃcid śakyam kalpayitum hṛdaya ādi saṃkīrtanāt
hṛdaya ādīni hi prāyeṇa upāsaneṣu āyatana ādi bhāvena upadiṣṭāni
tad dvāreṇa ca hṛdayam pravidhya iti evaṃjātīyakānām mantrāṇām upapannam upāsana aṅga tvam
dṛṣṭaḥ ca upāsaneṣu api mantra viniyogaḥ bhūḥ prapadye munā amunā amunā iti evamādiḥ
tathā pravargya ādīnām karmaṇām anyatra api viniyuktānām satām aviruddhaḥ vidyāsu viniyogaḥ vājapeyaḥ iva bṛhaspatisavasya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na eṣām upasaṃhāraḥ vidyāsu iti
kasmāt
vedha ādi artha bhedāt hṛdayam pravidhya iti evaṃjātīyakānām hi mantrāṇām ye rthāḥ hṛdaya vedha ādayaḥ bhinnāḥ an abhisaṃbaddhāḥ te upaniṣad uditābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ
na teṣām tābhiḥ saṃgantum sāmarthyam asti
nanu hṛdayasya upāsaneṣu api upayogāt tad dvārakaḥ upāsanā saṃbandhaḥ upanyastaḥ na iti ucyate
hṛdaya mātra saṃkīrtanasya hi evam upayogaḥ kathaṃcid utprekṣyeta
na ca hṛdaya mātram atra mantra arthaḥ
hṛdayam pravidhya dhamanīḥ pravṛjya iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ hi na sakalaḥ mantra arthaḥ vidyābhiḥ abhisaṃbadhyate
abhicāra viṣayaḥ hi eṣaḥ rthaḥ
tasmāt ābhicārikeṇa karmaṇā sarvam pravidhye iti etasya mantrasya abhisaṃbandhaḥ
tathā deva savitar prasuva yajñam iti asya yajña prasava liṅga tvāt yajñena karmaṇā abhisaṃbandhaḥ
tad viśeṣa saṃbandhaḥ tu pramāṇa antarāt anusartavyaḥ
evam anyeṣām api mantrāṇām keṣāṃcid liṅgena keṣāṃcid vacanena keṣāṃcid pramāṇa antareṇa iti evam artha antareṣu viniyuktānām rahasya paṭhitānām api satām na saṃnidhi mātreṇa vidyā śeṣa tva upapattiḥ
durbalaḥ hi saṃnidhiḥ śruti ādibhyaḥ iti uktam prathame tantre śruti liṅga vākya prakaraṇa sthāna samākhyānām samavāye pāra daurbalyam artha viprakarṣāt iti atra
tathā karmaṇām api pravargya ādīnām anyatra viniyuktānām na vidyā śeṣa tva upapattiḥ
na hi eṣām vidyābhiḥ saha aikārthyam kiṃcid asti
vājapeye tu bṛhaspatisavasya spaṣṭam viniyoga antaram vājapeyena iṣṭvā bṛhaspatisavena yajeta iti
api ca ekaḥ yam pravargyaḥ sakṛt utpannaḥ balīyasā pramāṇena anyatra viniyuktaḥ na durbalena pramāṇena anyatra api viniyogam arhati
agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tve hi pramāṇayoḥ evam syāt
na tu balavat abalavatoḥ pramāṇayoḥ agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tā saṃbhavati balavat abalavat tva viśeṣāt eva
tasmāt evaṃjātīyakānām mantrāṇām karmaṇām vā na saṃnidhi pāṭha mātreṇa vidyā śeṣa tvam āśaṅkitavyam
araṇya anuvacana ādi dharma sāmānyāt tu saṃnidhi pāṭhaḥ iti saṃtoṣṭavyam
hānau tu upāyana śabda śeṣa tvāt kuśācchanda stuti upagāna vat tat uktam
hāni adhikaraṇam
asti tāṇḍinām śrutiḥ aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam candraḥ iva rāhoḥ mukhāt pramucya dhūtvā śarīram akṛtam kṛtātmā brahma lokam abhisaṃbhavāmi iti
tathā ātharvaṇikānām tathā vidvān nāma rūpāt vimuktaḥ parāt param puruṣam upaiti divyam iti
tathā śāṭyāyaninaḥ paṭhanti tasya putrāḥ dāyam upayanti suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām dviṣantaḥ pāpa kṛtyām iti
tathā eva kauṣītakinaḥ tat sukṛta duṣkṛte vidhūnute tasya priyāḥ jñātayaḥ sukṛtam upayanti apriyāḥ duṣkṛtam iti
tat iha kvacid sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ hānam śrūyate
kvacid tayoḥ eva vibhāgena priyaiḥ apriyaiḥ ca upāyanam
kvacid tu ubhayam api hānam upāyanam ca
tat yatra ubhayam śrūyate tatra tāvat na kiṃcid vaktavyam asti
yatra api upāyanam eva śrūyate na hānam tatra api arthāt eva hānam saṃnipatati anyaiḥ ātmīyayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ upeyamānayoḥ āvaśyaka tvāt tad hānasya
yatra tu hānam eva śrūyate na upāyanam tatra upāyanam saṃnipatet vā na vā iti vicikitsāyām aśravaṇāt asaṃnipātaḥ vidyā antara gocara tvāt ca śākhā antarīyasya śravaṇasya
api ca ātma kartṛkam sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ hānam
para kartṛkam tu upāyanam
tayoḥ asati āvaśyaka bhāve katham ha anena upāyanam ākṣipyeta
tasmāt asaṃnipātaḥ hānau upāyanasya iti
asyām prāptau paṭhati hānau iti
hānau tu etasyām kevalāyām api śrūyamāṇāyām upāyanam saṃnipatitum arhati
tad śeṣa tvāt hāna śabda śeṣaḥ hi upāyana śabdaḥ samadhigataḥ kauṣītakirahasye
tasmāt anyatra kevala hāna śravaṇe pi upāyana anuvṛttiḥ
yat uktam aśravaṇāt vidyā antara gocara tvāt anāvaśyaka tvāt ca asaṃnipātaḥ iti tat ucyate bhavet eṣā vyavasthā uktiḥ yadi anuṣṭheyam kiṃcid anyatra śrutam anyatra
na tu iha hānam upāyanam vā anuṣṭheya tvena saṃkīrtyate
vidyā stuti artham tu anayoḥ saṃkīrtanam ittham mahābhāgā vidyā yad sāmarthyāt asya viduṣaḥ sukṛta duṣkṛte saṃsāra kāraṇa bhūte vidhūyete te ca asya suhṛd durhṛtsu niviśete iti
stuti arthe ca asmin saṃkīrtane hāna anantara bhāvi tvena upāyanasya kvacid śruta tvāt anyatra api hāna śrutau upāyana anuvṛttim manyate stuti prakarṣa lābhāya
prasiddhā ca arthavāda antara apekṣā arthavāda antara pravṛttiḥ ekaviṃśaḥ vai itas saḥ ādityaḥ iti evamādiṣu
katham hi iha ekaviṃśatā ādityasya abhidhīyeta an apekṣyamāṇe rthavāda antare dvādaśa māsāḥ pañca ṛtavaḥ trayaḥ ime lokāḥ asau ādityaḥ ekaviṃśaḥ iti asmin
tathā triṣṭubhau bhavataḥ sa indriya tvāya iti evamādi vādeṣu indriyam vai triṣṭubh iti evamādi arthavāda antara apekṣā dṛśyate
vidyā stuti artha tvāt ca asya upāyana vādasya katham anyadīye sukṛta duṣkṛte anyaiḥ upeyete iti na atīva abhiniveṣṭavyam
upāyana śabda śeṣa tvāt iti ca śabda śabdam samuccārayan stuti arthām eva hānau upāyana anuvṛttim sūcayati
guṇa upasaṃhāra vivakṣāyām hi upāyana arthasya eva hānau anuvṛttim brūyāt
tasmāt guṇa upasaṃhāra vicāra prasaṅgena stuti upasaṃhāra pradarśana artham idam sūtram
kuśācchanda stuti upagāna vat iti upamā upādānam
tat yathā bhāllavinām kuśāḥ vānaspatyāḥ stha tā mā pāta iti etasmin nigame kuśānām aviśeṣeṇa vanaspati yoni tva śravaṇe śāṭyāyaninām audumbarāḥ iti viśeṣa vacanāt audumbaryaḥ kuśāḥ āśrīyante
yathā ca kvacid deva asura chandasām aviśeṣeṇa paurvāparya prasaṅge deva chandāṃsi pūrvāṇi iti paiṅgya āmnānāt pratīyate
yathā ca ṣoḍaśi stotre keṣāṃcid kāla aviśeṣa prāptau samaya adhyuṣite sūrye iti ārca śruteḥ kāla viśeṣa pratipattiḥ
yathā eva ca aviśeṣeṇa upagānam kecid samāmananti viśeṣeṇa bhāllavinaḥ yathā eteṣu kuśa ādiṣu śruti antara gata viśeṣa anvayaḥ evam hānau api upāyana anvayaḥ iti arthaḥ
śruti antara kṛtam hi viśeṣam śruti antare na abhyupagacchataḥ sarvatra eva vikalpaḥ syāt
sa ca anyāyyaḥ satyām gatau
tat uktam dvādaśalakṣaṇyām api tu vākyaśeṣa tvāt itara paryudāsaḥ syāt SPr3O pratiṣedhe vikalpaḥ syāt SPr3O
iti
athavā etāsu eva vidhūnana śrutiṣu etena sūtreṇa etat cintayitavyam kim anena vidhūnana vacanena sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ hānam abhidhīyate kim vā artha antaram iti
tatra ca evam prāpayitavyam na hānam vidhūnanam abhidhīyate iti smaraṇāt dodhūyante dhvaja agrāṇi iti ca vāyunā cālyamāneṣu dhvaja agreṣu prayoga darśanāt
tasmāt cālanam vidhūnanam abhidhīyate
cālanam tu sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ kaṃcid kālam phala pratibandhanāt iti evam prāpayya prativaktavyam hānau eva eṣa vidhūnana śabdaḥ vartitum arhati upāyana śabda śeṣa tvāt
na hi para parigraha bhūtayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ aprahīṇayoḥ paraiḥ upāyanam saṃbhavati
yadi api idam parakīyayoḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ paraiḥ upāyanam na āñjasam saṃbhāvyate tathā api tad saṃkīrtanāt tāvat tad ānuguṇyena hānam eva vidhūnanam nāma iti nirṇetum śakyate
kvacid api ca idam vidhūnana saṃnidhau upāyanam śrūyamāṇam kuśācchanda stuti upagāna vat vidhūnana śrutyā sarvatra apekṣyamāṇam sārvatrikam nirṇaya kāraṇam saṃpadyate
na ca cālanam dhvaja agra vat sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ mukhyam saṃbhavati adravya tvāt
aśvaḥ ca romāṇi vidhūnvānaḥ tyajan rajaḥ saha eva tena romāṇi api jīrṇāni śātayati aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam iti ca brāhmaṇam
aneka artha tva abhyupagamāt ca dhātūnām na smaraṇa virodhaḥ
tat uktam iti vyākhyātam
sāmparāye tartavya abhāvāt tathā hi anye
sāṃparāya adhikaraṇam
deva yānena pathā paryaṅka stham brahma abhiprasthitasya vyadhvani sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ viyogam kauṣītakinaḥ paryaṅka vidyāyām āmananti saḥ etam deva yānam panthānam āsādya agni lokam āgacchati iti upakramya saḥ āgacchati virajām nadīm tām manasā eva atyeti tat sukṛta duṣkṛte vidhūnute iti
tat kim yathāśrutam vyadhvani eva viyoga vacanam pratipattavyam āhosvit ādau eva dehāt apasarpaṇe iti vicāraṇāyām śruti prāmāṇyāt yathāśruti pratipatti prasaktau paṭhati sāṃparāyaḥ iti
sāṃparāye gamane eva dehāt apasarpaṇe idam vidyā sāmarthyāt sukṛta duṣkṛta hānam bhavati iti pratijānīte
hetum ca ācaṣṭe tartavya abhāvāt iti
na hi viduṣaḥ saṃparetasya vidyayā brahma saṃprepsataḥ antarāle sukṛta duṣkṛtābhyām kiṃcid prāptavyam asti yat artham katicid kṣaṇān akṣīṇe te kalpeyātām
vidyā viruddha phala tvāt ca vidyā sāmarthyena tayoḥ kṣayaḥ
sa ca yadā eva vidyā phala abhimukhī tadā eva bhavitum arhati
tasmāt prāk eva san ayam sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣayaḥ paścāt paṭhyate
tathā hi anye pi śākhinaḥ tāṇḍinaḥ śāṭyāyaninaḥ ca prāc avasthāyām eva sukṛta duṣkṛta hānam āmananti aśvaḥ iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam iti tasya putrāḥ dāyam upayanti suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām dviṣantaḥ pāpa kṛtyām iti ca
chandatas ubhaya avirodhāt
yadi ca dehāt apasṛptasya deva yānena pathā prasthitasya ardha pathe sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣayaḥ bhyupagamyeta tatas patite dehe yama niyama vidyā abhyāsa ātmakasya sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣaya hetoḥ puruṣa yatnasya icchātaḥ nuṣṭhāna anupapatteḥ anupapattiḥ eva tad hetukasya sukṛta duṣkṛta kṣayasya syāt
tasmāt pūrvam eva sādhaka avasthāyām chandataḥ nuṣṭhānam tasya syāt tad pūrvakam ca sukṛta duṣkṛta hānam iti draṣṭavyam
evam nimitta naimittikayoḥ upapattiḥ tāṇḍi śāṭyāyani śrutyoḥ ca saṃgatiḥ iti
gateḥ arthavat tvam ubhayathā nyathā hi virodhaḥ
gateḥ arthavat tva adhikaraṇam
kvacid puṇya pāpa ahāna saṃnidhau deva yānaḥ panthāḥ śrūyate kvacid na
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim hānau aviśeṣeṇa eva deva yānaḥ panthāḥ saṃnipatet uta vibhāgena kvacid saṃnipatet kvacid na iti
yathā tāvat hānau aviśeṣeṇa eva upāyana anuvṛttiḥ uktā evam deva yāna anuvṛttiḥ api bhavitum arhati iti asyām prāptau ācakṣmahe gateḥ deva yānasya pathaḥ arthavat tvam ubhayathā vibhāgena bhavitum arhati kvacid arthavatī gatiḥ kvacid na iti
na aviśeṣeṇa
anyathā hi aviśeṣeṇa eva etasyām gatau aṅgīkriyamāṇāyām virodhaḥ syāt puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti asyām śrutau deśa antara prāpaṇī gatiḥ virudhyeta
katham hi nirañjanaḥ gantā deśa antaram gacchet
gantavyam ca paramam sāmyam na deśa antara prāpti āyattam iti ānarthakyam eva atra gateḥ manyāmahe
upapannaḥ tad lakṣaṇa artha upalabdheḥ loka vat
upapannaḥ ca ayam ubhayathābhāvaḥ kvacid arthavatī gatiḥ kvacid na iti
tad lakṣaṇa artha upalabdheḥ gati kāraṇa bhūtaḥ rthaḥ paryaṅkavidyā ādiṣu saguṇeṣu upāsaneṣu upalabhyate
tatra hi paryaṅka ārohaṇam paryaṅka sthena brahmaṇā saha saṃvadanam viśiṣṭa gandha ādi prāptiḥ ca iti evamādi bahu deśa antara prāpti āyattam phalam śrūyate
tatra arthavatī gatiḥ
na tu samyak darśane tad lakṣaṇa artha upalabdhiḥ asti
na hi ātma ekatva darśinām āpta kāmānām iha eva dagdha aśeṣa kleśa bījānām ārabdha bhoga karma āśaya kṣapaṇa vyatirekeṇa apekṣitavyam kiṃcid asti
tatra anarthikā gatiḥ
loka vat ca eṣa vibhāgaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ yathā loke grāma prāptau deśa antara prāpaṇaḥ panthāḥ apekṣyate na ārogya prāptau evam iha api iti
bhūyas ca enam vibhāgam caturtha adhyāye nipuṇataram upapādayiṣyāmaḥ
aniyamaḥ sarvāsām avirodhaḥ śabda anumānābhyām
aniyama adhikaraṇam
saguṇāsu vidyāsu gatiḥ arthavatī na nirguṇāyām paramātma vidyāyām iti uktam
saguṇāsu api vidyāsu kāsucid gatiḥ śrūyate yathā paryaṅkavidyāyām upakosalavidyāyām pañcāgnividyāyām daharavidyāyām iti
na anyāsu yathā madhu vidyāyām śāṇḍilya vidyāyām ṣoḍaśakalavidyāyām vaiśvānara vidyāyām iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim yāsu eṣā gatiḥ śrūyate tāsu eva niyamyeta
uta aniyamena sarvābhiḥ eva evaṃjātīyakābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ abhisaṃbadhyeta iti
kim tāvat prāptam
niyamaḥ iti
yatra eva śrūyate tatra eva bhavitum arhati prakaraṇasya niyāmaka tvāt
yadi anyatra a śrūyamāṇā api gatiḥ vidyā antaram gacchet śruti ādīnām prāmāṇyam hīyeta sarvasya sarva artha tva prasaṅgāt
api ca arciḥ ādikā ekā eva gatiḥ upakosala vidyāyām pañcāgni vidyāyām ca tulya vat paṭhyate
tat sarva artha tve narthakam punarvacanam syāt
tasmāt niyamaḥ iti evam prāpte paṭhati aniyamaḥ iti
sarvāsām eva abhyudaya prāpti phalānām saguṇānām vidyānām aviśeṣeṇa eṣā deva yāna ākhyā gatiḥ bhavitum arhati
nanu aniyama abhyupagame prakaraṇa virodhaḥ uktaḥ na eṣaḥ sti virodhaḥ
śabda anumānābhyām śruti smṛtibhyām iti arthaḥ
tathā hi śrutiḥ tat ye ittham viduḥ iti pañcāgni vidyāvatām deva yānam panthānam avatārayantī ye ca ime raṇye śraddhā tapaḥ iti upāsate iti vidyā antara śīlinām api pañcāgni vidyā vidbhiḥ samāna mārga tām gamayati
katham punar avagamyate vidyā antara śīlinām iyam gatiḥ iti
nanu śraddhā tapaḥ parāyaṇānām eva syāt tad mātra śravaṇāt na eṣa doṣaḥ
na hi kevalābhyām śraddhā tapobhyām antareṇa vidyā balam eṣā gatiḥ labhyate vidyayā tat ārohanti yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ
na tatra dakṣiṇāḥ yanti na a vidvāṃsaḥ tapasvinaḥ iti śruti antarāt
tasmāt iha śraddhā tapobhyām vidyā antara upalakṣaṇam
vājasaneyinaḥ tu pañca agni vidyā adhikāre dhīyate ye evam etat viduḥ ye ca amī araṇye śraddhām satyam upāsate iti
tatra śraddhālavaḥ ye satyam brahma upāsate iti vyākhyeyam satya śabdasya brahmaṇi asakṛt prayukta tvāt
pañcāgni vidyā vidām ca itthaṃvittayā eva upātta tvāt vidyā antara parāyaṇānām eva etat upādānam nyāyyam
atha ye etau panthānau na viduḥ te kīṭāḥ pataṅgāḥ yat idam dandaśūkam iti ca mārga dvaya bhraṣṭānām kaṣṭām adhogatim gamayantī śrutiḥ deva yāna pitṛyāṇayoḥ eva enān antarbhāvayati
tatra api vidyā viśeṣāt eṣām deva yāna pratipattiḥ
smṛtiḥ api śukla kṛṣṇe gatī hi ete jagataḥ śāśvate mate
ekayā yāti anāvṛttim anyayā āvartate punar iti
yat punar deva yānasya pathaḥ dvis āmnānam upakosala vidyāyām pañcāgni vidyāyām ca tat ubhayatra api anucintana artham
tasmāt aniyamaḥ
yāvadadhikāram avasthitiḥ ādhikārikāṇām
yāvat adhikāra adhikaraṇam
viduṣaḥ vartamāna dehapāta anantaram deha antaram utpadyate na vā iti cintyate
nanu vidyāyāḥ sādhana bhūtāyāḥ saṃpattau kaivalya nirvṛttiḥ syāt na vā iti nā iyam cintā upapadyate
na hi pāka sādhana saṃpattau odanaḥ bhavet na vā iti cintā saṃbhavati
na api bhuñjānaḥ tṛpyet na vā iti cintyate upapannā tu iyam cintā brahma vidām api keṣāṃcid itihāsa purāṇayoḥ deha antara utpatti darśanāt
tathā hi apāntaratamāḥ nāma veda ācāryaḥ purāṇa ṛṣiḥ viṣṇu niyogāt kali dvāparayoḥ saṃdhau kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ saṃbabhūva iti smaranti
vasiṣṭhaḥ ca brahmaṇaḥ mānasaḥ putraḥ san nimi śāpāt apagata pūrva dehaḥ punar brahma ādeśāt mitrāvaruṇābhyām saṃbabhūva iti
bhṛgu ādīnām api brahmaṇaḥ eva mānasa putrāṇām vāruṇe yajñe punar utpattiḥ smaryate
sanatkumāraḥ pi brahmaṇaḥ eva mānasaḥ putraḥ svayam rudrāya vara pradānāt skanda tvena prādurbabhūva
evam eva dakṣa nārada prabhṛtīnām bhūyasī deha antara utpattiḥ kathyate tena tena nimittena smṛtau
śrutau api mantra arthavādayoḥ prāyeṇa upalakṣyate
te ca kecid patite pūrva dehe deha antaram ādadate kecid tu sthite eva tasmin yoga aiśvarya vaśāt aneka deha ādāna nyāyena
sarve ca ete samadhigata sakala veda arthāḥ smaryante
tat eteṣām deha antara utpatti darśanāt prāptam brahma vidyāyāḥ pākṣikam mokṣa hetu tvam ahetu tvam vā iti
atas uttaram ucyate na teṣām apāntaratamaḥ prabhṛtīnām veda pravartana ādiṣu loka sthiti hetuṣu adhikāreṣu niyuktānām adhikāra tantra tvāt sthiteḥ
yathā asau bhagavān savitā sahasra yuga paryantam jagataḥ dhikāram caritvā tad avasāne udaya astamaya varjitam kaivalyam anubhavati atha tatas ūrdhvaḥ udetya na eva udetā na astametā ekalaḥ eva madhye sthātā iti śruteḥ
yathā ca vartamānāḥ brahma vidaḥ ārabdha bhoga kṣaye kaivalyam anubhavanti tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣye saṃpatsye iti śruteḥ evam apāntaratamaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ pi īśvarāḥ parameśvareṇa teṣu teṣu adhikāreṣu niyuktāḥ santaḥ sati api samyagdarśane kaivalya hetau akṣīṇa karmāṇaḥ yāvat adhikāram avatiṣṭhante tad avasāne ca apavṛjyante iti aviruddham
sakṛt pravṛttam eva hi te phalāt ānāya karma āśayam ativāhayantaḥ svātantryeṇa eva gṛhāt iva gṛha antaram anyam anyam deham saṃcarantaḥ sva adhikāra nirvartanāya a parimuṣita smṛtayaḥ eva deha indriya prakṛti vaśi tvāt nirmāya dehān yugapad krameṇa vā adhitiṣṭhanti
na ca ete jātismarāḥ iti ucyante te eva ete iti smṛti prasiddheḥ yathā hi sulabhā nāma brahma vādinī janakena vivaditu kāmā vyudasya svam deham jānakam deham āviśya vyudya tena paścāt svam eva deham āviveśa iti smaryate
yadi hi upayukte sakṛt pravṛtte karmaṇi karma antaram deha antara ārambha kāraṇam āvirbhavet tatas anyat api adagdha bījam karma antaram tadvat eva prasajyeta iti brahmavidyāyāḥ pākṣikam mokṣa hetu tvam ahetu tvam vā śaṅkyeta
na tu iyam āśaṅkā yuktā jñānāt karma bīja dāhasya śruti smṛti prasiddha tvāt
tathā hi śrutiḥ bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ
kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare iti smṛti lambhe sarva granthīnām vipramokṣaḥ iti ca evamādyā
smṛtiḥ api yathā edhāṃsi samiddhaḥ gniḥ bhasmasāt kurute rjuna
jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā iti bījāni agni upadagdhāni na rohanti yathā punar
jñāna Cp dagdhaiḥ PIPaM tathā  kleśaiḥ PIM na  ātmā SNM saṃpadyate SPr3InPv punar
iti ca evamādyā
na ca avidyā ādi kleśa dāhe sati kleśa bījasya karma āśayasya eka deśa dāhaḥ eka deśa prarohaḥ ca iti upapadyate
na hi agni dagdhasya śāli bījasya eka deśa prarohaḥ dṛśyate
pravṛtta phalasya tu karma āśayasya mukta iṣoḥ iva vega kṣayāt nivṛttiḥ tasya tāvat eva ciram iti śarīra pātau adhikṣepa karaṇāt
tasmāt upapannā yāvadadhikāram ādhikārikāṇām avasthitiḥ
na ca jñāna phalasya anaikāntika tā
tathā ca śrutiḥ aviśeṣeṇa eva sarveṣām jñānāt mokṣam darśayati tat yaḥ yaḥ devānām prati abudhyata saḥ eva tat abhavat tathā ṛṣīṇām tathā manuṣyāṇām iti
jñāna antareṣu ca aiśvarya ādi phaleṣu āsaktāḥ syuḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ
te paścāt aiśvarya kṣaya darśanena nirviṇṇāḥ paramātma jñāne pariniṣṭhāya kaivalyam prāpuḥ iti upapadyate brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare
parasya ante kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti param padam iti smaraṇāt
pratyakṣa phala tvāt ca jñānasya phala viraha āśaṅkā anupapattiḥ
karma phale hi svarga ādau anubhava an ārūḍhe syāt āśaṅkā bhavet vā na vā iti
anubhava ārūḍham tu jñāna phalam yat sāṃkṣāt aparokṣāt brahma iti śruteḥ tat tvam asi iti siddha vat upadeśāt
na hi tattvam asi iti asya vākyasya arthaḥ tat tvam mṛtaḥ bhaviṣyasi iti evam pariṇetum śakyaḥ
tat ha etat paśyan ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede ham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti ca samyak darśana kālam eva tad phalam sarva ātma tvam darśayati
tasmāt aikāntikī viduṣaḥ kaivalya siddhiḥ
akṣara dhiyām tu avarodhaḥ sāmānya tad bhāvābhyām aupasada vat tat uktam
akṣara dhi adhikaraṇam
vājasaneyake śrūyate etat vai tat akṣaram gārgi brāhmaṇāḥ abhivadanti a sthūlam an aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham a lohitam a sneham ityādi
tathā ātharvaṇe śrūyate atha parā yayā tat akṣaram adhigamyate yat tat a dreśyam a grāhyam a gotram a varṇam ityādi
tathā eva anyatra api viśeṣa nirākaraṇa dvāreṇa akṣaram param brahma śrāvyate
tatra ca kvacid kecid atiriktāḥ viśeṣāḥ pratiṣidhyante
tāsām viśeṣa pratiṣedha buddhīnām kim sarvāsām sarvatra prāptiḥ uta vyavasthā iti saṃśaye śruti vibhāgāt vyavasthā prāptau ucyate akṣara viṣayāḥ tu viśeṣa pratiṣedha buddhayaḥ sarvāḥ sarvatra avaroddhavyāḥ sāmānya tad bhāvābhyām samānaḥ hi sarvatra viśeṣa nirākaraṇa rūpaḥ brahma pratipādana prakāraḥ
tat eva ca sarvatra pratipādyam brahma abhinnam pratyabhijñāyate
tatra kimiti anyatra kṛtāḥ buddhayaḥ anyatra na syuḥ
tathā ca ānanda ādayaḥ pradhānasya iti atra vyākhyātam
tatra vidhi rūpāṇi viśeṣaṇāni cintitāni iha pratiṣedha rūpāṇi iti viśeṣaḥ
prapañca arthaḥ ca ayam cintā bhedaḥ
aupasada vat iti nidarśanam
yathā jāmadagnye hīne puroḍāśinīṣu upasatsu coditāsu puroḍāśa pradāna mantrāṇām agneḥ veḥ hotram veḥ adhvaram iti evamādīnām udgātṛ veda utpannānām api adhvaryubhiḥ abhisaṃbandhaḥ bhavati adhvaryu kartṛka tvāt puroḍāśa pradānasya pradhāna tantra tvāt ca aṅgānām evam iha api akṣara tantra tvāt tad viśeṣaṇānām yatra kvacid api utpannānām akṣareṇa sarvatra abhisaṃbandhaḥ iti arthaḥ
tat uktam prathame kāṇḍe guṇa mukhya vyatikrame tad artha tvāt mukhyena veda saṃyogaḥ iti atra
iyat āmananāt
iyat adhikaraṇam
dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānam vṛkṣam pariṣasvajāte
tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādvatti an aśnan anyaḥ abhicākaśīti iti adhyātma adhikāre mantram ātharvaṇikāḥ śvetāśvatarāḥ ca paṭhanti
tathā kaṭhāḥ ṛtam pibantau sukṛtasya loke guhām praviṣṭau parame parārdhye
chāyā ātapau brahma vidaḥ vadanti pañca agnayaḥ ye ca triṇāciketāḥ iti
kim atra vidyā ekatvam uta vidyā nānātvam iti saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
vidyā nānātvam iti
kutas
viśeṣa darśanāt dvā suparṇāḥ iti atra hi ekasya bhoktṛ tvam dṛśyate ekasya ca abhoktṛ tvam dṛśyate
ṛtam pibantau iti atra ubhayoḥ api bhoktṛ tvam eva dṛśyate
tat vedya rūpam bhidyamānam vidyām bhindyāt iti evam prāpte bravīti vidyā ekatvam iti
kutas
yatas ubhayoḥ api anayoḥ mantrayoḥ iyat tā paricchinnam dvi tva upetam vedyam rūpam abhinnam āmananti
nanu darśitaḥ rūpa bhedaḥ na iti ucyate
ubhau api etau mantrau jīva dvitīyam īśvaram pratipādayataḥ na artha antaram
dvā suparṇā iti atra tāvat an aśnan anyaḥ abhicākaśīti iti aśanāyādi atītaḥ paramātmā pratipādyate
vākyaśeṣe ca saḥ eva pratipādyamānaḥ dṛśyate juṣṭam yadā paśyati anyam īśam asya mahimānam iti
ṛtam pibantau iti atra tu jīve pibati aśanāya ādi atītaḥ paramātmā api sāhacaryāt chatri nyāyena pibati iti upacaryate
paramātma prakaraṇam hi etat anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt iti upakramāt
tad viṣayaḥ eva ca atra api vākyaśeṣaḥ bhavati yaḥ setuḥ ījānānām akṣaram brahma yat param iti
guhām praviṣṭau ātmānau hi iti atra ca etat prapañcitam
tasmāt na asti vedya bhedaḥ
tasmāt ca vidyā eka tvam
api ca triṣu api eteṣu vedānteṣu paurvāparya ālocane paramātma vidyā eva avagamyate
tādātmya vivakṣayā eva jīva upādānam na artha antara vivakṣayā
na ca paramātma vidyāyām bheda abheda vicāra avatāraḥ sti iti uktam
tasmāt prapañca arthaḥ eva eṣa prayogaḥ
tasmāt ca adhika dharma upasaṃhāraḥ iti
antarā bhūta grāma vat sva ātmanaḥ
antara tva adhikaraṇam
yat sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma yaḥ ātmā sarva antaraḥ iti evam dvis uṣastaka hola praśnayoḥ nairantaryeṇa vājasaneyinaḥ samāmananti
tatra saṃśayaḥ vidyā ekatvam vā syāt vidyā nānātvam vā iti
vidyā nānātvam iti tāvat prāptam abhyāsa sāmarthyāt
anyathā hi anūna anatirikta arthe dvis āmnānam anarthakam eva syāt
tasmāt yathā abhyāsāt karma bhedaḥ evam abhyāsāt vidyā bhedaḥ iti evam prāpte pratyāha antarā āmnāna aviśeṣāt svātmanaḥ vidyā eka tvam iti
sarva antaraḥ hi svātmā ubhayatra api a viśiṣṭaḥ pṛcchayate pratyucyate ca
na hi dvau ātmānau ekasmin dehe sarva antarau saṃbhavataḥ
tadā hi ekasya āñjasam sarva antara tvam avakalpeta ekasya tu bhūta grāma vat na eva sarva antara tvam syāt
yathā ca pañcabhūta samūhe dehe pṛthivyāḥ āpaḥ ntarāḥ adbhyaḥ tejaḥ ntaram iti sati api āpekṣike ntara tve nā eva mukhyam sarva antara tvam bhavati tathā iha api iti arthaḥ
athavā bhūta grāma vat iti śruti antaram nidarśayati
yathā ekaḥ devāḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā iti asmin mantre samasteṣu bhūta grāmeṣu ekaḥ eva sarva antaraḥ ātmā āmnāyate evam anayoḥ api brāhmaṇayoḥ iti arthaḥ
tasmāt vedya aikyāt vidyā eka tvam iti
anyathā bheda anupapattiḥ iti ced nā upadeśa antara vat
atha yat uktam an abhyupagamyamāne vidyā bhede āmnāna bheda anupapattiḥ iti tat parihartavyam
atra ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ
upadeśa antara vat upapatteḥ
yathā tāṇḍinām upaniṣadi ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti nava kṛtvā u pi upadeśe na vidyā bhedaḥ bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati
katham ca nava kṛtvas upi upadeśe vidyā bhedaḥ na bhavati
upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām eka artha tā avagamāt bhūyas eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu iti ca ekasya eva arthasya punar punar pratipipādayiṣita tvena upakṣepāt āśaṅkā antara nirākaraṇena ca asakṛt upadeśa upapatteḥ
evam iha api praśna rūpa abhedāt atas nyadā ārtam iti ca parisamāpti aviśeṣāt upakrama upasaṃhārau tāvat eka artha viṣayau dṛśyete
yat eva sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma iti dvitīye praśne evakāram prayuñjānaḥ pūrva praśna gatam eva artham uttaratra anukṛṣyamāṇam darśayati
pūrvasmin ca brāhmaṇe kārya karaṇa vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ sadbhāvaḥ kathyate
uttarasmin tu tasya eva aśanāya ādi saṃsāra dharma atīta tvam viśeṣaḥ kathyate iti ekārtha tā upapattiḥ
tasmāt ekā vidyā iti
vyatihāraḥ viśiṃṣanti hi itara vat
vyatihāra adhikaraṇam
yathā tat yaḥ ham saḥ sau saḥ sau saḥ ham iti āditya puruṣam prakṛti aitareyiṇaḥ samāmananti tathā jābālāḥ tvam vai aham asmi bhagavaḥ devate ham vai tvam asi iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha vyatihāreṇa ubhaya rūpā matiḥ kartavyā uta eka rūpā eva iti
eka rūpā eva iti tāvat āha
na hi atra ātmanaḥ īśvareṇa ekatvam muktvā anyat kiṃcid cintayitavyam asti
yadi ca evam cintayitavya viśeṣaḥ parikalpyeta saṃsāriṇaḥ ca īśvara ātmatvam īśvarasya saṃsāri ātmatvam iti tatra saṃsāriṇaḥ tāvat īśvara ātmatve utkarṣaḥ bhavet
īśvarasya tu saṃsārya ātma tve nikarṣaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt
tasmāt aikarūpyam eva mateḥ
vyatihāra āmnāyaḥ tu ekatva dṛḍhīkāra arthaḥ iti evam prāpte pratyāha vyatihāraḥ yam ādhyānāya āmnāyate
itaravat yathā itare guṇāḥ sarva ātma tva prabhṛtayaḥ ādhyānāya āmnāyante tadvat
tathā hi viśiṃṣanti samāmnātāraḥ ubhaya uccāraṇena tvam aham asmi aham ca tvam asi iti
tat ca ubhaya rūpāyām matau kartavyāyām arthavat bhavati
anyathā hi idam anarthakam syāt ekena eva kṛta tvāt
nanu ubhaya āmnānasya artha viśeṣe parikalpyamāne devatāyāḥ saṃsāri ātma tva āpatteḥ nikarṣaḥ prasajyeta iti uktam na eṣa doṣaḥ
aikātmyasya eva anena prakāreṇa anucintyamāna tvāt
nanu evam sati saḥ eva ekatva dṛḍhīkāraḥ āpadyeta na vayam ekatva dṛḍhīkāram vārayāmaḥ
kim tarhi vyatihāreṇa iha dvi rūpā matiḥ kartavyā vacana prāmāṇyāt na ekarūpā iti etāvat upapādayāmaḥ
phalatas tu ekatvam api dṛḍhībhavati
yathā satya kāma ādi guṇa upadeśe tad guṇaḥ īśvaraḥ prasidhyati tadvat
tasmāt ayam ādhyātavyaḥ vyatihāraḥ samāne ca viṣaye upasaṃhartavyaḥ bhavati iti
sā eva hi satya ādayaḥ
satya ādi adhikaraṇam
sa yaḥ ha etam mahat yakṣam prathama jam veda satyam brahma ityādinā vājasaneyake satya vidyām sanāma akṣara upāsanām vidhāya anantaram āmnāyate tat yat tat satyam asau saḥ ādityaḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ yaḥ ca ayam dakṣiṇe kṣan puruṣaḥ ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim dve ete satya vidye kim vai ekā eva iti
dve iti tāvat prāptam
bhedena hi phala saṃyogaḥ bhavati iti purastāt hanti pāpmānam jahāti ca iti upariṣṭāt
prakṛta ākarṣaṇam tu upāsya ekatvāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ekā eva iyam satya vidyā iti
kutas
tat yat tat satyam iti prakṛta ākarṣaṇāt
nanu vidyā bhede pi prakṛta ākarṣaṇam upāsya ekatvāt upapadyate iti uktam na etat evam
yatra tu vispaṣṭāt kāraṇa antarāt vidyā bhedaḥ pratīyate tatra etat evam syāt
atra tu ubhayathā saṃbhave tat yat tat satyam iti prakṛta ākarṣaṇāt pūrvavidyā saṃbaddham eva satyam uttaratra ākṛṣyate iti eka vidyā tva niścayaḥ
yat punar uktam phala antara śravaṇāt vidyā antaram iti atra ucyate tasya upaniṣad ahar
aham iti ca aṅga antara upadeśasya stāvakam idam phala antara śravaṇam iti adoṣaḥ
api ca arthavādāt eva phale kalpayitavye sati vidyā eka tve ca avayaveṣu śrūyamāṇāni bahūni api phalāni avayavinyām eva vidyāyām upasaṃhartavyāni bhavanti
tasmāt sā eva iyam ekā satya vidyā tena tena viśeṣeṇa upetā āmnātā iti atas sarve eva satya ādayaḥ guṇāḥ ekasmin prayoge upasaṃhartavyāḥ
kecid punar asmin sūtre idam ca vājasaneyakam akṣi āditya puruṣa viṣayam vākyam chāndogye ca atha yaḥ eṣaḥ ntarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ dṛśyate yaḥ eṣaḥ u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti udāhṛtya sā eva iyam akṣi āditya puruṣa viṣayā vidyā ubhayatra ekā eva iti kṛtvā satya ādīn guṇān vājasaneyibhyaḥ chandogānām upasaṃhāryān manyante
tat na sādhu lakṣyate
chāndogye hi karma saṃbandhinī udgītha vyapāśrayā vidyā vijñāyate
tatra hi ādi madhya avasāneṣu karma saṃbandhi cihnāni bhavanti iyam eva ṛc agniḥ sāma iti upakrame tasya ṛc ca sāma ca geṣṇau tasmāt udgīthaḥ iti madhye yaḥ evam vidvān sāma gāyati iti upasaṃhāre
na evam vājasaneyake kiṃcid karma saṃbandhi cihnam asti
tatra prakrama bhedāt vidyā bhede sati guṇa vyavasthā eva yuktā iti
kāma ādi itaratra tatra ca āyatana ādibhyaḥ
kāma ādi adhikaraṇam
atha yat idam asmin brahma pure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma daharaḥ smin antarākāśaḥ iti prastutya chandogāḥ adhīyate eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ viśokaḥ vijighatsaḥ pipāsaḥ satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ ityādi
tathā vājasaneyinaḥ sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā yaḥ yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu yaḥ eṣaḥ ntar hṛdaye ākāśaḥ tasmin śete sarvasya vaśī ityādi
tatra vidyā eka tvam paraspara guṇa yogaḥ ca kim vā na iti saṃśaye vidyā eka tvam iti
tatra idam ucyate kāma ādi iti satya kāma ādi iti arthaḥ yathā devadattaḥ dattaḥ satyabhāmā bhāmā iti
yat etat chāndogye hṛdaya ākāśasya satya kāma tva ādi guṇa jātam upalabhyate tat itaratra vājasaneyake sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā iti atra saṃbadhyeta
yat ca vājasaneyake vaśi tva ādi upalabhyate tat api itaratra chāndogye eṣaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti atra saṃbadhyeta
kutas
āyatana ādi sāmānyāt
samānam hi ubhayatra api hṛdayam āyatanam samānaḥ ca vedyaḥ īśvaraḥ samānam ca tasya setu tvam loka a saṃbheda prayojanam iti evamādi bahu sāmānyam dṛśyate
nanu dṛśyate chāndogye hṛdaya ākāśasya guṇa yogaḥ vājasaneyake tu ākāśa āśrayasya brahmaṇaḥ iti na daharaḥ uttarebhyaḥ iti atra chāndogye pi ākāśa śabdam brahma eva iti pratiṣṭhāpita tvāt
ayam tu atra vidyate viśeṣaḥ sa guṇā hi brahma vidyā chāndogye upadiśyate atha ye iha ātmānam a nuvidya vrajanti etān ca satyān kāmān iti ātma vat kāmānām api vedya tva śravaṇāt vājasaneyake tu nirguṇam eva brahma upadiśyamānam dṛśyate atha urdhvam vimokṣāya brūhi a saṅgaḥ hi ayam puruṣaḥ ityādi praśna prativacana samanvayāt
vaśi tva ādi tu stuti artham eva guṇa jātam vājasaneyake saṃkīrtyate
tathā ca upariṣṭāt saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmā ityādinā nirguṇam eva brahma upasaṃharati
guṇavataḥ tu brahmaṇaḥ eka tvāt vibhūti pradarśanāya ayam guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ sūtritaḥ na upāsanāya iti draṣṭavyam
ādara āda lopaḥ
ādara adhikaraṇam
chāndogye vaiśvānara vidyām prakṛtya śrūyate tat yat bhaktam prathamam āgacchet tat homīyam sa yām prathamām āhutim juhuyāt tām juhuyāt prāṇāya svāhā ityādi
tatra pañca prāṇa āhutayaḥ vihitāḥ
tāsu ca parastāt agnihotra śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ yaḥ etat evam vidvān agnihotram juhoti iti yathā iha kṣudhitāḥ bālāḥ mātaram paryupāsate
evam sarvāṇi bhūtāni agnihotram upāsate iti ca
tatra idam vicāryate kim bhojana lope lopaḥ prāṇa agnihotrasya uta alopaḥ iti
tat yat bhaktam iti bhakta āgamana saṃyoga śravaṇāt bhakta āgamanasya ca bhojana artha tvāt bhojana lope lopaḥ prāṇa agnihotrasya iti evam prāpte na lupyeta iti tāvat āha
kasmāt
ādarāt
tathā hi vaiśvānara vidyāyām eva jābālānām śrutiḥ tithibhyaḥ śnīyāt
yathā ha vai svayam a hutvā agnihotram parasya juhuyāt evam tat iti atithi bhojanasya prāthamyam ninditvā svāmi bhojanam prathamam prāpayantī prāṇa agnihotre ādaram karoti
yā hi na prāthamya lopam sahate natarām sā prāthamyavataḥ gnihotrasya lopam saheta iti manyate
nanu bhojana artha bhakta āgamana saṃyogāt bhojana lope lopaḥ prāpitaḥ na tasya dravya viśeṣa vidhāna artha tvāt
prākṛte hi agnihotre payaḥ prabhṛtīnām dravyāṇām niyata tvāt iha api agnihotra śabdāt kauṇḍapāyi nāmayana vat tad dharma prāptau satyām bhakta dravya tā guṇa viśeṣa vidhāna artham idam vākyam tat yat bhaktam iti
atas guṇa lope na mukhyasya iti evam prāptam
bhojana lope pi adbhiḥ vā anyena vā dravyeṇa a viruddhena pratinidhāna nyāyena prāṇa agnihotrasya anuṣṭhānam iti
atas uttaram paṭhati
upasthite taḥ tad vacanāt
upasthite bhojane atas tasmāt eva bhojana dravyāt prathama upanipatitāt prāṇa agnihotram nirvartayitavyam
kasmāt
tad vacanāt
tathā hi tat yat bhaktam prathamam āgacchet tat homīyam iti siddha vat bhakta upanipāta parāmarśena parārtha dravya sādhya tām prāṇa āhutīnām vidadhāti
tāḥ aprayojaka lakṣaṇa āpannāḥ satyaḥ katham bhojana lope dravya antaram pratinidhāpayeyuḥ
na ca atra prākṛta agnihotra dharma prāptiḥ asti
kuṇḍapāyinām ayane hi māsam agnihotram juhoti iti vidhi uddeśa gataḥ gnihotra śabdaḥ tadvat bhāvam vidhāpayet iti yuktā tad dharma prāptiḥ
iha punar arthavāda gataḥ gnihotra śabdaḥ na tadvat bhāvam vidhāpayitum arhati
tad dharma prāptau ca abhyupagamyamānāyām agni uddharaṇa ādayaḥ pi prāpyeran
na ca asti saṃbhavaḥ
agni uddharaṇam tāvat homa adhikaraṇa bhāvāya
na ca ayam agnau homaḥ bhojana artha tā vyāghāta prasaṅgāt
bhojana artha upanīta dravya saṃbandhāt ca āsyaḥ eva eṣa homaḥ
tathā ca jābāla śrutiḥ tithibhyaḥ śnīyāt iti āsya ādhārām eva imām homa nirvṛttim darśayati
atas eva ca iha api sāṃpādikāni eva agnihotra aṅgāni darśayati uraḥ eva vediḥ lomāni barhiḥ hṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ manaḥ nu āhāryapacanaḥ āsyam āhavanīyaḥ iti
vedi śrutiḥ ca atra sthaṇḍila mātra upalakṣaṇa arthā draṣṭavyā mukhya agnihotre vedi abhāvāt tad aṅgānām ca iha saṃpipādayiṣita tvāt
bhojanena eva ca kṛta kālena saṃyogāt na agnihotra kāla avarodha saṃbhavaḥ
evam anye pi upasthāna ādayaḥ dharmāḥ kecid kathaṃcid virudhyante
tasmāt bhojana pakṣe eva ete mantra dravya devatā saṃyogāt pañca homāḥ nirvartayitavyāḥ
yat tu ādara darśana vacanam tat bhojana pakṣe prāthamya vidhāna artham
na hi asti vacanasya atibhāraḥ
na tu anena asya nitya tā śakyate darśayitum
tasmāt bhojana lope lopaḥ eva prāṇa agnihotrasya iti
tad nirdhāraṇa aniyamaḥ tad dṛṣṭeḥ pṛthak hi apratibandhaḥ phalam
tad nirdhāraṇa adhikaraṇam
santi karma aṅga vyapāśrayāṇi vijñānāni om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti evamādīni
kim tāni nityāni eva syuḥ karmasu parṇa mayī tva ādi vat
uta anityāni godohana ādi vat iti vicārayāmaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
nityāni iti
kutas
prayoga vacana parigrahāt an ārabhya adhītāni api hi etāni udgītha ādi dvāreṇa kratu saṃbandhāt kratu prayoga vacanena eva aṅga antara vat saṃspṛśyante
yat tu eṣām sva vākyeṣu phala śravaṇam āpayitā ha vai kāmānām bhavati ityādi tad vartamāna apadeśa rūpa tvāt arthavāda mātram eva apāpa śloka śravaṇa ādi vat na phala pradhānam
tasmāt yathā yasya parṇa mayī juhūḥ bhavati na sa pāpam ślokam śrṛṇoti iti evamādīnām a prakaraṇa paṭhitānām api juhu ādi dvāreṇa kratu praveśāt prakaraṇa paṭhita vat nitya tā evam udgītha ādi upāsanānām api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tad nirdhāraṇa aniyamaḥ iti
yāni etāni udgītha ādi karma guṇa yāthātmya nirdhāraṇāni rasatamaḥ āptiḥ samṛddhiḥ mukhya prāṇaḥ ādityaḥ iti evamādīni na etāni nitya vat karmasu niyamyeran
kutas
tad dṛṣṭeḥ
tathā hi anitya tvam evaṃjātīyakānām darśayati śrutiḥ tena ubhau kurutaḥ yaḥ ca etat evam veda yaḥ ca na veda iti a viduṣaḥ kriyā abhyanujñānāt
prastāva ādi devatā vijñāna vihīnānām api prastotṛ ādīnām yājana adhyavasāna darśanāt prastotar yā devatā prastāvam anvāyattā tām ced a vidvān prastoṣyasi tām ced a vidvān udgāsyasi tām ced a vidvān pratihariṣyasi iti ca
api ca evaṃjātīyakasya karma vyapāśrayasya vijñānasya pṛthak eva karmaṇaḥ phalam upalabhyate karma phala siddhi apratibandhaḥ tad samṛddhiḥ atiśaya viśeṣaḥ kaścid tena ubhau kurutaḥ yaḥ ca etat evam veda yaḥ ca na veda
nānā tu vidyā ca avidyā ca yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaniṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti
tatra nānā tu iti vidvat avidvat prayogayoḥ pṛthakkaraṇāt vīryavattaram iti ca tarap pratyaya prayogāt vidyā hīnam api vīryavat iti gamyate
tat ca anitya tve vidyāyāḥ upapadyate
nitya tve tu katham tad vihīnam karma vīryavat iti anujñāyeta
sarva aṅga upasaṃhāre hi vīryavat karma iti sthitiḥ
tathā loka sāma ādiṣu pratiniyatāni pratyupāsanam phalāni śiṣyante kalpante ha asmai lokāḥ ūrdhvāḥ ca āvṛttāḥ ca iti evamādīni
na ca idam phala śravaṇam arthavāda mātram yuktam pratipattum
tathā hi guṇa vādaḥ āpadyeta
phala upadeśe tu mukhya vāda upapattiḥ
prayāja ādiṣu tu itikartavya tā ākāṅkṣasya kratoḥ prakṛta tvāt tādarthye sati yuktam phala śruteḥ arthavāda tvam
tathā an ārabhya adhīteṣu api parṇa mayī tva ādiṣu na hi parṇa mayī tva ādīnām akriyā ātmakānām āśrayam antareṇa phala saṃbandhaḥ
godohana ādīnām hi prakṛta ap praṇayana ādi āśraya lābhāt upapannaḥ phala vidhiḥ
tathā bailva ādīnām api prakṛta yūpa ādi āśraya lābhāt upapannaḥ phala vidhiḥ
na tu parṇamayī tva ādiṣu evaṃvidhaḥ kaścid āśrayaḥ sti
vākyena eva tu juhū ādi āśrayatām vivakṣitvā phale vidhim vivakṣataḥ vākya bhedaḥ syāt
upāsanānām tu kriyā ātmaka tvāt viśiṣṭa vidhāna upapatteḥ udgītha ādi āśrayāṇām phale vidhānam na virudhyate
tasmāt yathā kratu āśrayāṇi api godohana ādīni phala saṃyogāt anityāni evam udgītha ādi upāsanāni api iti draṣṭavyam
atas eva ca kalpasūtra kārāḥ na evaṃjātīyakāni upāsanāni kratuṣu kalpayāṃcakruḥ
pradāna vat eva tat uktam
pradāna adhikaraṇam
vājasaneyake vadiṣyāmi eva aham iti vāc dadhre iti atra adhyātmam vāc ādīnām prāṇaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ adhidaivatam agni ādīnām vāyuḥ
tathā chāndogye vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ iti atra adhidaivatam agni ādīnām vāyuḥ saṃvargaḥ prāṇaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ iti atra adhyātmam vāc ādīnām prāṇaḥ
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim pṛthak eva imau vāyu prāṇau upagantavyau syātām uta apṛthak iti
apṛthak iti tāvat prāptam tattva abhedāt
na hi abhinne tattve pṛthak anucintanam nyāyyam
darśayati ca śrutiḥ adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca tattva abhedam agniḥ vāc bhūtvā mukham prāviśat iti ārabhya
tathā te ete sarve eva samāḥ sarve nantāḥ iti ādhyātmikānām prāṇānām ādhidaivikīm vibhūtim ātma bhūtām darśayati
tathā anyatra api tatra tatra adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca bahudhā tattva abheda darśanam bhavati
kvacid ca yaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti spaṣṭam eva vāyum prāṇam ca ekam karoti
tathā udāhṛte pi vājasaneyi brāhmaṇe yatas ca udeti sūryaḥ iti asmin upasaṃhāra śloke prāṇāt vai eṣaḥ udeti prāṇe stameti iti prāṇena eva upasaṃharan ekatvam darśayati
tasmāt ekam eva vratam caret prāṇyāt ca eva apānyāt ca iti ca prāṇa vratena eva ekena upasaṃharan etat eva draḍhayati
tathā chāndogye pi parastāt mahātmanaḥ caturaḥ devaḥ ekaḥ kaḥ sa jagāra bhuvanasya gopāḥ iti ekam eva saṃvargam gayam ati
na bravīti ekaḥ eva eṣām caturṇām saṃvargaḥ aparaḥ pareṣām iti
tasmāt apṛthak tvam upagamanasya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ pṛthak eva vāyu prāṇau upagantavyau iti
kasmāt
pṛthak upadeśāt
ādhyāna arthaḥ hi ayam adhyātma adhidaiva vibhāga upadeśaḥ
saḥ asatya adhyāna pṛthaktve anarthakaḥ eva syāt
nanu uktam apṛthak anucintanam tattva abhedāt iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
tattva abhede pi avasthā bhedāt upadeśa bheda vaśena anucintana bheda upapatteḥ śloka upanyāsasya ca tattva abheda abhiprāyeṇa api upapadyamānasya pūrva udita dhyeya bheda nirākaraṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt sa yathā eṣām prāṇānām madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ evam etāsām devatānām vāyuḥ iti ca upamāna upameya karaṇāt
etena vrata upanyāsaḥ vyākhyātaḥ
ekam eva vratam iti ca eva kāraḥ vāc ādi vrata nivartanena prāṇa vrata pratipatti arthaḥ
bhagna vratāni hi vāc ādīni uktāni tāni mṛtyuḥ śramaḥ bhūtvā upayeme iti śruteḥ
na vāyu vrata nivṛtti arthaḥ atha atas vrata mīmāṃsā iti prastutya tulya vat vāyu prāṇayoḥ abhagna vrata tvasya nirdhārita tvāt
ekam eva vratam caret iti ca uktvā tena u etasyai devatāyai sāyujyam salokatām jayati iti vāyu prāptim phalam bruvan vāyuvratam anivartitam darśayati
devatā iti atra vāyuḥ syāt aparicchinna ātmaka tvasya purastāt prayogāt ca sā eṣā an astamitā devatā yat vāyuḥ iti
tathā tau vai etau dvau saṃvargau vāyuḥ eva deveṣu prāṇaḥ prāṇeṣu iti bhedena vyapadiśati
te vai ete pañca anye pañca anye daśa santaḥ tat kṛtam iti ca bhedena eva upasaṃharati
tasmāt pṛthak eva upagamanam
pradāna vat yathā indrāya rājñe puroḍāśam ekādaśa kapālam indrāya adhirājāya indrāya sva rājñe iti asyām tri puroḍāśinyām iṣṭau sarveṣām abhigamayan avadyati a chaṃbaṭkāram iti atas vacanāt indra abhedāt ca saha pradāna āśaṅkāyām rāja ādi guṇa bhedāt yājyā anuvākyā vyatyāsa vidhānāt ca yathānyāsam eva devatā pṛthaktvāt pradāna pṛthaktvam bhavati
evam tattva abhede pi ādhyeya aṃśa pṛthaktvāt ādhyāna pṛthaktvam iti arthaḥ
tat uktam saṃkarṣe nānā vā devatā pṛthak jñānāt iti
tatra tu dravya devatā bhedāt yāga bhedaḥ vidyate
na evam iha vidyā bhedaḥ sti upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām adhyātma adhidaiva upadeśeṣu eka vidyā vidhāna pratīteḥ
vidyā aikye tu adhyātma adhidaiva bhedāt pravṛtti bhedaḥ bhavati agnihotre iva sāyaṃprātar kāla bhedāt iti etāvat abhipretya pradāna vat iti uktam
liṅga bhūyaḥ tvāt tat hi balīyaḥ tāt api
liṅga bhūyaḥ tva adhikaraṇam
vājasaneyinaḥ gnirahasye na eva vai idam agre sadā āsīt iti etasmin brāhmaṇe manaḥ dhikṛtya adhīyate tat ṣaṭtriṃśatam sahasrāṇi apaśyat ātmanaḥ gnīn arkān manaḥ mayān manaḥ citaḥ ityādi
tathā eva vāc citaḥ prāṇa citaḥ cakṣuḥ citaḥ śrotra citaḥ karma citaḥ gni citaḥ iti pṛthak agnīn āmananti sāṃpādikān
teṣu saṃśayaḥ kim ete manaḥ cit ādayaḥ kriyā anupraveśinaḥ tad śeṣa bhūtāḥ uta svatantrāḥ kevala vidyā ātmakāḥ iti
tatra prakaraṇāt kriyā anupraveśe prāpte svātantryam tāvat pratijānīte liṅga bhūyaḥ tvāt iti
bhūyāṃsi hi liṅgāni asmin brāhmaṇe kevala vidyā ātmaka tvam eṣām upodbalayanti dṛśyante tat yat kiṃca imāni bhūtāni manasā saṃkalpayanti teṣām eva sā kṛtiḥ iti tān ha etān evaṃvide sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāni cinvanti api svapate iti ca evaṃjātīyakāni
tat hi liṅgam prakaraṇāt balīyaḥ
tat api uktam pūrvasmin kāṇḍe śruti liṅga vākya prakaraṇa sthāna samākhyānām samavāye pāra daurbalyam artha viprakarṣāt iti
pūrva vikalpaḥ prakaraṇāt syāt kriyā mānasa vat
na etat yuktam svatantrāḥ ete gnayaḥ an anya śeṣa bhūtāḥ iti
pūrvasya kriyā mayasya agneḥ prakaraṇāt tad viṣayaḥ eva ayam vikalpa viśeṣa upadeśaḥ syāt na svatantraḥ
nanu prakaraṇāt liṅgam balīyaḥ satyam evam etat
liṅgam api tu evaṃjātīyakam na prakaraṇāt balīyaḥ bhavati
anya artha darśanam hi etat sāṃpādika agni praśaṃsā rūpa tvāt
anya artha darśanam ca asatyām anyasyām prāptau guṇa vādena api upapadyamānam na prakaraṇam bādhitum utsahate
tasmāt sāṃpādikāḥ api ete gnayaḥ prakaraṇa atikraya anupraveśinaḥ eva syuḥ
mānasa vat yathā daśarātrasya daśame hani avivākye pṛthivyā pātreṇa samudrasya somasya prajāpataye devatāyai gṛhyamāṇasya grahaṇa āsādana havana āharaṇa upahvāna bhakṣaṇāni mānasāni eva āmnāyante sa ca mānasaḥ api graha kalpaḥ kriyā prakaraṇāt kriyā śeṣaḥ eva bhavati evam ayam api agni kalpaḥ iti arthaḥ
atideśāt ca
atideśaḥ ca eṣām agnīnām kriyā anupraveśam upodbalayati ṣaṭtriṃśat sahasrāṇi agnayaḥ rkāḥ teṣām ekaikaḥ eva tāvān yāvān asau pūrvaḥ iti
sati hi sāmānye atideśaḥ pravartate
tatas ca pūrveṇa iṣṭakā citena kriyā anupraveśinā agninā sāṃpādikān agnīn atidiśan kriyā anupraveśam eva eṣām dyotayati
vidyā eva tu nirdhāraṇāt
tu śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati
vidyā ātmakāḥ eva ete svatantrāḥ manaḥ cit ādayaḥ gnayaḥ syuḥ na kriyā śeṣa bhūtāḥ
tathā hi nirdhārayati te ha ete vidyā citaḥ eva iti vidyayā ha eva ete evaṃvidaḥ citāḥ bhavanti iti ca
darśanāt ca
dṛśyate ca eteṣām svātantrye liṅgam
tat purastāt darśitam liṅga bhūyaḥ tvāt iti atra
nanu liṅgam api asatyām anyasyām prāptau asādhakam kasyacid arthasya iti apāsya tat prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt kriyā śeṣa tvam adhyavasitam iti atas uttaram paṭhati
śruti ādi balīyaḥ tvāt ca na bādhaḥ
na evam prakaraṇa sāmarthya atikraya aśeṣa tvam adhyavasāya svātantrya pakṣaḥ bādhitavyaḥ śruti ādeḥ balīyaḥ tvāt
balīyāṃsi hi prakaraṇāt śruti liṅga vākyāni iti sthitam śruti liṅga sūtre
tāni ca iha svātantrya pakṣam sādhayanti dṛśyante
katham
śrutiḥ tāvat te ha ete vidyā citaḥ eva iti
tathā liṅgam sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāni cinvanti api svapate iti
tathā vākyam api vidyayā ha eva ete evaṃvidaḥ citāḥ bhavanti iti
vidyā citaḥ eva iti hi sa avadhāraṇām iyam śrutiḥ kriyā anupraveśe mīṣām abhyupagamyamāne pīḍitā syāt
nanu abāhya sādhanatva abhiprāyam idam avadhāraṇam bhaviṣyati na iti ucyate
tad abhiprāya tāyām hi vidyā citaḥ iti iyatā sva rūpa saṃkīrtanena eva kṛta tvāt anarthakam avadhāraṇam bhavet sva rūpam eva hi eṣām abāhya sādhanatvam iti
abāhya sādhana tve tu mānasa graha vat kriyā anupraveśa śaṅkāyām tad nivṛtti phalam avadhāraṇam arthavat bhaviṣyati
tathā svapate jāgrate ca evaṃvide sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāni etān agnīn cinvanti iti sātatya darśanam eṣām svātantrye yathā sāṃpādike vāc prāṇa maye gnihotre prāṇam tadā vāci juhoti
