vācam tadā prāṇe juhoti iti ca uktvā ucyate ete anante amṛte āhutī jāgrat ca svapan ca satatam juhoti iti tadvat
kriyā anupraveśe tu kriyā prayogasya alpa kāla tvāt na sātatyena eṣām prayogaḥ kalpeta
na ca idam arthavāda mātram iti nyāyyam
yatra hi vispaṣṭaḥ vidhāyakaḥ liṅ ādiḥ upalabhyate yuktam tatra saṃkīrtana mātrasya arthavāda tvam
iha tu vispaṣṭa vidhi antara anupalabdheḥ saṃkīrtanāt eva eṣām vijñāna vidhānam kalpanīyam
tat ca yathā saṃkīrtanam eva kalpayitum śakyate iti sātatya darśanāt tathābhūtam eva kalpyate
tatas ca sāmarthyāt eṣām svātantrya siddhiḥ
etena tat yat kiṃca imāni bhūtāni manasā saṃkalpayanti teṣām eva sā kṛtiḥ ityādi vyākhyātam
tathā vākyam api evaṃvide iti puruṣa viśeṣa saṃbandham eva eṣām ācakṣāṇam na kratu saṃbandham mṛṣyate
tasmāt svātantrya pakṣaḥ eva jyāyān iti
anubandha ādibhyaḥ prajñā antara pṛthaktva vat dṛṣṭaḥ ca tat uktam
itas ca prakaraṇam upamṛdya svātantryam manaḥ cit ādīnām pratipattavyam yat kriyā avayavān manaḥ ādi vyāpāreṣu anubadhnāti te manasā eva ādhīyanta manasā acīyanta manasā eva grahāḥ agṛhyanta manasā astuvan manasā aśaṃsan yat kiṃca yajñe karma kriyeta yat kiṃca yajñiyam karma manasā eva teṣu tat manaḥ mayeṣu manaḥ citsu manaḥ mayam eva kriyate ityādinā
saṃpad phalaḥ hi ayam anubandhaḥ
na ca pratyakṣāḥ kriyā avayavāḥ santaḥ saṃpadā lipsitavyāḥ
na ca atra udgītha ādi upāsana vat kriyā aṅga saṃbandhāt tad anupraveśi tvam āśaṅkitavyam śruti vairūpyāt
na hi atra kriyā aṅgam kiṃcid ādāya tasmin adaḥ nāma adhyavasitavyam iti vadati
ṣaṭtriṃśat sahasrāṇi tu manaḥ vṛtti bhedān ādāya teṣu agni tvam graha ādīn ca kalpayati puruṣa yajña ādi vat
saṃkhyā ca iyam puruṣa āyuṣasya ahar su dṛṣṭā satī tad saṃbandhinīṣu manaḥ vṛttiṣu āropyate iti draṣṭavyam
evam anubandhāt svātantryam manaḥ cit ādīnām
ādi śabdāt atideśa ādi api yathāsaṃbhavam yojayitavyam
tathā hi teṣām ekaikaḥ eva tāvān yāvān asau pūrvaḥ iti kriyā mayasya agneḥ māhātmyam jñāna mayānām ekaikasya atidiśan kriyāyām anādaram darśayati
na ca sati eva kriyā saṃbandhe vikalpaḥ pūrveṇa uttareṣām iti śakyam vaktum
na hi yena vyāpāreṇa āhavanīya dhāraṇa ādinā pūrvaḥ kriyāyām upakaroti tena uttare upakartum śaknuvanti
yat tu pūrvapakṣe pi atideśaḥ upodbalakaḥ iti uktam sati hi sāmānye tideśaḥ pravartate iti tat asmad pakṣe pi agni tva sāmānyena atideśa saṃbhavāt pratyuktam asti hi sāṃpādikānām api agnīnām agni tvam iti
śruti ādīni ca kāraṇāni darśitāni
evam anubandha ādibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ svātantryam manaḥ cit ādīnām
prajñā antara pṛthaktva vat yathā prajñā antarāṇi śāṇḍilya vidyā prabhṛtīni svena svena anubandhena anubadhyamānāni pṛthak eva karmabhyaḥ prajñā antarebhyaḥ ca svatantrāṇi bhavanti evam iti
dṛṣṭaḥ ca aveṣṭeḥ rājasūya prakaraṇa paṭhitāyāḥ prakaraṇāt utkarṣaḥ varṇa traya anubandhāt
rājayajña tvāt ca rājasūyasya
tat uktam prathame kāṇḍe kratu arthāyām iti ced na varṇa traya saṃyogāt iti
na sāmānyāt api upalabdheḥ mṛtyu vat na hi loka āpattiḥ
yat uktam mānasa vat iti tat pratyucyate
na mānasa graha sāmānyāt api manaḥ cit ādīnām kriyā śeṣa tvam kalpyam pūrva uktebhyaḥ śruti ādi hetubhyaḥ kevala puruṣa artha tva upalabdheḥ
na hi kiṃcid kasyacid kenacid sāmānyam na saṃbhavati
na ca tāvatā yathāsvam vaiṣamyam nivartate
mṛtyu vat yathā sa vai eṣaḥ eva mṛtyuḥ yaḥ eṣaḥ etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ iti agniḥ vai mṛtyuḥ iti ca agni āditya puruṣayoḥ samāne mṛtyu śabda prayoge na atyanta sāmya āpattiḥ
yathā ca asau vāva lokaḥ gautama agniḥ tasya ādityaḥ eva samidh iti atra na samidh ādi sāmānyāt lokasya agni bhāva āpattiḥ tadvat
pareṇa ca śabdasya tādvidhyam bhūyaḥ tvāt tu anubandhaḥ
parastāt api ayam vāva loke eṣaḥ gniḥ citaḥ iti asmin anantare brāhmaṇe tādvidhyam kevala vidyā vidhi tvam śabdasya prayojanam lakṣyate na śuddha karma aṅga vidhi tvam
tatra hi vidyayā tat ārohanti yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ
na tatra dakṣiṇāḥ yanti na a vidvāṃsaḥ tapasvaniḥ iti anena ślokena kevalam karma nindan vidyām ca praśaṃsan idam gamayati
tathā purastāt api yat etat maṇḍalam tapati iti asmin brāhmaṇe vidyā pradhāna tvam eva lakṣyate saḥ mṛtaḥ bhavati mṛtyuḥ hi asya ātmā bhavati iti vidyā phalena eva upasaṃhārāt na karma pradhāna tā
tad sāmānyāt iha api tathātvam
bhūyān tu agni avayavāḥ saṃpādayitavyāḥ vidyāyām iti etasmāt kāraṇāt agninā anubadhyate vidyā na karma aṅga tvāt
tasmāt manaḥ cit ādīnām kevala vidyā ātmaka tva siddhiḥ
eka ātmanaḥ śarīre bhāvāt
śarīrebhāva adhikaraṇam
iha deha vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ sadbhāvaḥ samarthyate bandha mokṣa adhikāra siddhaye
na hi asati deha vyatirikte ātmani para loka phalāḥ codanāḥ upapadyeran
kasya vā brahma ātmatvam upadiśyeta
nanu śāstra pramukhe eva prathame pāde śāstra phala upabhoga yogyasya deha vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ stitvam uktam satyam uktam bhāṣyakṛtā
na tu tatra ātma astitve sūtram asti
iha tu svayam eva sūtrakṛtā tat astitvam ākṣepa puraḥsaram pratiṣṭhāpitam
itas eva ca ākṛṣya ācāryeṇa śabarasvāminā pramāṇa lakṣaṇe varṇitam
atas eva ca bhagavatā upavarṣeṇa prathame tantre ātma astitva abhidhāna prasaktau śārīrake vakṣyāmaḥ iti uddhāraḥ kṛtaḥ
iha ca idam codanā lakṣaṇeṣu upāsaneṣu vicāryamāṇeṣu ātma astitvam vicāryate kṛtsna śāstra śeṣa tva pradarśanāya
api ca pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe prakaraṇa utkarṣa abhyupagamena manaḥ cit ādīnām puruṣa artha tvam varṇitam
kaḥ sau puruṣaḥ yad arthāḥ ete manaḥ cit ādayaḥ iti asyām prasaktau idam deha vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ stitvam ucyate
tad astitva ākṣepa artham idam ādimam sūtram ākṣepa pūrvikā hi parihāra uktiḥ vivakṣite rthe sthūṇā nikhanana nyāyena dṛḍhām buddhim utpādayet iti
atra eke deha mātra ātma darśinaḥ lokāyatikāḥ deha vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ bhāvam manyamānāḥ samasta vyasteṣu bāhyeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu adṛṣṭam api caitanyam śarīra ākāra pariṇateṣu bhūteṣu syāt iti saṃbhāvayantaḥ tebhyaḥ caitanyam mada śakti vat vijñānam caitanya viśiṣṭaḥ kāyaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca āhuḥ
na svarga gamanāya apavarga gamanāya vā samarthaḥ deha vyatiriktaḥ ātmā asti yat kṛtam caitanyam dehe syāt
dehaḥ eva tu cetanaḥ ca ātmā ca iti pratijānate
hetum ca ācakṣate śarīre bhāvāt iti yat hi yasmin sati bhavati asati ca na bhavati tat tad dharma tvena adhyavasīyate yathā agni dharmau auṣṇya prakāśau
prāṇa ceṣṭā caitanya smṛti ādayaḥ ca ātma dharma tvena abhimatāḥ ātma vādinām te pi antar eva dehe upalabhyamānāḥ bahis ca anupalabhyamānāḥ asiddhe deha vyatirikte dharmiṇi deha dharmāḥ eva bhavitum arhanti
tasmāt a vyatirekaḥ dehāt ātmanaḥ iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ
vyatirekaḥ tad bhāva abhāvi tvāt na tu upalabdhi vat
na tu etat asti yat uktam a vyatirekaḥ dehāt ātmanaḥ iti
vyatirekaḥ eva asya dehāt bhavitum arhati
tad bhāva abhāvi tvāt
yadi deha bhāve bhāvāt deha dharma tvam ātma dharmāṇām manyeta tatas deha bhāve
api abhāvāt a tad dharma tvam eva eṣām kim na manyeta
deha dharma vailakṣaṇyāt
ye hi deha dharmāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ te yāvat deham bhavanti
prāṇa ceṣṭā ādayaḥ tu sati api dehe mṛta avasthāyām na bhavanti
deha dharmāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ paraiḥ api upalabhyante na tu ātma dharmāḥ caitanya smṛti ādayaḥ
api ca sati hi tāvat dehe jīvat avasthāyām eṣām bhāvaḥ śakyate niścetum na tu asati abhāvaḥ
patite
api kadācid asmin dehe jīvat avasthāyām eṣām bhāvaḥ śakyate niścetum na tu asatya bhāvaḥ
patite
api kadācid asmin dehe deha antara saṃcāreṇa ātma dharmāḥ anuvarteran
saṃśaya mātreṇa pi parapakṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate
kimātmakam ca punar idam caitanyam manyate yasya bhūtebhyaḥ utpattim icchati iti paraḥ paryanuyoktavyaḥ
na hi bhūta catuxṭaya vyatirekeṇa lokāyatikaḥ kiṃcid tattvam pratyeti
yat anubhavanam bhūta bhautikānām tat caitanyam iti ced tarhi viṣaya tvāt teṣām na tad dharma tvam svātmani kriyā virodhāt
na hi agniḥ uṣṇaḥ san sva ātmānam dahati
na hi naṭaḥ śikṣitaḥ san sva skandham adhirokṭati
na hi bhūta bhautika dharmeṇa satā caitanyena bhūta bhautikāni viṣayīkriyeran
na hi rūpa ādibhiḥ sva rūpam para rūpam vā viṣayīkriyate
viṣayīkriyante tu bāhya ādhyātmikāni bhūta bhautikāni caitanyena
atas ca yathā eva asyāḥ bhūta bhautika viṣayāyāḥ upalabdheḥ
abhyupagamyate evam vyatirekaḥ
api asyāḥ tebhyaḥ
abhyupagantavyaḥ
upalabdhi svarūpaḥ eva ca naḥ ātmā iti ātmanaḥ deha vyatirikta tvam
nitya tvam ca upalabdheḥ aikarūpyāt
yat tu uktam śarīre bhāvāt śarīra dharmaḥ upalabdhiḥ iti tad varṇitena prakāreṇa pratyuktam
api ca satsu pradīpa ādiṣu upakaraṇeṣu upalabdhiḥ bhavati asatsu na bhavati
na ca etāvatā pradīpa ādi dharmaḥ eva upalabdhiḥ bhavati
evam sati dehe upalabdhiḥ bhavati asati ca na bhavati iti na deha dhearmaḥ bhavitum arhati
upakaraṇa tva mātreṇa api pradīpa ādi vat deha upayoga upapatteḥ
na ca atyantam dehasya upalabdhau upayogaḥ
api dṛśyate niśceṣṭaḥ
api asmin dehe svapet nānāvidha upalabdhi darśanāt
tasmāt anavadyam deha vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ
astitvam
iti triṃśam aikātmya adhikaraṇam
aṅga avabaddhāḥ tu na śākhāsu hi prativedam
aṅga avabaddha adhikaraṇam
samāptā prāsaṅgikī kathā
saṃprati prakṛtām eva anuvartāmahe
om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta uktham uktham iti vai prajāḥ vadanti tat idam eva uktham iyam eva pṛthivī ayam vāva lokaḥ eṣaḥ gniḥ citaḥ iti evamādyāḥ ye udgītha ādi karma aṅga avabaddhāḥ pratyayāḥ prativedam śākhā bhedeṣu vihitāḥ te tad śākhā gateṣu eva udgītha ādiṣu bhaveyuḥ athavā sarva śākhā gateṣu iti viśayaḥ
pratiśākham ca svara ādi bhedāt udgītha ādi bhedān upādāya ayam upanyāsaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
sva śākhā gateṣu eva udgītha ādiṣu vidhīyeran iti
kutas
saṃnidhānāt udgītham upasīte iti hi sāmānya vihitānām viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām saṃnikṛṣṭena eva sva śākhā gatena viśeṣeṇa ākāṅkṣā ādi nivṛtteḥ tad atilaṅghanena śākhā antara vihita viśeṣa upādāne kāraṇam na asti
tasmāt pratiśākham vyavasthā iti evam prāpte bravīti aṅga avabaddhā astu iti
tu śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati
na ete prativedam sva śākhāsu eva vyavatiṣṭheran api tu sarva śākhāsu anuvarteran
kutas
udgītha ādi śruti aviśeṣāt
sva śākhā vyavasthāyām hi udgītham upāsīta iti sāmānya śrutiḥ aviśeṣa pravṛttā satī saṃnidhāna vaśena viśeṣe vyavasthāpyamānā pīḍitā syāt
na ca etat nyāyyam
saṃnidhānāt hi śrutiḥ balīyasī
na ca sāmānya āśrayaḥ pratyayaḥ na upapadyate
tasmāt svara ādi bhede sati api udgītha tva ādi aviśeṣāt sarva śākhā gateṣu eva udgītha ādiṣu evaṃjātīyakāḥ pratyayāḥ syuḥ
mantra ādi vat vā virodhaḥ
athavā na eva atra virodhaḥ śaṅkitavyaḥ katham anya śākhā gateṣu udgītha ādiṣu anya śākhā vihitāḥ pratyayāḥ bhaveyuḥ iti mantra ādi vat avirodha upapatteḥ
tathā hi mantrāṇām karmaṇām guṇānām ca śākhā antara utpannānām api śākhā antare upasaṃgrahaḥ dṛśyate
yeṣām api hi śākhinām kuṭaruḥ asi iti aśma ādāna mantraḥ nāmnā ātaḥ teṣām api asau viniyogaḥ dṛśyate kukkuṭaḥ si iti aśmānam ādatte kuṭaruḥ asi iti vā iti
yeṣām api samidh ādayaḥ prayājāḥ na āmnātāḥ teṣām api teṣu guṇa vidhiḥ āmnāyate ṛtavaḥ vai prayājāḥ samānatra hotavyāḥ iti
tathā yeṣām api ajaḥ gnīṣomīyaḥ iti jāti viśeṣa upadeśaḥ na asti teṣām api tad viṣayaḥ mantra varṇaḥ upalabhyate chāgasya vapāyāḥ medasaḥ nubrūhi iti
tathā veda antara utpannānām api agneḥ veḥ hotram veḥ adhvaram iti evamādi mantrāṇām veda antare parigrahaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
tathā bahvṛca paṭhitasya sūktasya yaḥ jātaḥ eva prathamaḥ manasvān ityasya adhvaryave sajanīyam śasyam iti atra parigrahaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
tasmāt yathā āśrayāṇām karma aṅgānām sarvatra anuvṛttiḥ evam āśritānām api pratyayānām iti avirodhaḥ
bhūmnaḥ kratu vat jyāyaḥ tvam tathā hi darśayati
bhūma jyāyaḥ tva adhikaraṇam
prācīnaśālaḥ aupamanyavaḥ iti asyām ākhyāyikāyām vyastasya samastasya ca vaiśvānarasya upāsanam śrūyate
vyasta upāsanam tāvat aupamanyava kam tvam ātmānam upāsse iti divam eva bhagavaḥ rājan iti ha uvāca eṣa vai su tejāḥ ātmā vaiśvānaraḥ yam tvam ātmānam upāsse ityādi
tathā samasta upāsanam api tasya ha vai etasya ātmanaḥ vaiśvānarasya mūrdhā eva su tejāḥ cakṣuḥ viśva rūpaḥ prāṇaḥ pṛthak vartmā ātmā saṃdehaḥ bahulaḥ vastiḥ eva rayiḥ pṛthivī eva pādau ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha ubhayathā api upāsanam syāt vyastasya samastasya ca uta samastasya eva iti
kim tāvat prāptam
pratyavayavam su tejaḥ prabhṛtiṣu upāsse iti kriyā pada śravaṇāt tasmāt tava sutam prasutam āsutam kule dṛśyate iti ādi phala bheda śravaṇāt ca vyastāni api upāsanāni syuḥ iti prāptam
tatas abhidhīyate bhūmnaḥ padārtha upacaya ātmakasya samastasya vaiśvānara upāsanasya jyāyastvam prādhānyena asmin vākye vivakṣitam bhavitum arhati na pratyekam avayava upāsanānām api
kratu vat yathā kratuṣu darśa pūrṇamāsa prabhṛtiṣu sāmastyena sa aṅga pradhāna prayogaḥ eva ekaḥ vivakṣyate na vyastānām api prayogaḥ prayāja ādīnām na api eka deśa aṅga yuktasya pradhānasya tadvat
kutas etat bhūmā eva jyāyān iti
tathā hi śrutiḥ bhūmnaḥ jyāyaḥ tvam darśayati eka vākya tā avagamāt
ekam hi idam vākyam vaiśvānara vidyā viṣayam paurvāparya ālocanāt pratīyate
tathā hi prācīnaśāla prabhṛtayaḥ uddālaka avasānāḥ ṣaṭ ṛṣayaḥ vaiśvānara vidyāyām pariniṣṭhām a pratipadyamānāḥ aśvapatim kaikeyam rājānam abhyājagmuḥ iti upakramya ekaikasya ṛṣeḥ upāsyam dyu prabhṛtīnām ekaikam śrāvayitvā mūrdhā tu eṣaḥ ātmanaḥ iti ha uvāca ityādinā mūrdha ādi bhāvam teṣām vidadhāti
mūrdhā te vyapatiṣyat yat mām na agamiṣyaḥ ityādinā ca vyasta upāsanam apavadati
punar ca vyasta upāsanam vyāvartya samasta upāsanam eva anuvartya sa sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu ātmasu annam atti iti bhūma āśrayam eva phalam darśayati
yat tu pratyekam sutejaḥ prabhṛtiṣu phala bheda śravaṇam tat evam sati aṅga phalāni pradhāne eva abhyuccinoti iti draṣṭavyam
tathā upāsse iti api pratyavayavam ākhyāta śravaṇam para abhiprāya anuvāda artham na vyasta upāsana vidhāna artham
tasmāt samasta upāsana pakṣaḥ eva śreyān iti
kecid tu atra samasta upāsana pakṣam jyāyāṃsam pratiṣṭhāpya jyāyas tva vacanāt eva kila vyasta upāsana pakṣam api sūtrakāraḥ nu manyate iti kalpayanti
tat ayuktam ekavākyatā avagatau satyām vākya bheda kalpanasya anyāyya tvāt mūrdhā te vyapatiṣyat iti ca evamādi nindā virodhāt spaṣṭe ca upasaṃhāra sthe samasta upāsana avagame tad abhāvasya pūrvapakṣe vaktum aśakya tvāt sautrasya ca jyāyastva vacanasya pramāṇavat tva abhiprāyeṇa api upapadyamāna tvāt
nānā śabda ādi bhedāt
śabda ādi bheda adhikaraṇam
pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe satyām api sutejaḥ prabhṛtīnām phala bheda śrutau samastasya upāsanam jyāyaḥ iti uktam
atas prāptā buddhiḥ anyāni api bhinna śrutīni upāsanāni samasya upāsiṣyante iti
api ca na eva vedya abhede vidyā bhedaḥ vijñātum śakyate
vedyam hi rūpam vidyāyāḥ dravya daivatam iva yāgasya
vedyaḥ ca ekaḥ eva īśvaraḥ śruti nānātve pi avagamyate manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ kam brahma kham brahma satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evamādiṣu tathā ekaḥ eva prāṇaḥ prāṇaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ prāṇaḥ vāva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca prāṇaḥ ha pitā prāṇaḥ mātā iti evamādiṣu
vedya eka tvāt ca vidyā eka tvam
śruti nānātvam api asmin pakṣe guṇa antara paratvāt na anarthakam
tasmāt sva para śākhā vihitam eka vedya vyapāśrayam guṇa jātam upasaṃhartavyam vidyā kārtsnyāya iti evam prāpte pratipādyate nānā iti
vedya abhede pi evaṃjātīyakā vidyā bhinnā bhavitum arhati
kutas
śabda ādi bhedāt
bhavati hi śabda bhedaḥ vedaḥ upāsīta sa kratum kurvīta iti evamādiḥ
śabda bhedaḥ ca karma bheda hetuḥ samadhigataḥ purastāt śabda antare karma bhedaḥ kṛta anubandha tvāt iti
ādi grahaṇāt guṇa ādayaḥ pi yathāsaṃbhavam bheda hetavaḥ yojayitavyāḥ
nanu vedaḥ ityādiṣu śabda bhedaḥ eva avagamyate na yajati ityādi vat artha bhedaḥ sarveṣām eva eṣām manaḥ vṛtti artha tva abhedāt artha antara asaṃbhavāt ca
tat katham śabda bhedāt vidyā bhedaḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ manaḥ vṛtti artha tva abhede pi anubandha bhedāt vedya bhede sati vidyā bheda upapatteḥ
ekasya api īśvarasya upāsyasya prati prakaraṇam vyāvṛttāḥ guṇāḥ śiṣyante
tathā ekasya api prāṇasya tatra tatra upāsyasya abhede anyādṛś guṇaḥ nyatra upāsitavyaḥ anyādṛś guṇaḥ ca anyatra iti evam anubandha bhedāt vidhi bhede sati vidyā bhedaḥ vijñāyate
na ca atra ekaḥ vidyā vidhiḥ itare guṇa vidhayaḥ iti śakyam vaktum vinigamanāyām hetu abhāvāt aneka tvāt ca prati prakaraṇam guṇānām prāpta vidyā anuvādena vidhāna anupapatteḥ
na ca asmin pakṣe samānāḥ santaḥ satya kāma ādayaḥ guṇāḥ asakṛt śrāvayitavyāḥ
prati prakaraṇam ca idaṃkāmena idam upāsitavyam idaṃkāmena ca idam iti nairākāṅkṣya avagamāt na ekavākya tā āpattiḥ
na ca atra vaiśvānara vidyāyām iva samasta codanā aparā asti yad balena prati prakaraṇa vartīni avayava upāsanāni bhūtvā ekavākya tām iyuḥ
vedya ekatva nimitte ca vidyā ekatve sarvatra niraṅkuśe pratijñāyamāne samasta guṇa upasaṃhāraḥ śakyaḥ pratijñāyeta
tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate nānā śabda ādi bhedāt iti
sthite ca etasmin adhikaraṇe sarva vedānta pratyayam ityādi draṣṭavyam
vikalpaḥ viśiṣṭa phala tvāt
vikalpa adhikaraṇam
sthite vidyā bhede vicāryate kim āsām icchayā samuccayaḥ vikalpaḥ vā syāt athavā vikalpaḥ eva niyamena iti
tatra sthita tvāt tāvat vidyā bhedasya na samuccaya niyame kiṃcid kāraṇam asti
nanu bhinnānām api agnihotra darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīnām samuccaya niyamaḥ dṛśyate na eṣa doṣaḥ
nitya tā śrutiḥ hi tatra kāraṇam
na evam vidyānām kācid nityatā śrutiḥ asti
tasmāt na samuccaya niyamaḥ
na api vikalpa niyamaḥ vidyā antara adhikṛtasya vidyā antara a pratiṣedhāt
pāriśeṣyāt yāthākāmyam āpadyate
nanu aviśiṣṭa phala tvāt āsām vikalpaḥ nyāyyaḥ
tathā hi manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ kam brahma kham brahma satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evamādyāḥ tulya vat īśvara tva prāpti phalāḥ lakṣyante na eṣa doṣaḥ samāna phaleṣu api svarga ādi sādhaneṣu karmasu yāthākāmya darśanāt
tasmāt yāthākāmya prāptau ucyate vikalpaḥ eva āsām bhavitum arhati na samuccayaḥ
kasmāt
a viśiṣṭa phala tvāt
a viśiṣṭam hi āsām phalam upāsya viṣaya sākṣātkaraṇam
ekena ca upāsanena sākṣātkṛte upāsye viṣaye īśvara ādau dvitīyam anarthakam
api ca asaṃbhavaḥ eva sākṣātkaraṇasya samuccaya pakṣe citta vikṣepa hetu tvāt
sākṣātkaraṇa sādhyam ca vidyā phalam darśayanti śrutayaḥ yasya syāt addhā na vicikitsā asti iti devaḥ bhūtvā devān apyeti iti ca evamādyāḥ
smṛtayaḥ ca sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ iti evamādyāḥ
tasmāt a viśiṣṭa phalānām vidyānām anyatamām ādāya tatparaḥ syāt yāvat upāsya viṣaya sākṣātkaraṇena tad phalam prāptam iti
kāmyāḥ tu yathākāmam samuccīyeran na vā pūrva hetu abhāvāt
kāmya adhikaraṇam
a viśiṣṭa phala tvāt iti asya pratyudāharaṇam
yāsu punar kāmyāsu vidyāsu sa yaḥ etam evam vāyum diśām vatsam veda na putra rodam roditi sa yaḥ nāma brahma iti upāste yāvat nāmnaḥ gatam tatra asya yathākāma cāraḥ bhavati iti ca evamādyāsu kriyā vat adṛṣṭena ātmanā ātmīyam phalam sādhayantīṣu sākṣātkaraṇa apekṣā na asti
tāḥ yathākāmam samuccīyeran na vā samuccīyeran pūrva hetu abhāvāt pūrvasya a viśiṣṭa phala tvāt ityasya vikalpa hetoḥ abhāvāt
aṅgeṣu yathā āśraya bhāvaḥ
yathā āśraya bhāva adhikaraṇam
karma aṅgeṣu udgītha ādiṣu ye āśritāḥ pratyayāḥ veda traya vihitāḥ kim te samuccīyeran kim vā yathākāmam syuḥ iti saṃśaye yathā āśraya bhāvaḥ iti āha
yathā eva eṣām āśrayāḥ stotra ādayaḥ saṃbhūya bhavanti evam pratyayāḥ api āśraya tantra tvāt pratyayānām
śiṣṭeḥ ca
yathā vā āśrayāḥ stotra ādayaḥ triṣu vedeṣu śiṣyante evam āśritāḥ api pratyayāḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ aṅgānām tad āśrayāṇām ca pratyayānām iti arthaḥ
samāhārāt
hotṛṣadanāt ha eva api durudgītam anusamāharati iti ca praṇava udgītha eka tva vijñāna māhātmyāt udgātā sva karmaṇi utpannam kṣatam hautrāt karmaṇaḥ pratisamādadhāti iti bruvan veda antara uditasya pratyayasya veda antara udita padārtha saṃbandha sāmānyāt sarva veda udita pratyaya upasaṃhāram sūcayati iti liṅga darśanam
guṇa sādhāraṇya śruteḥ ca
vidyā guṇam ca vidyā āśrayam santam oṃkāram veda traya sādhāraṇam śrāvayati tena iyam trayī vidyā vartate om iti āśrāvayati om iti śaṃsati om iti udgāyati iti ca
tatas ca āśraya sādhāraṇyāt āśrita sādhāraṇyam iti liṅga darśanam eva
athavā guṇa sādhāraṇya śruteḥ ca iti
yadi ime karma guṇāḥ udgītha ādayaḥ sarve sarva prayoga sādhāraṇāḥ na syuḥ na syāt tatas tad āśrayāṇām pratyayānām sahabhāvaḥ
te tu udgītha ādayaḥ sarva aṅga grāhiṇā prayoga vacanena sarve sarva prayoga sādhāraṇāḥ śrāvyante
tatas ca āśraya sahabhāvāt pratyaya sahabhāvaḥ iti
na vā tad sahabhāva aśruteḥ
na vā iti pakṣa vyāvartanam
na yathā āśraya bhāvaḥ āśritānām upāsanānām bhavitum arhati
kutas
tad sahabhāva aśruteḥ
yathā hi tri veda vihitānām aṅgānām stotra ādīnām sahabhāvaḥ śrūyate graham vā gṛhītvā camasam vā unnīya stotram upākaroti stutam anuśaṃsati prastotar sāma gāya hotar etat yaje ityādinā
na evam upāsanānām sahabhāva śrutiḥ asti
nanu prayoga vacanaḥ eṣām sahabhāvam prāpayet na iti brūmaḥ puruṣa artha tvāt upāsanānām
prayoga vacanaḥ hi kratu arthānām udgītha ādīnām sahabhāvam prāpayet
udgītha ādi upāsanāni tu kratu artha āśrayāṇi api godohana ādi vat puruṣa arthāni iti avocāma pṛthak hi apratibandhaḥ phalam iti atra
ayam eva ca upadeśa āśrayaḥ viśeṣaḥ aṅgānām tad ālambanānām ca upāsanānām yat ekeṣām kratu artha tvam ekeṣām puruṣa artha tvam iti
param ca liṅga dvayam akāraṇam upāsana sahabhāvasya śruti nyāya abhāvāt
na ca pratiprayogam āśraya kārtsnya upasaṃhārāt āśritānām api tathātvam vijñātum śakyam a tad prayukta tvāt upāsanānām āśraya tantrāṇi api hi upāsanāni kāmam āśraya abhāve mā bhūvan
na tu āśraya sahabhāvena sahabhāva niyamam arhanti tad sahabhāva aśruteḥ eva
tasmāt yathākāmam eva upāsanāni anuṣṭhīyeran
darśanāt ca
darśayati ca śrutiḥ asahabhāvam pratyayānām evaṃvid ha vai brahmā yajñam yajamānam sarvān ca ṛtvijaḥ bhirakṣati iti
sarva pratyaya upasaṃhāre hi sarve sarva vidaḥ iti na vijñānavatā brahmaṇā paripālya tvam itareṣām saṃkīrtyeta
tasmāt yathākāmam upāsanānām samuccayaḥ vikalpaḥ vā iti
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ dhyāyaḥ
caturthaḥ pādaḥ
puruṣa arthaḥ taḥ śabdāt iti bādarāyaṇaḥ
puruṣa artha adhikaraṇam
te iti
asmāt vedānta vihitāt ātma jñānāt svatantrāt puruṣa arthaḥ sidhyati iti bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
kutas etat avagamyate
śabdāt iti āha
tathā hi tarati śokam ātma vid sa yaḥ ha vai tat paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati brahma vid āpnoti param ācāryavān puruṣaḥ veda tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣye saṃpatsye yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā iti upakramya sa sarvān ca lokān āpnoti sarvān ca kāmān yaḥ tam ātmānam anuvidya vijānāti iti
ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ iti upakramya etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ kevalāyāḥ vidyāyāḥ puruṣa artha hetu tvam śrāvayati
atha atra pratyavatiṣṭhate
śeṣa tvāt puruṣa artha vādaḥ yathā nyeṣu iti jaiminiḥ
kartṛ tvena ātmanaḥ karma śeṣa tvāt tad vijñānam api vrīhi prokṣaṇa ādi vat viṣaya dvāreṇa karma saṃbandhi eva iti atas tasmin avagata prayojane ātma jñāne yā phala śrutiḥ sā arthavādaḥ iti jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
yathā anyeṣu dravya saṃskāra karmasu yasya parṇa mayī juhūḥ bhavati na sa pāpam ślokam śrṛṇoti yat āṅkte cakṣuḥ eva bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte yat prayāja anūyājāḥ ijyante varma vai etat yajñasya kriyate varma yajamānāya bhrātṛvya abhibhūtyai iti evaṃjātīyakā phala śrutiḥ arthavādaḥ tadvat
katham punar asya an ārabhya adhītasya ātma jñānasya prakaraṇa ādīnām anyatamena api hetunā vinā kratu praveśaḥ āśaṅkyate
kartṛ dvāreṇa vākyāt tad vijñānasya kratu saṃbandhaḥ iti ced na vākyāt viniyoga anupapatteḥ avyabhicāriṇā hi kenacid dvāreṇa an ārabhya adhītānām api vākya nimittaḥ kratu saṃbandhaḥ
kartā tu vyabhicāri dvāram laukika vaidika karma sādhāraṇyāt
tasmāt na tad dvāreṇa ātma jñānasya kratu saṃbandha siddhiḥ iti na vyatireka vijñānasya vaidikebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ nyatra anupayogāt
na hi deha vyatirikta ātma jñānam laukikeṣu karmasu upayujyate sarvathā dṛṣṭa artha pravṛtti upapatteḥ
vaidikeṣu tu dehapāta uttara kāla phaleṣu deha vyatirikta ātma jñānam antareṇa pravṛttiḥ na upapadyate iti upayujyate vyatireka vijñānam
nanu apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇāt asaṃsāri ātma viṣayam aupaniṣadam darśanam na pravṛtti aṅgam syāt na priya ādi saṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇaḥ eva ātmanaḥ draṣṭavya tva upadeśāt
apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇam tu stuti artham bhaviṣyati
nanu tatra tatra prasādhitam etat adhikam asaṃsāri brahma jagat kāraṇam
tat eva ca saṃsāriṇaḥ ātmanaḥ pāramārthikam svarūpam upaniṣatsu upadiśyate iti satyam prasādhitam
tasya eva tu sthūṇā nikhanana vat phala dvāreṇa ākṣepa samādhāne kriyete dārḍhyāya
ācāra darśanāt
janakaḥ ha vaidehaḥ bahu dakṣiṇena yajñena īje yakṣyamāṇaḥ vai bhagavantaḥ ham asmi iti evamādīni brahma vidām api anya pareṣu vākyeṣu karma saṃbandha darśanāni bhavanti
tathā uddālaka ādīnām api putra anuśāsana ādi darśanāt gārhasthya saṃbandhaḥ vagamyate
kevalāt ced jñānāt puruṣa artha siddhiḥ syāt kimartham aneka āyāsa samanvitāni karmāṇi te kuryuḥ
atke ced madhu vindeta kimartham parvatam vrajet iti nyāyāt
tad śruteḥ
yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaniṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti ca karma śeṣa tva śravaṇāt vidyāyāḥ na kevalāyāḥ puruṣa artha hetu tvam
samanvārambhaṇāt
tam vidyā karmaṇī samanvārabhete iti ca vidyā karmaṇoḥ phala ārambhe sāhitya darśanāt na svātantryam vidyāyāḥ
tadvataḥ vidhānāt
ācārya kulāt vedam adhītya yathā vidhānam guroḥ karma atiśeṣeṇa abhisamāvṛtya kuṭumbe śucau deśe svādhyāyam adhīyānaḥ iti ca evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ samasta veda artha vijñānavataḥ karma adhikāram darśayati
tasmāt api na vijñānasya svātantryeṇa phala hetu tvam
nanu atra adhītya iti adhyayana mātram vedasya śrūyate na artha vijñānam na eṣa doṣaḥ
dṛṣṭārtha tvāt veda adhyayanam artha avabodha paryantam iti sthitam
niyamāt ca
kurvan evā iha karmāṇi jijīviṣet śatam samāḥ
evam tvayi na anyathā itas sti na karma lipyate nare iti tathā etat vai jarā maryam satram yat agnihotram jarayā vā hi eva asmāt mucyate mṛtyunā vā iti evaṃjātīyakāt niyamāt api karma śeṣa tvam eva vidyāyāḥ iti
evam prāpte pratividhatte
adhika upadeśāt tu bādarāyaṇasya evam tad darśanāt
tu śabdāt pakṣaḥ viparivartate
yat uktam śeṣa tvāt puruṣa artha vādaḥ iti tat na upapadyate
kasmāt
adhika upadeśāt
yadi saṃsārī eva ātmā śārīraḥ kartā bhoktā ca śarīra mātra vyatirekeṇa vedānteṣu upadiṣṭaḥ syāt tatas varṇitena prakāreṇa phala śruteḥ arthavāda tvam syāt
adhikaḥ tāvat śārīrāt ātmanaḥ asaṃsārī īśvaraḥ kartṛ tva ādi saṃsāri dharma rahita upahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇaḥ paramātmā vedya tvena upadiśyate vedānteṣu
na ca tat vijñānam karmaṇām pravartakam bhavati pratyuta karmāṇi ucchinatti iti vakṣyati upamardam ca iti atra
tasmāt puruṣa arthaḥ taḥ śabdāt iti yat matam bhagavataḥ bādarāyaṇasya tat tathā eva tiṣṭhati
na śeṣa tva prabhṛtibhiḥ hetvābhāsaiḥ cālayitum śakyate
tathā hi tam adhikam śārīrāt īśvaram ātmānam darśayanti śrutayaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate mahat bhayam vajram udyatam etasya vai akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi tat aikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tat tejaḥ sṛjate iti evamādyāḥ
yat tu priya ādi saṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇaḥ eva ātmanaḥ vedya tayā anukarṣaṇam ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati
ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ prāṇena prāṇiti sa te ātmā sarva antaraḥ yaḥ eṣa u kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ dṛśyate iti upakramya etam tu eva te bhūyas nuvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca evamādi tat api asya mahataḥ bhūtasya niḥśvasitam etat yat ṛgvedaḥ śanāyā pipāse śokam moham jarām mṛtyum atyeti param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti evamādibhiḥ vākyaśeṣaiḥ satyām eva adhika upadidikṣāyām atyanta abheda abh
pārameśvaram eva hi śārīrasya pāramārthikam svarūpam
upādhi kṛtam tu śārīra tvam tattvam asi na anyat atas sti draṣṭṛ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
sarvam ca etat vistareṇa asmābhiḥ purastāt tatra tatra varṇitam
tulyam tu darśanam
yat tu uktam ācāra darśanāt karma śeṣaḥ vidyā iti atra brūmaḥ tulyam ācāra darśanam a karma śeṣa tve pi vidyāyāḥ
tathā hi śrutiḥ bhavati etat ha sma vai tad vidvāṃsaḥ āhuḥ ṛṣayaḥ kāvaṣeyāḥ kimarthāḥ vayam adhyeṣyāmahe kimarthāḥ vayam yakṣyāmahe
etat ha sma vai tat pūrve vidvāṃsaḥ gnihotram na juhavāṃcakrire etam vai tam ātmānam viditvā brāhmaṇāḥ putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca loka eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam caranti iti evaṃjātīyakā
yājñavalkya ādīnām api brahma vidām a karma niṣṭha tvam dṛśyate etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti ha uktvā yājñavalkyaḥ pravavrāje ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
api ca yakṣyamāṇaḥ vai bhagavantaḥ ham asmi iti etat liṅga darśanam vaiśvānara vidyā viṣayam
saṃbhavati ca sa upādhikāyām brahma vidyāyām karma sāhitya darśanam
na tu atra api karma aṅga tvam asti prakaraṇa ādi abhāvāt
yat punar uktam tat śruteḥ iti atra brūmaḥ
a sārvatrikī
yat eva vidyayā karoti iti eṣā śrutiḥ na sarva vidyā viṣayā prakṛta vidyā abhisaṃbandhāt
prakṛtā ca udgītha vidyā om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta iti atra
vibhāgaḥ śatavat
yat api uktam tam vidyā karmaṇī samanvārabhete iti etat samanvārambha vacanam asvātantrye vidyāyāḥ liṅgam iti tat pratyucyate vibhāgaḥ tra draṣṭavyaḥ vidyā anyam puruṣam anvārabhate karma anyam iti
śatavat yathā śatam ābhyām dīyatām iti ukte vibhajya dīyate pañcāśat ekasmai pañcāśat aparasmai tadvat
na ca idam samanvārambha vacanam mumukṣu viṣayam iti nu kāmayamānaḥ iti saṃsāri viṣaya tva upasaṃhārāt atha a kāmayamānaḥ iti ca mumukṣoḥ pṛthak upakramāt
tatra saṃsāri viṣaye vidyā vihitā pratiṣiddhā ca parigṛhyate viśeṣa abhāvāt
karma api vihitam pratiṣiddham ca yathā prāpta anuvādi tvāt
evam sati avibhāgena api idam samanvārambha vacanam avakalpate
yat ca etat tadvataḥ vidhānāt iti atas uttaram paṭhati
adhyayana mātravataḥ
ācārya kulāt vedam adhītya iti atra adhyayana mātrasya śravaṇāt adhyayana mātra kṣavataḥ eva karma vidhiḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ
nanu evam sati avidyā tvāt anadhikāraḥ karmasu prasajyeta na eṣa doṣaḥ
na vayam adhyayana prabhavam karma avabodhanam adhikāra kāraṇam vārayāmaḥ
kim tarhi aupaniṣadam ātma jñānam svātantryeṇa eva prayojanavat pratīyamānam na karma adhikāra kāraṇatām pratipadyate iti etat pratipādayāmaḥ
yathā ca na kratu antara jñānam kratu antara adhikāreṇa apekṣyate evam etat api draṣṭavyam iti
yat api uktam niyamāt ca iti atra abhidhīyate
na aviśeṣāt
kurvan eva iha karmāṇi jijīviṣet iti evamādiṣu niyama śravaṇeṣu na viduṣaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ sti aviśeṣeṇa niyama vidhānāt
stutaye numatiḥ vā
kurvan eva iha karmāṇi iti atra aparaḥ viśeṣaḥ ākhyāyate
yadi api atra prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt vidvān eva kurvan iti saṃbadhyeta tathā api vidyā stutaye karma anujñānam etat draṣṭavyam
na karma lipyate nare iti hi vakṣyati
etat uktam bhavati yāvajjīvam karma kurvati api tvayi viduṣi puruṣe na karma lepāya bhavati vidyā sāmarthyāt iti tat evam vidyā stūyate
kāmakāreṇa ca eke
api ca eke vidvāṃsaḥ pratyakṣīkṛta vidyā phalāḥ santaḥ tad avaṣṭambhāt phala antara sādhaneṣu prajā ādiṣu prayojana abhāvam parāmṛśanti kāmakāreṇa iti śrutiḥ bhavati vājasaneyinām etat ha sma vai tat pūrve vidvān
upamardam ca
api ca karma adhikāra hetoḥ kriyā kāraka phala lakṣaṇasya samastasya prapañcasya avidyā kṛtasya vidyā sāmarthyāt sva rūpa upamardam āmananti yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet tat kena kam jighret ityādinā
vedānta udita ātma jñāna pūrvikām tu karma adhikāra siddhim pratyāśāsānasya karma adhikāra ucchittiḥ eva prasajyeta
tasmāt api svātantryam vidyāyāḥ
ūrdhvaretaḥsu ca śabde hi
ūrdhvaretaḥsu ca āśrameṣu vidyā śrūyate
na ca tatra karma aṅga tvam vidyāyāḥ upapadyate karma abhāvāt
na hi agnihotra ādīni vaidikāni karmāṇi teṣām santi
syāt etat ūrdhvaretasaḥ āśramāḥ na śrūyante vedaḥ iti tat api nā asti
te pi hi vaidikeṣu śabdeṣu avagamyante trayaḥ dharma skandhāḥ ye ca ime raṇye śraddhā tapaḥ iti upāsate tapaḥ śraddhe ye hi upavasanti araṇye etam eva pravrājinaḥ lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet iti evamādiṣu
pratipanna apratipanna gārhasthyānām apākṛta anapākṛta ṛṇa trayāṇām ca ūrdhvaretaḥ tvam śruti smṛti prasiddham
tasmāt api svātantryam vidyāyāḥ
parāmarśam jaiminiḥ acodanā ca apavadati hi
parāmarśa adhikaraṇam
trayaḥ dharma skandhāḥ ityādayaḥ ye śabdāḥ ūrdhvaretasām āśramāṇām sadbhāvāya udāhṛtāḥ na te tad pratipādanāya prabhavanti
yatas parāmarśam eṣu śabdeṣu āśrama antarāṇām jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate na vidhim
kutas
na hi atra liṅ ādīnām anyatamaḥ codanā śabdaḥ sti
artha antara para tvam ca eṣu pratyekam upalabhyate
trayaḥ dharma skandhāḥ iti atra tāvat yajñaḥ dhyayanam dānam iti prathamaḥ tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ brahmacārī ācārya kula vāsī tṛtīyaḥ u tyantam ātmānam ācārya kule vasādayan sarve ete puṇya lokāḥ bhavanti iti parāmarśa pūrvakam āśramāṇām anātyantika phala tvam saṃkīrtya ātyantika phala tayā brahma saṃstha tā stūyate brahma saṃsthaḥ mṛta tvam eti iti
nanu parāmarśe pi āśramāḥ gamyante eva satyam gamyante
smṛti ācārābhyām tu teṣām prasiddhiḥ na pratyakṣa śruteḥ
atas ca pratyakṣa śruti virodhe sati an ādaraṇīyāḥ te bhaviṣyanti anadhikṛta viṣayāḥ vā
nanu gārhasthyam api saha eva ūrdhvaretobhiḥ parāmṛṣṭam yajñaḥ dhī ayanam dānam iti prathamaḥ iti satyam evam
tathā api tu gṛhastham prati eva agnihotra ādīnām karmaṇām vidhānāt śruti prasiddham eva hi tad astitvam
tasmāt stuti arthaḥ eva ayam parāmarśaḥ na codanā arthaḥ
api ca apavadati hi pratyakṣā śrutiḥ āśrama antaram vīra hā vai eṣa devānām yaḥ gnim udvāsayate ācāryāya priyam dhanam āhṛtya prajā tantum mā vyavacchetsīḥ na a putrasya lokaḥ sti iti tat sarve paśavaḥ viduḥ iti evamādyā
tathā ye ca ime raṇye śraddhā tapaḥ iti upāsate tapaḥ śraddhe ye hi upavasanti araṇye iti ca deva yāna upadeśaḥ na āśrama antara upadeśaḥ
saṃdigdham ca āśrama antara abhidhānam tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ iti evamādiṣu
tathā etam eva pravrājinaḥ lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti iti loka saṃstavaḥ yam na pārivrājya vidhiḥ
nanu brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet iti vispaṣṭam idam pratyakṣam pārivrājya vidhānam jābālānām satyam evam etat
an apekṣya tu etām śrutim ayam vicāraḥ iti draṣṭavyam
anuṣṭheyam bādarāyaṇaḥ sāmya śruteḥ
anuṣṭheyam āśrama antaram bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate vede śravaṇāt agnihotra ādīnām ca avaśya anuṣṭheya tvāt tad virodhāt anadhikṛta anuṣṭheyam āśrama antaram iti hi imām matim nirākaroti gārhasthya vat eva āśrama antaram api an icchatā pratipattavyam iti manyamānaḥ
kutas
sāmya śruteḥ
samā hi gārhasthyena āśrama antarasya parāmarśa śrutiḥ dṛśyate trayaḥ dharma skandhāḥ ityādyā
yathā iha śruti antara vihitam eva gārhasthyam parāmṛṣṭam evam āśrama antaram api iti pratipattavyam yathā ca śāstra antara prāptayoḥ eva nivīta prācīnāvītayoḥ parāmarśaḥ upavīta vidhi pare vākye
tasmāt tulyam anuṣṭheya tvam gārhasthyena āśrama antarasya
tathā etam eva pravrājinaḥ lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti iti asya veda anuvacana ādibhiḥ samabhivyāhāraḥ
ye ca ime raṇye śraddhā tapaḥ iti upāsate iti asya ca pañcāgni vidyayā
yat tu uktam tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ ityādiṣu āśrama antara abhidhānam saṃdigdham iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ niścaya kāraṇa sadbhāvāt
trayaḥ dharma skandhāḥ iti hi dharma skandha tri tvam pratijñātam
na ca yajña ādayaḥ bhūyāṃsaḥ dharmāḥ utpatti bhinnāḥ santaḥ anyatra āśrama saṃbandhāt tritve ntarbhāvayitum śakyante
tatra yajña ādi liṅgaḥ gṛhāśramaḥ ekaḥ dharma skandhaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ brahmacārī iti ca spaṣṭaḥ āśrama nirdeśaḥ tapaḥ iti api kaḥ nyaḥ tapaḥ pradhānāt āśramāt dharma skandhaḥ bhyupagamyeta
ye ca ime raṇye iti ca araṇya liṅgāt śraddhā tapobhyām āśrama gṛhītiḥ
tasmāt parāmarśe pi anuṣṭheyam āśrama antaram
vidhiḥ vā dhāraṇa vat
vidhiḥ vā ayam āśrama antarasya na parāmarśa mātram
nanu vidhi tva abhyupagame eka vākya tā pratītiḥ uparudhyeta
pratīyate caṃ atra eka vākya tā puṇya loka phalāḥ trayaḥ dharma skandhāḥ brahma saṃstha tā tu amṛta tva phalā iti satyam etat
satīm api tu ekavākyatā pratītim parityajya vidhiḥ eva abhyupagantavyaḥ apūrva tvāt vidhi antarasya adarśanāt vispaṣṭāt ca āśrama antara pratyayāt guṇavāda kalpanayā ekavākyatva yojana anupapatteḥ
dhāraṇa vat yathā adhastāt samidham dhārayan anudravet upari hi devebhyaḥ dhārayati iti atra satyām api adhas dhāraṇena eka vākya tā pratītau vidhīyate eva upari dhāraṇam apūrva tvāt
tathā ca uktam śeṣa lakṣaṇe vidhiḥ tu dhāraṇe pūrva tvāt iti
tadvat iha api āśrama parāmarśa śrutiḥ vidhiḥ eva iti kalpyate
yadā api parāmarśaḥ eva ayam āśrama antarāṇām tadā api brahma saṃstha tā tāvat saṃstava sāmarthyāt avaśyam vidheyā abhyupagantavyā
sā ca kim caturṣu āśrameṣu yasya kasya cit āhosvit parivrājakasya eva iti vivektavyam
yadi ca brahmacarya anteṣu āśrameṣu parāmṛśyamāneṣu parivrājakaḥ u pi parāmṛṣṭaḥ tatas caturṇām api āśramāṇām parāmṛṣṭa tva aviśeṣāt anāśrami tva anupapatteḥ ca yaḥ kaścid caturṣu āśrameṣu brahma saṃsthaḥ bhaviṣyati
atha na parāmṛṣṭaḥ tatas pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāj eva brahma saṃsthaḥ iti setsyati
tatra tapaḥ śabdena vaikhānasa grāhiṇā parāmṛṣṭaḥ parivrāj api iti kecid
tat ayuktam
na hi satyām gatau vānaprastha viśeṣaṇena parivrājakaḥ grahaṇam arhati
yathā atra brahmacāri gṛhamedhinau asādhāraṇena eva svena svena viśeṣaṇena viśeṣitau evam bhikṣu vaikhānasau api iti yuktam
tapaḥ ca asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ vānaprasthānām kāya kleśa pradhāna tvāt tapaḥ śabdasya tatra rūḍheḥ
bhikṣoḥ tu dharmaḥ indriya saṃyama ādiḥ lakṣaṇayā eva tapaḥ śabdena abhilapyeta
catuṣṭvena ca prasiddhāḥ āśramāḥ tri tvena parāmṛśyante iti anyāyyam
api ca bheda vyapadeśaḥ bhavati trayaḥ ete puṇya loka bhājaḥ ekaḥ mṛta tva bhāj iti
pṛthaktve ca bheda vyapadeśaḥ
na hi evam bhavati devadatta yajñadattau manda prajñau anyataraḥ tu anayoḥ mahā prajñaḥ iti
bhavati tu evam devadatta yajñadattau manda prajñau viṣṇumitraḥ tu mahā prajñaḥ iti
tasmāt pūrve trayaḥ āśramiṇaḥ puṇya loka bhājaḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāj amṛta tva bhāj
katham punar brahma saṃstha śabdaḥ yogāt pravartamānaḥ sarvatra saṃbhavan parivrājakaḥ eva avatiṣṭheta
rūḍhi abhyupagame ca āśrama mātrāt amṛta tva prāpteḥ jñāna ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ iti atrā ucyate brahma saṃsthaḥ iti hi brahmaṇi parisamāptiḥ ananya vyāpāra tā rūpam tad niṣṭhatvam abhidhīyate
tat ca trayāṇām āśramāṇām na saṃbhavati sva āśrama vihita karma ananuṣṭhāne pratyavāya śravaṇāt
parivrājakasya tu sarva karma saṃnyāsāt pratyavāyaḥ na saṃbhavati an anuṣṭhāna nimittaḥ
śama dama ādiḥ tu tadīyaḥ dharmaḥ brahma saṃsthāyāḥ upodbalakaḥ na virodhī
brahma niṣṭha tvam eva hi tasya śama dama ādi upabṛṃhitam sva āśrama vihitam karma
yajña ādīni ca itareṣām
tad vyatikrame ca tasya pratyavāyaḥ
tathā ca nyāsaḥ iti brahmā brahmā hi paraḥ paraḥ hi brahmā
tāni vai etāni avarāṇi tapāṃsi nyāsaḥ eva atyarecayat vedānta vijñāna su niścita arthāḥ saṃnyāsa yoga ādi atayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ smṛtayaḥ ca tad buddhayaḥ tad ātmānaḥ tad niṣṭhāḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ ityādyāḥ brahma saṃsthasya karma abhāvam darśayanti
tasmāt parivrājakasya āśrama mātrāt amṛta tva prāpteḥ jñāna ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ iti eṣaḥ u pi doṣaḥ na avatarati
tat evam parāmarśe itareṣām āśramāṇām pārivrājyam tāvat brahma saṃstha tā lakṣaṇam labhyeta eva
an apekṣya eva jābāla śrutim āśrama antara vidhāyinīm ayam ācāryeṇa vicāraḥ pravartitaḥ
vidyate eva tu āśrama antara vidhi śrutiḥ pratyakṣā brahmacaryam samāpya gṛhī bhavet gṛhī bhūtvā vanī bhavet vanī bhūtvā pravrajet
yadi vā itarathā brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet gṛhāt vā vanāt vā iti
na ca iyam śrutiḥ anadhikṛta viṣayā śakyā vaktum aviśeṣa śravaṇāt pṛthak vidhānāt ca anadhikṛtānām atha punar r eva vratī vā a vratī vā snātakaḥ vā a snātakaḥ vā utsanna agniḥ anagnikaḥ vā ityādinā
brahma jñāna paripāka aṅga tvāt ca pārivrājyasya na anadhikṛta viṣaya tvam tat ca darśayati atha parivrāj vivarṇa vāsāḥ muṇḍaḥ parigrahaḥ śuciḥ adrohī bhaikṣāṇaḥ brahma bhūyāya bhavati iti
tasmāt siddhāḥ ūrdhvaretasām āśramāḥ
siddham ca ūrdhvaretaḥsu vidhānāt vidyāyāḥ svātantryam iti
stuti mātram upādānāt iti ced na apūrva tvāt
stuti mātra adhikaraṇam
saḥ eṣa rasānām rasatamaḥ paramaḥ parārdhyaḥ ṣṭamaḥ yat udgīthaḥ iyam eva ṛc agniḥ sāma ayam vāva lokaḥ eṣaḥ gniḥ citaḥ tat idam eva uktham iyam eva pṛthivī iti evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ kim udgītha ādeḥ stuti arthāḥ āhosvit upāsanā vidhi arthāḥ iti asmin saṃśaye stuti arthāḥ iti yuktam udgītha ādīni karma aṅgāni upādāya śravaṇāt
yathā iyam eva juhūḥ ādityaḥ kūrmaḥ svargaḥ lokaḥ āhavanīyaḥ ityādyāḥ juhū ādi stuti arthāḥ tadvat iti ced na iti āha
na hi stuti mātram āsām śrutīnām prayojanam yuktam apūrva tvāt
vidhi artha tāyām hi apūrvaḥ rthaḥ vihitaḥ bhavati
stuti artha tāyām tu ānarthakyam eva syāt
vidhāyakasya hi śabdasya vākyaśeṣa bhāvam pratipadyamānā stutiḥ upayujyate iti uktam vidhinā tu ekavākya tvāt stuti arthena vidhīnām syuḥ iti atra
pradeśa antara vihitānām tu udgītha ādīnām iyam pradeśa antara paṭhitā stutiḥ vākyaśeṣa bhāvam a pratipadyamānā anarthikā eva syāt
iyam eva juhūḥ ityādi tu vidhi saṃnidhau eva āmnātam iti vaiṣamyam
tasmāt vidhi arthāḥ eva evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ
bhāva śabdāt ca
udgītham upāsīta sāma upāsīta aham uktham asmi iti vidyāt ityādayaḥ ca vispaṣṭāḥ vidhi śabdāḥ śrūyante
te ca stuti mātra prayojana tāyām vyāhanyeran
tathā ca nyāya vidām smaraṇam kuryāt kriyeta kartavyam bhavet syāt iti pañcamam
etat syāt sarva vedeṣu niyatam vidhi lakṣaṇam iti
liṅ ādi arthaḥ vidhiḥ iti manyamānāḥ te evam smaranti
prati prakaraṇam ca phalāni śrāvyante āpayitā ha vai kāmānām bhavati eṣa hi eva kāma āgānasya iṣṭe kalpante ha asmai lokāḥ ūrdhvāḥ ca āvṛttāḥ ca ityādīni
tasmāt api upāsana vidhāna arthāḥ udgītha ādi śrutayaḥ
pāriplava arthāḥ iti ced na viśeṣita tvāt
pāriplava adhikaraṇam
atha ha yājñavalkyasya dve bhārye babhūvatuḥ maitreyī ca kātyāyanī ca pratardanaḥ ha vai daivodāsiḥ indrasya priyam dhāma upajagāma jānaśrutiḥ ha pautrāyaṇaḥ śraddhā deyaḥ bahu dāyī bahu pākyaḥ āsa iti evamādiṣu vedānta paṭhiteṣu ākhyāneṣu saṃśayaḥ kim imāni pāriplava prayoga arthāni āhosvit saṃnihita vidyā pratipatti arthāni iti
pāriplava arthāḥ imāḥ ākhyāna śrutayaḥ ākhyāna sāmānyāt ākhyāna prayogasya ca pāriplave codita tvāt
tatas ca vidyā pradhāna tvam vedāntānām na syāt mantra vat prayoga śeṣa tvāt iti ced tat na
kasmāt
viśeṣita tvāt pāriplavam ācakṣīta iti hi prakṛtya manuḥ vaivasvataḥ rājā iti evamādīni kānicid eva ākhyānāni tatra viśeṣyante
ākhyāna sāmānyāt ced sarva gṛhītiḥ syāt anarthakam eva idam viśeṣaṇam bhavet
tasmāt na pāriplava arthāḥ etāḥ ākhyāna śrutayaḥ
tathā ca eka vākya tā upabandhāt
asati ca pāriplava artha tve ākhyānānām saṃnihita vidyā pratipādana upayogi tā eva nyāyyā eka vākya tā upabandhāt
tathā hi tatra tatra saṃnihitābhiḥ vidyābhiḥ ekavākyatā dṛśyate prarocana upayogāt pratipatti saukarya upayogāt ca maitreyībrāhmaṇe tāvat ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ ityādyayā vidyayā ekavākyatā dṛśyate
prātardane pi prāṇaḥ smi prajñā ātmā iti ādyayā
jānaśrutiḥ iti atra api vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ ityādyayā yathā saḥ ātmanaḥ vapām udakhidat iti evamādīnām karma śruti gatānām ākhyānānām saṃnihita vidhi stuti artha tā tadvat
tasmāt na pāriplava artha tvam
atas eva ca agni indhana ādi anapekṣā
agni indhana ādi adhikaraṇam
śabdāt iti etat vyavahitam api saṃbhavāt atas iti parāmṛśyate
atas eva ca vidyāyāḥ puruṣa artha hetu tvāt agni indhana ādīni āśrama karmāṇi vidyayā svārtha siddhau na apekṣitavyāni iti ādyasya eva adhikaraṇasya phalam upasaṃharati adhika vivakṣayā
sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśva vat
sarva apekṣā adhikaraṇam
idam idānīm cintyate kim vidyāyāḥ atyantam evā anapekṣā āśrama karmaṇām uta asti kācid apekṣā iti
tatra atas eva agni indhana ādīni āśrama karmāṇi vidyayā sva artha siddhau na apekṣyante
evam atyantam eva anapekṣāyām prāptāyām idam ucyate sarva apekṣā ca iti
apekṣate ca vidyā sarvāṇi āśrama karmāṇi na atyantam anapekṣā eva
nanu viruddham idam vacanam apekṣate ca āśrama karmāṇi vidyā na apekṣate ca iti
na iti brūmaḥ
utpannā hi vidyā phala siddhim prati na kiṃcid anyat apekṣate utpattim prati tu apekṣate
kutas
yajña ādi śruteḥ
tathā hi śrutiḥ tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣanti yajñena dānena tapasā anāśakena iti yajña ādīnām vidyā sādhana bhāvam darśayati
vividiṣā saṃyogāt ca eṣām utpatti sādhana bhāvaḥ vasīyate
atha yat yajñaḥ iti ācakṣate brahmacaryam eva tat iti atra ca vidyā sādhana bhūtasya brahmacaryasya yajña ādibhiḥ saṃstavāt yajña ādīnām api hi sādhana bhāvaḥ sūcyate
sarve vedāḥ yat padam āmananti tapāṃsi sarvāṇi ca yat vadanti
yat icchantaḥ brahmacaryam caranti tat te padam saṃgraheṇa bravīmi iti evamādyā ca śrutiḥ āśrama karmaṇām vidyā sādhana bhāvam sūcayati
smṛtiḥ api kaṣāya paktiḥ karmāṇi jñānam tu paramā gatiḥ
kaṣāye karmabhiḥ pakve tatas jñānam pravartate iti evamādyā
aśva vat iti yogyatā nidarśanam yathā ca yogyatā vaśena aśvaḥ na lāṅgala ākarṣaṇe yujyate rathacaryāyām tu yujyate evam āśrama karmāṇi vidyayā phala siddhau na apekṣyante utpattau ca apekṣyante iti
śama dama ādi upetaḥ syāt tathā api tu tad vidheḥ tad aṅga tayā teṣām avaśya anuṣṭheya tvāt
yadi kaścid manyeta yajña ādīnām vidyā sādhana bhāvaḥ na nyāyyaḥ vidhi abhāvāt
yajñena vividiṣanti iti evaṃjātīyakā hi śrutiḥ anuvāda svarūpā vidyā abhiṣṭava parā na yajña ādi vidhi parā ittham mahābhāgā vidyā yat yajña ādibhiḥ etām avāptum icchanti iti tathā api tu śama dama ādi upetaḥ syāt vidyā arthī tasmāt evaṃvid śāntaḥ dāntaḥ uparataḥ titikṣuḥ samāhitaḥ bhūtvā ātmani eva ātmānam paśyati iti vidyā sādhana tvena śama dama ādīnām vidhānāt vihitānām ca avaśya anuṣṭheya tvāt
nanu atra api śama ādi upetaḥ bhūtvā paśyati iti vartamāna apadeśaḥ upalabhyate na vidhiḥ na iti brūmaḥ tasmāt iti prakṛta praśaṃsā parigrahāt vidhi tva pratīteḥ
paśyet iti ca mādhyaṃdināḥ vispaṣṭam eva vidhim adhīyate
tasmāt yajña ādi anapekṣāyām api śama ādīni apekṣitavyāni
yajña ādīni api tu apekṣitavyāni yajña ādi śruteḥ eva
nanu uktam yajña ādibhiḥ vividiṣanti iti atra na vidhiḥ upalabhyate iti satyam uktam
tathā api tu apūrva tvāt saṃyogasya vidhiḥ parikalpyate
na hi ayam yajña ādīnām vividiṣā saṃyogaḥ pūrvam prāptaḥ yena anūdyeta
tasmāt pūṣā prapiṣṭa bhāgaḥ dantakaḥ hi iti evamādiṣu ca aśruta vidhikeṣu api vākyeṣu apūrva tvāt vidhim parikalpya pauṣṇam peṣaṇam vikṛtau pratīyeta ityādi vicāraḥ prathame tantre pravartitaḥ
tathā ca uktam vidhiḥ vā dhāraṇa vat iti
smṛtiṣu api bhagavadgītā ādyāsu an abhisaṃdhāya phalam anuṣṭhitāni yajña ādīni mumukṣoḥ jñāna sādhanāni bhavanti iti prapañcitam
tasmāt yajña ādīni śama dama ādīni ca yathāśramam sarvāṇi eva āśrama karmāṇi vidyā utpattau apekṣitavyāni
tatra api evaṃvid iti vidyā saṃyogāt pratyāsannāni vidyā sādhanāni śama ādīni vividiṣā saṃyogāt tu bāhyatarāṇi yajña ādīni iti vivektavyam
sarva anna anumatiḥ ca prāṇātyaye tad darśanāt
sarva anna anumati adhikaraṇam
prāṇa saṃvāde śrūyate chandogānām na ha vai evaṃvidi kiṃcana anannam bhavati iti
tathā vājasaneyinām na ha vai asya an annam jagdham bhavati na an annam pratigṛhītam iti
sarvam asya adanīyam eva bhavati iti arthaḥ
kim idam sarva anna anujñānam śama ādi vat vidyā aṅgam vidhīyate uta stuti artham saṃkīrtyate iti saṃśaye vidhiḥ iti tāvat prāptam
tathā hi pravṛtti viśeṣa karaḥ upadeśaḥ bhavati
atas prāṇa vidyā saṃnidhānāt tad aṅga tvena iyam niyama nivṛttiḥ upadiśyate
nanu evam sati bhakṣya abhakṣya vibhāga śāstra vyāghātaḥ syāt na eṣa doṣaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvāt bādha upapatteḥ
yathā prāṇi hiṃsā pratiṣedhasya paśu saṃjñapana vidhinā bādhaḥ yathā ca na kāṃcana striyam pariharet tat vratam iti anena vāmadevya vidyā viṣayeṇa sarva strī a parihāra vacanena sāmānya viṣayam gamya agamya vibhāga śāstram bādhyate evam anena api prāṇa vidyā viṣayeṇa sarva anna bhakṣaṇa vacanena bhakṣya abhakṣya vibhāga śāstram bādhyeta iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na idam sarva anna anujñānam vidhīyate iti
na hi atra vidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ upalabhyate na ha vai evaṃvidi kiṃcana anannam bhavati iti vartamāna apadeśāt
na ca asatyām api vidhi pratītau pravṛtti viśeṣa kara tva lobhena eva vidhiḥ abhyupagantum śakyate
api ca śva ādi maryādam prāṇasya annam iti uktvā idam ucyate na evaṃvidaḥ kiṃcid anannam bhavati iti
na ca śva ādi maryādam annam mānuṣeṇa dehena upabhoktum śakyate
śakyate tu prāṇasya annam idam sarvam iti vicintayitum
tasmāt prāṇa anna vijñāna praśaṃsā arthaḥ yam arthavādaḥ na sarva anna anujñāna vidhiḥ
tat darśayati sarva anna anumatiḥ ca prāṇātyaye iti
etat uktam bhavati prāṇa atyayaḥ eva hi parasyām āpadi sarvam annam adanīya tvena abhyanujñāyate tad darśanāt
tathā hi śrutiḥ cākrāyaṇasya ṛṣeḥ kaṣṭāyām avasthāyām abhakṣya bhakṣaṇe pravṛttim darśayati maṭacī hateṣu kuruṣu iti asmin brāhmaṇe cākrāyaṇaḥ kila ṛṣiḥ āpad gataḥ ibhyena sāmi khāditān kulmāṣān cakhāda
anupānam tu tadīyam ucchiṣṭa doṣāt pratyācacakṣe
kāraṇam ca atra uvāca na vai ajīviṣyam imān akhādan iti kāmaḥ me udapānam iti ca
punar ca uttaredyus tān eva sva para ucchiṣṭān paryuṣitān kulmāṣān bhakṣayāṃbabhūva iti
tat etat ucchiṣṭa ucchiṣṭa paryuṣita bhakṣaṇam darśayantyāḥ śruteḥ āśaya atiśayaḥ lakṣyate prāṇa atyaya prasaṅge prāṇa saṃdhāraṇāya abhakṣyam api bhakṣayitavyam iti
svastha avasthāyām tu tat na kartavyam vidyāvatā api iti anupāna pratyākhyānāt gamyate
tasmāt arthavādaḥ na ha vai evaṃvidi iti evamādiḥ
a bādhāt ca
evam ca sati āhāra śuddhau sattva śuddhiḥ iti evamādi bhakṣya abhakṣya vibhāga śāstram abādhitam bhaviṣyati
api ca smaryate
api ca āpadi sarva anna bhakṣaṇam api smaryate viduṣaḥ viduṣaḥ ca aviśeṣeṇa jīvita atyayam āpannaḥ yaḥ nnam atti yatas tatas
lipyate na sa pāpena padma patram iva ambhasā iti
tathā madyam nityam brāhmaṇaḥ surā pasya brāhmaṇasya uṣṇām āsiñceyuḥ surā pāḥ kṛmayaḥ bhavanti abhakṣya bhakṣaṇāt iti ca smaryate varjanam anannasya
śabdaḥ ca a taḥ kāmakāre
śabdaḥ ca anannasya pratiṣedhakaḥ kāmakāra nivṛtti prayojanaḥ kaṭhānām saṃhitāyām śrūyate tasmāt brāhmaṇaḥ surām na pibet iti
saḥ u pi na ha vai evaṃvidi iti asya arthavāda tvāt upapannataraḥ bhavati
tasmāt evaṃjātīyakāḥ arthavādāḥ na vidhayaḥ iti
vihita tvāt ca āśrama karma api
āśrama karma adhikaraṇam
sarva apekṣā ca iti atra āśrama karmaṇām vidyā sādhanatvam avadhāritam
idānīm tu kim amumukṣoḥ api āśrama mātra niṣṭhasya vidyām akāmayamānasya tāni anuṣṭheyāni uta aho na iti cintyate
tatra tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣanti ityādinā āśrama karmaṇām vidyā sādhana tvena vihita tvāt vidyām an icchataḥ phala antaram kāmayamānasya nityāni an anuṣṭheyāni
atha tasya api anuṣṭheyāni na tarhi eṣām vidyā sādhana tvam nitya anitya saṃyoga virodhāt iti asyām prāptau paṭhati āśrama mātra niṣṭhasya api amumukṣoḥ kartavyāni eva nityāni karmāṇi yāvajjīvam agnihotram juhoti ityādinā vihita tvāt
na hi vacanasya atibhāraḥ nāma kaścid asti
atha yat uktam na evam sati vidyā sādhana tvam eṣām syāt iti atas uttaram paṭhati
sahakāri tvena ca
vidyā sahakārīṇi ca etāni syuḥ vihita tvāt eva tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣanti ityādinā
tat uktam sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśva vat iti
na ca idam vidyā sahakāri tva vacanam āśrama karmaṇām prayāja ādi vat vidyā phala viṣayam mantavyam avidhi lakṣaṇa tvāt vidyāyāḥ asādhya tvāt ca vidyā phalasya
vidhi lakṣaṇam hi sādhanam darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi svarga phala siṣādhayiṣayā sahakāri sādhana antaram apekṣate na evam vidyā
tathā ca uktam atas eva ca agni indhana ādi anapekṣāḥ iti
tasmāt utpatti sādhana tve eva eṣām sahakāri tva vācoyuktiḥ
na ca atra nitya anitya saṃyoga virodhaḥ āśaṅkyaḥ karma abhede pi saṃyoga bhedāt
nityaḥ hi ekaḥ saṃyogaḥ yāvat jīva ādi vākya kalpitaḥ na tasya vidyā phala tvam
anityaḥ tu aparaḥ saṃyogaḥ tam etam veda anuvacanena ityādi vākya kalpitaḥ tasya vidyā phala tvam yathā ekasya api khādira tvasya nityena saṃyogena kratu artha tvam anityena saṃyogena puruṣa artha tvam tadvat
sarvathā tu te eva ubhaya liṅgāt
sarvathā api āśrama karma tva pakṣe vidyā sahakāri tva pakṣe ca te eva agnihotra ādayaḥ dharmāḥ anuṣṭheyāḥ
te eva iti avadhārayan ācāryaḥ kim nivartayati
karma bheda śaṅkām iti brūmaḥ
yathā kuṇḍapāyinām ayane māsam agnihotram juhvati iti atra nityāt agnihotrāt karmāntaram upadiśyate na evam iha karma bhedaḥ sti iti arthaḥ
kutas
ubhaya liṅgāt śruti liṅgāt smṛti liṅgāt ca
śruti liṅgam tāvat tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣanti iti siddha vat utpanna rūpāṇi eva yajña ādīni vividiṣāyām viniyuṅkte na tu juhvati ityādi vat apūrvam eṣām rūpam utpādayati iti
smṛti liṅgam api anāśritaḥ karma phalam kāryam karma karoti yaḥ iti vijñāta kartavyatākam eva karma vidyā utpatti artham darśayati
yasya ete ṣṭācatvāriṃśat saṃskārāḥ ityādyā ca saṃskāra tva prasiddhiḥ vaidikeṣu karmasu tad saṃskṛtasya vidyā utpattim abhipretya smṛtau bhavati
tasmāt sādhu idam abheda avadhāraṇam
an abhibhavam ca darśayati
sahakāri tvasya eva etat upodbalakam liṅga darśanam
anabhibhavam ca darśayati śrutiḥ brahmacarya ādi sādhana saṃpannasya rāga ādibhiḥ kleśaiḥ eṣa hi ātmā na naśyati yam brahmacaryeṇa anuvindate ityādinā
tasmāt yajña ādīni āśrama karmāṇi ca bhavanti vidyā sahakārīṇi ca iti sthitam
antarā ca api tu tad dṛṣṭeḥ
vidhura adhikaraṇam
vidhura ādīnām dravya ādi saṃpad rahitānām ca anyatama āśrama pratipatti hīnānām antarāla vartinām kim vidyāyām adhikāraḥ sti kim vā na asti iti saṃśaye na asti iti tāvat prāptam āśrama karmaṇām vidyā hetu tva avadhāraṇāt āśrama karma asaṃbhavāt ca eteṣām iti evam prāpte idam āha antarā ca api tu anāśrami tvena vartamānaḥ vidyāyām adhikriyate
kutas
tad dṛṣṭeḥ raikva vācaknavī prabhṛtīnām evaṃbhūtānām api brahma vid tva śruti upalabdheḥ
api ca smaryate
saṃvarta prabhṛtīnām ca nagna caryā ādi yogāt an apekṣita āśrama karmaṇām api mahā yogi tvam smaryate itihāse
nanu liṅgam idam śruti smṛti darśanam upanyastam
kā nu khalu prāptiḥ iti sā abhidhīyate
viśeṣa anugrahaḥ ca
teṣām api ca vidhura ādīnām aviruddhaiḥ puruṣa mātra saṃbandhibhiḥ japa upavāsa devatā ārādhana ādibhiḥ dharma viśeṣaiḥ anugrahaḥ vidyāyāḥ saṃbhavati
tathā ca smṛtiḥ japyena eva tu saṃsidhyet brāhmaṇaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ
kuryāt anyat na vā kuryāt maitraḥ brāhmaṇaḥ ucyate iti japye dhikāram darśayati
janma antara anuṣṭhitaiḥ api ca āśrama karmabhiḥ saṃbhavati eva vidyāyāḥ anugrahaḥ
tathā ca smṛtiḥ aneka janma saṃsiddhaḥ tatas yāti parām gatim iti janma antara saṃcitān api saṃskāra viśeṣān anugrahītṛn vidyāyām darśayati
dṛṣṭa arthā ca vidyā pratiṣedha abhāva mātreṇa api arthinam adhikaroti śravaṇa ādiṣu
tasmāt vidhura ādīnām api adhikāraḥ na virudhyate
atas tu itarat jyāyaḥ liṃṅgāt ca
atas tu antarāla varti tvāt itarat āśrama varti tvam jyāyaḥ vidyā sādhanam śruti smṛti saṃdṛbdha tvāt
śruti liṅgāt ca  tena  eti SPr3In brahma Cp vid SNM puṇya Cp kṛt SNM taijasaḥ SNM ca
iti
anāśramī na tiṣṭheta dinam ekam api dvijaḥ
saṃvatsaram anāśramī sthitvā kṛcchram ekam caret iti ca smṛti liṅgāt
caturthaḥ dhyāyaḥ
prathamaḥ pādaḥ
āvṛttiḥ asakṛt upadeśāt
āvṛti adhikaraṇam
ātmā vai are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ tam eva dhīraḥ vijñāya prajñām kurvīta saḥ nveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti ca evamādi śravaṇeṣu saṃśayaḥ kim sakṛt pratyayaḥ kartavyaḥ āhosvit āvṛttyā iti
kim tāvat prāptam
sakṛt pratyayaḥ syāt prayāja ādi vat tāvatā śāstrasya kṛtārtha tvāt
a śrūyamāṇāyām hi āvṛttau kriyamāṇāyām a śāstra arthaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavet
nanu asakṛt upadeśāḥ udāhṛtāḥ śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti evamādayaḥ evam api yāvacchabdam āvartayet sakṛt śravaṇam sakṛt mananam sakṛt nididhyāsanam ca iti na atiriktam
sakṛt upadeśeṣu tu vedaḥ upāsīta iti evamādiṣu anāvṛttiḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ pratyaya āvṛttiḥ kartavyā
kutas
asakṛt upadeśāt śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakaḥ hi asakṛt upadeśaḥ pratyaya āvṛttim sūcayati
nanu uktam yāvacchabdam eva āvartayet na adhikam iti na darśana paryavasāna tvāt eṣām
darśana paryavasānāni hi śravaṇa ādīni āvartyamānāni dṛṣṭa arthāni bhavanti yathā avaghāta ādīni taṇḍula ādi niṣpatti paryavasānāni hi tadvat
api ca upāsanam nididhyāsanam ca iti antarṇīta āvṛtti guṇā eva kriyā abhidhīyate
tathā hi loke gurum upāste rājānam upāste iti ca yaḥ tātparyeṇa guru ādīn anuvartate saḥ evam ucyate
tathā dhyāyati proṣita nāthā patim iti yā nirantara smaraṇā patim prati sa utkaṇṭhā sā evam abhidhīyate
vidi upāstyoḥ ca vedānteṣu a vyatirekeṇa prayogaḥ dṛśyate
kvacid vidinā upakramya upāsinā upasaṃharati yathā yaḥ tat veda yat sa veda sa mayā etat uktaḥ iti atra anu me etām bhagavaḥ devatām śādhi yām devatām upāsse iti
kvacid ca upāsinā upakramya vidinā upasaṃharati yathā manaḥ brahma iti upāsīta iti atra bhāti ca tapati ca kīrtyā yaśasā brahmavarcasena yaḥ evam veda iti
tasmāt sakṛt upadeśeṣu api āvṛtti siddhiḥ
asakṛt upadeśaḥ tu āvṛtteḥ sūcakaḥ
liṅgāt ca
liṅgam api pratyaya āvṛttim pratyāyayati
tathā hi udgītha vijñānam prastutya ādityaḥ udgīthaḥ iti etat eka putra tā doṣeṇa apodya raśmīn tvam paryāvartayāt iti raśmi bahu tva vijñānam bahu putra tāyai vidadhat siddha vat pratyaya āvṛttim darśayati
tad sāmānyāt sarva pratyayeṣu āvṛtti siddhiḥ
atra āha bhavatu nāma sādhya phaleṣu pratyayeṣu āvṛttiḥ teṣu āvṛtti sādhyasya atiśayasya saṃbhavāt
yaḥ tu para brahma viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam eva ātma bhūtam param brahma samarpayati tatra kimarthā āvṛttiḥ iti
sakṛt śrutau ca brahma ātmatva pratīti anupapatteḥ āvṛtti abhyupagamaḥ iti ced na āvṛttau api tad anupapatteḥ
yadi hi tat tvam asi iti evaṃjātīyakam vākyam sakṛt śrūyamāṇam brahma ātmatva pratītim na utpādayet tatas tat eva āvartyamānam utpādayiṣyati iti kā pratyāśā syāt
atha ucyeta na kevalam vākyam kaṃcid artham sākṣātkartum śaknoti
atas yukti apekṣam vākyam anubhāvayiṣyati brahma ātmatvam iti tathā api āvṛtti ānarthakyam eva
sā api hi yuktiḥ sakṛt pravṛttā eva svam artham anubhāvayiṣyati
atha api syāt yuktyā vākyena ca sāmānya viṣayam eva vijñānam kriyate na viśeṣa viṣayam
yathā asti me hṛdaye śūlam iti atas vākyāt gātra kampa ādi liṅgāt ca śūla sadbhāva sāmānyam eva paraḥ pratipadyate na viśeṣam anubhavati yathā saḥ eva śūlī
viśeṣa anubhavaḥ ca avidyāyāḥ nivartakaḥ
tad arthā āvṛttiḥ iti ced na asakṛt api tāvat mātre kriyamāṇe viśeṣa vijñāna utpatti asaṃbhavāt
na hi sakṛt prayuktābhyām śāstra yuktibhyām anavagataḥ viśeṣaḥ śata kṛtvas u pi prayujyamānābhyām avagantum śakyate
tasmāt yadi śāstra yuktibhyām viśeṣaḥ pratipādyeta yadi vā sāmānyam eva ubhayathā api sakṛt pravṛtte eva te sva kāryam kurutaḥ iti āvṛtti anupayogaḥ
na ca sakṛt prayukte śāstra yuktī kasyacid api anubhavam na utpādayataḥ iti śakyate niyantum vicitra prajña tvāt pratipattṛṇām
api ca aneka aṃśa upete laukike padārthe sāmānya viśeṣavati ekena avadhānena ekam aṃśam avadhārayati apareṇa aparam iti syāt api abhyāsa upayogaḥ yathā dīrgha prapāṭhaka grahaṇa ādiṣu
na tu nirviśeṣe brahmaṇi sāmānya viśeṣa rahite caitanya mātra ātmake pramā utpattau abhyāsa apekṣā yuktā iti
atrā ucyate bhavet āvṛtti ānarthakyam tam prati yaḥ tat tvam asi iti sakṛt uktam eva brahma ātmatvam anubhavitum śaknuyāt
yaḥ tu na śaknoti tam prati upayujyate eva āvṛttiḥ
tathā hi chāndogye tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti upadiśya bhūyas eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu iti punar punar paricodyamānaḥ tat tat āśaṅkā kāraṇam nirākṛtya tat tvam asi iti eva asakṛt upadiśati
tathā ca śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ ityādi darśitam
nanu uktam sakṛt śrutam ced tattvamasi vākyam svam artham anubhāvayitum na śaknoti tatas āvartyamānam api nā eva śakṣyati iti nā eṣa doṣaḥ
na hi dṛṣṭe nupapannam nāma
dṛśyante hi sakṛt śrutāt vākyāt manda pratītam vākya artham āvartayantaḥ tad tad ābhāsa vyudāsena samyak pratipadyamānāḥ
api ca tat tvam asi iti etat vākyam tvam padārthasya tad padārtha bhāvam ācaṣṭe
tad padena ca prakṛtam sat brahma īkṣitṛ jagataḥ janma ādikāraṇam abhidhīyate satyam jñānam anantam brahma vijñānam ānandam brahma adṛṣṭam draṣṭṛ avijñātam vijñātṛ ajam ajaram amaram a sthūlam an aṇu a hrasvam adīrgham iti ādi śāstra siddham
tatra aja ādi śabdaiḥ janma ādayaḥ bhāva vikārāḥ nivartitāḥ
a sthūla ādi śabdaiḥ ca sthaulya ādayaḥ dravya dharmāḥ
vijñāna ādi śabdaiḥ ca caitanya prakāśa ātmaka tvam uktam
eṣa vyāvṛtta sarva saṃsāra dharmakaḥ nubhava ātmakaḥ brahma saṃjñakaḥ tad padārthaḥ vedānta abhiyuktānām prasiddhaḥ
tathā pratyagātmā śrotā dehāt ārabhya pratyagātma tayā saṃbhāvyamānaḥ caitanya paryanta tvena avadhāritaḥ
tatra yeṣām etau padārthau ajñāna saṃśaya viparyaya pratibaddhau teṣām tat tvam asi iti etat vākyam svārthe pramām na utpādayitum śaknoti padārtha jñāna pūrvaka tvāt vākya artha jñānasya iti atas tān prati eṣṭavyaḥ padārtha viveka prayojanaḥ śāstra yukti abhyāsaḥ
yadi api ca pratipattavyaḥ ātmā niraṃśaḥ tathā api adhyāropitam tasmin bahu aṃśa tvam deha indriya manaḥ buddhi viṣaya vedanā ādi lakṣaṇam
tatra ekena avadhānena ekam aṃśam apohati apareṇa aparam iti yujyate tatra kramavatī pratipattiḥ
tat tu pūrvarūpam eva ātma pratipatteḥ
yeṣām punar nipuṇa matīnām na ajñāna saṃśaya viparyaya lakṣaṇaḥ padārtha viṣayaḥ pratibandhaḥ u sti te śaknuvanti sakṛt uktam eva tattvam asi vākya artham anubhavitum iti tān prati āvṛtti ānarthakyam iṣṭam eva
sakṛt utpannā eva hi ātma pratipattiḥ avidyām nivartayati iti na atra kaścid api kramaḥ bhyupagamyate
satyam evam yujyeta yadi kasyacid evam pratipattiḥ bhavet
balavatī hi ātmanaḥ duḥkhi tva ādi pratipattiḥ
atas na duḥkhi tva ādi abhāvam kaścid pratipadyate iti ced na deha ādi abhimāna vat duḥkhi tva ādi abhimānasya mithyā abhimāna tva upapatteḥ
pratyakṣam hi dehe chidyamāne dahyamāne vā aham chidye dahye iti ca mithyā abhimānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
tathā bāhyatareṣu api putra mitra ādiṣu saṃtapyamāneṣu aham eva saṃtapye iti adhyāropaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
tathā duḥkhi tva ādi abhimānaḥ syāt deha ādi vat eva caitanyāt bahis upalabhyamāna tvāt duḥkhi tva ādīnām suṣupta ādiṣu ca ananuvṛtteḥ
caitanyasya tu suṣupte anuvṛttim āmananti yat vai tat na paśyati paśyan vai tat na paśyati ityādinā
tasmāt sarva duḥkha vinirmukta eka caitanya ātmakaḥ ham iti eṣaḥ ātmā anubhavaḥ
na ca evam ātmānam anubhavataḥ kiṃcid anyat kṛtyam avaśiṣyate
tathā ca śrutiḥ kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ yeṣām naḥ yam ātmā ayam lokaḥ iti ātma vidaḥ kartavya abhāvam darśayati
smṛtiḥ api yaḥ tu ātma ratiḥ eva syāt ātma tṛptaḥ ca mānavaḥ
ātmani eva ca saṃtuṣṭaḥ tasya kāryam na vidyate iti
yasya tu na eṣaḥ nubhavaḥ drāk iva jāyate tam prati anubhava arthaḥ eva āvṛtti abhyupagamaḥ
tatra api na tattvamasi vākya arthāt pracyāvya āvṛttau pravartayet
na hi vara ghātāya kanyām udvāhayanti
niyuktasya ca asmin adhikṛtaḥ ham kartā mayā idam kartavyam iti avaśyam brahma pratyayāt viparīta pratyayaḥ utpadyate
yaḥ tu svayam eva manda matiḥ apratibhānāt tam vākya artham jihāset tasya etasmin eva vākya arthe sthirīkāraḥ āvṛtti ādi vācoyuktyā abhyupeyate
tasmāt para brahma viṣaye pi pratyaye tad upāya upadeśeṣu āvṛtti siddhiḥ
ātmā iti tu upagacchanti grāhayanti ca
ātma tva upāsana adhikaraṇam
yaḥ śāstra ukta viśeṣaṇaḥ paramātmā sa kim aham iti grahītavyaḥ kim vā mad anyaḥ iti etat vicārayati
katham punar ātma śabde pratyagātma viṣaye śrūyamāṇe saṃśayaḥ iti ucyate ayam ātma śabdaḥ mukhyaḥ śakyate bhyupagantum sati jīva īśvarayoḥ abheda saṃbhave
itarathā tu gauṇaḥ yam abhyupagantavyaḥ iti manyate
kim tāvat prāptam
na aham iti grāhyaḥ
na hi apahatapāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ viparīta guṇa tvena śakyate grahītum viparīta guṇaḥ vā apahatapāpma tva ādi guṇa tvena
apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ ca parameśvaraḥ tad viparīta guṇaḥ tu śārīraḥ
īśvarasya ca saṃsārya ātma tve īśvara abhāva prasaṅgaḥ
tatas śāstra ānarthakyam
saṃsāriṇaḥ pi īśvara ātma tve adhikāri abhāvāt śāstra ānarthakyam eva pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ ca
anya tve pi tādātmya darśanam śāstrāt kartavyam pratimā ādiṣu iva viṣṇu ādi darśanam iti ced kāmam evam bhavatu
na tu saṃsāriṇaḥ mukhyaḥ ātmā īśvaraḥ iti etat naḥ prāpayitavyam
evam prāpte brūmaḥ ātmā iti eva parameśvaraḥ pratipattavyaḥ
tathā hi parameśvara prakriyāyām jābālāḥ ātma tvena eva etam upagacchanti tvam vai aham asmi bhagavaḥ devate ham vai tvam asi devate iti
tathā anye pi aham brahma asmi iti evamādayaḥ ātma tva upagamāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ
grāhayanti ca ātma tvena eva īśvaram vedānta vākyāni eṣa te ātmā sarva antaraḥ eṣa te ātmā antaryāmī amṛtaḥ tat satyam saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti evamādīni
yat uktam pratīka darśanam idam viṣṇu pratimā nyāyena bhaviṣyati iti tat ayuktam gauṇa tva prasaṅgāt vākya vairūpyāt ca yatra hi pratīka dṛṣṭiḥ abhipreyate sakṛt eva tatra vacanam bhavati yathā manaḥ brahma ādityaḥ brahma ityādi
iha punar tvam aham asmi aham ca tvam asi iti āha atas pratīka śruti vairūpyāt abheda pratipattiḥ
bheda dṛṣṭi apavādāt ca
tathā hi atha yaḥ nyām devatām upāste sau anyaḥ ham asmi iti na sa veda mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati sarvam tam parādāt yaḥ nyatra ātmanaḥ sarvam veda iti evamādyā bhūyasī śrutiḥ bheda darśanam apavadati
yat tu uktam na viruddha guṇayoḥ anyonya ātmatva saṃbhavaḥ iti na ayam doṣaḥ viruddha guṇa tāyāḥ mithyātva upapatteḥ
yat punar uktam īśvara abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti tat asat śāstra prāmāṇyāt anabhyupagamāt ca
na hi īśvarasya saṃsāryātmatvam pratipādyate iti abhyupagacchāmaḥ
kim tarhi saṃsāriṇaḥ saṃsāri tva apohena īśvara ātma tvam iti
evam ca sati advaita īśvarasya apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇatā viparīta guṇatā tu itarasya mithyā iti vyavatiṣṭhate
yat api uktam adhikāri abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ ca iti tat api asat prāk prabodhāt saṃsāri tva abhyupagamāt tad viṣaya tvāt ca pratyakṣa ādi vyavahārasya
yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet ityādinā hi prabodhe pratyakṣa ādi abhāvam darśayati
pratyakṣa ādi abhāve śruteḥ api abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na iṣṭa tvāt
atra pitā a pitā bhavati iti upakramya vedāḥ a vedāḥ iti vacanāt iṣyate eva asmābhiḥ śruteḥ api abhāvaḥ prabodhe
kasya punar ayam aprabodhaḥ iti ced yaḥ tvam pṛcchasi tasya te iti vadāmaḥ
nanu aham īśvaraḥ eva uktaḥ śrutyā yadi evam pratibuddhaḥ si na asti kasyacid aprabodhaḥ
yaḥ pi doṣaḥ codyate kaiḥ cit avidyayā kila ātmanaḥ sa dvitīya tvāt advaita anupapattiḥ iti saḥ u pi etena pratyuktaḥ
tasmāt ātmā iti eva īśvare manaḥ dadhīta
na pratīke na hi saḥ
pratīka adhikaraṇam
manaḥ brahma iti upāsīta iti adhyātmam atha adhidaivatam ākāśaḥ brahma iti tathā ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ sa yaḥ nāma brahma iti upāste iti evamādiṣu pratīka upāsaneṣu saṃśayaḥ kim teṣu api ātma grahaḥ kartavyaḥ na vā iti
kim tāvat prāptam
teṣu api ātma grahaḥ eva yuktaḥ kartum
kasmāt
brahmaṇaḥ śrutiṣu ātma tvena prasiddha tvāt pratīkānām api brahma vikāra tvāt brahma tve sati ātma tva upapatteḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na pratīkeṣu ātma matim badhnīyāt
na hi sa upāsakaḥ pratīkāni vyastāni ātmatvena ākalayet
yat punar brahma vikāra tvāt pratīkānām brahmatvam tatas ca ātma tvam iti tat asat pratīka abhāva prasaṅgāt
vikāra svarūpa upamardena hi nāma ādi jātasya brahmatvam eva āśritam bhavati
sva rūpa upamarde ca nāma ādīnām kutas pratīka tvam ātma grahaḥ vā
na ca brahmaṇaḥ ātma tvāt brahma dṛṣṭi upadeśeṣu ātma dṛṣṭiḥ kalpyā kartṛ tva ādi anirākaraṇāt
kartṛ tva ādi sarva saṃsāra dharma nirākaraṇena hi brahmaṇaḥ ātmatva upadeśaḥ
tad anirākaraṇena ca upāsana vidhānam
atas ca upāsakasya pratīkaiḥ sama tvāt ātma grahaḥ na upapadyate
na hi rucaka svastikayoḥ itaretarātma tvam asti
suvarṇa ātmanā iva tu brahma ātmanā ekatve pratīka abhāva prasaṅgam avocāma
atas na pratīkeṣu ātma dṛṣṭiḥ kriyate
brahma dṛṣṭiḥ utkarṣāt
brahma dṛṣṭi adhikaraṇam
teṣu eva udāharaṇeṣu anyaḥ saṃśayaḥ kim āditya ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ brahmaṇi adhyasitavyāḥ kim vā brahma dṛṣṭiḥ āditya ādiṣu iti
kutas saṃśayaḥ
sāmānādhikaraṇye kāraṇa anavadhāraṇāt
atra hi brahma śabdasya āditya ādi śabdaiḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam upalabhyate ādityaḥ brahma prāṇaḥ brahma vidyut brahma ityādi samāna vibhakti nirdeśāt
na ca atra āñjasam sāmānādhikaraṇyam avakalpate artha antara vacana tvāt brahma āditya ādi śabdānām
na hi bhavati gauḥ aśvaḥ iti sāmānādhikaraṇyam
nanu prakṛti vikāra bhāvāt brahma āditya ādīnām mṛd śarāva ādi vat sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt na iti ucyate
vikāra pravilayaḥ hi evam prakṛti sāmānādhikaraṇyāt syāt tatas ca pratīka abhāva prasaṅgam avocāma
paramātma vākyam ca idam tadānīm syāt tatas ca upāsana adhikāraḥ bādhyeta parimita vikāra upādānam ca vyartham
tasmāt brāhmaṇaḥ gniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ ityādi vat anyataratra anyatara dṛṣṭi adhyāse sati kva kiṃdṛṣṭiḥ adhyasyatām iti saṃśayaḥ
tatra aniyamaḥ niyama kāriṇaḥ śāstrasya abhāvāt iti evam prāptam
athavā āditya ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ eva brahmaṇi kartavyāḥ iti evam prāptam
evam hi āditya ādi dṛṣṭibhiḥ brahma upāsitam bhavati
brahma upāsanam ca phalavat iti śāstra maryādā
tasmāt na brahma dṛṣṭiḥ āditya ādiṣu iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ brahma dṛṣṭiḥ eva āditya ādiṣu syāt iti
kasmāt
utkarṣāt
evam utkarṣeṇa āditya ādayaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ bhavanti utkṛṣṭa dṛṣṭeḥ teṣu adhyāsāt
tathā ca laukikaḥ nyāyaḥ anugataḥ bhavati
utkṛṣṭa dṛṣṭiḥ hi nikṛṣṭe dhī asitavyā iti laukikaḥ nyāyaḥ yathā rāja dṛṣṭiḥ kṣattari
sa ca anusartavyaḥ viparyaye pratyavāya prasaṅgāt
na hi kṣattṛ dṛṣṭi parigṛhītaḥ rājā nikarṣam nīyamānaḥ śreyase syāt
nanu śāstra prāmāṇyāt an āśaṅkanīyaḥ pratyavāya prasaṅgaḥ na ca laukikena nyāyena śāstrīyā dṛṣṭiḥ niyantum yuktā iti atrā ucyate nirdhārite śāstra arthe etat evam syāt
saṃdigdhe tu tasmin tad nirṇayam prati laukikaḥ nyāyaḥ āśrīyamāṇaḥ na virudhyate
tena ca utkṛṣṭa dṛṣṭi adhyāse śāstra arthe vadhāryamāṇe nikṛṣṭa dṛṣṭim adhyasyan pratyaveyāt iti śliṣyate
prāthamyāt ca āditya ādi śabdānām mukhya artha tvam avirodhāt grahītavyam
taiḥ svārtha vṛttibhiḥ avaruddhāyām buddhau paścāt avatarataḥ brahma śabdasya mukhyayā vṛttyā sāmānādhikaraṇya asaṃbhavāt brahma dṛṣṭi vidhāna artha tā eva avatiṣṭhate
iti paratvāt api brahma śabdasya eṣaḥ eva arthaḥ nyāyyaḥ
tathā hi brahma iti ādeśaḥ brahma iti upāsīta brahma iti upāste iti ca sarvatra iti param brahma śabdam uccārayati śuddhān tu āditya ādi śabdān
tatas ca yathā śuktikām rajatam iti pratyeti iti atra śukti vacanaḥ eva śuktikā śabdaḥ rajata śabdaḥ tu rajata pratīti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ pratyeti eva hi kevalam rajatam iti na tu tatra rajatam asti evam atra api āditya ādīn brahma iti pratīyāt iti gamyate
ca dvitīyā nirdeśena āditya ādīn eva upāsti kriyayā vyāpyamānān darśayati sa yaḥ etat evam vidvān ādityam brahma iti upāste yaḥ vācam brahma iti upāste yaḥ saṃkalpam brahma iti upāste iti ca
yat tu uktam brahma upāsanam eva atra ādaraṇīyam phalavat tvāya iti tat ayuktam uktena nyāyena āditya ādīnām eva upāsya tva avagamāt
phalam tu atithi ādi upāsane iva āditya ādi upāsane brahmā eva dāsyati sarva adhyakṣa tvāt
varṇitam ca etat phalam atas upapatteḥ iti atra
īdṛśam ca atra brahmaṇaḥ upāsya tvam yat pratīkeṣu tad dṛṣṭi adhyāropaṇam pratimā ādiṣu iva viṣṇu ādīnām
āditya ādi matayaḥ ca aṅge upapatteḥ
āditya ādimati adhikaraṇam
yaḥ eva asau tapati tam udgītham upāsīta lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta vāci saptavidham sāma upāsīta iyam eva ṛc agniḥ sāmaḥ iti evamādiṣu aṅga avabaddheṣu upāsaneṣu saṃśayaḥ kim āditya ādiṣu udgītha ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ vidhīyante kim vā udgītha ādiṣu eva āditya ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ iti
tatra aniyamaḥ niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt iti prāptam
na hi atra brahmaṇaḥ iva kasyacid utkarṣa viśeṣaḥ vadhāryate
brahma hi samasta jagat kāraṇatvāt apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇa yogāt ca āditya ādibhyaḥ utkṛṣṭam iti śakyam avadhārayitum
na tu āditya udgītha ādīnām vikāra tva aviśeṣāt kiṃcid utkarṣa viśeṣa avadhāraṇe kāraṇam asti
athavā niyamena eva udgītha ādi matayaḥ āditya ādiṣu adhyasyeran
kasmāt
karma ātmaka tvāt udgītha ādīnām karmaṇaḥ ca phala prāpti prasiddheḥ
udgītha ādi matibhiḥ upāsyamānāḥ āditya ādayaḥ karma ātmakāḥ santaḥ phala hetavaḥ bhaviṣyanti
tathā ca iyam eva ṛc agniḥ sāmaḥ iti atra tat etat etasyām ṛci adhyūḍham sāmaḥ iti ṛk śabdena pṛthivīm nirdiśati sāma śabdena agnim
tat ca pṛthivī agnyoḥ ṛk sāma dṛṣṭi cikīrṣāyām avakalpate na ṛk sāmayoḥ pṛthivī agni dṛṣṭi cikīrṣāyām
kṣattari hi rāja dṛṣṭi karaṇāt rāja śabdaḥ upacaryate na rājani kṣattṛ śabdaḥ
api ca lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta iti adhikaraṇa nirdeśāt lokeṣu sāma adhyasitavyam iti pratīyate
etat gāyatram prāṇeṣu protam iti ca etat eva darśayati
prathama nirdiṣṭeṣu ca āditya ādiṣu carama nirdiṣṭam brahma adhyastam ādityaḥ brahma iti ādeśaḥ ityādiṣu
prathama nirdiṣṭāḥ ca pṛthivī ādayaḥ carama nirdiṣṭāḥ hiṃkāra ādayaḥ pṛthivī hiṃkāraḥ ityādi śrutiṣu
atas anaṅgeṣu āditya ādiṣu aṅgam atikṣepaḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ āditya ādi matayaḥ eva aṅgeṣu udgītha ādiṣu kṣipyeran
kutas
upapatteḥ
upapadyate hi evam apūrva saṃnikarṣāt āditya ādi matibhiḥ saṃskriyamāṇeṣu udgītha ādiṣu karma samṛddhiḥ
yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaniṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti ca vidyāyāḥ karma samṛddhi hetu tvam darśayati
bhavatu karma samṛddhi phaleṣu evam
svatantra phaleṣu tu katham yaḥ etat evam vidvān lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāste ityādiṣu
teṣu api adhikṛta adhikārāt prakṛta apūrva saṃnikarṣeṇa eva phala kalpanā yuktā godohana ādi niyama vat
phala ātmaka tvāt ca āditya ādīnām udgītha ādibhyaḥ karma ātmakebhyaḥ utkarṣa upapattiḥ
āditya ādi prāpti lakṣaṇam hi karma phalam śiṣyate śrutiṣu
api ca om iti etat akṣaram udgītham upāsīta khalu etasya eva akṣarasya upavyākhyānam bhavati iti ca udgītham eva upāsya tvena upakramya āditya ādimatīḥ vidadhāti
yat tu uktam udgītha ādi matibhiḥ upāsyamānāḥ āditya ādayaḥ karma bhūyam bhūtvā phalam kariṣyanti iti tat ayuktam svayam eva upāsanasya karma tvāt phalavat tva upapatteḥ āditya ādi bhāvena api ca dṛśyamānānām udgītha ādīnām karma ātmaka tva anapāyāt
tat etat etasyām ṛci adhyūḍham sāma iti tu lākṣaṇikaḥ eva pṛthivī agnyoḥ ṛk sāma śabda prayogaḥ
lakṣaṇā ca yathāsaṃbhavam saṃnikṛṣṭena viprakṛṣṭena vā sva artha saṃbandhena pravartate
tatra yadi api ṛk sāmayoḥ pṛthivī agni dṛṣṭi cikīrṣā tathā api prasiddhayoḥ ṛk sāmayoḥ bhedena anukīrtanāt pṛthivī agnyoḥ ca saṃnidhānāt tayoḥ eva eṣaḥ ṛk sāma śabda prayogaḥ ṛk sāma saṃbandhāt iti niścīyate
kṣattṛ śabdaḥ u pi hi kutaścid kāraṇāt rājānam upasarpan na nivārayitum pāryate
iyam eva ṛc iti ca yathākṣaranyāsam ṛcaḥ eva pṛthivī tvam avadhārayati
pṛthivyāḥ hi ṛk tve vadhāryamāṇe iyam ṛgā iva iti akṣara nyāsaḥ syāt
yaḥ evam vidvān sāma gāyati iti ca aṅga āśrayam avavijñānam upasaṃharati na pṛthivī ādi āśrayam
tathā lokeṣu pañcavidham sāma upāsīta iti yadi api saptamī nirdiṣṭāḥ lokāḥ tathā api sāmni eva te adhyasyeran dvitīyā nirdeśena sāmnaḥ upāsya tva avagamāt
sāmani hi lokeṣu adhyasyamāneṣu sāma loka ātmanā upāsitam bhavati anyathā punar lokāḥ sāma ātmanā upāsitāḥ syuḥ
etena etat gāyatram prāṇeṣu protam ityādi vyākhyātam
yatra api tulyaḥ dvitīyā nirdeśaḥ atha khalu amum ādityam saptavidham sāma upāsīta iti tatra api samastasya khalu sāmnaḥ upāsanam sādhu tu pañcavidhasya atha saptavidhasya iti ca sāmnaḥ eva upāsya tva upakramāt tasmin eva āditya ādi adhyāsaḥ
etasmāt eva ca sāmnaḥ upāsya tva avagamāt pṛthivī hiṃkāraḥ ityādi nirdeśa viparyaye hiṃkāra ādiṣu eva pṛthivī ādi dṛṣṭiḥ
tasmāt anaṅga āśrayāḥ āditya ādi matayaḥ aṅgeṣu udgītha ādiṣu kṣipyeran iti siddham
āsīnaḥ sambhavāt
āsīnādhikaraṇam
karma aṅga saṃbaddheṣu tāvat upāsaneṣu karma tantra tvāt na āsana ādi cintā
nā api samyak darśane vastu tantra tvāt vijñānasya
itareṣu tu upāsaneṣu kim aniyamena tiṣṭhan āsīnaḥ śayānaḥ vā pravarteta uta niyamena āsīnaḥ eva iti cintayati
tatra aniyamaḥ śarīra sthiteḥ iti evam prāpte bravīti āsīnaḥ eva upāsīta iti
kutas
saṃbhavāt
upāsanam nāma samāna pratyaya pravāha karaṇam
na ca tat gacchataḥ dhāvataḥ vā saṃbhavati gati ādīnām citta vikṣepa kara tvāt
tiṣṭhataḥ pi deha dhāraṇe vyāpṛtam manaḥ na sūkṣma vastu nirīkṣaṇa kṣamam bhavati
śayānasya api akasmāt eva nidrayā abhibhūyate
āsīnasya tu evaṃjātīyakaḥ bhūyān doṣaḥ su pariharaḥ iti saṃbhavati tasya upāsanam
dhyānāt ca
api ca dhyāyati arthaḥ eṣaḥ yat samāna pratyaya pravāha karaṇam
dhyāyatiḥ ca praśithila aṅga ceṣṭeṣu pratiṣṭhita dṛṣṭiṣu eka viṣaya ākṣipta citteṣu upacaryamāṇaḥ dṛśyate dhyāyati bakaḥ dhyāyati proṣita bandhuḥ iti
āsīnaḥ ca anāyāsaḥ bhavati
tasmāt api āsīna karma upāsanam
acala tvam ca apekṣya
api ca dhyāyati iva pṛthivī iti atra pṛthivī ādiṣu acala tvam eva apekṣya dhyāyati vādaḥ bhavati
tat ca liṅgam upāsanasya āsīna karma tve
smaranti ca
smaranti api ca śiṣṭāḥ upāsana aṅga tvena āsanam śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ ityādinā
atas eva padmaka ādīnām āsana viśeṣāṇām upadeśaḥ yoga śāstre
yatra ekāgra tā tatra aviśeṣāt
ekāgra tā adhikaraṇam
diś deśa kāleṣu saṃśayaḥ kim asti kaścid niyamaḥ na asti vā iti
prāyeṇa vaidikeṣu ārambheṣu diś ādi niyama darśanāt syāt iha api kaścid niyamaḥ iti yasya matiḥ tam pratyāha diś deśa kāleṣu artha lakṣaṇaḥ eva niyamaḥ
yatra eva asya diśi deśe kāle vā manasaḥ saukaryeṇa ekāgra tā bhavati tatra eva upāsīta prācī diś pūrvāhṇa prācīna pravaṇa ādi vat viśeṣa aśravaṇāt ekāgra tāyāḥ iṣṭāyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt
nanu viśeṣam api kecid āmananti same śucau śarkarā vahni vālukā vivarjite śabda jala āśraya ādibhiḥ
manaḥ nukūle na tu cakṣu pīḍane guhā nivāta āśrayaṇe prayojayet iti yathā iti ucyate
satyam asti evaṃjātīyakaḥ niyamaḥ
sati tu etasmin tad gateṣu viśeṣeṣu aniyamaḥ iti suhṛd bhūtvā ācāryaḥ ācaṣṭe
manaḥ nukūle iti ca eṣā śrutiḥ yatra ekāgra tā tatra eva iti etat eva darśayati
ā prāyaṇāt tatra api hi dṛṣṭam
āprāyaṇa adhikaraṇam
āvṛttiḥ sarva upāsaneṣu ādartavyā iti sthitam ādye dhikaraṇe
tatra yāni tāvat samyak darśana arthāni upāsanāni tāni avaghāta ādi vat kārya paryavasānāni iti jñātam eva eṣām āvṛttiṃparimāṇam
na hi samyak darśane kārye niṣpanne yatna antaram kiṃcid śāsitum śakyam a niyojya brahma ātmatva pratipatteḥ śāstrasya aviṣaya tvāt
yāni punar abhyudaya phalāni teṣu eṣā cintā kim kiyantaṃcid kālam pratyayam āvartya uparamet uta yāvajjīvam āvartayet iti
kim tāvat prāptam
kiyantaṃcid kālam pratyayam abhyasya utsṛjet āvṛtti viśiṣṭasya upāsana śabda arthasya kṛta tvāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ā prāyaṇāt eva āvartayet pratyayam antya pratyaya vaśāt adṛṣṭa phala prāpteḥ
karmāṇi api hi janma antara upabhogyam phalam ārabhamāṇāni tad anurūpam bhāvanā vijñānam prāyaṇa kāle ākṣipanti sa vijñānaḥ bhavati sa vijñānam eva anvavakrāmati yad cittaḥ tena eṣa prāṇam āyāti prāṇaḥ tejasā yuktaḥ saha ātmanā yathā saṃkalpitam lokam nayati iti ca evamādi śrutibhyaḥ
tṛṇa jalūkā nidarśanāt ca
pratyayāḥ tu ete svarūpa anuvṛttim muktvā kim anyat prāyaṇa kāla bhāvi bhāvanā vijñānam apekṣeran
tasmāt ye pratipattavya phala bhāvanā ātmakāḥ pratyayāḥ teṣu ā prāyaṇāt āvṛttiḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ sa yāvat kratuḥ ayam asmāt lokāt praiti iti prāyaṇa kāle pi pratyaya anuvṛttim darśayati
smṛtiḥ api yam yam vā api smaran bhāvam tyajati ante kalebaram
tam tam eva eti kauntaya sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ iti prayāṇa kāle manasā acalena iti ca
saḥ nta velāyām etat trayam pratipadyeta iti ca maraṇa velāyām api kartavya śeṣam śrāvayati
tad adhigame uttara pūrva aghayoḥ aśleṣa vināśau tad vyapadeśāt
tad adhigama adhikaraṇam
gataḥ tṛtīya śeṣaḥ
atha idānīm brahma vidyā phalam prati cintā pratāyate
brahma adhigame sati tad viparīta phalam duritam kṣīyate na kṣīyate vā iti saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
phala artha tvāt karmaṇaḥ phalam a dattvā na saṃbhāvyate kṣayaḥ
phala dāyinī hi asya śaktiḥ śrutyā samadhigatā
yadi tat antareṇa eva phala upabhogam apavṛjyeta śrutiḥ kadarthitā syāt
smaranti ca na hi karma kṣīyate iti
nanu evam sati prāyaścitta upadeśaḥ narthakaḥ prāpnoti na eṣa doṣaḥ prāyaścittānām naimittika tva upapatteḥ gṛha dāha iṣṭi ādi vat
api ca prāyaścittānām doṣa saṃyogena vidhānāt bhavet api doṣa kṣapaṇa artha tā
na tu evam brahma vidyāyām vidhānam asti
nanu an abhyupagamyamāne brahma vidaḥ karma kṣaye tad phalasya avaśya bhoktavya tvāt anirmokṣaḥ syāt nā iti ucyate
deśa kāla nimitta apekṣaḥ mokṣaḥ karma phala vat bhaviṣyati
tasmāt na brahma adhigame durita nivṛttiḥ iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tad adhigame brahma adhigame sati uttara pūrvayoḥ aghayoḥ aśleṣa vināśau bhavataḥ uttarasya aśleṣaḥ pūrvasya vināśaḥ
kasmāt
tad vyapadeśāt
tathā hi brahma vidyā prakriyāyām saṃbhāvyamāna saṃbandhasya āgāminaḥ duritasya anabhisaṃbandham viduṣaḥ vyapadiśati yathā puṣkarapalāśe āpaḥ na śliṣyante evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma na śliṣyate iti
tathā vināśam api pūrva upacitasya duritasya vyapadiśati tat yathā iṣīkā tūlam agnau protam pradūyeta evam ha asya sarve pāpmānaḥ pradūyante iti
ayam aparaḥ karma kṣaya vyapadeśaḥ bhavati bhidyate hṛdaya grandhiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ
kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare iti
yat uktam anupabhukta phalasya karmaṇaḥ kṣaya kalpanāyām śāstram kadarthitam syāt iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
na hi vayam karmaṇaḥ phala dāyinīm śaktim avajānīmahe
vidyate eva sā
sā tu vidyā ādinā kāraṇa antareṇa pratibadhyate iti vadāmaḥ
śakti sadbhāva mātre ca śāstram vyāpriyate na pratibandha apratibandhayoḥ api
na hi karma kṣīyate iti etat api smaraṇam autsargikam na hi bhogāt ṛte karma kṣīyate tad artha tvāt iti
iṣyate eva tu prāyaścitta ādinā tasya kṣayaḥ sarvam pāpmānam tarati tarati brahmahatyām yaḥ u śvamedhena yajate yaḥ ca enam evam veda ityādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ
yat tu uktam naimittikāni prāyaścittāni bhaviṣyanti iti tat asat doṣa saṃyogena codyamānānām eṣām doṣa nirghāta phala saṃbhave phala antara kalpanā anupapatteḥ
yat punar etat uktam na prāyaścitta vat doṣa kṣaya uddeśena vidyā vidhānam asti iti atra brūmaḥ saguṇāsu tāvat vidyāsu vidyate eva vidhānam tāsu ca vākyaśeṣe aiśvarya prāptiḥ pāpa nivṛttiḥ ca vidyāvataḥ ucyate tayoḥ ca avivakṣā kāraṇam na asti iti atas pāpma prahāṇa pūrvaka aiśvarya prāptiḥ tāsām phalam iti niścīyate
nirguṇāyām tu vidyāyām yadi api vidhānam nā asti tathā api akartṛ ātma tva bodhāt karma pradāha siddhiḥ
aśleṣaḥ iti ca āgāmiṣu karmasu kartṛ tvam eva na pratipadyate brahma vid iti darśayati
atikrānteṣu tu yadi api mithyājñānāt kartṛ tvam pratipede iva tathā api vidyā sāmarthyāt mithyājñāna nivṛtteḥ tāni api pravilīyante iti āha vināśe iti
pūrva siddha kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva viparītam hi triṣu api kāleṣu akartṛ tva abhoktṛ tva svarūpam brahma aham asmi na itas pūrvam api kartā bhoktā vā aham āsam na idānīm na api bhaviṣyat kāle iti brahma vid avagacchati
evam eva ca mokṣaḥ upapadyate
anyathā hi anādi kāla pravṛttānām karmaṇām kṣaya abhāve mokṣa abhāvaḥ syāt
na ca deśa kāla nimitta apekṣaḥ mokṣaḥ karma phala vat bhavitum arhati
anitya tva prasaṅgāt parokṣa tva anupapatteḥ ca jñāna phalasya
tasmāt brahma adhigame durita kṣayaḥ iti sthitam
itarasya api evam asaṃśleṣaḥ pāte tu
itarā saṃśleṣa adhikaraṇam
pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe bandha hetoḥ aghasya svābhāvikasya aśleṣa vināśau jñāna nimittau śāstra vyapadeśāt nirūpitau
