dharmasya punar śāstrīya tvāt śāstrīyeṇa jñānena avirodhaḥ iti āśaṅkya tad nirākaraṇāya pūrva adhikaraṇa nyāya atideśaḥ kriyate itarasya api puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ evam agha vat asaṃśleṣaḥ vināśaḥ ca jñānavataḥ bhavataḥ
kutas
tasya api sva phala hetu tvena jñāna phala pratibandhi tva prasaṅgāt ubhe u ha eva eṣa ete tarati ityādi śrutiṣu ca duṣkṛta vat sukṛtasya api praṇāśa vyapadeśāt akartṛ ātmatva bodha nimittasya ca karma kṣayasya sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ tulya tvāt kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi iti ca aviśeṣa śruteḥ
yatra api kevalaḥ eva pāpma śabdaḥ paṭhyate tatra api tena eva puṇyam api ākalitam iti draṣṭavyam jñāna apekṣayā nikṛṣṭa phala tvāt
asti ca śrutau puṇye pi pāpma śabdaḥ na enam setum ahar rātre tarataḥ iti atra saha duṣkṛtena sukṛtam api anukramya sarve pāpmānaḥ tasmāt nivartante iti aviśeṣeṇa eva prakṛte puṇye pāpma śabda prayogāt
pāte tu iti tu śabdaḥ
evam dharma adharmayoḥ bandha hetvoḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt aśleṣa vināśa siddheḥ avaśyaṃbhāvinī viduṣaḥ śarīrapāte muktiḥ iti avadhārayati
anārabdha kārye eva tu pūrve tad avadheḥ
anārabdha adhikaraṇam
pūrvayoḥ adhikaraṇayoḥ jñāna nimittaḥ sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ vināśaḥ vadhāritaḥ
sa kim aviśeṣeṇa ārabdha kāryayoḥ anārabdha kāryayoḥ ca bhavati uta viśeṣeṇa anārabdha kāryayoḥ eva iti vicāryate
tatra ubhe u ha eva eṣa ete tarati iti evamādi śrutiṣu aviśeṣa śravaṇāt aviśeṣeṇa eva kṣayaḥ iti evam prāpte pratyāha anārabdha kārye eva tu iti
apravṛtta phale eva pūrve janma antara saṃcite asmin api ca janmani prāk jñāna utpatteḥ saṃcite sukṛta duṣkṛte jñāna adhigamāt kṣīyete
na tu ārabdha kārye sāmi bhukta phale yābhyām etat brahma jñāna āyatanam janma nirmitam
kutas etat
tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣye saṃpatsye iti śarīrapātau adhikaraṇāt kṣema prāpteḥ
itarathā hi jñānāt aśeṣa karma kṣaye sati sthiti hetu abhāvāt jñāna prāpti anantaram eva kṣemam aśnuvīta
tatra śarīrapāta pratīkṣām na ācakṣīta
nanu vastu balena eva ayam akartṛ ātma avabodhaḥ karmāṇi kṣapayan katham kānicid kṣapayet kānicid ca upekṣeta
na hi samāne agni bīja saṃparke keṣāṃcid bīja śaktiḥ kṣīyate keṣāṃcid na kṣīyate iti śakyam aṅgīkartum iti
ucyate na tāvat an āśritya ārabdha kāryam karma āśayam jñāna utpattiḥ upapadyate
āśrite ca tasmin kulāla cakra vat pravṛtta vegasya antarāle pratibandha asaṃbhavāt bhavati vega kṣaya pratipālanam
akartṛ ātma bodhaḥ u hi mithyājñāna bādhanena karmāṇi ucchinatti
bādhitam api tu mithyājñānam dvi candra jñāna vat saṃskāra vaśāt kaṃcid kālam anuvartate eva
api ca na eva atra vivaditavyam brahma vidā kaṃcid kālam śarīram dhriyate na vā dhriyate iti
katham hi ekasya sva hṛdaya pratyayam brahma vedanam deha dhāraṇam ca apareṇa pratikṣeptum śakyeta
śruti smṛtiṣu ca sthita prajña lakṣaṇa nirdeśena etat eva nirucyate
tasmāt anārabdha kāryayoḥ eva sukṛta duṣkṛtayoḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt kṣayaḥ iti nirṇayaḥ
agnihotra ādi tu tad kāryāya eva tad darśanāt
agnihotra ādi adhikaraṇam
puṇyasya api aśleṣa vināśayoḥ aghanyāya u tidiṣṭaḥ
saḥ u tideśaḥ sarva puṇya viṣayaḥ iti āśaṅkya prativakti agnihotra ādi tu iti
tu śabdaḥ āśaṅkām apanudati
yat nityam karma vaidikam agnihotra ādi tat tad kāryāya eva bhavati
jñānasya yat kāryam tat eva asya api kāryam iti arthaḥ
kutas
tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣanti yajñena dānena ityādi darśanāt
nanu jñāna karmaṇoḥ vilakṣaṇa kārya tvāt kārya ekatva anupapattiḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ jvara maraṇa kāryayoḥ api dadhi viṣayoḥ guḍa mantra saṃyuktayoḥ tṛpti puṣṭi kārya darśanāt tadvat karmaṇaḥ api jñāna saṃyuktasya mokṣa kārya upapatteḥ
nanu anārabhyaḥ mokṣaḥ katham asya karma kārya tvam ucyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ ārāt upakāraka tvāt karmaṇaḥ
jñānasya eva hi prāpakam sat karma praṇāḍyā mokṣa kāraṇam iti upacaryate
atas eva ca atikrānta viṣayam etat kārya ekatva abhidhānam
na hi brahma vidaḥ āgāmi agnihotra ādi saṃbhavati a niyojya brahma ātmatva pratipatteḥ śāstrasya aviṣaya tvāt
saguṇāsu tu vidyāsu kartṛ tva anativṛtteḥ saṃbhavati āgāmi api agnihotra ādi
tasya api nirabhisaṃdhinaḥ kārya antara abhāvāt vidyā saṃgati upapattiḥ
kiṃviṣayam punar idam aśleṣa vināśa vacanam kiṃviṣayam vā adaḥ viniyoga vacanam ekeṣām śākhinām tasya putrāḥ dāyam upayanti suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām dviṣantaḥ pāpa kṛtyām iti atas uttaram paṭhati
atas nyā pi hi ekeṣām ubhayoḥ
atas gnihotra ādeḥ nityāt karmaṇaḥ anyā api hi asti sādhu kṛtyā yā phalam abhisaṃdhāya kriyate tasyāḥ eṣa viniyogaḥ uktaḥ ekeṣām śākhinām suhṛdaḥ sādhu kṛtyām upayanti iti
tasyāḥ eva ca idam agha vat aśleṣa vināśa nirūpaṇam itarasya api evam asaṃśleṣaḥ iti
tathājātīyakasya kāmyasya karmaṇaḥ vidyām prati anupakāraka tve saṃpratipattiḥ ubhayoḥ api jaimini bādarāyaṇayoḥ ācāryayoḥ
yat eva vidyayā iti hi
vidyā jñāna sādhanatva adhikaraṇam
samadhigatam etat anantara adhikaraṇe nityam agnihotra ādikam karma mumukṣuṇā mokṣa prayojana uddeśena kṛtam upātta durita kṣaya hetu dvāreṇa sattva śuddhi kāraṇatām pratipadyamānam mokṣa prayojana brahma adhigama nimitta tvena brahmavidyayā saha eka kāryam bhavati iti
tatra agnihotra ādi karma aṅga vyapāśraya vidyā saṃyuktam kevalam ca asti yaḥ evam vidvān yajati yaḥ evam vidvān juhoti yaḥ evam vidvān śaṃsati yaḥ evam vidvān gāyati tasmāt evaṃvidam eva brahmāṇam kurvīta tena ubhau kurutaḥ yaḥ ca etat evam veda yaḥ ca na veda ityādi vacanebhyaḥ vidyā saṃyuktam asti kevalam api asti
tatra idam vicāryate kim vidyā saṃyuktam eva agnihotra ādikam karma mumukṣoḥ vidyā hetutvena tayā saha eka kāryatvam pratipadyate na kevalam
uta vidyā saṃyuktam kevalam ca aviśeṣeṇa iti
kutas saṃśayaḥ
tam etam ātmānam yajñena vividiṣanti iti yajña ādīnām aviśeṣeṇa ātma vedana aṅgatvena śravaṇāt vidyā saṃyuktasya ca agnihotra ādeḥ viśiṣṭa tva avagamāt
kim tāvat prāptam
vidyā saṃyuktam eva karma agnihotra ādi ātma vidyā śeṣa tvam pratipadyate na vidyā hīnam vidyā upetasya viśiṣṭa tva avagamāt vidyā vihīnāt yat ahar eva juhoti tat ahar punar mṛtyum apajayati evam vidvān ityādi śrutibhyaḥ buddhyā yuktaḥ yayā pārtha karma bandham prahāsyasi dūreṇa hi avaram karma buddhi yogāt dhanaṃjayaḥ ityādi smṛtibhyaḥ ca iti evam prāpte pratipādyate yat eva vidyayā iti hi
satyam etat vidyā saṃyuktam karma agnihotra ādikam vidyā vihīnāt karmaṇaḥ gnihotrāt viśiṣṭam vidvān iva brāhmaṇaḥ vidyā vihīnāt brāhmaṇāt
tathā api na atyantam anapekṣam vidyā vihīnam karma agnihotra ādikam
kasmāt
tam etam ātmānam yajñena vividiṣanti iti aviśeṣeṇa agnihotra ādeḥ vidyā hetutvena śruta tvāt
nanu vidyā saṃyuktasya agnihotra ādeḥ vidyā vihīnāt viśiṣṭa tva avagamāt vidyā vihīnam agnihotra ādi ātma vidyā hetutvena anapekṣam eva iti yuktam na etat evam
vidyā sahāyasya agnihotra ādeḥ vidyā nimittena sāmarthya atiśayena yogāt ātma jñānam prati kaścid kāraṇatva atiśayaḥ bhaviṣyati na tathā vidyā vihīnasya iti yuktam kalpayitum
na tu yajñena vividiṣanti iti atra aviśeṣeṇa ātma jñāna aṅgatvena śrutasya agnihotra ādeḥ anaṅgatvam śakyam abhyupagantum
tathā hi śrutiḥ yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaniṣadā tat eva vīryavattaram bhavati iti vidyā saṃyuktasya karmaṇaḥ gnihotra ādeḥ vīryavattara tva abhidhānena sva kāryam prati kaṃcid atiśayam bruvāṇā vidyā vihīnasya tasya eva tad prayojanam prati vīryavat tvam darśayati
karmaṇaḥ ca vīryavat tvam tat yat sva prayojana sādhana saha tvam
tasmāt vidyā saṃyuktam nityam agnihotra ādi vidyā vihīnam ca ubhayam api mumukṣuṇā mokṣa prayojana uddeśena iha janmani janmāntare ca prāk jñāna utpatteḥ kṛtam tat yathā sāmarthyam brahma adhigama pratibandha kāraṇa upātta durita kṣaya hetutva dvāreṇa brahma adhigama kāraṇa tvam pratipadyamānam śravaṇa manana śraddhā tātparya ādi antaraṅga kāraṇa apekṣam brahma vidyayā saha eka kāryam bhavati iti sthitam
bhogena tu itare kṣapayitvā sampadyate
itara kṣapaṇa adhikaraṇam
anārabdha kāryayoḥ puṇya pāpayoḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt kṣayaḥ uktaḥ
itare tu ārabdha kārye puṇya pāpe upabhogena kṣapayitvā brahma saṃpadyate tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣye saṃpatsye iti brahma eva san brahma apyeti iti ca evamādi śrutibhyaḥ
nanu sati api samyagdarśane yathā prāk dehapātāt bheda darśanam dvi candra darśana nyāyena anuvṛttam evam paścāt api unuvarteta na nimitta abhavāt
upabhoga śeṣa kṣapaṇam hi tatra anuvṛtti nimittam na ca tādṛśam atra kiṃcid asti
nanu aparaḥ karma āśayaḥ bhinavam upabhogam ārapsyate na tasya dagdha bīja tvāt
mithyājñāna avaṣṭambham hi karmāntaram dehapāte upabhoga antaram ārabheta
tat ca mithyājñānam samyak jñānena dagdham iti atas sādhu etat ārabdha kārya kṣaye viduṣaḥ kaivalyam avaśyam bhavati iti
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ

caturthaḥ dhyāyaḥ
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ
vāc manasi darśanāt śabdāt ca
vāc adhikaraṇam
asti prāyaṇa viṣayā śrutiḥ asya somya puruṣasya prayataḥ vāc manasi saṃpadyate manaḥ prāṇe prāṇaḥ tejasi tejaḥ parasyām devatāyām iti
kim iha vācaḥ eva vṛttimattyāḥ manasi saṃpattiḥ ucyate uta vāc vṛtteḥ iti viśayaḥ
tatra vāc eva tāvat manasi saṃpadyate iti prāptam
tathā hi śrutiḥ anugṛhītā bhavati
itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt
śruti lakṣaṇā viśaye ca śrutiḥ nyāyyā na lakṣaṇā
tasmāt vācaḥ eva ayam manasi pralayaḥ iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ vāc vṛttiḥ manasi saṃpadyate iti
katham vāc vṛttiḥ iti vyākhyāyate yāvatā vāc manasi iti eva ācāryaḥ paṭhati
satyam etat
paṭhiṣyati tu parastāt avibhāgaḥ vacanāt iti
tasmāt atra vṛtti upaśama mātram vivakṣati iti gamyate
tattva pralaya vivakṣāyām tu sarvatra eva avibhāga sāmyāt kim paratra eva viśiṃṣyāt avibhāgaḥ iti
tasmāt atra vṛtti upasaṃhāra vivakṣā
vāc vṛttiḥ pūrvam upasaṃhriyate manaḥ vṛttau avasthitāyām iti arthaḥ
kasmāt
darśanāt dṛśyate hi vāc vṛtteḥ pūrva upasaṃhāraḥ manaḥ vṛttau vidyamānāyām
na tu vācaḥ eva vṛttimattyā manasi upasaṃhāraḥ kenacid api draṣṭum śakyate
nanu śruti sāmarthyāt vācaḥ eva ayam manasi apyayaḥ yuktaḥ iti uktam na iti āha a tad prakṛti tvāt
yasya hi yatas utpattiḥ tasya tatra pralayaḥ nyāyyaḥ mṛdi iva śarāvasya
na ca manasaḥ vāc utpadyate iti kiṃcana pramāṇam asti
vṛtti udbhava abhibhavau tu aprakṛti samāśrayau api dṛśyete
pārthivebhyaḥ hi indhanebhyaḥ taijasasya agneḥ vṛttiḥ udbhavati apsu ca upaśāmyati
katham tarhi asmin pakṣe śabdaḥ vāc manasi saṃpadyate iti
atas āha śabdāt ca iti
śabdaḥ upi asmin pakṣe vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ abheda upacārāt iti arthaḥ
atas eva ca sarvāṇi anu
tasmāt upaśānta tejāḥ punarbhavam indriyaiḥ manasi saṃpadyamānaiḥ iti atra aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām eva indriyāṇām manasi saṃpattiḥ śrūyate
tatra api atas eva vācaḥ iva cakṣuḥ ādīnām api sa vṛttike manasi avasthite vṛtti lopa darśanāt tattva pralaya asaṃbhavāt śabda upapatteḥ ca vṛtti dvāreṇa eva sarvāṇi indriyāṇi manaḥ nuvartante
sarveṣām karaṇānām manasi upasaṃhāra aviśeṣe sati vācaḥ pṛthak grahaṇam vāc manasi saṃpadyate iti udāharaṇa anurodhena
tat manaḥ prāṇaḥ uttarāt
manaḥ dhi karaṇam
samadhigatam etat vāc manasi saṃpadyate iti atra vṛtti saṃpatti vivakṣā iti
atha yat uttaram vākyam manaḥ prāṇe iti kim atra api vṛtti saṃpattiḥ eva vivakṣyate uta vṛttimat saṃpattiḥ iti vicikitsāyām vṛttimat saṃpattiḥ eva atra iti prāptam śruti anugrahāt
tad prakṛti tva upapatteḥ ca
tathā hi anna mayam hi somya manaḥ āpaḥ mayaḥ prāṇaḥ iti anna yoni manaḥ āmananti ap yonim ca prāṇam
āpaḥ ca annam asṛjanta iti śrutiḥ
atas ca yat manaḥ prāṇe pralīyate annam eva tat apsu pralīyate
annam hi manaḥ āpaḥ ca prāṇaḥ prakṛti vikāra abhedāt iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ tat api āgṛhīta bāhya indriya vṛtti manaḥ vṛtti dvāreṇa eva prāṇe pralīyate iti uttarāt vākyāt avagantavyam
tathā hi suṣupsoḥ mumūrṣoḥ ca prāṇa vṛttau parispanda ātmikāyām avasthitāyām manaḥ vṛttīnām upaśamaḥ dṛśyate
na ca manasaḥ sva rūpa apyayaḥ prāṇe saṃbhavati
a tad prakṛti tvāt
nanu darśitam manasaḥ prāṇa prakṛti tvam na etat sāram
na hi īdṛśena tad prakṛti tvena manaḥ prāṇe saṃpattum arhati
evam api hi anne manaḥ saṃpadyeta apsu ca annam apsu eva ca prāṇaḥ
na hi etasmin api pakṣe prāṇa bhāva pariṇatābhyaḥ dbhyaḥ manaḥ jāyate iti kiṃcana pramāṇam asti
tasmāt na manasaḥ prāṇe sva rūpa apyayaḥ
vṛtti apyaye tu śabdaḥ vakalpate vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ abheda upacārāt iti darśitam
saḥ dhī akṣe tad upagama ādibhyaḥ
adhyakṣa adhikaraṇam
sthitam etat yasya yatas na utpattiḥ tasya tasmin vṛtti pralayaḥ na svarūpa pralayaḥ iti
idam idānīm prāṇaḥ tejasi iti atra cintyate kim yathāśruti prāṇasya tejasi eva vṛtti upasaṃhāraḥ kim vā deha indriya pañjara adhyakṣe jīve iti
tatra śruteḥ anatiśaṅkya tvāt prāṇasya tejasi eva saṃpattiḥ syāt aśruta kalpanāyāḥ anyāyya tvāt iti evam prāpte pratipadyate saḥ dhyakṣaḥ iti
sa prakṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ adhyakṣe avidyā karma pūrva prajñā upādhike vijñāna ātmani avatiṣṭhate
tad pradhānā prāṇa vṛttiḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ
kutas
tad upagama ādibhyaḥ evam eva imam ātmānam anta kāle sarve prāṇāḥ abhisamāyanti yatra etat ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva ūrdhva
viśeṣeṇa ca tam utkrāmantam prāṇaḥ nu utkrāmati iti pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya adhyakṣa anugāmi tām darśayati tad anuvṛtti tām ca itareṣām prāṇam anūtkrāmantam sarve prāṇāḥ anūtkrāmanti iti
sa vijñānaḥ bhavati iti ca adhyakṣasya antar vijñānavat tva pradarśanena tasmin apīta karaṇa grāmasya prāṇasya avasthānam gamayati
nanu prāṇaḥ tejasi iti śrūyate
katham prāṇaḥ dhyakṣe iti adhika āvāpaḥ kriyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ adhyakṣa pradhāna tvāt utkramaṇa ādi vyavahārasya śruti antara gatasya api ca viśeṣasya apekṣaṇīya tvāt
katham tarhi prāṇaḥ tejasi iti śrutiḥ iti atas āha
tad śruteḥ
sa prāṇa saṃpṛktaḥ dhyakṣaḥ tejaḥ sahacariteṣu bhūteṣu deha bīja bhūteṣu sūkṣmeṣu avatiṣṭhate iti avagantavyam prāṇaḥ tejasi iti śruteḥ
nanu ca iyam śrutiḥ prāṇasya tejasi sthitim darśayati na prāṇa saṃpṛktasya adhyakṣasya na eṣa doṣaḥ saḥ iti adhyakṣasya api antarāle upasaṃkhyāta tvāt
yaḥ u pi hi srughnāt mathurām gatvā mathurāyāḥ pāṭaliputram vrajati saḥ u pi srughnāt pāṭaliputram yāti iti śakyate vaditum
tasmāt prāṇaḥ tejasi iti prāṇa saṃpṛktasya adhyakṣasya eva etat tejaḥ sahacariteṣu bhūteṣu avasthānam
katham tejaḥ sahacariteṣu bhūteṣu iti ucyate yāvatā ekam eva tejaḥ śrūyate prāṇaḥ tejasi iti
atas āha
na ekasmin darśayataḥ hi
na ekasmin eva tejasi śarīra antara prepsā velāyām jīvaḥ vatiṣṭhate kāryasya śarīrasya aneka ātmaka tva darśanāt
darśayataḥ ca etam artham praśna prativacane āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ iti
tat vyākhyātam tri ātmaka tvāt tu bhūyaḥ tvāt iti atra
śruti smṛtī ca etam artham darśayataḥ
śrutiḥ pṛthvī mayaḥ āpaḥ mayaḥ vāyu mayaḥ ākāśa mayaḥ tejaḥ mayaḥ ityādyā
smṛtiḥ api aṇvyaḥ mātrā vināśinyaḥ daśārdhānām tu yāḥ smṛtāḥ
tābhiḥ sārdham idam sarvam saṃbhavati anupūrvaśas ityādyā
nanu ca upasaṃhṛteṣu vāc ādiṣu karaṇeṣu śarīra antara prepsā velāyām kva ayam tadā puruṣaḥ bhavati iti upakramya śruti antaram karma āśraya tām nirūpayati tau ha yat ūcatuḥ karma ha eva tat ūcatuḥ atha ha yat praśaśaṃsatuḥ karma ha eva tat praśaśaṃsatuḥ iti
atrā ucyate tatra karma prayuktasya graha atigraha saṃjñakasya indriya viṣaya ātmakasya bandhanasya pravṛttiḥ iti karma āśraya tā uktā
iha punar bhūta upādānāt deha antara utpattiḥ iti bhūta āśraya tvam uktam
praśaṃsā śabdāt api tatra prādhānya mātram karmaṇaḥ pradarśitam na tu āśraya antaram nivāritam
tasmāt avirodhaḥ
samānā ca asṛti upakramāt amṛta tvam ca an upoṣya
āsṛti upakrama adhikaraṇam
sā iyam utkrāntiḥ kim vidvat aviduṣoḥ samānā kim vā viśeṣavatī iti viśayānānām viśeṣavatī iti tāvat prāptam
bhūta āśraya viśiṣṭā hi eṣā
punarbhavāya ca bhūtāni āśrīyante
na ca viduṣaḥ punarbhavaḥ saṃbhavati
amṛta tvam hi vidvān aśnute iti sthitiḥ
tasmāt a viduṣaḥ eva eṣā utkrāntiḥ
nanu vidyā prakaraṇe samāmnānāt viduṣaḥ eva eṣā bhavet na svāpa ādi vat yathā prāpta anukīrtanāt
yathā hi yatra etat puruṣaḥ svapiti nāma aśiśiṣati nāma pipāsati nāma iti ca sarva prāṇi sādhāraṇāḥ eva svāpa ādayaḥ nukīrtyante vidyā prakaraṇe pi pratipipādayiṣita vastu pratipādana ānuguṇyena na tu viduṣaḥ viśeṣavantaḥ vidhitsyante
evam iyam api utkrāntiḥ mahā jana gatā eva anukīrtyate yasyām parasyām devatāyām puruṣasya prayataḥ tejaḥ saṃpadyate saḥ ātmā tat tvam asi iti etat pratipādayitum
pratiṣiddhā ca eṣā viduṣaḥ na tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti iti
tasmāt a viduṣaḥ eva eṣā iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ samānā ca eṣā utkrāntiḥ vāc manasi ityādyā vidvat aviduṣoḥ āsṛti upakramāt bhavitum arhati aviśeṣa śravaṇāt
avidvān deha bīja bhūtāni bhūta sūkṣmāṇi āśritya karma prayuktaḥ deha grahaṇam anubhavan saṃsarati vidvān tu jñāna prakāśitam mokṣanāḍī dvāram āśrayate tat etat āsṛti upakramāt iti uktam
nanu amṛta tvam viduṣā prāptavyam na ca tat deśa antara āyattam tatra kutas bhūta āśraya tvam sṛti upakramaḥ vā iti atra ucyate an upoṣya ca idam a dagdhvā atyantam avidyā ādīn kleśān apara vidyā sāmarthyāt āpekṣikam amṛta tvam prepsate saṃbhavati tatra sṛti upakramaḥ
bhūta āśraya tvam ca na hi nirāśrayāṇām prāṇānām gatiḥ upapadyate
tasmāt adoṣaḥ
tadā apīteḥ saṃsāra vyapadeśāt
saṃsāra vyapadeśa adhikaraṇam
tejaḥ parasyām devatāyām iti atra prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt tat yathā prakṛtam tejaḥ sa adhyakṣam sa prāṇam sa karaṇa grāmam bhūta antara sahitam prayataḥ puṃsaḥ parasyām devatāyām saṃpadyate iti etat uktam bhavati
kīdṛśī punar iyam saṃpattiḥ syāt iti cintyate
tatra ātyantikaḥ eva tāvat svarūpa pravilayaḥ iti prāptam tad prakṛti tva upapatteḥ
sarvasya hi janimataḥ vastu jātasya prakṛtiḥ parā devatā iti pratiṣṭhāpitam
tasmāt ātyantikī iyam avibhāga āpattiḥ iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ tat tejaḥ ādi bhūta sūkṣmam śrotra ādi karaṇa āśraya bhūtam āpīteḥ ā saṃsāra mokṣāt samyak jñāna nimittāt avatiṣṭhate yonim anye prapadyante śarīra tvāya dehinaḥ
sthāṇum anye nusaṃyanti yathākarma yathāśrutam iti ādi saṃsāra vyapadeśāt
anyathā hi sarvaḥ prāyaṇa samaye eva upādhi prati astamayāt atyantam brahma saṃpadyeta tatra vidhi śāstram anarthakam syāt vidyā śāstram ca
mithyā jñāna nimittaḥ ca bandhaḥ na samyak jñānāt ṛte visraṃsitum arhati
tasmāt tad prakṛti tve pi suṣupti pralaya vat bīja bhāva avaśeṣā eva eṣā sat saṃpattiḥ iti
sūkṣmam pramāṇataḥ ca tathā upalabdheḥ
tat ca itara bhūta sahitam tejaḥ jīvasya asmāt śarīrāt pravasataḥ āśraya bhūtam svarūpataḥ parimāṇataḥ ca sūkṣmam bhavitum arhati
tathā hi nāḍī niṣkramaṇa śravaṇa ādibhyaḥ sya saukṣmyam upalabhyate
tatra tanu tvāt saṃcāra upapattiḥ
svaccha tvāt ca apratighāta upapattiḥ
atas eva ca dehāt nirgacchat pārśva sthaiḥ nā upalabhyate
na upamardena atas
atas eva ca sūkṣma tvāt na asya sthūlasya śarīrasya upamardena dāha ādi nimittena itarat sūkṣmam śarīram upamṛdyate
asya eva ca upapatteḥ eṣaḥ ūṣmā
asya eva ca sūkṣmasya śarīrasya eṣaḥ ūṣmā yam etasmin jīvat śarīre saṃsparśena ūṣmāṇam vijānanti
tathā hi mṛta avasthāyām avasthite dehe vidyamāneṣu api ca rūpa ādiṣu deha guṇeṣu na ūṣmā upalabhyate jīvat avasthāyām eva tu upalabhyate iti atas upapadyate prasiddha śarīra vyatirikta vyapāśrayaḥ eva eṣaḥ ūṣmā iti
tathā ca śrutiḥ uṣṇaḥ eva jīviṣyan śītaḥ mariṣyan iti
pratiṣedhāt iti ced na śārīrāt
pratiṣedha adhikaraṇam
amṛta tvam ca an upoṣyaḥ iti atas viśeṣaṇāt ātyantike mṛta tve gati utkrāntyoḥ abhāvaḥ bhyupagataḥ
tatra api kenacid kāraṇena utkrāntim āśaṅkya pratiṣedhati atha a kāmayamānaḥ yaḥ kāmaḥ niṣkāmaḥ āpta kāmaḥ ātma kāmaḥ bhavati na tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti brahma eva san brahma apyeti iti
atas para vidyā viṣayāt pratiṣedhāt na para brahma vidaḥ dehāt prāṇānām utkrāntiḥ asti iti ced nā iti ucyate yatas śārīrāt ātmanaḥ eṣaḥ utkrānti pratiṣedhaḥ prāṇānām na śarīrāt
katham avagamyate
na tasmāt prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti iti śākhā antare pañcamī prayogāt
saṃbandha sāmānya viṣayā hi ṣaṣṭhī śākhā antara gatayā pañcamyā saṃbandha viśeṣe vyavasthāpyate
tasmāt iti ca prādhānyāt abhyudaya niḥśreyasa adhikṛtaḥ dehī saṃbadhyate na dehaḥ
na tasmāt uccikramiṣoḥ jīvāt prāṇāḥ apakrāmanti saha eva tena bhavanti iti arthaḥ
sa prāṇasya ca pravasataḥ bhavati utkrāntiḥ dehāt iti
evam prāpte pratyucyate
spaṣṭaḥ hi ekeṣām
na etat asti yat uktam para brahma vidaḥ api dehāt asti utkrāntiḥ utkrānti pratiṣedhasya dehi apādāna tvāt iti
yatas deha apādāne eva utkrānti pratiṣedhaḥ ekeṣām samāmnātṛṇām spaṣṭaḥ upalabhyate
tathā hi ārtabhāgapraśne yatra ayam puruṣaḥ mriyate ud asmāt prāṇāḥ krāmanti āho na iti iti atra na iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ iti an utkrānti pakṣam parigṛhya na tarhi ayam an utkrānteṣu prāṇeṣu mṛtaḥ iti asyām āśaṅkāyām atra eva samavanīyante iti pravilayam prāṇānām pratijñāya tad siddhaye saḥ ucchvayati ādhmāyati ādhmātaḥ mṛtaḥ śete iti sa śabda parāmṛṣṭasya prakṛtasya utkrānti avadheḥ ucchvayana ādīni samāmananti
dehasya ca etāni syuḥ na dehinaḥ
tad sāmānyāt na tasmāt prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti atra eva samavanīyante iti atra api abheda upacāreṇa deha apādānasya eva utkramaṇasya pratiṣedhaḥ yadi api prādhānyam dehinaḥ iti vyākhyeyam yeṣām pañcamī pāṭhaḥ
yeṣām tu ṣaṣṭhī pāṭhaḥ teṣām vidvat saṃbandhinī utkrāntiḥ pratiṣidhyate iti prāpta utkrānti pratiṣedha artha tvāt asya vākyasya deha apādānā eva sā pratiṣiddhā bhavati dehāt utkrāntiḥ prāptā na dehinaḥ
api ca cakṣuṣṭas vā mūrdhnaḥ vā anyebhyaḥ vā śarīra deśebhyaḥ tam utkrāmantam prāṇaḥ nu utkrāmati prāṇam anūtkrāmantam sarve prāṇāḥ anūtkrāmanti iti evam avidvat viṣaye sa prapañcam utkramaṇam saṃsāra gamanam ca darśayitvā iti nu kāmayamānaḥ iti upasaṃhṛtya avidvat kathām atha a kāmayamānaḥ iti vyapadiśya vidvāṃsam yadi tad viṣaye pi utkrāntim eva prāpayet asamañjasaḥ eva vyapadeśaḥ syāt
tasmāt avidvat viṣaye prāptayoḥ gati utkrāntyoḥ vidvat viṣaye pratiṣedhaḥ iti evam eva vyākhyeyam vyapadeśa arthavat tvāya
na ca brahma vidaḥ sarvagata brahma ātma bhūtasya prakṣīṇa kāma karmaṇaḥ utkrāntiḥ gatiḥ vā upapadyate nimitta abhāvāt
atra brahma samaśnute iti ca evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayaḥ gati utkrāntyoḥ abhāvam sūcayanti
smaryate ca
smaryate ca mahābhārate gati utkrāntyoḥ abhāvaḥ sarva bhūta ātma bhūtasya samyak bhūtāni paśyataḥ
devāḥ api mārge muhyanti apadasya pada eṣiṇaḥ iti
nanu gatiḥ api brahma vidaḥ sarvagata brahma ātma bhūtasya smaryate śukaḥ kila vaiyāsakiḥ mumukṣuḥ āditya maṇḍalam abhipratasthe pitrā ca anugamya āhūtaḥ bho iti pratiśuśrāva iti na
sa śarīrasya eva ayam yoga balena viśiṣṭa deśa prāpti pūrvakaḥ śarīra utsargaḥ iti draṣṭavyam sarva bhūta dṛśya tva ādi upanyāsāt
na hi aśarīram gacchantam sarva bhūtāni draṣṭum śaknuyuḥ
tathā ca tatra eva upasaṃhṛtam śukaḥ tu mārutāt śīghrām gatim kṛtvā antarikṣa gaḥ
darśayitvā prabhāvam svam sarva bhūta gataḥ bhavat iti
tasmāt abhāvaḥ para brahma vidaḥ gati utkrāntyoḥ
gati śrutīnām tu viṣayam upariṣṭāt vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
tāni pare tathā himāha
vāc ādi laya adhikaraṇam
tāni punar prāṇa śabda uditāni indriyāṇi bhūtāni ca para brahma vidaḥ tasmin eva parasmin ātmani pralīyante
kasmāt
tathā hi āha śrutiḥ evam eva asya paridraṣṭuḥ imāḥ ṣoḍaśa kalāḥ puruṣāyaṇāḥ puruṣam prāpya astam gacchanti iti
nanu gatāḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa pratiṣṭhāḥ iti vidvat viṣayā eva aparā śrutiḥ parasmāt ātmanaḥ nyatra api kalānām pralayam āha sma na
sā khalu vyavahāra apekṣā pārthiva ādyāḥ kalāḥ pṛthivī ādīḥ eva sva prakṛtīḥ apiyanti iti
itarā tu vidvat pratipatti apekṣā kṛtsnam kalā jātam para brahma vidaḥ brahma eva saṃpadyate iti
tasmāt adoṣaḥ
a vibhāgaḥ vacanāt
a vibhāga adhikaraṇam
sa punar viduṣaḥ kalā pralayaḥ kim itareṣām iva sa avaśeṣaḥ bhavati āhosvit niravaśeṣaḥ iti
tatra pralaya sāmānyāt śakti avaśeṣa tā prasaktau bravīti avibhāga āpattiḥ eva iti
kutas
vacanāt
tathā hi kalā pralayam uktvā vakti bhidyete tāsām nāma rūpe puruṣaḥ iti evam procyate saḥ eṣa u kalaḥ mṛtaḥ bhavati iti
avidyā nimittānām ca kalānām na vidyā nimitte pralaye sa avaśeṣa tva upapattiḥ
tasmāt avibhāgaḥ eva iti
tad okaḥ tad prakāśita dvāraḥ vidyā sāmarthyāt tad śeṣa gati anusmṛti yogāt ca hārda anugṛhītaḥ śata adhikayā
tadā okaḥ dhikaraṇam
samāptā prāsaṅgikī para vidyā gatā cintā
saṃprati tu apara vidyā viṣayām eva cintām anuvartayati
samānā ca āsṛti upakramāt vidvat aviduṣoḥ utkrāntiḥ iti uktam
tam idānīm sṛti upakramam darśayati
tasya upasaṃhṛta vāc ādi kalāpasya uccikramiṣataḥ vijñāna ātmanaḥ okaḥ āyatanam hṛdayam saḥ etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyādadānaḥ hṛdayam eva anvavakrāmati iti śruteḥ tad agra prajvalana pūrvikā cakṣuḥ ādi sthāna apādānā ca utkrāntiḥ śrūyate tasya ha etasya hṛdayasya agram pradyotate tena pradyotena eṣaḥ ātmā niṣkrāmati cakṣuṣṭas vā mūrdhnaḥ vā anyebhyaḥ vā śarīra deśebhyaḥ iti
sā kim aniyamena eva vidvat aviduṣoḥ bhavati atha asti kaścid viduṣaḥ viśeṣa niyamaḥ iti vicikitsāyām śruti aviśeṣāt aniyama prāptau ācaṣṭe samāne hi vidvat aviduṣoḥ hṛdaya agra pradyotane tad prakāśita dvāra tve ca mūrdha sthānāt eva vidvān niṣkrāmati sthāna antarebhyaḥ tu itare
kutas
vidyā sāmarthyāt
yadi vidvān api itara vat yatas kutaścid deha deśāt utkrāmet na eva utkṛṣṭam lokam labheta tatra anarthikā eva vidyā syāt
tad śeṣa gati anusmṛti yogāt ca vidyā śeṣa bhūtā ca mūrdhanyanāḍī saṃbaddhā gatiḥ anuśīlayitavyā vidyā viśeṣeṣu vihitā
tām abhyasyan tayā eva pratiṣṭhate iti yuktam
tasmāt hṛdayālayena brahmaṇā su upāsitena anugṛhītaḥ tad bhāvam samāpannaḥ vidvān mūrdhanyayā eva śata adhikayā śatāt atiriktayā ekaśatatamyā nāḍyā niṣkrāmati itarābhiḥ itare
tathā hi hārda vidyām prakṛtya samāmananti śatam ca ekā ca hṛdayasya nāḍyaḥ tāsām mūrdhānam abhiniḥsṛtā ekā
tayā ūrdhvam āyan amṛta tvam eti viṣvaṅ anyāḥ utkramaṇe bhavanti iti
raśmi anusārī
raśmi adhikaraṇam
asti hārdavidyā atha yat idam asmin brahmapure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma iti upakramya vihitā
tad prakriyāyām atha yāḥ etāḥ hṛdayasya nāḍyaḥ iti upakramya sa prapañcam nāḍī raśmi saṃbandham uktvā uktam atha yatra etat asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati atha etaiḥ eva raśmibhiḥ ūrdhvam ākramate iti
punar ca uktam tayā ūrdhvam āyan amṛta tvam eti iti
tasmāt śata adhikayā nāḍyā niṣkrāman raśmi anusārī niṣkrāmati iti gamyate
tat kim aviśeṣeṇa eva ahani rātrau vā mriyamāṇasya raśmi anusāri tvam āhosvit ahani eva iti saṃśaye sati aviśeṣa śravaṇāt aviśeṣeṇa eva tāvat raśmi anusāri iti pratijñāyate
niśi nā iti ced na sambandhasya yāvaddehabhāvi tvāt darśayati ca
asti ahani nāḍī raśmi saṃbandhaḥ iti ahani mṛtasya syāt raśmi anusāri tvam
rātrau tu pretasya na syāt nāḍī raśmi saṃbandha vicchedāt iti ced na nāḍī raśmi saṃbandhasya yāvaddehabhāvi tvāt
yāvat deha bhāvī hi śirā kiraṇa saṃparkaḥ
darśayati ca etam artham śrutiḥ amuṣmāt ādityāt pratāyante tāḥ āsu nāḍīṣu sṛptāḥ ābhyaḥ nāḍībhyaḥ pratāyante te muṣmin āditye sṛptāḥ iti
nidāgha samaye ca niśāsu api kiraṇa anuvṛttiḥ upalabhyate pratāpa ādi kārya darśanāt
stoka anuvṛtteḥ tu durlakṣya tvam ṛtu antara rajanīṣu śaiśireṣu iva durdineṣu
ahar eva etat rātrau dadhāti iti ca etat eva darśayati
yadi ca rātrau pretaḥ vinā eva raśmi anusāreṇa ūrdhvam ākrameta raśmi anusāra ānarthakyam bhavet
na hi etat viśiṣya abhidhīyate yaḥ divā praiti sa raśmīn apekṣya ūrdhvam ākramate yaḥ tu rātrau saḥ n apekṣya eva iti
atha tu vidvān api rātri prāyaṇa aparādha mātreṇa na ūrdhvam ākrameta pākṣika phalā vidyā iti apravṛttiḥ eva tasyām syāt mṛtyu kāla aniyamāt
atha api rātrau uparataḥ hara āgamam udīkṣeta ahar āgame pi asya kadācid a raśmi saṃbandha arham śarīram syāt pāvaka ādi saṃparkāt
sa yāvat kṣipyet manaḥ tāvat ādityam gacchati iti ca śrutiḥ anudīkṣām darśayati
tasmāt aviśeṣeṇa eva idam rātriṃdivam raśmi anusāri tvam
atas ca ayane pi dakṣiṇe
dakṣiṇāyana adhikaraṇam
atas eva ca udīkṣā anupapatteḥ a pākṣika phala tvāt ca vidyāyāḥ aniyata kāla tvāt ca mṛtyoḥ dakṣiṇāyane mriyamāṇaḥ vidvān prāpnoti eva vidyā phalam
uttarāyaṇa maraṇa prāśastya prasiddheḥ bhīṣmasya ca pratīkṣā darśanāt āpūryamāṇapakṣāt yān ṣaṭ udaṅ eti māsān tān iti ca śruteḥ apekṣitavyam uttarāyaṇam iti imām āśaṅkām anena sūtreṇa apanudati
prāśastya prasiddhiḥ avidvat viṣayā
bhīṣmasya pratipālanam ācāra paripālana artham pitṛ prasāda labdha svacchanda mṛtyu tā khyāpana artham ca
śruteḥ tu artham vakṣyati ātivāhikāḥ tad liṅgāt iti
nanu ca yatra kāle tu anāvṛttim āvṛttim ca eva yoginaḥ
prayātāḥ yānti tam kālam vakṣyāmi bharata ṛṣabhaḥ iti kāla prādhānyena upakramya ahar ādi kāla viśeṣaḥ smṛtau anāvṛttaye niyataḥ
katham rātrau dakṣiṇāyane vā prayātaḥ na āvṛttim yāyāt iti atra ucyate
yoginaḥ prati ca smaryate smārte ca ete
yoginaḥ prati ca ayam ahar ādi kāla viniyogaḥ anāvṛttaye smaryate
smārte ca ete yoga sāṃkhye na śraute
atas viṣaya bhedāt pramāṇa viśeṣāt ca na asya smārtasya kāla viniyogasya śrauteṣu vijñāneṣu avatāraḥ
nanu agniḥ jyotiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ uttarāyaṇam
dhūmaḥ rātriḥ tathā kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṣ māsāḥ dakṣiṇāyanam iti ca śrautau etau deva yāna pitṛyāṇau pratyabhijñāyete smṛtau api iti ucyate tam kālam vakṣyāmi iti smṛtau kāla pratijñānāt virodham āśaṅkya ayam parihāraḥ uktaḥ
yadā punar smṛtau api agni ādyāḥ devatāḥ eva ātivāhikyaḥ gṛhyante tadā na kaścid virodhaḥ iti
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ

caturthaḥ udhyāyaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
arciḥ ādinā tad prathiteḥ
arciḥ ādi adhikaraṇam
arciḥ ādinā iti
sarvaḥ brahma prepsuḥ arciḥ ādinā eva adhvanā raṃhati iti pratijānīmahe
kutas
tad prathiteḥ
prathitaḥ hi eṣa mārgaḥ sarveṣām viduṣām
tathā hi pañcāgni vidyā prakaraṇe ye ca amī araṇye śraddhām satyam upāsate iti vidyā antara śīlinām api arciḥ ādikā sṛtiḥ śrāvyate
syāt etat yāsu vidyāsu na kācid gatiḥ ucyate tāsu iyam arciḥ ādikā upatiṣṭhatām
yāsu tu anyā śrāvyate tāsu kim iti arciḥ ādi āśrayaṇam iti atra ucyate bhavet etat evam yadi atyanta bhinnāḥ eva etāḥ sṛtayaḥ syuḥ
ekā eva tu eṣā sṛtiḥ aneka viśeṣaṇā brahma loka prapadanī kvacid kenacid viśeṣaṇena upalakṣitā iti vadāmaḥ sarvatra eka deśa pratyabhijñānāt itaretara viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva upapatteḥ
prakaraṇa bhede pi hi vidyā eka tve bhavati itaretara viśeṣaṇa upasaṃhāra vat gati viśeṣaṇānām api upasaṃhāraḥ
vidyā bhede tu gati eka deśa pratyabhijñānāt gantavya abhedāt ca gati abhedaḥ eva
tathā hi te teṣu brahma lokeṣu parāḥ parāvataḥ vasanti tasmin vasanti śāśvatīḥ samāḥ sā yā brahmaṇaḥ jitiḥ yā vyuṣṭiḥ tām jitim jayati tām vyuṣṭim vyaśnute tat yaḥ eva etam brahma lokam brahmacaryeṇa anuvindati iti ca tatra tatra tat eva ekam phalam brahma loka prāpti lakṣaṇam pradarśyate
yat tu etaiḥ eva iti avadhāraṇam arciḥ ādi āśrayaṇe na syāt iti na eṣa doṣaḥ raśmi prāpti paratvāt asya
na hi ekaḥ eva śabdaḥ raśmīn ca prāpayitum arhati arciḥ ādīn ca vyāvartayitum
tasmāt raśmi saṃbandhaḥ eva ayam avadhāryate iti draṣṭavyam
tvarā vacanam tu arciḥ ādi apekṣāyām api gantavya antara apekṣayā kṣaiprya artha tvāt na uparudhyate yathā nimeṣa mātreṇa atra āgamyate iti
api ca atha etayoḥ pathoḥ na katareṇa cana iti mārga dvaya bhraṣṭānām kaṣṭam tṛtīyam sthānam ācakṣāṇā pitṛyāṇa vyatiriktam ekam eva deva yānam arciḥ ādi parvāṇam panthānam prathayati
bhūyāṃsi arciḥ ādi sṛtau mārga parvāṇi alpīyāṃsi tu anyatra
bhūyasām ca ānuguṇyena alpīyasām nayanam nyāyyam iti atas arciḥ ādinā tad prathiteḥ iti uktam
vāyum abdāt aviśeṣa viśeṣābhyām
vāyu adhikaraṇam
kena punar saṃniveśa viśeṣeṇa gati viśeṣaṇānām itaretara viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ iti tat etat suhṛd bhūtvā ācāryaḥ grathayati
saḥ etam deva yānam panthānam āsādya agni lokam āgacchati sa vāyu lokam sa varuṇa lokam saḥ indra lokam sa prajāpati lokam sa brahma lokam iti kauṣītakinām deva yānaḥ panthāḥ paṭhyate
tatra arciḥ agni loka śabdau tāvat eka arthau jvalana vacana tvāt iti na atra saṃniveśa kramaḥ kaścid anveṣyaḥ
vāyuḥ tu arciḥ ādau vartmani katamasmin sthāne niveśayitavyaḥ iti ucyate te rciṣam eva abhisaṃbhavanti arciṣaḥ har ahnaḥ āpūryamāṇapakṣam āpūryamāṇapakṣāt yān ṣaṭ udaṅ eti māsān tān māsebhyaḥ saṃvatsaram saṃvatsarāt ādityam iti atra saṃvatsarāt parāñcam ādityāt arvāñcam vāyum abhisaṃbhavanti
kasmāt
aviśeṣa viśeṣābhyām
tathā hi sa vāyu lokam iti atra aviśeṣa upadiṣṭasya vāyoḥ śruti antareṇa viśeṣa upadeśaḥ dṛśyate yadā vai puruṣaḥ u smāt lokāt praiti sa vāyum āgacchati tasmai sa tatra vijihīte yathā ratha cakrasya kham tena saḥ ūrdhvam ākramate saḥ ādityam āgacchati iti
etasmāt ādityāt vāyoḥ pūrva tva darśanāt viśeṣāt abda ādityayoḥ antarāle vāyuḥ niveśayitavyaḥ
kasmāt punar agneḥ paratva darśanāt viśeṣāt arciṣaḥ nantaram vāyuḥ na niveśyate
na eṣaḥ sti viśeṣaḥ iti vadāmaḥ
nanu udāhṛtā śrutiḥ saḥ etam deva yānam panthānam āsādya agni lokam āgacchati sa vāyu lokam sa varuṇa lokam iti
ucyate kevalaḥ tra pāṭhaḥ paurvāparyeṇa avasthitaḥ na atra krama vacanaḥ kaścid śabdaḥ sti
padārtha upadarśana mātram hi atra kriyate etam etam ca āgacchati iti
itaratra punar vāyu prattena ratha cakra mātreṇa chidreṇa ūrdhvam ākramya ādityam āgacchati iti avagamyate kramaḥ
tasmāt sūktam a viśeṣa viśeṣābhyām iti
vājasaneyinaḥ tu māsebhyaḥ deva lokam deva lokāt ādityam iti samāmananti
tatra āditya ānantaryāya deva lokāt vāyum abhisaṃbhaveyuḥ
vāyum abdāt iti tu chandoga śruti apekṣayā uktam
chāndogya vājasaneyakayoḥ tu ekatra deva lokaḥ na vidyate paratra saṃvatsaraḥ
tatra śruti dvaya pratyayāt ubhau api ubhayatra grathayitavyau
tatra api māsa saṃbandhāt saṃvatsaraḥ pūrvaḥ paścimaḥ deva lokaḥ iti vivektavyam
taḍitaḥ dhi varuṇaḥ sambandhāt
taḍit adhikaraṇam
ādityāt candramasam candramasaḥ vidyutam iti asyāḥ vidyutaḥ upariṣṭāt sa varuṇa lokam iti ayam varuṇaḥ saṃbadhyeta
asti hi saṃbandhaḥ vidyut varuṇayoḥ
yadā hi viśālāḥ vidyutaḥ tīvra stanita nirghoṣāḥ jīmūta udareṣu pranṛtyanti atha āpaḥ prapatanti
vidyotate stanayati varṣiṣyati vā iti ca brāhmaṇam
apām ca adhipatiḥ varuṇaḥ iti śruti smṛti prasiddhiḥ
varuṇāt adhi indra prajāpatī sthāna antara abhāvāt pāṭha sāmarthyāt ca
āgantuka tvāt api varuṇa ādīnām ante eva niveśaḥ vaiśeṣika sthāna abhāvāt
vidyut ca antyā arciḥ ādau vartmani
ātivāhikāḥ tad liṅgāt
ātivāhika adhikaraṇam
teṣu eva arciḥ ādiṣu saṃśayaḥ kim etāni mārga cihnāni uta bhogabhūmayaḥ athavā netāraḥ gantṛṇām iti
tatra mārga lakṣaṇa bhūtāḥ arciḥ ādayaḥ iti tāvat prāptam tad svarūpa tvāt upadeśasya
yathā hi loke kaścid grāmam nagaram vā pratiṣṭhā samānaḥ nuśiṣyate gaccha itas tvam amum girim tatas nyagrodham tatas nadīm tatas grāmam tatas nagaram vā prāpsyasi iti evam iha api arciṣaḥ har ahnaḥ āpūryamāṇapakṣam ityādi āha
atha vā bhogabhūmayaḥ iti prāptam
tathā hi loka śabdena agni ādīn anubadhnāti agni lokam āgacchati ityādi
loka śabdaḥ ca prāṇinām bhogāyataneṣu bhāṣyate manuṣya lokaḥ pitṛ lokaḥ deva lokaḥ iti ca
tathā ca brāhmaṇam ahar rātreṣu te lokeṣu sajjante ityādi
tasmāt na ativāhikāḥ arciḥ ādayaḥ
acetana tvāt api eṣām ātivāhika tva anupapattiḥ
cetanāḥ hi loke rāja niyuktāḥ puruṣāḥ durgeṣu mārgeṣu ativāhyān ativāhayanti iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ ātivāhikāḥ eva ete bhavitum arhanti
kutas
tad liṅgāt
tathā hi candramasaḥ vidyutam tatpuruṣaḥ mānavaḥ saḥ etān brahma gamayati iti siddha vat gamayitṛ tvam darśayati
tad vacanam tad viṣayam evā upakṣīṇam iti ced na prāpta mānavatva nivṛtti paratvāt viśeṣaṇasya
yadi arciḥ ādiṣu puruṣāḥ gamayitāraḥ prāptāḥ te ca mānavāḥ tatas yuktam tad nivṛtti artham puruṣa viśeṣaṇam amānavaḥ iti
nanu tat liṅga mātram agamakam nyāya abhāvāt
na eṣa doṣaḥ
ubhaya vyāmohāt tad siddheḥ
ye tāvat arciḥ ādi mārga gāḥ te deha viyogāt saṃpiṇḍita karaṇa grāmāḥ iti asvatantrāḥ
arciḥ ādīnām api acetana tvāt asvātantryam iti atas arciḥ ādi abhimāninaḥ cetanāḥ devatā viśeṣāḥ atiyātrāyām niyuktāḥ iti gamyate
loke hi matta mūrchita ādayaḥ saṃpiṇḍita karaṇāḥ para prayukta vartmānaḥ bhavanti
anavasthita tvāt api arciḥ ādīnām na mārga lakṣaṇa tva upapattiḥ
na hi rātrau pretasya ahar sva rūpa abhisaṃbhavaḥ upapadyate
na ca pratipālanam asti iti uktam purastāt
dhruva tvāt tu devatā ātmanām na ayam doṣaḥ bhavati
arciḥ ādi śabda tā ca eṣām arciḥ ādi abhimānāt upapadyate
arciṣaḥ haḥ ityādi nirdeśaḥ tu ātivāhika tve pi na virudhyate arciṣā hetunā ahar abhisaṃbhavati ahnā hetunā āpūryamāṇapakṣam iti
tathā ca loke prasiddheṣu api ātivāhikeṣu evaṃjātīyakaḥ upadeśaḥ dṛśyate gaccha tvam itas balavarmāṇam tatas jayasiṃham tatas kṛṣṇaguptam iti
api ca upakrame te rciḥ abhisaṃbhavanti iti saṃbandha mātram uktam na saṃbandha viśeṣaḥ kaścid
upasaṃhāre tu saḥ etān brahma gamayati iti saṃbandha viśeṣaḥ ativāhya ativāhaka tva lakṣaṇaḥ uktaḥ
tena saḥ eva upakrame pi iti nirdhāryate
saṃpiṇḍita karaṇa tvāt eva ca gantṛṇām na tatra bhoga saṃbhavaḥ
loka śabdaḥ tu an upabhuñjāneṣu api gantṛṣu gamayitum śakyate anyeṣām talloka vāsinām bhogabhūmi tvāt
atas agni svāmikam lokam prāptaḥ agninā ativāhyate vāyu svāmikam prāptaḥ vāyunā iti yojayitavyam
katham punar ātivāhika tva pakṣe varuṇa ādiṣu tad saṃbhavaḥ
vidyutaḥ hi adhi varuṇa ādayaḥ upakṣiptāḥ vidyutaḥ tu anantaram ā brahma prāpteḥ amānavasya eva puruṣasya gamayitṛ tvam śrutam iti atas uttaram paṭhati
vaidyutena eva tatas tad śruteḥ
tatas vidyut abhisaṃbhavanāt ūrdhvam vidyut anantara vartinā eva amānavena puruṣeṇa varuṇa loka ādiṣu ativāhyamānāḥ brahma lokam gacchanti iti avagantavyam tān vaidyutāt puruṣaḥ mānavaḥ saḥ etya brahma lokam gamayati iti tasya eva gamayitṛ tva śruteḥ
varuṇa ādayaḥ tu tasya eva apratibandha karaṇena sāhāyya anuṣṭhānena vā kenacid anugrāhakāḥ iti avagantavyam
tasmāt sādhu uktam ātivāhikāḥ devatā ātmānaḥ rciḥ ādayaḥ iti
kāryam bādariḥ asya gati upapatteḥ
kārya adhikaraṇam
saḥ enān brahma gamayati iti atra vicikitsyate kim kāryam aparam brahma gamayati āhosvit param eva avikṛtam mukhyam brahma iti
kutas saṃśayaḥ
brahma śabda prayogāt gati śruteḥ ca
tatra kāryam eva saguṇam aparam brahma enān gamayati amānavaḥ puruṣaḥ iti bādariḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
kutas
asya gati upapatteḥ asya hi kārya brahmaṇaḥ gantavya tvam upapadyate pradeśavat tvāt
na tu parasmin brahmaṇi gantṛ tvam gantavya tvam gatiḥ vā avakalpate sarvagata tvāt pratyagātma tvāt ca gantṛṇām
viśeṣita tvāt ca
brahma lokān gamayati te teṣu brahma lokeṣu parāḥ parāvataḥ vasanti iti ca śruti antare viśeṣita tvāt kārya brahma viṣayā eva gatiḥ iti gamyate
na hi bahuvacanena viśeṣaṇam parasmin brahmaṇi avakalpate
kārye tu avasthā bheda upapatteḥ saṃbhavati bahuvacanam
loka śrutiḥ api vikāra gocarāyām eva saṃniveśa viśiṣṭāyām bhogabhūmau āñjasī
gauṇī tu anyatra brahmā eva lokaḥ eṣa samrāj ityādiṣu
adhikaraṇa adhikartavya nirdeśaḥ pi parasmin brahmaṇi anāñjasaḥ syāt
tasmāt kārya viṣayam eva idam nayanam
nanu kārya viṣaye pi brahma śabdaḥ na upapadyate samanvaye hi samastasya jagataḥ janma ādikāraṇam brahma iti sthāpitam iti atra ucyate
sāmīpyāt tu tad vyapadeśaḥ
tu śabdaḥ āśaṅkā vyāvṛtti arthaḥ
para brahma sāmīpyāt aparasya brahmaṇaḥ tasmin api brahma śabda prayogaḥ na virudhyate
param eva hi brahma viśuddha upādhi saṃbandham kvacid kaiścid vikāra dharmaiḥ manaḥ maya tva ādibhiḥ upāsanāya upadiśyamānam aparam iti sthitiḥ
nanu kārya prāptau anāvṛtti śravaṇam na ghaṭate
na hi parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ nyatra kvacid nitya tām saṃbhāvayanti
darśayati ca deva yānena pathā prasthitānām anāvṛttim etena pratipadyamānāḥ imam mānavam āvartam na āvartante iti teṣām iha na punarāvṛttiḥ asti tayā ūrdhvam āyan amṛta tvam eti iti ca
atra brūmaḥ
kārya atyaye tad adhyakṣeṇa saha atas param abhidhānāt
kārya brahmaloka pralaya pratyupasthāne sati tatra eva utpanna samyak darśanāḥ santaḥ tad adhyakṣeṇa hiraṇyagarbheṇa saha atas para pariśuddham viṣṇoḥ paramam padam pratipadyante iti ittham krama muktiḥ anāvṛtti ādi śruti abhidhānebhyaḥ bhyupagantavyā
na hi añjasā eva gati pūrvikā para prāptiḥ saṃbhavati iti upapāditam
smṛteḥ ca
smṛtiḥ api etam artham anujānāti brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare
parasya ante kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti param padam iti
tasmāt kārya brahma viṣayāḥ eva gati śrutayaḥ iti siddhāntaḥ
kam punar pūrvapakṣam āśaṅkya ayam siddhāntaḥ pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ kāryam bādariḥ ityādinā iti saḥ idānīm sūtraiḥ eva upadarśyate
param jaiminiḥ mukhya tvāt
jaiminiḥ tu ācāryaḥ saḥ enān brahma gamayati iti atra param eva brahma prāpayati iti manyate
kutas
mukhya tvāt
param hi brahma brahma śabdasya mukhyam ālambanam gauṇam aparam
mukhya gauṇayoḥ ca mukhye saṃpratyayaḥ bhavati
darśanāt ca
tayā ūrdhvam āyan amṛta tvam eti iti ca gati pūrvakam amṛta tvam darśayati
amṛta tvam ca parasmin brahmaṇi upapadyate na kārye vināśi tvāt kāryasya atha yatra anyat paśyati tat alpam tat martyam iti pravacanāt para viṣayā eva ca eṣā gatiḥ kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate
na hi tatra vidyā antara prakramaḥ u sti anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt iti parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ prakrānta tvāt
na ca kārye pratipatti abhisandhiḥ
api ca prajāpateḥ sabhām veśma prapadye iti na ayam kārya viṣayaḥ pratipatti abhisaṃdhiḥ nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yat antarā tat brahma iti kārya vilakṣaṇasya parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ prakṛta tvāt
yaśaḥ ham bhavāmi brāhmaṇānām iti ca sarva ātma tvena upakramaṇāt
na tasya pratimā asti yasya nāma mahat yaśaḥ iti ca parasya eva brahmaṇaḥ yaśaḥ nāma tva prasiddheḥ
sā ca iyam veśma pratipattiḥ gati pūrvikā hārdavidyāyām uditā tad aparājitā pūḥ brahmaṇaḥ prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam iti atra
padeḥ api ca gati artha tvāt mārga apekṣa tā avasīyate
tasmāt para brahma viṣayāḥ gati śrutayaḥ iti pakṣa antaram
tau etau dvau pakṣau ācāryeṇa sūtritau gati upapatti ādibhiḥ ekaḥ mukhya tva ādibhiḥ aparaḥ
tatra gati upapatti ādayaḥ prabhavanti mukhya tva ādīn ābhāsayitum na tu mukhya tva ādayaḥ gati upapatti ādīn iti ādyaḥ eva siddhāntaḥ vyākhyātaḥ dvitīyaḥ tu pūrvapakṣaḥ
na hi asati api saṃbhave mukhyasya eva arthasya grahaṇam iti kaścid ājñāpayitā vidyate
para vidyā prakaraṇe ca tad stuti artham vidyā antara āśraya gati anukīrtanam upapadyate viṣvaṅ anyāḥ utkramaṇe bhavanti itivat
prajāpateḥ sabhām veśma prapadye iti tu pūrva vākya vicchedena kārye pi pratipatti abhisaṃdhiḥ na virudhyate
saguṇe ca brahmaṇi sarva ātma tva saṃkīrtanam sarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ ityādi vat avakalpate
tasmāt apara viṣayāḥ eva gati śrutayaḥ
kecid punar pūrvāṇi pūrvapakṣa sūtrāṇi bhavanti uttarāṇi siddhānta sūtrāṇi iti etām vyavasthām anurudhyamānāḥ para viṣayāḥ eva gati śrutīḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti
tat anupapannam gantavya tva anupapatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ
yat sarva gatam sarva antaram sarva ātmakam ca param brahma ākāśa vat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ yat sākṣāt aparokṣāt brahma yaḥ ātmā sarva antaraḥ ātmā eva idam sarvam brahma eva idam viśvam idam variṣṭham ityādi śruti nirdhārita viśeṣam tasya gantavya tā na kadācid api upapadyate
na hi gatam eva gamyate
anyaḥ hi anyat gacchati iti prasiddham loke
nanu loke gatasya api gantavya tā deśa antara viśiṣṭasya dṛṣṭā yathā pṛthivī sthaḥ eva pṛthivīm deśa antara dvāreṇa gacchati tathā ananyatve pi bālasya kāla antara viśiṣṭam vārddhakam svātma bhūtam eva gantavyam dṛṣṭam tadvat brahmaṇaḥ sarva śakti upeta tvāt kathaṃcid gantavya tā syāt iti na pratiṣiddha sarva viśeṣa tvāt brahmaṇaḥ
niṣkalam niṣkriyam śāntam niravadyam nirañjanam a sthūlam an aṇu a hrasvam a dīrgham sa bāhya abhyantaraḥ hi ajaḥ sa vai eṣa mahān ajaḥ ātmā ajaraḥ maraḥ mṛtaḥ bhayaḥ brahma saḥ eṣa na iti na iti ātmā ityādi śruti smṛti nyāyebhyaḥ na deśa kāla ādi viśeṣa yogaḥ paramātmani kalpayitum śakyate yena bhū pradeśa vayaḥ vasthā nyāyena asya gantavya tā syāt
bhū vayasoḥ tu pradeśa avasthā ādi viśeṣa yogāt upapadyate deśa kāla viśiṣṭā gantavya tā
jagat utpatti sthiti pralaya hetutva śruteḥ aneka śaktitvam brahmaṇaḥ iti ced na viśeṣa nirākaraṇa śrutīnām ananya artha tvāt
utpatti ādi śrutīnām api samānam ananyārthatvam iti ced na tāsām ekatva pratipādana paratvāt
mṛd ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ hi sataḥ brahmaṇaḥ ekasya satya tvam vikārasya ca anṛta tvam pratipādayat śāstram nā utpatti ādi param bhavitum arhati
kasmāt punar utpatti ādi śrutīnām viśeṣa nirākaraṇa śruti śeṣa tvam na punar itara śeṣa tvam itarāsām iti ucyate viśeṣa nirākaraṇa śrutīnām nirākāṅkṣa artha tvāt
na hi ātmanaḥ eka tva nitya tva śuddha tva ādi avagatau satyām bhūyas kācid ākāṅkṣā upajāyate puruṣa artha samāpti buddhi utpatteḥ tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ ekatvam anupaśyataḥ abhayam vai janaka vidvān na bibheti kutaścana
eta iha vāva na tapati
kim ahä sādhu na akaravam
kim aham pāpam akaravam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tathā eva ca viduṣām tuṣṭi anubhava ādi darśanāt vikāra anṛta abhisaṃdhi apavādāt ca mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti
atas na viśeṣa nirākaraṇa śrutīnām anya śeṣa tvam avagantum śakyam
na evam utpatti ādi śrutīnām nirākāṅkṣa artha pratipādana sāmarthyam asti
pratyakṣam tu tāsām anya artha tvam samanugamyate
tathā hi tatra etat śuṅgam utpatitam somya vijānīhi na idam amūlam bhaviṣyati iti upanyasya udarke sataḥ eva ekasya jagat mūlasya vijñeya tvam darśayati
yatas vai imāni bhūtāni jāyante
yena jātāni jīvanti
yat prayanti abhisaṃviśanti
tat vijijñāsasva
tat brahma iti ca
evam utpatti ādi śrutīnām aikātmya avagama para tvāt na aneka śakti yogaḥ brahmaṇaḥ
atas ca gantavya tva anupapattiḥ
na tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti brahma eva san brahma apyeti iti ca parasmin brahmaṇi gatim nivārayati
tat vyakhyātam spaṣṭaḥ hi ekeṣām iti atra
gati kalpanāyām ca gantā jīvaḥ gantavyasya brahmaṇaḥ avayavaḥ vikāraḥ anyaḥ vā tatas syāt atyanta tādātmye gamana anupapatteḥ
yadi evam tatas kim syāt
atas ucyate yadi eka deśaḥ tena eka deśinaḥ nitya prāpta tvāt na punar brahmagamanam upapadyate
eka deśa eka deśi tva kalpanā ca brahmaṇi anupapannā niravayava tva prasiddheḥ
vikāra pakṣe pi etat tulyam vikāreṇa api vikāriṇaḥ nitya prāpta tvāt
na hi ghaṭaḥ mṛd ātma tām parityajya avatiṣṭhate parityāge vā abhāva prāpteḥ
vikāra avayava pakṣayoḥ ca tadvataḥ sthira tvāt brahmaṇaḥ saṃsāra gamanam api anavaklṛptam
atha anyaḥ eva jīvaḥ brahmaṇaḥ saḥ ṇuḥ vyāpī madhyama parimāṇaḥ vā bhavitum arhati
vyāpi tve gamana anupapattiḥ
madhyama parimāṇa tve ca anitya tva prasaṅgaḥ
aṇu tve kṛtsna śarīra vedanā anupapattiḥ
pratiṣiddhe ca aṇu tva madhyama parimāṇa tve vistareṇa purastāt
parasmāt ca anyatve jīvasya tat tvam asi ityādi śāstra bādha prasaṅgaḥ
vikāra avayava pakṣayoḥ api samānaḥ yam doṣaḥ
vikāra avayavayoḥ tadvataḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced na mukhya ekatva anupapatteḥ
sarveṣu ca eteṣu pakṣeṣu anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ saṃsāri ātma tva anivṛtteḥ
nivṛttau vā svarūpa nāśa prasaṅgaḥ brahma ātmatva anabhyupagamāt ca
yat tu kaiścid jalpyate nityāni naimittikāni ca karmāṇi anuṣṭhīyante pratyavāya anutpattaye kāmyāni pratiṣiddhāni ca parihriyante svarga naraka anavāptaye sāṃprata deha upabhogyāni ca karmāṇi upabhogena eva kṣipyante iti atas vartamāna dehapātāt ūrdhvam deha antara pratisaṃdhāna kāraṇa abhāvāt svarūpa avasthāna lakṣaṇam kaivalyam vinā api brahma ātmatayā evaṃvṛttasya setsyati iti tat asat pramāṇa abhāvāt
na hi etat śāstreṇa kenacid pratipāditam mokṣa arthī ittham samācaret iti
sva manīṣayā tu etat tarkitam yasmāt karma nimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ tasmāt nimitta abhāvāt na bhaviṣyati iti
na ca etat tarkayitum śakyate nimitta abhāvasya durjñāna tvāt
bahūni hi karmāṇi jāti antara saṃcitāni iṣṭa aniṣṭa vipākāni ekaikasya jantoḥ saṃbhāvyante
teṣām viruddha phalānām yugapad upabhoga asaṃbhavāt kānicid labdha avasarāṇi idam janma nirmimate kānicid tu deśa kāla nimitta pratīkṣāṇi āsate iti atas teṣām avaśiṣṭānām sāṃpratena upabhogena kṣapaṇa asaṃbhavāt na yathā varṇita caritasya api vartamāna dehapāte deha antara nimitta abhāvaḥ śakyate niścetum
karma śeṣa sadbhāva siddhiḥ ca tat ye iha ramaṇīya caraṇāḥ tatas śeṣeṇa ityādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ
syāt etat nitya naimittikāni teṣām kṣepakāṇi bhaviṣyanti iti tat na virodha abhāvāt
sati hi virodhe kṣepya kṣepaka bhāvaḥ bhavati
na ca janma antara saṃcitānām sukṛtānām nitya naimittikaiḥ asti virodhaḥ śuddhi rūpa tva aviśeṣāt
duritānām tu aśuddhi rūpa tvāt sati virodhe bhavatu kṣapaṇam
na tu tāvatā deha antara nimitta abhāva siddhiḥ sukṛta nimitta tva upapatteḥ duritasya api aśeṣa kṣapaṇa anavagamāt
na ca nitya naimittika anuṣṭhānāt pratyavāya anutpatti mātram na punar phala antara utpattiḥ iti pramāṇam asti phala antarasya api anuniṣpādinaḥ saṃbhavāt
smarati hi āpastambaḥ tat yathā āmre phala arthe nimitte chāyā gandhau anūtpadyete evam dharmam caryamāṇam arthāḥ anūtpadyante iti
na ca asati samyak darśane sarva ātmanā kāmya pratiṣiddha varjanam janma prāyaṇa antarāle kenacid pratijñātum śakyam su nipuṇānām api sūkṣma aparādha darśanāt
saṃśayitavyam tu bhavati
tathā api nimitta abhāvasya durjñāna tvam eva
na ca an abhyupagamyamāne jñāna gamye brahma ātmatve kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ kaivalyam ākāṅkṣitum śakyam agni auṣṇya vat svabhāvasya aparihārya tvāt
syāt etat kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva kāryam anarthaḥ na tad śaktiḥ tena śakti avasthāne pi kārya parihārāt upapannaḥ mokṣaḥ iti tat ca na
śakti sadbhāve kārya prasavasya durnivāra tvāt
atha api syāt na kevalā śaktiḥ kāryam ārabhate an apekṣya anyāni nimittāni
atas ekākinī sā sthitā api nā aparādhyati iti tat ca na nimittānām api śakti lakṣaṇena saṃbandhena nitya saṃbaddha tvāt
tasmāt kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva svabhāve sati ātmani asatyām vidyā gamyāyām brahma ātmatāyām na kathaṃcana mokṣam prati āśā asti
śrutiḥ ca na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate yanāyaḥ iti jñānāt anyam mokṣa mārgam vārayati
parasmāt ananya tve pi jīvasya sarva vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa apravṛtteḥ iti ced na prāk prabodhāt svapna vyavahāra vat tad upapatteḥ
śāstram ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itaraḥ itaram paśyati ityādinā aprabuddha viṣaye pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāram uktvā punar prabuddha viṣaye yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tat kena kam paśyet ityādinā tad abhāvam darśayati
tat evam para brahma vidaḥ gantavya ādi vijñānasya bādhita tvāt na kathaṃcana gatiḥ upapādayitum śakyā
kiṃviṣayāḥ punar gati śrutayaḥ iti ucyate sa guṇa vidyā viṣayāḥ bhaviṣyanti
tathā hi kvacid pañcāgni vidyām prakṛtya gatiḥ ucyate kvacid paryaṅka vidyām kvacid vaiśvānara vidyām
yatra api brahma prakṛtya gatiḥ ucyate yathā prāṇaḥ brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti atha yat idam asmin brahmapure daharam puṇḍarīkam veśma iti ca tatra api vāmanī tva ādibhiḥ satyakāma ādibhiḥ ca guṇaiḥ sa guṇasya eva upāsya tvāt saṃbhavati gatiḥ
na kvacid para brahma viṣayā gatiḥ śrāvyate yathā gati pratiṣedhaḥ śrāvitaḥ na tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti iti
brahma vid āpnoti param ityādiṣu tu sati api āpnoteḥ gati artha tve varṇitena nyāyena deśa antara prāpti asaṃbhavāt svarūpa pratipattiḥ eva iyam avidyā adhyāropita nāma rūpa pravilaya apekṣayā abhidhīyate brahma eva san brahma apyeti ityādi vat iti draṣṭavyam
api ca para viṣayā gatiḥ vyākhyāyamānā prarocanāya vā syāt anucintanāya vā
tatra prarocanam tāvat brahma vidaḥ na gati uktyā kriyate sva saṃvedyena eva avyavahitena vidyā samarpitena svāsthyena tad siddheḥ
na ca nitya siddha niḥśreyasa nivedanasya asādhya phalasya vijñānasya gati anucintane kācid apekṣā upapadyate
tasmāt apara viṣayā gatiḥ
tatra para apara brahma viveka anavadhāraṇena aparasmin brahmaṇi vartamānāḥ gati śrutayaḥ parasmin adhyāropyante
kim dve brahmaṇī param aparam ca iti
bāḍham etat vai satyakāma param ca aparam ca brahma yat oṃkāraḥ ityādi darśanāt
kim punar param brahma kim aparam iti ucyate yatra avidyā kṛta nāma rūpa ādi viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt a sthūla ādi śabdaiḥ brahma upadiśyate tat param
tat eva yatra nāma rūpa ādi viśeṣeṇa kenacid viśiṣṭam upāsanāya upadiśyate manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ iti ādi śabdaiḥ tat aparam
nanu evam advitīya śrutiḥ uparudhyeta na avidyā kṛta nāma rūpa upādhika tayā parihṛta tvāt
tasya ca apara brahma upāsanasya tad saṃnidhau śrūyamāṇam sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ bhavati ityādi jagat aiśvarya lakṣaṇam saṃsāra gocaram eva phalam bhavati anivartita tvāt avidyāyāḥ
tasya ca deśa viśeṣa avabaddha tvāt tad prāpti artham gamanam aviruddham
sarvagata tve pi ca ātmanaḥ ākāśasya iva ghaṭa ādi gamane buddhi ādi upādhi gamane gamana prasiddhiḥ iti avādiṣma tad guṇa sāra tvāt iti atra
tasmāt kāryam bādariḥ iti eṣaḥ eva sthitaḥ pakṣaḥ
param jaiminiḥ iti tu pakṣa antara pratibhāna mātra pradarśanam prajñā vikāsanāya iti draṣṭavyam
apraṃtīka ālambanāt nayati iti bādarāyaṇaḥ ubhayathā doṣāt tad kratuḥ ca
apratīka ālambana adhikaraṇam
sthitam etat kārya viṣayā gatiḥ na para viṣayā iti
idam idānīm saṃdihyate kim sarvān vikāra ālambanān aviśeṣeṇa eva amānavaḥ puruṣaḥ prāpayati brahma lokam uta kāṃścid eva iti
kim tāvat prāptam
sarveṣām eva eṣām viduṣām anyatra parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ gatiḥ syāt
tathā hi aniyamaḥ sarvāsām iti atra aviśeṣeṇa eva eṣā vidyā antareṣu avatāritā iti
evam prāpte pratyāha a pratīka ālambanān iti
pratīka ālambanān varjayitvā sarvān anyān vikāra ālambanān nayati brahma lokam iti bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
na hi evam ubhayathābhāva abhyupagame kaścid doṣaḥ sti aniyama nyāyasya pratīka vyatirikteṣu api upāsaneṣu upapatteḥ
tad kratuḥ ca asya ubhayathābhāvasya samarthakaḥ hetuḥ draṣṭavyaḥ
yaḥ hi brahma kratuḥ sa brāhmam aiśvaryam āsīdet iti śliṣyate tam yathā yathā upāsate tat eva bhavati iti śruteḥ na tu pratīkeṣu brahma kratu tvam asti pratīka pradhāna tvāt upāsanasya
nanu abrahma kratuḥ api brahma gacchati iti śrūyate
yathā pañcāgni vidyāyām saḥ enān brahma gamayati iti bhavatu yatra evam āhatyavādaḥ upalabhyate
tad abhāve tu autsargikeṇa tad kratu nyāyena brahma kratūnām eva tad prāptiḥ na itareṣām iti gamyate
viśeṣam ca darśayati
nāma ādiṣu pratīka upāsaneṣu pūrvasmāt pūrvasmāt phala viśeṣam uttarasmin uttarasmin upāsane darśayati yāvat nāmnaḥ gatam tatra asya yathākāma cāraḥ bhavati vāc vāva nāmnaḥ bhūyasī yāvat vācaḥ gatam tatra asya yathākāma cāraḥ bhavati manaḥ vāva vācaḥ bhūyaḥ ityādinā
sa ca ayam phala viśeṣaḥ pratīka tantra tvāt upāsanānām upapadyate
brahma tantra tve tu brahmaṇaḥ viśiṣṭa tvāt katham phala viśeṣaḥ syāt
tasmāt na pratīka ālambanānām itaraiḥ tulya phala tvam iti
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ

caturthaḥ dhyāyaḥ
caturthaḥ pādaḥ
sampadya āvirbhāvaḥ svena śabdāt
saṃpadi āvirbhāva adhikaraṇam
kevalena eva ātmanā āvirbhavati na dharma antareṇa iti
kutas
svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti sva śabdāt
anyathā hi sva śabdena viśeṣaṇam anavaklṛptam syāt
nanu ātmīya abhiprāyaḥ sva śabdaḥ bhaviṣyati na tasya avacanīya tvāt
yena eva hi kenacid rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate tasya eva ātmīya tva upapatteḥ svena iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam syāt
ātma vacanatāyām tu arthavat kevalena eva ātma rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate na āgantukena apara rūpeṇa api iti
kaḥ punar viśeṣaḥ pūrva avasthāsu iha ca svarūpa anapāya sāmye sati iti atas āha
muktaḥ pratijñānāt
yaḥ tra abhiniṣpadyate iti uktaḥ sa sarva bandha vinirmuktaḥ śuddhena eva ātmanā avatiṣṭhate
pūrvatra tu andhaḥ bhavati api roditi iva vināśam eva api itas bhavati iti ca avasthā traya kaluṣitena ātmanā iti ayam viśeṣaḥ
katham punar avagamyate muktaḥ yam idānīm bhavati iti
pratijñānāt iti āha
tathā hi etam tu eva te bhūyas nuvyākhyāsyāmi iti avasthā traya doṣa vihīnam ātmānam vyākhyeya tvena pratijñāya aśarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti ca upanyasya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate saḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca upasaṃharati
tathā ākhyāyikā upakrame pi yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā ityādi mukta ātma viṣayam eva pratijñānam
phala tva prasiddhiḥ api mokṣasya bandha nivṛtti mātra apekṣā na apūrva upajana apekṣā
yat api abhiniṣpadyate iti utpatti paryāya tvam tat api na apūrva avasthā apekṣam yathā roga nivṛttau arogaḥ bhiniṣpadyate iti tadvat
tasmāt adoṣaḥ
ātmā prakaraṇāt
katham punar muktaḥ iti ucyate yāvatā param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadye iti kārya gocaram eva enam śrāvayati jyotiḥ śabdasya bhautike jyotiṣi rūḍha tvāt
na ca anativṛttaḥ vikāra viṣayāt kaścid muktaḥ bhavitum arhati vikārasya ārta tva prasiddheḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ yatas ātmā eva atra jyotiḥ śabdena āvedyate prakaraṇāt
yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ iti prakṛte parasmin ātmani na akasmāt bhautikam jyotiḥ śakyam grahītum prakṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriyā prasaṅgāt
jyotiḥ śabdaḥ tu ātmani api dṛśyate tat devāḥ jyotiṣām jyotiḥ iti
prapañcitam ca etat jyotiḥ darśanāt iti atra
avibhāgena dṛṣṭa tvāt
a vibhāga adhikaraṇam
param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate yaḥ sa kim parasmāt ātmanaḥ pṛthak eva bhavati uta avibhāgena eva avatiṣṭhate iti vīkṣāyām sa tatra paryeti iti adhikaraṇa adhikartavya nirdeśāt jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya iti ca kartṛ karma nirdeśāt bhedena eva avasthānam iti yasya matiḥ tam vyutpādayati avibhaktaḥ eva pareṇa ātmanā muktaḥ vatiṣṭhate
kutas
dṛṣṭa tvāt
tathā hi tattvam asi aham brahma asmi yatra na anyat paśyati na tu tat dvitīyam asti tatas yat paśyet iti evamādīni vākyāni avibhāgena eva paramātmānam darśayanti
yathā darśanam eva ca phalam yuktam tad kratu nyāyāt
yathā udakam śuddhe śuddham āsiktam tādṛś eva bhavati
evam muneḥ vijānataḥ ātmā bhavati gautamaḥ iti ca evamādīni mukta svarūpa nirūpaṇa parāṇi vākyāni avibhāgam eva darśayanti
nadī samudra ādi nidarśanāni ca
bheda nirdeśaḥ tu abhede pi upacaryate sa bhagavaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti sve mahimni iti ātma ratiḥ ātma krīḍaḥ iti ca evamādi darśanāt
brāhmeṇa jaiminiḥ upanyāsa ādibhyaḥ
brāhma adhikaraṇam
sthitam etat svena rūpeṇa iti atra ātma mātra rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate na āgantukena apara rūpeṇa iti
adhunā tu tad viśeṣa bubhutsāyām abhidhīyate svam asya rūpam brāhmam apahata pāpma tva ādi satya saṃkalpa tva avasānam tathā sarvajña tvam sarva īśvara tvam ca tena sva rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
kutas
upanyāsa ādibhyaḥ tathātva avagamāt
tathā hi yaḥ ātmā apahata pāpmā ityādinā satya kāmaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti evam antena upanyāsena evamātmaka tām ātmanaḥ bodhayati
tathā sa tatra paryeti jakṣat krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ iti aiśvarya rūpam āvedayati tasya sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati iti ca
sarvajñaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ ityādi vyapadeśāḥ ca evam upapannāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti
citi tanmātreṇa tad ātmaka tvāt iti auḍulomiḥ
yadi api apahatapāpma tva ādayaḥ bhedena eva dharmāḥ nirdiśyante tathā api śabda vikalpa jāḥ eva ete
pāpma ādi nivṛtti mātram hi tatra gamyate
caitanyam eva tu asya ātmanaḥ svarūpam iti tanmātreṇa svarūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ yuktā
tathā ca śrutiḥ evam vai are yam ātmā anantaraḥ bāhyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ prajñāna ghanaḥ eva iti evaṃjātīyakā anugṛhītā bhaviṣyati
satyakāmatva ādayaḥ tu yadi api vastu svarūpeṇa eva dharmāḥ ucyante satyāḥ kāmāḥ asya iti tathā api upādhi saṃbandha adhīna tvāt teṣām na caitanya vat svarūpa tva saṃbhavaḥ aneka ākāra tva pratiṣedhāt
pratiṣiddham hi brahmaṇaḥ na eka ākāra tvam na parasya ubhaya liṅgam iti atra
atas eva ca jakṣaṇa ādi saṃkīrtanam api duḥkha abhāva mātra abhiprāyam stuti artham ātma ratiḥ ityādi vat
na hi mukhyāni eva rati krīḍā mithunāni ātma nimittāni śakyante varṇayitum dvitīya viṣaya tvāt teṣām
tasmāt nirasta aśeṣa prapañcena prasannena avyapadeśyena bodha ātmanā abhiniṣpadyate iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
evam api upanyāsāt pūrva bhāvāt avirodham bādarāyaṇaḥ
evam api pāramārthika caitanya mātra svarūpa abhyupagame vyavahāra apekṣayā pūrvasya api upanyāsa ādibhyaḥ vagatasya brāhmasya aiaiśvarya rūpasya a pratyākhyānāt avirodham bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ manyate
saṃkalpāt eva tu tad śruteḥ
saṃkalpa adhikaraṇam
hārdavidyāyām śrūyate sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ bhavati saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhanti ityādi
tatra saṃśayaḥ kim saṃkalpaḥ eva kevalaḥ pitṛ ādi samutthāne hetuḥ uta nimitta antara sahitaḥ iti
tatra sati api saṃkalpāt eva iti śravaṇe loka vat nimitta antara apekṣa tā yuktā
yathā loke asmad ādīnām saṃkalpāt gamana ādibhyaḥ ca hetubhyaḥ pitṛ ādi saṃpattiḥ bhavati evam muktasya api syāt
evam dṛṣṭa viparītam na kalpitam bhaviṣyati
saṃkalpāt eva iti tu rājñaḥ iva saṃkalpita artha siddhi karīm sādhana antara sāmagrīm sulabhām apekṣya yokṣyate
na ca saṃkalpa mātra samutthānāḥ pitṛ ādayaḥ manoratha vijṛmbhita vat cañcala tvāt puṣkalam bhogam samarpayitum paryāptāḥ syuḥ iti
evam prāpte brūmaḥ saṃkalpāt eva tu kevalāt pitṛ ādi samutthānam iti
kutas
tad śruteḥ
saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhanti ityādikā hi śrutiḥ nimitta antara apekṣāyām pīḍyeta
nimitta antaram api tu yadi saṃkalpa anuvidhāyi eva syāt bhavatu
na tu prayatna antara saṃpādyam nimitta antaram iṣyate prāk saṃpatteḥ vandhya saṃkalpa tva prasaṅgāt
na ca śruti avagamye rthe loka vat iti sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam kramate
saṃkalpa balāt eva ca eṣām yāvat prayojanam sthairya upapattiḥ prākṛta saṃkalpa vilakṣaṇa tvāt mukta saṃkalpasya
atas eva ca an anya adhipatiḥ
atas eva ca avandhya saṃkalpa tvāt ananya adhipatiḥ vidvān bhavati na asya anyaḥ dhipatiḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ
na hi prākṛtaḥ saṃkalpayan anya svāmika tvam ātmanaḥ satyām gatau saṃkalpayati
śrutiḥ ca etat darśayati atha ye iha ātmānam anuvidya vrajanti etān ca satyān kāmān teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati iti
abhāvam bādariḥ āha hi evam
abhāva adhikaraṇam
saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhanti iti atas śruteḥ manaḥ tāvat saṃkalpa sādhanam siddham
śarīra indriyāṇi punar prāpta aiśvaryasya viduṣaḥ santi na vā santi iti samīkṣyate
tatra bādariḥ tāvat ācāryaḥ śarīrasya indriyāṇām ca abhāvam mahīyamānasya viduṣaḥ manyate
kasmāt
evam hi āha āmnāyaḥ manasā etān kāmān paśyan ramate ye ete brahma loke iti
yadi manasā śarīra indriyaiḥ ca vihareta manasā iti viśeṣaṇam na syāt
tasmāt abhāvaḥ śarīra indriyāṇām mokṣe
bhāvam jaiminiḥ vikalpa āmananāt
jaiminiḥ tu ācāryaḥ manaḥ vat śarīrasya api sa indriyasya bhāvam muktam prati manyate
yatas saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādinā anekadhā bhāva vikalpam āmananti
na hi anekavidha tā vinā śarīrabhedena āñjasī syāt
yadi api nirguṇāyām bhūmavidyāyām ayam anekadhā bhāva vikalpaḥ paṭhyate tathā api vidyamānam eva idam saguṇa avasthāyām aiśvaryam bhūmavidyā stutaye saṃkīrtyate iti atas saguṇa vidyā phala bhāvena upatiṣṭhate iti
ucyate
dvādaśa ahavat ubhayavidham
bādarāyaṇaḥ punar ācāryaḥ atas eva ubhaya liṅga śruti darśanāt ubhayavidha tvam sādhu manyate yadā sa śarīra tām saṃkalpayati tadā sa śarīraḥ bhavati yadā tu aśarīra tām tadā aśarīraḥ iti
satya saṃkalpa tvāt saṃkalpa vaicitryāt ca
dvādaśa aha vat yathā dvādaśa ahaḥ satram ahīnaḥ ca bhavati ubhaya liṅga śruti darśanāt evam idam api iti
tanu abhāve sandhya vat upapatteḥ
yadā tanoḥ sa indriyasya śarīrasya abhāvaḥ tadā yathā saṃdhye sthāne śarīra indriya viṣayeṣu a vidyamāneṣu api upalabdhi mātrāḥ eva pitṛ ādi kāmāḥ bhavanti evam mokṣe syuḥ
evam hi etat upapadyate
bhāve jāgrat vat
bhāve punar tanoḥ yathā jāgarite vidyamānāḥ eva pitṛ ādi kāmāḥ bhavanti evam muktasya api upapadyate
pradīpa vat āveśaḥ tathā hi darśayati
pradīpa adhikaraṇam
bhāvam jaiminiḥ vikalpa āmananāt iti atra sa śarīra tvam muktasya uktam
tatra tridhābhāva ādiṣu aneka śarīra sarge kim nirātmakāni śarīrāṇi dāruyantra vat sṛjyante kim vā sātmakāni asmat ādi śarīra vat iti bhavati vīkṣā
tatra ca ātma manasoḥ bheda anupapatteḥ ekena śarīreṇa yogāt itarāṇi śarīrāṇi nirātmakāni iti evam prāpte pratipadyate pradīpa vat āveśaḥ iti
yathā pradīpaḥ ekaḥ aneka pradīpa bhāvam āpadyate vikāra śakti yogāt evam ekaḥ pi san vidvān aiśvarya yogāt aneka bhāvam āpadya sarvāṇi śarīrāṇi āviśati
kutas
tathā hi darśayati śāstram ekasya aneka bhāvam saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati pañcadhā saptadhā navadhā ityādi
na etat dāruyantra upama abhyupagame na api jīva antara āveśe
na ca nirātmakānām śarīrāṇām pravṛttiḥ saṃbhavati
yat tu ātma manasoḥ bheda anupapatteḥ aneka śarīra yoga asaṃbhavaḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
eka manaḥ nuvartīni sa manaskāni eva aparāṇi śarīrāṇi satya saṃkalpa tvāt srakṣyati
sṛṣṭeṣu ca teṣu upādhi bhedāt bhedena adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam yokṣyate
eṣā eva ca yoga śāstreṣu yoginām aneka śarīra yoga prakriyā
katham punar muktasya aneka śarīra āveśa ādi lakṣaṇam aiśvaryam abhyupagamyate yāvatā tat kena kam vijānīyāt na tu tad dvitīyam asti tatas vibhaktam yat vijānīyāt salilaḥ ekaḥ draṣṭā advaitaḥ bhavati iti ca evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ viśeṣa vijñānam vārayati iti atas uttaram paṭhati
sva apyaya sampattyoḥ anyatara apekṣam āviṣkṛtam hi
sva apyayaḥ suṣuptam svam apītaḥ bhavati tasmāt enam svapiti iti ācakṣate iti śruteḥ
saṃpattiḥ kaivalyam brahma eva san brahma apyeti iti śruteḥ
tayoḥ anyatarām avasthām apekṣya etat viśeṣa saṃjñā bhāva vacanam kvacid suṣupta avasthām apekṣya ucyate kvacid kaivalya avasthām
katham avagamyate
yatas tatra eva etat adhikāra vaśāt āviṣkṛtam etebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni eva anu vinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt yatra suptaḥ na kaṃcana kāmam kāmayate na kaṃcana svapnam paśyati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ
sa guṇa vidyā vipāka sthānam tu etat svarga ādi vat avasthā antaram yatra etat aiśvaryam upavarṇyate
tasmāt adoṣaḥ
jagat vyāpāra varjam prakaraṇāt asaṃnihita tvāt ca
jagat vyāpāra adhikaraṇam
ye saguṇa brahma upāsanāt saha eva manasā īśvara sāyujyam vrajanti kim teṣām niravagraham aiśvaryam bhavati āhosvit sāvagraham iti saṃśayaḥ
kim tāvat prāptam
niraṅkuśam eva eṣām aiśvaryam bhavitum arhati āpnoti svārājyam sarve smai devāḥ balim āvahanti teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāraḥ bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ iti
evam prāpte paṭhati jagat vyāpāra varjam iti
jagat utpatti ādi vyāpāram varjayitvā anyat aṇima ādi ātmakam aiśvaryam muktānām bhavitum arhati jagat vyāpāraḥ tu nitya siddhasya eva īśvarasya
kutas
tasya tatra prakṛta tvāt
asaṃnihita tvāt ca itareṣām
paraḥ eva hi īśvaraḥ jagat vyapāre dhikṛtaḥ tam eva prakṛtya utpatti ādi upadeśāt nitya śabda nibandhana tvāt ca
tad anveṣaṇa vijijñāsana pūrvakam tu itareṣām aṇima ādi aiśvaryam śrūyate
tena asaṃnihitāḥ te jagat vyāpāre
samanaska tvāt eva ca eteṣām anaikamatye kasyacid sthiti abhiprāyaḥ kasyacid saṃhāra abhiprāyaḥ iti evam virodhaḥ pi kadācid syāt
atha kasyacid saṃkalpam anu anyasya saṃkalpaḥ iti avirodhaḥ samarthyeta tatas parameśvara ākūta tantra tvam eva itareṣām iti vyavatiṣṭhate
pratyakṣa upadeśāt iti ced na ādhikārika maṇḍala stha ukteḥ
atha yat uktam āpnoti svārājyam ityādi pratyakṣa upadeśāt niravagraham aiśvaryam viduṣām nyāyyam iti tat parihartavyam
atrā ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ ādhikārika maṇḍala stha ukteḥ
ādhikārikaḥ yaḥ savitṛ maṇḍala ādiṣu viśeṣa āyataneṣu avasthitaḥ paraḥ īśvaraḥ tad āyattā eva iyam svārājya prāptiḥ ucyate
yatkāraṇam anantaram āpnoti manasaspatim iti āha
yaḥ hi sarva manasām patiḥ pūrva siddhaḥ īśvaraḥ tam prāpnoti iti etat uktam bhavati
tad anusāreṇa eva ca anantaram vākpatiḥ cakṣuṣpatiḥ
śrotra patiḥ vijñāna patiḥ ca bhavati iti āha
evam anyatra api yathāsaṃbhavam nitya siddheśvara āyattam eva itareṣām aiśvaryam yojayitavyam
vikāra āvarti ca tathā hi sthitim āha
vikāra āvarti api ca nityam uktam pārameśvaram rūpam na kevalam vikāra mātra gocaram savitṛ maṇḍala ādi adhiṣṭhānam
tathā hi asya dvirūpām sthitim āha āmnāyaḥ tāvān asya mahimā tatas jyāyāḥ ca puruṣaḥ
pādaḥ u sya sarvā bhūtāni tri pādasya amṛtam divi iti evamādiḥ
na ca tat nirvikāra rūpam itara ālambanāḥ prāpnuvanti iti śakyam vaktum a tad kratu tvāt teṣām
atas ca yathā eva dvirūpe parameśvare nirguṇam rūpam an avāpya saguṇe eva avatiṣṭhante evam saguṇe pi niravagraham aiśvaryam an avāpya sa avagrahe eva avatiṣṭhante iti draṣṭavyam
darśayataḥ ca evam pratyakṣa anumāne
darśayataḥ ca vikāra āvarti tvam parasya jyotiṣaḥ śruti smṛtī na tatra sūryaḥ bhāti na candra tārakam na imāḥ vidyutaḥ bhānti kutas yam agniḥ iti na tat bhāsayate sūryaḥ na śaśāṅkaḥ na pāvakaḥ iti ca
tat evam vikāra āvarti tvam parasya jyotiṣaḥ prasiddham iti abhiprāyaḥ
bhoga mātra sāmya liṅgāt ca
itas ca na niraṅkuśam vikāra ālambanānām aiśvaryam yasmāt bhoga mātram eva eṣām anādisiddhena īśvareṇa samānam iti śrūyate tam āha apaḥ vai khalu mīyante iti sa yathā etām devatām sarvāṇi bhūtāni avanti evam ha evaṃvidam sarvāṇi bhūtāni avanti tena u etasyai devatāyai sāyujyam salokatām jayati ityādi bheda vyapadeśa liṅgebhyaḥ
nanu evam sati sa atiśaya tvāt antavat tvam aiśvaryasya syāt
tatas ca eṣām āvṛttiḥ prasajyeta iti atas uttaram bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ ācāryaḥ paṭhati
anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt
nāḍī raśmi samanvitena arciḥ ādi parvaṇā deva yānena pathā ye brahma lokam śāstra ukta viśeṣaṇam gacchanti yasmin naraḥ ca ha vai brahma loke tṛtīyasyām itas divi yasmin airam madīyam saraḥ yasmin aśvatthaḥ soma savanaḥ yasmin aparājitā pūḥ brahmaṇaḥ yasmin ca prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam veśma yaḥ ca anekadhā mantra arthavāda ādi pradeśeṣu prapañcyate te tam prāpya na candra lokāt iva bhukta bhogāḥ āvartante
kutas
tayā ūrdhvam āyan amṛta tvam eti teṣām na punar āvṛttiḥ etena pratipadyamānāḥ imam mānavam āvartam na āvartante brahma lokam abhisaṃpadyante na ca punar āvartate ityādi śabdebhyaḥ
antavat tve tu aiśvaryasya yathā anāvṛttiḥ tathā varṇitam kārya atyaye tat adhyakṣeṇa saha atas param iti atra
samyak darśana vidhvasta tamasām tu nitya siddha nirvāṇa parāyaṇānām siddhā eva anāvṛttiḥ
tad āśrayaṇena eva hi saguṇa śaraṇānām api anāvṛtti siddhiḥ iti
anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt iti sūtra abhyāsaḥ śāstra parisamāptim dyotayati
iti śrīmat paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācārya asya śrī govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya śrīmat śaṃkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ
iti śrīmat śārīraka mīmāṃsā sūtra bhāṣyam saṃpūrṇam
